MAT 1:1 Ishitabu ishashikholo isha Yesu Klisiti umwana wa Daudi, umwana wa Ibrahimu.
MAT 1:2 U Ibrahimu ahali yise wa Isaka, Uisaka ahali yise wa Yakobo, u Yakobo ahali yise wa Yuda na bhaholo bhakwe.
MAT 1:3 U Yuda ahali yise wa Peresi nu Sera hwa Tamari, Peresi yise wa Hezeroni, u Hezeroni yise wa Ramu.
MAT 1:4 U Ramu ahali yise wa Aminadabu, u Aminadabu ahali yise wa Nshoni, u Nashoni yise wa Salimoni.
MAT 1:5 U Salimoni ahali yise wa Boazi hwa Rahabu, u Boazi yise wa Obedi hwa Ruth, U Obedi yise wa Yese,
MAT 1:6 u Yese ahali yise wa mfalume u Daudi. U Daudi ahali yise wa Sulemani hwa nshi wa Uria.
MAT 1:7 Usulemani ahali yise wa Rehoboamu, u Rehoboamu yise wa Abiya, u Abiya yise wa Asa.
MAT 1:8 U Asa ahali yise wa Yehoshafati, u Yehoshafati yise wa Yoramu, u Yoramu yise wa Uzia.
MAT 1:9 U Uzia ahali yise wa Yothamu, u Yothamu yise wa Ahazi, u Ahazi yise wa Hezekia.
MAT 1:10 U Hezekia ahali yise wa Manase, u Manase yise wa Amoni u Amoni yise wa Yosia.
MAT 1:11 U Yosia ahali yise wa Yekonia na kaka bhakwe lwebhahegwaga abhale hu Babeli.
MAT 1:12 Baada ya hwegwe abhale hu Babeli, u Yekonia ahali yise wa Shatieli, u Shatieli ahali mwizukulu wa Zerubabeli.
MAT 1:13 u Zerubabeli ahali yise wa Abiudi, u Abiudi yise wa Eliakimu, u Eliakimu yise wa Azori.
MAT 1:14 U Azori ahali yise wa Zadoki, u Zadoki yise wa Akimu u Akimu yise wa Eliudi.
MAT 1:15 U Eliudi ahali yise wa Elieza, u Elieza yise wa Matani u Matani yise wa Yakobo.
MAT 1:16 U Yakobo ahali yise wa Yusufu unume wa Mariamu, yehwamwene u Yesu ahapapwilwe, yahwitwa Klisiti.
MAT 1:17 Impapo zyonti afume hwa Ibrahimu hadi hwa Daudi zyahali impapo kumi na nne, afume hwa Daudi hadi hwegwe abhale hwa Babeli impapo kumi na nne, na afume ahwegwe afume hu Babeli hadi hwa Klisiti impapo kumi na nne.
MAT 1:18 Apapwe hwa Yesu Klisiti hwahali ishi. Unyina wakwe u Mariamu, ahazinjiwilwe nu Yusufu, ishi shebhasili alolane ahaloleshe aje alinivyanda hwa mpepo umfinjile.
MAT 1:19 Unume wakwe u Yusufu, ahali muntu wi lyoli zaga ahauzaga hukenyesye hubhantu. Ahamuye ahwimilisye husili.
MAT 1:20 Nahasibhaga ahusu amamba iga, uwantumi uwa ngumbhi ahamfumiiye hunjozi, ahaga, “Yusufu mwana wa Daudi, usahogope humweje u Mariamu unshi waho pipo ulwanda lwali nalwo lufumiline nu Mepo umfinjile.
MAT 1:21 Abhapape umwana unsahala ubhalunkwize itawa lyakwe yu Yesu, papo anzahubhokole abhantu bhakwe ni dhambi zyabho.”
MAT 1:22 Gonti gahafumiye aje nkezibhombeshe zyezyayangwile nu gosi hwidala lya kuwa aje,
MAT 1:23 “Enya, u bikira ahayibha ni vyanda ahayipapa umwana uwishilume itawa lyakwe abhahukwizye yu Imanueli” — imaana yakwe, “Ungulubhi ali natwi.”
MAT 1:24 U Yusufu ahadamushe mutulo na bhombe ndeshe abhantumi ngosi she bhahamuzizye na ahamwejile unshi wakwe.
MAT 1:25 Hata shinisho, sagahagonile nawo mpaka lwahapapa umwana uwishilume ahankwizya itawa lyakwe yu Yesu.
MAT 2:1 Baada ya Yesu apapwe Mubethelehem iya Huuyahudi hu nsiku izya mwene u Herode, abhantu bhebhazizye afume humashariki iya patali bhahafishile hu Yerusalemu bhahaga,
MAT 2:2 “Ali hwoshi yapapilwe umwene wabhayahudi? Tahayilolile inzota ya humashariki nati tinzile humpute.”
MAT 2:3 Umwene u Herode la ahumvwa iga ahalalamushe ni Yerusalemu youti peka nu mwene.
MAT 2:4 Uherode ahabhabhunginye agosi bhaadimi bhonti na asimbi bha bhantu, ahabhabhuzya, “Klisiti abhapapwe hwi?”
MAT 2:5 Bhamuzya, “Hu Bethelehemu iya Huyahudi, ishi sheyahasimbilwe na akuwa,
MAT 2:6 Naawe Bethelehemu, munsi iya Yuda, siga ndodo peka na alongozi abha hu Yuda, pipo afume huliwe abhahwinze umwene yahayibhadima abhantu bhani abha Israeli.”
MAT 2:7 Isho u Herode ahabhakwizizye bhala abhazyi hu siri na hubhabhuzye aje habhalilizyo bhuli inzota iloleshe.
MAT 2:8 Ahabhatuma hu Bethelehemu, ahaga, “Bhalaji na hwenyelezye mumwanze umwana ya papilwe. Nkemwanola mundetele ihabari aje nani nkininze humpute.”
MAT 2:9 Baada ya manye aje bhamwimvwizye umwene bhahendeliye ashule, ni mota ila yebhahayilolile humashariki yahabhalongoleye mpa lweyahimilila pala pa mwanya umwana ahapapilwe pansi yakwe.
MAT 2:10 Lwe bhahayilola inzota bhahashiye hani.
MAT 2:11 Bhahinjiye munyumba nahunole umwana yapapilwe nu Mariamu unyina wakwe. Bhamwinamiye na humpute. Bhahiguye ivintu vyabho nahumfumizye izawadi zyabho izahabu nu uvumba ni manemane.
MAT 2:12 U Ngulubhi ahabhasoshile mndoto aje bhasahawele hwa Herode, kwa hiyo bhahasoguye abhale hunsi yabho hwidala ilyinji.
MAT 2:13 Baada ya sogole abhantumi bha Ngulubhi bhahamfumiye u Yusufu hunjozi ahadamushe, “Ua, humweje umwana nu nyina wakwe nu mwana na ahashimbiliye hu Misri. Mukhale hunuhwo mpaka lwe nahayibha bhuzya pipo u Herode ahumwana ili agoje.
MAT 2:14 Nunsiku u Yusufu ahadamusha na humweje umwana nu nyina wakwe ashimbilile Humisri.
MAT 2:15 Ahakhiye uhwo mpa u Herode nahafwa. Izi zyahafishiye shila Ungulubhi shahayinje ashilile hwa nkuwa, “Afume humisri inkwizizye mwana wani.”
MAT 2:16 U Herode, laahalola bhansufizye na bhantu abhazya, ahavitilwe hani. Ahalajizizye agoje abhana na bhonti abhishilume bhebhahali hu Bethelehemu na bhonti bhebhali pala ahwaudile amaha gabhili ahwishe pansi afume shebha yinje abhazyi.
MAT 2:17 Pe twalibhombile izwi lila lyelyaha yangwilwe nukuwa u Yeremia,
MAT 2:18 “Izi lyahimvwiha hu Ramah, impungo na zonde hani, u Raheli ahabhalililaga abhana bhakwe, na ahakhanile apumilizwe pipo abhana nabhamo.”
MAT 2:19 U Herode lwa hafwa abhantumi bha Ngulubhi bhahamwinziye u Yusufu mutulo uhwo hu Misri na yanje.
MAT 2:20 “Bhuha umweje umwa nu nyina wakwe mubhale hunsi iya hu Israeli pipo bhahanzaga uwumi wa mwana aje bhasahagoje.”
MAT 2:21 U Yusufu ahimiliye, amwega umwana nu mayi wakwe, ahinza munsi iyamu Israeli.
MAT 2:22 Ishi la ahwumvwa aje u Arikelau ahali mwini wa hu Yuda pala pa yise wakwe u Herode, ahogope abhale uhwo. Baada ya Ngulubhi hunsoshe mutulo, ahasogoye abhale humukoa ugwa hu Galilaya,
MAT 2:23 ahabhalile akhale munsi yihwitwa Nazareti. Ili lyahatimiye hu zila zyezyahayangwilwe hwi dala lya kuwa aje bhasiakwizye Mnazareti.
MAT 3:1 Munsiku zila u Yohana Umwozyo ahinzile alumbilile hunyika iya hu Yuda ahaga,
MAT 3:2 “Mulambe pipo ubhumwini uwahumwanya bhusojeliye.”
MAT 3:3 Pipo unu yahayangwilwe nukuwa u Isaya ahaga, “Izwi lya muntu ya kwizya afume hujangwani; 'mubhishe tayari idala lya gosi, mugagoloshe amashilo gakwe.”
MAT 3:4 Ishi Uyohana ahakwite amasepe agingamia ni lamba ilyingozi musana wakwe, ishalye shakwe shahali nzije nu woshi uwa mwisengo.
MAT 3:5 Habhili Muyerusalemu, Iyuda yonti, ni sehemu yonti yeyahazyangulile isoho Iyordani bhahabhala hukwakwe.
MAT 3:6 Bhahozewaga nawo mwisoho mu Yordani bhalambaga hwangwubhi imbibhi zyabho.
MAT 3:7 Lwahabhalola abhinji abhamafalisayo na masadukayo lwebhahwuzya, “Amwe mwimpapo izyi nzoha izyi sumu wenu yabhasoshile huyishimbile inkuni yihwinza?
MAT 3:8 Mupape amadondo gegahwanziwa alaabe.
MAT 3:9 Mgandi asibhe na ayanjizanye hulimwe mwe, 'Tulinawo u Ibrahimu ye yise witu.' Pipo imbabhuzya aje Ungulubhi angamwimishizya u Ibrahimu abhana afumilane na mawe iga.
MAT 3:10 Intemu iliho ibhihwile hunzizi ugwi kwi. Ishi ikwi lyolyonti lyesalipapa amadondo lidumulwa na tajilwe mu mwoto.
MAT 3:11 Ihubhozya na manzi hunongwa ya lambe. Ishi umwene yahwinza badala yani ngosi kuliko ani. Nanisihwanziwa abhusye iyilyatu vyakwe. Umwene asibhozye hwa mpepo umfinjile na humwoto.
MAT 3:12 Na ulupapike lwakwe lulimunyobhe zyakwe lupepeta nziila na hwozye na abhunganye ingano zyakwe mushanga. Nantele abhapembe amakapi mumwoto wesebhuzimiha.
MAT 3:13 Nantele u Yesu ahinza afume hu Galilaya mpaka mwisoho Iyorodani ahwozewe nu Yohana.
MAT 3:14 Uyohana ahandaga akhane aje, “Asahamwozye pipo u Yesu gosi ashile u Yohana?”
MAT 3:15 U Yesu ahayanga ahaga, “Nini ihurusu awe unozye, maana ihwanziwa aje inkamilisye ilyoli yonti.” U Yohana pa ahamwozya u Yesu.
MAT 3:16 Baada ya hwozewe u Yesu ahafumile muminzi ahenya imwaaya zyahamwigushiye, nantele ahanola umpepo wa Ngulubhi ahwiha hushifwani shinjibha na ahwimilile pamwanya yakwe.
MAT 3:17 Izwi, lyahafumile humwanya lyahaga, “Unu mwana wani uganwa. Indi ni insungwo nawo hani.”
MAT 4:1 U Yesu ahalongozowilwe nu Mpepe mpaka hujangwa ili ajelwe nu setano.
MAT 4:2 Ahafunjile insiku arobaini nunsanya na nunsiku ahali ni nzala.
MAT 4:3 Uwinjelo ahinza ahamuzya, “Ahaga awe ukewe mwana wa Ngulubhi ugobhuzye amawe iga gabhe makati.”
MAT 4:4 Lelo u Yesu ahaga ahamuzya, “Iyandihwilwe, 'Umuntu sangakhala munsi umu alyanje gamakati gini, hata hwizwi lyolyonti lyelifuma hwa Ngulubhi.”
MAT 4:5 Habhili usetano ahantwalile mpaka munsi nyinza na humishe pamwanya hani pinyumba iyishibhanza,
MAT 4:6 na humuzye, hujenkushe awe uli mwana wa Ngulubhi, yidomosye mpaka pansi, pipo isimbilwe bhakwe bhinze bhatone nantele bhasibhusye humakhono gabho nkusahabumile mu mawe.”
MAT 4:7 U Yesu ahambula, “Ahaga habhili ahaga, 'Uganje hunjele u Ngulubhi waho.”
MAT 4:8 Habhili, usetano ahamwega na huntwale pigamba pamwanya hani ahanolesya insi zyontiinyinza.
MAT 4:9 Ahaga, “Inzahupele ivintu vyonti ivi nkewaninamila na humpute ani.”
MAT 4:10 U Yesu ahabhula, “Sogolaga uyepe ipa, setano! Pipo isimbilwe ihwanziwa humpute Ungulubhi waho, umombele yuyo mwimi.”
MAT 4:11 Usetano ahaneha, nahabhalola, abhantumi bhahinza humpute na humbhombele.
MAT 4:12 U Yesu naahanvwa aje u Yohana akhitwe, ahasoguye mpaka hu Galilaya.
MAT 4:13 Ahasoguye Hunazareti ahabhalile akhale Hukapernaumu, yilimunshinji mu bahari ya Hugalilaya, mumpaha mmajimbo ga Zabuloni nu Naftali.
MAT 4:14 Ili lyahafumiye aje likamiliswe lyelyahayangwile nu kuwa u Isaya,
MAT 4:15 “Munsi iya Zabuloni na munsi iya Naftali, abhale munsumbi mwisyila ilya Huyorodani, Hugalilaya iya hubhinsi!
MAT 4:16 Abhantu bhebhakhiye muhisi bhabhulolile umwanga ungosi hawi, na bhala bhebhahakhiye mwidala ilyifwe pamwanya ulukhozyo lukhozizye.”
MAT 4:17 Afume ahabhalilizyo iho u Yesu ahandile alumbilile aje, “Mulambe pipo ubhumwini uwahumwanya bhusojeliye.”
MAT 4:18 Lwahajendaga mushinji munsunbi iya Hugalilaya, ahabhalola aholo bhabhili, u Simoni yebhahakwizyaga yu Petro, nu Andrea ukaka wakwe, bhahatega inyavu mwusumbi pipo bhahasukulaga inswi.
MAT 4:19 U Yesu ahabhabhula ahaga, “Inzaji munfwate, imbabhabhishe mubhebhasukule abhantu.”
MAT 4:20 Pinipo bhahaluleha ulwelo bhaufwata u Yesu.
MAT 4:21 U Yesu lwahajendelelaga afume ipo ahabhalola aholobbhabhili abhamwabho, Yakobo umwana wa Zebedayo, nu Yohana ukaka wakwe. Bhahali mwitoli peka nu Zebedayo uyise wabho bhahasonaga ulwelo lwabho. Ahabhakwizwa,
MAT 4:22 pinipo bhahalileha itoli nu yise wabho bhope bhahanfuata.
MAT 4:23 U Yesu ahabhalile Mugalilaya yonti, ahamanyizyaga mu Masinagogi gabho, ahalumbililaga ibhangili ubhumuini aponye impungo ni mbina zyonti zya bhantu.
MAT 4:24 Inongwa zyakwe zyahayeshile Isiria yonti na abhantu bhahaleta abhabhinu bhebhali ni inpungo zinyinji, bhebhahali ni mpepo izyi shifafa na bhebhapoozizye. U Yesu ahabhaponizye.
MAT 4:25 Impuga ya bhantu yahali ngosi abhantu bhebhafuataga afume hu Galilaya, na Dekapoli, na Huyerusalemu na Huyahudi na afume mwisyila ilya hu Yorodani.
MAT 5:1 U Yesu lwahayilola impuga, ahasoguye abhale hwigamba. Lwahakhiye pansi asambilizyi bhakwe bhalinza.
MAT 5:2 Ahigula ilomu lyakwe ahabhamanyizya, ahaga,
MAT 5:3 “Hwashi abhapina bhi mwoyo pipo ubhumwini uwahumwanya wabho.
MAT 5:4 Hwashi abhaswimilizu pipi bhahayisubhizwa.
MAT 5:5 Hwashi abhapole, bhahayibha bhapyani bhi insi.
MAT 5:6 Hwashi abhinzala ni shumwilwa shilyoli pipo bhahayikuta.
MAT 5:7 Hwashi abhirehema pipo bhayibha ni rehema.
MAT 5:8 Hwashi abhimwoyo umwinza pipo bhayinola Ungulubhi.
MAT 5:9 Hwashi akundanyi, pipi bhabhabhe bhana bha Ngulubhi.
MAT 5:10 Hwashi bhebhayimba kwa ajili yi lyoli pipo ubhumwini uwahumwanya wabho.
MAT 5:11 Hwashi amwi yemuligwa na bhantu ua yimbe na yangwe hwilenga ubhibhi kwa ajili yani.
MAT 5:12 Mushanje ua lulutile pipo amasombo ginyu magosi hwa Ngulubhi. Pipo abhantu abhahwande bhahabha yimvizye akuwa bhebhali kabla yinyu.
MAT 5:13 Amwi libheya lyinsi ishi ibheya nkelitezizye uwinza wakwe selibhabhe libhe ya habhili? Selingabha lyinza habhili hu hantu hohonti, hulitaje hunzi ua akhanywe ni vinama vya bhantu.
MAT 5:14 Amwi lukhozyo lwinsi. Ikhaya yizengwilwa pamwanya pi gamba sihuyifisa.
MAT 5:15 Abhantu sebhahwansya itala nahuyibhishe pansi yishikapu, ila bhabhiha pamwanya imuliha bhonti bhebhali muhati munyumba.
MAT 5:16 Muleshe ulukhozyo lwinyu lukhozye hwilongolela hwa bhantu ihwanziwa huje abhantu bhagalole amatendo ginyu aminza na huutime u Ngulubhi uwahumwanya.
MAT 5:17 Msahaje ininzile ananganye indajizyo wa akuwa. Sininzile ananganye ininzile atomizye.
MAT 5:18 Amba lyoli ihumbabhuzya huje mpaka imwanya ninsi zyonti zishile nimo iyodi yeka wala inukuta yeka iyi sheria seyahayiyepa kila hantu lwehayibha tiyari.
MAT 5:19 Ishi wowonti yavunza iamuli indodo mojawapo yi amli izi na hubhamanyizye abhanji abhombe isho ahwitwa ndodo hubhumwini uwahumwanya. Lakini yeyote azishikaye na kuzifundisha ataitwa mkubwa katika ufalme wa mbinguni.
MAT 5:20 Pipo ihumbabhuzya ihaki yinyu nkeseyabhashila abhaandishi ya Mafalisayo, shoshonti shila semwahayiyinjila humwanya.
MAT 5:21 Mwinvwizye yahayangwilwe imandi aje, “usahagoje”'wowonti yagoga ahayilongwa.'
MAT 5:22 Ishi ihumbabhuzya wowonti yahumvitwa uholo wakwe ahayilongwa. Na yeyote amwambiaye ndugu yake kuwa, 'Wewe ni mtu uisyefaa!' atakuwa katika hatari ya baraza. Na yeyote asemaye, 'Wewe mjinga!' atakuwa katika hatari ya moto wa jehanamu.
MAT 5:23 Nkufumya isadaka yaho pashiputo ukumbuha huje uholo waho alininongwa nawe,
MAT 5:24 yileshe isadaka paushiputo ubhale ukundane nawo uholo waho nkuyinze ufumye isadaka yaho.
MAT 5:25 Kundana nu unongwi waho lubhilo lulipeka nawo mwidala lwemubhala humahakama, mukundane ili usahakungwe mwigereza.
MAT 5:26 Mwitishe ihumbabhuzya semwahayibha ahinza mpaka musombe amalando gemlongwa.
MAT 5:27 Mwinvwizye aje iyandihwilwe, 'Usahazini.'
MAT 5:28 Lelo ihubhabhuzya wowonti ya humwenya unshi hwahunsungwe uyo azinile nawo mumoyo wakwe.
MAT 5:29 Nki ilinso lyaho ilya hulilo lihusababisya abumile ulikunye ulitaji apatali nawe. Pipo hwashi ishilungo sheka mumbili waho shinanjishe kuliko ubili ngwonti gubhale hujehanamu.
MAT 5:30 Na nkushe inyobhe yaho indilo isababisya aje ubumile, udumule yoonti uyitajle apatali nawe. Pipo hwashi ishilungo sheka shinanjishe kuliko ubili gwonti gubhale hujehanamu.
MAT 5:31 Isimbilwe wowonti ya huminga unshi wakwe ampele italaka.'
MAT 5:32 Lelo ani ihumbabhuzya wowonti yahuneha unshi wakwe hunongwa yizanaa uyo amishile aje muzinzi. Na wowonti yahumwega unshi uyo wope uzinzi.
MAT 5:33 Tena, mwinvwizye aje yahayangwilwe hubhala abhimandi, 'Musaha lape ilenga lelo muntwalile Ungulubhi ilape hwinyu.'
MAT 5:34 Lelo ihumbabhuzya musahalape hata hadodo hata hwimwanya pipo imwanya enzi ya Ngulubhi;
MAT 5:35 Wala hunsi pipo mahali pakwe pabhishe itengo ilyakhanyile ivinama vyakwe, wala hwa Yerusalemu, maana khaya yamwini ugosi.
MAT 5:36 Usahalape hwitwe lyaho maana sungabhomba ulusisi lweka lubhe zeru au lwiru.
MAT 5:37 Lelo inongwa zyinyu zibhanje, 'Ena, ena, Ndali, ndali.' Pipo nkegonjela ipo gafuma hwa nugu.
MAT 5:38 Mwinvwizye aje iyangwilwe aje, “Jicho kwa jicho, na jino kwa jino.'
MAT 5:39 Lelo ani ihumbabhuzya mugandi atolane nu muntu umibhi; Lelo umuntu nkahukhoma imbuguzi iya hulilo umpele ni lya humongo.
MAT 5:40 Nu muntu wowonti yasungwa abhale nawe humahakama na afyula inkanzu yaho neshele ni joho lyaho.
MAT 5:41 Wowonti yahulazimisya ibhale umaili yeka bhala umaili zibhili.
MAT 5:42 Wowonti yahulabha umpele, yakhopa khopele.
MAT 5:43 Mwinvwizye iyangwile ugane, 'Umpalamani waho, unvitwe unugu waho.'
MAT 5:44 Lelo imbabhuzya mubhagane alugu bhinyu mubhaputile bhebhalubhavisya,
MAT 5:45 Nkemubhe bhana bha daada uwahumwanya. Pipo alamya isaya likholo hwabhibhi na bhinza, imvula itonya hwa bhabhibhi na bhinza.
MAT 5:46 Nkemwabhagana bhebhabhaganile amwi, mubhapate faida nshii? Mbona bhebhasongozya insoho sebhabhomba isho.
MAT 5:47 Nke mwabhalamuha aholo bhinyu bhini mubhapa ahenu ashile abhanji? Ishi!, abhantu bhinsi sebhabhomba isho?
MAT 5:48 Ishi ihwanziwa huje mubhe bhagolosu ndeshe Udada winyu uwahumwanya shali golosu.
MAT 6:1 Uyenyaje ungandi abhombe imbo inyinza hubhantu ili huyilolesye, subhapate ifaida hwa Dada uwahumwanya.
MAT 6:2 Ishi nufumya isadaka usahayitufye sana usahabhe ndeshe abhanafiki shebhabhomba mumasinagogi na mumitaa, nkaabhantu bhabhatime semubhapae ifaida nkiimo.
MAT 6:3 Lelo awe lufumya ukhona gwaho ugwa humongo gusahamanye sheshibhombeha hundilo,
MAT 6:4 ili huje isadaka yaho ufumye hu siri. Nkhu Udada waho yalola muhati abhalupele ithawabu yaho.
MAT 6:5 Na luputa usahabhe, udeshe anafiki, pipo abhene bhasungwa ahwimilile na pute, mumasinagogi na mukona izya mukhaya zyabho nka abhantu bha bhenye. Lelo ihumbabhuzya bhapite ithawabu yabho.
MAT 6:6 Awe luputa injila hu hati ufunje ulwiji upuute hwa Daada uwamumwoyo udaada ya lola muhati asipele ithawabu yaho.
MAT 6:7 Nu puta ungandi pyanile inongwa zyesezili ni maana, ndeshe abhamunsi shebhabhomba pipo bhasibha abhantu bhabhahubhiuvwe pipo bhayanga inongwa inyinji.
MAT 6:8 Ishi usahabhe ndeshe abhene pipo uDada aminye uhwanza henu shusile alabhe hukwakwe.
MAT 6:9 Uputaje ishi: Dada witu uwahumwanya itawa lyaho lyimishilwaje.
MAT 6:10 Ubhumwini waho winze, ulugano lwaho lubhombeshe pansi na humwanya.
MAT 6:11 Utipele ishalye shitu insiku zyonti.
MAT 6:12 Utukhobhoshele amalando gitu, ndeati shetihubhakhobhoshela abhimalando bhitu.
MAT 6:13 Usahatipe injelo, utidime nu setano.
MAT 6:14 Nkemwabhakhobhoshela abhantu amalando gabho, Udada winyu uwahumwanya abhahubhakhobhoshele namwi.
MAT 6:15 Nkushe mubhabhakhobhoshele abhantu Udada abhabhakhobhoshele makosa ginyu.
MAT 6:16 Hu gonti, lufunga usahalolesye uzugunizu humaso ndeshe abhanafiki shebhabhomba bhazugumila humiso nke abhantu bhamanye aje bhafunjile. Lyooli ihubhuzya bhapite ithawabu yabho.
MAT 6:17 Lelo, lufunga pahala amafuta hwitwe lyaho uyoje hunaso.
MAT 6:18 Subhaloleshe humaso gabhantu aje ufunjile, u Ngulubhi mweene yabhamanye Udada yamanya muhati abhahupele ithawabu yaho.
MAT 6:19 Usahabhishe amali gaho munsi umu zinanjiha na bhole na bhibha bhahwibha.
MAT 6:20 Badala yakwe, abhishe amali gaho hwa Ngulubhi, sibhahwibha, sigabhola wa segananjiha.
MAT 6:21 Pipo amali gaho pegali umwoyo waho pebhubhabhe.
MAT 6:22 Ilinso lukhozyo lwi bili. Nkushele, ilyinso lyaho lyumi ubili wonti, bhubhabhe nulukhozyo.
MAT 6:23 Nkushele ilyinso lyaho lifwiye, ubili waho wonti bhuli hisi haani. Ishi nkulukhozyo lweluli muhati muliwe hisi ahagosi ndeshe bhuli!
MAT 6:24 Numo nka weka yangabha na lume bha bhili, pipo abhahunvitwe unu na hugane uwinji lumo abhahwepe hwunu abhahu sufye uwinji. Hamuwezi kumtumikia Mungu na mali.
MAT 6:25 Ishi ihuhabhe nu sanje ahusu amaisha gaho aje ubhalyeshi, ubhamweleshi, ahusu ubili waho ubhakwate shi! Amaisha se haani yi shalye ubili haani yi meenda?
MAT 6:26 Enya inyonyi zyezipuluha humwanya. Saazitota sazivunza sazibhunganya na bhishe mushanka, lelo Udada uwahumwanya ahuzilisya. Je amwisemulibhi maana hani kuliko inyonyi?
MAT 6:27 Weemu hulimwe uwahuyitamye ankayonjezya idhiraa yeka huwomi wimaisha gakwe?
MAT 6:28 Ye enu mubha musaga aje yibhakwate nshi? Msubhilile amaua mmashamba shegabha segabhomba imbombo segahuyikwatizya.
MAT 6:29 Bado ihumbabhuzya hata yu Sulemani nu tuntumu wakwe saga ahakwatiziwilwe mojawapo yiga.
MAT 6:30 Nkushele Ungulubhi ahugakwatizya amasole agamumagunda, gegakhala isiku lyeka ni ndabhi gatagwa mumwoto je bhulibhuli angabhakwatizya amwi mwemuli nulwitiho uludodo?
MAT 6:31 Eshi musahasaje aje, 'Je tibhalyeshi?' au “Je tibhamweleshi?” au “Je tibhakhwate menda bhuli?”
MAT 6:32 Pipo abhinsi bhahuganza amambo iga, nu Dada winyu uwahumwanya aminye aje muhuganza igo.
MAT 6:33 Ishi nasuti mwanze ubhumwini wakwe ni lyoli yakwe nigo gonta gabhahwonjeleshe huliwe.
MAT 6:34 Ishi usahalole usahasaje kwa ajili yi ndabhi, pipo indabhi zibhamanyishe hunuhwo. Isiku lyolyonti likwiliye hwi tatizizo lyakwe.
MAT 7:1 Nkulonga, nawe wahayilongwa.
MAT 7:2 Alonje shuloonga nawe wahayilongwa na shuhubhapimila abhantu nawe wahayi pimilwa shinisho.
MAT 7:3 Yeenu uhwenya ishipande shikwi sheshili mwilyinso holo waho suminye ishipande shikwi shesheli mwilyinso lyaho ikwi liliho mwilyinso lyaho?
MAT 7:4 Unganda bhuli ayanje hwa holo waho aje ambaihwefwe ishipande sheshili mwilinso lyaho, wakati nawe wayo ulinasho mwilinso lyaho?
MAT 7:5 Ulinilenga awe; kwanza uyefwe ishipande sheshili mwilinso lyaho, nkubhahwefwe ahinza ishipande isha mwilinso lyaholo waho.
MAT 7:6 Usahazipele imbwa ivintu ivyinza usahazisumbile ungurubhi ishalye ishinza zinzananganye na khanye ni vinama habhili bhanza hulye nawe.
MAT 7:7 Labha ubhaposhele. Anza, nawe ubhapate. Khoma ihodi, anzahuhwigulile.
MAT 7:8 Pipo ya labha aposhela, na wowonti yahwanza aposhela. Umuntu yakhoma ihodi, ahumwigulila.
MAT 7:9 Aliho humwinyu umuntu umwana wakwe nkalabha umukate ahupela iwe?
MAT 7:10 Au nkanabha isamaki ahupela inzoha?
MAT 7:11 Nkushele, mubhimbibhi muminye hubhapele abhana bhinyu ivintu ivyinza, Je! Ungulubhi wenyu uwahumwanya sangabhapela hanii ivyinza bhebha hunabha umweene?
MAT 7:12 Ishi shuhwanza huje ubhombelwe na bhanji, nawe shubhombaje hwamwinyu, pipo izyo ndajizyo zya kuwa.
MAT 7:13 Mwinjile mulwiji unyeela. Pipo ulwiji lugosi idala ligosi lyelilongozya humwoto abhantu bhinji bhebhabhala idala ilyo.
MAT 7:14 Ulwiji unyeela lwa huwomi, abhantu bhadodo bhebhahwinjila umwo.
MAT 7:15 Muyenyaje na kuwa abhilenga, bhebhahwinza bhakwite ikwembe ilyingole, lakini muhati mbwa londe ihali.
MAT 7:16 Mubhabhamanye amadondo gabho. Je abhantu bhangatungula amadondo muminvwa, au mwikwi humbeyu iyi mbaruti?
MAT 7:17 Ishi ikwi lyolyonti, ilyinza lipapa amadondo aminza, lakini ikwi ibhibhi lipapa amadondo amabhibhi.
MAT 7:18 Ikwi ilyinza salingapapa amadondo amabhibhi, wala ikwi ibhibhi selingapapa amadondo aminza.
MAT 7:19 Ikwi lyolyonti lyesagalipapa amadondo aminza litemwa na pembele umwoto.
MAT 7:20 Abhantu abha bhibhi ubhabhamanye amadondo gabho.
MAT 7:21 Siga muntu wowonti yayiga, 'Ngurubhi, Ngulubhi,' yahayiyinjila hubhumwini uwahumwanya, ila yuyula yabhomba inyinza zya Ngulubhi uwahumwanya.
MAT 7:22 Abhantu abhinji isiku ilyo bhahayiyiga 'Ngulubhi, Ngulubhi, twahafumizye ukuwa hwitawa lyaho, hwitawa lyaho twahabhombile amambo minji aminza amagosi?'
MAT 7:23 U Ngulubhi ahayibhabhu aje, 'simbaminye mwepe! Ipa amwe, mubhabhomba imbibhi!'
MAT 7:24 Ishi kila muntu yahwinvwa amazwi gani na hugitishe alingana nu muntu uwihekima yazenjile inyumba yakwe pamwanya pa mawe.
MAT 7:25 Invura yatonya, awinzi gamema ahanvulungwe hinza hayikhoma inyumba iyo seya, gwa pansi pipo yahazengwilwe pamwanya pamawe.
MAT 7:26 Lelo umutu wowonti yahwunvwa uzwi lyani lyani sahulyitiha uyo abhafane nu muntu umpumbavu yazenga inyumba yakwe pamwanya pansanga.
MAT 7:27 Invula yinza, na minzi gamema na hamvulungwi hinza hayikhoma inyumba iyo yagwa na malishe pepala.”
MAT 7:28 U Yesu lwa hamala ayanje amazwi iga, abhantu bhahaswijile lwa hamanyizyaga.
MAT 7:29 Pipo ahamanyizyaga ndeshe umuntu uwimamlaka siyo ndeshe asimbi bhabho.
MAT 8:1 U Yesu lwahiha pansi afume mwigamba, impuga ya bhantu yahasojeliye.
MAT 8:2 Umukoma umo ahasugamiye hwilongolela lyakwe ahaga gosi inlabha umponye.”
MAT 8:3 U Yesu agolosyaa inyabhe yakwe ankhata amponya apona unkoma wepa.
MAT 8:4 Uyesu amuuzya aga, “Usahayanje hwa muntu wowonti. Bhalaga uyilolesye hwa mputi ufumye ni sadaka ye u Musa ahalajizizye ajili yiushuhuda hubhabhinu bhebhaponile mbina”
MAT 8:5 U Yesu lwahafiha hu Kapernaumu, un'gosi umo ahinza ahamuuzya
MAT 8:6 ahaga, “Gosi uwimbombo wani agonile hukhaya apoozizye ivinama vibhabha haani.”
MAT 8:7 U Yesu aga ishi, “Imbahwinze humponye.”
MAT 8:8 Ugosi ayanga aga, 'Yesu, ani si ndinithamani mapaka uyinjile muhati munyumba yani yanga izwi lwene uwimbombo abhapone.
MAT 8:9 Pipo ani indi na mamlaka, indina sikari bhebhali pansi yani. Nkenaga bhala 'nkenaga inza ahwinza nuuwimbo wani abhomba shinisho.'
MAT 8:10 U Yesu lwaahinvwa iga, ahaswijile nahubha bhuzye bhala bhebhahafwataga, “Lyoli ihumbabhuzya sindolile nkalumo umuntu uwilwitiho mu Israeli.
MAT 8:11 Ihubhabhuzya, bhinji bhahayiyinza afume humashariki na humagharibi, bhabhakhale pameza peka nu Abrahimu, Isaka, nu Yakobo, hu bhumwini uwahumwanya.
MAT 8:12 Lelo abhana bhibhumwini bhahayitagwa huhisi ha hunzi, hwehwaha yibha na lile na sye amino.”
MAT 8:13 U Yesu ahamuzya ugosi, “Bhalaga! ndeshe shuyitishe zibhombeshe shinisho huliwe uwimbombo ahaponile isaa yiyila.
MAT 8:14 U Yesu lwahafiha hukhaya hwa Petro, ahanola umayivyala wakwe wa Petro agonile abhinile inzegema.
MAT 8:15 U Yesu ahakhata inyobhe yakwe ni nzegema yepa apona. Adamuha ahande humpute hubhombele imbombo.
MAT 8:16 Lwe hwabha lyabhela, bhahabhaleta hwa Yesu abhantu abhimpepo. Abhaputila impepo zyepa bhapona.
MAT 8:17 Pepinipo gahaloleshe gala gegahayangwilwe nu ukuwa u Isaya aje, “U Yesu ahejile inpungo zyitu na ahazibhusizye imbina zyitu”
MAT 8:18 U Yesu lwahalola abhantu bhabhungine bhanzyunguliye, ahajile bhabhale uupande uwinji uwi nsumbi iya hu Galilaya.
MAT 8:19 Unsimbi ahinza hwa Yesu ahaga, “Mwalimu, imbahufwate poponti pubhala.”
MAT 8:20 U Yesu amuzya imbweha zilina mina ni uyonyi zilinivyanswi, lakini u Yesu sali ni nyumba na pagone na pamo.”
MAT 8:21 Umwanafunzi uwamwabho ahamwuzya ahaga, “Gosi ilabha uruhusa imbale insyile uyise wani.”
MAT 8:22 Lakini u Yesu ahamuzya ahaga, “Unifwate, bhaleshe abhafwe bhasyilane bhibho.”
MAT 8:23 U Yesu na ahinjila mwitooli, abhanafunzi bhakwe bhahinjiye mwitooli.
MAT 8:24 Aminzi, gaha yingana munsumbi mpaka itooli lyahagubishilwe na minzi, lakini u Yesu ahagonile.
MAT 8:25 Abhanafunzi bhakwe bhahinza hudamusye bhahaga twokole tihwanda afwe!”
MAT 8:26 U Yesu ahaga, “Muhwogopanshi, mubhilwitiho uludodo?” Ahadamuha na huyikhajile impepo ni nsumbi pamandi hwabha myee,
MAT 8:27 abhalume bhahaswijile bhaga, “Umuntu unu alibhulibhuli huje ni mpepo izya munsumbi zihumwitiha umwene?”
MAT 8:28 U Yesu lwa ahinza hunsi iya Magadala, abhalume bhabhili bhahali ni mpepo bhahakhomana nawo. Bhahafumiye humbipa bhahali bhakhali haani numo umuntu wahashilaga idala lila.
MAT 8:29 Bhahakholile na jeishi, tilinahenu nawe mwana wa Ngulubhi? Uyinzile ipa hutiyinvye ahabhalilizyo she hasili?”
MAT 8:30 Ishi hwahali impuga ingosi iyingurubhi lyahadimaga sepahali patali hani pebhahali,
MAT 8:31 impepo zyahalilaga hwa Yesu naje, “Tifume titwale mumpuga yingurubhi.”
MAT 8:32 U Yesu ahazibhuzya impepo ahaga, bhalaji mungurubhi. Impepo zila lwezyahinjila mungurubhi, ingurubhi zyahashimbiliye munsumbi afume, mwigamba zyahafwila muminzi.
MAT 8:33 Abhalume bhebhahadimaga ingurubhi bhashimbiye. Lwe bhahala humujini bhahayinje zyonti zyezyahafuniye hwa alume bhebhahali nimpepo.
MAT 8:34 Ikhaya yonti yahinza atangane nu Yesu. Lwe bhahanola u Yesu bhahamuzya aje ayepe mumpaha zyabho.
MAT 9:1 U Yesu ahinjila mwitoli, ahafwimila ahafiha hunsi ya hakhalaga.
MAT 9:2 Bhahanetela, umuntu ya polile ubili agonile pashitala. Lwahahulola ulwitiho lwabho u Yesu ahamuzya umuntu yapolile, “Mwanawi ushanje, ukhombhosheye imbibhi zyaho.”
MAT 9:3 Abhalimu bhamo abhilenga bhahayanjizanya bhibho hu bhibho, “Umuntu unu alinindigo”
MAT 9:4 U Yesu ahamanya insibho zyabho naje yeenu musibha imbibhi mumyoyo ginyu?
MAT 9:5 Henu hehinza aje ikhobhosheye, 'Imbibhi zyaho na aje, 'imililila ujende?'
MAT 9:6 Ishi mumanye aje wa Adamu alini nguvu izyahubhakhobhoshele imbibhi.” ahayanjile izi hwula yapolile, “Imilila, uyitwinshe igodoro lyaho ubhale hukhaya yaho”
MAT 9:7 Umuntu ula ahimilila nasogole abhale hukhaya yakwe.
MAT 9:8 Impuga ya bhantu lwe bhahalola igo, bhahaswijile na huntime u Ngulubhi, yabhapiye inguvu izyo abhantu.
MAT 9:9 U Yesu lwahashilaga afume ipo ahanola umuntu yahwitwa itawa Mathayo, yahakhiye pebhafumizya insoho. Wope ahabhabhuzya, “Munfuate ani” Wope ahimilila ahafwata.
MAT 9:10 U Yesu lwahakhiye alye ishalye munyumba, bhahinzi bhebhafumya insoho bhabhinji na bhantu abhimbibhi bhahaliye peka ishalye nu Yesu peka abhasunde bhakwe.
MAT 9:11 Afalisayo lwe bhahalola isho bhahabhabhuzya abhasende bhakwe, yeenu u Yesu alya ishalye na bhantu abhafumya insoho na bhantu abhimbibhi?”
MAT 9:12 U Yesu lwa ahivwa igo, wope ahayanga “Abhantu bhesebhabhinile sebhahwanza unganga, ila bhebhabhinile.
MAT 9:13 Ihwanziwa huje mubhale mumanyile imaana yakwe, “Insungwa irehema siga izabihu” Pipo senahinzile hubhantu abhimbibhi.
MAT 9:14 Abhasunde bha Yohana bhahinza hukwakwe na aje, “Yeenu ati na mafalisayo tifunga, lakini abhasunde bhaho sebhafunga?”
MAT 9:15 U Yesu ahabhabhuzya ahaga, Je abhalolezi bhi weji bhangaswimalwe bhali peka nu gosi wiweji? Lakini insiku zihwinza insiku ugosi wi weji ahayisogola pebhahayifunga.
MAT 9:16 Nuumo umuntu yabhiha ishipande shimwenda umpya humwenda uwimandi, ishulaka shibhadebushe afume humwenda na abazushe haani hubhafumile.
MAT 9:17 Nabhamo abhantu bhebhabhiha ihombwa mushombo ishihombwa inkuulu, nkushele bhabhomba, ingozi ibhadebushe ihambwa ibhafume na nanjishe. Badala yakwe, ubhiha ihombwa impya mungozi impya vyonti vibhabha salama.
MAT 9:18 U Yesu lwahabhabhuzya amambo iga, ahali, ugosi umo ahamwinamila mwilongolela lyakwe ahaga, “Unindu wani afwiye shinishi inza umponye abhapone abhabhe mwoomi.
MAT 9:19 U Yesu ahimilila na huusojelele na bhasunde bhakwe.
MAT 9:20 Ahali, ushi yahafumaga idanda amaha kumi na mbili ahasojelela pipi nu Yesu ahayikhata inkanzu ya Yesu.
MAT 9:21 Pipo ahayile, “Nkushele na bhukhata umweudo wa Yesu imbapone.”
MAT 9:22 U Yesu ahagaluhana na humwenye na humuuzye, “Ninda uyipele umwoyo, nu ulwitiho lwaho lubhombile aje upone,” Ahabhalilizyo hiniho unshi ula ahapona.
MAT 9:23 U Yesu lwahafiha hukhaya ya gosi, ahabhalola bhebhakhoma ifilimbi na impuga ya bhantu yahakhomaga ahalanga.
MAT 9:24 Wope ahaga, “Epi ipa, unindu saafwiye agonile. Lelo abheene bhahanseshile haani.
MAT 9:25 Abhantu bhala lwebha fuma hunzi, wope ahinjila huhati na hunkhate inyobhe unindu ahadamuna.
MAT 9:26 Inongwa zyahayeha insi yonti.
MAT 9:27 U Yesu lwahashilaga afume pala, abhalume bhabhili bhesebhahwenya amaso bhahausejelela. Bhahendeliye akhole bhahaga, “Tilabha utiponye, Mwana wa Daudi.”
MAT 9:28 U Yesu lwahafishile hukhaya, bhala bhesabhahwenya amaso bhahinza hukwake. U Yesu ahabhabhuzya, “Muhwitiha huje ingabhaponya?” Bhope bhahaga “Ena, Gosi”
MAT 9:29 U Yesu ahakhata amaso gabho naje zibhombeshe isho hulimwe ndeshe ulitiho lwinyu sheluhi”
MAT 9:30 Na amaso gabho gahanda ahwenye. Pe Yesu ahakhajilizya hunguvu na yanje “Mwenyaje umuntu wowonti asahamanye ijambo ili.”
MAT 9:31 Lelo abhantu bhabhili bhahasogoye alumbilile ahusu amambo iga isehemu zyonti izyinkhaya.
MAT 9:32 Pe pinipo abhalume bhala bhabhili lwe bhahasogolaga, ahali, umuntu umo aliyububu impepo zyahamwinjiye bhahaletwa hwa Yesu.
MAT 9:33 Impepo lwezyahamwepa umuntu ububu ahanda ayanje. Impuga yahaswiga naje setilolile nkalumo amambo iga gegafumiye mu Israeli.
MAT 9:34 Lelo afalisayo bhayangaga hwa gosi wi impepo ahugabhinga amapepo.”
MAT 9:35 U Yesu ahabhalile ikhaya zyonti ni vijiji vyonti. Ahendeliye amanyizye mumasinagogi, alumbilile izwi ilyibhumwene na ponye impungo zyonti nu bhuzaifu wonti.
MAT 9:36 Lwa ahenya impuga, ahabhaloleye inkumbu, pipo bhahayimbile navunzishe mumwoyo. Bhahali ndeshi ingole zyesazili nu udimi.
MAT 9:37 Wope ahabhabhuzya abhasunde bhakwe ahaga, “Amavuno minji, abhabhomba mbombo bhadodo.
MAT 9:38 Ishi lubhilo tinabhe ugosi wi mavuno, nke huje atume abhabhomba mbombo mugunda gwakwe.”
MAT 10:1 U Yesu abhakwizya abhanafunzi bhakwe kumi na bhabhele peka nahupele amamulaka juu yimpepo imbibhi, hubha khalipile na habhadigizye na ponyle iayina zyonti zimagonjwa ni ayina zi mpongo.
MAT 10:2 Amatawa kumi na gabhele gatumwa. Lyawhande u Simeoni (ambaye tena agiziwaga yu Petro), nu Andrea ukolo wakwe, u Yakobo umwana wa Zebedayo, nu Yohana ukolo wakwe:
MAT 10:3 U Philipo, nu Bartelemayo, Thomaso, nu Mathayo usonkolezya uwushuru, u Yakobo umwana wa Alfayo, nu Tadeo,
MAT 10:4 U Simoni mkananayo, nu Yuda Iskariote, walisaliti.
MAT 10:5 Ebha kumi na bhabhele u Yesu abha sontelezezye. Nape abhaelekezezye ayanjile “Msahabhale isehemu uhabhakhala amataifa na msahinjile mizikhaya zya Bhasamalia.
MAT 10:6 Badala yakwe, mubhale hungole zizitejile ziyumba yi Israeli.
MAT 10:7 Na lwamubhala lumbililaji na yanje uwumwene wa humwanya upalamiye.'
MAT 10:8 Bhaponylaji abhabhinu, zyosyaji abhafwe, safisyaji bhiukoma na digizye impepo. Mposheleye wene fumyaji wene.
MAT 10:9 Usaheje iwe lihela, ialmasi au ishaba mumpogoso zyenyu.
MAT 10:10 Usaheje imbugulu katika isafari yenyu, au amenda giziada, vilyato au endesa, afatanaje umombi ahanziwa ishalye shakwe.
MAT 10:11 Ikhaya yoyonti au ishijiji shamwayihijila, anzi wahubhafaa na mukhale epo hadi lwamwayisogola.
MAT 10:12 Lwamwayihinjila munyumba lamubhi,
MAT 10:13 nkesho inyumba ifaa, uwinza wenyu u syale epo, ila nkesho inyumba sigiifwa, uwinza wusogole peka namwe,
MAT 10:14 Na whabhala bhasaga bhahubhaposhela amwe au atejelezye amazu genyu, isala zyamusogola hunyumba au hukhaya eyo, jipukuti masuto gilwayo lwenyu pamahali epo.
MAT 10:15 Lyoli ihumbawozya, gayibha gajimbe hani amiji gi Sodoma ni Gomorah whisiku lilongwe kuliko umuji ago.
MAT 10:16 Enyi, ihubhatuma hansi ingole pakasi yimbwalonde, eshi bhanje nuwelewa hansi inzoha na bhapomakati hansi enjebha.
MAT 10:17 Mubhanje bhenyelezi na bhantu bhanza hubhatwale humabaraza, na hubhakhome muvibhanza.
MAT 10:18 Na mwayiletwa whilongolela lyabha gosi na bhamwene husabu yane, hansi usimisizyo humwawo na humataifa.
MAT 10:19 Hubala lwabhayituhumu, musahabhe niwasiwasi shinamunawele shayanje, afwatanaje ishintu shayanje mwayipewa husala eyo.
MAT 10:20 Afwatanaje sagamwemwe mwayiyanga, ila Upepo wa Baba wenyu ayiyanga muhanti yenyu.
MAT 10:21 Uholo ayihumwinushila uholo wakwe hugoje, baba whamwana wakwe. Abhana bhayiwhemelela dhidi ya pafi, na hubasababisizye ufwe.
MAT 10:22 Namwe mwanyivitilwa na kila muntu husabu yitawa lyane. Ila wowonti wayijimbilila hadi humwisho umuntu oyo ayiauliha.
MAT 10:23 Isala yabhahubhatesa katikaikhaya ene, shembelelaji ikhaya yifatila, lyoli ihabhawozya, zyonti zi Israeli kabla ya mwana wa Adamu sagawelile.
MAT 10:24 Umwanafunzi saga gosi ashile umwalimu wakwe, wala umutumwa walihumwanya ya Gosi wakwe.
MAT 10:25 Itosya wha mwanafunzi aje abhe hansi umwalimu wakwe, nu mutumishi hansi u Gosi wakwe. Nkesho bhan'kwizizye Ugosi winyumba Belzabuli, hushiasi wele hani bhanzahubha kashifu bhinyumba yakwe!
MAT 10:26 Esho basi musawogope abhene, afwatanaje hamuna ijambo lyasagalyayi kwinkuliwa, nalimo lilifishe lyasagalyaimanyiha.
MAT 10:27 Shila shihubhawozya muhisi, shiyangaji umuzelu na shamushevwa huulayini mumakutu genyu mshitangazye lwamuli pamwanya yinyumba.
MAT 10:28 Mubawogope bhala bhabhagogo obele ila sagabhalinuwuwezo wagoje umwoyo. Badala yakwe, mogopaji ola wawezya ahangamizye ubele nu moyo hula whilongo.
MAT 10:29 Eshi ikaziwa husenti indodo? Hata shesho enemo yiwezya agwe pansi bila ubaba wenyu amanye.
MAT 10:30 Ila hata iidadi yinsisi zyenyu zi bhaziwilwe.
MAT 10:31 Mugaje abhe niwoga, afwatanaje mlinithani hani kuliko ikasuku inyinji.
MAT 10:32 Esho basi kila weka wayihuneteha whilongolela lya bhantu, nane tena nayihumweteha whilongolela lya Baba wane walihumwanya.
MAT 10:33 Ila uwene wayihukhana whilongolela lya bhantu, nane tena nayihukhana whilongolela lya Baba wane walihumwanya.
MAT 10:34 Musasebhe aje enenzele alete uwinza panse. Saganahenzele aete uwinza, ila ipanga.
MAT 10:35 Afwatanaje nahenzele ahumehse umuntu ashindane nubaba wakwe, nu mwale dhidi ya maye wakwe, ukhoyi dhidi ya khoyi wakwe.
MAT 10:36 Umibhi wa muntu bhanzabhe bhabhala bha munyumba yakwe.
MAT 10:37 Uwene wagene ubaba au umaye hani kuliko ane oyo saga ahufhaa. Nu wene wagene ovwele au umwale hani kuliko ane oyo sagaahufhaa.
MAT 10:38 Uwene wasaga bhawhangate ikhobhehanyo na hufhate ane saga ahufhaa.
MAT 10:39 Uwene wayiwhanza ukhalo ayihugatezya. Ila uwene wayitezya ukhalo kwa ajili yane ayihwuwaga.
MAT 10:40 Uwene wayihubhakaribisya ankalibisizye nene, nu mwene wayihunkalibisya ane ankalibisizye iwene wantumile ane.
MAT 10:41 Nu mwene wayihunkalibisya ukuwe kwa sababu kuwe ayiposhela ithawabu ya kuwe. Nuwene wayihunkalibisya uwihaki kwa sababu muntu wihaki ayiposhela isawabu ya muntu wi haki.
MAT 10:42 Wowonti ayihupela weka wa dodo ebha, hata ishikombe shimenze gamwele gagakhateye, kwa sababu uwene yumwanafunzi, lyoli ihumbawozya, uwene sagayiwezya akose whidala lyolyonti ithawabu yakwe.”
MAT 11:1 Yabha baada ya Yesu amale hubhaelekezye abhanafunzi bhakwe kumi na bhabhele asogoye hu plae abhale amanyizye na lombelele katika ikhaya zyawo,
MAT 11:2 nu Yohana lwali mwigereza lwahevwezye lwalihumwanya yimbombo zya Klisiti, atumile uwujumbe abhilile abhanafunzi bhakwe,
MAT 11:3 na bhamozelezya, “Awe yoyola wawhenza au huliuwamwawo tiwhanziwa humwenyelezye?”
MAT 11:4 U Yesu ajibu na yanje humwawo “Bhaji mumozye u Yohana gala gamuhugalola na gala gamuhugevwa.
MAT 11:5 Abhantu bhasabhalola, bhapata alole, iviwete bhajenda, abhakoma bhatakasiha, abhantu bhasaga bhawhevwa bhahevwa tena, abhantu bhabhafwiye bhazyoswa apate uwomi, na abhantu bhabhanza bhalombelewa ihabari inyinza.
MAT 11:6 Na asayiwilwe ola wasagalola amashaka juu yane.
MAT 11:7 Humuda abhantu ebha lwabhasogola, u Yesu ahandile ayanje ni mpoga juu ya Yohana, “Mwabhulile awhenye iyenu whijangwa __itete liyinzanywa ninkongu?
MAT 11:8 Ila yenu mwabhalile awhenye__ umuntu wakwete amenda amalayini? Lyoli, bhala bhabhakwata amenda amalaini bhakhala munyumba zishimwene.
MAT 11:9 Ila mwasogoye alole iyenu- Ukuwe? Ee, ihumbwawozya ni zaidi ya Kuwe. Ono yuyo wasimbiwilwe, 'Enya, ihutuma ujumbe wane whilongolela yimaso gakwe, wayi andaa idala iyaho whilongolela lyaho.
MAT 11:11 Ane ihumbawozya ilyoli, kati ya bhapapwilwe na bhashe nomo waligosi kuliko u Yohana umozyaji. Ila walidodo katika umwene wa humwanya gosi ashile umwene.
MAT 11:12 Afume insiku zya Yohana umozyaji hadi isalezi, umwene wa humwanya wuli wengovo, na bhantu bhabhali bhengovo, bhahuwega hongovo.
MAT 11:13 Afwatanaje akuwe ni ndajizyo, bhakuwilwe hadi wha Yohana.
MAT 11:14 Na nkesho mulitayari awheteshe, ono yu Eliya, ola wawhenza.
MAT 11:15 Wali na makutu gawhevwe nayevwaje.
MAT 11:16 Endanganisye ni yenu ishi papo eshi? Shi fano shabhana bhabhawhanga mumaeneo gisoko, bhabhakhala na kwizanye
MAT 11:17 na yanje, 'Tabhakhomeye izomari na sagamwahanjile. Talilile na sagamwakholile.'
MAT 11:18 Afwataje u Yohana ahenzele bila alye amabumunda au amwele ihombwa, na bhabha bhayanga, 'Ali ni pepo.'
MAT 11:19 Umwana wa Adamu ahenzele alya na mwele na bhayanga 'Enya, muntu unylavi na ukholwe, rafiki wa sonkola uwushuru na bhimbibhi!' Ila injele iloleha humbombo zyakwe.”
MAT 11:20 U Yesu ahandile huyikhalipile ikhaya ambamo baadhi yimbombo zyakwe zimayele zyatendebhe, afwatanaje bhuli sagabhutubule,
MAT 11:21 Ahele waho, Kolazini, Ole waho Bethsaida! Nkesho imbombo ingosi gngwawombeshe hu Tiro na Husidoni gala gagawombeshe epa, andi bhatubule hale whakwate amagunila na hujipashe amalota.
MAT 11:22 Ila yayibha ujivwi hu Tiro ni Sidoni isiku lilongwi kuliko hulliwe.
MAT 11:23 Aise, Kapernaum, ubheshele wayiwosewa hadi humwanya? Ndadi wayiwhiswa hadi pansi whilongo. Hansi hu Sodoma hungawombeshe matendo amagosi, hansi gagawombeshe huliwe andiileho hadi ilelo.
MAT 11:24 Eshi iyanga huliwe aje yayibha vyepesi honse yi Sodoma awhemelele whisiku lilongwi kuliko awe.
MAT 11:25 Katika humuda ogo u Yesu ayanjile, “Ihutema awe, Baba, Gosi wahumwanya na panse, husababu wabhafisile amambo ega bhinjele vwelewa, na hugagubule whabhasaga bhali ni elimu, hansi abhana abhadodo.
MAT 11:26 Baba afwatanaje yasongozewelwe esho pamaso gaho.
MAT 11:27 Amambo gonti impewilwe ane afume wha Baba. Na nomo wamenye u Baba ila umwana, na wowonti ambaye umwana ali ni hamu ya hugubulile.
MAT 11:28 Enzi huline, amwe mwenti mumuyemba na wuwonelwa na mazigo amamwamu, nane imbahubhatozye.
MAT 11:29 Jiponyaji ijoko lyane na mumanyilaje afume huline, afwatanaje ane niwawhishe na mpole wimoyo na munza pate ulotoyo lwi nafsi zyenyu.
MAT 11:30 Afwatanaje ijoko lyane lilayini na izigo lyane lipoposu.
MAT 12:1 Umuda ogo u Yesu abhalile isiku litoyo ashilile humagonda. Abhanafunzi bhakwe bhali ni nzala na bhanda avunze amansale na hugalye.
MAT 12:2 Ila Amafarisayo lwabhalola ego, bhamozya u Yesu “Enya abhanafunzi bhaho bhavunza indajizyo bhawomba isiku zasagagaluhusiwilwe isiku lilutoyo.”
MAT 12:3 Ila u Yesu abhawozya, “Sagamubhazizye u Daudi shawombile, umuda lwali ni nzala, pamoja na bhantu bhalinawo?
MAT 12:4 Shahinjiye muhati yinyumba ya Ngulubhi nalye amabumunda gilulolesyo, ambago sagayahali halali hukwakwe alye nabhala bhalinawo, ila halali whadimi?
MAT 12:5 Bado saga mubhazizye katika indajizyo, aje katika isiku lilutuyo ndimi muhati yishibhanza bhahuyinanganya ilutoyo, ila sagabhali ni hatiya?
MAT 12:6 Ila iyanga humwenyu aje wali gosi kuliko ishibhanza aleho epa.
MAT 12:7 Nkesho mwamenya eli lijulisya iyenu; iwhanza irehema na saga insayo; andisagamwalonjile bhasaga bhali ni hatiya,
MAT 12:8 Afwatanaje Umwana wa Adamu ndiyo Gosi wilutoyo.”
MAT 12:9 Tena Uyesu asogola pala abhala hushibhanza shawo.
MAT 12:10 Enya whali nu mundu wapolile inyobhe. Amafarisayo bhamozelezya u Yesu, bhayanga. “Eshi, sawa aponyile isiku lilutoyo?” ili aje bhawezye hunshitaki wha wombe imbibhi.
MAT 12:11 U Yesu abhawozya, “Yunanu pakasi yenyu, wali ni ngole yeka, neyo ingole yagwa mhati yishimo isiku lilutoyo, sagabhahuyileme na huyefwe hongovo muhati yishimo?
MAT 12:12 Eshi, shipimo shishili shithamani, hani huje, saga hani yingole! Eshi shinza awombe aminza ibiku lilutoyo.”
MAT 12:13 Tena u Yesu amozya ola umuntu, “Nyosya inyobhe yaho” Ayinyosya napate uwinza hansi ela iyamwawo.
MAT 12:14 Ila Amafarisayo bhafuma honze bhapanga inamuna shahunteketezye bhabhalile honze apanje hushinyume shakwe. Bhawhanzaga inamuna yahugoje.
MAT 12:15 U Yesu lwahelewa elyo asogoye epo. Abhantu abhinji bhafwatile, na abhaponyila bhonti.
MAT 12:16 Abhalajizizye bhasahafanye afahamishe hubhamwawo,
MAT 12:17 aje ikamilishe ela ilyoli, yaya yangwilwe nukuwe u Isaya, ayanjile,
MAT 12:18 Enya, mombi wane wisaluye, ugonwe wane, katika uwene inafusi yane isongwezwe. Imbabhoshe umpepo wane humwanya yakwe, na abhatangazye ulongwe humataifa.
MAT 12:19 Sagaayihangayiha wala alile hungovo; wala waliwowonti awhevwe isauti yakwe mumitaani.
MAT 12:20 Sagaayihulibudala itete lilialushe, sagayizimanya uwutambi wowonti wuwufumya ilyosi, hadi lwayileta ulongwe lwamena.
MAT 12:21 Na Mataifa bhayibha udandamazu mwitawa lyakwe.
MAT 12:22 Umuntu omo ukipofu nu bubu, wachanganyishiwilwe ni pepo aletilwe whilongolela lya Yesu. Aponilwe, pamoja namatokewo gaje umuntu ububu ayanjile na lole.
MAT 12:23 Amakutano wonti bhaswijile na yanje, “Awezya umuntu ono abhe mwana wa Daudi?”
MAT 12:24 Ila umuda Amafarisayo lwabhahevwa amayele ega, bhayanjile, “Ono umuntu sagaafumya impepo hungovo zyakwe yuyo ila hongovo zya Belzebuli, ugosi wimpepo.
MAT 12:25 “Ila u Yesu lwamunya insewo zyawo na hubhawozye, “Kila umwene wuwugabhanyishe uwene wunanjiha, na kila ikhaya au inyumba yigabhanyiha yene sagayayihemelela.
MAT 12:26 Nkesho Usetano, abhahumwefwe Usetano, bhasi ahujikhana hunafsi yakwe mwene.
MAT 12:27 Ni namuna wele uwomwene wakwe ubhawhemelele? Na nkesho ifumya ipepo hongovo zya Belizabuli, abhafwasi bhenyu bhafumya whidala wele? Wheli bhayibha bhalonzanyi bhenyu.
MAT 12:28 Na nkesho bhafumya ipepo hongovo zya Mpepo wa Ngulubhe, eshi umwene wa Ngulubhi wenzele humwenyu.
MAT 12:29 Nu muntu abhawezye wele awhinjile muhati yinyumba yewe ngovo na whibhe, bila hupinye wengovo kwanza? Epo panzawhibhe intabhalo zyakwe afume muhati yinyumba.
MAT 12:30 Wowonti wasagaali pamoja nane ali shinyume shane, nape wasaga awonganya pamoja nane uyo asambazya.
MAT 12:31 Eshi iyanga humwenyu, kila imbibhi ni kufuru abhantu bhayisamehewa, ila ahukufuru Umpepo ufinjile sagabhayisamehewa.
MAT 12:32 Na wowonti wayanga izu shinyume cha Mwana wa Adamu, elyo ayisamehewa. Ila wowonti wayanga shinyume nu Mpepo ufinjile, oyo sagayisamehewa, honse ene na wala ela yiwhenza.
MAT 12:33 Au liwombe ikwi abhe linza nitunda lyakwe linza, au linanganye ikwi ni tunda lyakwe, afatanaje ikwi limanyiha whitunda lyakwe.
MAT 12:34 Amwe bhimpapo bhi nzoha, amwe mulibhabhibhi, muwezizye ayanje amambo aminza? Afatanaje ilomu liyanga afume mumbeho gagali mumoyo.
MAT 12:35 Umuntu umwinza humbeho inyinza yahumoyo gwakwe afumya inyinza, na umuntu umibhi humbeho imbibhi yimoyo gwakwe, afumya shishili shibhibhi.
MAT 12:36 Ihumbawozya whisiku li longwi abhantu bhayifumya ihesabu yikila izu lyasaga lili ni mana lyabhayanjile.
MAT 12:37 Afwatanaje humazu gaho ayibhaziwa ihaku na humazu gaho wayilongwa.”
MAT 12:38 Tena baadhi ya simbi na Mafarisayo bhajibule u Yesu bhayanjile “Mwalimu, tasongwezye alole iishara afume huliwe.”
MAT 12:39 Ila Uyesu ajibule na hubhawozye, “Ishipapo ishibhibhi na shiumulala shiwhanza iishara. Ila nemo iishara yifafumwe humwawo ila ela iishara ya Yona ukuwe.
MAT 12:40 Hansi shila u Yona shahali muhati yivyanda vinswe ingosi hunsiku zitatu shasenya na nusiku, esho shesho Umwana wa Adamu shanzabhe muhati gwimoyo gwense hunsiku zitatu shasenya na nu siku.
MAT 12:41 Abhantu bhi Ninawi bhayihemelela whilongolela pamoja nishipapo sha bhantu ebha na bhayihushilonga. Afwatanaje walitubu humalombelelo ga Yona, na enya, umuntu omwugosi wizaidi ya Yona aleho epa.
MAT 12:42 Umalikiya wahukusini aiwhemelela hulongwe peka na bhantu bhishi papo eshi nahushilonje. Ahenzele afume humwisho wense ahenze atejelezye injele ya Selemani, na enya, umuntu omo ugosi ashile u Selemani aleho epa.
MAT 12:43 Umuda ipepo ibhibhi lwalihufuma umuntu, lishilila isehemu yasagaili na menze liwhanza patoye, ila sagilihupalola.
MAT 12:44 Tena ayanga, 'Imbawele hunyumba yane yinfumile.' Lwawela ahuyaga ela inyumba ifanyiwilwe uwusafi na ili tayali.
MAT 12:45 Tena abhala na hubhalete abhanje impepo imbibhi saba zizilimbibhi hani ashile iyene, bhahenza akhale wonti pala. Ni hali yakwe ya humwisho ibha mbibhi azidi iyawhande. Esho shasho shayayibha hushipapo eshi ishibhibhi.
MAT 12:46 Umuda Uyesu lwazyongolaga ne mpoga enya, umaye wakwe na holo bhakwe bhahemeleye honze, bhahanzaga ayanje nawo.
MAT 12:47 Umuntu weka amozya, “Enya umaye waho na aholo bhaho bhemeleye honze, bhawhanza ayanje nawe”.
MAT 12:48 Ila u Yesu ajibule na hubhawozye wamozezye, “Umaye wane yu nanu? Na aholobhane bhananu?”
MAT 12:49 Nape anyosizye inyobhe yakwe whabhanafunzi na yanje, “Enya, ebha bhamaye naholo bhane!
MAT 12:50 Afwatanaje wowonti wawomba amagano ga Baba wane wali humwanya, umuntu oyo ndiyo holo wane, uyilombo wane numaye wane.”
MAT 13:1 Whisiku lila u Yesu asogoye munyumba na khale hunshenje yibahavi.
MAT 13:2 Empoga ingosi yiwongene whahu zyongole, ahinjiye mkasi yitoli nakhale mhati yakwe. Empoga yonti yahemeleye hunshenje yibahari.
MAT 13:3 Tena u Yesu ayanjile amazu aminji hushifwani, ayanjile, “Enya, utote abhalile atote.
MAT 13:4 Lwatotaga baadhi yimbeyu zyagwiye hunshenje yidala ni nyonyi zyahenzele zyajobile.
MAT 13:5 Imbeyu izyamwawo zyagwiye pamwanya yipakhome, ambazyo saga zyapatile ilongo lyakwelane. Gafla zyamelile afwatanaje ilongo sagalya li nishimo.
MAT 13:6 Tena isenya lwalyatukula zyapembwilwe kwa sababu sagazuali namazi zyahoma.
MAT 13:7 Imbeyu izyamwawo zyagwiye muhati yimakwi gimivwa. Amakwi gimivwa gatalimpine humwanya gaziziba.
MAT 13:8 Imbeyu izyamwawo zyagwiye mwilongo ilinza na pape imbeyu, zimo mara mia moja hani, zimo sitini ni zyamwawo thelasini.
MAT 13:9 Wali namakutu ayevwaje.
MAT 13:10 Abhanafunzi bhahenzele nahumozye u Yesu, “Yenu uyanga numukutano hushifwani?”
MAT 13:11 U Yesu abhajibu abhawozya, “Mupewilwe uganilizi wa manye isiri ziumwene wahumwanya, ila humwao sagabhapewilwe.
MAT 13:12 Ila wowonti walinasho, whamwene anzahonjezewe hani, na ayipata ifaida ingosi. Ila wasagaalinasho hata shila shali nasho ayifyolwa.
MAT 13:13 Esho alihizya anawo hushifwani husababu hata bhalola, sagabhalola lyoli. Na hata bhahevwa sagabhahevwa wala ahelewe.
MAT 13:14 Ukwe wa Isaya wutimiye humwawo, wula wuwuyanga, “Iwamuhevwa sagamuhevwa, ila hunamuna yoyonti ela sagamumanya.
MAT 13:15 Na moyo gabhantu ebha galihisi, shikhome ahevwe, na bhagubishe amaso gawo, ili bhasawezye alole humaso gawo, au ahovwe humakutu gawo, au amanye humoyo gawo, esho bhangewushilaga tena, nenzagahubhaponyle.'
MAT 13:16 Ila amambo genyu gasayiwilwe, afwatanaje galola, namakutu genyu afwatanaje gawhevwa.
MAT 13:17 Lyoli iwhumbawozya akuwe abhinji na bhantu bhihaki bhali ni hamu yalole amambo gala gamuhu galola, sagabhawezizye hugalole. Bhasongwelwe awhevwe amambo gula gamuhugevwa, sagabhagevwelwe.
MAT 13:18 Eshi tejelezi umufano gwatote.
MAT 13:19 Isala yeyonti lwahevwa izu liumwene na asalyelewe, epo umibhi awhenza nahushifwampe shishi malishe atotwe muhati yimoyo gwakwe. Ene mbeyu ela yitotilwe hunshenje yidala.
MAT 13:20 Uwene watolile mukhome yoyola ahulyevwa izu na huliposhele whadigane hulusongo.
MAT 13:21 Bado sagaalinamazi muhati yakwe, ila ajimbilila humuda ufupi uwakati amashida au mayemba lwagafumila kwa sababu yizu abomela gafla.
MAT 13:22 Watotile mhati yimivwa, ono yoyola wahevwa izu ila amatatizo gense nu gobezi wi utabhazi guhulifuniha lila izu lisahapape amatunda.
MAT 13:23 Watotilwe mwilongo ilinza, ono yoyola wahulyevwa izu na hulyelewe ono yoyola wapapa amatunda na whendelele apape lyeka hani yimala mia, ilyamwowo sitini, iyamwawo thelathini.”
MAT 13:24 U Yesu abhapiye usifwani ishamwawo. Ayanga, “Umwene wa humwanya ulenganiswa nu muntu watotile imbeyu inyinza mugonda gwakwe.
MAT 13:25 Ila abhantu lwabhasinzila, umibhi wakwe ayenza nape atota amagogo mhati yingano tena abhala mweene.
MAT 13:26 Pamande ingano lwayamela na fumye amazawo gakwe, nape amagogo gajitokezyezye.
MAT 13:27 Na awombi bhamwenesho gonda bhahenza bhamozya, 'Gosi, sagawatotile imbeyu inyinza mogonda gwaho? Iliwele eshi lili namagogo?
MAT 13:28 Abhawozya, umibhi awombile eli.' Awombi bhamozezye, “Eshi uwhanzaje tibhale tigasenye?”
MAT 13:29 We gonda ayanjile, 'Ndadi, umuda gwamusenya amagogo munzasenye pamo ni ngano.
MAT 13:30 Galeshi gakule pamo hadi umuda gwa vune. Isala zimavuno nayiyanga whavunaji, 'Kwanza senyi amagogo nagapinyi mpoga mpoga nahugapembe, ila kusanyi ingano mwighala lyane.”
MAT 13:31 Tena u Yesu abhafumizizye ishifani ishawawo. Ayanga, uwumwene wa humwanya ulengene ni mbeyu yiharadali ambayo umuntu ahejile na huyitote mogonda gwakwe.
MAT 13:32 Imbeyu ene huwuhakika ndodo ashile imbeyu izyamwawo zyonti. Ila nkayamela ibha ngosi ashile amakwi gonti gamubustani, libha likwi, ikiasi aje inyonyi zya humwanya ziwhenza na zenje vitenjeli mmatawi gakwe.”
MAT 13:33 Abhawozya ishifani ishamwawo tena, “Uwumwene wahumwanya hansi usafu wula yiyegwiwilwe noshe nahuyisanganye huvipimilo vitatu huwusu hadi vitute.
MAT 13:34 Ego gonti u Yesu gayanjile whempoga yabhantu hushifwani. Na nila shifwani sagayanjile shoshonti humwawo.
MAT 13:35 Eli lyali aje shila shashamalishe ayangwe ashilile akuwe shiwezye atimile, pala payangaga, “Nayiwhasama ilomu lyane hushifwani. Nayiyanga amambo gala gagaleho gafisiwilwe afume umusingi gwense.”
MAT 13:36 Tena u Yesu abhaleshile amakutano na bhale kukhaya. Abhanafunzi bhakwe bhamaliye nayanje, “Tifafabulile ishifani shimagogo gahugonda.”
MAT 13:37 U Yesu ajibu nayanje, “Watolile imbeyu inyinza yumwana wa Adamu.
MAT 13:38 Ugonda anse; ni mbeyu inyinza, ebha bhana bhiemwene. Amagogo bhana bhola umibhi, numibhi wazitotile yusetano.
MAT 13:39 Na mavuno mwisho wense, na wavunaji yuntumi.
MAT 13:40 Hansi shila amagogo shagakusanywa na pembwe mmoto, asho shesho shayayibha pamwisho wense.
MAT 13:41 Umwana wa Adamu ayihusontelezya untumi wakwe, na wonganye afume umwene wakwe amambo gonti gagasababisizye imbibhi na bhala bhabha womba imbibhi.
MAT 13:42 Bhayihubhataga wonti mwitanulu li moto, ambaho whayibha iholo nasye amino.
MAT 13:43 Epo abhantu bhi haki lwabha yizelupa hansi isenya mwiwumwene wa Baba wawo. Umwene wali namakutu na ayevwaje.
MAT 13:44 Umwene wahumwanya ulihansi ihazina yifisiwilwe mugonda. Umuntu ayilola nahuyifise. Katika ulusongo lwakwe abhala akazye vyonti vyalinavyo nakale ogonda.
MAT 13:45 Tena, uwumwene wa humwanya uli hansi umuntu wawomba ibiashara ahanza ilulu yi thamani.
MAT 13:46 Umuda gwayilola ela yi thamani, abhala akazya kila hantu shali nasho na huyikale.
MAT 13:47 Uwomwene wa humwanya ulihansi ulwego wauli muhati yibahari, naluwonganya iviwumbe vinamuna yonti.
MAT 13:48 Lwalwamema ulwego bhaluvutiye pamwanya. Tena bhakhala pansi bhawonganya ivintu ivinza muhati yivyombo, ila vyasaga vili ni thamani vyatagwilwe uhutali.
MAT 13:49 Yayibha inamuna ene humwisho wense. Antumi bhayihenza nahubhatenje abhantu abhabhibhi afume mu myongoni mubhihaki.
MAT 13:50 Na tagwe muhati yitanuli limoto, uho whayibha akhole nasye amino.
MAT 13:51 Mumenye amambo gonti ega? Bhanafunzi bhajibule, “Ee.”
MAT 13:52 Tena u Yesu abhawozya, “Kila simbi wali mwanafunzi wiwumwene alengene numwenebho nyumba wafumya muhazina yakwe ivintu ivipya nivihale.”
MAT 13:53 Baada ya Yesu lwamala amifano gonti ego, asogola isehemu eyo.
MAT 13:54 Tena u Yesu afiha humukowa gwakwe nahubhafundizye abhantu mwishibhanza. Amatokeo gajwe bhaswijile nayanje, “Hoshi umuntu ono whapatile injele ene na mayele ega?
MAT 13:55 Umuntu ono saga mwana wa Seremala? Umariamu saga mayewakwe? Na aholo bhakwe saga yu Yakobo, Yusufu, Simoni nu Yuda?
MAT 13:56 Na ayilombo bhakwe filinabho penepa pamwetu? Eshi umuntu ono agaje whi ega gonti?”.
MAT 13:57 Abhavisizye, ila u Yesu abhawozezye, “Ukuwe sagakosa abhe ninshinshi ila humwawo na honse yawo.
MAT 13:58 Na sagawezizye awombe amayele aminji kwa sababu sagabhali nolweteho anawo.
MAT 14:1 Husala ezyo, Uherode ahevwezye ihabari ya Yesu.
MAT 14:2 Abhawozya ahoyi bhakwe, “Ono yu Yohana Umozyaji azyoshele afume whazimu. Eshi engovo ezyo zili hukwakwe.”
MAT 14:3 Afwatanaje u Herode ali anemile u Yohana apinya na hutaje mwijela husababu ya Herodia, oshe wa Filipo okolo wakwe.
MAT 14:4 Afwatanaje u Yohana amozezye, “Sagashinza ahumweje umwene abhe shee wakwe.”
MAT 14:5 U Herode andiagojile ila ahogope abhantu husababu bhanolile u Yohana aje kuwe.
MAT 14:6 Ila isala ninsiku zya papwe u Herode lwazyafiha umwale wa Herode ahanjile pakasi ya bhantu nahasongwezye u Herode.
MAT 14:7 Katika ajibu shila shasobhe zezye hundapo aje anzahupele shoshonti shanzalabhe.
MAT 14:8 Baada yashauliwe nu maye wakwe, ayanjile, “Mpele ane epa pikombe itwe lya Yohana Umozi.”
MAT 14:9 Umwene ali na masikitiho humalawo gamwale, ila kwa ajili yindapo zyakwe, afwatanaje wonti bhabhaleho pashalye pamo numwene ayanjile aje lifanyishe.
MAT 14:10 Atumile u Yohana aletwe afume whigeleza,
MAT 14:11 ili atemwe itwe lyakwe na litemwe pamwanya yisinia na apewe umwale na alitwale whamaye wakwe.
MAT 14:12 Tena abhanafunzi bhakwe bhenza awheje gula ombele na syele, baada yeli bhabhalile humozye u Yesu.
MAT 14:13 Nape Uyesu lwahevwa ega, ajitenga afume isehemu ela azubha mukasi yimashua abhala esehemu yijitenjile. Umuda empoga lwayanya whali, bhafwatile lwimanama afume humijini.
MAT 14:14 Tena u Yesu ahenzele whilongolela lyawo alola empoga ingosi. Abhalolela enkombo na hubhaponyle impongo zyawo.
MAT 14:15 Ishalyabhela yakamiliha, abhanafunzi bhahenza hukwakwe na yanje, “Ene sehemu yijangwa ni siku tayari lishilile. Bhatabhanye amakutano ili bhabhale muvijiji ni bhakale ishalye kwa ajili yawo.
MAT 14:16 Ila Yesu ayanjile, “Sagabhali ni haja yabhalebhewo. Bhapeli amwe ishalye”
MAT 14:17 Bhamozya, “Epa tilinago amabumunda gasanu neswe zebhele tu.”'
MAT 14:18 U Yesu ayanga, “Galeti huline.”
MAT 14:19 Tena u Yesu ayiwozya empoga akhale pansi yimasole. Ayega amabumunda gasanu neswe zebhele. Ayenya humwanya, asaya nabudulanye amabumunda abhapela abhanafunzi. Abhanafunzi bhayipela empoga.
MAT 14:20 Bhalya wonti bhihuta. Tena bhavikusanya ivipande vyonti vishalye nameme iviseje kumi navibhele.
MAT 14:21 Bhala bhabhaliye bhabhakadiliya aje abhalume elfu zisanu bila yabhazye abhashe na bhana.
MAT 14:22 Mara heka abhawozya abhanafunzi bhinjile mukasi yimashuwa, isala ezyo umwene abhalaga empoga bhabhaje bhewo.
MAT 14:23 Lwabhalaga empoga bhabhala bhene, azubha pamwanya yigamba apute mwene. Isala lwayali yilyabhela alihoho mwene.
MAT 14:24 Ila eshi imashua lwayali pahati yibahari yayumbaga husababu yimawimbi kwani inkongu yali yimpisho.
MAT 14:25 Katika uusiku wi zamu ya nne u Yesu abhasojeleye ajenda pamwanya yemenze.
MAT 14:26 Isala abhanafunzi bhakwe lwabhanola ajenda pamwanya yi bahari, bhahogope nayanje, “Yuzimu ka,” na zuvye isauti katika ihali yiwoga.
MAT 14:27 U Yesu abhawozya heka, ayanga, “Jipelaji umoyo! Nene! mugajihogope.”
MAT 14:28 U Petro anjibu whayanje, “Gosi, nkesho wewe, mbozye enenze huliwe pamwanya yimenze.”
MAT 14:29 U Yesu ayanga, “Enza.” Esho Upetro afuma mukasi yimashua na ajenda pamwanya yimenze abhale wha Yesu.
MAT 14:30 Ila u Petro lwalola amawimbi, ahogope, na whande adwine, pansi, akwizya husauti nayanje, “Gosi, nokole!”
MAT 14:31 Digana Yesu anyosya inyobhe yakwe amosya u Petro, na humozye, “Awe wilweteho udodo, yenu ulinamashaka?”
MAT 14:32 Epo u Yesu nu Petro bhahinjiye mumashua, inkongu yaleshile avugule.
MAT 14:33 Abhanafunzi mmashua bhansayile u Yesu na yanje, “Lyoli awe wamwana wa Ngolobhi.”
MAT 14:34 Na lwabhafwemela, bhafishile panse yi Genesareti.
MAT 14:35 Na bhantu bhi sehemu ela lwabhamanya u Yesu, bhatumile uujumbe kila sehemu zipembeni nahunete kila wabhinile.
MAT 14:36 Bhamozezye aje bhawezye aguse ikunjo limwenda gwakwe, na bhinji bhabhagubile bhaponilwe.
MAT 15:1 Na Amafarisayo na asimbi bhahenzele wha Yesu afume Huyerusalemu. Na yanje,
MAT 15:2 “Yenu abhanafunzi bhananganya amalisizi gazehe? Afwatanaje sagabhanawa inyobhe zyawo lwabhalya ishalye.”
MAT 15:3 U Yesu abhajibu nahubhawozya, “Namwe__ yenu munanganya indajizyo ya Gosi kwa ajili yamalisizi genyu?
MAT 15:4 Afwatanaje o Ngolobhi ayanjile, 'Ubheninshinshi wha baba waho nu maye waho; na 'Wayanga imbibhi wha baba wakwe na whamaye wakwe, na hakika afwe.'
MAT 15:5 Ila amwe muyanga, na wahumozya ubaba wakwe nu maye wakwe, “Kila ulwavwe ambalo andapatile afume huline eshe mpesya afume wha Ngolobhi,”
MAT 15:6 “Umuntu oyo sagaalinihaja yabheninshinshi wha baba wakwe. Katika inamuna ene mubadilisizye izulya Ngolobhi kwa ajili yimalisizi genyu.
MAT 15:7 Amwe bhanafiki, shinza hansi u Isaya shakuwilwe pamwanya yenyu shayanjile,
MAT 15:8 'Abhantu ebha bhahwfpanyila inshinshi ane humalomu gawo, ila amioyo gawo galihutali nane.
MAT 15:9 Bhahunsaya wene, kwa sababu bhafundizya amamanyizyo agali malajizyo gabhanadamu.”
MAT 15:10 Epo abhakwizizye ikusanyiho na hubhawozye, “Tejelezi na mumanye__
MAT 15:11 Nahamo ahantu hahahinjila mwilomu lya muntu nahumombe ubhibhi. Ila, shila shishifuma mwilomu eshi shesho shimomba umuntu abhe mibhi.”
MAT 15:12 Epo abhanafunzi bhamalila nayanje nu Yesu, “Eshi!, Uwhele Amafarisayo lwabhalyevwa lila izu bhavisiwilwe?”
MAT 15:13 U Yesu abhajibu na yanje, “Kila likwi lwasagatotile ubaba wane wahumwanya lyayisenywa.
MAT 15:14 Bhaleshi bhene, abhene bhalongozi bhivipofu. Hansi umuntu shipofu abhahunongozye ushipofu uwamwawo, wonti bhabhele bhanzagwe mwilende.”
MAT 15:15 Upetro ajibu na humozye u Yesu, “Tiwozye umfano ogu hulite,
MAT 15:16 U Yesu ajibu, “Namwe bado sagamuhelewa?
MAT 15:17 Namwe sagamuwhenya aje shila shishi bhala mwilomu shishilila muvyanda na bhale muchoho?
MAT 15:18 Ila ivintu vyonti vivifuma mwilomu vifuma mhati yimoyo. Shesho ivintu vihumeha umuntu ubhibhi.
MAT 15:19 Afwatanaje katika umoyo gafuma amawazo amabhibhi, ugoji, uumalaya, uashelati, uwibha, uashuda wilenga ni ndigo.
MAT 15:20 Ega gamambo gahumeha umuntu ubhibhi. Ila alye bila anawe inyobhe sagahuumomba umuntu abhe mibhi.”
MAT 15:21 Epo u Yesu ayepa isehemu ela nahujisegusye aeleshela uhupande wi miji gi Tiro ni Sidoni.
MAT 15:22 Enya ayenza onshe Umkanani afume uwupande owo. Azuvya isauti ayanga, “Ndolele inkombo, Gosi, Mwana wa Daudi; umwale wane ayemba hani ni mpepo.”
MAT 15:23 Ila u Yesu sagaajibule izu. Abhanafunzi bhakwe bhenza bhanabha bhayanga, “Mwefwe abhaje ulwakwe, maana ahutikhomela ihalanga.”
MAT 15:24 U Yesu abhajibule nayanje, Saganatumwile wha muntu wowonti ila whingole zizitejile zinyumba yi Israeli.”
MAT 15:25 Ila ahenzele na whiname whilongolela lyakwe, ayanga, “Gosi navwe.”
MAT 15:26 Ajibule na yanje, “Sagashinza awheje ishalye shabhana na huzitajile embwa.”
MAT 15:27 Ayanga, “Eshi, Gosi, hata esho embwa indodo zilya ishalye shishigwa pameza pa Gosi wawo.”
MAT 15:28 Epo u Yesu ajibu na yanje “Anshe, ulweteho lwaho gosi.” Na ifanyishe huliwe hansi shuwhanza.” Nu mwale wakwe ali aponile husala yeyo.
MAT 15:29 U Yesu asogoye isehemu ela nabhale karibu ni bahari yi Galilaya. Tena abhala humwanya yigamba na khale oho.
MAT 15:30 Empoga ingosi yahenza hukwakwe. Na hunetele bhasaga bhajenda avipofu, abubu, bhishilema na bhanje vinji, bhabhali bhabhinile. Bhabhabheshele pamanama ga Yesu abhaponyla.
MAT 15:31 Na bhene empoga bhaswijile lwabhalolile amabubu bhayanga, ni vilema bhabhewha womi, aviwete bhajenda, nivipofu bhalola. Bhatemele Ongolobhi wi Israeli.
MAT 15:32 U Yesu abhakwizizye abhanafunzi bhakwe nayanje, “Imbaloleye inkombo impoga, husababu bhali nane hinsiku zitatu bila alye ahantu hohonti, sigimbahubhalaje bhabhale humwawo bila alye, bhasa hazimile mwidala.”
MAT 15:33 Abhanafunzi bhakwe bhamozya, “Tibhawezye apate amabumunda gatosye epa pinyiha awhigutizye empoga ingosi eshi?”
MAT 15:34 U Yesu abhawozya, “Muli na mabumunda galenga?” Bhayanga, “Saba, neswe indodo ndodo.”
MAT 15:35 U Yesu ayiwozya empoga ikhale pansi.
MAT 15:36 Ahejile gala amabumunda saba neswe, na baada ya husalifwe, agamensula na hubhapele abhanafunzi. Abhanafunzi bhabhapela empoga.
MAT 15:37 Abhantu bhonti bhalya natosewe. Bwawonganya gagasyalile ivipande vivyalye vya vyasageye vipande vipande, vyamemile iviseje saba.
MAT 15:38 Wonti bhabhaliye bhali alume elfu zene bila abhashe na bhana.
MAT 15:39 Tena u Yesu alaga empoga bhabha bhewo na ayinjila mkasi yi mashua na bhale isehemu zi Magadani.
MAT 16:1 Amafalisayo na Masadukayo bhamwenzeye na hunenje u Yesu abhalolesye iishara yifuma humwanya.
MAT 16:2 Ila u Yesu abhajibule na hubhawozye aje “Nkayabha lyabhela muyanga aje ihali yihewa nyinza, afwatanaje ianga lishamamu.
MAT 16:3 Ni shapwi muyanga ihali yihewa yilelo saganyinza afwatanaje ianga lishamamu na mabhengo galigubishe ianga lyonti, mumenye afasiri uloleho wianga, ila sagamuwezya afasiri iishara zimusala.
MAT 16:4 Ishizazi ishibhibhi nishi umalaya shiwhanza iishara ila nemo ishara yoyonti shashaipewa, ila ela ya Yona. Na tena u Yesu abhaleha nasogole ulwakwe.
MAT 16:5 Abhanafunzi bhenza uwupande wabhele, ila bhahewelwe aheje amabumunda.
MAT 16:6 U Yesu abhawozya “Shebhaji na mubhanje shinza nusafwe Wimafarisayo na Masadukayo.”
MAT 16:7 Abhanafunzi bhayangana mwikundi lyawo na yanje. “Afwatanaje saga tahejile amabumunda.”
MAT 16:8 U Yesu alimanya elyo nayanje, “Amwe mwelweteho udodo, yenu msebhele nayangane mkati yenyu nayanje aje kwasababu sagatahejile amabumunda?
MAT 16:9 Eshi bado sagamutambula wala saga mukomboha gala amabumunda gasanu hubhantu elfu zisanu nivitondo vilenga vyamwa wonganyenye?
MAT 16:10 Au amabumunda saba huabhantu elfu zene ni vitondo vielenga mwawonganyenye?
MAT 16:11 Iliwele hata sagamuhelewa yabhe nalisigiyanganamwe pamwanya yimabumunda? Jitunzaji na shebhaji nu safwe Wimafarisayo na Masadukayo.”
MAT 16:12 Tena bhamanya aje alisagayanga pamwanya yashebhe na mabumunda gagali nu safu ila ashebhe amamanyizyo gi Mafarisayo na Masadukayo.
MAT 16:13 Isala u Yesu lwafishile sehemu zi Kaisaria yi Filipi, abhawozelezya abhanafunzi bhakwe, ayanga, “Abhantu bhayanga umwana wa muntu yu nanu?”
MAT 16:14 Bhayanga, “bhamo bhayanga aje yu Yohana Umozi; bhamo, yu Eliya; na bhamo, yu Yeremia, au wiweka na kuwa.
MAT 16:15 Abhawozya, amwe muyiga ane ni nanu?
MAT 16:16 Ajibu, Usimoni Petro ayanga, “Awe wa Klisiti wamwana wa Ngulubhi wali momi.”
MAT 16:17 U Yesu ajibu na humozye, “Usayiwilwe awe, Simoni Bar Yona, afwatanaji idanda ni nyama sagavyafunuliye eli, ila Ubaba wane wali humwanya.
MAT 16:18 Nane tena ihuwozya aje awe wa Petro, na pamwanya yikhome ogu nayihulizenga ishi bhanza shane. Amalyango gawhilongo sagagayi hulishinda.
MAT 16:19 Nayihupela awe infwungulo zi umwene wahumwanya. Shoshonti shawayishigalila panse shayibhashi galililwe humwanya, na shoshonti shawayihungula panse shayibha shuguliwilwe humwanya.”
MAT 16:20 Tena u Yesu abhawozya abhanafunzi bhasamozye umuntu wowonti aje umwene ali yu Klisiti.
MAT 16:21 Afume isala ezyo u Yesu ahandile hubhawozye abhanafunzi aje lazima abhale Huyerusalemu, ayembe humambo aminji hunyobhe zya zehe na abhagosi bhadimi na simbizi, agoywe na zyoshe isiku lya tatu.
MAT 16:22 Tena u Petro amwega u Yesu hunshenje, nahukhalipile whayanje, “Ijambo eli nalibhe hutali nawe, ugosi, eli lisatokele huliwe.
MAT 16:23 Ila u Yesu agewushe na humozye u Petro, “Wela whisalo lgane setano! awe ulishipingimizi huline, kwasabu sugusaga amambo ga Ngolobhi, ila amambo gabhanadamu.”
MAT 16:24 Tena u Yesu abhawozya abhanafunzi bhakwe, “Nkesho umuntu wowonti nkawanza hufwate ane, lazima ajikhane umene mwene, ayeje ikhobhehanyo lyakwe, na afwate.
MAT 16:25 Afwatanaje wawhanza agokole amakhalo gakwe ayihugatezya, na whawowonti wahugatezya amakhalo gakwe kwa ajili yane ayihugokola.
MAT 16:26 Eshi! Faida wele yayi huyipata umuntu nkapata ense yonti ila atezya amakhalo gakwe? Je! Ni kitu gani atakachotoa mtu katika kubadilishana na maisha yake?
MAT 16:27 Alenganaje umwana wa Adamu ayinza katika utuntumu wa Baba wakwe. Nape ayihunipa kila mutnu alengane ni mbombo yakwe.
MAT 16:28 Lyoli imbawozya huli baadhi yenyu mu mweleye epa ambao sagabhayilenga ufwe hadi lwabhayihunola umwana wa Adamu lwayihenza katika umwene wakwe.
MAT 17:1 Insiku sita pamande u Yesu abhajile wonti nu Petro, nu Yakobo, nu Yohana uholo wakwe, na abhega hadi humwanya yigamba itali bhewo bhene.
MAT 17:2 Ageusiwa whilongolela lyawo isola yakwe yan'gaa hansi isenya, na menda gakwe yaloleshe gagang'aa hansi umwanga.
MAT 17:3 Enya, pala bhaloleshe u Musa nu Eliya bhayanga nawo.
MAT 17:4 U Petro ajibule na humozye u Yesu, “Gosi, shinza hulite abhe penepa. Nkesho unyonywa, imbazenje ivyegu vitatu sheka shaho, na sheka kwa ajili ya Musa, na sheka kwa ajili ya Eliya.”
MAT 17:5 Isala yayangaga, enya ibhengo izelu lyabhabheha inzunda, na enya, yafumile isauti afume humabhengo, iyanga, “Oyo mwanawane uganwe wiganwa nawo. Mwivwi umwene.”
MAT 17:6 Abhanafunzi lwabhahevwa ego, bhagwiye shigubama na bhahogope hani.
MAT 17:7 Tena u Yesu ahenza na hubhaguse na yanje, “Woshi wala mugaje ahogope.”
MAT 17:8 Nape bhahinuye isola zyawo humwanya ila sagabhanolile umuntu ila u Yesu mwene.
MAT 17:9 Na lwabhahihaga mwigamba, u Yesu abhalajizya, ayanga, “Musahafumye infumi zimaono ega hadi umwana wa Adamu lwaizyoha afume whazimu.”
MAT 17:10 Abhanafunzi bhakwe bhamozelezya, bhayanga, “Yenu asimbi bhayanga aje u Eliya ayihenza kwanza?
MAT 17:11 U Yesu abhajibu na yanje, “U Eliya ayihenza lyoli na wezye amambo ganti.
MAT 17:12 Ila ihumbawozya amwe, u Eliya ayenzele tayali ila sagabhamenye. Badala yakwe, bhamombeye amambo gabhawhanza abhene. Nesho shesho umwana wa Adamu shanzayembwe katika inyobhe zyawo.”
MAT 17:13 Epo abhanafunzi bhagundula aje ayanga habari zya Yohana umozi.
MAT 17:14 Lwabhafiha pakasi yempoga ya bhantu, umunt weka amaliye, akhama amafugamo whilongolela lyakwe, na humozye,
MAT 17:15 “Gosi, ukhowoshele umwana wane, kwa sababu aliningwa nayembe hani. Afwatanaje hahinji agwa mmoto au mmenze.
MAT 17:16 Inetile wha bhanafunzi bhaho, ila sagabhawe/i/ye huponye.
MAT 17:17 U Yesu ajibu ayanga, “Amwe ishizazi shasagashiwheteha na shishinanjishe naikhula pamo namwa hadi ndii? Imbajivwanye namwe hadi ndii? Neti epa huline.”
MAT 17:18 U Yesu akhalipiye, na impepo yafumile. Usahala aponwa afume isala yeyela.
MAT 17:19 Tena abhanafunzi bhamaliye u Yesu hu siri na humozelezye, “Yenu sagatawezizye uhudigizye?”
MAT 17:20 U Yesu abhawozya, “Kwa sababu ulweteho lwenyu dodo. Lyoli ihumbawozya, nkesho munzabhe nulweteho hata udodo hansi ipunje yimbeyu yiharadali mubhawezye huliwozye igamba eli, sama afume epa, ubhale hula, nape libhasame na saguhabhabhe na hantu hohonti haha bhashindihane humwenyu.
MAT 17:21 (Simisizya: Amazu gimusitari wi 21 “Ila, iayina ene yimpepo sigiwezehana afume, ila hunsayo na galile” Sagagaloleha humasamizyo aminza gihale).
MAT 17:22 Isala zyabhali bado Hugalilaya, u Yesu abhawozya abhanafunzi bhakwe, “Umwana wa Adamu abhabheshwe munyobhe zya bhantu.
MAT 17:23 Na bhanzahugoje, ni siku lya tatu ayizyoha.” Abhanafunzi bhazugumiye hani.
MAT 17:24 Nape lwabhafiha Hukapernaumu, abhantu bhabhawonganya ikodi yinusu shekeli bhamalila u Petro na yanje, “Aje umwalimu wenyu alipa ikodi yinusu shekeli?”
MAT 17:25 Ayanga, “Ee” Ila u Petro lwayinjila mukasi yinyumba, u Yesu ayanga nu Petro kwanza na yanje, “Usebhelelanshi Simoni? Amwene bhense, bhaposhela ikodi au uwushuru afume whananu? Whabhala bhahubhatabhala afume wha bhajenu?
MAT 17:26 Ni sala u Petro lwayangaga, “Afume whajenu” U Yesu amozya esho bhabhatabhalwa bhefiwilwe kati alipe.
MAT 17:27 Ila tisabhawombe asonkolezya ikodi bhawombe imbibhi bhala mbahari taga udobhani na uyeje ila eswe yewhenza kwanza. Baada ya hugule ilomu lyakwe ubhahuyaje omo asonkolezya ikodi kwa ajili yane na we.
MAT 18:1 Isala zezyo zezyo abhanafunzi bhenza wha Yesu na humozye, “Yu nanu waligosi huwo mwene wa humwanya?”
MAT 18:2 U Yesu akwizya umwana udodo, ameha pakasi yawo,
MAT 18:3 na yanje, “Lyoli ihumbawozya, nkagamtubu na bhe hansi abhana abhadodo sagamwayiweza hawhinjile huwomwene wa Ngolobhi.
MAT 18:4 Nesho wowonti wawhiha hansi umwana udodo, umuntu hansi oyo gosi huwomwene wa humwanya.
MAT 18:5 Na wowonti wahuposhele umwana udodo whitawa lyane ahumposhela nene.
MAT 18:6 Ila wowonti wasababisya uwana kati ya weka abha bhabhahuneteha asaliti, yayibha shinza wha muntu oyo iwe igosi lya syela lipinywe msingo yakwe, na hudwinizye mwidimi li bahari.
MAT 18:7 Aheli honse husababu yisala izya viswe huje saga hulini budi husala ezyo awhenze, ila ahele whakwe muntu ola isala ezyo zibhawhenze kwa ajili yamwene!
MAT 18:8 Nkesho inyobhe yaho au inama lyaho nkalyasabisizya aviswe lidumule na litaje uhuli nawe. Shinza hani whaho awe ahinjile huwomi luli bila nyobhe au shilema, kuliko atagwe mwimoto wiwila uli ni nyobhe zyonti au amanama gonti.
MAT 18:9 Nkesho iliso lyaho livisizye, lisenye na ulitaje uhutali nawe. Shinza hani huliwe awe uinjile huwoni ni liso lyeka kuliko ataywe mumoto wiwila ali na maso gonti.
MAT 18:10 Enyi aje msanzalau weka wabha dodo ebha. Kwa maana ihumbabhawozya aje humwanya huli antumi abhene insiku zyonti bhawhenya sha Baba wane wali humwanya.
MAT 18:11 (Simisizya: Amazu gagaloleha hansi gimsitali gwa 11, “Kwa kuwa umwana wa Adamu ahenzele awhaule shila shasha tejile” Sagagaloleshe mnakala nyinza zihale).
MAT 18:12 Msabhanshi? Nkesho umuntu alini ngole mya moja, na yeka yawo yatega, eshi sagabhahuzileshe tisini na tisa mwigamba na abhale afwate yeka yitejile?
MAT 18:13 Na nkayaga, lyoli ihumbawozya, asongwa kuliko zila tisini na tisa zyasaga zitejile.
MAT 18:14 Shesho shesho, saga lugano lwa Baba wenyu wa humwanya aje weka wa dodo ebha ateketele.
MAT 18:15 Nkesho uholo waho avisizye, bhalaga, unolesye ishida yeleho awe numene lyali mwene. Nkabhahutejelezye, unzabhe umwezizye uholo waho.
MAT 18:16 Ila nkasagabhahutejelezye, mweje, uholo weka au uwabhele hani pamo nawe, humalomu gasimisizi bhabhele au bhatatu kila izu liwezizye asimisizwe.
MAT 18:17 Na nkasholonya ahubhatejelezye wozi ishibhanza iswala elyo, nkesho asholanya tena ashitejelezye ishibhanza, eshi na abhe hansi umuntu upagani na unsonkolozya kodi.
MAT 18:18 Lyoli ihumbawozya, shoshonti shila shamwayipinya panse na humwanya shayipinywa. Na shoshonti shamwa yisatula panse na humwanya shayisatulwa.
MAT 18:19 Eshi ihumbawozya aje abhantu bhabhele pakashi yenyu nkabhetehana pamwanya yiswala lyo lyonti panse lya bhasaya, elyo u Baba wane wahumwanya ayihuliwomba.
MAT 18:20 Nkabhabha bhabhele au bhatatu wawongene peka whitawa lyane, ene endi pakasi yawo.
MAT 18:21 Tena u Petro ayenza nahumozye Yesu, “Gosi, halenga uhole wane avwisye nane insamehe? Hata mala saba?”
MAT 18:22 U Yesu amozya, “Sigiehuwozya mala saba, ila hata sabini mala saba.
MAT 18:23 Kwa sababu eyo awomwene wa humwanya ni sawa nu mwene omo wahanzaga asahihi sye ihesabu afume whaboyi bhakwe.
MAT 18:24 Lwahanda asahihisye ihesabu, uboyi weka bhaneta whamwene wali ahudayi italanta elfu kumi.
MAT 18:25 Afwatanaje sagaali ni dala lyalipe, ugosi wakwe alajizizye akazwe, onse wakwe pamo na bhana bhakwe na hantu honti hali naho, na malipo gafanyishe.
MAT 18:26 Esho uboyi agwiye, akhoma amafugamo whilongo lela lyakwe ayanga, 'Gosi, ubhe na golele pamo nane, na imbahulipe kila hantu.'
MAT 18:27 Esho ugosi wola uboyi, afwatanaje asukumwi we hani ninkombo, anesheye na husamehe iliga elyo.
MAT 18:28 Ila uboyi ola asogoye na humwaje weka kati ya boyi bhakwe, wali ahudayi idinali mia. Akwesa, abida whimilo na humozye, 'Ndipe shila shihudai.
MAT 18:29 ILa ola uboyi uwamwawo agwiye nahu nsisitizye hani, ayanjile, 'Ubhe nugolele nane, imbahulipe.'
MAT 18:30 Ila uboyi ola wawhande akhanile. Hubadala yakwe, abhalile na huntaje mwijela, hadi lwayihunipa shila shahudayi.
MAT 18:31 Na lwabhalola aboyi bhamwawo shila shishifumiye. Bhasononeshwe hani. Bhahenzele na humozye, ugosi wawo shila hantu hatokeye.
MAT 18:32 Ndiyo ola ugosi wa boyi ola akwizizye, na humozye, awe boyi mibhi nasamehile ane iliga lyane lyonti kwa sababu wandabhile hani.
MAT 18:33 Ashi! Sagawahanziwaga abhe ninkombo wha boyi abhamwenyu, hansi ane shanaloleye enkombo awe?
MAT 18:34 Ugosi wakwe avitilwe na humeshe whabhala bhabhayemva hadi lwailipa ishipimo shonti shadayiwaga.
MAT 18:35 Esho shesho Ubaba wane wa humwanya shaihubhawombela, nkesho kila weka wenyu saga ayihusamehe uholo wakwe afume mmoyo genyu.”
MAT 19:1 Hafumiye abhazyo u Yesu lwemalile amazu ego, asogoye Hugalilaya, na abhalile mu mpaho mwi Yudea whilongolela yisoho li Yordani.
MAT 19:2 Impoga ingosi yafwatile, na abhaponwe oho.
MAT 19:3 Afalisayo bhamaliye, bhanenjele, bhamozya, “Eshi halali wha muntu huneshe oshe wakwe husababu yoyonti?”
MAT 19:4 U Yesu abhajibu na yanje, “Sagamwabhazizye, aje uwene wabhawombele hulwawhande abhawombele unume noshe?
MAT 19:5 Na tena ayanjile, 'Hu sababu ene u nume ayihuneha ubaba wakwe nu maye wakwe na aungane nubhe wakwe, newo bhabhele bhayibha bele gweka?'
MAT 19:6 Esho saga bhabhele tena, ila bele gweka. Eshi, hala haunganisizye o Ngolobhi, umuntu wowonti asalehanye.”
MAT 19:7 Bhamozya, “Eshi yenu u Musa atiwozezye afumye ihati yitalaka na huneshe?”
MAT 19:8 Abhawozya, “Hukhome wimoyo genyu u Musa abharuhusile ahubhaleshe abhashe bhenyu, lakini afume lwawhande sagayali esho.
MAT 19:9 Ihumbawozya, aje wowonti wahuneha oshewakwe, ila husabu yiumalaya, na humweje uwamwawo, afanya umalaya. Nu nume wanzahumweje oshe walewhilwe awomba umalaya.”
MAT 19:10 Abhanafunzi bhamozya u Yesu, “Nkashenesho whanume na whunshe wake sagashinza awheje.”
MAT 19:11 Ila u Yesu abhawozya, “Saga kila muntu awezya aposhele amamanyizyo ega, ila whabhale tu bhaluhusiwilwe aposhele.
MAT 19:12 Ila bhaleho agomba bhapapwilwe afume mu vyanda vya maye wawa. Na shesho bhaleho agomba bhafanyiwilwe na bhantu. Na bhaleho agomba kwa ajili yiwu mwene wa humwanya. Wawezya aposhele amamanyizyo ega na agaposhele.”
MAT 19:13 Tena bhanetela abhana bhamo abhadodo ili abhabheshele inyobhe humwanya yawo na pute, ila abhanafunzi bhakwe bhabhakhalipiye.
MAT 19:14 Ila u Yesu ayanjile, “Bhaleshi abhana abhela, wala mungaje hubhakhane awhenze huline, afwatanaje umwene wa humwanya wibhantu hansi ebha.
MAT 19:15 Nepe abhabheshela inyobhe zyakwe pamwanya yawo, natena asogola pala.
MAT 19:16 Enya umuntu weka ayenza wha Yesu na yanje, “Mwalimu, hantu wele ahinza hihanziwa awombe ili impate uwomi wiwila?”
MAT 19:17 U Yesu amozya, “Yenu uhombozelezya aje hantu wele ahinza? Aleho weka mwene umwinza, ila nkuwhanza apate uwomi, lema indajizyo zya Ngulubhi.”
MAT 19:18 Ula umuntu amozelezya, “Ndajizyo ziwhi?” U Yesu amozya, “Usahagoje, usahibhe, usawombe uwumalaya, usahasimisizye ilenga,
MAT 19:19 ubhanje nishishi wha baba waho na whamaye waho, na ugane wapashenje yaho hansi umoyo gwaho.”
MAT 19:20 Umuntu ola amozya, “Amambo ego gonti ingakhete. Igolelanshi?
MAT 19:21 “U Yesu amozya, “Hansi nkuwhanza abhe golosu, bhalaga, ukazye vyuli navyo, na ubhapele apena ubhabhe nihazina humwanya. Eshi inzaga ufwate.”
MAT 19:22 ILa usahala ola lwahevwa gala u Yesu gamozezye, asogoye whazugumile, kwa sababu alikuwa na amemiliki mali nyingi.
MAT 19:23 U Yesu abhawozya abhanafunzi bhakwe, “Lyoli ihubhawozya, shikhome wha muntu utabhazi awhinjile huwo mwene wahumwanya.
MAT 19:24 Tena ihumbawozya, lahisi hungamia ashile mwishimo lisindani, kuliko wha muntu utabhazi awhinjile huwomwene wawha Ngolobhi”
MAT 19:25 Abhanafunzi lwabhahevwa esho bha swijile hani na yanje, “Yu nanu wayipenduha?”
MAT 19:26 U Yesu abhenya nayanje, “Whabhanadamu elyo sagaliwezehana ila wha Ngolobhi gonti gawezehana.”
MAT 19:27 Tena u Petro ajibu na humozye, “Enya, tileshile vyonti na hufwate awe. Hantu wele hataipata?”
MAT 19:28 U Yesu abhawozya, “Lyoli ihumbawozya, umwene wafwatileane, huu papo upya wakati umwana wa Adamu lwaikhala pitengo liumwene lituntumu wakwe, namwe mwaikhala pamwanya yimatengo kumi na gabhele giumwene, hubhalonje amakabela kumi na gabhele gi Israeli.
MAT 19:29 Kila weka wenyu waleshile inyumba, onkolo, uyilombo, ubaba, umaye, abhana, au ugonda kwa ajili yitawa lyane ayiposhela mala mia na pyane uwomi wiwila.
MAT 19:30 ILa abhinji bhabhali bhawhande isalezi, bhayibha bha humwisho, na bhabhali bhamisho bhayibha bhahande.
MAT 20:1 Hwa huje uumwene wa humwanya ulengene yalinugunda yadamuye ishandawe napwi, awale aweshe awawomba mbombo huugonda gwankwe lwa mizabibu.
MAT 20:2 Baada ya huentehana na awawomba mbombo dinari yeka hwisiku, ahawatuma awale hugonda gwankwe gwa mizabibu.
MAT 20:3 Ahawalo antele lwagashila amasala gatatu eshi ahawalola awawomba mbombo awamwao wahahemeleye bila mbombo husokoni.
MAT 20:4 Awawozyo, 'Amwe walaji hugonda wa mizabibu, hahonti hahali sawa imbalahuwapele.' Newowahavyala awombe imbombo.
MAT 20:5 Ahawala nantele lwagashila amasala sita ahawomba sheesho na masala tisa.
MAT 20:6 Ahawalilo awhamwao nantele mumasala gakumi na moja, akhawala ahawanga awantu awhamwao wemeleye bila mbombo. Ahawawozya, 'Shonu mwemeleye epa bila mbombo yuyonti husiku lyonti?
MAT 20:7 Wahamuonzya aje numo umuntu wowonti yatipelile imbombo. Ahawawozya, 'Amwe namwe walanji hugonda ugwi mizabibu.'
MAT 20:8 Amasala giliewela lwagaia, umwenesho gonda gwi mizabibu ahamozya umwemelizi wakwe, wakwunzye awawomba mbombo uwasombe umshahala, uyande uwa mwisho mpaka uwahwande.'
MAT 20:9 Lwawafiha wala wamasala ga kumi na moja, shilaweka ahaposheye idinari.
MAT 20:10 Lwawafiha owawomba mbombo awagwande wahasewele aje wazaposheye dinari yeka kila muntu.
MAT 20:11 Lwawaposhela amalipo gao, waha nalamishila umwenesho gonda.
MAT 20:12 Wahayanga, 'Ewa awawomba mbombo wa mwisho wejile isala lyenka wene kaliko awombe imbombo, lakini atifananisizye nate, ate linyumoye izigo hwisiku lyonti, nawine ni lyonto.'
MAT 20:13 Eshi umwenesho goda ahajibu weka wao, 'Kundanu, sagaimbombile ijambo lwiwi. Je! sagalahentehene nane idinari yeka?
MAT 20:14 Ega hahali haho halali sogolaga. Ane ishiye huwapele ewa awawomba mbombo wimbagwelezizye humwisho sawa sawa nawe.
MAT 20:15 Je! Sagagolosu huliwe awombe shihwanza ni maliyane? Au ilisolyaho li wiwi aje ane indi minza?
MAT 20:16 Eshi uwamwisho anzawe wa hwande na uwahwande azawe wa humwisho.”
MAT 20:17 U Yesu lwahazuwa awale Huyerusalemu, awawenjile awanafunzi wakwe kumi na wawele pambembe mwidala ahawawozya,
MAT 20:18 “Enyi tiwala Huyerusalemu, na umwana wa Adamu wanzahumeshe mnyowe inzya wagosi wa Amakuhani na awandisi. Wanzahunonje afye,
MAT 20:19 wanzahufumye hwa wantu wa munsi na munsi ili wasonsye, washente, na hukhowehenye. Lakini isiku ilya tatu ahaizyoha.”
MAT 20:20 Eshi umanye wa wana wa Zebedayo ahezele hwa Yesu na wana wakwe. Ahasugamila amafugamo hwitangalila lyankwe ahanawa ahantu afume hwakwe.
