MAT 20:21 U Yesu ahamozya, “Uhulanzashi?” Ahamozya, “Lajizwa aje ewa awana wane wawele wakhale, weka hukhono waho wa hunelo na weka hukhono waho wa humwongo huu umwene waho.”
MAT 20:22 Walakini u Yesu ahayanga na humuozye, “Saga umenye ahantu hulawa. Je! Uwajie amwelele ishikombe shinza mwelele?” Wamuozya, “Tuwajie.”
MAT 20:23 Awawawuzya, “Ishikombe shane lioli munza mwelele. Lakini akhale ukhono gwane wahunelona ukhona gwane ugwa humongo, sanga mbombo yane huwapele, lakini Udada wane awaweshe wala yawamenye.”
MAT 20:24 Awanafunzi awamwawo kumi lwawovya esho, wahazungumila hani na wala awahola wawele.
MAT 20:25 Lakini u Yesu ahawakwizya wawewo ahawa wozya, “Mmenye aje awalawala wa munsi wahongofya na awagosi wao wawomba amamlaka ganu mwanya yao.
MAT 20:26 Lakini isahawye esho humwenyu ishinyumw shakwe. Wowonti yahwazawe gosi hulimwe awe lazima amwe muwomba mbombo wenyu.
MAT 20:27 Na yanzawe wa hwanda hulimwe amwe lazima awye muomba mbombo wenyu.
MAT 20:28 Nanzi umwana wa Adamu sagaahezele awombelwe imbombo bali awombe imbombo hulimwe amwe, na afumye uwomi wakwe uwe ukombolewa huwinchi.”
MAT 20:29 Lwawahepanga Huyeriko, ikundi igosi lyahafuatile.
MAT 20:30 Wahawalolile wawabadiye amaso wawele wakheye mumbembe mubarabara. Lwawonvwa aje u Yesu wa shilaga, waha wajile ishogo na yanje, “Bwana mwana wa Daudi utusajile.”
MAT 20:31 Lakini ikundi lyahawadamie na huwawozye wapume niyie. Hatesho awene wahabwajile ishongo, hani nayanje, “Bwana, mwana wa Daudi, utusanjile.”
MAT 20:32 Epo u Yesu akhemelela na huwakwinzye na huwawuzye, “Mhwanza aje imbawombele iyenu?”
MAT 20:33 Wahayanga, “Bwana amaso gentu gafumbulilwe.”
MAT 20:34 Epo u Yesu avutwa awasajila, wapalamasya amaso gao, waposhela pepo ingovu ya lole wahafyenta.
MAT 21:1 U Yesu na wanafunzi wakwe bhahafia karibu Huyerusalemu na wakhawala mpaka Bethfage, hwi gamba ilya mizeituni, nantele u Yesu akhabhawonzya awanafunzi wawele,
MAT 21:2 akhawawozya, “Walaji hushijiji shishili hwilongolela isala zyezi munza huyanje idogobhi ipinyilwe pala, inyanadango yakwe. Mubhaule na huwalete huline.
MAT 21:3 Nkha muntu wowonti ahuwawozya lioliontu ahusu elyo, munza, `U Bwana ahubhanza, ` umuntu unyo hani hani anza huwenteshe ahwenze nayo”
MAT 21:4 Ijambo elyo lyahafumie lilila lyakhayangwilwe na watumi lazima lifumile. Shakhabhawozezye,
MAT 21:5 Bhawozye abhalendu bhahusayuni, enyhi uumwene wakho hu za humwenyu umwololo akhangaliye idogobhi umwana dogobhi unume, umwana dogobhi umembha.
MAT 21:6 Nantele awanafunzi bhahasogola nawombhe nanzi u Yesu shabhalajizizye.
MAT 21:7 Bhakhanetela idogobhi nu mwana dogobhi nawhesha amenda gao humwanya yao, nape u Yesu ahakhala pala.
MAT 21:8 Whinchi bhakhawongeni wakhala amenda gao mwidala, na awamo bhahadumuye amadhanzala afume mumakwi bhahalile mubalabala.
MAT 21:9 Awhinchi bhabhahatagaliye u Yesu bhala bhabhahafuatile u Yesu bhahabhanjile bhahayanga, “Hosana umwana wa Daudi! Usayhiwilwe uyezela hwitawa lya Bwana. Hosana humwa hani!”
MAT 21:10 U Yesu lwahafia Huyerusalemu, umji ghonti gwakhongopa nayanje aje, “Uno yu nanu?
MAT 21:11 “Awhichi wakhayanga, “Onho yu Yesu utumwa, afume Hunazareti ya Hugalilaya.”
MAT 21:12 Nantele u Yesu ahinjila hushiwanza sha Ngolobhe ahawamanyizya hoze wunti bhahakalaga na kazye mshiwanza. Antele ahagwisizye imeza zya bhahakalananga ihela ni vinti vyakhabhakazianga iunda.
MAT 21:13 Akhawawozya, “Isimbwilwe, “Inyumba yane inzakwiziwe nyumba ya puutile, `eshi amwe muyiweshele lipaho lya hupele.”
MAT 21:14 Naulele bwawabadiye bhakhalemeye bhahamalila hushibhanza nape akhabhaponizye.
MAT 21:15 Lakini awagosi wishiwanzya na abhasimbi lwabhakhalola amayele gawombile, na lwabhahovya awana bhabwanga ishongo mshibhaza na ayanje, “Hosana amwana wa Daudi,” bhakhakhatwilwe ni lioyo.
MAT 21:16 Bhakhamuozezye, uyumvyezye shabhayanga ewa abhantu?” U Yesu akhabhawozya, “Eee! inovyezye, lakini sagamuwahile abhazye afume humalomo gabhana na awasanga bhabhahoha muli indombo kamili?”
MAT 21:17 Nantele u Yesu akhawaleha akhawala honze yikhaya huu Bethania na ahagona khuho.
MAT 21:18 Ishandabhe lwakhawelanga humjini akhali ni nzala.
MAT 21:19 Akhalola ikwi pambembe yi barabara. Akhawala, lakini sagaahapente ahantu humwanya yankwe ila amatundu. Akhaliwozezye, “Usahabhe namadondo wila wila nantele.” Amasala gengo ikwi lila lyahoma.
MAT 21:20 Abhansukulu lwabhakhalola, bhakhaswinjile na yanje, “Yabhawele ikwi lyomele sheshi sheshikhani?”
MAT 21:21 U Yesu akhabhajimbu akhabhawozya lyoli ihumbawozya aje khamli nu lwetekho bila uwonga, sangamzawombe shishiwhumbeshe hwikwi tu, lakini mnzahuwhuzye hata elugamba lyengwe na hulitanje mwidimi igosi na inzawombeshe.
MAT 21:22 Lyolyonti lyamza labhe na punte nkhamli nulweuteho munzaposhele.”
MAT 21:23 U Yesu lwakhafika mshibhanza awagosi bha makuhani na bhagogolo bha bhantu wakhamalila lwahamanyizianga, na wakhamozya, “Hungovu wele uwomba amambo enga? Na yu nanu apiye ingovu enzi?”
MAT 21:24 U Yesu ahawajibu na hubhawozye, “Nane ihumba whuzya iswali lyekha. Nkhamuhubozya anje anane iwombo enga hungovu ya nanu.
MAT 21:25 Uwhoziwa wa Yohana- wakhafumile hwii, humwanya au hwa wantu?” Bhanayangana wene, aje, nkhatiyanje whakhafumile humwanya, `anzahutiwhozye shonu sangamwaha mweteshe? `
MAT 21:26 Nantele nkhatiyanje whakhafumile hwabhantu, `tihuwongopa wishiwaza, sababu whunti bhahunola u Yohana aje yutumi.”
MAT 21:27 Nantele bhahajibu u Yesu, “Sagatimanye” Akhabhawozya nape nane sangaihumbawhuzya hungovu wele iwhomba amambo ega.
MAT 21:28 Eshi msebha yenu? Umuntu yalinawana wawele. Akhabhala hwa weka akhamozya, `Mwanawane, bhala uwombe imbombo hugonda gwi mizabibu,
MAT 21:29 ilelo. `Umwana ahajibu na yan sangaimbala, Lakini pamande akhabadilisya isewho zyakwe akhabhala.
MAT 21:30 Na umuntu ula akhabhala hwamana wabhile humuozye shishila. Umwana ola ahajibu na yanje aje imbala, gosi,' lakini sagawabhala.
MAT 21:31 Yunanu kati ya wana bhabhile yawhombiole shahwanza uudada wakwe? Bhakhamuzya, “Umwana uwahuande.” U Yesu akhabhawonganya ikondi na bhamalaya bhahaiinjila hwa mwene hwa Ngolobhe shamsele amwe ahwinjile.
MAT 21:32 Huje u Yohana akhenzele hulimwe hwidala liligoloshe, lakini amwe sagamwahaposheye, eobha whunga nya ikodi na bhamalaya bhakhaposheye. Amwe, iwamwakhalola elyo liwhombeha sangamwakha lambihe aje pamande mposhele.
MAT 21:33 Tejelezi ufyana ungwamwao. Hwakhali umuntu, umuntu yalini sehemu ingosi iyinsi. Ahatotile amizabibu akhaga wesheye imbanga ahagombile ishombo sha nkhamile idivai, ahazenga iboma lyawalizi, ahapanjizya bhabhalimilila umuzabibu. Ahasongola akhawala insi inyamwao.
MAT 21:34 Uwakati wavune imizabibu lwabhafiha ahabhalajizya abhawomba mbombo hwabhalima amizabibu ahweje amizabibu gankwe.
MAT 21:35 Lakini bhabhalima amizabibu bhahawenga abhawomba mbombo wakwe, bhahakhoma weka bhabuda uwamwao bhakhoma weka na mawe.
MAT 21:36 Nantele ugosi ahatuma abhawomba mbombo abhamwao, winchi hani ashile wala abhahuande, bhabhalima amizabibu bha khawobile shishila.
MAT 21:37 Baada yepo ugosi ula akhatuma umwana wakwe, ahaga, 'Wazahutinishe umwana wane.'
MAT 21:38 Lakini bhabhalima amizabibu lwabhanola usahala ula, bhakhayangana, “Onu yu mrithi, Inzaji, tibude na tenye urithi.'
MAT 21:39 `Basi bhahatanga hunze mugonda gwi mizabibu na hubude.
MAT 21:40 Jee ugosi wigonda wa mizabibu lwanza ahwenze anza huwawombe wele bhabhalima imizabibu?”
MAT 21:41 Bhakhamuozya, “Anzahubhananganye ewho awantu abhabhibhi, hwidala ikhali hani, na anza panjizye ugonda gwi mizabibu hwa bhakulima abhamwawo wamizabibu, awantu bhabhaza sombe kwajili ya mizabibu lwagazatone.”
MAT 21:42 U Yesu akhabhawozya, “Aje sangamubhazizye amaandiko, iwe lwabha akhanile awazenje lyabha liwe ligosi lya msingi. Eli kyakhafumile hu Bwana, lishwizisya pamaso gentu?”
MAT 21:43 Eshi ihumbawhuzya, u Umwene wa Ngolobhe unzahungwe agume humwenyu, wanzapelwe bhamunsi bhabhasnga amadondu gankwe.
MAT 21:44 Whowhitu yazangwe humwanya yi iwe elyo anzabuduhane buduhane. Lakini whowhunti yalinzahugwele linzahusye.”
MAT 21:45 Abhagosi wishiwanza na Amafarisayo lwawhonvya ishifano shakwe, bhakhamanya aje ahubhayanga wewo.
MAT 21:46 Lakini lwabhanzaga agolosye inyobhe hwa mwene, bhahogope awashibhaza, awantu bhakhamwenyizye aje mtumi.
MAT 22:1 U Yesu akhayanga anao nantele hushifano, ahaga,
MAT 22:2 “Uumwene wa humwanya ulingana nu mwene yayandaile isikulukulu ya weji ya mwana wakwe.
MAT 22:3 Akhatuma abhawomba mbombo wakwe huwakaribisye bhabhahanilwe ahuenzi hushi kulukulu yi weji, lakini sagabhaheza.
MAT 22:4 Umwene akhabhatuma nantele abhawomba mbombo abhamwao aje bhabhawozye wonti, bhabhahanilwe, enyi inandaile, ishalye bhawolile ni ndama yane nyinonile, na mambo gonti gali tayari, Inzaji hushukulukulu yiweji.”
MAT 22:5 Lakini abhantu sagabhahovyezye shiza inyanwa yakwe. Abhamo bhakhabhalile humagonda na abhamo bhakhawelile humbombo zyao zya kazye ibiashala.
MAT 22:6 Abhamo bhakhabhavitililwe abhawomba mbombo wa mwene na hubhasosye na hubhabude.
MAT 22:7 Lakini umwene akhavitilwe. Akhatumile abhalungu wakwe akhabhabuda bhala abhabudi na hubhalongolezye nu moto peka ni khaya yao.
MAT 22:8 Nantele akhabhawozya abhawomba mbombo bhakwe, “Uwenji uli tayari, lakini bhabhahanilwe sagawasajie.
MAT 22:9 Eshi bhalaji humadala amagosi mubhane abhantu winchi, wonti bhabhanza loleshe, wenze hushukulukulu yiwenji.”
MAT 22:10 Abhawomba mbombo bhakhawala mumadala amagosi, hubhakalibisye abhantu wonti bhabhakhoneha, awinza na abhawiwi. Isebule yiweje ikhamema abhajenu.
MAT 22:11 Lakini umwene lwawinjila huwenye abhajenu, akhanola umuntu weka yasanga akhali numwenda gwiweji!
MAT 22:12 Umwene akhamozyo, 'Miya ufishile wele mhanti umu bila mwenda gwiweji?' Nu muntu ula saga akhajibu nalimo.
MAT 22:13 Shesho umwene akhabhawozya abhawomba mbombo bhakwe mpinyi umuntu uno inyobhe namanama, mtaje khonze hunkisi ukhohulikhole na asye amino.
MAT 22:14 Huje abhantu bhinchi wakwiziwa, lakini bhabhasalulwa, wadodo.”
MAT 22:15 Epo Amafarisayo bhakhasogola bhakhapanga isha hukhate u Yesu hunjango yakwe yuyo.
MAT 22:16 Bhakhabhatuma abhana wisukulu abhawo peka na Bhaherode. Na bhakhamuzya u Yesu, “Mwalimu, timenye aje awe uli munti wanalyoli naje umanyizya gahuanza Ungolobhe angalyoli. Sagausanga inongwa zya upendelelo hwa bhantu.
MAT 22:17 Eshi tiwozye usebha yenu? Je, shinza husheria asombe ikondi hwa Kaisari au sagashinza?”
MAT 22:18 U Yesu akhamenye ubwibwi wao akhabhawozya, shuno mulugela amwe mubwilenkha?
MAT 22:19 Mbonesi ihela yamsombela ikondi pabhahanetela impeya.
MAT 22:20 U Yesu akhabhawozya, “Isura ni tawa eli vyananu?”
MAT 22:21 Bhakhajibu, “Vya Kaisari.” Pepo u Yesu akhabhawozya mpeli Ukaisari ivintu vyakwe na ivya Ngolobhe mpele u Ngolobhe.”
MAT 22:22 Lwawovya esho bhakhasyinjile. Nantele bhakhenekha bhakhasogola swe.
MAT 22:23 Isiku Amasadukayo abhamo bhaheza hwa Yesu, wala bhabhayanga aje azyoshe nahumo awafye, bhakhamuozya.
MAT 22:24 Wakhayanga, “Mwalimu, Umusa ahajile, nkashe umuntu afyiye bila apape umwana, uhholao wakwe amurithi uyo ushe apele umwana uholo wakwe uyo.
MAT 22:25 Bhakhali abhaholo saba. Uwahuande ahejile nantele akhafya bila apape ubhana. Akhabha leshela mshe ukholowakwe.
MAT 22:26 Nepe ukholo wakwe uwabwile akhawomba shesho, nuwatatu, ihabha shesho hadi ula uwa saba.
MAT 22:27 Lwabhawombesho wonti, ula ushi nape wafwa.
MAT 22:28 Eshi uwakati wazyoshe uno ushe anzawe ashe wananu huwaholo ewa saba? Kwa maana wonti bhakhamwejile.”
MAT 22:29 Lakini u Yesu akhayanga nahubhawozye, “Mkosele sanga mgamenye amazyi wala ingovu izya Ngolobhe.
MAT 22:30 Shazili azyoshe, abhantu saga bhahuenga wala ahungwe. Shazibha aje abhantu bhawaje watumi wa Ngolobhe.
MAT 22:31 Lakini ahusu azyosye ufye sanga muwahile abhazye shila Ungolobhe shayenje hulimwe, ahayenje,
MAT 22:32 Ane ni Ngolobhe wa Ibrahimu, Ngolobhe wa Isaka, na Ngolobhe wa Yakobo? Ungolobhe saga yu Ngolobhe wa bhabhafyiye, bali yu Ngolobhe wa bhaliwomi.”
MAT 22:33 Awashiwanza lwabhahovyo elyo bhakhashijile imanyizyo zyakwe.
MAT 22:34 Lakini Amafarisayo lwabhahovwa aje u Yesu abhapumezezye Amasadukayo, bhakhawongene wene peka.
MAT 22:35 Weka ahali mwanasheria, akhamunzya ishwali lialuyele.
MAT 22:36 “Mwalimu, indajizyo yili ngosi ashile zyonti musheria nyihwi?”
MAT 22:37 U Yesu akhabhajibu, “Lazima ugana Ubwana hu moyo gwaho gonti, hupepo yaho yonti hujele ziaho zyonti.
MAT 22:38 Ene ndiyo ndajizyo ingosi na yahuande.
MAT 22:39 Na iyabwile ifwana neyo- Lazima ugane upalamani waho nazishuhuigana awe.
MAT 22:40 Isheria zyonti na Abhakuwa itegemela indajizyo enzi zibwile.”
MAT 22:41 Na Amafarisayo bhakhalisha bhawongene peka, u Yesu akhabhawozya ishwali.
MAT 22:42 Akhabhawozya, “Je!, Msebha yenu ahusu Ukrisiti? Umwene mwana wa nanu?” Nape bhajibu mwana wa Daudi.”
MAT 22:43 U Yesu akhabhajibu, “Ni kwa namna wele u Daudi humpepo ufijile ahukwinzya Bwana, ahumuozya,
MAT 22:44 'Bwana akhamuozezye u Bwana wane, “Nkhala hukhonogwana ugwa hunelo, mpaka pinzahubhaweshe abhabwibwi bhaho bhakhale pasi yi manama goho?”
MAT 22:45 Nkishe u Daudi ahukwinzya Uklisiti “Bwana,” Inzabhe wele mwana wakwe?”
MAT 22:46 Hakuna yabhajiye hujibu izyi nantele na nomuo yajelile nantele humuozye amashwali hani ahwande isiku ilyo na hundelelee.
MAT 23:1 Pamande ahizizye nu wungano wa bhantu paka na bhanafunzi bhakwe akhayanga,
MAT 23:2 “Abhasimbi na Mafarisayo bhakhalila itengo ilya Musa.
MAT 23:3 Eshi lyolyonti lyabhalajizya wombaji, muwombaje nuhu mubhanajizyaje. Lakini msahinjile mmbhiwi zyao, maana awene bhayanga amambo ngasanga bhawomba.
MAT 23:4 Lyoli, awene wapinya amazingo amamwamu gasanga bhabhajie ayumule alafu bhahuwatwiha abhantu muvipungo vyao. Lakini awene sagabhayembezya hata hayobhe anyumule.
MAT 23:5 Imbombo zyao zyonti bhawomba ili abhantu. Bhabhenye maana awene. Wahovyezya amabokosi gao na bhahonjezya ungosi wao na menda gao.
MAT 23:6 Awene wasongwa akhale isehemu inyinza yi shikulukulu, humatengo gishishi mvibhanza,
MAT 23:7 na alamshilwe hushishi isehemu yakazizye na akwiziwe “Mwalimu” na bhantu.
MAT 23:8 Lakini amwe sangamhwaziwa akwiziwe “Mwalimu” Mli nu mwalimu weka, amwe wonti mli kholo.
MAT 23:9 Msakha kwinzye umuntu wowonti munsi umu Daada wenyu maana mlinu Daada weke, tu nape ali humwanya.
MAT 23:10 Nantele msahakwiziwe 'mwalimu.' maana mli nu mwalimu weka napo yu Klisiti.
MAT 23:11 Eshi yali gosi kati yenyu anzavye muwomba mbombo wenyu.
MAT 23:12 Wowonti yahuisomba anza hulishe na wowonti yazahwishe anzazuwe.
MAT 23:13 Lakini mwashela amwe awasimbi na Amafarisayo, awilenkha! Muhubhagalilila abhantu umwene wa humwanya. Amwesangamubhajie huwinjile na sangamuhubha ruhusu bhabhahuaza hwinjile.
MAT 23:14 (Enya: Usitari ugwa 14 sagaulolekha isimbo inyiza izikhale, izimo isimbo zikhovyezya umstari ugu ugwa 12. Umsitari ugwa 14 “Mwashela amwe mubhasimbi na Mafarisayo muwilenkha amwe muhubhamila abhafyele”).
MAT 23:15 Mwashela amwe mubhasimbi na Mafarisayo, muwilenkha! Mfwemela hwisyela yi idimi igosi na humwombe umuntu weka awenu lwentekho hwagala mmanyizya, na lwabha na zimwe, Mhumwombela mala hawile abhe mwana wa hujehanamu nazi amwe shamlekho.
MAT 23:16 Mwashela amwe mubhalongozi mbadiye amwe mumuyanga, wowonti yalapa hushi bhanza sagahuli nazimo. Lakini yalapa hwiwye lihela yishibhanza apinyilwe na lapa hwankwe.
MAT 23:17 Amwe mubadiye wapumbavu, shenu ishi gosi ashile isha mwao iweilihela au ishibhanza, liliweshilwe tayari iwyelihela hwa Ngolobhe?
MAT 23:18 Wowonti ya lapa apafinjile, hamna ahatu, ila yalapa husadaka yili humwanya yakwe, apinyilwe ni ndopo yakwe.
MAT 23:19 Amwe mubhantu mubadiye shenu ishi gosi ashile isha mwao, isadaka au apafinjile papali tayari afumizye isadaka hwa Ngolobhe?
MAT 23:20 Eshi, uumwene yalapa pashifinjile alapa hwisho ni vintu vyonti vivili pamwanya yakwe.
MAT 23:21 Nape yalapa pashibhanza, alapa hulepo, nuyoakheye pakhanti yakwe.
MAT 23:22 Nape yalapa humabhengo, alapa hwitengo lgosi lya Ngolobhe na hwamwene yakhenye pamwanya yakwe.
MAT 23:23 Mwashela amwe mubhasimbi na Mafarisayo, Mubhilenka! Msomba izaka zya bizali, mnamwamu ingindajizyo, ingi haki, isanjilo, ni ulwenlekho. Lakini enga muhwaziwa mugawombe, siyohugaleshe agamo bila hugawombe.
MAT 23:24 Amwe mubhalongozi mubadiye, amwe myunga utududu utudondo lakini mumila idogobhi!
MAT 23:25 Mwashela amwe mubhasimbi na Mafarisayo, bhilenkha! Aje mkhozya honzya ishikombe na honze nyi mbakuli, lakini mkhanti mumemile imbhiwi sangamli nu wonga.
MAT 23:26 Amwe Mafarisayo mubadiye, ozyaji ahuande mukhanti yishikombe na mukhanti yimbakuli, na uupande wakhonzi nape ubhe zeru.
MAT 23:27 Mwashela amwe, mubhasimbi na Mafarisayo, Mubhilenkha! Mlinifyano yimakaburi gagapashilwe ichokaa, khoze gawhonekha miza lakini mukhanti gamemile amafupa gabhafyinye na shila khanti hintavu.
MAT 23:28 Shishesho namwe, namwe honze muwhonekha winza hwilongolela lya bhantu, lakini mukhanti mumemile ilenkha nu walangani.
MAT 23:29 Mwashela amwe, mubhasimbi na Mafarisayo, Mubhilenkha! Mzenga amakaburi ya wakuwa nahugapambe amakaburi gabhagolosu.
MAT 23:30 Namwe muyanga, aje mngakheye isiku izya waadadawenyu, indisanga muwombile peka akhinte ianda ilya wakuwa.
MAT 23:31 Amwe muhuyanga muwyene aje amwe muli bhana bhewo bhabhakhabha budile awakuwa.
MAT 23:32 Nantele amwe mumalezezya amenye isehemu yihwanziwa imbibhi izyabhadaada wenyu.
MAT 23:33 Amwe mzokha, bhana wimazokha, mwidala wele munza kwepe idongwa ya hujehanamu?
MAT 23:34 Eshi, enyi ihumbatuma aawakuwa hulimwe, abhantu winjele, na waasimbi, abhamo munza hubhabude ua hubhakhobhekhanye. Na abhamo munza hubhashente muhanti yivibhanza vyenyu na hubhadaje afume mkhaya yeka hadi iyamwao.
MAT 23:35 Hakhanza fumilepo hulimwe pazafumile idada zyonti izya wagolofu zyazyahitilwe munsi, ahuande idada lya Habili ugolosu, mpaka idanda ilya Zakaria umwana wa Barakia, yamwahabudile pahanti yapafinjile na pashibhanza.
MAT 23:36 Lyoli ihumbawhuzya, amambo enga gonti gakhaibhanga ishikholo eshi.
MAT 23:37 Yerusalemu, Yerusalemu, awe uhuwabuda abhakuwa na uhubhakhoma na mawe wala bhabhatumwilwe huliwe! khalenga imba whunganyenye abhana bhakho peka nanzi shila inkuku shiwhunganya inyana zyakwe pasi yi maapamikho agakwe, lakini sagahuentekha!
MAT 23:38 Enya inyumba yakho isangeye wene.
MAT 23:39 Nane ihuwozya, ahuande isala enzi nahundelele sangaunza hudole, mpaka lwahaiyanga, 'Asayiwilwe umwene yahwenze hwitawa ilya Bwana.”
MAT 24:1 U Yesu akhafuma mshibhanza na akhasogola. Abhanafunzi bhakwe bhakhamalila na hunolesye inyumba yishibhanza.
MAT 24:2 Lakini akhajibu na hubhawhunzye, “Je, muhungolola amambo enga gonti? Lyoli ihumbawhozyo nalimo Iwe lyalyahisagala humwanya yilya mwawho bila abomolewe.”
MAT 24:3 Na pakhakheye mwingamba li Mizeituni, awanafunzi wakwe bhakhamalila, “Pambembe, Tiwhuzye amambo enga gahaifumila ndii? Hantu wele khakhaiwonekha ahwenze huliwe na humwisho wa munsi?”
MAT 24:4 U Yesu akhabhajibu, akhabhawozya, “Msimisizyaje aje umuntu asakhabhatezye.
MAT 24:5 Maana winchi wanzahwenze hwi tawa lyane. Wanzayanje, 'Ane nene Klisiti,' na wanza huwatezye winchi.
MAT 24:6 Munza akhovye ulugo ni kholo yi lugo Enyanji musakhawye nii wonga, maana amambo engo lazima gafumile; lakini ula umalishilo unzabhe usele.
MAT 24:7 Hwamaana insi ni insi uwamwao zibhalalwe na umwene na umwene uwamwao. Hunzabhe inzala na nanyinje insi isehemu izimo zimo.
MAT 24:8 Lakini amambo enga gonti gahunde tu uchungu wa pape.
MAT 24:9 Ndipo wanza hubhafumye wapate amalabha na hubhabude. Mnza vitilwe na bhamnsi wonti husababu yi tawa lyane.
MAT 24:10 Epo winchi bhanza bomele na zilane navitilanwe bhewokwa bhewo.
MAT 24:11 Awakuwa winchi bhilenkha bhakhaifumila na hubhakhopela bhinchi.
MAT 24:12 Epo imbibhi ziahainyonjelela, ulugano ulwawinchi wahaipola.
MAT 24:13 Lakini yakhaijimba mpaka mumalishilo ahaiokolewa.
MAT 24:14 Eli inzwi ilya umwene lyakhailumbelelwa monti abhe ushaihidi mubha munsi mwonti. Epo owhavmalishilo unzahwenze.
MAT 24:15 Eshi, lwamwalilola ichukizo ilya nanganye, liliyangwile na u Danieli lyemeleye amahali pafinjile [Yabhazya amanye],
MAT 24:16 epo bhabhali huayunda washembelele humagamba.
MAT 24:17 Nula yali pamwanya panyumba asahajezye ahwishe pansi ahueuje ahantu hakhonti afume mkhanti yi nyumba yakwe,
MAT 24:18 nape yalekho hugonda asakha wele ahuenje umwenda gwakwe.
MAT 24:19 Washelile ewo bhali na bhana bhala bhabhakhosya husiku izyo!
MAT 24:20 Lawanji aje ashmbele hwenyu husakhabhe wakati wisasa, wala lisiku lya sabato.
MAT 24:21 Kwa kuwa hwaibha ishinda ingosi, yasanga iwahile afumile ahuande awhumbwe insi hadi isala enzi, na sagaikhaibha nantele.
MAT 24:22 Insiku izyo nkhasanga hupungoshe numo uyo angonkokho. Lakini hwa bhala bhabhasalulilwe isiku zyaipungukha.
MAT 24:23 Nantele nkhashe umuntu wowonti anzahubhawozye 'Enya, Klisiti alekho epa! au, 'Uklisiti alekho hula msakhakheteshe inongwa eyo.
MAT 24:24 Maana Amaklisiti wilenkha na abhatumi wilenkha bhanza huenze, na bhanza lolesye amayele amagosi nagashinjisye, hwilengo iliyatenzye, bhabhajie hata bhabhasalulilwe.
MAT 24:25 Enyanji, imbasundile shangasele amambo enga afumile.
MAT 24:26 Kwa huje khabhanza hubhawhunzye, “Uklisiti alihumbuga,' msahabhale ukho humbuga. Au, 'Enyaji, alimuhanti munyumba,' musakhakheteshe inongwa eyo.
MAT 24:27 Nanzi shila ilandi shinglala afume humashariki nakhoye hadi humaghalibi shishesho shanza huenze umwana wa Adamu.
MAT 24:28 Poponti papali uwozu, ukho pabhawhungana impanga.
MAT 24:29 Insiku zila amalabha amagosi nkhageza, isenya lyahaiwehwa ahinsi, nu mwenzi sangagwakha ifumya ukhozya wakwe, inzonto zyingwa afume humwanya, na ingovo izya humwanya zyakhaiyinga.
MAT 24:30 Epo amayele ga Mwana wa Adamu gakhailolekha humwanya, na amakabila gonti gamunsi gakhaikhola. Bhakhainola umwana wa Adamu ahuenze humabhengo gahumwanya hungonvu nu tunndumu ungosi.
MAT 24:31 Akhaimatuma abhatumi bhakwe ni isauti ingosi yi tarumbeta, ewho bhanza hubha whuganye peka abhasalulwe bhakwe afume ipane zinne izya munsi, afume humalishilo weka wahumwanya, hadi ungwamwao.
MAT 24:32 Manyizyaji isunkulu afume hwikwi. Lwalimela lifumya amatundu ni samba mumanya aje shisenya shikalibiye.
MAT 24:33 Nantele lwamzalole amambo gonti enga, muhuanzia amanye aje akalibiye, alikalibu munjango.
MAT 24:34 ihumbawhunzya, ishikholo eshi sangashishila, hadi amambo ganti enga ganzabhe gafumiye.
MAT 24:35 Imwanya ninsi zizashile, lakini izwi liane sangalishila kamwe.
MAT 24:36 Lakini isiku elyo ni saa inyo numo ya menye, hata abhatumi bhahumwanya wala umwana, yudaada mweene.
MAT 24:37 Nanzi shikhali isiku izya Nuhu, shinzabhe ahwenza umwana wa Adamu.
MAT 24:38 Isiku izyo shisele igalika, abhantu walinga, na bhamwelanga bheganga na huengwe, hadi isiku lila u Nuhu ahwinjile musafina,
MAT 24:39 sangabhakha menye ahantukhahonti khakhazafumile hadi egalika lwayenza na hubhazyole wonti - shinzabhe shesho lwakhaiyenza umwana wa Adamu.
MAT 24:40 Abhantu bhabhile bhahaibha humagonda- weka akhaiyengwa na weka akhailehwa hwisinda.
MAT 24:41 Abhashe bhabhile bhahaiwa asye peka - weka akhaiyengwa na weka akhaisagala.
MAT 24:42 Sanga mumenye isiku lyahaiyeza U Bwana wenyu kwa hiyo khalaji maso.
MAT 24:43 Mumanye aje umwenesho nyumba angamenye isala ya hwenze umwibha indi alimaso andasaga aleshile inyumba yakwe bha mwinjilile.
MAT 24:44 Shesho ihuanziwa abhe tayari, isala musangamuimenye umwana wa Adamu akhaiyenza.
MAT 24:45 Eshi yunanu aligolosu, umuwomba mbombo yali nijele, leyo ubwana wake apinye ugosi abhapelaje ishalye bhabhali muyumba yakwe husala yifaa?
MAT 24:46 Asayiwilwe umuwomba mbombo uyo, aje ubwana wakwe anzahumwaje awomba esho uwakati uuhuenza.
MAT 24:47 Lyoli ihumbawozya ubwana wakwe anzahumeshe humwanya kila hatu khalinakho.
MAT 24:48 Lakini nkashe umuwomba mbombo umibhi anzayanje mumoyo gwake, 'Ubwana wane akheye,'
MAT 24:49 na waanda hubhakhome abhawomba mbombo wakwe na alie kholwe amakholwa.
MAT 24:50 UBwana wa bhawomba mbombo uyo anzahuenze hwisiku lyasanga alimeye ni sala yasanga amenye.
MAT 24:51 UBwana wakwe anza hudumlanye ivipande vibhile na humeshe inafasi yeka na abhilenkha, ewo bhanza lile nasie amino.
MAT 25:1 Umwene wa humwanya ulinishifano wabhalende kumi bhahejile itala zyao na sogoke abhale huposhele ubwana wenji.
MAT 25:2 Bhasanu khanti yao bhakhali bhapumbavu na abhamwao bhasanu bhahali ni nejele.
MAT 25:3 Abhalendu abhapumbafu bhahejile itara zyao, sangabhahejile amafuta gogonti.
MAT 25:4 Abhalundu bhinjele ivyombo vimafuta peka ni tara zyao.
MAT 25:5 Uwakati ubwana weji achelewa afishe, whunti bhakhakhatwa nutulo na bhagona.
MAT 25:6 Lakini uwakati wa nusiku pakhanti khahali ni shingo, 'ENyi, ubwana weji! Fumi khonze mposhele.'
MAT 25:7 Ndipo ewho abhalendu bhakhadamula na khonzye itala zyao.
MAT 25:8 Bhala abhapumbavu bhabhawhuzya bhala bhinjele, 'Mtipele isehemu yi mafuta genyu ate itala zyetu zizima.'
MAT 25:9 Lakini bhala bhinjele bhakhayanga na hubhawhuzye, 'Huje sanganganza hutikwele ate namwe, eshi bhalaji hwabhakazya mkale madodo gagenyu.'
MAT 25:10 Lwabhabhala ukho akale, Ubwana wenji akhafikha, whunti bhabhakhali tayari bhakhabhala nao husikulukulu ya wenji, na uniango bhakhagalila.
MAT 25:11 Pamande bhala abhalendu abhamwao bhakhafikha, na yanje, 'Bwana, bwana tungulile.'
MAT 25:12 Lakini bhakhabhawozya, ane sangaimba meye.'
MAT 25:13 Eshi enyanji, aje sagamumenye isiku wala isaa.
MAT 25:14 Fuandi sawa nu muntu yahuanza shola abhala hunsi iyamwao. Ahabhakwinzizye abhawomba mbombo bhakwe na hubhaleshele uutajili wakwe.
MAT 25:15 Weka akhapinye italanta zisanu, uwamwao akhapinye zibhile, ula umuntu akhashola akhasogola weee.
MAT 25:16 Ula yakhaposhea italanta zisanu akhasongoye ishandabhe abhale husiwhombele, na ziakhapapa italanta iziamwao zisanu.
MAT 25:17 Nape yakhaposheye italanta zibhile ziakhapapa italanta iziamwao zibhile.
MAT 25:18 Lakini umuomba mbombo yakhaposheye italanta yeka, akhasongoye akhabana igondi pasi, akhazieshela ihela ya bwana wakwe.
MAT 25:19 Gwa hashila umuda utali, ula bwana wa bhawombambombo ahawela na akhagomba amahesabu anao.
MAT 25:20 Ula umuombambombo yahaposheye italanta zisanu akhenzele na lente italanta iziamwao zisanu, akhamuozya, 'Ubwana ukhampelile italanta zisanu. Enya, impente ifaida italanta iziamwao zisanu.'
MAT 25:21 Ubwana wakwe akhamuozya, 'Eshee, muwomba mbombo mwinza na uligolosu! Uligolosu huvinti ividodo. Inzahupele atabhale ivintu vinchi vya pamwanya. Injila ashe nu bwana whakho.'
MAT 25:22 Umuwombambombo yahaposheye italanta zibhele ahenzele na yanje, 'Bwana, ukhampinye italanta zibhile. Enya, impente ifaida italanta iziamwao zibhile,'
MAT 25:23 Ubwana wakwe akhamuozya, 'Ehee, muomba mbombo mwinza na ugolosu! uligolosu huvintu vinchi vya pamwanya. Injila ashe nu bwana wakho.'
MAT 25:24 Pamande yakhaposheye italanta yeka ahezele na yanje, 'Bwana, imenye aje awe ulimuntu khali. Uyibhila vyasanga utotile, na uhwenga vyasanga uweshele.
MAT 25:25 Ane nakhogope, nakhasogola ane nafisa italanta yakho pilongo. Enya, enepa yukhapiye yiliyakho.'
MAT 25:26 Lakini ubwana wake akhayanga na humuozye, 'Awe muomba mbombo mibhi na molo, ukhamenye aje iyibhila pasangaintontile na pasanga imbeshele.
MAT 25:27 Ihela yane uhuaziwilwe uwapele abhantu bhi benki, wakati wawele ane naposhelaga ela yahuline ni faida peka.
MAT 25:28 Eshi muopi eyo italanta na mpele ula umuomba mbombo yalini talanta kumi.
MAT 25:29 Shila muntu yalinasho anzahojelezewe zaidi- hata azidishibhe sana. Walakini wowonti yasanga alina hantu, hata hala khali nasho anzahupwe.
MAT 25:30 Taji khonze muhinsi uyo umuomba mbombo umibhi yasangafaa, ukho hwahusabhe alile nasie amino.'
MAT 25:31 Umwakati umwana wa Adamu lwakhaiyeza nu sisya wakwe, na abhatumi wonti peka numwene, panza akhale pamwanya yitengo lyakwe isisya.
MAT 25:32 Abhamunsi wonti bhahaiwongangana hwitagalila lyakwe, nape ahaibagula abhantu nanzi undimi shabagula ingole ni mbuzi.
MAT 25:33 Anza hubhabheshe ingole ukhono gwake wa hunelo, bali imbuzi anza hubhabheshe ukhono wahumongo.
MAT 25:34 Nantele umwene anzahubhabhuzya wala bhabhali ukhono wahunelo, 'Nnzaji, mumusaiwilwe nu Daada wenyu, murithi uumwene uulekho kwa ajili yenyu ahuande huwandilo wa munsi.
MAT 25:35 Lwanahali ni nzala mwakha mpelile ishalye; lwanakhali jenu mwahakalibisizye;
MAT 25:36 Lwanakhali bwinda, mwakhankwatizizye amenda; Lwanakhali minu mwakhanenyizye; Lwanakhafungwilwe mwakhezele.'
MAT 25:37 Ndipo abhagolosu bhahaiyanga na humuonzye, “Bwana, ndi lwatahalolile uli ni zala, lakhapela ishalye? Au uyumele ntakhapela amenze?
MAT 25:38 Na ndii takhalolile ulijenu takhakalibisya? Au uli bwindu takhakwatizya amenda?
MAT 25:39 Na ndii takhalolile uli minu, au ufungwilwe na twahenza?
MAT 25:40 Na uumwene akhaiyanga na hubhawonzye, 'Lyoli ihumbawhuzya lyamuwombile epa hwakholowane udodo weka, mumbombeye nene.'
MAT 25:41 Panza hubhawhuzye bhabhali ukhono gwakwe gwa humongo, 'Epanji huline mkhanilwe bhalaji hwanguli umoto wa wilawila uuweshelwe kwa ajili ya usietano ni impepo imbibhi,
MAT 25:42 ane nakhali ni zala lakini sagumwakhampiye ishalye; nakhomele lakini sagamwakhampiye amenze;
MAT 25:43 Nakhali fenu sangamwahankalibisizye; Nakhali bwinda sanga mwakha mpinye amenda; nakhali minu na nakhapinyilwe, lakini sangamwakhanenyizye.'
MAT 25:44 Ewo nape bhaimuozya na yanje, 'Bwana, ndi twakhalolile uli ni zala, au uyumele, au ulijenu au uli bwinda au uliminu, au ufungwilwe sangatakhasajiye?
MAT 25:45 Epo akhaiyanga na hubhawuozye, 'Lyoli ihumbawuozya, shila sanga mwahawombile hwaweka hwa bhadodo ewo, sangamwakhambombeye nene.'
MAT 25:46 Ebha bhakhabhala humalabha giwilawila bali abhagolosu huwomi wa wilawila.”
MAT 26:1 U Yesu lwabhamala ayanje inongwa ezyo zyonti, akhabhawozizye abhanafunzi wakwe,
MAT 26:2 “Mumenye aje baada yisiku zibhile huzabhe ishikulukulu ishi pasaka na umwana wa Adamu bhanza hufumye hukhobhehanye.”
MAT 26:3 Pamande abhagosi wi makuhani nabhagogolo bha bhantu, bhakhatangeni peka hwakhala ukukhani ugosi yakhakwiziwanga Kayafa.
MAT 26:4 Bhahali peka bhakhapanga ishahukhate u Yesu husiri na hubude.
MAT 26:5 Bhakhajili isakhawombeshe uwakati wa sikulukulu, aje isahafumile ivurugu hwabhantu.”
MAT 26:6 U Yesu lwahali Hubethania hunyumba ya Simoni mkoma,
MAT 26:7 lwahaigolosizye pameza, ushi weka akhezele akhanyumuye umkembe wahali na mafuta igi samani ingosi, akhanyunyulizya pitwe lyakwe.
MAT 26:8 Lakini abhanafunzi wakwe lwabhalola ijambo elyo bhakhavitilwe nayanje, “Yenu ihasala ine?
MAT 26:9 Ega tahabhajie ishiasi shigosi tibhapele abhapena.”
MAT 26:10 Lakini u Yesu, akhamenye eli, akhabhawuzya, “Shunu muhunavya ushe uno? Maana awombile ishintuishinza huline.
MAT 26:11 Abhapena mlinao isiku zyonti, lakini sangamzabhe peka nane wila.
MAT 26:12 Hwapashile amafuta mpele gwana, awombile esho kwa ajili ya sielwe ane.
MAT 26:13 Lyoli ihumbawozya, poponti izwi eli linzalimbelelwe munsi mwonti, ishitendo shawombile ushe uno, nantele shinzayangwa kwa ajili ya kumboshe.”
MAT 26:14 Weka wa bhala kumi na bhabhile, yahakwiziwanga Yuda Iskariote, akhabhalile huwagosi bha makuhani
MAT 26:15 na yange, “Mnza hupeleshi nkisalinti?” Bhakhapimila u Yuda ivipande selathini ivihela.
MAT 26:16 Ahwande umuda ugo ahazile inafasi yahusaliti.
MAT 26:17 Hata isiku iliahuande makate gasanga gaweshelwe ichachu, abhanafunzi bhahamalila u Yesu na yanje, “Uhwanza hwi tiweshele ishalye shi Pasaka?”
MAT 26:18 Akhabhawozya, “Bhalaji humjini hwa muntu fulani na mumwonzye, Umwalimu ayinga, “Umuda gwakwe ukalibiye. Ahwanza huimalezye ipasaka peka na bhanafunzi wakwe hu nyumba yakho.”
MAT 26:19 Abhanafunzi bhakhawomba nazi u Yesu shabhalajizizye, na bhakhandaile ishalye ishi Pasaka.
MAT 26:20 Lwayafika iliewela, akhakheye alye ishalye peka na bhanafunzi wakwe kumi na bhabhile.
MAT 26:21 Lwabhalianga ishalye ahabhawonzya, “Lyoli ihumbawozya aje weka kati yunyu anzahusaliti.”
MAT 26:22 Bhakhazungumiye sana, weka weka bhahandile humwonzye, “Je, saga nene, Bwana?”
MAT 26:23 Ahabhawozya, “Ula yanzatobhele inyobhe yakwe peka nane humbakuli yanza husaliti.
MAT 26:24 Umwana wa Adamu azasogole, nanzi shisimbililwe. Lakini umuntu yanza husaliti umwana wa Adamu! Indishinza hwa muntu uyo nkasanga ahapapwilwe.”
MAT 26:25 U Yuda, ula ahali msaliti akhayanga, “Je!, Nene Rabi?” U Yesu ahamonzya, “Uyanjile ijambo elyo awe wewe.”
MAT 26:26 Lwabhalianga ishalye, u Yesu ahenjile ikate, alisaya na akhamenya. Ahabhapela abhanafunzi wakwe akhayanga, “Eji mlye. Ungu bele gwane.”
MAT 26:27 Ahenga ishikombe ahasalipya, ahabhapela na yanje, “Mwelaji mwenti hweshi.
MAT 26:28 Ene danda yaindagano yane, yihwitikha kwa ajili ya winchi hubhasajile imbibhi zyao.
MAT 26:29 Lakini ihumbawhozya sanganahimwela antele amadondu ga mizabibu ega, hadi namwe huumwene wa Daada wane.”
MAT 26:30 Lwabhamalezya ahwembe ulwembo, bhakhasogola abhle hwigamba ilya mizeituni.
MAT 26:31 Nantele u Yesu akhawozya usiku uwhu amwe mwonti vitwe kwa ajili yane, kwa kuwa iyandihulilwe, Inzahukhome umchungaji ngole bhanza tabhanyishe.
MAT 26:32 Lakini lwanazyokha ane nakhaibhata ngalila abhale Hugalilaya.”
MAT 26:33 Lakini u Petro akhamwonzya, “Hata nkawonti bhakhane humambo gaganza hu hwaje, ane sangainza hukhane.”
MAT 26:34 U Yesu akhamwonzya, “Lyoli ihuwonzya, usiku uwhu shisele ihanda akunte, anzahukhane mara hatatu.”
MAT 26:35 U Perto akhamwozya, “Hata nkimbajie afye nawe, sangaimbala hukhane.” Na bhanafunzi wonti bhayanga shishesho.
MAT 26:36 Pamande u Yesu ahabhala nao amahali papahwetwa Gethsemane na akhabhawonzya abhanafunzi bhakwe, “Khali epa wakati ane imbala ukho alabhe.”
MAT 26:37 Akhamwenga u Petro na abhana bhabhile wa Zebedayo na akhanda azungumile na sononoshe.
MAT 26:38 Nantele akhawonzya, “Umpepo ufinjile wane izungumie pangosi sana, hata ihwanza afye. Lakini epa mubhe masopeka nane.”
MAT 26:39 Akhabhala pilongolela hadondo, angwa gubama na alabhe. Akhayanga, “Daada wane, nkashe bhajie ishikombe eshi shinepe. Isakhabhe shihwanza ane bali nanzishuhwanza awe.”
MAT 26:40 Akhabhabhalila abhanafunzi ahaweje bhagonile utulo, akhabhawozya Petro, “Shunu sangamlimaso nane hata isala lyeka?
MAT 26:41 Kesyanji na labhe ili msahahinjili mumajaribu. Iroho ili radhi, lakini ubele niwolo.”
MAT 26:42 Akhabhala wee imala ya bhele na labhe, akhayanga, “Daada wane, ijambo eli sagalibhajie hunepe ni lazima imwelele ishikombe eshe, amapenzi gakho gatimile.”
MAT 26:43 Akhawela nantele akhabhaga wagonile utulo, amasogakho gakhali mamwamu.
MAT 26:44 Nantele akhabhalekha akhabhala akhalabha amara ya utatu akhayanga inongwa zizila.
MAT 26:45 Pamande u Yesu akhabhabhalila abhanafunzi wakwe na hubhawhuzye, “Mulisha mgonile tu natozye? Enyanji isaa ilikaribu, na umwana wa Adamu akhatwa mumakhono mwabha bhibhi.
MAT 26:46 Damulaji, tisongolanje. enyi ula yahusalinti akaribiye.”
MAT 26:47 Lwakhali bado ayanga, u Yuda weka wa bhala kumi na bhabhile akhenza namapanga ni ndungu.
MAT 26:48 Nantele umuntu wahusaliti u Yesu akhabhapelile ishara, ahayenje, ula yinza hubusu, ndiyo yuyo. Khante.”
MAT 26:49 Papepo akhezele hwa Yesu akhayanga, “Salamu, Mwalimu!” Na akhabusu.
MAT 26:50 U Yesu akhamwozya, “Kondani, liwhombe lila ulinalyo lililetile.” Ndipo bhahenza, nagolosye inyobhe hwa Yesu na hukhante.
MAT 26:51 Enyi, umuntu weka yakhalipeka nu Yesu, akhagolosesye inyonbhe yakwe, akhachomola ipanga lyakwe, akhakhoma umuomba mbombo wa kuhani ugosi, na hudumule ikutu lyakwe.
MAT 26:52 Ndipo u Yesu akhamuozya, wezya ipanga lyakho puyejile, kwa kuwa wonti bhabhatumila ipanga bhanza hwangamile ni panga.
MAT 26:53 Myinga sangaimbajie hukwinzye udaada wane, nape angantumila abhalugu zaidi ya kumi na bhabhile ya awatumi?
MAT 26:54 Eshi shihwaziwa atokele ili amandiko katimile hwidala elyo?”
MAT 26:55 Uwakati whuwho u Yesu akhabhawuzyo bhabhawungene, “Je! Mwenzele namapanga nidungu hukhante nazi yahupa? Kila lisiku nakhakheye namwe mshibhanza, nabhamayizyanga sanga mwakha kheute!
MAT 26:56 Lakini gonti enga gawombeshe ili amaandiko ga watumi gatimile.” Ndipo abhanafunzi wakwe bhakhanekha bhakhashembela.
MAT 26:57 Bhala bhabhakhate u Yesu bhakhatwala hua Kayafa, ukuhani ugosi, amahali epo abhasimbi na agogolo bhahawongene peka.
MAT 26:58 Lakini u Petro akhafuatle hwisinda huhutali mpaka hushumba sha kuhani ugosi. Ahinjila mhanti akhakhala peka nu ninzi alole shashinza fumile.
MAT 26:59 Basi abhagosi bha makuhani ni baraza lyonti liahazanga uushaidi wileukha juu ya Yesu, ili bhapate hubude.
MAT 26:60 Bhakhafumie amashaidi winchi, lakini sangabhahayeje imbibhi yoyuti. Lakini pamandi amashahidi bhabhile bhakhafumila hwilongolela
MAT 26:61 na bhayanga, “Umuntu uno akhayenje, “Imbajiye agwisye ishibhaza isha Ngolobhe na hushizenje nantele husiku zitatu.”
MAT 26:62 Ukuhani ugosi ahemelela na humwonzye, “Saga ujibu? Ewa bhahuwhuzya wele juu yakho?”
MAT 26:63 Lakini u Yesu akhapuma mye. Ukuhani ugosi ahamwozya, “Nanzi uNgolobhe shakhala ihulazimisya utawhuzye, awe wewe Klisiti, Umwana wa Ngolobhe.”
MAT 26:64 U Yesu ahabhawuzya, “Awe wewe uyanjele ijambo elyo. Lakini ihuwozyo, ahwande eshi nahwendelele, unza hunole Umwana wa Adamu akheye ukhono unelo uulinigovo, na ahuenza humawengo gahumwanya.”
MAT 26:65 Ndipo ukuhani ugosi akhazebula amenda gakwe nayanje, “Akhanile! Je, tihwanza washi nayanje uushahidi?
MAT 26:66 Je! Msebhashi bhayanga nahumwozye, “Ahuanziwa afye.”
MAT 26:67 Nantele bhakhashelela amate humasona hukhome ingumi na huchete amakofi ni nyobhe zyao,
MAT 26:68 na bhakhamuozya, “Yanga, wewe Klisiti. Yunanu yachapile?”
MAT 26:69 Isala izyo u Petro ahakheye huoze huu kumbi, umuomba mbombo wishishi ahamalila nahumuozye, “Awe nawe ulipeka nu Yesu wa Galilaua.”
MAT 26:70 Lakini ahakhanile hubele yao wonti, ahanga sangaimenye ahantu huyanga.”
MAT 26:71 Lwabhala hunze huniango, umuomba mbombo uwamwao wishishi ahanola na hubhawhuzyebhabhahali epo, “Umuntu uno nope alipeka nu Yesu wa Nazareti.”
MAT 26:72 Akhakhana tena na lape, ana sangaimenye umuntu uno.”
MAT 26:73 Umuda kidogo pamande, wala bhabhahemeleye karibu, bhakhamalila nahumuozye u Petro, “Na lyoli awe nawe ulipeka nao, hata njango yakho ilolesya.”
MAT 26:74 Pahandile akhana na lape, ane sanga imenye umuntu uno,” papepo ihanda ikhakuta.
MAT 26:75 U Petro ahakumbukha inongwa yakhamuozezye u Yesu, kabla yihanda isele akute unza hukhane mara hatatu.”
MAT 27:1 Amasala gishandabhe akhafikha, khabhagosi wonti bha makuhani na bhazee bha bhantu bhakhaliye injama juu ya Yesu wapate hubude.
MAT 27:2 Bhakhapinya, bhakhanongozya, bhafishia hwa liwali u Pilato.
MAT 27:3 Nantele u Yuda, yahali msaliti, akhalolile aje u Yesu tayari alomgwile, akhazungumie wawezya ivipande selasini ivi hela, hwabhagosi wa makuhani na bhazee,
MAT 27:4 na akhayanga, “Imbombile imbibhi ya huisaliti idada yisanga ilimbibhi.” Lakini bhakhamonzya, “lihutuhusu lyenu ate? Genyaye ego wewe.”
MAT 27:5 Nantele wavitanga pasi vila ivipande vinhela hwishibhanza, na ahasogola na huiyoje mwene.
MAT 27:6 Ugosi wa makuhani ahavyenga vila ivipande vi hela na ahayanga, “Sagashiza kuibheshe ihela ine mhazina, kwa sababu yi danda.”
MAT 27:7 Bhakhayangana peka ihela itumishe akalile ugonda gwa whumbile azyeshele abhajenu.
MAT 27:8 Kwa sababu eyo ugunda ugwa likwiziwa “Guda gwi danda” hadi ilelo eshe.
MAT 27:9 Nantele ela inongwa yikhayangwile na abhatumii u Yeremia liahatimila, aje, “Bhakhejile ivipande selasini ivi hela, ibeyi yihapangwilwe na bhantu bha Israeli hwa ajili yakwe,
MAT 27:10 bhakhatumie ugonda gwa muwhumbaji nazi u Bwana shakhelezezye.”
MAT 27:11 Eshi u Yesu ahemeleye hwilongolela lya Liwali na uliwali akhamwozya, “Je! Awe uli mwene wa Wayahudi?” U Yesu akhajibu, “Awe uyejesho.”
MAT 27:12 Lakini lwawasitakiwa na bhagosi wa makuhani na bhazee, saga ahajibu lyolyonti.
MAT 27:13 Nantele u Pilato akhamuozya, “Sagauyuvyezye amashitaka gonti agakho?”
MAT 27:14 Lakini sanga akhajibu ineno hala lyenka akhaswinga uliwali.
MAT 27:15 Hwisiku zisikulukulu ihali kawaida uliwali humungulile yapimyilwe weka yasalulilwe na winchi.
MAT 27:16 Uwakati uwo bhahali nuyoapinyilwe wimatata ilawa lyakwe yu Baraba.
MAT 27:17 Lwabhawungene peka upilato akhabha wuzya yunanu yamuhunza imungulile kwa ajili yunyu?” Ubaraba au Uyesu yahwetwa Klisiti?”
MAT 27:18 Maana akhamenye aje tayari bhakhe kwa sababu bhavitililwe.
MAT 27:19 Wakati akheye hwitengo ililonzi, ushe wakwe akhatwalila ineno aje, “Usakawombe lyolyonti hwa muntu uyo yasanga alini mbibhi. Yaani indawile hani ilelo mundonto kwa ajili yakwe.”
MAT 27:20 Ndipo abhagosi wa makuhani na bhazee bhakhabhakondelezya amakutano aje bhanabhe u Baraba, u Yesu afye.
MAT 27:21 Uliwali akhabhawuzya, “Yunani kati ya bhabhile yamuhwa nza amwe ineshele?” Bhakhayanga, “Ubaraba.”
MAT 27:22 U Pilato ahawawuzya, “Imombe wele u Yesu yahwetwa Klisiti?” Wonti bhahamuozyo, “Amayembe”
MAT 27:23 Nape ahayanga, “Shunu likosashi awombile?” Lakini bhahojelela apwaje isauti hata humwanya hani, “Ayembe.”
MAT 27:24 Epo Upilato lwa saga awajiye awombe lyolyonti, ivurugu ziahandile ahenga amenze ahazuguzila inyobhe zyakwe hwilogolela ilya winchi, na yanje aje, “Ane sagandi ninogwa juu yi danda iya muntu uno yasanga alinibibhi. Genyanji ega mwe mwemwe.”
MAT 27:25 Awanti wonti bhahayanga, “Idanda lyakwe liwe juu yetu na bhana wetu.”
MAT 27:26 Epo ahamungulila u Baraba wao, lakini ahakhoma amijeledi u Yesu na ahabhapela awene abhale hukhobhehanye.
MAT 27:27 Nantele abharugu bha liwali bhahamwenga u Yesu mpaka Praitorio ni kundi igosi lya bhalongu wonti bhakhamunganila.
MAT 27:28 Bhahavula amenda gwakwe na hukwatizye igololeli langi ishamamu.
MAT 27:29 Tena bhahagomba itaji yi mivwa na bhaiwehe hwitwe lyakwe na hususye, bhahayanga, “Salamu, Wamwene wa Wayahudi?”
MAT 27:30 Na bhaswelela amate, na bhahenga imwanzi na hukhome hwitwe.
MAT 27:31 Wakati bhahususya bhakhavulile igolole na hukwatizye amenda gakwe, na hunogole abhale hukhobhehanye.
MAT 27:32 Lwabhafuma hoze, bhahanola umuntu afume ilawa Krene ilawa likwa yu Simeoni, uyo bhakhanazimisya abhale nao ili anyumule ishikhomehayo shakwe.
MAT 27:33 Lwabhafikha pala Pagaligotha, imaana yakwe, “Ieneo lya ifupa litwe.”
MAT 27:34 Bhakhapela siki yabhasnganyenye ni nyongo amwele. Lakini lwawonga saga ahamwela.
MAT 27:35 Lwabha khomehanya, bhahagabhana amenda gakwe bhahahoma ikura.
MAT 27:36 Na bhahakhala na humwenye.
MAT 27:37 Hwitwe lya Yesu bhahaweshele inongwa yakwe ihabhaziwanga, “Uno yu Yesu, umwene wa Wayahudi.”
MAT 27:38 Bhabhahupa bhabhile bhahakhobhe nywepeka numwene, weka ahali upande wa nelo wakwe na uwamwao wa humongo.
MAT 27:39 Bhala bhabhashilanga bhasosyanga bhahayizianga amatwe gao
MAT 27:40 na humozya, “Awe wawazaga anaganye ishibhanza na azenye husiku zitatu uyokole wewe! Nkuli mwana wa Ngulubhe, ikha pasi uyepe mumalabha!”
MAT 27:41 Katika ihali yiyela abhagosi wa makuhani bhasosyanga peka na abhasimbi na abhazee, na humuozye,
MAT 27:42 “Ahokoye abhanche. Yu mwene wa Wayahudi. Na ayishi pasi afume mumalabha, epo tinza humweteshe.
MAT 27:43 Ahasobhenye Ungulobhe. Lekha Ungolobhe amwokole eshi nkashele ahuanza, nkashele ahuanza, nkashila ahayenje, 'Ane nene mwana wa Ngolobhe.”
MAT 27:44 Na wala bhabhahupa bhabhakhomagenywe peka nu Yesu nape bhahayenje hususye.
MAT 27:45 Eshi afume msaa sita hwahali ahinsi munsi yonti hata saa tisa.
MAT 27:46 Lwayafiha saa tisa, u Yesu ahalila husauti ingosi, “Eloi, Eloi, lama thabakithan?” Imana yakwe, “Ngolobhe wane, Ngolobhe wane mbona undeshile?”
MAT 27:47 Uwakati uwo bhahali awamo bhemeleye pala bhahovya lwayanga, “Ahukwinza u Eliya.”
MAT 27:48 Haraka weka ahashembela ahwenje isifongo na huimyeme isha mwele ishikhali, ahaibhiha huwanya yikwi na hupele ili amwele.
MAT 27:49 Nape bhabhahasageye bhahayanga, “Neshe mwene, leshe tenye u Eliya nkahwenza humwokole.”
MAT 27:50 Nantele u Yesu ahalila husauti ingosi aifumya iloho yakwe.
MAT 27:51 Enya, ipazia lya mshibhanza lyahazembukha isehemu zibhile, afume humwanya mpaka pasi. Na insi ihayingile, na amawe gahabazushe vipande.
MAT 27:52 Amakaburi gahugushe amabele gabhagolosu wichi bhabhahagonile utulo bhahazyoshile.
MAT 27:53 Bhahafumile mumakaburi lwawazyoha, bhahawinjila umji ugolosu, na bhahakhoneha na winchi.
MAT 27:54 Basi ula uakida na walabhahamwenyaga u Yesu bhahalola itetemeko na amambo gagahafumiye, bhahabha nuwongo sana nayanji aje, “Lyoli onu ahali mwana wa Ngolobhe.”
MAT 27:55 Awashe winchi bhahafuatile u Yesu afume Hugalilaya ili humwombele bhahali pala humwenye afume hulali.
MAT 27:56 Mhati yao bhahali, Umariam Magdarena, Umariamu umaye wa Yakobo na Josefu, na umaye wa wana wa Zebedayo.
MAT 27:57 Lwayafiha ilyebhela umuntu utajili afume Arimathayo, yahetelwa u Yusufu, nantele ahali mwanafunzi wa Yesu.
MAT 27:58 Ahamalila u Pilato hunabhe ubele gwa Yesu. Upilato ahalajizya bhapele.
MAT 27:59 Uyusufu ahawejile ubele ahaupinya na menda gi sufi inzeru,
MAT 27:60 ahaugonya mwikaburi lyakwe ipya lyalyahachonjilwe mwiwe, alafu ahawungulusya iwe igosi lyahazinga uniongo gwi kaburi ahasogolo.
MAT 27:61 Umariamu Magdalena na Umariamu uweche bhahali pala, bhahenye pikaburi.
MAT 27:62 Isiku lilyahafuata lyahali lisiku lya maandalizi, abhagosi wa makuhani na Mafarisayo bhahawungeni peka hwa Pilato.
MAT 27:63 Bhahamuozya, “Bwana, tuzushe aje ula wilenkho lwahali momi ahajile, 'Baada yi siku zitatu anzazyoshe.'
MAT 27:64 Eshi lajizya aje ikaburi bhalinde sallama mpaka isiku ilyatatu. Nkasanga shisheshe abhanafunzi wakwe bhanza hweze humwibhe na wazayanje hwa wantu aje azyoshele afume mfye, na ilenkha ilyamwisho linzabhe libhibhi ashile ilyahwande.”
MAT 27:65 U Pilato ahabhawuozya, “Eji abhalizi. Bhalaji muweshe usalama shamulolile.”
MAT 27:66 Basi bhahabhalile aweshe usalama hwikaburi iwe lyahahomwa umuhuri naweshe abhalinzi.
MAT 28:1 Pamande ilyewele isiku ili Sabato, isenye lwalyaswanga awale isiku ilyahuande ijuma, Umariamu Magdalena, nula Umariamu uweche bhahawalile ahwenye ikaburi.
MAT 28:2 Bhenya hwahali itetemeko igosi, maana ukuwa wa Bwana ahishile huliwungu lushe iwe lila, alafu ahali khalila.
MAT 28:3 Isura yakwe ihalije umeme na amenda gakwe gahali mazelu aje choka.
MAT 28:4 Bhala abhalizi bhahamema uwonga bhabhaje wofyinye.
MAT 28:5 Ola ukuwa akhabhalanganyizwa wala awashe akhabhawozya bhasahahongope maana imenye aje muhumwanza u Yesu, yahakhomayenywe.
MAT 28:6 Numo epa, lakini azyoshele nanzi shakhabhawuzezye. Inzaji mwenye pabhakhagonezye u Bwana.
MAT 28:7 Bhalaji nalinali hubhawuzye abhanafunzi wakwe, 'Azyoshile afume hwabhafwe, enyi abhatagaliye Hugalilaya. Ukho hwamuzahunole.' Anya ane imbawozezye.”
MAT 28:8 Bhala abhashe bhakhasongola pale pikaburi nalinali shabhali nuwoga na bhahashiye sana, bhakhashembele hubhabhuzye abhanafunzi wakwe.
MAT 28:9 Enya u Yesu ahatangana nao ahangaa, “Salamu.” Bhala abhashe bhahenza na hukhante amanama gakwe, nantele bhahapunta.
MAT 28:10 Nantele u Yesu ahabhabhuzya, “Musakhahongope, bhalaji mubhawuzye abhaholo bhane bhalongolele Hugalilaya. Ukho bhaza hundele.
MAT 28:11 Wakati wala awashe bhabhalaga enya abhamo abhalinzi bhahabhala humjini na hubhabhuzye abhagosi wamakuhani amambo gonti gagafumiye.
MAT 28:12 Nepe amakuhani twabhahatangana na bhazee, nayangane ijambo elyo peka nao, bhahafumizye ishiasi ishigosi shi hela lwabhala abhalogo
MAT 28:13 na hubhabhuzye, “Yangaji hwabhamwao aje, 'abhanafunzi wa Yesu bhahezele nusuku ahwibhe ubele gwa Yesu lwatigonile ante.'
MAT 28:14 Ihabali ene nkifishile uliwali, ate linza hubebelezye na hubhefuezye amwe amashaka gonti.”
MAT 28:15 Bhala abhalugu bhahazienga ihela zila nawombo shabhawuzewelwe. Ihabari ikheneyesana hwabhayahudi ilekho mpaka ilelo.
MAT 28:16 Lakini bhala abhatumi kumi na moja bhahabhalile Hugalilaya, hula hwigamba hwakhabhawuzezye.
MAT 28:17 Lwabhahanola bhakhaputile. Walakini abhamo bhakhalola ishaka.
MAT 28:18 Yesu akaja akawambia akisema, “Nimepewa mamlaka yote duniani na mbinguni.
MAT 28:19 Eshi bhalaji mubhabheshe abha munsi wonti abhe bhanafunzi, wuoziaji hwitawa lya Daada nalya mwana nilya upepo ufijile.
MAT 28:20 Mubhamanyizye nabhenishishi humambo gonti gimbalajizizye, eye ane indipeka namwe wilawila, hata mumalishilo wa munsi.
MAR 1:1 Ugu wandilo uwanlumbilile izya Yesu uKilisiti.
MAR 1:2 Nishi pihasi mbilwe nukuwa Isaya, “Enya, ituma umuntu wani witazi lwaho, uumo uwandale idala lwaho.
MAR 1:3 Sauti ya muntu uwakhola wipoli, “Kamiliswaji idala lwa Bwana; zigolosuaji amdala gakwe.”
MAR 1:4 U Yohana ahinza, ahanzhele awonzwa wipoli nalumbelele ulwozwo ulwawiyiswe sameshe imbivhi.
MAR 1:5 Inzi yunti iya Yudaa na wantu bhudi wa Yelusalemu bhala yawamwene bhanga bhawozewa numwene isoho yo ndani bhasangamaga imbi zyao.
MAR 1:6 U Yohana ahali akwata amenda gimoya gingamiya nukanda ngui nkwembe musana gwakwe, alwanga ikhopha nu woonshi wa wipoli.
MAR 1:7 Alumhelelaga nayaje, “Ajwele omo aweza palene ya nikhonsana ani sayaiwezwa, sasga imbajile awishe pansi nawaule inyao zya malato gakwe.
MAR 1:8 Anle ihabhabhozyaga humhenze, lelo umwene aibhozya humheze huhala Uzelu Umuiza.”
MAR 1:9 Lihafumila isikulimo insiku izyo huje uYesu ahizele afume hu Nazareti ya wiGalilaya, ahozewa nu Yohana wisoho Yorodani,
MAR 1:10 Epou uYesu pauha afumemeze, ahalola imwanya awihiha pamwanya pa mwene nishi injibha.
MAR 1:11 Isauti ihafuma amwanya, “Awe uli Mwana Wani. Niphendeziwe sana nawe.”
MAR 1:12 Shisho uhala alazima hwa awale wipoli.
MAR 1:13 Ali wipoli insiku amarogo ganhi, shajelwa nuSetano. Hali pandwemo na makhanu gamwipoli, abhandumi bhambela.
MAR 1:14 Ahishi afume Yohana akhatwe, Yesu ahiza hu Galilaya alumbelila inongwa zya Ngulubhi,
MAR 1:15 ahayanga, “Abhalilo na utawala wa Ngulubhi mbhelile lambi nahwenteshe nishi alumbhelele”.
MAR 1:16 Ashizanya mushenje mushejenje ya Galilaya, halola uSimoni nu Andeleya uholowakwe usimoni bhaponya inyavu zwao mu nsumbi, pipo bhahali bhabhalobha.
MAR 1:17 U Yesu ahabhabhuli, “Ajeiza, nhizaji, dangaji izabhambeshe walolombe samantu.”
MAR 1:18 Nahazileha inyavu zyao na hunfwate.
MAR 1:19 U Yesu pajendanga apatali hashe, ahabola u Yakobo umwana wa Zebedayo na Yohana uholo wakwe; bhali mwitori bhalinganya lyavu.
MAR 1:20 Abhakuga bhope bhafuta bhahaleha inyise wao za Zebedayo wahaleha mhati mwitori natumishi abhanji abhakondilwe, wahafuta.
MAR 1:21 Pa bhahafiha Kaperinaumu, isiku ku Lwatuye, uYesu ahinjila aputile nawamanyizye.
MAR 1:22 Bhaswiga asunde wakwe, alingane aje asundaga nishi umntu ulwali ni amuli nikama bhabhamanyizya na abhabhasimba.
MAR 1:23 Npepo umunda gwogwa ahali umuntu wahijila paputilepao ali ni pepo ichafu, naakholaihalo,
MAR 1:24 ayanga, “Tuli na henu ahabhombe nawe, uYesu wa Nazaleti? Uyinzile watwangamizye? Imenye uli winanu. Awe uuli mwaushe ulihovhe umwana wa Ngulubhi!”
MAR 1:25 U Yesu aidamila ipepo nayanje, “Bhuma na hufume muhati!”
MAR 1:26 Na iloho ibhibhi vhiihagwisya paka pazhi nafume wa mwene lwulwo shalila wisa utisana ya pamwanya.
MAR 1:27 Awantu bhunti wa haswingaa, bhahabhuzanya na shila muntu, “Ili lwenu? Izinsundo phaa ilwali amuli? Hata ipepo azyamlila ipepo zyope zimwiente haa!”
MAR 1:28 Inongwa afumilane numwene zyahenela uwakati bhobho mhati yikowa Galilaya.
MAR 1:29 Ishi lelo bada yafume huzi panyi poto, bhahinjila khaya wa Simoni nu uAndeleya bhali nu Yakobo nu Yohana.
MAR 1:30 Ishi ukhoyi wakwe uSimoni ali agonile bhinu alinihoma, mala yiyo bhahabhula uYesu ihali zyakwe.
MAR 1:31 Bhisho aheza, ahakata ukhata ukhono, na ubhisye humwanya; homa ihaleha wa mwene, handa wabhele.
MAR 1:32 Ulwebhe labhobho isanyapa liswile, bhaletelawa mwene abhali wa winu amabhasanyishilwe ni pepo.
MAR 1:33 Ikaya yundi ibhongana pandwimo mundwango.
MAR 1:34 Ahabhonwa bhundhi abhali bhanwinzeele ibhungo zinyinji, nakemele ipepo haga lehanga ipepo huje zhi yangaje pipo zwamenye.
MAR 1:35 Abhuha na sha pwii sana, wali shahuli siku habhala pasa pabhoneha alabhanga uhwo.
MAR 1:36 U Simoni na bhunti bhala abhalibhunthi bhahaza humwaze.
MAR 1:37 Bhahumwaga handa bhule, “Bhunti bha huwanza”
MAR 1:38 Abhabhula, “Salitubhale apanji nnzi yunti izyungula ili bhope oubho indumbilile. Shashisho inzile ipa.”
MAR 1:39 Ahala ajenda mugali ya mwunti, abha azyugula mnyipoto zyabho mwunti nakemele vhepele ipepo.
MAR 1:40 Uwikoma ahezawamwene. Ali ahulamba; ahafugamila amafugamo agabhala, “Khashele uwanza ugawezaa mbeshe mwinza.”
MAR 1:41 Abuwagwa ni phana uYesu hagolozya ukhono gwakwe nahukhate habhala, “Nina. Uwe safi.”
MAR 1:42 Hashe lwene ukoma bhuhamwepa, ahabhasa safi.
MAR 1:43 U Yesu ahasunda hukhali shilaga shaulilo, ahabhola,
MAR 1:44 “Uhakiswaje saga unyama muntu yaya hyanyunti, lelo shilaga, uwibhonesye wa puti, natowe dhabihu hunoyaje u Mose alajizye shasha awi yozye isha manyishe wane.”
MAR 1:45 Lelo abhala aubhula kila muntu na wenezye ineno sana hata uYesu haga ayendela abhale humujini huwa bhuushe. Hivho pa falanga nabhantu abha heza wamwene abha bhafume wunti.
MAR 2:1 Ahabhuya Kaperinaumu husiku indolwene ihuvhewa hujeinsiku nyishe lwene alihukhaya.
MAR 2:2 Abhantu wabhinji sana waliwha bhunghine pala ha gahali shinafani mwakwe atieleile ya pala mu ndwango, nu Yesu ahayanga izwo wa bhene.
MAR 2:3 Abhantu bhashe bhahinza wa mwene bhahata umuntu uwa polile; abhantu bhantenine.
MAR 2:4 Lelo pahakunwa hufishile alengane yau winji wantu bhahefwa bhasanyangulanya humwanya yinyuma pipo awantu walivhinji. Wakununwaga palitubhulailina bahiswa ishitandashila bhanyemulile umtu wa polile ali agonile.
MAR 2:5 Halola umwoyo gwa mbanago, Yesu alibhule mutu ulayapolile, “mwanawani, ibhimbi zwaho zihombashilwe.”
MAR 2:6 Lelo bhamo abhasimbi bhala khale bhawitosa humoyo gawo,
MAR 2:7 “Bhahayanga moyo gao awezizye bhule ayanje eshi? Aliligaa! Bhaga umuntu huje awa uweefe idhambi isipokuwa Ungulubhi mwene mwene yawezya?”
MAR 2:8 U Yesu awimenye amwo gwakwe izyabhasibhaga kati yabho. Abhabhula bhebho, “Lelo yenu mushebhabhisho moyo nginyu?
MAR 2:9 Lwenu iphuphusho sana aayanje wa muntu uwapolile, 'Aje imbibhi zyaho usajilwe' ama ayanje' Imelila, ega ishigonelo nishitala shaho, ujenda jee?'
MAR 2:10 Lelo ili bhapate amanye aje Mwana wa Muntu ani uwamuzi uwa huhoshele umuntu imbibhizyaho zihoshilwe ahabhulau uwahobhushile uwapolile,
MAR 2:11 “Ibhula awe, bhuha, ega ishigonelo shaho, ubhalaje huliwe.”
MAR 2:12 Ahemenlila phepo naweje ishigonelo shakwe, ahanje nda munyumba yashala muntu, esho bhundhi bhaswinga nahusalifwe Ungulubhi usisya, bhayanga “Shikulu, satulole inongwa na shiine.”
MAR 2:13 Ahashila andhele munshinje munshije idimi nikundi ilwa bhantu bhundhi bhala gawa mwene abhansunda.
MAR 2:14 Aliashizanya alola uLawi mwana Alfayo akhele isehemu yakusanya isongo abhula, ahaga “Nfhatanje.” Ahimenlhila nahudaje.
MAR 2:15 Uwakati uYesu alwangai ishale munyumba ya Lawi bhabhuganyaga na wantu imbibhi bhaha bha bhalwanga nu Yesu nasudwe bhakwe, phepo phipo bhalibhinji bhali bhahudaga.
MAR 2:16 Ulwo asimbi, abhahali, Mafalisayo pabhahalola uYesu alwa na mbibhi adhele bhahunganya isongo, bhahabhula asunda abhakwe, “Lelo yenu anabhunganya isengo nata nabhomba imbibhi?”
MAR 2:17 U Yesu pahuvha isho ayanga, “Ishi awantu ahali bhiza amhele gao hawaziwa husiphitali; bhatu abhinu tuu bhabha waza saga ize. Awanzea bhiza abhihaki, lelo abhibhi.”
MAR 2:18 Asudwa awa Yohana na Amafalisayo wali haga bhalwa. Wamo bhalila bhabhulile henu asundwa abha Yohana na mafalisayo habhaleha alwe, lelo asundwa bhaho bhala habha ngalila?
MAR 2:19 U Yesu ahabhula, “Ishi uwa tanjile hushahe agawezya agalilaje alwe uwakati bhobho umwani sha nabhene? Khashele umwani shikukukulu shali pepo nao? Lelo walwalwunthi umwa khashele bhalinabho hawezihujefunje.”
MAR 2:20 Insiku ziwhiza alo ubwana nashikulukulu paishila nhipopo bhaifunga.
MAR 2:21 Numo umuntu uwamama umwenda ukulu mumwenda upha mu mwenda ukulu kulu, pakashinzavhe shashe piletu, nazembushe uluwiwi afumine ni lwolizaduhane shibhibhi.
MAR 2:22 Numo umuntu uwaponya ihobwa ipha muvhilhelo ivilazu, lelo ihobwa sibhavibazulanye vhonti vibhele nai hombwa navivho vibhabazushe nateje. Amana gakwe, nhviha imbwa ephwa muvilo ivipha.”
MAR 2:23 Isiku limo uYesu ahashizanya pisiku ilwantu ye humagunda gamo gamo enya afundiwa bhakwe handa bhamo bhamo bhanda alwe amazhali ingingano.
MAR 2:24 Na Amafarisayo bhabhabhula, “Enya, yenu bhamba gasa ganghigo ahandhu hasa haho inje yitalatibu pisiku ituye Sabato?”
MAR 2:25 Habhabhula, “Sagamumanyile hala habhomba u Daudi pahazaga palini nizala— umwene nabhala ali nao umwene?
MAR 2:26 Ishahabho munyumba ya Ngulubhi ulwa Abiathari pali puti ugosi ahalwa ibhumnda ilwa bhiewelwa pitazi— ilwa shali shizyonga ishitalatibu wamuntu wabhodhi ila waputu—-apele ga vimo vimo wabhala bhali nabho?”
MAR 2:27 U Yesu ayaga, “Sabato ihabhombilwe kwa ajili ya mwanadamu, saga wamwanadamu kwa ajili ya Sabato.
MAR 2:28 Isho Umwana wa Adamu ni Bwana, hata wi Sabato.”
MAR 3:1 Antele ahijila muhati mwaputile muka mwali nu muntu uwikono ugwaupolile.
MAR 3:2 Abhantu bhamo bhadagaga muphiphi huje bhenye khashele azahuponyeisi kuli Sabato aje bhatake.
MAR 3:3 U Yesu ahabhula umuntu uwikhono ugwagupolile bhuha imilila pahati iyibhugaine.”
MAR 3:4 Ishihabhala abhantu, “Jee shinza abho iliza lwaponwe pisiku li Sabato au ilwa joje; ulwa sikeli, au gasa?” Gawaziwa aponwe agoje.
MAR 3:5 Bhamamhee ahabhenya wilwoyo asononoha pipoiliyaukhame wimoyo gao ahabhula muntu, “Goloswa ukhono gwaho.” Augoloswa nu Yesu aguponwa ukho gwakwe.
MAR 3:6 Mafalisayo bhafumahuzi bhahabhomba zimozimo nu Mahelode aziade umwene nahugoje.
MAR 3:7 Phipo uYesu, nasandwa bhakwe bhashila hunzumbi, ni mbhuga nhingosi iyabhantu ihabhadagaga ihafumaga hu Galilaya na Uyahudi
MAR 3:8 na fume Yelusalemu nafume indumaya na witanzi yi Yolodani na vhelane yitilo ni Sidoni, imbhuga ingosi, phihuvhwa shila hantu ahaga ahabhomba, bhabhiza wa mwene.
MAR 3:9 Ahabhamhula asundwa bhakwe atayalisye itulyi idodo kwa ajili ya mwene phipo imbhuga, ili bhangaje husoje.
MAR 3:10 Pipo abhapo mwaga winji, ilikila mntu uwali na malamba anihu hufishile ili apata manzwe.
MAR 3:11 Paphunti ipepo ichafu panwalolaga zywa gwaga paka panzi witanzilwa kwe nalile, bhayangaga, “Awa uli Mwana wa Ngulubhi”.
MAR 3:12 Abhamlila abhasimisizya agamde awubhushe.
MAR 3:13 Abhala pamwanya pigamba, abhakuda abhanzaga, mbahabhala wa mwene.
MAR 3:14 Abhasalula ilongo limo na bhantu bhabhili(abhakaga atumwa), ili bhambe palushimo nu mwene ili awe zywaje atume alu bhilile,
MAR 3:15 na bhamlila azywefhe iphepo.
MAR 3:16 Abhasalula ilongo nabhaji bhabhile uSimoni iyapela itawa ilya Petulo,
MAR 3:17 Yakobo umwana wa Zebedayo, nu Yohana uholo wakwe uYakobo, apelilwe itawa ilwahuje Bonagesi, ibho ni bhana awungume,
MAR 3:18 na Andeleya, Filipo, Bartholomayi, Mathayo, Tomaso, Yakobo, umwana wa Alfayo, thadato, Simoni Mkananayo,
MAR 3:19 na uYuda Iskariote, ambaye asambushila.
MAR 3:20 Nhipo ahabhala khaya, mbhuga ya bhantu bhahinzha bhunti nabho nanthele, saga bhahawezywa na hulwe imbumunda.
MAR 3:21 Abhana bhakwe pabhuvha ahapango mhiho, bhahabhala hukhute leloinjele, zyakwe zulushile, “Amerukwa na akili”.
MAR 3:22 Asimbi bhahenza afume mu Yelusalemu bhayanga, “Asangi ne Beelzebuli,” uwa tawali ni phepo awefwa amapepo”.
MAR 3:23 Yesu abhakuga wamwene nana yanje navho hushifwani, “Haga pauli uSetano aha mwefya Setano?
MAR 3:24 Utawala khaugabhanishe bhuwo, utawa uwo ungimilila.
MAR 3:25 Inyumba khigabhanishe yiyo i nyumba iyosigawezya awemelele.
MAR 3:26 Ngashele uSetano ainushe shinje ishashivhi yuyo na gabhanishe, hangi mivhila, na azabhe afishile hu mwisho wakwe.
MAR 3:27 Lelo nomo uwagawezya hata umo awinjile muhati nyumba iya muntu uwikone nawivhe ivintu vhakwe bila hupinye umwanikhone nasoti khasha abhunga nyaje ivya nyumba.
MAR 3:28 Lyoli imbabhula ibhivhi zyunthi izywa bhanabha bhantu zyai hobhoshelwa, naligo gawayanga,
MAR 3:29 lelo uwiliga uhala uzelu hagaihoshe lwa na mwaha anu lozi uwimbivhih uwawila nawila.”
MAR 3:30 Yesu alilisema hili kwa sababu walikuwa wakisema, “Ana roho chafu”.
MAR 3:31 Pepo anyina naholo bhakwe bhahenza na bhemelele huzi. Bhahatuma umuntu, hukuje.
MAR 3:32 Abhantu bhali bhinji bhalipepe numwene bhabhula, “unyina waho naholo bhaho bhali hunzi, bhahu waza awe”.
MAR 3:33 Abhanjibula, “Yu nanu inyina wani na holo bhani?”
MAR 3:34 Ahabhenya bhali bhakhele bhazyungulele, ahayanga, “Enya, ibha bhamaibhani na holo bhani!
MAR 3:35 Ngunthi mapezi gakwe Unguluvhi, umuntu uyo holo wani, nanyirumbu wani na yumayi wani.”
MAR 4:1 Ahanda abha manyizywe mu shinjhe izhumbi. Ni bhunga ingosi ihubhungana ihazyhungula, ahinjila muhati inyitu li musumbi, ahakhala. Ibhuga yunthi ihali izywungulile mushinje munsumbi mu fukweni.
MAR 4:2 Abhamanyizhwa inongwa inyinji huvifwani, ayanga wa bhene hunsundo zyakwe.
MAR 4:3 Uvhi ikopba ihabhalile atote.
MAR 4:4 Pali atota, zimo imbeyu zyalagala mwidala, inyonyizywahinza zywalya.
MAR 4:5 Imbeyu zimo zywalaga mumwala, pasipali ninzhi inyinji iyaye. Mara zikanyauka, kwa sababu hazikuwa na udongo wakutosha.
MAR 4:6 Lelo isanya palyahatukula, zywatenguha, lelo pheposazywali na kholo zyahumaa.
MAR 4:7 Imbeyu zimo zywalagala pahati pamivhwa. Amivhwagazi puta, saga zhwasiga indundu zywa zwunthi.
MAR 4:8 Imbeyu izwenje zhwalagala munzhi inyinza zhwapa indundu pazi wonjelela, zimo zihasagala along gatatu sana, zimo malogo tanda, na zimo malogo mia.”
MAR 4:9 Ahayanga, “Wabhunti uwi makutu agahuvhwe, naayuvhaje!”
MAR 4:10 U Yesu pahavha mwene, bhala habha phiphi nu mwene bhala ilongo nabhantu bhantu bhahabhuzywa ehusu ivifwani.
MAR 4:11 Ahayanga wavhene, “Amwe mpewilwe utawala uwa Nguluvhi. Lelo bhala abhalihunzi shila hatu wayanje nivifwani, ili gawenya, ena wenya,
MAR 4:12 lelo hawenya, phepo pahuvhwa, lelo sahuvhwa wawenya, lelo sawenya wala hawe lewa nahuvhe, lelo gabhe bhagaluhananga Ungulubhi abhahoshelanga.”
MAR 4:13 Ahayanga wabhene, “Ishi samuwelewa ivifwani ivhi? Mugawezwa bhuli awelewe ifwani ivhinje?
MAR 4:14 Ikopha itotile izyo.
MAR 4:15 Lelo bhala bhalagala mushinjhe mwidala, papizywa lwatotilwe. Pala pabhahuvha, pepo uSetano ahiza naweje izywo lila lwatotilwe muhati yao.
MAR 4:16 Na bhamo bhala bhatwa mumwala palyuvha izywa, shalubhilo shalulo bhalipola huwaushe.
MAR 4:17 Sabhanakholo gangunthi muhahati yao, lelo vhajimba humuda ufupi. Amayimba na yushe wao paviweza hunongwa yizyo vhafiha bhambumila.
MAR 4:18 Bhamo vhala bhatotwa kati yimivha bhahuvha izywo,
MAR 4:19 lelo ayimba agamunzhi akhopelwe nishuma nivinyonya zwa mambo aganji, huhuwaingia nasupe izywo na limenwa apape amadudu.
MAR 4:20 Na bhawili abhabhatotilwe munzhi inyinza. Bhalwuvha izywo nali pashele bhapapa amandundu: bhamo malongo gatatu bhamo malongo tanda bhamo mia moja.”
MAR 4:21 U Yesu abhambula, “Je unaleta ta ndani ya nyumba nakuweka panzhi ishitundu, au pansi pashitala? Uleta muhati na bhishe pamwanya pakinara.
MAR 4:22 Na hami hahabhajile afise asahagabhoneha, nahakuna siri iyasiga abhapazeru.
MAR 4:23 Khawele uwimakutu gahuvhe ayuvhwaje!”
MAR 4:24 Akawaambia, “Mubhanje maso na hala amuhuvhwa, alingane ishipimo shila ishampima ndio shisho shamwapimilwa shayonjelezewa hulimwe.
MAR 4:25 Afutane aje uhula uwanao ayejelela vinji tee, ulakwasanao afume wamwe ene vyayegwa navila uvya navyo.”
MAR 4:26 Ayanga, “Utawala uwa Ngulubhi ufananasiwa nu muntu uwa vyala imbeyu mwilongo.
MAR 4:27 Pahagona adamula na shabwi imbeyu zyatiuha nakule, ikiwa haga hamanya shifumile.
MAR 4:28 Izhi ifumia imbeyu yiiyo asoti amatundu baada yipo uwezya, nanthele imbeyu izyazikhomile.
MAR 4:29 Lelo imbeyu ya payakho ma atwala inhengo, pipo avune hufishile.”
MAR 4:30 Ayaanga, “Tufwananiswe utawala wa Ngulubhi nahanthushi, au tumile hanthuuli amatumile hanthu uwuli awelezyezye?
MAR 4:31 Ili nishi imbeyu yiladai, lelo pihatotwaga hali hadodo sana kuko imbeyu zywunthi munshi.
MAR 4:32 Hata lula ulwitothilwe igosi sana kuliko vhu nthi ivha vitotilwe mubusitani ivheha inzamba ingosi nazi inyenji ziwezya akhale nabheshe ivhansu ali nganaje inzunda yakwe.”
MAR 4:33 Amafano aminji amanyizywe ayanjile inongwa wa bhene, shinza ishabhawezizye awelewe,
MAR 4:34 haga ayangaga anabho bila fwano. Lelo lula ulimwene, ahabha bhula asundwa bhakwe shila hantu.
MAR 4:35 Lelo isiku ilwo ulwe vhela pawafishile, ayanga wabhene,
MAR 4:36 “Sanli upande uwa bhili”. Pipo bhaileha ibhuga, bhahamwenga uYesu, uwakati bhuwo ahavha mwituli. Amatuli aganji galipandwimo numwene.
MAR 4:37 Ihala ihali ihavhulungwe amawimbi gahijilaga muhati mwintuli na ituli nagamimile.
MAR 4:38 Lelo uYesu yuyo alikuwa kwenye shetri, ali agonelile mwisoho. Bhahadamusya, bhayanga, “Wamwalimo, hangu saga ati tufwa?”
MAR 4:39 Abhuha audamila ihala aibhula inzumbi, '“Ibhe shinza, huwaushe”. Ihala ihaleha, wahavha miee sana.
MAR 4:40 Ayanga wa bhene, “Yenu mu hwogopa? Samulinima bado?”
MAR 4:41 Bhahabha nihofu moyo gabho bhayangana vhene kwa vhene, “Unu yunanu antele, hata ihula ihumwogopa?”.
MAR 5:1 Bhabhiza upande uwinje uwinsumbi ukowa ungwa hu Gelasi
MAR 5:2 Gafula uwakati uYesu afumaga hunzhi iyituli, umuntu uwipepi ichafu anhiza wa mwene afume wazili inghugwa.
MAR 5:3 Muntu uyo akhalaga wazili inghughwa. Numo untu uwa zigaga zaidi, numo hata hu manyololo.
MAR 5:4 Apinyilwe ahabhalilo ahinji apinyilwe namanyololo. Alikata minyololo naphingo adadulaga ipbingo na gamanyololo gambuduhaga. Na numo uwanga nikhone nahu mene.
MAR 5:5 Usiku nusanya shali hu ngungwa na huagamba, alilaga na wivhale na mawe amakhali.
MAR 5:6 Pahalola uYesu litali, anyililile wa mwene naundame witazi wa mwene.
MAR 5:7 Ahalila usauti igozi, “Uwaza ibhombele yenu, uYesu, Umwana wa Ngulubhi uwali Humwanya sana? Ihuwiniha wa Ngulubhi yuyo, ungandedavhwe.”
MAR 5:8 Pipo ali abholile, “Huje ufume mwa muntu bhunu, awe wipepo imbivhi.”
MAR 5:9 Wope abhuzya, “Itawa lwaho wi nanu?” Wope ajibule, “Itawa lwani Legion, pipo tuli bhinji.”
MAR 5:10 Amwiniha sana sana angande hutwale hunzi yikowa.
MAR 5:11 Ishi ikundi igosi ilinguluvhe zywa lwanga pamwanya paha gamba,
MAR 5:12 nabha mwiniha, bhayanga, “Tutume huguluvhe; tinjile muhati yavho.”
MAR 5:13 Bhalisiwa; aroho achafu bhahafuma nawinjile muhati mungulivhi, bhape bhahanyilapanzipa gamba paka munsumbi zyabhezya afishe elufu zibhili bhatumbushila munzumbi.
MAR 5:14 Na bhala bhali bhaziliswa igumi bhatumbaga nafumine italifa abafumile ikhaya ni nsi pipo bhuhafwa abhale awenye ahahafumile.
MAR 5:15 Epo bhahinza wa Yesu na bhahalola umuntu uwayinjililwe namapepo—uwali ni jeshi—akhele panzi, bhakwatizye, abhoneha huhakili zyakwa halali bhope bhahogopa.
MAR 5:16 Bhala bhalole hafumile wa muntu uwa hinjililwe ni pepo bhahabhula hafumile wa mwene ahafumile ahusu inguluvhi.
MAR 5:17 Bhope bhada humwinishe ayepe mkoa gwao.
MAR 5:18 Pali pawinjila muhati mwintoli umuntu uwahinjililwe nipepo amwiniha huje bha shilaje bhudhi nu mwene.
MAR 5:19 Lelo haga amwitishile, lelo habhala, “Shilaga hunumba yaho nawabhantu bhao na bhabhule uwabhombile Bwana, iphana ilowapile.”
MAR 5:20 Isho ahashila atanganza amambo amagosi uYesu agabhombile wamwene hu Dekapoli, ula muntu aswijile.
MAR 5:21 Umuda uYesu palobhoa upande uwinje muhati mwituli ibhunga inyinji ihazywungulaga pati mushinje munsumbi.
MAR 5:22 Uumo uwali longozi wasinagogi, ahitwaga Yailo, ahizile, pali alole, angwile pamagaga agamwene.
MAR 5:23 Amwinishe sana amwiniha sana sana, ayanga, “Ulindu wani udodo abhezywa afwe. Ihulamba unyinze ubhishe amakhono pamwene apate ihafya hulamba.”
MAR 5:24 Isho habhala nawo na ibhuga ingosi sana ihada gana bhavhelaga mpepe vhahunzwungula.
MAR 5:25 Wali nu shi uli afuma ama danda amaha ilongo limo na maha gavhili.
MAR 5:26 Alavhile sana waganga abhinji atumila kila hatu anaho hutaisho sashahavha na hamo. Hata hivyo hakusaidika kwa chochote, lelo pipo ali ihali mbivhi.
MAR 5:27 Ahuvwa ihali huje uYesu. Aheza khosi wa mwene na pajendaga muhati mubhuga, apala zwa umwenda gwakwe.
MAR 5:28 Pipo alyanjile, “Khanapela nvuzywa amenda agakwe lwe, izavhe mwumi.”
MAR 5:29 Pahakhata, afume wakwe idanda iha leha awiyuvwa hula alavhewakwe huleha afume humalabha gakwe.
MAR 5:30 Mala Yesu agundua ndani yake mwenyewe huje ikhone lwa fuma. Agaluhana uhu nuhu mu phuga mwa bhantu navhuzye, “Yunanu uwagusa umwenda gwani?”
MAR 5:31 Asudwa bhakwe bhabhulile ulola ibhunga izywungulile nawe uyiga 'Yu nanu uwa ngusa?”'
MAR 5:32 Lelo uYesu ahenya wondi wondi uwa bhombileili.
MAR 5:33 Ushi, palole ilili fumile afume wa mwene ahogopa nateteme. Aheza nagwe pansi witazi lwakwe nahu bhute izywaziwili zyunti.
MAR 5:34 Ayanga wa mwene, “Lendu, awamini waho huponizywe avhemwumi. Shilaga hu himani upone uponywe afume huvhinu waho.”
MAR 5:35 Pali aliayanga, bhamo avhatu bhahinza afume walongozi uwi Sinagogi, bhayangaga, “Ulindu waho afwile. Henu uhumbula umwalimo?”
MAR 5:36 U Yesu pahuvha avhyanga, ahabhula ulongozi uwi Sinagogi, “Unganje awogope. Aminiangatu.”
MAR 5:37 Haga alusu yayunti alongozanye nawo, ila uPetulo, uYakobo, nu Yohana, uholo wakwe Yakobo.
MAR 5:38 Bhahiza khaya walongozi wi Sinagogi wope ahalola ivhujo akhole sana nalile.
MAR 5:39 Pahinza khaya, abhabhulile, “Henu musiliha antele yenu mlila? Umwahaga afwile ila agonile.”
MAR 5:40 Bhaseshile, lelo umwene, abhafumya huzi, amwega uYisu wa mwana nunyina nabhala bhabhali palishimo numwene, ahijila muhati mwali umwana.
MAR 5:41 Ahega ukhono ugwa mwana ahabhula, “Talitha koum,” ambayo huwayanje, “Lindu umwana bhuha.”
MAR 5:42 Umda ufupi umwana adamula na ajende (pipo alina maha ilogo limo naganji gavhili).
MAR 5:43 Gafula bhahakhatwa nushanga ougosi. Numo yayunthi uyiwaziwa amanye wili. Abha bhula peli ulendu ula ishalye.
MAR 6:1 Na ahepa ipo nabhale humuji ni wabho asundwa abhakwe bhahadaga.
MAR 6:2 Ulutuyo palwahafiha, ali anza amanyizywe mwi Sinagogi. Abhantu abhinji bhahamuvhaga. Naswijiziwe bhahayaga, “Azwajile wihiizi izywa manyizwa?” “Liphana ashi ili ilwapewilwe?” “Abhomba amanjele iga humakhono gakwe?”
MAR 6:3 “Ishi unu sawa selemala, umwana wa Maria uholo wabho aYakobo, Yose, Yuda na Simoni? Je adada bhakwe tukhalanabho mumu nanthi?” Hakufulaisha nu Yesu.
MAR 6:4 U Yesu abhabhula, “Ukuwa haga akosa awogopwe, ilakati yikhaya yakwe na mubhamo muholo bhakwe na munyumba mwakwe.”
MAR 6:5 Hagawezyaga abhombe amanjele epo, lelo abheha amakhono abhini bhashe abhaponwa.
MAR 6:6 Ahaswiga sana pasaga wamini wabho. Ajendelela ikhaya izywapalamani ahamanyizya.
MAR 6:7 Ahabha kuga asudwa bhakwe ilongo limo nabhantu bhabhili ahanda atume bhabhili bhabhili. Apela amulaka juu yipepo ichafu,
MAR 6:8 na bhamulile bhaanganje aweje hahunti pabhajenda ila ulusansotu bhanganda aweje ibumunda wala ifhulushi wala ihela pahosi;
MAR 6:9 lelo bhakwataje ishilato, lelo siyo amakanzu gabhili.
MAR 6:10 Ahabhabhula, “Nyumba yayundti iyamunza winjile, khalanji upa pamwaishila.
MAR 6:11 Ikhaya yayundti iyasi habhejela wala abhuvhe, shilaji pabhene, kunyu ntaji amakundi agamagaga genyu, bhawiloleje abene.”
MAR 6:12 Nabhope bhahashila bhatangazwa abhantu bhalambaje imbivhi zyabho.
MAR 6:13 Bhanyi ipepo inyinji, na bhapahaga amafuta abhinu bhaponaga.
MAR 6:14 Utawala uHalode pahuvhwa ingo, afutane itawa lwa Yesu lwamanyishe sana. Bhamo bhayanga, “U Yohana uyabhozwa azyushile pipo isho inkuniimaanjele ibhomba imbombo mhati yakwe.”
MAR 6:15 Bhamo bhahayanga huje, “Unu yu Eliya,” Lelo bhamo bhayanga, “Unu yukuwa, uwali nishi bhala akuwa abhimandi.”
MAR 6:16 Lelo uHalode pahuvhaigo ahayanga, “Ahaga uYohana, uwihandumule itwe azywushile.”
MAR 6:17 Lelo Helode yuyo alajizwe huje uYohana akhatwe ahapinya nahubhishe mwigeleza hunongwa Herodia (ushi wa kuluwakwe Filipo) pipo lelo umwene ali agojile.
MAR 6:18 Lelo uYohana ali abhulile uHerode, “Sagashizha aweje ushi uwa khulubho.”
MAR 6:19 Lelo uHerodia ahanda huvhitililwe na azaga ahugoje, lelo haga awezizwe,
MAR 6:20 lelo uHerode amwogupe uYohana; amenye muntu wana lwoli nzhelu ahaleha huwinza, pahendelela hu mwuvhe. Asulumana sana lelo ahamoga hutejelezywe.
MAR 6:21 Po uhafi uwakati uwene pabhelaga isiku ilwa papwe Herode abhandalila atalamu abhakwe ishelehe, na adadamu nalongozi ami Galialaya.
MAR 6:22 Phipo ulendu wa Herodia ahinjila nacheze witazi wabhene, afulaiswa uHarode na jenyu abhakhile uwakati uwishalwe shalwevhela. Epo utawala abhula ulendu, “Undavhe hahondti uwaza nani izahupele.”
MAR 6:23 Alapilizya huje, hahudi hubha ndavhe, izahupele, ahata inusu iyitala wani.”
MAR 6:24 Afuma huzi avhuzya anyina wakwe, “Indavhe yenu?” Abhula, “Itwe ilwa Yohana uwa Wonza.”
MAR 6:25 Shisho ahinjila watawala ahanda ayanje, “Iwaza muhati musahani, itwe lwa Yohana uyawozwa.”
MAR 6:26 Utawala aswiga sana, lelo ululapo ulwalapile na ajenyi, haga hawezywa hukhanile ilwa labhile.
MAR 6:27 Isho, mutawala ahatuma asinjala abha gulaga abhalajizywe abhale alilete itwelwa yahanaulizi abhatile adumule wijela.
MAR 6:28 Ahaleta itwe kwenye sahani na hupele ulindu ulindu apela unyina wakwe.
MAR 6:29 Asundwa bhakwe pabha huvha isho, bhahabhala abhale aweje ubhilyi gwakwe bhala asywile hunghugwa.
MAR 6:30 Atumwa bha bhungana witazi wa Yesu, bhabhula gunthi agabhombile na gabhamanyizyaga.
MAR 6:31 Wope abhabhula, “Izaji mwemwe pasili tutuye hashe.” Abhantu abhinji bhali bhahweza nashile wala habhapata inafusi iyolye.
MAR 6:32 Bhinjila mumashuwa bhala amahali pasili bhene.
MAR 6:33 Lelo bhahabha lola pabhashila bhahabhamanya abhahanyila lwimagaga upaka humiji guthi, bhope bhafiha shavhasili abhene.
MAR 6:34 Pahafiha pwani, bhalola ibhuga ingosi bhahabhasajila, pipo bhali nishi ingole izwasazili nu ndimii. Ahanda abha manyizye amambo aminji.
MAR 6:35 Abhazyo pahedelela sana, asudwa abhahemwizila bhaha bhula,”Ipa tuli mahali pisili umuda gubhalile.
MAR 6:36 Ubhalaje bhashilaje aweze ishalye humiji hujiji ivipipi.”
MAR 6:37 Lelo abhajibhula ayanga, “Bhapeli amwe ishalye.” Tugawezwa awepe nakale amabumunda angisamani na mimbili tubhapele hahalye?”
MAR 6:38 Ahabhabhula,” Muna amabumunda galinga? Mubhale mwenye.” pabhavhaga bhahabhula, “Amabumunda gasanu ni samaji nsivhile.”
MAR 6:39 Bhahamuliswa abhantu bhakhale mumasole amolo.
MAR 6:40 Bhaha khazywa makundi; makundi mamia na amhamsini.
MAR 6:41 Ahenga amabumunda gasanu na samaki zibhili, na wenye humwanya, ahasanya aha pela asudwa waweke mbele ya umati. Bhabhishe nasamaki zibhili, na zitatu wabhathu bhuthi.
MAR 6:42 Bhahalya bhuthi bhayile.
MAR 6:43 Bhabhunganya amabumuda sangile, Vyaha mema ivitundu vhibhele, nivindumushila ivisamaki.
MAR 6:44 Bhali alume elufuzisanu abhalile amabunda.
MAR 6:45 Abhabhula huje bhande mashua bhabhale isemu iyinji, Bethsaida, uwakati abhalaga ulubhungano.
MAR 6:46 Pabha habha bhashila, abhala wi gamba alavhe.
MAR 6:47 Pawahahavha shalyevhela na mashua yabho ulwo ili pahati pazhumbi alimwene panzi inyumu.
MAR 6:48 Ahalola bhatamiwa akhome makasiapipo ihala ihapingaga. Pahuhabha hupambazuha nashaphii abha bhalila, ajendaga amizi ahazaga ashizanye.
MAR 6:49 Lelo pahalola ajenda amwanya iyimeze, bhapata uwasi wasi bhagazimu hata bhakhola.
MAR 6:50 pipo bhahalola vhahijila ishaka. Ahagana yanje anabho abhabhula, “Mubhanje bhadadamu! nene! Mganje abhe nihofu.”
MAR 6:51 Ahinjila muhati mumashua, na ihala ihaleha avungume na haswiga kabisa.
MAR 6:52 Haga bhahelewa imana iyagala amabumunda. Injele zhwabho zyalidodo.
MAR 6:53 Bhope pali bhaloushe isyila bhafiha insi ya Genesareti mashua ikati nanga.
MAR 6:54 Pabhahaguma huzi iye mashua, bhahatabula.
MAR 6:55 Bhahanyila atangazwe mkowa gwundhi bhahandu abhalete avhinu mzego mzega, shila pahuvhaga huje awiza.
MAR 6:56 Pundi pahinjilaga huvijiji, au mumiji, au munzhi, bhabhihaga avhinu pasoko, bhalamba huje bhapala mazhwaje amenda gakwe. Na bhundti abhakhete bhaponile.
MAR 7:1 Mafalisayo nabhamo asimbi ambao bhafumila hu Yelusalemu bhahabhungana huzhwongule umwene.
MAR 7:2 Bha hulolie bhamobhamo huje asunda bhakwe bhalile ibumunda humakhono amachafu; saga gahoziwe.
MAR 7:3 (wa Mafalisayo na Yahudi bhundti sabhalya upaka bhozizye amakhono gao shishinza; bhakhatila utamanduni agosibhabho. Huwakati
MAR 7:4 Amafalisayo pabhabhuya afume mahali pasoko, sabhalya paka bhoje kwanza na huli ishelia zimo zimo abhuzywo bhazida gakabisa, ikiwa abhozye ivikombe, amafulila, ivhombo ivhishaba, na hata amatengo agatuniha uwakati uwishalye.)
MAR 7:5 Amafalisayo na asimbi bhalihubhuzye uYesu, “Kwa nini asudwa bhaho sabhakhala afatane nagosi, bhao bhalwaibunda nabila asungusule amakhono?”
MAR 7:6 Lelo umwene ahabhabhabhula, “Isaya ahakuwashinza huje amwe mulibhivhi, asimba, 'Aje abhantu ibha bhanogopa humalo mu golo, lelo amoyo ga bho gali hutaloi nani.
MAR 7:7 Bhabhombela inyiputoizywaswazya zyizyo izyasazi welewelewewa sazimuhimu bhamanyiziwa italabu izywa bhanadamu gabha poshala agao.'
MAR 7:8 Muleshile iatalatibu izywa Nguluvhi namuzywejile izishibinadamu ugatwaposhile.”
MAR 7:9 Ahayanga wa bhene muzikhanile amuli izwa Nguluvhi ishilaisi ili muziute izyinyu!
MAR 7:10 Lelo pipo uMose ayajile, umwogopaje udada waho nunyina waho,' uwayanga amavhivhi wa dada au wamai wakwe lywoli aifwa.'
MAR 7:11 Lelo amwe, 'muyanga huje umuntu akhayanga wadada wakwe au mai, “Usada gwagwunti gula ugwa hunda mwe jelela je afume hulini iyo mbuta yinyiputo,”' (ubho wayanje huje ifumile wa Ngulubhi')
MAR 7:12 isho ahuruhusu abhombe ijambo lwa lwunti alibhombe kwaajili ya dada au ya mai wakwe.
MAR 7:13 Muyi bheha amuli Nguluvhi huje yilwene alete inyiho zywinyu. Na mambo aminji aga gali isho angamuomba.”
MAR 7:14 Abhakujile amakutano andthele nabhabhule, “Huje munuvhaje ane, amwe mwindhe, namu nelewe.
MAR 7:15 Nahamo hahunti huziwa muntu hahuchafula mtu kiingiapo kwake. Bali ni kile kimtokacho mtu ndicho kimchafuacho.
MAR 7:16 (Azingatile: usitali ugu, “khamba umuntu amakutu agahuvhwe ayuvhaaje” nashimo munakili izihalyi).
MAR 7:17 U Yesu ahagaleha amakutano abhala khaya, asundwe bhahabhuzwa ufwano ugwo.
MAR 7:18 U Yesu ahayanga, “Namwe nantele saga muwelewa? Samulola hahunti ahahumwinjila umuntu hawezwa huchafule,
MAR 7:19 pipo sahabhala huwoyo gwakwe, lelo ishashiwinjila muvhanda vhakwe shishizanya nabhale hucho.” Hu ma elezo iga uYesu abhiha ivhalwe vhunti abhe vinza.
MAR 7:20 Ayanjile, “Shila isha shihufuma umuntu shashi huchafula.
MAR 7:21 Pipo hafuma muhati mwa muntu, huzihu mwoyo gafuma amawazo amachafu, akwesane, uwibha, agoje,
MAR 7:22 amabhibhi iga gunti hutamani ishibhibhi, ubhibhi uwaswovhe, akwesane, uwivu aphuyile, awivune, nulema.
MAR 7:23 Amabhibhi iga gunti gafuma muhati, gaga huchafula umuntu.”
MAR 7:24 Abhuha afume pala nashile ukowa wa Tiro na Sidoni. Ahainjila muhanti haga ahazaga umuntu yayundhe amanyaje huje aliipo, lelo haga ihazehana hufise.
MAR 7:25 Lelo ghafla ushi, ula umwana wakwe udodo ani roho ichafu, ahuvha ihabali hakwe, ahiza, naha gwa magaga agakwe.
MAR 7:26 Ushi uyo Muyunani, wikambela ilwa Kifoeniki. Alambile umwene anyizhwe ipo afume wa lyindu wakwe.
MAR 7:27 U Yesu ahabhula ushi, “Bhateshe abhana bhaliziwaje huje sashili aweje ibumunda ilwabhana azitajile ibwa.”
MAR 7:28 Lelo ushi ajibule nayanje, “Ena Bwana, ibwa panzi yimeza ivhavhi sagala ivhalye vha bhana.”
MAR 7:29 Abhula, “Ahuje pepo uyanjile ishi, uli mwaushe ashile. Iphepo ifumile ulindu waho.”
MAR 7:30 Ushi ahabhuya khaya yakwe ahamwaga ulindu wakwe agonile pashitala, iphepo ali afumile.
MAR 7:31 U Yesu afumile inje yikowa wa Tiro na ashizanije Sidoni abhalile hunsumbi ya Galilaya pakakanda ya Dikapolisi.
MAR 7:32 Bhahaleta umuntu uya sahuvha uyasawezya ayanje shishiza, bhalambile uYesu huje abhishe amakhono pamwanya yakwe.
MAR 7:33 Ahumwefwa hunzhi ikundi shisili abhiha inyovhe makutu gakwe, bada ya aswe amate apala manzywa ulumili lyakwe.
MAR 7:34 Ahenyizhwe humwanya amaso ahutuya na hubhule, “Efata,” isuo wa huyanje “fuguha!”
MAR 7:35 Umuda gwagula amakutu gahiguha, nahala ahazijile awezywa ayanjeshishinza.
MAR 7:36 Abhamulila bhaganje hubhele umuntu wabhunti. Lelo pali abhamulila bhanje hubhule umuntu pabha zidile ayanje ibhahalileizyo zinyijii.
MAR 7:37 Lyoli bhashijizhiwe, nayanje, “Abhombile shila hantu shishinza. Hata abhombile abhasa bhahuvha amakutu ahuvhe na bhabubu ayanje.”
MAR 8:1 Lele inzhiku izyo, paliiibuga ingosi, salinishalwe. U Yesu abhakuga asundwa bhakwe ahabhula,
MAR 8:2 “Injisajila ibuga ini bhendelile abhe nani inzhiku zitatu na sani shalye.
MAR 8:3 Khimba nyaphanye huje bhabhuye huzinyumba zyabho bila alye bhagazimila mwidala nizala. Mhati yabho bhamo bhafuma hutali sana.”
MAR 8:4 Asundwa bhakwe bhajibula, “Tubhagaje wii amabumunda agabhaye bhutnthi ibha nabha kutizye abhantu ibha ineo ilyaleshilye?”
MAR 8:5 Ahabhabhuzya, “mulini vipande vhilinga ivhimabumunda?” Bhayanga, “Saba.”
MAR 8:6 Awamulila ibhuga bhakhale panzi. Ahega amabumunda saba, ahasalifya Ungulubhi, na budulanye. Abhapela asunda bhakwe bhagabhishe witanzi lyabho, bhahagahiha witanzi libhuga.
MAR 8:7 Bhope bhali ni samaki zindodo nyishe, na bada yahusalifye, abhamulila asudwa bhakwe bhaganyiivhi vhope.
MAR 8:8 Na bhahalya naye. Nabhabhunganya ipande ivhisangele ivitundu, ivigasi saba.
MAR 8:9 Bhelega abhantu elufu zine. Aheleha bhashalaje.
