MAR 8:10 Mara ahinjila mashua nasundwa bhakwe, nabhashila katika ukanda wa Dalmanuta.
MAR 8:11 Amafalisayo bhafumahuzina wande adalisanye nawo. Bhazaga ishimanyilo afume humwanya, bhajelaga.
MAR 8:12 Asebha sana mmwoyo gwakwe ayanga, “Yenu ishizazi ishi shiwaza imanyilo? Imbabhula amwe lyoli, na shimo ishimanyilo ishashaifuma hushi zazi ishi.”
MAR 8:13 Ipo ahambaleha, ahinjila muhati mmashua anthele ahashila awelekele upauwenje.
MAR 8:14 Umuda ugwo asudwa bhahi wilwe aweje amabumunda. Sagabhali nishipande shashundhi ishibumunda hata shimo ishali mashua.
MAR 8:15 Abhonya hayanje, “Mubhanje maso na witunze ishilela aluzu iya Mafalisayo na haluzu aHarode.
MAR 8:16 Asundwa bhayangana bhene wabhene, “Pipo sagatuli namabumunda.”
MAR 8:17 U Yesu ahamanya ili nabhabhula, “Yenu muyangana pasamuli namabumunda? Hamuminye bado? Hagamuwelewa? Amoyo ginyu mapupusu?
MAR 8:18 Amaso hamulola? Munakutu, sagamuhuvhwa? Hagaamukumbuha?
MAR 8:19 Pihagabhaya amabumunda gasanu wa bhantu elufu zisanu, mwahejile ivitundu vhilyinga ivhavimemile amabumunda?” Bhahajibula “ilongo navhele.”
MAR 8:20 Pahagabhanya amabumunda saba huelufu ine, muhega ivitundu vhilinga?”
MAR 8:21 Bhahayanga, “Saba.” Ahabhabhula, “Bado haga muwelewa?”
MAR 8:22 Bhajiza Bethsaida. Abhantu ibho bhahuleta wa Yesu umuntu uwafyile amaso bhahalamba uYesu akhate.
MAR 8:23 U Yesu ahukhata nukhano ola uwafyile amaso nahulongole huzi ishijiji ahaswa amante pamwanya yimaso nagolosye amakhono pamwanya yakwe, ahabhuzwa, “Uhalola hahunte?”
MAR 8:24 Ahenyizywe humwanya nayanje, “Imbalola abhantu bhabhoneha nishi amapishi gajenda.”
MAR 8:25 Ipo ahagolosya amakono gakwe pa mwanay iyimaso gakwe, umuntu ola gafunguha amaso gakwe, ahalola nanhele, ahalola shilahandu shishiza.
MAR 8:26 U Yesu ahaleha ashila akhaya yakwe nahabhula, “Unganje aeinjile hujini.”
MAR 8:27 U Yesu ashila nasundwa bhakwe huvijiji ivha Kaiseria ya Filipi. Bhali mwidala abhabhuzwa asundwa, “Abhantu bhayiga ni nanu?”
MAR 8:28 Bhahajibula bhahayanag, “Yohana uwabhozwa. Bhamo bhayanga, 'Eliya' na bhamo, 'Muntu umo Nakuwa.”
MAR 8:29 Ahabhabhuzwa, “Lelo amwe muiga ane ninanu?” Petulo ahabhula, “Awe wi Kristi.”
MAR 8:30 U Yesu abhula bhanje hibhule umuntu yayunti uwahusu umwene.
MAR 8:31 Ahanda abhamanyinzye huje umwene Mwana wa Adamu lazima alavhe humambo aminji, ayikanwa nalongozi na achungaji agosi nasimbi, na gagwe bada yinsiku zitatu aizyuuha.
MAR 8:32 Aliyanjile iga apazelu. Epo uPetulo ahamwega paka pashinje anda hudamile.
MAR 8:33 Lelo uYesu agaluhana na bhenye asundwa bhakwe na ahadamila uPetulo nayanje, “Sahinzanya huhosi yane Setano! Haga usaga amambo aga Ngulubhi, ila amambo agabhantu.”
MAR 8:34 Ipo ahakuga ibuga nabhasundwa abhakwe palishimo, nabhabhule, “Kama huli umuntu uya wanza afwuate awikhane nyuyo, ayegaje ishikhovhehanyo shakwe na afhunte.
MAR 8:35 Wahuje wabhunti uya wanza awokole amaisha gakwe aigatenzwa nauyantezywa amaisha gakwe kwa ajili ya lini na kwa ajili izyo ayokola.
MAR 8:36 Aipata yenu umuntu khapate inzhi yunthi wa pante ihasala akahle wakwe?
MAR 8:37 Umuntu agawezya afumwe yenu badala yaifumwe ubhumi wakwe?
MAR 8:38 Uwaindolela inshoni ninogwa zywani ishizazi ishinishi zazi ishabhivhivhi, Umwana wa Adamu ayilolela inshoni paiyinza nubhutawala uwa dada wakwe palishimo naa wandumi azelu.
MAR 9:1 Ayanjile wabhene, “Lwoliiyanga hulimwi bhawili abhanthu abhabhimilile epha ambao hagabhaibhoja ufye shausilye utawala uwa Ngulubhi pawayinza wikhone.”
MAR 9:2 Na bada yinshikutanda, uYesu abhega aPetulo, Yakobo na Yohana palishimo numwene wigamba, bhene. Ndipo ahandile agaluhane mbele yao.
MAR 9:3 Amenda gakwe gaga luhana gana amulishe alabhe sana nabhe mazelu zaidi uzeluuwasa bhulavha wabhonthi munthi.
MAR 9:4 Phepo aEliya pamoja nu Mose bhahafumila witazi lwabho, bhali bhayanga nu Yesu.
MAR 9:5 U Petulo ajibula uYesu, “Umwalimo, shinza ati akhale epa, shimo shaliwe, shimo kwa ajili ya Mose na isha mwabhosha Eliya.”
MAR 9:6 (Haga amenye ahawaziwa ayanje, bhahogopha sana.)
MAR 9:7 Ibhingo lwa fumila nabha kwi shile. Ipo isauti ihafuma mwibhingo ihayanga, “Unu mwana wane uwingine. Mutejele zyaje yuyo.”
MAR 9:8 Ghafla, pali bha wenya sabha halola uyalinao palishimo, ila uYesu mwene.
MAR 9:9 Pali bhahwiha afume wigamba, amulila huje bhasaheze hubhele umuntu numo gala gunti agabha galolile, paka Umwana wa Adamu piizhyuha afume wabhafwe.
MAR 9:10 Ipo paha ga uta amambo bhibho. Lelo bhayangana bhene kwa bhene lwenu imana yakwe “azyushe afume wa bhafwe”
MAR 9:11 Bhaha bhuzya uYesu,”Yenu abhandishi bhaiga uEliya ayize nasonti?”
MAR 9:12 Abhabhula, “lwoli Eliya sagabhiza afume ivhintu vhunti. Yenu isimbilwe Mwana wa Adamu lazima apate amalabha gaminji navhitililwe?
MAR 9:13 Lelo iyanga hulimwi lelo uEliya ahezele, bhahabhomba shabhayingine nishishila shaiganile, nishi amasimbo shaga yanga ahusu umwene.”
MAR 9:14 Pabha habhuya wasudwa, bhaha ilola imbunga ingosi izyungulile na Masadukayo bhabisanyaga ahabho bhabisanyaga anabho.
MAR 9:15 Pala pahalola, ibhunga yunti bhahashyiga nahunyilile hulamushe.
MAR 9:16 Abha bhuzywa asundwa abhakwe, “Mubisanya nao kuhusu iyenu?”
MAR 9:17 Umuntu umo muhati yabho ahajibula, “Mwalimo ihale ta umwana wane huliwe; ana iroho iyithavu ihubhomba huje anganda yayanje,
MAR 9:18 ihu fanya aje atete mamanje na hugwisye panzi, nafume ipofu mwilomu nasye amino naga gandane. Ihabhalabhile asundwa bhaho humwefye, lelo hagabhawezizwe.
MAR 9:19 Abhajibu, “Ishizazi ishasa shiwamini izakhale namwe humuda bhuli? Izawejelane namwe paka lii leti hulini? Mleteni kwangu.”
MAR 9:20 Bhaleta umwana wakwe. Iroho inhavhu palalala uYesu, gafla ihapela ateteme. Usahala agwile paka panzi naafumhe ipovhu wilomu.
MAR 9:21 U Yesu ahabhuzya uyise, “Ihali ine ili awande muda ulyi?” Uyise ayanjile, “Aje afume uwana wakwe.
MAR 9:22 Mumomumo itwala humwoto au mumenze naije la humwanga mizywe, kama uwezwa abhombe hahunthi utuhulumile natusaidile.”
MAR 9:23 U Yesu abhulyile, “Akhashele uli tayali? Hala hantu hawezeha na waya yunthi uya wamini.”
MAR 9:24 Ghafla uyise wa mwana ahalila nayanje huje, “Iwamini! Nisaidie asinte awamini wane.”
MAR 9:25 Uwakati uYesu pahalola imbuga inyila abhale wabhene, ayikemela iroho inthavu nayanje, “awenohobubu uwasaga uhuvha, ihuwamuruleshe, usahinjile wamwene nanthele.”
MAR 9:26 Ahalila wikhone na huhangaisye umwana na iroho ihafumile. Umwana abhoneha uga afyile, Ipo abhinji bhayanjile, “Aje afyile,”
MAR 9:27 Lelo uYesu amwega nukhono abhusywa, umwana ahimelila.
MAR 9:28 Lula uYesu pahinjila muhatyi, asundwa bhakwe bhahabhuzya shisili, “Yenu satawezizye humwefye?”
MAR 9:29 Abhabhulile, “pipo ini haga iwepa ila pwavhile.”
MAR 9:30 Bhahepa pala najendele wi Galilaya. Haga ahazanga umuntu yayuthi amanye pawilyi,
MAR 9:31 pipo amanyizywaga asudwa bhakwe. Abhabhulile, “Umwana wa Adamu atwalya makhono mwa bhantyu, nahugoje. Paivha afwile, baada yinsiku tatu aizyuha nanthele.”
MAR 9:32 Lelo haga bhaha mwelewa agawelezya iza, bhahogopa hubhuzywe.
MAR 9:33 Ipo vhahafiha Karperinaumu. Wakati uhuo pali muhanthi nyumba abhuzizye, “Mwayanga naga yenu mwidala”?
MAR 9:34 Lelo bhaha puma mie. Yani bisanya mwidala huje yunanu uwazabhe gosi zaidi.
MAR 9:35 Ahakhala pansi abhakuga ilongo na bhamo bhabhilye pamo, ayanga nabho, “Umuntu khawaza abhe wa kwanza, nilazima abhe wa malishilo na wabhatumishile bha bhunthi.”
MAR 9:36 Ahamwanya umwana udodo abhiha pahati yabho. Amwega makhono gakwe, ayanga,
MAR 9:37 “Wabhodthi nishi unu witawa lyane, oyaabha amboshile ninengashele umuntu aposha, saga aphola nene tu, lelo nayula uwantumile.”
MAR 9:38 U Yohana abhula, “Umwalimu tulolile umuntu kwa wefya iphepo witawa lwaho tuhathubhila, pepo haga atidaga anti.”
MAR 9:39 Lelo uYesu ayanga, “Munganda hukhane pipo numo uwaibhomba imbombo ingosi witawa lwani na ipi pamandi ayanje injango imbivhi lwa lyunti.
MAR 9:40 Wa bhuntyi uwasagali tofauti natwe ali hu pande witu.
MAR 9:41 Wabhuntyi uya yipela ishikombe iminzye agamwele pipo uli Kilisite, lyoli imba bhala hagaitezya usahala gwakwe.
MAR 9:42 Wa bhuntyi uyakosezwa hawa bhali bhali bhadodo abhanamini anye, wali shinza wa mwene apinyilwe inganga ilwasyele huzhingo natagwe muzhumbi.
MAR 9:43 Khamba ukhono gwaho kha hukosela gundumulaje. Hubha washi awinjile huwomi bila khono kwiko awinjile kwenye hulozi ulinamakhono gutyi. Mula mumwoto “ugwasaguzimiha”.
MAR 9:44 (Inatila: Ulutanani ulu, “Pamahali ambapo intofyi sazifwa numwoto ugwasazimiha.” saga uwili katika nakala zakale).
MAR 9:45 Igaga khashele likosezywa, lidumula. Je shiza huliwe awijile huwumi khalilema, kuliko atagwe hulozi namagaga gavhili.
MAR 9:46 (Inatila: Ulutanani ulu, “Amahali itofi hazifwa numwoto usiyoweza azimishe hagagu wili nakala izihali).
MAR 9:47 Kama iliso lwaho khahukosezwa lisenyaje shinza hwilwe awinjile Utawala uwa Ngulubhi uli niso limo, kuliko kwingia ukiwa maso guntyi ulaje huje mwoto.
MAR 9:48 Pala apali nintafyi izya sazifya, numwoto ugwa saguzimia.
MAR 9:49 Lelo phipo shila muntyu aifyula numwoto.
MAR 9:50 Umwonyi mwinza, lelo umwonyi khagutezye uwiza wakwe, gubhabhombe bhuli uwinza bhuye nathyena? Munje mwonyi muhatyi yinyu, na uwaushe wa shila umo.”
MAR 10:1 U Yesu ashila amali pala na habhala katika ukowa ugwa Huyahudi ni eneo ilya witanzi ili Soho Yorodani, amakutano gadagaga na tyena. Abhamanyizwe tyena, nishi pibha kawaida yamwene abhombe.
MAR 10:2 Na Amafalisayo bhaheza hujele bhahabhuzwa, “Ni halali wa muntu ulume aleha nushi awakwe?”
MAR 10:3 U Yesu abhajibula, “U Mose amulile yenu?”
MAR 10:4 Bhayanga, “Mose aruhusu ahusimbile ikalata iyalene nahunyizywe ushi.”
MAR 10:5 “Pipo amoyo nginyu makhome shashisho abhasimbila ishalia ini, “U Yesu ahabhala.
MAR 10:6 “Afume huwandilo wiumbaji, 'Ungulubhi aumba ulume nushi.'
MAR 10:7 Inamuna ini ulume aileha uyise wakwe nu nyina wakwe aibhungana nushi wakwe,
MAR 10:8 na eo bhabhili bhaibhabhili gumo; Pipo saga bhabhiatyele, lelo bhali bili gumo.
MAR 10:9 Kwa hiyo abhunganisye Ungulubhi, umwanadamu anje alehanye.”
MAR 10:10 Pali muhati inyumba, asundwa bhakwe bhahahuzywa nantyena asuili.
MAR 10:11 Abhabhula, “Ula uwileha ushi wakwe na weje uwinji uyo abhomba malaya pamwanya yakwe.
MAR 10:12 Na ushi wope khaila ulume wakwe na wegwe nulume uwinji, abhomba malaya.”
MAR 10:13 Bhope bhahuleta abhana adodo akhate, lelo asimbi bhakwe bhahabha damila.
MAR 10:14 Lelo uYesu pahamanya ilwo, haga amojelela nalwo kabisa abhabhula, “Bhalesheli abhana adodo bhinze hulini, munganjebhazije, pipo abhabhalinishi ibha utawala uwa Ngulubhi wabhene.
MAR 10:15 Lyoli imbaula, yayunti uwa saposhela utawala wa Ngulubhi nishi abhana adodo lyoli haga aiwezywa awinjile utawala wa Ngulubhi.
MAR 10:16 Ipo abhega abhana makhono agakwe abhasaya nabhabhishe akhono panya yabho.
MAR 10:17 Pahanda isafali yakwe umuntu umo anyililila ahafugamila amafuugamo witazi lwakwe, abhuzwa, “Mwalimu Umwinza, imbombe yenu ili bweze erithi uwomi uwa wilawila?”
MAR 10:18 U Yesu ayanga, “Unguga mwema? Numo ulimwema ila yu Ngulubhi mwene.
MAR 10:19 Uziminye imuli: 'Uganje agoje, unganje afunye umalaya, unganda awibhe ungande ande ilenga unganje akhopele, uheshimwaje uyese waho nu nyina waho'.”
MAR 10:20 Umutyu ulo ahayanga, “Mwalimo, iganguntyi awande uwana wanhe.”
MAR 10:21 U Yesu amwenya nahugane. Abhula, “Upungushilwe ahatyu hamo. Uwaziwa ukazye uvhili navho nabhapele apina, uhaibha ni mbuto humwanya. Khasha winzaje andaje.”
MAR 10:22 Lelo akatile itama hunongwa iyaheleziwe iga; aliondoka akiwa mwenye huzuni, ahepa nusumane phepo alimale nyinji.
MAR 10:23 U Yesu ahenya upande bhutyi abhabhula asundwa bhakwe, “Nishi bhuli ishashashilyi pakhome utajili awinjile hutawala uwa hu mwanya!
MAR 10:24 Asundwa bhaswijiziwa humaneno iga. Lelo uYesu abhabhula nantyele, “Bhana, ni jinsi bhule ishili shikhome awinjile utawala Ungulubhi!
MAR 10:25 Laisi wingamia ashizanye mwilina lisindano, pakuliko umutyu utajili awinjile hufalume uwa Ngulubhi.”
MAR 10:26 Bhaswijiziwa sana nayangana bhene, “Esho yunanu uwa yokolewa”
MAR 10:27 U Yesu abhenya nayayanje, “Wabinadamu hagaiwezehana, lelo saga wa Ngulubhi. Wavhavhuthi wa Ngulubhi shiwezehana wa Ngulubhi shiwezehana.”
MAR 10:28 “Petulo handa ayanje nabho, “Enya tuleshile vhutyi tudajile.”
MAR 10:29 U Yesu ayanga, “Lyolyi imbabhula amwe, numouwaila inyumba, au ukulu, au uilumbu, au unyina, au uyise, au abhana, au ugunda, kwa ajili yangu, na kwa ajili ya lumbelele,
MAR 10:30 uwaha gaiposhela mala mia zaidi yisalaini ipa pansi: inyumba, ukulu, uyilumbu, au unyina, au abhana, au uinsi, humalabha, ulimwengu ugwa guweza, uwumi uwawila na wila.
MAR 10:31 Lelo vhinji avhali wanda bhaibhabhahumalishilo abhali bhahumalishilo bhawanda.”
MAR 10:32 Pabhabha mwidala, bhabhala Yelusalemu, uYesu abhatangulila witanzi lyabho. Asundwa bhasyijile, nabhala abhali bhafuta khosi yabho bhahogopa. Ipo uYesu abhefa pashinje antele bhala ilongo nabhabhili ahanda abhabhule hala hazafumile ishi papipi:
MAR 10:33 “Enya, tushila hula hu Yelusalemu, nu Mwana wa Adamu anzafisiwe wachungaji agosi nasimbi. Bhanzahulonje afwe bhanza humwefwe wa Bhapanzi.
MAR 10:34 Bhanza hulyeule, bhanza huswile amate, bhanzahukhome nusanzo, nahugaje. Lelo bada yinsiku zitatu azyuha.”
MAR 10:35 U Yakobo nu Yohana, abhana bha Zebedayo, bhahinza wamwene nayanje, “Mwalimu, tuwanza tubhombele hahundi atuhulabha.”
MAR 10:36 Ahagamuyiga, “Imbabho mbele yenu?”
MAR 10:37 Bhahayanga, “Turuhusu tukhale nae husisya waho, umo hukhona ugwahulilo umo hukhono gwa humongo.”
MAR 10:38 Lelo uYesu abhajibula, “Sagammenye ilyamulabha. Mugawezya amwelele ishikombe ishimwela ane au ajimbe au uwoziwa uwi woziwa?”
MAR 10:39 Bhaha bhala huje, “Tuwezya” uYesu abhabhula, “Ishikombe ishimwela mgawezya, amwe mwelele. Na ulyozyo ambao ininoziwe, mnzajimbilile.
MAR 10:40 Lelo uwakale ukhono ugwa hulilo au uugwa humongo saga nini uwafumwe, lelo wabhala ambao wavhene bhala ibhahandaliwe.”
MAR 10:41 Bhala asundwa bhamo ilongo pahahuvhaiga bhaha vitililya aYakobo nu Yohana.
MAR 10:42 U Yesu abhakuga wamwene nayanje, “Mumenye ahuje bha abhasivhililwa bhatabhalwa bhabhatyu abhapansi bhatabhala, nabhantyu avhikhapho bhalanga mamlaka pamwanya yabho.”
MAR 10:43 Lelo saga iwanziwa avhe ishi muhati yinyu. Wabhundi uwanza abhe gosi kati yinyu atumishilaje abhanji,
MAR 10:44 na wabhutyi uwawaza abhewanda pahati lazima abhanje watumishe wabhuntyi.
MAR 10:45 Wahuje Umwana wa Adamu hagaahiza atumishilwe bali atumishe nafume maisha gakwe abhvhe lisombo wa vhinji.”
MAR 10:46 Bhahinza Yeriko. Pahali ashilaga Yeriko nasundwa bhakwe ni mbuga ingosi, umwana wa Timayo, Batimayo, uwafwile amaso, uwalabha mashinje insumbi.
MAR 10:47 Pahavha huje yu Yesu Mnazareti, ahanda akhole nayanje, “Yesu, Mwana wa Daudi, hulumile!”
MAR 10:48 Abhinji bhahadamila ula uyafumile amaso, bhabhulaga phumaa. Lelo alilaga husauti sana, “Mwana wa Daudi, hulumile!”
MAR 10:49 U Yesu ahima nahumula mulile akugwe. Bhahakuga ula uyafwile amaso, bhahayanga, “Huje shuja! Bhuha! U Yesu ahukuga.”
MAR 10:50 Ataga ikoti lwakwe hushinji ahanyila sana, na winze wa Yesu.
MAR 10:51 U Yesu ahajibu nayanje, “Uwanza huje ibhombele yenu?” Ula ulume uwafwile amaso ahajibu, “Mwalimo, iwanza alole.”
MAR 10:52 U Yesu ahabhula, “Bhalanga. Awamini waho huponizye.” Pepo amaso gakwe gahalola; ahadaga uYesu wibalabala.
MAR 11:1 Ulyo ulya bha hizaga hu Yelusalemu, pabha hyela ga Besthfage na Bethania, wi Gamba ilya Mizeituni, uYesu abhatuma bhabhili muhati umwo mwa sundwa bhakwe
MAR 11:2 abhabhula, “Bhalaji hushijiji isha shi bhelana natyi. Pamu winjila umwo munzayaje idogovhi iya siinjilwe. Muyaule muilete hulini.
MAR 11:3 Nakhashele yayutyi uwabhula, 'Huje yenu mu bhomba ishi?', mubhajile ayanje ishi, 'U Bwana amwanza khashele abhuzwa ipa.'”
MAR 11:4 Bhabhalile nayaje idovhi ipinyile huzi hulyango uta ugwaguliwaza, bhayabhulila.
MAR 11:5 Bhamo abhantu bhalivhimile pala bhaha bhabhula, “Mubhomba yenu, ayaulile idogovhi ini?”
MAR 11:6 Bhabha bhulile nishi uYesu ishabhulele, na abhanya bhaleha bhashila.
MAR 11:7 Asundwa bhabhili bhahaleta idogovhi wa Yesu bhahalanga amenda gao pamwa yakwe ili uYesu awezyaje awinjile.
MAR 11:8 Abhantu ibhinji bhahalaga amenda mwibalabala, nabhamo bhalanga amasamba agabhatemile afume humagunda.
MAR 11:9 Bhala abhabha bhatile witanzi lwakwe na bhala abhadajile bhakhoma kelele, “Hosana! Asayiwe nuyahweza witawa ilwa Bwana.
MAR 11:10 Usaiwe hutawala bhuwinza wayise witu Daudi! Hosana bhunu uli humwanya”
MAR 11:11 Epo uYesu ahinjila hu Yelusalemu abhala hukanisa ahenya shila hantu. Ishi uwakati wali bhubhalile ahabhala hu Bethania bhala ilongo na bhabhili.
MAR 11:12 Isiku ilyalya fwata pali bha bhuya afume hu Bethania, ali ni nzala.
MAR 11:13 Alola ikwi ilya mtini amantyundu shahutali, abhala awenye huje agawezwa ahaje hahundti mwanya yakwe. Uwakati ula bhalaga wilyo, haga ahaga hahuthi ila amatundu, pipo hawali wakati mitini.
MAR 11:14 Alibhula, “Numo yayuthi uwa ilwa udundu afume huliwe nathele”. Asundwa bhahuvha.
MAR 11:15 Bhahinza hu Yelusalemu, wope ahinjila mushibhanza anda afumwe huzi abha kazwa nabhagula muhati iyikanisa. Agaluzanya imeza tana nwa nihela namatengo gabhala abhali bhakazwa injibha.
MAR 11:16 Haga aluhusu ya yunthi anyemule hahuthi mukanisa ahali hakaziwa.
MAR 11:17 Abhamanyizywa nayanje, “Lelo haga isimbilwe, 'nyumba yane ihaitwa ya labhe wabha panzi bhudti'? Lelo muvhishile ligwenyo lya bhafyula”.
MAR 11:18 Achungaji agosi hasimbi vhahuvha ishali ayanjile ilwa hugoje. Hata isho bhamwogopa pipo imbuga ihaswijiziwe namanyizye wakwe.
MAR 11:19 Shila wakati nishalyevhela pihafihaga, bhashilaga hujini.
MAR 11:20 Pali bhajenda nashaphi, bhalilola ikwi ili mutini lyumile paka pamakholo gakwe.
MAR 11:21 U Petulo ahinzuha nayanje, “Mwalimu! Enya, ikwiimitini ilyuhalilanile lyumile”.
MAR 11:22 U Yesu ajibule, “Mubhanje ni imani lelo mwa Ngulubhi.
MAR 11:23 Mwini imbabhula mubhanje ni imani ushili bhula igambaili, 'Epa, liwitaje lyilyo munsumbi khashele huli mashaka mmwoyo gwakwe lelo awamini ishayanjile shaibhoneha, isho shawanza Ungulubhi shawanza.
MAR 11:24 Lelo imbabhula: shila hatyu isha mushilavha nishamubhuzwa kwaajili yumwene, mwaminilaje huje poshala vhape vhwibhe vinyu.
MAR 11:25 Pala pamuwimilila na labhe, muwaziwa abhahumile hahundi amunaho ashizanye wabhene ashele hahuntyi ili uyise winyu uwali humwanya ambhahoshele amwe pia izwa mutulile.
MAR 11:26 
MAR 11:27 Bhahafiha hu Yelusalemu nandele. Hata pali ajenda mushibhaza, bhaha bhalila agosi bhachungaji na asimbi na ashigosi.
MAR 11:28 Bhahabhula, “Mamulaka bhuli ubhomba amambo iga?” Wope yunanu uwa pelile ama mulaka huje ugabhombaje?”
MAR 11:29 U Yesu abhabhula, “Imbabhuzwa limo. Namwe mujibu khimba bhule huje nihumamulaka ashi ingabhomba iga.
MAR 11:30 Ulwozyo ulwa Yohana lwa hafuma humwanya au wabhanadamu? Ntabulili.”
MAR 11:31 Bhayangana bhene wa bhene bhahayanga, “Khashele khatuje, 'Wafumile humwanya', abhayanje, 'Mbona basi haga mwamwamini?'
MAR 11:32 Lelo khatuje wabhaha fuma wa bhanadamu,'....” Ibhahogopa abhantu, mana abhantu bhalolile uYohana huje kuwa kamili.
MAR 11:33 Bhahajibu uYesu bhayanga, “Hagatumenye. U Yesu abhula, “Wala ane simba bhula amwe humamulaka ashi ibhomba iga.
MAR 12:1 Ipo uYesu ahanda abhamanyizye huvhi fwani. Ayanga, “Umuntu atotile hugunda amizabibu, azyunguzwa ulubhaga, ahadiba ilina ilwa khandile ahamwele. Ahazenga ahantu atali bada yipo apanjizywa ugunda ugwimizabibu ashula isafali iya hutali.
MAR 12:2 Uwakati pawahafika hatu ma utumishi walimi imizabibu aposhele afume wabhene vimo ivimadudu gahugunda igimizabibu.
MAR 12:3 Lelo bhakata, bhakhoma nahanyizywa bila haiduhahutde.
MAR 12:4 Atuma utumishi uwinji bhavhahwalazywa mwitwe na hubhombele amambo agisoni.
MAR 12:5 Bado atuma uwinji, unuuwinji bha goga bhahabhombela abhinji amambo kama gigo, bhakoma bhamo bhabha goga.
MAR 12:6 Alisile umuntu umozaidi uwahutume, umwana uyangenwe. Wope aliwamwisho uwatumilwe wabhene. Ayanga, “Bhaza huheshimuu mwana wane”.
MAR 12:7 Lelo apangaji bhayanga na bhene kwa bhene, “Unu yuyo uwaliyhi. Izaji, natugoje, uhu ulithi uzabhewetu.”
MAR 12:8 Bhahavhamila, bhahagoga nahutaje huzi iyigunda gwa mizabibu.
MAR 12:9 Isho, Lelo ayibhomba bhuli utawala uwi gunda ili mizabibu? Ayinza na vhangamizywe abhalinza amizabibu na aipela abhanji ishamba ili mizabibu wa bhantu abhanji.
MAR 12:10 Hapete amanyile isimbo ili? “Iwe ilwa zenji bhalikhanile, lihabha liwe lwa nshinje.
MAR 12:11 Ili lihafuma wa Bwana, na liswizywa pamaso gityu.”
MAR 12:12 Bhahanza hukhate uYesu, Lelo bha hogopa umbungano. Pipo vhaminye huje bhayanjile ishifwano zaidi yao. Isho bhahaleha wabho.
MAR 12:13 Pipo bhahatuma bhamo na mahelodia wa mwene ili huteje hunongwa.
MAR 12:14 Pabhahafiha, bhahabhula, “Huje Mwalimo, tuminye huje haga usaga inzibho zhwazyunti haga ubhonesya apendelele pahati iya bhantu. Umanyizwa idala ilwa Ngulubhi pamwana lyoli. Lelo haki afumwe ikodi wakali sali au haa?
MAR 12:15 Lelo uYesu amenye aje bhalyeula na abhabhula, “Yenu munjela? Mbheli ihela injenye.”
MAR 12:16 Nabhayileta imo wa Yesu, Abhabhula, “Isura yana nu asimbo agagaliipa gananu? Bhayanga, “Ya Kaisari.”
MAR 12:17 U Yesu abhabhula, “Panji u Kaisari ivintu ivha Kaisari vavha Ngulubhi panji Ungulubhi.” Bhahaswiga.
MAR 12:18 Ipo Amasadukayo, abhayanga nahumo azywoshe, bhahabhalila. Bhabhuzya, bhahaga,
MAR 12:19 “Mwalimo, uMose atusimbile huje, 'Gashele uholo uwa muntu khafwile aleshile ushi khosi yakwe, lelo haga aleshile umwana, mutu ayimwenga ushi uwaholo, nawipatile abhana kwajili yaholo wakwe.'
MAR 12:20 Wali na holo saba, uwa wandilo ahamwega ula ushi afwa, haga ahaleha abhana.
MAR 12:21 Antele wope uwabhili amwega wope afwa, aleha abhana. Uwatatu wope shisho.
MAR 12:22 Nawa saba afwa bila aleshe abhana. Hu mwisho wakwe wope ushi ahafwa.
MAR 12:23 Uwakati uzyushe, pabhaizyuha nandtele, Ishi ayibhawananu? Maana bhala aholo bhunthi saba bhundthi bhali bhalume bhakwe.”
MAR 12:24 U Yesu abhabhula, Lelo! Ili sagalila huje mukhopilwe, pipo samuminye amasimbo wala ikhone ilwa Ngulubhi?”
MAR 12:25 Uwakati uwazyushe uwafume bhabhafile, haga bhayenga wala awinjile mundowa ila bhaibha na sha awandumi ahumwanya.
MAR 12:26 Lelo, ahusu abhafwe abhaizyuha, Lelo! Samwamanyila afume mushitabu isha Mose, ihabali ziha poli, shila Ungulubhi isha yanga abhula, 'Ani ni Ngulubhi uwa Ibulahimu, nani Ngulubhi Isaka, nani Ngulubhi uwa Yakobo?'
MAR 12:27 Umwene sa Ngulubhi uwa bhafwa, ila wali bhumi. Lili wazi atejile.”
MAR 12:28 uwa bhawasimbi ahenza ahuvha izyabhayangaga inongwa zyabho; alola huje uYesu abhajibule shinza. Ahabhuzya, “Lelo! amuli ishi ili mana ishilizywe zyunti?”
MAR 12:29 U Yesu ahajibula, “Ilimana yayini, “Uvha Israeli, U Bwana Ungulubhi uwetu, Bwana umo.
MAR 12:30 Ilazimiha hugane uBwana Ungulubhi uwaho, hunwoyo hwaho gwundti, huroho yaho yundti hunjele zyaho zyundti nawikhone lwaho lyundti.'
MAR 12:31 Iamuli iyabhili yayini, 'Iwanziwa ugane upalamani waho nishi amuli iyinje ingosi zaidi yizi.”
MAR 12:32 Usimbi ayanga, “Shinza Mwalimo! Uyanjile lyoli huje Ungulubhi aliumo na huje numo, uwinji zaidi yamwene.
MAR 12:33 Ugane umwene humwoyo gwundti, nahugane upalamani nishi puwiga ne wewe, nimuhimu mno kuliko uvifumwa nadhahibu izya lungulizye.”
MAR 12:34 Ulya Yesu pala pahalola ahafumwa ijibu ilinza, ayanga, “Awe haga ulihutali nu tawala uwa Ngulubhi.” Pipo numo hata umo uwa ajela hubhuzwe uYesu amaswali gagundti.
MAR 12:35 U Yesu ahajibu, lula uli amanyizya mushi vhanza ayanga, “Lelo! Asimbi bhayigabhuli huje uYesu Kilisiti ni mwana wa Daudi?
MAR 12:36 Daudi yuyo katika Roho Uuzelu, ayanjile, 'Bwana' ayanjile Bwana wane, khala kati yikho gwani hukhono ugwishulume pakaimbabhombe alugo pansi iyi magagagaho.'
MAR 12:37 U Daudi ahukuga Kilisiti, 'Bwana' Lelo! mwana wa Daudi nishi uli pugaishi gosi shimojile?”
MAR 12:38 Amanyizywe wakwe uYesu ayanga, “Muwiyenyeje nasimbi abhasugwa ajende ni kazu intali nalamuwe musokoni
MAR 12:39 na khale humatengo aga gosi umwaputile namu shikulukulu humaeneo agashigosi.
MAR 12:40 Natena bhalwa nyumba inzwainzwafwile bhala bha amaombi amatali sana abhantu khabha bhenyaje. Ibha abhantu bhaipaulozi uwa uli gosi.”
MAR 12:41 Pala uYesu akhala panzi apalamane ni phogoso isadaka muhati inyi shi bhaza. Ali abhenya abhenya abhandtu abhafumiga panyanga indalama muphogoso. Abhandtu abhinji atajili bhahabhehanyishe huwinji uwindalama.
MAR 12:42 Ushi ufwile umaskini ahenza naponye ivipande vibhili thamani yasenti.
MAR 12:43 Ipo abhakuga asundwa wakwe na bhabhule, “Amini imbabhula, ushi unu ufwile afumizwe agosi zaidi ya bhundti bhala amalizizizye apanye mpongoso iyisa ndaka.
MAR 12:44 Kwani bhundthi bhaponyizye elingananje huwinji uwivhi pato vhavho. Lelo ushiuda ufwile unu, afume humasikini wakwe, afumwa idalama yundti amabyo iziwanga.”
MAR 13:1 U Yesu pajendaga afume hushi bhaza, umo kati yabho asunda bhakwe ahabhuza, “Mwalimo, enya amawe gahunswisywa na mayumba!”
MAR 13:2 Abhula, Mugalola ayumba amagosi? Nalimo ilyalya isangala hatalimo pamwanya yilyenje ilyasa lya igwisiwa paka pansi”.
MAR 13:3 Nawope pali akhele pamwanya yi Gamba ilyi Mizaituni khosi ishibhanzu, Petulo, na Yakobo, Yohana nu Andeleya bhabhuzya husili,
MAR 13:4 “Tubhule, amambo igagaibhali? Na henu atenyeje amambo paga ifumila?”
MAR 13:5 U Yesu anda abhabhule, “Mubhanje maso umuntu yayundti asabhatezye.
MAR 13:6 Bhinji bhainza witawalwa ni bhaiyanga, 'Ane nene', na bhai bhatezya abhinji.
MAR 13:7 Pamwayuvha ivita na itetesi ili vita, mundawogope; amambo igalazima afumile, lelo umwisho gusili.
MAR 13:8 Insi iyifuma alye ninsi iyinje, utawala akhomane nutawala uwinji. Wayibha antezywa mwunti mwunti munsi, waibha ni zala. Uwo mwanzo wichungu.
MAR 13:9 Namwi munje maso. Munafisi nzyinyu maana bhai bhatwala amwe humabalaza nahusinagosi. Mwaikhomwa namwimwayegwa witanzi wa maliwali na watawala kwa ajili yalini, abheshuhuda wa bhene.
MAR 13:10 Lelo izyo lazima alumbililye wa pansi bhunti.
MAR 13:11 Paibhakata nabha vitwililye, munganje awogope huje munzayanje ayenu. Uwakati uwo, mungandasibhe izya munzayanje uwakati uwo pabhuzya saga mwimwe umzayanje ilyanza bhapele uwakati bhula; liyangaji maana sa mweme mwamuyanga yu Roho Uzelu.
MAR 13:12 Uholo aitaka uhola wakwe huje bhagoje nubaba nu mwana. Umwana ayepaasu ayise bhabho nabhagoje.
MAR 13:13 Mwayegwa nashila muntu hasababu iyitawa lyani. Lelo uwaijimba paka pamalishilo, umuntu uyo aipona.
MAR 13:14 Pailola ilyavitililye lyiwima pasaliwaziwa awime (imanyila amanyaje), epo abhali muhati iya Yuda bhanyilaje humagamba,
MAR 13:15 wope uyali wigulu anganda wishe aweje ivhapansi nyumba au aweje hahunti hali hunzi,
MAR 13:16 naulihugunda angandaa bhuye aweje umwenda gwakwe.
MAR 13:17 Lelo ole wabho abhashi abhikhanda nabhabha wonzya kati yisiku inzyo!
MAR 13:18 Mulabhaje huje ingandafumile uwakati uwisasa.
MAR 13:19 Maana waibha na malabha amagosi gala gasa gawahile afumile awande Ungulubhi paumbaga insi, pakaishi, na hamo wala haifumila andtele.
MAR 13:20 Bwana ugabhe haga azipunguzwaga insiku nanumo uwaponaga, lelo kwa ajili yate uliwa, azifupizye insiku izyo.
MAR 13:21 Umuda ugwo umuntu yayunti uwayibhabhula, Enyi, uKilisti ali ipa!' au 'Enyi, pala!' mungandawamini.
MAR 13:22 Maana Akilisti abhilenga nakuwa abhilenga bhaifumila nabhaifumila ivhawenye na hajabu, ili amwe bhabhakhopele, yamukini nateuliwa.
MAR 13:23 Mubhanje maso! Imalishe imba bhulile igagundti kabula yu wakati.
MAR 13:24 Lelo bada yimaimba iginsiku izyo, isanya lwaibhewa ikhisi, umwezi hagwaifumia umwanga gwakwe,
MAR 13:25 intontwe zyaigwa afume humwanya, nikhone izywazi lihumwanya zyaiyinga.
MAR 13:26 Pailola Umwana Adamu pawinza mabhingo nikhone igosi nusisya.
MAR 13:27 Ipo paituma awandumi bhakwe aibhabhunganya pandimo nateliwa bhakwe ipande zyunti ingosi nzene izinsi, afume humwisho uwidunia upaka umwisho uwimwanya.
MAR 13:28 Munyilaje wipishi ulusamba lubhi ha amatundu gakwe, pamwanya huje ulusanya lulipiphi.
MAR 13:29 Isho shashili, pailola amambo igapagafumila, mumanye ahuje alipipe, mundwango.
MAR 13:30 Lyoli, imbaula, ishizazi sashisizanya hutali kabula ya mambo hagafumile.
MAR 13:31 Imwanya ninsi zyainsinzanya, lelo amazyo gani haga insizanya na mwaha.
MAR 13:32 Lelo ahusu isiku au isaa, numo uwaminye, hata awandumi ahumwanya, hata Umwana, ila Uyise.
MAR 13:33 Munje maso, Pipo sagamumuminye mudashi gaifumila.
MAR 13:34 Ishifwani shakwe shili nishi umuntu uwanza asafili: aileshile inyumba yakwe, apela atumwa bhakwe iamuli, nashila muntu imbombo ayakwe. Amula andalyango bhagonaje maso.
MAR 13:35 Bhanji masolelo! Piposaminye painza ubwana uwinyumba huje ulwebhela au usiku umanane, au pazikuga ihanda au ushaphii.
MAR 13:36 Asahinze mundunyu abhaje shamugonile.
MAR 13:37 Ili ilimbabula amwe imbabhula mwindti: Bhajimaso”!
MAR 14:1 Zyali nsiku zibhili afume iPasaka nama Bumunda gasa gaponyeziwe Amila. Achungaji agosi nsimbi wabha hanzaga isha hukhate uYesu huhila nahugoje.
MAR 14:2 Pipo bhayanjile, “Haga wabhuuwishi kulukulu, abhantu bhasihinze elete itaka.”
MAR 14:3 Ulyo uYesu pali Bethania hukhaya wa Simoni umukoma, palije awelekela pameza, ushi umo ahenza wa mwene nisupa malashi ya nardo amiza agigalama ingosi sana, abojola isupa nasulule pamwanya iyitwe lyakwe.
MAR 14:4 Lelo kati yabho bhavitwa. Bhabhulana bhibho wabhibho bhahayanga, “Nayenu isababu uwateje uhuu?
MAR 14:5 Manukato iga gewezyanga eguziwe winali miazitatu twabha panag asikini.” Na hadamila.
MAR 14:6 Lelo uYesu ahayanga, “Leshi yuyo mwene. Yenu musubula? Abhombile linza hu lini.
MAR 14:7 Isiku zyunti amasikini munabho, umuda gwa gundti pamusungwa mugawenza abhombe aminza wabhene, lelo saga munzabhe nane uwakati waundti.
MAR 14:8 Ambombile shila ishawezya: abhombe agupashile ubhili gwani amafuta kwa ajili yasyile.
MAR 14:9 Lyoli imbabhula, shila mahali izyo palumbililwa insi yundti, lila ilibhambile ushi unu shaiyangwa akubhuwe wakwe.
MAR 14:10 Pipo uYuda Iskariote, umo uwabhala ilongo na bhabhili, abhalile wagosi uwachungaji ili apate hutwale wa bhene.
MAR 14:11 Uwakati agosi Abhachungaji pabha hu vha isho, bhamojile bhahaidi hupele ihela. Andile awanze inafasi iyapele abhene.
MAR 14:12 Isiku ilya wande ilibumunda ilyasaliponyeziwe imila, uwakati uwabhafumia inyama ingole ipasaka, wanafunzi wake walimwambia, “Unataka twende wapi tukaandae ili upate kula mlo wa Pasaka?”
MAR 14:13 Atuma asundwa bhakwe bhabhili nabhabhule, “Aje bhalaji hujini, na ulume uwanza tangane namwi akhente ulusai lyiminzi. Dagaji.
MAR 14:14 Inyumba yanza winjile, dagaji nahubhule umwani nyumba iyo, 'Mwalimo ayanga, “Shi ibuba ishajenyu ailye iPasaka umwo pandwimo na asundwa bhakwe?”
MAR 14:15 Wope yuyo abhalanje igolofa ingosi isimbilwe tayali. Umwo tayalisyaji.”
MAR 14:16 Asundwa bhahabhala hujini; bhaga kila handu haisha yangaga, bhatayalisya iPasaka.
MAR 14:17 Pawahafiha ulyebhela, ahinza na bhala humi na bhabhili.
MAR 14:18 Pabhanga bhaibhelela imeza naje bhalye uYesu ayanga, “Lyoli imbaula, umo kati yenyu abhanenelele.”
MAR 14:19 Bhanda asononeshe, bhaha bhala umo umo, “Lelo nine?”
MAR 14:20 U Yesu ahajibu ihubhula, “Ali umo ulilongo nabhabhili muhati yinyu, umo ambaye ishi atovhela uluntonji mubhakuli palushimo nane.
MAR 14:21 Pipo Umwana wa Adamu abha bhale nishi amasimbo ishaga yanag pamwanya yakwe. Lelo ole wa mwene umuntu ula uwanza hu nenelele Umwana wa Adamu washinza! umuntu uyo gabhe haga apapwaga.”
MAR 14:22 Pali bhalya, uYesu ahega ibumunda, alisaya na limesule. Apela nayanje, “Chukueni. Ugu ubile gwani.
MAR 14:23 Ahega ishikombe, akasarifwa, apela, bhamwelela.
MAR 14:24 Abhabhulile, “Ili idada lyane ililagana, idada ilya liwitiha kwaajili yabhinji.
MAR 14:25 Lyoli imbabhula, sigaihamwela nantele paka pisiku lila paimwala ipha hutawala ula uwa Ngulubhi.”
MAR 14:26 Pabha habha bhamalile atele ulyimbo, bhahashilainje Igamba ili Mizeituni.
MAR 14:27 U Yesu abhabhula, “Amwe mwinthe munza wibangule huhutari kwaajili ya yane, phepo isimbilwe, 'Aikhoma umchungaji naingole zinza nyabhane.'
MAR 14:28 Lelo baada yazyushe wani, aibha tangula witazi lyinyu wi Galilaya.”
MAR 14:29 Petulo ahabhula, “Hata kama bhundti bhaileha, aani sihaileha.”
MAR 14:30 U Yesu abhabulile, “Lyoli ihubhula, usiku hubhu ihanda shazili akuje habhili, uhanile mala hatatu.”
MAR 14:31 Lelo u Petulo ayanjile, “Ibhadazimisye afwe nawesaga imba hu lyije bhunti bhafumia ihadi ile ile.
MAR 14:32 Bhahinzele kwenye ieneo ilyaitwaga Gethsemane, uYesu ahabhula asundwa bhakwe, “Khalaji ipa uwakati ilabha.”
MAR 14:33 Abhega Petulo, Yakobo, na Yohana pandwemo nawo, nahanda asononeshe hata miwe sana.
MAR 14:34 Ahabhula, “Inafsi yani yani isoneneha sana, hata afwe. Sagalaji phepa nabhemaso.”
MAR 14:35 U Yesu abhala witanzi hashe, ahagwa paka panzi, ahalabha, ghashiwezena, huje isaili linepushe.
MAR 14:36 Ahayanga, “Aba, Baba, Amambo gunte huliwe gawezehana. Unefenzwe ishikombe ishi. Lelo saga hu mapenzi gane, ila amapenzi gaho.”
MAR 14:37 Abhuya abhaga shabha gonile, abhula aPetro, “Simoni, we ulishugonile? Hagauwezizya abhe maso hata isaa hatalimo?
MAR 14:38 Khalaji maso mulabhaje musahenze. Agwile mujelo. Lyoli roho ili tayali, lelo ubhele dhaifu.”
MAR 14:39 Ahashila nantele alabhe, atumila zinongwa zyazila.
MAR 14:40 Ahenza nantele ahega shagonile, pipo amaso goo galimamwamu nahamenye henu ahabhule.
MAR 14:41 Ahenza mala hatatu shabhabhula, “Muli sha mugonile na tuyaji? Muyile! Saa ifishile. Enya! Mwana wa Adamu bhanza hutake wilenga makhono agabhibhivhi.
MAR 14:42 Bhuhaji, sali. Enya, ola uwantake wilenga alipipi.”
MAR 14:43 Enya alishanga uYuda uwalipadwimo na abhilongo na bhabhile, afiha, nimbuga ingosi afume wagosi bhachungaji, asimbi agosi napanga na madugu.
MAR 14:44 Umuda gwugwo uhutake wilenga wakwe ali apile ishimanyilo, ayagaula uhbinza hununile yuyo khataji nahutwale nabhe chini alidwaje.”
MAR 14:45 Lelo uYuda pahafiha, moja kwa moja ahabhala wa Yesu nayanje, “Mwalimo!” Anunila.
MAR 14:46 Pipo uwaponye panzi yagulye nahukhatwe.
MAR 14:47 Lelo umo muhati yao amenlela paphephe nao achomola ipanga lyakwe akhoma utumishi uwa chunga ugosi nahudumule ikutu.
MAR 14:48 U Yesu abhabhulile, “Mwenzele ahate namapanga nadugu nishi uwafula?
MAR 14:49 Uwakati shilasiku nabha namwe shimbamanyizya, mushibhanza. Sagamwahataga. Lelo ili libhobishe ili amasimbo gatimile.
MAR 14:50 Bhala bhunti bhali nu Yesu bhaleha nahunyile.
MAR 14:51 Usaha umo ahakunya, uwali akwite ishuka lyene awikwishile hu zyugule; bhakhata lelo
MAR 14:52 apulumuha alileha ishuka pala ahanyila bhululu.
MAR 14:53 Bhahalongola uYesu wachungaji ugosi pala paungene padwemo nao nabha chungaji agosi bhunti nashi gosi nasimbi.
MAR 14:54 U Petulo wope ahadaga uYesu shahutali, awelekele wizyala wachungaji ugosi. Akhala pandwemo nabhagula bhali bheline numwoto bhahotaga ili apate ilyoto.
MAR 14:55 Umuda ugwo achungaji agosi bhunti ni balaza lyundti bhanzaga uketi zaidi ya mwene uYesu ili bhapate hugoje. Lelo habhamwaga.
MAR 14:56 Huje abhantu ambinji bha haleta ilenga ashile umwene, lelo uketi wabho hawalinganaga.
MAR 14:57 Bhamo bhahemelye lyanelete uketi uwilenga ashe wa mwene; bhayanga,
MAR 14:58 “Tumamwuvha ayanag, 'Iha inanganya ishibhanza ishi ilyaliganiziwe humakhono, nahuku zitatu ihaizenga ilyta mwao ilyasa linganiziwe humakhono.”'
MAR 14:59 Lelo hata uketi wao hali nganaga.
MAR 14:60 Uchungaji ugosi amelila pahati yao abhuzwa uYesu, “We, hagaulinijibu? Aa hantu ibha bhayanga yenu kwaji yaliwe?”
MAR 14:61 Lelo ahapuma mee hagajibula nalimo. Pipo uchungaji ugosi ahabhuzya nantele awe wi Kilisti, umwana Uwasaiwa?”
MAR 14:62 U Yesu ayanje, “Huje ani nini. Uhailola Umwana wa Damu akhele hukhono ulilo ugwikhone awinza na mabhingo aga humwanya.”
MAR 14:63 Uchungaji ugosi azembula amenda gakwe nayanje, “Lelo tuli shatu wanza aketi?
MAR 14:64 Muhuvha amatusi. Uwamuzi winyu vhulihu?” Na bhunti vhalongaga nishi iyabhajile ufwe.
MAR 14:65 Bhamo bhahanda huswile amate nahu kwishile amaso nahukhome nahu bhule, “Loto!” Maafisa bhamwega na hukhome.
MAR 14:66 U Petulo pahali bado panzi pizyala, utumishi umo uwalindu uwa chungaji ugosi ahizile wamwene.
MAR 14:67 Ahalola uPetulo pahiminlele awota umwoto, ahamwenya nahubhelele. Ipo ahayanga na wewe uhali nawa Mnazareti, uYesu”.
MAR 14:68 Lelo akhana, ayanga, “Saga imenye wala siwelewa ahusu hala uhuyanga!” Ipo ahepa abhala huzi wizyala ihada ihakuga.
MAR 14:69 Lelo utumishi uwishishi pala, ahalola ahandile hubhule na dtele bhala abha bhalivhimile pala, “Umuntu unu alipamoja anao!”
MAR 14:70 Lelo akhana natele ndtele pamandi hashe bhala abha hali himilile pala bhali bhahubhula uPetulo, lyali awe ulipamoja anao, “Maana na wewe uli mu Galilaya”
MAR 14:71 Lelo ahandile awibhishe pansi ishigune nawande alape, “Saga imenye umuntu unu uwanuhuyanga.”
MAR 14:72 Ipo ihanda ihakuga ulwabhilye. Ipo Petulo ahizuha izya yangaga gala uYesu agali ahubhula: “Shasili ihanda shisili akuje malahabhili, uzahane mala hatatu.” Ahagwa paka pansi nalile.
MAR 15:1 Nashaphi shausili agosi abhachungaji bhatangana pandwimo nagosi na simbi na bhibalaza sha lyundti ilyangosi. Kisha wakamfunga Yesu wakampeleka kwa Pilato. Pilato akamwuliza, “wewe ni Mfalme wa Wayahudi?”
MAR 15:2 “Ahabhajibu, “Awe unjele isho.”
MAR 15:3 Agosi abhachungaji bhahelezya amashitaka gaminji ju ya Yesu.
MAR 15:4 U Pilato abhuzya nanthele, “Haga ujibu hahundte? Haga ulola ishabha hukata humambo aminji?
MAR 15:5 Lelo uYesu haga ahajibu uPilato, ilya lya syizwa.
MAR 15:6 Nishi ikawaida uwakati uwishikulukulu awigulilya ufungwa omo, ufunga uwalabhile.
MAR 15:7 Wali atulanongwa wijela, palushimo nabha goga muhati bhali asawogopa. Abhatumishila ulozi wao. Ahali umuntu umo uya witwa Barnaba.
MAR 15:8 Ibuga ihenza wa Pilato, na hulavhe abhombe ishabhombaga uwo khosi.
MAR 15:9 U Pilato abha jibu nayanje, “Munza imba fungulile Utawala uwa Yahudi?”
MAR 15:10 Pepo amenye pipo hunongwa ikelo agosi bhachungaji bhakata uYesu nahutwale wamwene.
MAR 15:11 Lelo agosi bha chungaji bhansonjelezya ibunga akhome iholo usauti uje ayigulilye Baranaba bada yamwene.
MAR 15:12 U Pilatoi abhajibu andtele nayanje, “Ibhombe bhuli Utawala Uyahudi?
MAR 15:13 Bhaha bwaga nandtele, “Musulibishe!”
MAR 15:14 U Pilato ayanga, “Abhombile lijambo nshi?” Lelo bhahazida akhome ikelele zaidi na zaidi “Musulubishe.”
MAR 15:15 U Pilato ahanza abhalizisye ibuga, abhigula Baraba. Akhama uYesu nujalindi afumia ili asulubiwe.
MAR 15:16 Askali bhahalogola hadi muhanti izyala (bhula uwali muhati ikambi) bhabhungene pandwemo ishikundi ishasikali.
MAR 15:17 Bhakwatizya uYesu ikhanzu iyilangi izambarau, bhapota inginga imivhwabha kwatizya.
MAR 15:18 Bhanda hulyeule nayanje, “Mwagona, Mutawala uwa Yahudi!”
MAR 15:19 Bhakhoma witwe namenda nahuswile amanti. Bhaha fugama amafugamo witanzi lyakwe huheshimu.
MAR 15:20 Paka pahali bhalyeule, bhahaula ikhanzu ilangi izambarau, nahukwatizye amena gakwe, bhahafumila hunzi abhale husulubisye.
MAR 15:21 Bhalazimisya ajende idala humwavhe, uwa winjila hujini afume hu gunda. Uyawitwa Simoni Mkirene(uyise wakwe Iskanda na Rufo); bhalazimisya anyemule ishikhovhehanyo isha Yesu.
MAR 15:22 Asikali bhahatwala uYesu apawitwa Goligotha (amana gakwe itafsiri ine, mahali ipo yi fuvulitwe).
MAR 15:23 Bhapela ihobwa isangine ni manemane, lelo haga amwela.
MAR 15:24 Bhasubisya bhahagabhana amenda gakwe, bhagakhomela ikula awamule ishi pande ishabha pante shila sikali.
MAR 15:25 Ibhanga ibhala saa tatu nashaphi pabha sulubisyaga.
MAR 15:26 Bhabhiha pamwanya yakwe ulubao ululyasibilye ishitaka “Mutawala wa Yahudi.”
MAR 15:27 Bhasulubisya pandwimo na majambazi bhabhili, umo hukhono ulilo uwinji hukhono ugwa hu mongo gwakwe.
MAR 15:28 
MAR 15:29 Bhope pali bhajenda bhaligaga bhayizyaga, amatwe gao bhayangaga, “Aha! awe bhuhajile uhaibomola ishibhaza hunsiku zitatu,
MAR 15:30 wiyokole bhumwene iyish pansi afume pashi khovhe hanyo!”
MAR 15:31 Inamuna yila agosi bhachungaji bhalyeula bhayangana, pandwimo nasimbi nayanje, “Ahupaga abhanji, Lelo hagawezya awiyupe yuyo.
MAR 15:32 Kilisiti Mtawala wa Israeli, iha panzi ishi fuma pashikhovhehanyo, ilituwezye alole na waamini.” Na bhala abhasulubisye pamoja anao bhalye.
MAR 15:33 Pihafiha isantanda, ikisi ihenza pamwanya insi yundti paka musatisa.
MAR 15:34 Pahafi itisa, uYesu ahakhoma ikelele husauti ingosi, “Eloi, Eloi, lama sabaktani?” ihabhanga namana “Ngulubhi wani, Ngulubhi wani, yenu undeha?”
MAR 15:35 Bhamo abhahimilyile pahuvha bhayanga, “Enya, ahuku ga Eliya.”
MAR 15:36 Umuntu umo anyila, amemia siki mu sponji nabhi she amwanya mwipishi ili la lanzi, ahapela ili mwele. Umuntu umo ahayanga, “Gula tulole khashele Eliya kama awinza humwisye pansi.”
MAR 15:37 Phepo uYesu ahalila nu sauti ingosi afwa.
MAR 15:38 Ipazia lishibhanza lyalyaganiha tupande tubhili afume humwanya hadi panzi.
MAR 15:39 Afisa umo uwahemelele abhelelaga wa Yesu, pahalola huje afile hunamuna ila, ayanjile, “Lyoli unu umuntu ali Mwana wa Ngulubhi.”
MAR 15:40 Bhanga pipo abhashibhali wenya shahutali muhati yao umo ahali. Umaliamu Magdalena, uMaliya (unyina wakwe Yakobo udodo wakwe Yose), na Salome.
MAR 15:41 Uwakati pahali Galialaya bhadajile nahutumishile. Abhashi bhamo abhanji bhambatana nao hadi uYelusalemu.
MAR 15:42 Pawabha lyebhela, pipo lyali wiyandale, isiku kabula isiku Lyatule,
MAR 15:43 U Yusufu wa Arimathaya ahizile pala. Alijumbe uwi Balaza uwaheshimiwaga umuntu uwatalajila utawala wa Ngulubhi husajili abhala wapi ahabhala wa Pilato, ugulabhe ubili ugwa Yesu.
MAR 15:44 U pilato asyiga huje lyoli tayali uYesu afwile ahakuga ola afisa aha bhuzya huje lyoli uYesu afwile.
MAR 15:45 Pawaga uwanalyoli wa afisa aluhusu uYusufu agweje ubili.
MAR 15:46 U Yusufu ali akalile umwenda. Amwisya afume pashikho bhehanyo. Apinya numwenda nahubhishe muhati mukhungwa ilyandibilye mumwamba. Ipo augulusya ingaga pahali pa mahali pakhugwa.
MAR 15:47 U Maliya Magdalena na Maliya unyina wakwe uYose bhahalola amahali pasyilwa uYesu.
MAR 16:1 Uwakati ulutoyo palyafiha, Maliya Magdalena na Maliya unyina wakwe u Yakobo, na Salome, bhahakala anukato aminza, bhahenza nagupashe amafuta ubinle ugwa Yesu pipo bhaza syele.
MAR 16:2 Nashaphi naizashi pisiku ilya wandilo ililungo, bhaha bhala awenye igugwa uwakati isanya shalisile atukule.
MAR 16:3 Bhayangana bhene kwa bhene, “Yunanu uwanza libhungulusye ingaga kwaajili yalitni ili tinjile mungugwa?”
MAR 16:4 Pala pali bhawenya bhahalola umuntu aliungulusye ingaga, ilyali gosi sana.
MAR 16:5 Bha hinjila mukhugwa bhahalola usahala usahala akwete ijoho izelu, akhele upande uwililo, bhasyijiziwa.
MAR 16:6 Abhabhula, “Mungandawogope. Muhumwanza yu Yesu, wa Nazareti, uwabhasulubisye. Azyushele! Numo ipa. Enya pala palibhabhishile.
MAR 16:7 Bhalaji, mubhabhule asundwa bhakwe na Petulo huje abhatangulile abhale Galialaya. Uwo munzahulole, nishi paulaga.”
MAR 16:8 Bhashila nanyile awepe pangugwa bhatetema nasyije hagabhayanga nazimo wa muntu wawundti pipo bhahogopa ntee.
MAR 16:9 Wope pazyuha nashaphii pisiku ilyawande ilungu, afumila asonti u Maliya Magdalene, ula uwabha mwefizye iphepo saba.
MAR 16:10 Uyo akhata idala ahanda abhabhule inongwa bhala abhali pamoja nu mwene, bhope bhalishazinda nalile.
MAR 16:11 Lelo ibho pabhahuvha huje ali mwume, wophe alolile sagahamini.
MAR 16:12 Baada yisho, abhafumila abhandtu bhabhili kati yao anuwaji uwinji, bhope khete idala ilya bhal ehugunda.
MAR 16:13 Bhope ibho bhahashila na habhabhula inongwa bhala abhanji, bhope ibhoha gabhahamini.
MAR 16:14 Pamandi abhoneha nabhala ilongo nomo palibhalya, abhadamila hula asinte nawamini wabho ukhome wimoyo gabho, pipo sahamini bhala abhalolile pazyuha.
MAR 16:15 Abhabhula, “Uje bhalaji mnsi yundti, mulubhelaje inyo wa shila shiumbe.
MAR 16:16 Uya wamini na woziwe aipona uwasiga awa mini ailogwa.
MAR 16:17 Ishi bhoneshelo ishi zyaidagana nebho abhayamini witawa lyani bhayefha iphepo. Bhayanga ijango iphaa.
MAR 16:18 Bhaikhata azhoha hata mwele ahantu hazholo vhisya, hagabhaithuliha kabisa bhaivhiha amakhono pavhinu bhaibhani hafya.”
MAR 16:19 Na uBwana Yesu, baada ya njenao, ahegwa humwanya wingo, akhala hukhono ugwishilume ugwa Ngulubhi.
MAR 16:20 Bhope bhala bhahepa bhalumbilila wundti, Bwana abhomba nao imbombo nao nazyusyelila ineno nivibhoneshelo ivha bhahena nalyo.
LUK 1:1 Afwanaje abhantu abhinji bhabheshela amakhono asebhe eshe tukalibu owe nongwa nelwe mombia gula gagu timiziwe pahati yetu,
LUK 1:2 Neshe bhala shubhatihudithiga bhala bhabhahali bhashahidi bhagalolaga. na bhula atumishi abhalila izu elyufume ahwande.
LUK 1:3 Endolile shinza ane nane, afwanaje ehwiyanzie ulwilyoli amambo ega gonti afume huwandilo husimbire hupanjililo Theafilo hwutukfu.
LUK 1:4 Opate amanye elyoli emambo gala gohasambelezewe.
LUK 1:5 Umwaha gwa Herode, umwene uwa Yudea, palino kohani omo itawa lyakwe Zakaria, uwa tandilane no Abya. No she wakwe bhulibhabhebho ya Haruni, itawa lyakwe Elizabeti.
LUK 1:6 Na hwonti bhabhele bhali bhelyoli hwitagalila elya NGOLOBHE; bhahendeleye ne ndajizwo zwonti ezwa gosi ne ndajizwo lyakwe bila eyaune.
LUK 1:7 Bhape sebhali no mwana eshi Elizabethi ali gomba, na bhonti bhabhule bhali bhagogolo tee.
LUK 1:8 Basi nashi nabhombaga embombo eye ukuhani uwa taratibu uwa tandilane hwakwe hwitagalila elyu NGOLOBHE.
LUK 1:9 Neshe shashahali ekawaida yao eye Ukuhani, ekora ehangweleye ahwinjile mshibhanza esha gosi ili kufukizo uvumba.
LUK 1:10 Na mabungano gonti ega bhantu bhali puta hwonze esaa ya kufukiza uvumba.
LUK 1:11 Wafumilya no malaika uwa gosi ayemeleye upani uwendelo paluputo ya kufukiza.
LUK 1:12 Zakaria nawalola adhugumiye owoga wamwinjiye.
LUK 1:13 Lelo ula umalaika wabhola uganje, “Awogope Zakaria, eshi apute hwaohwo vwehwe. Na ushe waho Uzabeth aihupapila umwana. Olume na itawa lyakwe wayihumweta Yohana.
LUK 1:14 Nawe wabha nolunzongwo na shangwe nabhantu abhinji bhayihusongwa apapwa hwakwe.
LUK 1:15 Kwasababu ayibha gosi hwitagalile gosi sagayimwela idivai wala akholwe wape aimemezewe.
LUK 1:16 Upepo umwololo hata afume mvyanda mwanyi wakwa Na abhini abha Israeli aibhaweziye hwa gosi UNGOLOBHE wao.
LUK 1:17 Wapa aitangulila hwitalilo lyakwe ne roho ye hwa Eliya. Enguvu zwakwe ili agagalusye amoyo gabhuise igabhalile abhana, na abhabheshela bhabhatejile enjele ezye bhelyoli na hubheshele ugosi tayali abhantu bhabhalenganyinziwe.”
LUK 1:18 Zakaria abholele malaika, “Naimayawele izu ulyo eshi endigogolo na ushe wane gogolo wensiku nyinji.”
LUK 1:19 Umalaika wagalula wabhozya, “Ane ne Gabrieli, nenemeleye, hwitagalalilo lya NGOLOBHE. Nane entunuwilye anjanje nawe, na hubhole lenongwa ezi enyinza.
LUK 1:20 Na nyenye, ubhabhe bubu, sobhayanje, mpaka isiku lila nayayibhombeha. Ego kwasababu sewahovwezye enongwa zyane gape gayitimila huwakati wakwe.”
LUK 1:21 Nabhala abhantu bhalibhahugolela uZakaria. Bhaswiga akhalilihwakwe mla mshibhanza.
LUK 1:22 Nawafuma alisagawezya, ayanje nao bhamenye aje. alolile amaono mhati mshibhanza. Wape ahendeleye abhalolesya akhale abhebubu.
LUK 1:23 Zyabha ensiku ezye utumishi wakwe nuzyafiha abhalile akhaya yakwe.
LUK 1:24 Huta ensiku zila ushe wakwe ulizabethi apate evyanda wabha na amezi gasanu. Nawayanga, “
LUK 1:25 Eshi shambombeye UGOSI ensiku zila zyanenyizya esoni yane hwitagalilo elyabhantu.”
LUK 1:26 Umwezi uwa tanda umalaika uGabrieli asontezywe no NGOLOBHE abhalile mpaka mji wa hu Galilaya, itawa lyakwe Nazareti,
LUK 1:27 Hwa rendu ubikira ya pabhiliwa no muntu itawa lyakwe Yusufu. Wa hutali hwa Daudi, na itawa lyakwe ubikira uyo yu Mariamu.
LUK 1:28 Ahinjila munyumba yakwe wayanga, “Mwagona, upewewe eneema! no GOSI alipandwemo nawe.”
LUK 1:29 Wapa ashelile tee afwatana nenongwazyakwe. Asebha humwoyo endamuho ene yeshe.
LUK 1:30 Umalaika abhola, “Ugaje hogope, Mariamu, afwanaje upate eneema afume hwa NGOLOBHE.
LUK 1:31 Enya ubhahweje, uyanda na pape umewna ulume, na itawa lyakwe ubha hwumwete u 'Yesu.'
LUK 1:32 Oyo aibha GOSI abhahwetwe mwana yali humwanya uGOSI UNGOLOBHE alihupela itengo elye umwene u Daudi use wakwe.
LUK 1:33 Abhaitawale ekhaya eya Yakobo wilawila na umwene wakwe sewayibha no umalisholo.
LUK 1:34 UMariamu wabhola umalaika, zibhabhe wele enongwa ezi, afwanaje semenye ulume?
LUK 1:35 UMalaika wajibu wabhola, “Upepo Uselu abhahumwenzele pamwanya yaho, na engulu zyakwe yalipamwanya zibhahu vwenwsye. Neshe izyongozi afwatanaje oyo yayipapwa ayibha zelu mwana wa NGOLOBHE.
LUK 1:36 Antele, enye uholo waho Elizabeti wape apete ulyanda ulya mwana ulume.
LUK 1:37 Afwatanaje nalimo izu lyasagaliwezehala hwa NGOLOBHE.”
LUK 1:38 UMariamu wayanga, “Waga, enye ane endi wembombo wa GOSI. Ebhehuline neshe shoyajele.” Antele umalaika wasogola wabhala hwamwahale.
LUK 1:39 Basi u Mariamu wasogola ensiku ezyo wabhola hata ensi ya humagamba nanali mpaka ensi emo ya hwa Yudea.
LUK 1:40 Winjelo munyumba mwa Zekaria walamuha u Elizabeti.
LUK 1:41 Yabha, Elizabeti nahwovwa hula alamushe kwakwe uMariamu, ahana ahela handa ahwanje mvyanda vyakwe, Elizabeti wamema opepo Uzelu.
LUK 1:42 Wakhola hwizu elyemaha wanyaga usayilye, “Hwabhashe bhonti nawe empapwo yaho esaiwe.
LUK 1:43 Unfumiye izu eli, hata omaye uwu GOSI wane anenzelene?
LUK 1:44 Nenshe izu ilyalamusha gane ahana ahela hanga hasongwelwe mhati mvyanda vyane.
LUK 1:45 Wape nafu yayovyezye neshe naga itimila gabholelwe no GOSI.”
LUK 1:46 Omariamu wayanga, omwoyo gwane gwamwenye ONGOLOBHE,
LUK 1:47 Roho yane esongwezye ONGOLOBHE yanauye ane.
LUK 1:48 Afwanaje agwenyizye unyonge uwe mbombo wakwe. Eshe, enyaga ahwandileshi evikholo vyonti vyayikwizya osayilwe.
LUK 1:49 Afwatanaje owemaha ambombeye amagasi, lyape itawalyakwa lizelu.
LUK 1:50 ERehema zyakwe zidela evikholo ne vikholo hwebho bhahahuputa.
LUK 1:51 Abhombile amaha uhukhono gwakwe; abhanyampenye abhemashento afume masebho ezye moyo gabho.
LUK 1:52 Abhagwisizye agosi mmatengo gabho ageshimwene na nyonge abhabhosezye.
LUK 1:53 Abhenzala abhakutizizye aminza, bhape abhemali abhefwizye makhono wene.
LUK 1:54 Amwavwizye u Israeli uwembombo wakwa ili ahwizushe rehema zyakwe.
LUK 1:55 (Neshe shubhabhozezye ababa bhetu) Ibrahimu empapwo yakwe mpaka welawila.”
LUK 1:56 UMariamu wakhala nawo mpaka amezi gatatu nantele wawela abheale akhayayakwe.
LUK 1:57 Zyabha ensiku ezya pape hwakwe u Elizabeti nazya timila, wapapa umwana lume.
LUK 1:58 Bhahovwezye ajirani na mwabho bhakwe, aje GOSI amwonjezyezye erehema bhasongwa pandwemo nao.
LUK 1:59 Lyabha isiku elya nane wakati wa kutahiri omwana. Bhahanza hupele itawa elyayise, “Zakaria,”
LUK 1:60 Unyino wakwe wagalula wayanga, “Nkashele; seshasho basi ayibha yo Yohana.”
LUK 1:61 Bhabhola sepali amuntu afume hwamwenyu bhaho akwiziwe itawa elya Yohana.
LUK 1:62 Bhamwanya usewakwe sabhu hwmwete.
LUK 1:63 Wanza ahabampa wasimba aje, “itawa lyakwe yo Yohana.” Bhaswijitie bhonti.
LUK 1:64 Pepo na pepo ilomu lyakwe liguha numele lyakwe antele wanda ayaje. Nautelele ONGOLOBHE.
LUK 1:65 Bhinjilwa nowoga bhonti bhali bhakheye pandwemo, na. mambo ego gonti gatangazezwe ensi yonti yammagamba mgamba e Yudea.
LUK 1:66 Na bhonti bhabhagovwezye bhagabheha humoyo gabho, bhayanga, “Umwana uno ayibha wefwane hwele?” Afwaneje ukhono ogwa GOSI gwali pandwemo no mwane.
LUK 1:67 UZakaria uyise wamema opepo ozelu, wakuwawanyanga,
LUK 1:68 “Abhosewe OGSI, ONGOLOBHE wa Israeli, afwanaje abhenzeye abhantu bhakwe na bhaule.
LUK 1:69 Atemelesezye empeta eyataule afume mlyango ugwa Daudi, uwe mbombo wakwe.
LUK 1:70 Nenshe ayanjile afume huwandilo hwilumu elyakuwe akuwe bhakwe azelu.
LUK 1:71 Tisatulwe na bhibhi bhentu na mma khono gabho bhonti bhabhativitwa
LUK 1:72 Ili abhabhombele aminza ababa bhetu na hwizushe ipatano lyakwe izelu,
LUK 1:73 Ishilapo shalapiye Ibrahimu uyise wetu.
LUK 1:74 Afwanaje anzatavwilizya ate taushe nimakhono gabhibhi bhetu na humpute bila woga.
LUK 1:75 Nazelu nelyoli hwitagalilo lyakwe ensiku zyonti.
LUK 1:76 Nawe, womwana wahwetwa, ukuwe ukuwe wakwe yalimwanya, afwaneje awa wayitangulila hwita galila humaso ega GOSI ulenga nyizizye amadala gakwe,
LUK 1:77 Obhabhozye abhantu bhakwa usatule aje asajilwe embibhi zyabho.
LUK 1:78 Hwidala elye rehema lya NGOLOBHE wetu, afwatanaje hwezyo okhozyo lwalufumile amwanya lutifishiye,
LUK 1:79 Abhakhozye bhabhakhala hukisi hunzunda eyenfwa. nagalongozwa unamana getu hwidala ilinza.”
LUK 1:80 Ula, mwana wakula wonjelela amaha roho wakhala humapoli hata hwisiku elye fumila hwakwe u Israeli.
LUK 2:1 Enku zila endajizyo zyafumile hwa Kaisari Agusto ya je esimbwe eye matawa aga bhantu wonti mnsi.
LUK 2:2 Hii ilikuwa ene ebabhe ya hwande yehasimbwilwe epo Krenio nali liwali wa hushamu.
LUK 2:3 Abhantu wonti bhabhalile ahwinsimbisizye shila muntu amwao.
LUK 2:4 UYusufu wape asogoye hu galilaya afume hushijiji sha hu Nazareti azubhile abhale huu Yudea hadi humji ugwa Daudi, gukwiziwa Bethelehemu, afwatanaje umwahale wahutayari namwao abhahwa Daudi.
LUK 2:5 Ili asimbwe pandwemo no Mariamu, ushe wakwe bhapabhiliye wape ano lwanda.
LUK 2:6 Shabha katika akhale ohwo ensiku zyakwe ezya pape zya fishile.
LUK 2:7 Wapapa umwana wakwe uwahwande, wavwenesya amenda agubha na wagonia mwitori mwanzilela eng'ombe, afwanaje sebhapete enafsi munyumba ezya jenyi.
LUK 2:8 Na ensi yeyela, bhahali adimi bhakhalaga mwipoli na linde ikundi lwao bhatandilunaga nosiku.
LUK 2:9 Umalaika wa GOSI abhafumiye, nanali uzelu wa GOSI wabhakhozizye epande zyonti, bhinjilwa nowoga ogosi.
LUK 2:10 Umalaika abhabholele, “Mganje ahigope, afanaje ane embaletela enongwa enyinza eya she engosi yayayibho hwabantu wonti.
LUK 2:11 Eshe sanyono mnsi eya Daudi! apepwe kwa jili eyahulimwe uwataule wape yu Kristo GOSO!
LUK 2:12 Na ene ndiyo ndago hwilimwe, mbhahu mwaje umwa umwela bhavwenesyezye amenda ageshiwela agonile mwitori mwelela eng'ombe.
LUK 2:13 Nantele bhahali pandwemo nayo omalaika abhinji ajeshi abhamwanya bhahutelela ONGOLOBHE, na ya je,
LUK 2:14 “ Ayemehwaje ONGOLOBHE amwanya, na pansi ehwe amani hwabhantu bhabhagalile.”
LUK 2:15 Shabha, omalaika ebho na bhasogola abhule hwabho amwanya bhala udimi bhabholene, “Eshe sali mpaka Bethlehemu, tilirole elwo lwali bhombeshe lyati bhonezyezye ONGOLOBHE.”
LUK 2:16 Bhabhalile nanali, bhamwanjile oMariamu no Yusufu, nola umwana umwela agonile mwitori.
LUK 2:17 Na walipomwona bhafumizye enongwa yabhabholelwe afwatone nomwana oyo.
LUK 2:18 Wonti bhabhahovwezye bhaswijile hwago gabhobholelwe na dimi.
LUK 2:19 Lelo o Mariamu wazibhaha humwoyo gwakwe.
LUK 2:20 Bhala adimi bhawelile ohu bhahusomba ONGOLOBHE na hutelile humombo gonti gabhovwezye na galale eshe shabhabholelwe.
LUK 2:21 Hata nazyafishele ensiku nana ezya hutahiri ahetelwe tawa lwakwe Yesu, neshe nahetelwe no malaika sasele abhe lwanda.
LUK 2:22 Alafu nazyafishele ensiku hwabho, neshe sheri endogo ya anusa bhabhalile nao mpaka Yerusalemu bhabheshele OGOSI.
LUK 2:23 Neshe nshesibwilwe mdogo ya GOSI, “Shila mwana ulume wali lwanda ulwahwanda hwanyinawakwe akwiziwaje Golosu wa GOSI.”
LUK 2:24 Bhafumye sadaka neshe sheyajile katika endogo eya GOSI, “Enko nda bhabhele au makind abhenjebha bhabhele.”
LUK 2:25 Enya, pala payerusalemu palinomntu itawa lyakwe akwiziwaga Simoni. Umuntu ono alihwelyoli na humpute ONGOLOBHE. Umwahole agolaga ya zizya wa Israeli, na upepo uzelu ali pamwana yakwe.
LUK 2:26 Yali imalishe abhoneshewe hwakwe ahilile hupepo uzelu aje umwahale saga ehenzaga afwe bila hulole Kristi wa GOSI.
LUK 2:27 Isikulimo ahenzele mhatimwibhaiza alongozehwe no pepo uzelu. ambapo ayise bhakwe bhaletile umwana oYesu hubhombele gala gagahanziwuga mkawaida eye ndogo,
LUK 2:28 Eshi o Simioni aposheye mmakhono gakwe na hulimbe ONGOLOBHE na yanje,
LUK 2:29 “Eshi nduhusu nemtumwa waho embale mshinza alengane nizu lyaho.
LUK 2:30 Afwatanaje amaso gane gahalile uwaule waho,
LUK 2:31 Afwanaje uonesha humaso gabhantu bhonti.
LUK 2:32 Umwahale rukhozyo mataifa na bhe zelu wabhantu bhakwe Israeli.”
LUK 2:33 UYise nonyine wakwe bhali bhaswiga ego gagayangwilwe juu yakwe.
LUK 2:34 OSimoni wabhasaila abhabhola Mariamu unyina wakwe, “Eye ono abhehwelwe wagwe na bhoshe abhinji bhabali kati Israeli na bhe mbonesyo zyazya yiyangwa.
LUK 2:35 Nawe hwehwe imaje lwaijila humwoyo gwaho ilizibhoneshe esebho ezya moyo aga bhinji.”
LUK 2:36 Ahali ukuwa ushe itawa lyakwe Ana uledu wa Fanueli wa shikholo sha Asheri. Nu umri wakwe alina maha minji. Akheye nolume amaha saba baada eyelendu wakwe,
LUK 2:37 Wape fwele owemaha amarongo nane na mahaganne. Sasogolo mwibhanza ila aputa usiku no sanya na funje na labhe.
LUK 2:38 Oyo afumele sala yeyo asalifizye ONGOLOBHE. Na wonti bhali bhahwenyelezya eshahwaulwe katika Yerusalemu abhafumizyo enongwa zyakwe.
LUK 2:39 Basi nabhamala gonti gagalajiziwe aga mndongozi eya GOSi, bhahwelile hu Galilaya, mpaka iboma lwao, Nazareti.
LUK 2:40 Ola umwana wakula, na hwonjele amahaa amemile enshinshi, na neema ya NGOLOBHE yali juu yakwe.
LUK 2:41 Basi ayise bhakwe bhabhala hu Yerusalemu shila mwaha uwakati uweshikurukuru ya Pasaka.
LUK 2:42 Na fishiye umri wakwe amaha kumi na gabhle bhazubhile neshe sheli emila eye shikurukuru.
LUK 2:43 Nabhamalila ensiku wakati uwahwele hwabhoola umwana uYesu asageye hwisaro ohwo hu Yerusalemu na bhayise bhakwe sebhalolene.
LUK 2:44 Bhape bhamenyeje bhalipandwemo mshora, bhabhalile enjendo uwisiku lyonti bhanda humwanza mwa mwabho.
LUK 2:45 Nu sebhamwanga bhahwelile hu Yerusalemu ohu bhahumwanza.
LUK 2:46 Yabha na zyafiha ensiku zitatu, bhalola mwibhinza, akheye pahati ya manyizi, abhatejelezya nabhabhozye amaswali.
LUK 2:47 Wape wonti bhabhamwovwaga bhanswijile uwelewa wakwe na amajibu gakwe.
LUK 2:48 Na bhalolile, bhanswijile. Nonyina wakwe wabhola, “Mwana wane, mbone otibhombeye eshi? enye, uyise waho nane talili humwanza uzugumie”
LUK 2:49 Wabhabhola, “Yenu mnanza sagamwamenye aje ehwanziwa akhale munyumba eya yise wane?
LUK 2:50 Unape sebhalyelewe izu elyo lyabha bhozezye.
LUK 2:51 Hwiho pandwemo nabho mpaka hu Nazareti wape ali abeshimu, onyina agabheshele ego gonti humwoyo gwakwe.
LUK 2:52 Wape uYesu wazidi ahwonjelele katika hekima kimo, wapendezya ONGOLOBHE na bhantu.
LUK 3:1 Umwaha, ugwa kumi na tano owalongozye hwakwe Kaisari Tiberia, Pantio Pilato nali liwali owayahudi, na Herode omwene owa Galilaya, no Filipo oholo wakwe omwene uwa Iturea nensi eya Trakoniti, na Lisania no mwene owa Abilene,
LUK 3:2 Wakati owa kohani ogosi owa anasi no Kayafa, izu elya NGOLOBHE lya fishiye oYohana omwana owa Zakaria, mwipoli.
LUK 3:3 Afishele mnsi yonti yelikaribu ne Yordani, alombeleye owoziwa owa lete usajilwa olwa hwefwe embibhi.
LUK 3:4 Neshe shahwasimbilwe chuo eshe mazu aga kuwe Isaya, “Izu ya mntu wali mwipoli, “Lilenganyi idala elya GOSI, gagalosyaji omwashile hwakwe.
LUK 3:5 Entebha yonti yayimema nigamba nagamba hayisiwa, papatejile payibha pagoloshe papakwanyushe paile nganiha.
LUK 3:6 Bhonti abhebele bhayihulo owaule owa NGOLOBHE.”
LUK 3:7 Basi, abhabholele amabongano bhala bhabhaliye ili abhoziwe amwe mpapwo wenzoha wenu yabhasundile amwe ayinjile enkuni yehayenza?
LUK 3:8 Basi fumyaje amadondo gagahwanziwa ulusajilo, wala mgajeahwanza ayanje mmoyo genyu, “Tilinawo udada uIbrahimu eshi embabhola yaje amawe ega, ONGOLOBHE abhajiye ahwubhosrzye uIbrahimu abhana.
LUK 3:9 Neshi etwanga tayari ebhehwelwe pamashinshi age makwi. Basi, kila likwi lya sagalipapa amadondo aminza, lidumlwa nalitaje mmwoto.
LUK 3:10 Amabungano gabhozya, “Tikhozye wole eshi?”
LUK 3:11 Wabhajibu wabhabhozya, “Yali na magolola gabhele na apele yasaga aunigolola yali nevyalye wape abhombe eshoshesho.”
LUK 3:12 Bhabhasonjezya bhape bhenza ahwoziwe, bhabhozya,”Manyiziji, tubhombe yenu ate?
LUK 3:13 Wabhabhola, “Mgaje sonjezye ahantu zaidi ya hata hahapangwilwe.
LUK 3:14 Asikali bhape bhabhozya bhayanga, “ate nate tibhombe wele? Wabhabhole msafwele omntu wala msashitake ilenka antele myanje no mshahara gwenyu.”
LUK 3:15 Basi, abhantu nabhali bhabhagola gaganzafumile, wonti bhasega sebhaga mmoyo gabho enongwa ezya Yohana nkashe umwene Kristi.
LUK 3:16 UYohana wagalula wabhabhozya bhonti lyoli ane embozya namenze lelo ahwenza ohwemaha ashile ane sembwezizye ayengezye olwabho olye vilato vyakwe. omwahale ayibhoziwa hupepo ozelu no mwoto.
LUK 3:17 Afwanaje ubheto lwakwa lulimakho no wape ayozya tee mhati yakwe na bhonganye engano yakwe. Mshanga, antele amapetelo aigapemba mmwoto gwa sagaguzima.
LUK 3:18 Basi hurusundo hugamwabho aminji, abhalombeleye abhantu.
LUK 3:19 Lelo omwene oHerode akhalipiwe nomwe kwajili ya Herode, ushe wa holo wakwe, namabhibhi gonti gabhombile o Herode.
LUK 3:20 Ahonjezye eli neli afunjile oyohani mwijela.
LUK 3:21 Bhabhantu wonti bhabhamaushe ahinziwe no Yesu wape ahoziwe wape alabhile emwanya zya higushe.
LUK 3:22 Upepo uzelu ahishile pamwanya yakwe hufwano ongwebelebele, neshe enjebha izu lya fumile amwanya, “Awe wemwana wane wegene. Ensogwezewe nawe.”
LUK 3:23 No Yesu yoyo nahandile amanyizye, ali apate umri wakwe neshe amaha salathini. ategemelwa ajemwana wa Yusufu, wa Eli,
LUK 3:24 Wo Mathati, walawi, wa MeIki, wayana wa Yusufu,
LUK 3:25 Wa Matathia, wa Amosi, wa Nahumu, wa Esli, wa Nagai,
LUK 3:26 Wa Maati, wa Matathia, wa Semeini, wa Yusufu, wa Yuda,
LUK 3:27 Wa Yohana, wa Rese, wa Zerubabeli, wa SheaItieli, wa Neri,
LUK 3:28 MeIki, wa Adi, wa Kosamu, wa Elmadamu, wa Eri,
LUK 3:29 Wa Yoshua, wa Eliezeri, wa Yorimu, wa Matathi, wa Lawi,
LUK 3:30 Wa Simioni, wa Yuda, wa Yusufu, wa Yonamu, wa Eliyakimu,
LUK 3:31 Wa Melea, wa Mena, wa Matatha, wa nathani, wa Daudi,
LUK 3:32 Wa Yese, wa Obedi, wa Boazi wa Salmoni, wa Nashoni,
LUK 3:33 Wa Abinadabu, wa Aramu, wa Hesroni, wa Peresi, wa Yuda,
LUK 3:34 Wa Yakobo, wa Isaka, wa Ibrahimu, wa Tera, wa Nahori,
LUK 3:35 Wa Seruig, wa Ragau, wa Pelegi, wa Eberi, wa Sala,
LUK 3:36 Wa Kenani, wa Arfaksadi, wa Shemu, wa Nuhu, wa Lameki,
LUK 3:37 Wa Methusela, wa Henoko, wa Yaredi, wa Mahalalei, wa Kenani,
LUK 3:38 Wa Enoshi, wa Sethi, wa Adamu, wa NGOLOBHE.
LUK 4:1 UYesu amemile upepo uzelu, ahwelile afume hu Yordani, alongoziwe no pepo omuda ohwe nsiku arobaini mwipoli.
LUK 4:2 Apete amalabha no shetani. Nensiku ezyo sagalyanga ahantu mpaka nazyamalishe alolile enzala.
LUK 4:3 Oshetani wabholankoli, “Mwana wa NGOLOBHE, libhole ihwe eli wahe libumnga.”
LUK 4:4 UYesu agalula, “isimbwilwe: 'eyaje umntu sagaikhala hwibumunda tu.'”
LUK 4:5 Wizavwa pamwanya wabhonesya emilki zyonti ezyensi hudaka emo.
LUK 4:6 Oshetani wabhola, “Embahupele ahweenzi ene yonti, nefahari yakwe. Afanaje ehweli makhono gane, nane ehupele yayonti neshe shensongwele.
LUK 4:7 Basi ahwe nkoni namile hwitagalila lyane gonti ganzabhe gahuliwe.”
LUK 4:8 UYesu wagalula wabhola isimbwilwe, “omwinamile, “OGOSI ONGOLOBHE waho ompute omwahale mwene.”
LUK 4:9 Walongozya mpaka Yerusalemu wabheha pamwanya yemnala eshe shibhanza,” wabhola nkashile olimwana wa NGOLOBHE hwiponye pasi.
LUK 4:10 afwanaje esimbwilwe”, abhahwu lajizizye amalaika bhakwe bhalinde,
LUK 4:11 Na fwanaje, makhono gabho bhanzahumweje, osije ogabomula inama, lwaho mwiwe.”
LUK 4:12 OYesu wagalula, “Wabhashole, “eyagwilwe oganje hulenje GOSI ONGOLOBHE waho.”
LUK 4:13 Basi nawamala kila esha hulenje oshetani walehe wabhala humuda.
LUK 4:14 OYesu awelile humaha age opepo ozelu, wabhala hu Galilaya enongwa zyakwe zyazyambanile ensi zyonti ezya msheje msheje.
LUK 4:15 Wape asambelezyaga katika mmabhanza gabho ashimihwagwa nabhantu bhonti.
LUK 4:16 Wabhala hu Nazareti, epo pasongwelwe na isiku elye lutozyo hwinjila mwabhonza neshe sehali edeesturi yakwe wemelela ili abhazye.
LUK 4:17 Bhapela chuo esha akuwa Isaya, hwigula echuo, wanza papa simbwilwe,
LUK 4:18 Opepo owa GOSI au pamwanya yane afwatanaje amponyizye amafuta abhalombelele apena enongwa enyinza, antumile abhatangazizye bhabhapi nyilwe abhaule hwabho. Avipofu bhalolaje nantele abhaleshe bhashe huru bhabhabhonelwe.
LUK 4:19 Na tangazya omwaha ogwa GOSI gwagweteshehwe.
LUK 4:20 Washigalilo echuo, wahwezezya amtumishi wakhala, na bhantu bhonti bhabhahali mwisinagogi bhalangulila.
LUK 4:21 Wanda abhabhole sanyono ensimbo,”Ezi zitimiliye mmakutu genyu.”
LUK 4:22 Bhalola bhonti bhaswiga amazu age neema gagafumile mwilomu lyakwe, bhayanga ono semwana wa Yusufu?
LUK 4:23 Abhabhola, “bila shaka mbhambole eshilale eshi,” Ganga, hwiponye omwoyo gwaho, amambo gonti gatovwezye aje gabhombeshe hu Kapernaumu, gabhombeshe nepa na ntele katika ensi yaho wewe.”
LUK 4:24 Wayanga, “Amina embabhola aje nomo okuwa yabhahweteshewe mnsi ya kwa yoyo,”
LUK 4:25 Lelo lyoli embabhola bhahali afwele bhalibhinji katika ensi eya Israeli amaha aga Eliya, wakati amabhengo gafugwilwe amaha gatatu na miezi sita, enzala engosi yahinjiye ensi yonti.
LUK 4:26 Wala oEliya sagasontezyewe hwebho, ila hwafwele omo owa Sarepta katika ensi eya Sidoni.
LUK 4:27 Antele, bhahali abheukoma bhinji mwi Israeli omwaha wa kuwa Elisha, wala nomo yaponi ila oNaamani omntu wa Siria.
LUK 4:28 Bhamemile ilyoyo bhonti bhabhahali mwibhanza nabhovwa ego.
LUK 4:29 Bhasogola bhafumya hwonze eye boma bhantwala mpaka mshenje eyigamba, afanaje ekhaya yao enzegwilwe pamwanya yakwe, ili bhapate hutaje pansi.
LUK 4:30 Lelo omwahale ashilile pahati yao wabhola.
LUK 4:31 Hwiha mpaka hu Kaeernaumu, iboma elya Galilaya. Wabha asambelezwa isiku elya tunzye.
LUK 4:32 Bhanswiga nantele hunsambelezyo zyakwe, afwanaje izu lyakwe lili namaha.
LUK 4:33 Na mhati mwibhanza, mwoli omntu yali ne roho embibhi walila hwizu igosi,
LUK 4:34 “ Wayanga leha, endineye awe, u Yese wa Nazareti? uyenzele atitezye? Emenye aje hwewenu! wogolosu wa NGOLOBHE!”
LUK 4:35 QYesu wadamila, “Wayanga, biba ilomu mwepe ndipo lila!”Ipepo lya gwisya pahati, lyafuma asimbhombe nkahamo.
LUK 4:36 Bhakhatwa naswije bhont, bhayangana, bhayanga lizu hwele eli, afwatanaje, “abhatanga amapepo abhibhi huwezo na maha bhape bhafuma.”
LUK 4:37 Enongwa, zyakwe zyazyambona hwonti munsi ela.
LUK 4:38 Wafuma mwibhanza winjila munyumba ya Simoni. Wape, okhoi wakwe oSimoni onyina washe wakwe, akhetwe nensugusa ekhali bhalabha kwajili yakwe.
LUK 4:39 Hwemelela, papepe nao, waidamila ela ensugasa, yaleha mara eyo wapona wabhabhombela.
LUK 4:40 Na isanya nalya swanga, wonti bhali nabhinu abhe mpongo shahashaha bhabhaletile hwamwahale. Wabhabheha amakhon gakwe pamwanya ya shila mntu wabhaponia.
LUK 4:41 Ipepo bhape bhafumela mwabhantu abhinji bhakhoma ibwago nayanje, “Awe uli mwana wa NGOLOBHE!” Wabhadamila sagaleshile aje bhayangaje, kwasababu bhamanye aje yo Krisi.
LUK 4:42 Na hwasha, asogoye abhalile humo hwasehulina bhantu. Amabongano bhabha bhahumwanza bhafihahwamurahale bhazaga huzubhile agajesogola hwabhahale.
LUK 4:43 Wabhabhola, “Ehwanziwa alombelele enongwa enyinza ezya mwene uwa NGOLOBHE katika amaboma agamwabho nantele, afwanaje ensotelezewe.
LUK 4:44 “Basi ali alombelela katika amabhanza aga hu Uyahudi.
LUK 5:1 Yabha amabongono bhasonshezya alitejelezye izu elya NGOLOBHE, omwahule ali ayemeleye panshenje eye eyi dimi lya Genezareti.
LUK 5:2 Walola evyelelo vibhele vikheye panshenje eyi dimi. Lelo bhabhahwonza bhafumile bhahwozya enyavu zyabho.
LUK 5:3 Winjila mshelelo shimo, esho shakwe oSimoni, wamwanza ashibhesha hutali hashe neshe. Wakhala wabhamanyinzya mambongano ohu alimshelelo.
LUK 5:4 Hata nawamala ayanje, abholile oSimoni, “Isya mpaka pansi tee mwisye enyavuzyenyu mwonze esamaki.”
LUK 5:5 OSimoni wagalula wabhola, Gosi, tibhombile embombo eyalisye nosiku wonti setipete nkahamo, lelo hwizu lyaho ehwisya enyavu.
LUK 5:6 Basi nabhabhomba esho bhazyajile esamaki ziminji tee enyavu zyao zya hundile adumushe.
LUK 5:7 Bhabhapunjila okhono amwabho bhali mshombo esha bhele. bhenze abhavwe bhenzu bhavimemya vyonti vibhele hata nyahandile andwine.
LUK 5:8 OSimoni oPetro, na walola ego, agwiye pamafugamo ga Yesuwanyanga sogala hwiline, “Afwatanaj, ane endi mntu uwembibhi GOSI.”
LUK 5:9 Afwanaje akhetwe nenswigo, umwahale nabhonti bhabhali pa ndwemo nawo kwa sababu eyewinji uwesamaki wabhazyajili.
LUK 5:10 Antele Yakobo no Yohana bha Zebedao, bhali pandwemo no Simoni. O Yesu wabhola Simoni, “ogaje hwogope, afume eshi obhabha wahwonza abhantu.”
LUK 5:11 Hata nabhali bhavisagamishe pwani, evyelelo vyabho bhavileha vionti bhabhenjelela.
LUK 5:12 Yabha nahali humiongo ye maboma gala enya, palinomntu amemile ukoma, wape nawalola oYesu, agwiye dumbula walabha waga, GOSI,” nkohwanza owezizye anozye.”
LUK 5:13 Kisha Yesu alinyoosha mkono wake na kumugusa, akisema, “Nataka. Takasika.” Na saa ileile ukoma ukamwacha.
LUK 5:14 “Wakhana agaje hubhole omuntu, ila bhalaga ahwibhonesya hwa kohani, “ufumye, kwajili eya pone hwaho neshe oMusa shabhabholele ebhe ushuda, hwabhahale.”
LUK 5:15 Lelo enongwa zyakwa zyazida abwaje bhatangene amabongono aminji bhatejelezye na pone empungo zyabho.
LUK 5:16 Ilelo omwahale ali ahwiyefwa wabhala pasepali bhantu walabha.
LUK 5:17 Yabha isiku lila limo ali asambelezya na amafarisayo na amanyizi abhe ndongo bhali bhakheye epo, bhabhafumile kila shijiji eshe Galilaya na Yudea, na hu Yerusalemu. Na amaha aga GOSI wahali apate aponie.
LUK 5:18 Na enya, bhenza abhantu bhanyatiye mshitanda omntu yapoozile, bhahanzaga hutwale mhati na hubheshe hwitagalila lyakwe.
LUK 5:19 Hata nabhakosile enafsi eyahutwale mhati kwali eya mabungano ege bhantu bhazubhile hwigolo bhagefwa amatofali agapamwanya bhaswisya umwahale neshi tande shakwe pahati hwitagalila hwa Yesu.
LUK 5:20 Wape nalolile olweteho lwabho abhhdde, “Ee rafiki, usajilwe embibhi zyaho.”
LUK 5:21 Basi bhala asimbi na Mafarisayo bhada ayangane, “Aje wenu ono yayanga amazu agalije? Wenu yagasajila embibhi aliyo NGOLOBHE mwene?”
LUK 5:22 Na o Yesu, omenye onongwa zyabho wabhagalula wabhabhole, mhwibhozya yenu lumoyo genu?
LUK 5:23 Lyalili lyalolo lyalilihu, 'Aje usajilwe embibhi zyaho au aje sogola ubhale?'
LUK 5:24 Lelo mpate amanye aje omwana wa Adamu anazyo endajizo pansi epa ezya sajile embibhi, abholele, 'Ola ya poozile sogolahwitweshe eshitanda shaho bhalaga akhaya yaho.'
LUK 5:25 Shesho wemelela hwitagalila lyabho wahwitwehe shhila shagoneye wabhala akhaya yakwe ohwo wa mwembela ONGOLOBHE.
LUK 5:26 Wonti bhakhetwa na nswije bhateleye ONGOLOBHE. Bhamemele nowoga, bhayanga, “Sanyono tilolile amambo age ajabu.”
LUK 5:27 Baada yego wafuma walola yasonjezya esonga, itawa lyakwe yolawi akheye forodhani, wabhola nbejezye.”
LUK 5:28 Walehe vyonti wasogola wabheni ezya.
LUK 5:29 Na Lawi wabhombela eshikurunkuru eshigosi mnyumba yakwe hwali abungono ogosi, owa sonjezye esonga na bhuntu abhamwabho bhali bhakheye pashalye pandwemo nawo.
LUK 5:30 Yabha afarisayo na simbi bhabho bhabha bhabha una asambilizi wa bhakwe baje mbona mlyana mwele pandwemo nabhabhasonjezya esonga na bhubhali nembibhi?”
LUK 5:31 OYesu agalula wabhabhola, “Bhabhali bhinza sebhani nehaja eyaponywe, ila bhala bhabhinile.
LUK 5:32 Senahenzele abhakwinzye abhelyoli bali bhahali nembibhi bhapato alambe.”
LUK 5:33 Bhape bhabhola, “Asambelewa abha Yohana bhafunga maranyinji, na labhe eputo bhpe asambelewa abha Farisayo bhafunga. Lelo asambelewa bhaho bhalya nu mwele.”
LUK 5:34 LelooYesu abhubholele, “Mwagaga mgabhabhambo aje bhafunje bhabha anilye huhweji wakati ahweli ogosi owehweji pandwemo nao?
LUK 5:35 Lelo ennsiku zihwenza nayepe ogosi owehweje epo pabha ifunga ensiku ezyo.”
LUK 5:36 Wabhabhola eshilale. “Nomo yazembula shilakaeshi omwenda opya nabheshe mmwenda okolo na nkashile abheshele lila ipya. Na shila ishiraka sha omwenda opya, selilenganya na gula omwenda okolo.
LUK 5:37 Wala, nomo omntu yaponya edivai empya katika evyelelo evikolo. Na nkashile waponya ela, edivai empya ebha vibazule vila evyenlelo, edivai enyahale ebhahwitishe na vyelelo nibhanachishe.
LUK 5:38 Lelo edivai epya uwinza uwaponye katika evye lelo evipya.
LUK 5:39 Wala nomo yamwela edivai eyemwaha alafu ayisongwe epya, atafanaje ayanga ela eya mwaha, 'Yenyiza.”
LUK 6:1 Lyabha isiku elyatozye limo ali ashila katika mmagonda, asambelezyewabhakwe bhali bhadenya amasale na galye bhabhabhapalula mmakhono gabho.
LUK 6:2 Basi bhamo afarisayo bhabhabholo, “Mbona mbhomba lya selinza isiku elyatozye”?
LUK 6:3 OYesu, wabhagalula, wabhabhola, “Semwabhazizye hata lwelyo lyabhomile oDaudi nali nenzala, omwahale na bhala bhali nabho?
LUK 6:4 Jinsi shahinjiye katika enyumba eye NGOLOBHE, wega amabumunda gala agalanjizye wagalya, wabhapela nebho amwabho wakati seshinza agalye ila hwa Kuhani bene basi.”
LUK 6:5 Wabhabhola, “Amwana uwa Adamu yayoyo OGOSI owa tofye.”
LUK 6:6 Yabha isiku elyatozye elyamwabho ahinjiye mwisingogi wamanyizya na mwali omntu ambaye okho. Ogwakwe ogwendelo upozile.
LUK 6:7 Na simbi na bhafarisayo bhali bhauzijila ili balole aje abhaponie isiku elyatozye, li bhazyaje enongwa zyautake.
LUK 6:8 Lelo omwahale wagamanya gabhasebha wabhola ola yapoozile okhono, “Sogola, emelela pahati wasogola.”wemelela.
LUK 6:9 Eshi OYesu wabhabhola, “Embabozya amwe eshi, shinza isiku elyatozya abhombe aminza au abhombe amabhibhi, aponie omwoyo au atezye,
LUK 6:10 “Walangulila amaso wonti.”Epande zyonti wabhola ola omntu, golozya okhono gwaho wagolozya akhono gwakwe gwabha gwinza natele.
LUK 6:11 Lelo bhamemile nenkuni bhaynyana bhebho hwa bhebho bhabhombe we le Oyesu.
LUK 6:12 Yali ensiku zila asogoye abhalile mwigamba ili alabha. Ahendeleye osiku wonti hulabhe ONGOLOBHE.
LUK 6:13 Nayali sampwiti, abhakwizizye asambelezewe bhakwe, hwumwahale na abhasaluye kumi na bhabhele kati yabho bhebho nantele abhakwizizye “Bhamwa.”
LUK 6:14 Amatawa gabhala atumwa gali oSimioni (ambaye antele akwizizye yo Petro) no Andrea no holo wakwe, oYakobo, oYohana, oFilipo, oBartolomayo,
LUK 6:15 OMathayo, oTomaso, no Yakobo omwa wa Alfayo, oSimioni, ola okwiziwaga yo Zelote,
LUK 6:16 OYuda omwana wa Yakobo na oYuda oIskariote, ola yali goji.
LUK 6:17 Nantele oYesu ahishile pandwemo nabho afume hwigamba na hwemelele papali ntebha. Idadi engosi eyasambelezewa bhakwe (walikuwa huko, pamoja naidadi kubwa ya watu kutoka Uyahudi na Yerusalemu, na kutoka pwani ya Tiro na Sidoni.)
LUK 6:18 Na bhala bhabhalebhile ni mpepo embibhi. Bhaponizye.
LUK 6:19 Shila omo bhabhali pibhongano arenjele hu palamasye afwatanaje nguvu ezyaponye zyali zifuma mhati yakwe na aponizye bhonti.
LUK 6:20 Esho wabhenya amnyiziwa bhakwe, na yanje, “Msayilwe amwe mwemli bhapene, afwatanaje umwene owa NGOLOBHE wenyu.
LUK 6:21 Msayilwe amwe mwemli nenzala eshi, afwanaje mwakuta msayilwe mwemlila eshi. Afwanaje mwayiseha.
LUK 6:22 Msayilwe amwe ambao abhantu na yibhavitwa na bhahagule na bhalongonye amwe aje mlibhabhibhi kwajili ya omwana wa Adamu.
LUK 6:23 Shanji katika isiku elyo na rushe rushe nashe afwatanaje lyoli mwayibha ne thawabu egosi amwanya, afwanaje aise bhabho bhabhabhombeye shesho akuwa.
LUK 6:24 Lelo hele amwe mwemli bhatakili! Afwatanaje mmalishe ahweje ensombo zyenyu.
LUK 6:25 Aheli amwe mwemkute eshi! afwanaje mwayilola enzala hwitagalila. Aheli amwe mwemseha eshi! Afwanaje mwayizonda naline hwitagalila.
LUK 6:26 Aheli amwe, na mwasombwa nabhantu wonti! Afwanaje aYise bhabho bhabhabhombeye akuwa abhilenka shesha.
LUK 6:27 Lelo eyanga hwilimwe amwe mwemn tejelezya, bhagani abhibhi bhenyu na bhabhombele aminza bhabhavitwa.
LUK 6:28 Bhasayilaji bhala bhabhaswita amwena bhalabhilaji bhala bhabhabonela.
LUK 6:29 Hwamwahale ola yahukhoma imbuguzi limo, ugalusizyaje elyabhele. Neshe omntu ahufyola igolole lyaho opanje nelyabhele.
LUK 6:30 Opanje shila ya hulabha. Neshe omntu nkahufyola ahantu ambaho hahuliwe uganje alabha aje awezyezye.
LUK 6:31 Nenshe samsongwa abhantu aje sabhabhabhombele, namwe mubhombaje shesho.
LUK 6:32 Nkashe mubhaganaabhantu bhabhaibhaga na amwe tu, esho ihawobu shi hwilimwe? Afwanaje hata bhabhibhi bhabha gana bhala bhabhagana.
LUK 6:33 Nkashile mubhabhombela bhala bhabhabhombela amwe aminza esho abhabhe thawabu nshi hwilimwe? Afwanaje hata bhabhibhi bhabhombashesho.
LUK 6:34 Nkashile mkhopezya evintu hwabhantu ambabho mpambamala aje bhanza abhawezyezye, eyo thawabu ushi hwilimwe? Hata bhabhibhi bhabhakhopela abhibhi, na bhapambamala ahwejelele kiasi shesho nantele.
LUK 6:35 Lelo bhagani abhibhi bhenyu na bhabhombele aminza. Bhakhopelaji mgaje ahogepe ahusu awezyewe, na ethawabu yenyu yayibha ngosi. Mwaibha bhana abha yalimwanya afwanaje, umwahale yoyo mwinza hwabhantu bhasebhali nesombe.
LUK 6:36 Bhanji no lusajilo, neshe oYise hwenyu shali no lusajilo.
LUK 6:37 Mganje alonje, namwe semwayilongwa. Mgajerani, namwe semwayilaniwa. Sajilaji, namwe mwajisajilwa.
LUK 6:38 Bhapanji abhanje, namwe mwaipewa. Ekias eshe pyana - shashidinyiliwe, na tabhetabha na hwitishe hwitishe - mmafugamo genyu. Afwanaje eshi pimo sheshonti shamtumila, apimile shesho shayitumiha abhapimile amwe.”
LUK 6:39 Antele wabhabhola ofano. “Aje omntu yali shinsinzilu agalongozya ohwenje yali shinsinzilu? Nkashile bhabhombile esho, bas wonti bhaga dumbushila, mwilende?
LUK 6:40 Yasambelela sabha gosi ashile ya bhasambelezya, lelo shila mntu nkawasambelewa shinza abhaneshe osambelezi wakwe.
LUK 6:41 Yenu bas nkabhenye ahantu hahali mhati mwiliso elya holo waho, na ahantu hali mhati ya mwiliso lyaho sohwenya?
LUK 6:42 Obhahubhole hwele oholo waho, 'Holo, ehulabha enefwe ahantu hahali mhati yeliso lyaho,'nawe sohwenya aantu hahali mwiliso lyaho wewe? Olinafiki awe! Ahwande oyefwe ahantu mwiliso awe, ndipo nkobhalole shinza ahwefwe ahantu mwiliso elya holo waho.
LUK 6:43 Afwanaje nalimo ikwi ilinza lyalipa amadonda amabhibhi, antele nalimo ikwi ibhibhi lyalipapa amadondo aminza.
LUK 6:44 Afwanaje shila likwi limanyiha humadondo gakwe. Afwanaje abhantu sebhayabhila etini afume mumivwa, antele sebhayabhila ezabibu afume mmichongoma.
LUK 6:45 Omntu omwinza alishanga eshinza humwoyo gwakwe afumya gagaliminza, na omntu obhibhi alishanga eshibhibhi humwoyo gwakwe gafuma gagali mabhibhi. Afwanaje ilomu lyakwe liyanga gala gagamemile humwoyo gwakwe.
LUK 6:46 Yenu mnkwizya,'GOSI, GOSI', antele semgabhomba gala gegyanga?
LUK 6:47 Shilo mntu yahwenza hwiline na zyovwe enongwa zyane na bhombele embombo embabhalanje ejinsi shahweli.
LUK 6:48 Alengana no mntu yazenga enyumba yakwe, omwahale abana pansi, tee nazenje omsingi owenyumba pamwanya eyemwala imara. Amakoshi nagahenzele, na majenje agemenze gaikhomile enyumba, lelo segayizizye afwanaje yaze dwilwe shinza.
LUK 6:49 Lelo yayonti yahwovwa enongwa zyane sazitii; ofwano gwakwe yayola omntu yozenga enyumba pamwanya ma masanga pasepaliomsingi, amakoshi nagahishile humaha, enyumba ela yaseadilwe yonti.
LUK 7:1 Nawamala onongwa zyakwe zyonti mmakutu gabhantu ahinjiye, hupapernaumu.
LUK 7:2 Na obhambhambo wakwe oakida, omo ali bhinu tee alipapepe nefwa, wape alimntu yagene tee.
LUK 7:3 Nahovwezye enongwa ezye Yesu, asonte zyezye agosi abhayahudi, hwamwahale hulabhe aje aponie obhombambombo wakwe.
LUK 7:4 Bhope nabhafishile hwa Yesu, bhalabhile tee bhajile abhajiye, “Ono ombombele anongwa ezi,
LUK 7:5 Afanaje aligene itaifa lyetu, wape atizenjeye isinagogi.”
LUK 7:6 Basi oYesu abhalile pandwemo. Nabho nasagalihutali nenyumba, eyola oakida asontezyezye orafiki hwamwahale wabhola. 'GOSI, ogaje ahwiluvye afwanaje ane sefaa aje ewe oyinjile pansi pigalo lyane.
LUK 7:7 Eshi ehwilolile aje sefaa nene ahwinze hwaho, lelo panga izu tu obhombambo wane abhapone.
LUK 7:8 Afwanaje nane endi muntu nembehwelwe pansi eye ulongozi, endina sikari pansi yane, nkebholele ono bhala abhala na ono “enza” ahwenza, na obhomba mbombo, “Wane” bhomba eshi, abhomba.”
LUK 7:9 OYesu namwovwa ego aswijire, wagugalushila, obngano gwagwabhinjelelaga wanyaga.” Embabhola, hata bha Israeli, sendilolile olyweteho ogosi neshe olu.
LUK 7:10 Na bhala bhabhatumwilyu nabhahwela okhaya bhamwaga ola obhombambombo mwinza.
LUK 7:11 Napamande hashe, abhalile hwiboma limo lyakwiwaga Naini. Asambelezye wa bhakwe bhabhenjelezenye nalwo pandwemo no bongona ogosi.
LUK 7:12 Nawafiha apalamile nolwango ogwi boma eye, omntu yafyiye au anyetulwe, na mwana weka hwa nyina wakwe. Yali fwele, na mabungano wabhantu afume hwiboma bhali pandwemo nawo.
LUK 7:13 GOSI nawalola aloleye husajile wabhala, “Laha lile.”
LUK 7:14 Wasojela walipalamasya ijeneza bhala bhabanyetuye bhahemeleye, wayanga sahala ehubhala “imelela”
LUK 7:15 Ola ofwe wemelela. Wakhala wanda aje wapela onyina wakwe.
LUK 7:16 Owoga wabhakhata wonti. Bhasomba ONGOLOBHE bhayanga okuwa “OGOSI afumiye hwilite” na “ONGOLOBHE abhenyizye abhantu bhakwe”
LUK 7:17 Enogwa zyakwe ezi zyazyambanile huyudea hwonti na ensi zyonti zyazili mshe mshe.
LUK 7:18 Asambelezyewa abha Yohana bhaletela enogwa zyego gonti.
LUK 7:19 Esho oYohana wabhakwizya bhabhele asombeleziwa bhakwe wabhasondelezya hwa Yesu abhozye “Awe wewe ola yayenza, au timwenyelezyaje owenje?
LUK 7:20 Wape nabhafiha hwamwahale bhayanjile, “oYohana ya hwozya atisondezyezye hwiliwe aganjile aje awe, 'Wewe ola yahwenza au timwenyelezyaje owenje?”
LUK 7:21 Ne sala yeyo abhaponizye abhinji abhinu bhabho na efwa, eye mpepo embibhi, na avipofu abhinji bhalolile.
