LUK 7:22 Eshi nkawagalula. Wabhabhola, bhalaji mubhale oYohana ega gamgalolilena govwe. avipofu bhalola alema bhajenda, abheukoma bhapona, adinda makutu bhahwovwa, bhabhafwiye bhazyoba, apena bhalombelelwa enongwa enyinza.
LUK 7:23 Wape heri omntu yeyonti yasavisiwa nane.”
LUK 7:24 Basi eshi asontelezewe bha Yohana na bhasogola, ahandile abhabhole amabongono enongwa ezya Yohana, “Mwafumile abhale mwipoli ahwenye yenu, isole wauyiziwa nehala?
LUK 7:25 Eshi mwafumile abhale ahwenye yenu, omntu yakwatiziwe amenda aminza? mmanye abhantu bhabhali namwenda ageu tukufu bhabhalya raha bhali mnyumba ezye shimwene.
LUK 7:26 Eshi mwafumile abhale ahwegegenu okuwa, Antele? Embabhole, na yali zaidi ya okuwa.
LUK 7:27 Oyo yayo asimbiliwa, “Ega, enya ehusontelezya ojumbe wane hwitagalila elye maso gaho, yabhalenganya idala lyaho hwitagalila lyaho,
LUK 7:28 Nane embabhola, neshi bhala bhapepwe na bhashe, nomo yaligosi neshe oYohana, lelo yalidodo humwene owa NGOLOBHE GOSI ashile omwene.”
LUK 7:29 Abhantu bhonti bhabhasonjezya esonga nabhahovwezye ego bhaheteshe, elyoli ya NGOLOBHE afwanaje bhoziwe. Huwoziwa uYohana.
LUK 7:30 Lelo abhafarisayo na bhana sheria bhali khene isunde elya NGOLOBHEhwabhene afwanaje sebhohoziwe nomwene.
LUK 7:31 OGOSI wayanga embalenganisye neye abhantu abheshikho eshi? bhape bhalengene neyenu?
LUK 7:32 Bhalengene nabhana bhakheye pasokoni, na kwizanye nabhayanga, 'tabhakhomeye efilimbi antele semwahanjile, tazondile antele semwalilile.'
LUK 7:33 Afwanaje oYohana owahozye ahenzele salya ibumnda wala samwela divai, namwa myanga myiga “Ano pepo obhibhi.
LUK 7:34 Omwana owa Adamu ayenzile alya na mwele, namwe myanga, enye, lyavi ono, na mwezi owe divai, rafiki wabho asonjezya!
LUK 7:35 Neshinshi ebhoneshe aje elinelyoli hwabhana bhakwe bhonti.”
LUK 7:36 Omntu omo owa mafarisayo amwanile alye eshalye hwamwene. Winjila mnyumba yakwe ofarisayo, wakhala pashalye.
LUK 7:37 Enya oshe omo owiboma lila wali wemabhibhi. Nazyoyile enongwa aje akheye pashalye panyumba eyola ofarisayo, aletile insupa marimari yeli nemaruhamu.
LUK 7:38 Wemelela hwisalo papepe na manama gakwe nawalila. Wanda hulagazizye mmagaga gakwe amansozi gakwe, na syomwole ni sisi elyamwitwe lyakwe, na humyante myante mmagaya gwakwe, na pashe gala amaruhamu.
LUK 7:39 Basi ola ofarisayo yamwanile nawolola shila wanyanga humwoyo gwakwe, omntu ono khashile alikuwe, “Handamenye oshe ono yahupalamasyasya, wenu wape aliwelewele yaje wemabhibhi.
LUK 7:40 OYesu wagamla wabhozya, “Simoni endine nongwa mbahubhole. “Wayanga” “sambilizi yanga!”
LUK 7:41 Wayanga “Omntu omo yakhopezya alinabhe madeni bhabhele, omo adagaya ehela miatano nowabhele amsini.
LUK 7:42 Bhape nabhali sebhalinahahuripe, abhasajiye wonti. bhabhele neshe bhabhele yo nanu yayihugana tee?
LUK 7:43 Simoni wagalula wayanga, “Amenyeje yayola yasajiye enyinji.” Wabhola oyamliye lyoli.”
LUK 7:44 Wagarushila ola oshe wabhola Simoni, “Walota oshe. Ono nahinjiye mnyumba yaho. Sohampiye amenze mmagagagane, eshi ono andayazyezye amansozi mmagagagane, na syomwole nisisi elya mwitwe lyakwe.
LUK 7:45 Awe sohanjayiye, lelo ono, awande pana hinjiye sagaleshile njayile tee mmagaga gane.
LUK 7:46 Sagapashile mwitwe lyane amafuta, eshi ono ampeshe amagaga gane amaruhamu.
LUK 7:47 Afwanaje nago, ehubhozya asajiye embibhi zyekwe zyazyalinjili, afwanaje asongwezye tee. Lelo yasajilya hasheoyo asongwelye hashe.”
LUK 7:48 Eshi abholele oshe, “Osajilye embibhi zyaho zyonti”
LUK 7:49 Esho bhala bhabhakheye pandwemo nawo bhahandile ayanje humoyo gabho wenu ono yasajilo embibhi?”
LUK 7:50 Wabhola ola oshe, “Olweteho lyaho lumwauye. Bhalaga hulweteho lwaho”
LUK 8:1 Yabha baada yego ali azyongola azyongola mmaboa namvijiji ali alombelela, na tungazye enongwa enyinza ezye umwene owa NGOLOBHE na bhala athenashara bhali pandwemo nawo,
LUK 8:2 Na abhashe bhamo bhamo bhali ne mpepo embibhi nepongo abhaponyizye bhape yo Mariamu yakwiziwa magdalena yazya fumile epepo saba.
LUK 8:3 Na Yohana oshe wa kuza owakili wakwe oHerode, Susana, na bhamwabho bhabhinji, bhabhatenganyaga huvintu vyao.
LUK 8:4 Ubungano ogosi na watangene, na bhala bhabha fumile shila liboma bhabhaliye ayanjile hufano.
LUK 8:5 “Ompanzi afumile abhale atote embeyu, yakwe wape nali atota, zimo zyalagashiye papepe nidara, zyakhanyilye enyonyi.
LUK 8:6 Zimo zyalageye pamwalo na zyahandile amele zyahomele afwanaje zyaha kosa orutubo.
LUK 8:7 Zimo zyalageye mmivwa na amivwa gahamela pandwemo zyazyo ya zisonga.
LUK 8:8 Zimo zyalageye pilongo elinza ayunga ego atatushe izu waganga yalinamakutu agahwovwa na ayovwaje.”
LUK 8:9 Abhanafunzi bhakwe bhabhozya yenu ene omafano ogwo,
LUK 8:10 Wayanga, “Amwe apewewe azimanye esiri ezya mwene ONGOLOBHE, eshe bhamo humfwano, aje nkabhenye bhaganje alole nankabhovwe bhagale amanye.'
LUK 8:11 Na ogwo omfano. Emana yakwe ya yene embeyBhala lizu lya ngolobhe.
LUK 8:12 Bhala bhabhali papepe ni dala bhabhala bhahovwa, antele ahwenza oshetani alyefwa elyo izu mmoyo yaho, bhasibhe bhalyeteha na hwaulwe.
LUK 8:13 Na bhala abhapamwala bhabhala ambao nkabhovwa bhaliposhela lila izu sabhashiye, wape sebhana malandazi bhahweteha humda hashe, naufiha owa lengwe, bhahwibagula.
LUK 8:14 Zyazilagaliye pamivwa bhabhala bhabhovwenzwe, abhale hwabho bhosohwa ne shughuli no utabhazi na owalangani owemaisha ega, sebhatonia lyalyonti.
LUK 8:15 Na zila ezya pilongo elinza bhabala bhabhali no mwoyo ogwinza ogwa lyovwe izu, na likhate, esho lipapa amadondo esha jimbilizwe.
LUK 8:16 Nomo, omntu yahwasya, okhozyo na kwishile neshelelo. Au abheshe hwinzongo bali bhayibheha pamwanya pameza ili bhabhahwisya njila bhapataje alole okhizyo lwakwe.
LUK 8:17 Afwanaje nalimo izu lyalyobhele lyasagalya yibhoneha, antele lyalyobhele elyaje selyayi manyiha na fumile hwelele.
LUK 8:18 Hwiyenyi basi enamna shamhovwa afwanaje yalinahantu. Abhapewe na ola, yasanahantu abhafyolwe atahala, habhoneha aje anaho.”
LUK 8:19 Bhabhalila onyina wakwe na holo bhakwe bhashindwa abhapapepe afanaje amabungano.
LUK 8:20 Bhatwalile enongwa wabhola, “Onyina waho na holo bhaho bhemeleye hwonze bhahwanza alolane nawe.
LUK 8:21 Wagalula, wayanga “omaye wane naholo bhane bhabhebha bhabhahovwa izu elya NGOLOBHE na bhombe.”
LUK 8:22 Yabha ensiku zila wapanda mshelelo omwahale na sambelezyewa bhakwe, wabhabhola, “Nantele tilo woshe hadi hwisyela eyeidimi. “Bhasogola na matanga.
LUK 8:23 Bhape nabhali bhabhala, agonile otulo, yahishile etofani pamwanya eyidimi, eshelelo shahandile ameme ameze bhabha mhatari.
LUK 8:24 Bhabhalila bhadamuzya bhaga, “GOSI wa gosi! GOSI wa gosi! litega wabhoha!” Waidamila ehala na vwadangana ameze hwaleha hwabha hwinza.
LUK 8:25 Wabhabhola, “Olweteho lyenyu lulihwi?” Bhogope, bhaswiga, bhayango bhebho hwa bhebho,”Yenu ene paka, adamila ehalana menze gape gahumwogopa?”
LUK 8:26 Bhafiha mpwani mnsi ya bha wa Gerasini ye paramila hu Galilaya.
LUK 8:27 Wape na hishile hupwani, atangene nomntu omo owe boma, ola yaline mpepo, sagakwete amenda ensiku zinyinji, antele sagakheye pakhaya ila hamagwela.
LUK 8:28 Nalolile oYesu akholile eholo, agwiye hwitagalila lyakwe. Waganga hwizu igosi endi neyenu nawe, Yesu womwana wa NGOLOBHE yalimwanya? Ehulabha, ugajendavye”
LUK 8:29 Afanaje alidamiye lile ipepo ichafu limwepe omntu ola, afanaje apagewe wape mara nyinji, nantele bhalidaga mshifungo na apinyilye na manyolo ne mpengo, adumlaga gala amanyolo, ashembezyewaga mwipoli ne nguvu ezya lila ipepo.
LUK 8:30 OYesu wabhozya, “Itawa lyaho wewenu?” Wayanga, “Itawa lyane endijeshi” Afwanaje pepo bhinji bhamwinjiye.
LUK 8:31 Bhalabha asabhadamila aje bhafume abhale mwilende.
LUK 8:32 Eshi epo pali ikundi elye engorobhe enyinji bhadimazyaga mwigamba. Galabha agapele oruhusa ahwinjile zila, wagapele aruhusa.
LUK 8:33 Pepo bhafuma mwamntu ola bhinjila mgorobhe, lyape ikundi lyahishile mwigenge nanali, bhinjila mwidimi, bhafwa mmenze.
LUK 8:34 Adimi nabhalola lyalifumiye bhashembeye na zyambanye enongwa hwiboma, na mavueni.
LUK 8:35 Abhantu afumile abhale ahwenye gaga fumiye, bhabhalila oYesu bhalola omntu ola mwagafumile akwete amenda anenjele zyakwe, bhahogope.
LUK 8:36 Na bhala bhabhalolile bhabhabholele shasha hali shaponiziwe ola ya pageweni pepo.
LUK 8:37 Na mwabho abhantu abhensi ya bhagevasi yeli pasheje sheje bhalabhile aje asogole hwabhahale afwanaje bhali nowoga ogosi esho winjila mshelelo wawela.
LUK 8:38 No mntu ola yalya fumile ipepo alabhile oruhusa aje alondozyaje wape, lelo omwahale walaga wayanga,
LUK 8:39 “Wela amwenyu arombelele gagali mago ONGOLOBHE gabhombeye”Abhala, alombelele iboma lyonti, shangali magosi amambo ga bhombelwe no Yesu.
LUK 8:40 Eshi oYesu namwawela, obongano gwa karibizizye, esha seshelele afwanaje bhali bhahugolela wonti.
LUK 8:41 Enya omntu omo wenza itawa lya vwa yo yairo, wape mntu gosi owe shibhanza, wagwa pamagaga ga Yesu walabha iyinjile mnyumba yakwe,
LUK 8:42 Afwanaje elendu wakwe abhinile tee apalamila afwe, afwanaje mwana weka mwene, oumri wakwe alinamaha kumi na gabhele, wakati abhala obungano gwasonjile.
LUK 8:43 Noshe omo ambaye afumaga idanda omda ogwe maha kumi na gabhele, ali anankenye eshoma shakwe shonti abhapele aganga bila opone, nomntu yoyonti,
LUK 8:44 Abhalile hwisalo lyakwe wapalamazya opindo ohwemwenda gwakwe, mara elyo afume hwkwe idanda hwapoma.
LUK 8:45 OYesu wayanga, “Wenu ya mpalamasyezye?” Basi abhantu bhonti nabhakhana oPetro abholele, GOSI mgosi, amabonyano ega gahuzyongala na husonje.”
LUK 8:46 OYesu wayanga, “Omntu ampalamasyezye, afwanaje elola aje amaha gafumile.”
LUK 8:47 Ola oshe nawalola yaje sawezizye ahwobhe wenza ayinga, wagwa hwilagalila lyakwe, wabhola hwitagalila elya bhantu bhonti esababu eyahupalamasye nasha ponile nantele.
LUK 8:48 Wabhola, “Rendu, olyeteho lwaho luponizye. Bhalaga umwe no lweteho.”
LUK 8:49 Nali ayangaga ego ahenzele, omntu afume hukhaya eya ola ogosi, owe shibhanza, “Wabhola orendu waho afwiye. Ogajehuyanzyosambelezi.”
LUK 8:50 Lelo oYesu nawovwa, ego, wagalula ugajebhe, “Nowoga. Ateha awe wape, abhapone.”
LUK 8:51 Nawafiha mnyumba, sagaleshile omntu aje ayinjile hata omo, ila oPetro, no Yohana no Yakobo, no Yise wole, omwana no nyina.
LUK 8:52 Na bhantu bhonti bhali bhalilaga na zonde, wayanga, “Majelile safwiye, ono, eshi aganile tulo wene.”
LUK 8:53 Bhaseshile tee, afanaje bhamenye aje afwiye.
LUK 8:54 Wakhata, okhono, wakhola hwizu, wayanga, “sahala, bhoha”
LUK 8:55 URoho yakwe yawela, wape mara eyo wemelela. Wabhabhola wapele eshalye.
LUK 8:56 AYise bhakwe bhaswijile, tee lelo wabhakhana bhagaje hubhole omntu lyelifumiye.
LUK 9:1 Wabhakwizya bhala Thenashara, wabhapela owezo na mamlaka agahwefwe pepo bhonti na ponie empongo.
LUK 9:2 Wabhasontezya bhaulombelele oumwene owa NGOLOBHE na abhaponie empongo.
LUK 9:3 Wabhabhola, “Mganje hweje ahantu msafari yenyu endesa, wala echola, wala ibumnda, wala ehela wala omo wenye asahabhe na magolole gabhele.
LUK 9:4 Na enyumba yuyonti yamwayinjila, mkhalaje omwo anzaji omwo.
LUK 9:5 Na bhala bhasebhabhakalibizizye, na mfuma mwiboma omwo, kunyuntaji hata mankondi aga mmagaga egenyu abhe ushuda hwabhahale.”
LUK 9:6 Bhabhala bhasyongola shila shijiji, bhalombelela izu na abhunie abhantu shila mahali.
LUK 9:7 Nao Herode, omwene, wovwa enongwa zyonti zyazibhombeshe, wazugumila afwanaje abhantu bhamo bhayanjile eyejo oYohana azyoshele afume afwe,
LUK 9:8 Na bhamo bhagaga oEliya abhoneshe na bhamo, bhagaga bhabhala akuwa abhe mwaha azeyoshele.
LUK 9:9 Lelo oHerode wayanga, “OYohana, nadumuye itwe eshi wenu ono wehovwa amambo gakwe? Ahanzaga hulole.
LUK 9:10 Eshi bhala atumwa, nabhawelile bhabholele amambo gonti gabhabombile. wabhega wabhalanabho pa faragha paka piboma limo likwiziwa Bethsadia.
LUK 9:11 Namabongono nabhanya bhalondoleye wabhakari bizya, wabha ayanga nabho enongwa zya umwene owa NGOLOBHE, wabhaponia bhala bhabhali neshida eya pone.
LUK 9:12 Na isanyo lyahandile aswe, bhabhalila bhala Athenashara, bhabhola ulaje obongano ili bhabhale hushijiji na mmagondo aga mnshenje bhapaje apagone na evyalye afwanaje epa patihweli pigona wene.”
LUK 9:13 Wabhabhola, “Bhapeli amwe eshalye.”bhayaga” Seti na hantu zaidi eye mabumnda gasanu ne sanaki zibhele kasetibhala tibhakalile abhantu ebhabhonti evyalye.”
LUK 9:14 Afwanaje alume bhali elfu zisanu. Na wabhabhola asambelezewa bhakwe. “Bhakhazi abhantu shikundi shila shikundi bhantu hamsini.
LUK 9:15 Bhabhamba esho bhabhakhazya bhonti.
LUK 9:16 Wega gala amabumnda gasanu na zila esamaki zibhele wenya amwanya humbunguni, wavi sayila, wavimensula wabhapela, asambelezewe bhakwe ili bhabhapele abungano.
LUK 9:17 Bhalya bhakuta bhonti, na eshi vila evimensushilo vyavyasageye bhabhongenye evitondo kumi na vibhele.
LUK 9:18 Yabha na putaga hufalagha, amanyiwa bhakwe bhahari pandwemo nawo, wabhabhozya, eshi amabongano ebhabha bhayiga ane neweni?
LUK 9:19 Bhagalula, bhayanga, “oYohana yahwozya, lelo bhamo bhayiga yo Eliya, nabhamwabho bhayiga mojawapo mwa kuwa abhemwaha azyoshele.”
LUK 9:20 Wabhabhola, “amwe myiga ane newenu?” OPetro wagalula wayanga, “awe we kristi wa NGOLOBHE.”
LUK 9:21 Wabhasunda, wabhakhana bhagaje hubhole omntu enongwa ezyo,
LUK 9:22 Wayanga ahwanziwa omwana owa Adamu agaje amalabha aminji nakhanwe na zee na gosi abhe makohani na simbi na gakwe na isiku elya tatu lya zyoshe.
LUK 9:23 Wabhabhola wonti omntu yeyonti, “Yahwanza ambejezye na ahwikhane yoyo, ahwitweshe ikhobhehanyo lyakwe shila lisiku, andondolezyaje.
LUK 9:24 Afwanaje omntu yahwanza aponie enafsi yakwe ayiyitezya, na omntu yayitezye enafsi kwajili yane, esho ayiyiponya.
LUK 9:25 Afwanaje henu habhajiye omntu, azyagaezya mnsi omo zyonti, nkeshe wahwitezya yoyo na hwiyanganuzye?
LUK 9:26 Afwanaje shila yayindolela asoni ane na mazu gane, omwana owa Adamu wape ayihulole esoni omntu oyo nayenza no winza wakwe, no wayise no wa malaika abhinza.
LUK 9:27 Nane embabhola elyoli, bhahweli bhabhemeleye epa, ambao sebhayilenga efwa tee hata paka bhaulole oumwe owa NGOLOBHE.”
LUK 9:28 Afume amazu ego zyashilile ensiku nane abhejile oPetro, no Yohana, no Yakobo, wazubha mwigamba ili alabhe.
LUK 9:29 Yabha katika apute hwakwe esheni, esha hu maso gakwe shagaluhana, na amenda gakwe gabha mazelu gameta meta.
LUK 9:30 Na enya, abhantu bhabhele bhali bhayanga nawo! Bhape yo Musa no Eliya,
LUK 9:31 Bhabhoneshe huwinza. Bhayanga enongwa ezya fwe hwakwe, nayikamilisya hu Yerusalemu.
LUK 9:32 OPetro na bhala bhali pandwemo nabho bhali bhalemewe notulo. Lelo nabhadamla, bhalole owinza wakwe nabhala bhabhele bhabhemeleye pandwemo nabho.
LUK 9:33 Yabha ebho nabhahwibagula nawo, oPetro wabhila oYesu, GOSI, wabhagosi, shinza atee abhepa na tilenganye amahenje gatatu. Shimo shahwiliwa shimo shamusi esha mwabho sha Musa, no Eliya.” Esho ali samenye lyayanga.
LUK 9:34 Nali ayanga ego, lyafumiye ibhengo lyabhapola izunda bhogopa nabhinji mwibhengo elyo.
LUK 9:35 Izu lyafumile mwibhengo lyayanga, “Ono mwana wane teule. Wane mwovwaji omwahale.”
LUK 9:36 Na izu elyo nalyamaliha, Yesu abhoneshe ali mwene, bhape bhapona kati, sebhatangazya hwa mntu ensiku zila lyalyoli lilo gabhagalolile.
LUK 9:37 Yabha isiku, elya bhele yakwe nabhiha hwigamba, abugano ogosi watangene nawo.
LUK 9:38 Na enye, omntu omo katika obongano akholile hwiizu ayanjile, sambilizi, “Ehulabha mwenye omwana wane, afwanaje omwahale mwana wane mwene.
LUK 9:39 Na enye ipepo lihukhata wape akhoma ibwago, antele lihupela eshifapa, olu afuma itatafura wa sahuleha ila humalabha ohwikoyola koyola.
LUK 9:40 Embalabhile asambelezewe bhaho bhamwefe sebhawezizye.”
LUK 9:41 OYesu wagalula wayanga, “Amwe mshikholo mwase mlinolyeteho, mtejile embakhale nani we nahwejeshelane paka ndii? Rete omwana wa ho epe.”
LUK 9:42 Na ali ahubhalila, ipepo lyalagazya pansi. wapela eshifafa, oYesu wadamila ipepo ibhibhi, waponia omwana wawezyezya oYise.
LUK 9:43 Bhonti bhaswiga nabhaulola ogosi owa NGOLOBHE. Bhape nabhali bhaswiga amambo gonti gabhambile, abhabholele amanyiziwa bhakwe,
LUK 9:44 “ Gakhataji amazu ega mmakutu genyu, ufwanaje omwana owa Adamu abhala akhatwe mmakhono gabhantu.”
LUK 9:45 Lelo sebhalimenye izu lila, lyatisilwe hwabhale sebhalimenye, bhahogope hubhozye ofwano gwakwe gwenu izu elyo.
LUK 9:46 Bhahandile ayungane wenu yabhabhe gosi kati yabho.
LUK 9:47 Wape oYesu nawamanya esebho ezye moyo gabho, wamwega omwana ododo, wabhaha papepe no mwahale,
LUK 9:48 Wabhabhola, “yayonti yabhahuwejelele omwana ono hwitawa lyane anejeleye nene na yoyonti, yabhanejelele ane, abhabhe amwejeleye omwahale yasontezyezyeafwanaje yali mwana miongoni mwenyu mwenti oyo ndiye yo gosi”
LUK 9:49 OYohana wagalulawabhola, “Bwana, wogosi tilolile omntu afumya ipepo hwitawa lyaho tikhene, afwanaje salongozanyu natee.”
LUK 9:50 OYesu wabhola, “Mganje, hukhane afwanaje omwahale ambaye salilne mbibhi natee aliupande owahulite”
LUK 9:51 Yabha ensiku, ezya sogole nazyaparamiye afishe, omwahale alanguliye amaso gakwe abhale hu Yerusalemu.
LUK 9:52 Wasontezya abhajumbe atagalile hwita, galila elye maso gakwe, bhabhala bhinjila mshijiji esha bhasamaria ili kulengunyizye mahali.
LUK 9:53 Lelo akhaya sabhakaribizizye, afanaje shahenyizye amaso gakwe, abhale hu Yerusalemu.
LUK 9:54 Asambeleziwa bhakwe oYakobo no Yohana nabhalolile, ego bhayanjile, “GOSI ohwanza tirajizye (neshe oEliya wape shabhombile)?”
LUK 9:55 Wabhagalushila wabhasunda -(wayanga, semmenye eroho yeli hwelewele yamlinayo)
LUK 9:56 Apwanaje omwana owa Adamu sega henzele azitezye roho zya bhantu eshi azyaule, bhasogala bhabhala hushijiji esha mwabho.
LUK 9:57 Bhape nabhali bhabala mwidala, omntu omo abholele, “Embahulondolele hwohwonti hwobhale.”
LUK 9:58 OYesu wabhola, “Embela bhana magwenya, enyonyiabheangani bhane vitele, lelo omwana owa Adamu sali na pagone itwe lyakwa.”
LUK 9:59 Wabhola owa mwabho, “Ombenjelele.” Wayanga,”GOSI, pele oruhusa nasoti embale esyele oYise wane,”
LUK 9:60 Wabhala bhaleshe bhabhafwiye, “Bhaseyele naje abhafwe bhebho, eshi awe bhalagaolombelele aumwene owa NGOLOBHE.
LUK 9:61 Omntu owamwabho. “Nantele wabhola, GOSI, embahubhenjezye lelo mpele oruhusa nasoti embalaje abhantu bhapa khaya yane.”
LUK 9:62 OYesu wabhola umntu, yabheshele okhono gwakwe alima antele wagaluha hwisalo sahwanziwa humwene owa NGOLOBHE.”
LUK 10:1 Eshi baada eyego, GOSI abheshera na bhamwabho sabini wabhasontezya, bhabhele bhabhele bhatagalile bhale shila boma shila hwintu hwapambameye abhale yoyo.
LUK 10:2 Wabhabhola, “Eviyabho vinji, lelo abhombambo bhadodo. Eshi labhi hwu GOSI owe viyabho, utwale abhombamba mbombo mviyabho vyakwe.
LUK 10:3 Bhalaji. Enyaji, embasotezya nesheje bhana ngole mmahanyanga.
LUK 10:4 Mgaje ahweje ifuko wala echola, wala evilato, wala mgaje hulamushe omntu mwidala.
LUK 10:5 Ekhaya yoyonti yambahahwinjele, yanji na soti, 'Amani ebhanje mnyumba omu.
LUK 10:6 Nkashile ahweli omwana owe amani, eamani yenyu ebhawele hwilimwe.
LUK 10:7 Eshi khalaji pakhaya peepo, mlyonje na mwene evyabhahale, afanaje, obhombo mbombo ahwanziwa hupele omshahara gwakwe. Mgaje asame same afume ekhaya ene abhale ekhaya eyamwabho.
LUK 10:8 Na ibima lya lyonti, lyamuhwinjile, nkabhakaribizya lyanji elyalye vyabhabheshele hwitagalila lyenyu,
LUK 10:9 Bhaponyaji abhinu bhabhaliomwo. bhabholaji, 'Oumwene owa NGOLOBHE upalamiye'
LUK 10:10 Na iboma lyonti lyambhahwinjile, bhape sebhabhakaribizyo, fumaji omwo namwe nkamwashila katika idala lyakwa yangaji,
LUK 10:11 'Itata mankonji age boma lyenyu ggakhatene na mmanama getu tigasanyata gasagalaje hwilimwe! Lelo mmanye eli yaje, omwene owa NGOLOBHE upalamiye.'
LUK 10:12 Embahla eyaje isiku ila ayibharahisi zaidi eSodoma ajimbe amarabha gakwe ahile iboma eli.
LUK 10:13 Ehele awe Korazini, ehele awe Bethsaida! Afwanaje nkashile amajabu ega gagabhombeshe wilimwe gagabhombeshe katika Tiro na hu Sidoni, handa bhalabhile aje bhasajilwe afume epoohu nakhale na menda age magunila na malota.
LUK 10:14 Lelo ensiku elya longwe yayibha rahisi Tiro ne Sidoni ajimbe amalabha gakwe ashile amwe.
LUK 10:15 Nawe Kapernaumu, je! obhahwikuzye hata amwanya? Bhahwisiwe, paka hwazimu.
LUK 10:16 Yabhovwa amwe anvwezye nene, wape yabhakhana amwe ahene nene, wape yahenene akhene ola ya mntu”
LUK 10:17 Esho bhala sabini bhawelile nasesherere, bhayanga, “GOSI, na epepo zitogopa hwitawa lyaho.”
LUK 10:18 Wabhabhola, “Naloli oshetsni nagwa afume amwanya eneshe oumeme.
LUK 10:19 Enya, embapiye endajizyo ezya khanye enzohane nge, na maha goni golo oadui, wala na hamo ahantu hahayibha vwalazya.
LUK 10:20 Lelomgaje shime shilo amapepo nagabhopa, eshishimaji afwatanaje amatawa genyu gasimbilwe amwanya.”
LUK 10:21 Esaa yeyo yeyo ashanjiliye hupepo ozelu, wayanga, “Ehusalifya, wo Baba, wo GOSI owa mwanya na owa pansi, afwanaje amambo ega obhafisile bhabhali neshinshi ne njele, obhalanjile abhanaabhela, ena, Baba, afwanaje shashesho shosongwelwe.”
LUK 10:22 Wayanga empewelwe vyonti na Baba wane, wala nomo yamenye omwana na yeyonti ambaye omwana asongwe hulanje.”
LUK 10:23 Wabagalushila asambelezewa bhakwe, wayanga nabho hufaragha, “Heri amaso gagalola gamgalola amwe.
LUK 10:24 Afwanaje embabhola, ya je akuwa abhinji na mwene bhatamanile agalola gamgalola amwe sebhagalole, navgowe gamgavwazye amwe sebha govwezye.”
LUK 10:25 Na enya, olonzi omo ahemeleye aenje wayanga, sambelezi, “Embombe, yenu ili egale owomi owa hanihani?”
LUK 10:26 Wabhola, “Esibwilwe yenu mtorati? Obhazya wele?”
LUK 10:27 Wagalula wayanga, “Ogane OGOSI ONGOLOBHE waho humwoyo gwaho gwonti, na huroho yaho yonti, na hamaha gaho gonti, na hunjele zyaho zyonti, no jirani waho neshe nafsi yaho.”
LUK 10:28 Wabhola, “Ujibule shinza. Bhommba shesho nawe ubhakhale.”
LUK 10:29 Wape ahanzaga, ahwibhonesye ehaki, wabhozya, oYesu, “No jirani wane wenu?”
LUK 10:30 Oyesu wagalula wayanga, “Omntu omo ahishile afume hu Yerusalemu abhale hu Yeriko. Wagwela mwabhabhafepla wamwaula, amenda bhavwalazya bhahwibhalila bhaleha papepe nefwa.
LUK 10:31 Kwa bahati okohani omo ahishile hwidala alila na walola washila pashenje.
LUK 10:32 Na mlawi wape, shesho nawafiha pala walola washila pashenje.
LUK 10:33 Lelo oMsamaria omo, katika asafiri, hwakwe wafiha epo pahali. Na walola asajiye.
LUK 10:34 Wakaribila wapinya amalonda gakwe, waponya amafuta ne divai wamwinjizya pahamu wakwe. watwara mpaka kunyumba eya jenyi bhalela.
LUK 10:35 Hata isiku elyabhele wafumia dinari zibhele, wapela omwanesho nyumba eya jenyi, 'Wayanga orere ono na hahonti hobhatumile zaidi, ane nanayiwela nayisomba.'
LUK 10:36 Olola wele awe katika ebho bhatatu, wenu, wali jirani wakwe ola yagweleye mmakhona bhabhafyola?”
LUK 10:37 Wayanga, “Ya yono yaloleye husajile. “oYesu wabhola, “Bhalaga nawe obhombe shesho”
LUK 10:38 Shabha katika abhale hwabho, winjira mshijiji shimo, oshe omo itawa lyakwe yo Martha wakarihizya akhaya yakwe.
LUK 10:39 Wape ali no mwana kwabho wakwe akwiziwa Mariamu, yakheye pamagaga ga Yesu atejezyaga amazu gakwe.
LUK 10:40 Lelo o Martha ali ahangayiha huteleshere oYesu. Wabhalila wayanga, “GOSI, solola shibhibhi oholo wane? Shandishile etelehe nemwene?
LUK 10:41 Eshi bhole anavwe.” OGOSI wagalula wabhola, “Martha, Martha, ohwitamasya na sononeshe kwajili eye vintu evinji,
LUK 10:42 Lelo shihwanziwa ahantu hamo wane. No Mariamu asaluye ifungu lyali linza, ambalo sagayefwezyewe.”
LUK 11:1 Yabha nali humo humo alabhaga na wamala, omo wasambelezewa bhakwe abhole, “GOSI, umanyizye ate apute neshe shila oYohana shabha manyizizya asambelezewa bhakwe.'
LUK 11:2 Wabhabhola na mputa, yangaji, semeni, 'Baba, hwetu woli mwanya. Itawa lyaho lisaiwaje. Umwene waho wenze, amapenzi gaho gatimizi waje, epa padunia neshe ohwo amwanya.
LUK 11:3 Otipele isiku hwi siku eriziki yetu.
LUK 11:4 Otisajile embibhi zyetu, afwanaje nate ate tibhasajira shila yativisya. Na ogaje ati ponye mmalabha.” (lelo otaule nalo obhibhi)
LUK 11:5 Wabhabhola, “Wenu hwilimwe yali no rafiki, wabhalila nosiku, owe manane na hubhole, Rafiki wane hopele amabumnda gatatu.
LUK 11:6 Afwanaje orafiki wane afishile hwiline afamile msafari, nane sendi nahantu eshabheshe hwitagalila lyakwe.'
LUK 11:7 Na ola owa mhati galula ayanje, uganjenja zye, olyango engaliye nate tiganile nashitala ane na bhana bhane, sebwezizya abhoshe aje epele.
LUK 11:8 Embabhale yaje, ata nkashile bhoha apele afwanaje rafiki wakwe, lele shila shasaleha hulabhe, bhaso gale na hupele, kadli eyehaja yakwe.
LUK 11:9 Nane embabhola, Labhaji, mbhapewe; anzaji, namwe mbhalole, ganezyaje, nemwa mbhahwalwe.
LUK 11:10 Afwanaje shila yalabha apewa, wape ya hwanza alola, wape yadaliha ahwaulwa.
LUK 11:11 Eshi wenu hwalimwe, yali Yise wenyuyaje omwana wukwe, nkalabhe ibumnda ahupela iwe
LUK 11:12 au samaki badala ya samaki ahupela enzoha?
LUK 11:13 Eshi, ekiwa amwe mwemli bhibhi mmenye abhapele abhana bhenyu evintu evinza, eshi oBaba warimwanya sabhazide abhapele opepo ozelu bhala bhabhalabha?”
LUK 11:14 Wape ali, ahwefwa ipepo, ibubu. lyabha ipepo nalyepa, ola obubu wayanga, mabongano bhaswiga.
LUK 11:15 Bhamo bhayanga, ahwefwa pepo, Beelzebul, gosi we pepo.
LUK 11:16 Bhamo bhalenga bhamwanza ishala yefuma amwanya.
LUK 11:17 Wape azimenye esebho zyabho, wabhabhola, shila umwene wauvisenye wowo kwa wowo, ubhombeha sheukwa, nekhaya juu yekhaya egwa.
LUK 11:18 Eshi nkebhe Oshetani avisenye juu ye nafsi yakwe, umwene wakwa ubhahwemelele wele, afanaje amwe mjile ane ehwefwa mapepo hwa Belzebuli.
LUK 11:19 Eshi nkashile ane ehwefwa pepo Belzebuli, je abhana bhenu, mbhabhefwe hwananu, afwanaje, ebho bhabhayibhalonga.
LUK 11:20 Lelo, nkashele ane efumya amapepo hushidole sha Ngolobhe, eshu umwene owa Ngolobhe ubhenzeye.
LUK 11:21 Omntu yali namaha ahwipinyile endoso zyakwe, nalinda ekhaya yakwe, evintu evyakwa vilishinza.
LUK 11:22 Lelo omntu yali namaha ashile omwahale na bhahubhalile nahumene, na hufyole endoso zyakwe zyasobheye, na gabhanye amateka gakwe.
LUK 11:23 Omntu ambaye salipandwemo nane, oyo alishinyume nane na omntu yasabhonganya pandwemo nane anyapanya.
LUK 11:24 Opepo ochafu nafuma hwamntu, ashililila pasepali menze. Ahwanza apatoye sapalela, ayanga.
LUK 11:25 Embayiwelele enyumba yane mwefumele.
LUK 11:26 Hata nafiha nkawalola eyoselye na yipambe esho abhala ayeje pepe abhamwabho saba bhali bhabhibhi ashile elyahale lyelyo, ginjila na khale omwo, omntu oyo ehali yakwe eya humalisholo ebhambibhi shile eyahwande.
LUK 11:27 Yabha nawayanga amazu ego, oshe om katika obongano akholile hwizu lyakwe, wabhola heri evyanda vyavyapepe, na mabhele gohoshile.
LUK 11:28 Lelo omwahale ayanjile, nafu, aheli bhahwovwa izu elya Ngolobhe na likhate.
LUK 11:29 Na mabongano nabhali bhahubhonganila, ahandile ayanje, eshikholo eshi shikholo eshibhibhi. Shihwanza ishala, wala seshayipewa ishara ila ishara eya Yona.
LUK 11:30 Eshi, nkasile shila o Yona shari ishara hwa bhaninawi, shesho shayibha omwana owa Adamu hushikholo eshi.
LUK 11:31 Omalkia owa hukusini ayisogola isiku ilyalongwe pandwemo na bhantu abheshikholo eshi wape aibhalonga aje mnamakosa afatanaje omwahale ahenzele afume ncha ezye ensi ayovwe ehekimu eya Solomoni, na epa pali o gosi ashera Osolomoni.
LUK 11:32 Abhantu Bhaninawi bhayemelela isiku elya longwe pandwemo nesikholo eshi bhape bhayishilongu aje shikosile afwanaje abhahale bhasajilwe hundomelelo ezya Yona, nepa pali ogosi ashile o Yona.
LUK 11:33 Nomo omntu yahwasya okhozyo nabhesha pa pafisishe au pansi pameza, eshi ibhehwa pamwanya eye meza, ili bhabhahwinjila bhalolaje okhozyo.
LUK 11:34 Okhozyo olwebele liso. Eshi iliso lyaho nkalibhe shinza, obele gwao gwonti gubhabhelukhozyo. Lelo nkalibhe libhibhi obele gwaho gubhabhe nkisi.
LUK 11:35 Enya eshi olukhozyo lwalimhati yaho osije ogabha nkisi.
LUK 11:36 Eshi nkashile okhozyo guzyambanile mubele gwaho gwonti, wala segunesehemu eye nkisi, esho obele gwaho gwonti gubhabhe nokhozyo, nkashile lula okhozyo nkaukhozye obele gwaho gwonti gubhabhe no mwanga.”
LUK 11:37 Nali ayanga, o Falisayo omo akwizizye abhale hwamwahale alye ehsalye, winjila, wakhala pa shalye.
LUK 11:38 Farisayo oyo nalolile, aswijile afwanaje saganawile sasele alye.
LUK 11:39 Ogosi wabhola, “Amwe mwafalisayo mhwozya eshikombo ne sahani wonze lelo mhati yenyu mmemile afyole no ubhibhi.
LUK 11:40 Amwe mwalema yabhombile evya hwonza seyoyo yabhombile evya mhati antele?
LUK 11:41 Ulo fumyaji esadaka vila evya mhati ne enya, vyonti vibhovinza hwilimwe.
LUK 11:42 Lelo ole wenyu Mwafarisayo, afwatanaje mfumia ezaka za mnanaa ne zebwa na shila vilembe na ohu mleshile amamba age adili na lugane olya Ngolobhe. Mwanziwaga abhombe ego agahwande bla agalishe ego agabhele.
LUK 11:43 Ole wenyu Mwafarisayo, afwanaje msongwa akhale hwitagalila elye mabhanza na lamhane msokoni.
LUK 11:44 Ole wenyu, afwanaje mlengene na makabuli gasegabhone amago abhantu nabhashilla juu yakwe sebhali nehabari nago.”
LUK 11:45 Omntu omo katika abhanasheria wagalula, wabhalola sambelezi, ayanje esho otilajiye ate natee.
LUK 11:46 Wayanga, namwe mbhanasheria, ole wenyu afwanaje mbhatweha abhantu amazigo gasega nyeruha wala amwe bhenyewe semgapalamasya amazigo ego hata huvidole vyenyu shimo.
LUK 11:47 Ole wenyu afwanaje mzenga maziala aga kuwa na ayise bhenyu afwanaje bhabhagojile.
LUK 11:48 Eshi mshuhudila na zyetishe embombo ezya yise bhenyu, afwanaje bhahale bhabhagojile namwe mbhazenjela amaziala.
LUK 11:49 Na afwanaje esho ehekima eya Ngolobhe ihayanjila, enya, embasontezye hwabhahale akuwa na tumwa, bhape bhayibhagoga bhamo na bhutanje.
LUK 11:50 Ili hupapwa ene liwahwenze idanda elya kuwa wonti, yehitishe afume azengwe omsingi ogwensi.
LUK 11:51 Afume idanda elya Abeli hata idanda elya Zakaria, yagongwilye kati ya pampto eya pashibhanza. Nantele embabhola eyaje ebhahwanzye humpapo ene.
LUK 11:52 Ole wenyu amwe mbhana sheria afwanaje muwefwizye efukuro eye marifai mwemwe semwahinji yei nabhala bhabhahinjilaga mbhazubhiye.”
LUK 11:53 Nawafuma omwo asimbi na Mafalisayo bhandile husonje shibhibhi na husinjizye humaswali gaminji.
LUK 11:54 Bhahuzijila ili bhapata enongwa zya zifuma mwilumu lyakwe.
LUK 12:1 Wakati owo amabungano nabhatangene elfu elfu hata bhakhanyanaga, ahandile abhabhole asambe leziwa bhakwe nantele, “Hwilindi ne chachu eya Mafarisayo ambayo unafiki.”
LUK 12:2 Lelo nalimo izu lyalifisishe lyasalyaibhonaha wala lyalifisilye lyaselyayi julihana. Eshi gagonti gamuyanjile hunkisi gabhahwovwehwe pawelele.
LUK 12:3 Na gamuyanjile mmakutu mwa bhantu katika mpanda ezya mhati gayitu mbele wa pamwanya eye golu.
LUK 12:4 Nane ambabhola amwa rafiki bhane, mgaje bhaogapa ebho bhabhagoga oele afwanaje baada eyeso sebhanowezo abhombe zaidi.
LUK 12:5 Lelo embabhasunda owahumwogope. Mwogopaji ola ambaye nkashele wagoga omntu anakwezo huponye hujehanamu. Antele embabhola mwogapaji oyo.
LUK 12:6 Nkashe mshomolo gasanu segakatiwa husenti zibhele? Wala sebhahwewehwa hata om hwitagalila elya Ngolobhe.
LUK 12:7 Lelo hata lisisi eya mwi atwa genyu zibhaziwe zyonti, mganje ahwa gape esho. Nafu amwe ashile amashomolo gaminji.
LUK 12:8 Nane embabhola, nkashele yayineteha hwitagalile elya bhantu, omwana owa Adamu wapa ayihumweteha hwitagalila elya malaika owa Ngolobhe.
LUK 12:9 Wape wahana hwitagalila elya bhantu, oyo ayikhanwa hwitagalila elya malaika owa Ngolobhe.
LUK 12:10 Na shila mntu yayiyanga enongwa juu ya omwana wa Adamu, ayisajilwa, nkashele yayihuliga opepo uzelu sagayisajilwa.
LUK 12:11 Nabhayibhatwala amwe hwitagalila elye mabhanza, na hwaliwali na hwaongozi, msazugumile asebhe enongwa zyenyu shamwayigalula au ayanje,
LUK 12:12 afwanaje opepo ozeru ayibhasambelezya, esaa zyezyo zyazihwaziwa aziyanje.”
LUK 12:13 Omntu omo katika mabungano wabhola, “Sambelezi bhole oholo wane angabhile vulithi wetu.”
LUK 12:14 Wabhola, womntu awe, wenu yambeshele ane aje endi watazanye au wagabhanya juu yenyu?
LUK 12:15 Wabhabhola enyaji, hwilindaji no wimi afwanaje owomi wamntu sauhuvintu evinji evya mntu vyu unavyo.”
LUK 12:16 Wabhabhola eshilale wayanga ogonda ogwa mntu omo otajili lyali lipepe tee,
LUK 12:17 wanda asebhe humwoyo gwakwe, wayanga, embombo wele, afwanaje sendi nupabheshe eshanga eshe viyabho vyane?
LUK 12:18 Wayanga embabhombe eshi, embabozolanye evyanga vyane, ezenje eshamwabho eshi gosi tee, nomwo embabheshe evyelewa vyane vyonti nevintu vyane.
LUK 12:19 Nantele, nayihwibhozya, awe womwoyo gwane olinevintu evinza vinji vyo hwibheye mbuto humaha gaminji. Toyo eshi, alye, omwele, osongwe.”
LUK 12:20 Lelo Ongolobhe wabhozya, olilema awe, osiku ou owasanyono bhahwanza owomi waho, nevintu vyohwibhesheye vibhabhe vyananu?
LUK 12:21 Shesho shali omntu yahwibheye omwoyo gwakwe mbuto, asahwitajilisye hwa Ngolobhe.
LUK 12:22 Wabhabhola asambelezwa bhakwe, afwatana nesho embabhozya mgaje ahwihangayishile amayisha genyu__mbhalya yenu wala amabele genyu mbhakwate yenu.
LUK 12:23 Afwanaje amayisha gazaidieyeshu lya nobele zaidi yemenda.
LUK 12:24 Bhasebhaji enkogolo eyaje sebhato tuwala sebhayabhila, seline shanga wa eshitala, no Ngolobhe abhalisya, mrinafu amwe shila enyonyi!
LUK 12:25 Yonanu hwilimwe yabhajiye ahwi ngayisye nawezye ahwiyonjezye otali wakwe hata okhono gumo?
LUK 12:26 Eshi nkashele semwezizye hata lizu lyalili lidodo, yenu mhwiyazya kwajili yegamwabho?
LUK 12:27 Gasebhelaji amawowa ejinsi shamela segahuhambo embombo wala segabhilinga, neane embubhola yaje hata Osulemani katika efahali yakwe yonti saga kwatiziwe shinza kama neshe eyego,
LUK 12:28 Eshi nkebhe Ongolobhe akwatizya eshi amasole agamwipali, gagali sanyo no na sandabho gatagwa papepe. Je sagayibhabhombela amwe? Enyi amwe mwemli imani endodo!
LUK 12:29 Amwe msahwanza shamwayilya wala shamwaimwele wala mgaje abhombe nowoga.
LUK 12:30 Afwanaje egogonti ebhamnsi omu. Lelo o yise wenyu amenye aje mganza ego.
LUK 12:31 Eshi anzaji omwene owa NGOLOBHE, nego mwayonjezewa,
LUK 12:32 Mganje hwogope, amwe mwikundi idodo, afanaje oYise wenyu alolile shinza abhapele ula oumwene.
LUK 12:33 Kazi vyamlinavyo mfumye sadaka, hwibheshalaji amafuko yasagalala—embuto yasepogoha, humwanya pasaga afiha omwibha wala no ndo sana nkaya.
LUK 12:34 Afanaje embuto yenyu, pehweli pagayibha gahweli na moyo genyu.
LUK 12:35 Amasana genyu gabhe gapinyilya nehozyo, zyenyu zibhe zihwaha,
LUK 12:36 Namwe bhanji neshe abhantu bhabhahugolezya OGOSI wabho naiwela afume huweji, ili na hwenza na khome ehodi bhamwigulile.
LUK 12:37 Nafu asontezewa bhala, ambao OGOSI wabho nayenza ayibhaga bhagonezezye. Eteshi embabhola abhahwipinye nabhakaribizye pa shalye, ayenza nabhavwe.
LUK 12:38 Nankayenze olyondizanyo olwa bhele, au nkayenza olwandiznyo olwatatu nabhaje eshi, nafu ontezewa ebho.
LUK 12:39 Lelo mmanye, izu eli, aje omwane sho nyumba agamenye esaa ya bhahwenze omwibha, handa agone zyezye, wala handa sagaleshele enyumba yakwe ebozolwe.
LUK 12:40 Namwe hwibhehaji tayari afwanaje esaa yasagammenye shesho sha hwenza omwana wa Adamu.
LUK 12:41 OPetro wabhola, “GOSI, eshilale esho otibholele tele wene, au abhantu bhonti antele?
LUK 12:42 OGOSI wayanga, “Wenu eshi yali mtunzaji mwinza yali nebusara ambaye ogosi wakuwe abhahubheshe bhombambombo wakwe wonti, abhapele abhantu eposho huwakati wakwe?
LUK 12:43 Nafu osontezi ola, ambaye gosi wakwe nahwenza awahumwaje abhomba esho.
LUK 12:44 Lyoli embabhola abhahubheshe juu yevintu vyakwe vyonti.
LUK 12:45 Lelo osontelezewa ola nkayanje humwoyo gwakwe, “OGOSI wane wakhala ahwenze wanda; abhakhome aholo bhakwe, alume na bhashe, alya na mwele na kholwe,
LUK 12:46 Ogosi wakwe otumwa oyo ayenza isiku lyasategemeye nesaa yasayimenye, abhahudumranye evipande vibhele nahubheshe ifungu lyakwe pandwemo na bhasaga bhalino lyeteho'
LUK 12:47 No tumwa, ola yagamenye omapenzi ga gosi wakwe, sahwibhe tayari wala agabhombe amapenzi gakwe, ayikhomwa tee.
LUK 12:48 No ola yasagamenye wape abhombile gagahwanziwa akhomwe, akhomwa hashe. Na shila yapewewe evinji, hwamwahale oyo bhanza wanze vivinji, wape wabhesheye amana evintu evinji hwamwahale oyo wabhanza ahwanze zaidi.
LUK 12:49 Enenzere aponye omwoto pansi, na nkashile gwandue ahwanshe lyenu lyehwanza zaidi,
LUK 12:50 Lelo endi no wonzwe wauhwanziwa ahwoziwe, nene endi namalabha neshe eyenu ili gatimizwe!
LUK 12:51 Eshi! mwadhani eyaje enenzele alete eamani? Pansi, embabhola, la seshashesho eshi Mafarakano.
LUK 12:52 Afwanaje afume eshi enyumba emo bhayibha abhantu bhasanu bhavisenye, bhantu hwabhabhele, bhabhele hwa bhantu.
LUK 12:53 Bhayivisanya, oYise no mwana no mwana no Yise wakwe, onyino no lendu wakwe, khoyi wakwe, okhamwana no khamwana wa mntu.
LUK 12:54 Wabhabhola amabungano nantele, “Shila namlola ibhengo nkalifumile oupanda wa magharibi tiyanga, evula ehwenza, ibha shesho,
LUK 12:55 Na shila nevugula hukuskazini, liyanga, hubhabhe nilyoto, na shashi hweli.
LUK 12:56 Amwe mwanafiki, mmenye atambule amaso agensine mwanya, shiliwele eshi abhe semumenye atambule amajira ega?
LUK 12:57 Na mbona amwe mwemwe hunafsi zyenu semu hwamla gagali gelyoli?
LUK 12:58 Eshi namulongozenye no mshitaki waho abhale hwa lonzi, epo pidala bhomba ebidii akondane nawo, asabhe agaburuzya mpaka hwitagalila elya lonzi, ola olonzi wakhata mmakhono gakwe, hwamwenesho yagalipizya nola owalipizye asije agafunga mwijela.
LUK 12:59 Ehubhola, sofuma omwo nkahashe hata omale asombe esenti eya mwisho.
LUK 13:1 Na wakati ou na ou, bhahali abhantu bhabhabholele enongwa eya Bhagalilaya bhala ambabho oPilato asangenye idanda lyabho na dhabihu zyabho.
LUK 13:2 Wabhagagula wabhabhola, “Eshi msebhe eyaje Agalilaya ebho bhali bhabhibhi ashile Agalilaya wonti hata gabhajile amambo ego gonti?
LUK 13:3 Embabhola, siyo, lelo nkashile semlamba amwe mwenti mwaitega shesho.
LUK 13:4 Au bhala kumi na nane bhabhagwelewe no mnara ohwo hu Siloamu wabhagojile msebha eye je abhahale ali bhakosaji ashile abhantu bhonti bhabhakheyee hu Yerusalemu?
LUK 13:5 Embabhola, siyo lelo nkashile semlamba amwe mwenti mwaitega shesho.
LUK 13:6 Wayanga ofwano ogu, “Omuntu omo ali nikwi lyatotilwe mgonda gwakwe elya mizabibu wabhala awanze amadondo juu yakwe sewa gaga.
LUK 13:7 Wabhola omtunzaji owe gonda elye mazabibu enya amaha gatatu ega nenza ahwanze amadondo juu ye yikwi eli. Senahajile ahantu. Oudumre mbona hata ensi enachicha?
LUK 13:8 Wagalula wabhola ogosi oureshe omwaha ogu gwape, 'hata egufugutile enguponyezye eburi.
LUK 13:9 Lyape ugapapa amadodo pamande, shinza; nkashile sewaipapa ndipo odumraje!”'
LUK 13:10 Isiku elya tozye ali asambelezya msjiabhanza eshamwabho.
LUK 13:11 Na enya, pali noshe yali ni pepo lye udhaifu omda ogwe maha kumi naminane wape agolombene sawezizye ahwigolozye tee.
LUK 13:12 O Yesu nawalola akwizizye, wabholo, Maye, oyauliwe katika oudhaifu waho.”
LUK 13:13 Wabheha amakhono gakwe juu yakwe wape wagoroha pepo watukuzya Ongolobhe.
LUK 13:14 Eshi ogosi oweshibhanza avitilwe afwanaje oYesu aponizye omntu isiku elyatozye agalura wabhobhola mabongano zihweli esiku sita zyazihwaziwa abhombe embombo. Basi enzaji mponywe msiku ezyo wala siyo mnsiku ezyatoye.
LUK 13:15 Lelo Ogosi wagalula wayanga amwe, “wanafiki! Shila omo wenyu je sahwigulika eng'ombe yakwe isiku elyatoye mwigoma abhale nayo amwelezye?
LUK 13:16 Vono oshe yali shikholo sha Ibulahimu, ambaye oshetani apinyile amaha kumi na minane ega, sehwanziwa aje ayaulwe evifungo evi isiku elya toye?”
LUK 13:17 Nawayanga ego bhasauhana wonti bhadalihanaga nabho amabongano wonti bha shimo afwanaje eye mambo aminza gagabhombeshe no mwehale.
LUK 13:18 Esho ayanjile oumwene owa Ngolobhe ulengene ne yenu, nane embulenganisye ne yenu?
LUK 13:19 Ulengane ne punje eye haradali yayejile omntu wasasa mgonda gakwe yamela yabha likwii enyonyi ezya mwanya zakhala msamba zyakwe.
LUK 13:20 Wayanga olya bhele engulenganisye neyenu oumwene owa Ngolobhe?
LUK 13:21 Ulengane ne chachu yahejile oshe wayifisa mhati eye pishi zitatu ezye usu hatgwasapa gwonti nantele.”
LUK 13:22 Wope ali shila mmaboma nu mvijiji asambelezya esafari yakwe eyabhale hu Yerusalemu.
LUK 13:23 Omntu omo wabhozya eshi, “Gosi, abhantu bhabhahwaulwa bhadodo?” Wabhola,
LUK 13:24 “Hwitahidi ahwinjile mlyango gula onyela, afanaje embabhola eyaje abhinji bhayanza ahwinjile bhayipotwa.
LUK 13:25 Wakati omwanesho nyumba nayemelela na galile olyango namwe mwayanda ahwemelele hwonze nakhome ehodi palyango, na yanje ee Gosi, tigulile omwahale abhagalule na bhabhole sembamenye hwamufuma.'
LUK 13:26 Esho mwayanda ayanje, Taliye na mweele hwitagalile lyaho nawe wasambelezyezye idala elyetu.”
LUK 13:27 Wape abhayanje embabhola, `sembamenye hwamfumele sogalaji hwiline amwe mwenti mwemuli bhabhomba!'
LUK 13:28 Esho shashabha shililo nasye amino namwanyihulo oIbulahimu no Isaka, no Yakobo na khakuwa wonti abhe umwene owa Ngolobhe namwe mwemwe mponyezyewe hwonze.
LUK 13:29 Wope bhayenza abhantu afume hu Mashariki, na hu Magharibi, nafume hu Kaskazini na hu Kusini, wape bhayikhara pashalye pa umwene owa Ngolobhe.
LUK 13:30 Na enya, wahweli bhali bhamwisho bhayibha bhahwanda na abha hwanda bhayibha bha mwisho.”
LUK 13:31 Esaa yeyo Amafarisayo bhamo bhamo bhabhariye, “Bhabhola fuma epe, obhale pamwabho, afwanaje oHerode ahwanza hugoje.”
LUK 13:32 Wabhabhola, “Bhalaji mbhore ola ombela, `Enya, sanyono na sandabho efumila epepo na ponye empongo, isiku elyatatu ekamiliha.
LUK 13:33 Pandwemo nego enanziwe akhate idala lyane sanyono na shendabho na renda sandabho, afwanaje sehwaziwa aje okuwa atejele hwonze eye Yerusalemu.
LUK 13:34 Ee Yerusalemu, u Yerusalemu, wogoga abhakuwa na bhakhome na mawe bhabhasontezyewe, mara halenga enanzile abhabhonganye abhana bhaho nenshe shila ekuku nebhoganya evyana vyakwe pansi eya mapiho gakwe, wala semwahanzile.
LUK 13:35 Enyaji, mreshewe enyumba yenyu. Nane embabhola, se mwailondola nante na mwaha, hata namwayiyanga asalwe yalwenza hwitawa elya Gosi.”
LUK 14:1 Yabha nawinjila mhati mnyumba eya mntu omo mmiongoni mwagosi abhe Mafarisayo isiku elyatoye, alye eshalye bharibhahuzijira.
LUK 14:2 Enya, hwitagalila lyakwe hwalimntu obhino owe safura.
LUK 14:3 O Yesu wagalula wabhabhola abhane sheria na Farisayo, “Eshi, shinzi apome isiku Elyatoye, au seshasho?”
LUK 14:4 Abhahale bhapoma wakhata waponia, waruhusu abharaje omwene.
LUK 14:5 Wabhabhora wenu kati yenyu ambaye engombe yakwe au edogomi yakwe etumbushiye mwilende wenu yasaga agavumbula isiku elyatoye?”
LUK 14:6 Wape sebhawezizye galule enongwa ezi.
LUK 14:7 Abhabhola ofwano bhala bhahanilwe, nalolile nabhasalula amatengo aga hwitangalila wayanga,
LUK 14:8 “Nkoyanilwe no muntu hu harusi, oganje akhala amatengo aga hwitagalila, ogajebhe aje oyanilwe omntu yaheshimiwa ashile awe.
LUK 14:9 Wenza ola yabhanile awe nomwene, nahubhole osegulishe ono esho shobhahwande abhenesoni awene itengo elya hwisalo.
LUK 14:10 Ila nkoyanwe bhalaga okhala pitengo elya hwisalo, nkashile ola yamwanile abhole, `Rafiki wane, enzaga hwitagalila.” esho pobhabhe nehema hwitagalila elya bhantu wonti bhakheye pandwemo nawe.
LUK 14:11 Afanaje kila wahwikuzya ahwisiwa wape wahwiyisya azuviwa. '
LUK 14:12 Wabhola ola ya mwanile nobhomba eshalye esha pasanya au esha nandwebhela, uganje abhakwizye arafiki bhaho wala aholo bhaho wala amwenyu bhaho wala ajirani bhaho bhabhalineshoma wape bhasahenze bhamwana awe wapata alipe.
LUK 14:13 Eshi nobhomba eshikurukuru bhakwizye apena, alema, na viwete avipofu,
LUK 14:14 nawe obhabhe nafu afwanaje ebhoselinahahulipe afwanaje wayilipwa nawayi owazyoshe owelyoli.”
LUK 14:15 Nawe nawovwa ego omo owabhala bhakheye pashalye pandwemo nawo abholele, “Nafu ola yabhalye ibumunda katika Oumwene owa Ngolobhe!”
LUK 14:16 Wabhola omntu omo abhombile eshikurukuru eshigosi, ahanile abhantu abhinji.
LUK 14:17 Wasontezya obhomba mbombo wakwe esala eyeshalye abhabhole bhala bhabhanilwe, `'Enzaji, afwanaje evintu vyonti vibhehwelwe tayari.'
LUK 14:18 Bhahandile bhonti, afumye audhuru hunia emo. Owahwande abholele, 'Enkarile ogonda, ehwanzaje embale endwenye. Ehulabha onsajile.'
LUK 14:19 Owamwabho wayanga, `'Enkarile eng'ombe, ejozi zisanu embala azilenje ehulabha onsajile.'
LUK 14:20 Owamwabho wayanga, 'Enejile oshe, afwatanesho sebwezizye ahwenze.'
LUK 14:21 Ola osontelezi wabhala wabhola ogosi wakwa enongwa zye mambo ego. Basi ola omwanesho nyumba wavitwa, `'Wabhola osontizi wakwe fuma nanali obhale mwidara igosi na mvichochoto evi boma obhalete epa apena, na lema na vipofu na viwete.”
LUK 14:22 Osontizi wayanga, `Gosi ego golajizizye gamalishe abhombeshe, hata sheshi nemo enafasi.'
LUK 14:23 Ogosi wabhola osontezi, 'Fuma hwonze obhale hubalabala na mpaho obhashurutishe ahwinjile mhati, enyumba yane ebhe ememile.
LUK 14:24 Eshi embabhola yaje katika bhala bha bhahanilwe sahweli hata omo yabhayilenje eshikurukuru shane. '
LUK 14:25 Amabongano aminji nabhali bhahubhenjeya wape, agalushe wabhabhola,
LUK 14:26 'Nkashele omntu nkayeze hwiline wape sahuvitu oyise wakwe, no nyine wakwe, noshe wakwe, na bhana bhakwe, na holo bhakwe abheshilume na bhesheshe- nantele hata enafsi yakwe yoyo sawezizye abha mwanafunzi wane.
LUK 14:27 Omntu yoyonti yasayeji eshikhobhohanyo shakwe nahwenzi hwisalo lyane sawezizye abha mwanafunzi wane.
LUK 14:28 Eshi wenu kati amwe, nkashile ohwanza azenje omnara yasakhala nasoti na bhazye egharama aje alinavyo evyamalelezye?
LUK 14:29 Asibhe wamenwa amale baada eyazenje omsingi abhantu wonti bhabhalola bhaganda huseshe,
LUK 14:30 bhayanga, Omntu ono ahandile azenje wabha salinamaha aga malezyenje.'
LUK 14:31 Au huli no mwene wele, nkahwanza abhale alwe no mwene owenje yasakhala nsoti na abhombe ajehane, aje omwahale pandwemo na bhantu elfu kumi agawezya atangane nola yahwenza juu yakwe na bhantu elfu ishilini?
LUK 14:32 Na nkashile walola sewezizye asontezya oujumbe ogwahwanza eamani omntu ola salihutari.
LUK 14:33 Shila omo wenyu yasaleshile vyonti vyalinavyo sawezizye abhe mwanafunzi wane.
LUK 14:34 Omwoni hantu ahinza, lelo omwoni nkashile gunanjishe oponyeye nu ili gukhole?
LUK 14:35 Seguhwanziwa mnsi wala jaa abhantu bhaitaga hwonze. Yali namakutu agatejezye, na ayovwe.”
LUK 15:1 Basi asonjezya abhesonga bhonti na bhala abhibhi bhali bhahukaribira bhamwovwe.
LUK 15:2 Afalisayo na simbi bhauna bhayanga, “Omuntu ono abhakaribizya abhe mbibhi nantele alya nabho.”
LUK 15:3 Wabhabhola omfano ogu wayanga
LUK 15:4 “Wenu hwilimwe yali nengole mia nkatejire emo yasagazileha zira tisini na tisa mwipoli, abhale ayanze ele yetejile hata eyilore?
LUK 15:5 Wape nkashile walola ahubheha mmapongo gakwe ashimile.
LUK 15:6 Nafiha akhaya yakwe, abhakwizya arafiki bhakwe na jirani bhakwe abhabhore shimaji pandwemo nane, afwanaje enjajile engore yane yehatejire.'
LUK 15:7 embabhola shesho hwanyibha ashime amwanya kwajili ya bhibhi omo yaramba ashile abhinza tisini na tisa ambao sebhalamba
LUK 15:8 Nu hulino she wele yali nesilinje kumi nkawatezya esilinje emo, sahwasya okhozyo n ahwose mnyumba na hwanze hubidii hata ayilole?
LUK 15:9 Na nkashile ayilole abhakwizya arafiki bhakwa na jirani bhakwe abhabhola shimaji pandwemo nane afwanaje enjajile esilinje ela yehatejire.
LUK 15:10 Embabhola shesho hulisongwe hwitagalila elya kuwa abha Ngolobhe kwajiri yola obhibhi omo yaramba.”
LUK 15:11 Wayanga, “Omntu omo alinabhana bhabhele
LUK 15:12 ola ododo wabhola oyise, Baba mpele eshemu eye shoma yegwela. Wabhagabhila evintu vyakwe.
LUK 15:13 Hata pitagalila ensiku senyinji ola ododo wabhonganya vyonti wasogora abhale ensi eya ohutari wanankanya eshoma shakwe ohwo humaisha ege uhuni.
LUK 15:14 Nawabha anankenye eshoma shonti enzala egosi ehinjiye mnsi ela omwahale wape wanda ahwanze.
LUK 15:15 Wabhala wakhata nokhaya omo owensi ela, wape atwaliile hugonda gwakwe arere engorobhe.
LUK 15:16 Wabha atamari alya amakhondo gazyalyanga egorobhe wala nomo omntu yapanga ahantu.
LUK 15:17 Nawasebhelela humwoyo gwakwe ayanjila bhali bhalenga abhomba mbomba hwa babawane bhabhalya eshalye nasagazye nane epa efwa nenzala!
LUK 15:18 Embasogole embabhale hwa baba wane na hubhole, “Baba enkosile juu eye mwanya na hwitagalila lyaho.
LUK 15:19 Sehwanziwa akwiziwe mwana waho nantele; mbombo neshe abhombambo bhabho.”
LUK 15:20 Wasogola wabhala hwa yise. Nalisa hutali oyise wakwe alolile walolela husajire wabhala sashembela wagwele msingo wayayila tee.
LUK 15:21 Ola omwana wabhola, 'oyise enkosile juu yemwanya na hwitalila lyaho sehwanziwa akwiziwa mwana waho nantele.'
LUK 15:22 Lelo oyise abhabholele abhombambombo bhakwe, 'leti nanali omwenda gawguli gwinza, mkwenesye peli nepete mshidole na virato.
LUK 15:23 Reti endama ela yenonile msizile nate tilye nashime.
LUK 15:24 Afwanaje ono omwana wane ali afwiye wape azyoshele. Ali atejira wape abhoneshe bhanda ashanjilile.
LUK 15:25 Basi ola omwana wakwe ogosi ali hugonda. Nali ahwenza napalamile pakhaga ahovwezye amazu ege ngoma na shawa hwanga.
LUK 15:26 Wakwizya obhomba mbombo omo wabhozya amambo ego geyenu?
LUK 15:27 Wabhola oholo waho ayenzele no yise waho asinziye endama yenonile apwanje amwajile nantele ali mwomi.'
LUK 15:28 Wavitwa wakhana ahwinjile mhati basi oyise wafumire hwonze walabha.
LUK 15:29 Wagalula oyise wakwe wayanga, 'Enya ane ebhombeye amaha galenga ega wala senkosile endajizyo zyaho wakati wawonti, lelo sompiye ane enya na ye mbuzi embombe ashime na rafiki bhane.
LUK 15:30 Lelo nawenza ono omwana waho yaliye vintu vyaho pandwemo na malaya asinziye omwahale endama yenonile.
LUK 15:31 Wabhola, 'Mwana wane, awe olipandwemo nane ensiku zyonti vyendi navyo vya huliwe.
LUK 15:32 Antele abhombe ashima ne shangwe ehali yelazima afwanaje; ali atejile wape abhoneshe.”
LUK 16:1 Antele abhabholele asambelezwe bhakwe, “Pali no mntu omo alitakiri alino wakili wakwe, ono atakwilwe hwamwahale anankanya eshoma shakwe.
LUK 16:2 Wakwizya wabhola, “Nongwa wele ezi zyehwovwa juu ya hwiliwe? Fumia ehesabu eye owakili waho afwanaje sowezizye abhe wakili nantele.'
LUK 16:3 Ola owakili wayanga mumwoyo gwa kwao, Embombe wele, nkashere ogosi wane anefwa ouwakili? Alime sebwezizye alabhe, elola esoni.
LUK 16:4 Endimenye lyembabhombe ili nabhanefwe huwakili bhankaribizyaje mkhaya zyabho.
LUK 16:5 Wabhakwizya bhabhakhopile amadeni aga gosi wakwe shila omo wabhora owhwande, 'odayiwa nogosi wane?'
LUK 16:6 Wayanga eshipimo mia eshe mafuta wabhora 'ege ehati yaho simba hamsini.'
LUK 16:7 antele wabhora owamwaho na we odaiwa?' wayanga 'makanda mia age ngano wabhoro ega ehati yaho simba themanini.'
LUK 16:8 Ola gosi wasomba owakili dhalimu shashila shabhombile hubusara. Afwanaje abhana abhensi ene katika epapo yabho bhebho bhabha ne busara ashile abhana abhe lukhozyo.
LUK 16:9 Nane embabhola bhombelaji abhe rafiki weshoma eshe udhalimu ili nehaibhanemo bhabhakaribizyaje hukhaya eye umilele.
LUK 16:10 Yali mwamini lyalili lidodo tee abhamwamini hwi gosi nantele. na yali dhalimu hwidolo abhabhe dhalimu hata hwigosi nantele.
LUK 16:11 Basi nkashile amwe semwali bhaminifu hushoma eshe udhalimu wenu wabhapele amana eshoma eshelyoli?
LUK 16:12 Na nkashile semwali bhaminifu hushoma esha mntu owenje wenu yabhabhapele yeli yahulimwe mwemwe?
LUK 16:13 Nomo obhombambo yabhabhambele agosi bhabhele, afwanaje abhahuvitwe ono nahusongwe ono, au abhakhatane nono na hudhalau ono. Sawezizye hutumishile Ongolobhe ne shoma.”
LUK 16:14 Basi Mafarisayo, abhene bhebho bhasogwa ehela bhahovwezye ago gonti bha dhihaki.
LUK 16:15 Wabhabhola, “Mwe mwemwe mhwidai elyoli hwitagalila elya bhantu, lelo Ongolobhe abhamenye amoyo genyu afwanaje lyalisobwa hwa bhanadamu uhuvisya hwitagalila elya Ngolobhe.
LUK 16:16 Etorati na kuwa vyahali mpaka Yohani afume. Ouwakati wowo enongwa enyinza ezye umwene owa Ngolobhe zitangaziwa, na shila mntu ahwiyinjizya humaha.
LUK 16:17 Lelo nafu zaidi emwanya nensi vyepe ashile aje etanguliwe enukta emo eye torati.
LUK 16:18 Shila yahuleha oshe wakwe na humweje oshe owenje azini wape yahumwega yalehwilye nolume wakwe anazini.
LUK 16:19 Pali ono mntu takili akwete nu menda ege rangi ye zambarau na kitani nyinza na lye ensiku zyonti kwa anasa.
LUK 16:20 No pena omo itawa lyakwe yo Lazaro abhehwelya palyango gwakwe ali na malonda gaminji.
LUK 16:21 Wape ali akitamani akutiziwe amambo gagalagaliye pameza eyola otakiri hata embwa zyeza zya guna amaronda gakwe.
LUK 16:22 Yabha ola opena wagwa wegwano malaika paka pashifiwa esha Ibulahimu ola otakiri wape wafwa wa syelwa.
LUK 16:23 Basi ohula huzimu abhosezye amaso gakwe nali pamarabha walola Ibulahimu sahutari no Lazaro pashifua shakwe.
LUK 16:24 Walila wayanga, 'Ee baba Ibulahimu, sajire osontezye oLazaro atobhezye echa eye shidole shakwe mmenze, aluburudishe omele lwane; afwanaje elabha mu mwoto omu.
LUK 16:25 Ibulahimu wayanga, 'Mwanawane kumbuhaga eyaje awe waposheye amambo aminza gahuliwe katika amaisha gaho, no Lozaro shesho apete amabhibhi na eshi omwahale aliepa afarijiwa na awe ovwalala.
LUK 16:26 Na zaidi yego kati yetu ate na mwe libhehwelwe irende igosi, ili bhala bhabhafuma ohwo abhale hwilimwe bhagajeshile wala abhantu abhahwilimwe bhagaje shile ahwenze hwititi.'
LUK 16:27 Wayanga, 'Basi Baba ehulabha, osontezye akhaya hwa baba wane
LUK 16:28 afwanaje endi na holo bhasanu ili abhashudile bhasije bhape nantele bhafihe mahali epa pamalabha. '
LUK 16:29 Ibulahimu wayanga, 'Bhalinabho oMusa na kuwa. Na bhabhovwe ebho.
LUK 16:30 Wayanga, 'la, Baba Ibrahimu, lelo nkashile abhabhabhalile omntu yafuma hwa bhafwa bhanzarambe.'
LUK 16:31 Wabhola nkashele sebhabhowa aMusa nu kuwa sebhanzashawishiwe hata omntu nkashile azyoshe afume wabhafwe.
LUK 17:1 Wabhabhola asambelezewa bhakwe, “evisyo sevi nebudi ahwenze lelo ole wakwe omntu ola ambaye gahwenza afwatane nomwahale!
LUK 17:2 Yakhondeye zaidi omntu oyo iwe elyasyole lipinyeve msingo yakwe aponywe mwidimi, ashile abhavisye miongoni mwadodo ebha.
LUK 17:3 Hwirindi. Nkashile ohoro waho nkakoseye sunde, nkarambe sajire.
LUK 17:4 Nankashile akosire mara saba katika isiku limo, nawele hwiliwe mara saba nkayanje, 'erabha,' sajire!”
LUK 17:5 Atumwa bhabhola Gosi, “Tonjezye oweteho.”
LUK 17:6 Ogosi wayanga, “nkashele mgari no lweteho ekiasi eshe chembe eye haradali, mwezaga alibhole iko eli senyeha, 'utotwe mwidimi,' wope ungewaheshimu.
LUK 17:7 Lelo wenu hwilimwe, omwanesho obhomba yalima au yadima ing'ombe, yabhalubho nawera afume hugonda, 'Enzaa epa nanali khara olye eshalye?
LUK 17:8 Je sabhahulobhe mbombele tayari eshalye endwe, hwipinye ombombele hata endwe na mwele. Nawe pobhalya na mwele?
LUK 17:9 Je abhahupere emwasalipa ola obhomba mbombo afwanaje abhombile galajiziwe?
LUK 17:10 Shesho namwe namwayibha mumari abhombe gonti gamlajiziwe yangaje 'Ate tili bhasontezewa bhasebhali ne faida. Tibhombile wene gaganziwaga tibhombe.'
LUK 17:11 Yabha nabhali mwidara nabhala hu Yerusalemu, ali ashira mhati eye Samaria na Galilaya.
LUK 17:12 Nawinjira mshijiji shimo, atangene nu bhantu kumi bhali no ukoma. Bhemelela sahutari
LUK 17:13 bhakhora humaza bhayanga “Ee Yesu, Gosi owa Gosi otisajire.”
LUK 17:14 Nawabhalola wabhabhola, “Eshi bhalaji mhwibhonezye hwa kohani.” yabha nabhali bhabhale bhahozyewe.
LUK 17:15 Na omo miongoni mwabho nawalola aje aponile awelile, ohuu ahutukuzya Ongolobhe hwizu igosi.
LUK 17:16 Wagwa fugamila pamagaga gakwe na husalifwe wapa ali msamaria.
LUK 17:17 O Yesu wagalura, wayanga, “Sebhatakasyewe wonti kumi? Bhala tisa bhalihwi?
LUK 17:18 Eshi sebhabhonesha bhabhawelile hupele Ongolobhe, outukufu ila ojenyi ono?”
LUK 17:19 Wabhora, “Imelela walaga wewe olweteho lwaho lumwauye.”
LUK 17:20 Nabhozyewaga na mafarisayo umwene owa Ngolobhe wayenza ndii, Aglula wabhabhola, “Umwe owa Ngolobhe seuhwenza agodezyegozye.
LUK 17:21 Wala sebhayiyanga, 'Enya uhweli ohwo!' au, 'Hula!' afwanaje enya umwene owa Ngolobhe uhweli mhati yenyu.”
LUK 17:22 Wabhabhola asambeleziwa bhakwe, “Ensiku zihwenza namwitamani alole isiku limo katika ensiku zyakwe Omwana wa Adamu, samwaizilola.
LUK 17:23 Antele bhayibhabhola, 'Enyi, ohu! Mganje, sogole pala!' Paruhweli wala msabharondozye,
LUK 17:24 afwanaje neshe shila oumeme shaukhozya hata upande ou owensi eye mwanya. Esho shashayiha Omwana owa Adamu katika ensiku zyakwe.
LUK 17:25 Lelo ahwanda sali nebudi apate marabha aminji na khanwe neshikholo.
LUK 17:26 Ila nkashele shashahali ensiku ezya Nuhu, esho shashayibha katika ensiku zyakwe Omwana owa Adamu.
LUK 17:27 Bhali bhalya na mwele na hweje na hwegwe hata isiku ila o Nuhu yahinjile katika mwisafina amakhoshi gahishile gabhangamizizye wonti.
LUK 17:28 Na nkashile shahali katika ensiku zya Lutu, bhali bhalya na mwele, wali bhakala na kazye, bhatotaga nazenje.
LUK 17:29 Lelo isiku lila Lutu yafumile Msodoma, gwahishile omwoto neshibiriti afume amwanya gwabhatezizye wonti.
LUK 17:30 Esho shashayibha isiku lila lyayibhonesyewa owa Omwana owa Adamu.
LUK 17:31 Katika isiku lila yali juu yogoro na evyelelo vyakuwa vili mhati eyenyumba agaje hwishe ili ayeje. Nantele yali hugonda ga jewele hwisalo.
LUK 17:32 Izuhaji oshe wa Lutu.
LUK 17:33 Omntu yoyonti yabhaponje enafisi yakwe abhayitezye nayoyonti yayitezye, abhayiponie.
LUK 17:34 Wabhabhola, osiku owo abhantu bhabhele bhayibha ishitara shimo. Omo ayegwe omo ayilehwa.
LUK 17:35 Abhashe bhabhele bhayibha bhasya pandwemo, omo ayegwe omo ayilehwa.” Abhantu bhabheke bhayibha hugonda omo ayegwa omo ayirehwa.”
LUK 17:37 Bhagalula bhabhozya, “Woshi, Gosi?” Wabhabhola, “Peli efwe nyene pepo pabhayitanganila enyonyi.”
LUK 18:1 Wabhabhora omfano yaje ehwanziwa hulabhe Ongolobhe ensiku zyonti wala mgajekate etama.
LUK 18:2 wayanga, 'Pali no lozi katika iboma limlimo sahuputa Ongolobhe wala sahwogapa abhantu.
LUK 18:3 Na katika iboma elyo pali noshe ofwele ali ahubhaliila bhalila, ayanga, 'Pele ehaki na adui bhane.'
LUK 18:4 Wapa humda akhene antele wayanga humwoyo gwakwe, iwapo sehuputa Ongolobhe wala sehwogopa abhantu,
LUK 18:5 lelo afwanaje ofwele ono avisya ambahupe ehaki yakwe asayenza andisye anenzele tee.”
LUK 18:6 Ogosi wayanga tejerezi gayanga ola olozi odhalimu.
LUK 18:7 No Ngolobhe je Sabhabhapele elyoli bhaala bhateulie bhakwe bhabhahuli lila osaya no siku? wape jivi hwabhahale?
LUK 18:8 Embabhora ayibhapera ehaki nanali. Lelo nayenza Omwana owa Adamu je ayiyilola imani pa dunia? '
LUK 18:9 Wabhabhora ofano ogu abhantu bhabhahwikinalile eyaji abhabhare bhalinelyoli bhabhasolanya abhanje wonti,
LUK 18:10 'Abhantu bhabhele bhazumile mwibhanza apute: Omo Farisayo owabhele asonjezya esonga.
LUK 18:11 Ola oFarisayo wemelela arabhe eshi humwoyo gwakwe, 'Ee Ngolobhe, ehusalifwa afwanaje ane sendi neshe abhantu abhanje, bhabhafyala, adhalimu, ahuni, wala neshe ono yasonjezya esonga.
LUK 18:12 Ane efunga habhele hurungo. Efumia ifungu elyakumi katika amapato gane gonti. '
LUK 18:13 Lelo ola yasonjezya esonga ahemeleye sahutari, wala gagawezizye hata huhwenye amaso gakwe amwanya esho ahwikhamile khonile pashifubha ayanga, 'Ee Ngolobhe, osajile ane endibhibhi.'
LUK 18:14 Embabhola, ono ahishile abhara akhaya yakwe abhaziwe elyoli ashile ola afwanaje kila wa hwinyunula adhiriwa wape ajidhiliye abhakuziwe. '
LUK 18:15 Bhatwalila abhana abhere ili abhapalamasye, lelo asambelezewa bhakwe, nabhabhalola bhabhadamile.
LUK 18:16 Esho oYesu wakiwzya bhale hwamwe hale wayanga, 'Bhareshi abhana adodo bhenze hwiline wala msabhagomele afwanaje abhantu neshe ebho oumwene owa Ngolobhe wabho.
LUK 18:17 'Eteshi embabhola, omntu yeyonti ya sahwejelela oumwene owa Ngolobhe nenshe omwana ododo sagaayinjila nantele. '
LUK 18:18 Antale omntu ogosi omo abhozezye ayanjile sambelezi mwinza embombe wele ili empewe agale owomi owa hanihani?'
LUK 18:19 O Yesu wabhabhora, 'Eshi mnkwizya mwimza? Nomo omwinza ila aliomo wape yo Ngolobhe.
LUK 18:20 Ozimenye endijizwo- ogajebhe huni, ogajegoje, ogaje ahwibhe, ogaje ayanje ilenka obhaheshimu oYise waho no nyina waho.
LUK 18:21 Wayanga ege gonti engakhete afume huwana wane.'
LUK 18:22 O Yesu nawovwa ego abhorale, “Apongoshewe izu limo osele. Kazya vyolinavyo vyonti obhagabhile apena nawe abhabhe nembuto amwanya nantele enze ondodore. '
LUK 18:23 Lelo nahovwezye ego akongobheye tee, afwanaje alineshoma shiminji.
LUK 18:24 O Yesu nawalola shila wayanga, 'Hushida wele abheshoma bhayinjila oumwene owa Ngolobhe!
LUK 18:25 Afwanaje shororo engamia ashile pitundo elye shindano ashile otakili ahwinjile oumwene owa Ngolobhe. '
LUK 18:26 Bhape bhabahovwe bhayanjile wenu eshi yagaulwe?'
LUK 18:27 Wayanga, 'Gasegawezeha wabhanadamu gawezehana hwa Ngolobhe.”
LUK 18:28 O Petro wayanga, 'Enya, ate tivileshire evintu vyetu vyonti na hurondorere.
LUK 18:29 'Wabhabhora, Lyoli embabhora nomo omntu yayireshire enyumba yakwe, au oshe, au ohoro, au apafi, au abhana, kwajili eye Umwene owa Ngolobhe,
LUK 18:30 yasagayiposhera hahinji katika amaha ega, na katika ensi yihayinza no womi hanihani. '
LUK 18:31 Wabhega bhala thenashara, wabhabhora, 'Enyi, tizubha abhale hu Yerusalemu, amambo gonti gawatimiziwe Omwana owa Adamu gasibwililwe na kuwa.
LUK 18:32 Afwanaje abhakhatwe mmakhono age bha Mataifa aibhombelwa edhahaka, abhabhombelwe azyongolwe nu huswele amate.
LUK 18:33 Wape bhayihukhoma namajeredi esho bhayihugoga, isiku elyatatu ayizyoha. '
LUK 18:34 Lelo sebhahelewa enongwa ezyo atahashe, ejambo elyo lyafisilwe hwabhahale, wala sebhamenye gagayagwilwe.
LUK 18:35 Yabha na apalamie hu Yeriko, omntu omo kipofu ali akheye pashenje ye dara alabhaga esadaka,
LUK 18:36 na wovwa mabongano na bhashila wabhozya huliyenu.
LUK 18:37 Bhabhola oYesu owa hu Nazareti ashira.
LUK 18:38 Wakhora ehoro wayanga, Yesu Mwana wa Daudi, osajire.'
LUK 18:39 basi bhala bhatagaliye bhadamila ili apome, lelo umwahara ahonjezezye sana apayushe izu, 'Ee Mwana wa Daudi, osajire.
LUK 18:40 O Yesu wemerela wamurisya atwarwe hwamwahare nu paramiye abhozezye,
LUK 18:41 'Ohwanza ebhombele yenu?' Wayanga, 'Gosi, empate alole.'
LUK 18:42 O Yesu wabhora, 'Opewe alole. Olweteho olweho luponizye. '
LUK 18:43 Mara eyo wapata alore, wabhenjezye ohu ahusifu Ongolobhe. Na bhantu bhonti na bhalori ego bhasifure Ongolobhe.
LUK 19:1 Wape nahunjiye hu Yeriko ashirile pahati yakwe.
LUK 19:2 Na enya pali no mntu ityawa lyakwe Zakayo. Gosi hwabha sonjezya esonga wape takiri.
LUK 19:3 Ono ahanzaga hulore oYesu mntu yali welewele sagawezizye afwatane no winji wabhantu eshi fupi wekimo.
LUK 19:4 Watangulira sashembera winjira amwanya mwiko ilipate hurole afwanaje abhahwenze shilire idara lila.
LUK 19:5 Na oYesu ashilile esehemu ela, ehenyizye amwanya wabhora, 'Zakayo, iha nanali, afwanaje sanyono ehwanziwa alenda mnyumba yaho.'
LUK 19:6 Wabhomba nanali, wiha wakaribizya ohu ashiye.
LUK 19:7 Hata bhantu nabhavolire bhaunire wonti, bhayanga, 'Ayinjiye akhare hwa mntu owe mbibhi.'
LUK 19:8 Zakayo wemerela wabhora Gosi, Enya Gosi enusu eye shoma shane embapera apena nkashera efyelere omntu ahantu huhila ehuwezezya mara zinne. '
LUK 19:9 O Yesu wabhora sanyono owaule ufishire mnyumba omu afwanaje ono wape mwana wa Ibrahimu.
LUK 19:10 Afwanaje Mwana wa Adamu ahenzere ahwanze na hwaule shila shashitejire. '
LUK 19:11 Nabhahovwezye ego, ahonjeye ayanje omfano afwanaje aripapepe ne Yerusalemu, bhape bhasebhere aje oumwene owa Ngolobhe ubhonesha nunari.
LUK 19:12 Basi wayanga, 'Omntu omo kabaila asafiriye abhare ensi yahutari ili ahwipere oumwene na were.
LUK 19:13 Wabhakwizya abhantu kumi katika asontezi bhakwe awapera amafungu kumi agehela wabhabhora bhombaji ebiashara hata nehayenza.'
LUK 19:14 Lelo abhantu abhe boma lyakwa bhavititwe bhasontezyezye oujumbe hurondore na yanje setihumwanza ono atilongozye.'
LUK 19:15 Yabha nawawela apete oumwene wakwe wamuru bhakwizizwe bhala atumwa bhabhapiye ehela, ili amanye efaida yapete shila mntu huchuruzi wakwe.
LUK 19:16 Wenza owahwande wayanga, `Gosi, ifungu liretire efaida eye fungu kumi zaidi. '
LUK 19:17 Wabhora, Shinza mtumwa mwinza hwashila sholi mwaminifu hunongwa endodo obhe na mamlaka amafungu juu ya maboma kumi. '
LUK 19:18 Wenza owabhele wayanga, 'Gosi, ifungu lyaho liretire amafungu gasanu efiada.'
LUK 19:19 Wabhora ono wape awe owe juu eye maboma gasanu.'
LUK 19:20 Wenza owamwabho wayanga, `Gosi eli lifungu lyaho ambalo nabheshere mbuto mreso.'
LUK 19:21 afwanaje namwogope afwanaje oli mntu okhome ohwefu husobheshere okhome, ohwefu hasobheshere okonga hasaga ototire.
LUK 19:22 Wabhora ambahulonje hwiromu lyaho wotumwa wobhibhi awe wamenye aje endi mntu khome. Nehwefwe hasembeshere na ekonga husetolile.
LUK 19:23 Basi, eshi sohabheshere ehela yane hwa bhafumia eriba ili nehwenza enjagaje pandwemo nefaida yakwe?
LUK 19:24 Wabhabhola bhabhemeleye papepe fyori elyo ifungu mpere ola yali namafungu kumi.'
LUK 19:25 Bhabhora, `Gosi, anago amafungu kumi. '
LUK 19:26 Embabhora, shila yali nahantu abhapewe lelo ola yasalinahantu bhafyolwe hata halinaho.
LUK 19:27 Antele bhala adui bhane bhadebhahwanza aje embalongozye bhareti epa mbhabhole hwitagalila lyane.”
LUK 19:28 Nawamala ayanje ego atanguliye hwitagalila wazubha abhare hu Yerusalemu.
LUK 19:29 Yabha na paramiye pa Bethfage na Bethania, hwigamba lyalihwetwa Mizeituni, asontezyezye bhabhele katika bhala asambeleziwa,
LUK 19:30 wayanga: `Bhalaji mpaka nshijiji shila shashili papepe omwana-dogomi apinyilwe ambaye sawayile ahwinjilwe no mntu yoyonti asele mwauli mrete epa.
LUK 19:31 Na nkashile omntu abhabhozye eshi mhumwalayanji eshi Ogosi ane shida nawo.”
LUK 19:32 Na bhala bhasontezywe bhalile bhalolile ne nshe shabhabholele.
LUK 19:33 Nabhali bhahumwaula omwana-dogomi abhanesho bhabhabhozya mbona mhwaula edogomi?'
LUK 19:34 Bhayanga, `Ogosi aline shida nawo. '
LUK 19:35 Bhatwala hwa Yesu bhara amenda gabho juu ya mwana dogomi bhamwinjizya oYesu.
LUK 19:36 Na hali abhala bhabhambshe amenda gabho mwidara.
LUK 19:37 Hata nali aparamiye ahwishe mwigamba elya Mizeituni, ikundi lyonti elyasambelezewa wakwe bhahandira ashime na husifu Ongolobhe humazu amagosi eye mambo gakwe age mahaa gabhagalolile,
LUK 19:38 bhayanga, 'Ndiye yasayilwe mwene yahwenza hwitawa elya Gosi! Amani amwanya na utukufu ohwo amwanya!'
LUK 19:39 Bhamo Afarisayo bhabhahari pabongano bhabhora, Sambelezi obhakhane asambelezi wa bhaho. '
LUK 19:40 Wagalula wayanga embabhora amwe nkabhapome kati ebhe amawe gabhohomere ohoro. '
LUK 19:41 Nawafiha papepe walilola iboma walilillaa,
LUK 19:42 wayanga, lelo ogamenye hata awe katika isiku eli gagawanziwa amani! Lelo eshi gafisilye pamaso gaho.
LUK 19:43 Afwanaje isiku zyayenza adui bhaho nabhayihuzenjela boma, lizyongole bhaihuzyongola epande zyonti.
LUK 19:44 Bhayihugwisya pansi nabhana bhaho mhati yaho. Bhasiteshere iwe juu iwe, afwanaje sohamanyaga amajira agahwenzele hwaho'.
LUK 19:45 Winjita mwibhanza wanda abhafumie bhala bhabhabhombaga ebiashara,
LUK 19:46 abhabhola, “Isimbwilwe, 'Enyumba yane ebhabhe nyumba ye mputo.' lelo amwe muyibhombile abhe ligwenya lyo bhafyola”.
LUK 19:47 Wape wabha asambelezya shila lisiku mwibhanza. Lelo Gosi Abhakohani na simbi na agosi abhabhantu bhali bhahwanza idara elya hutezye,
LUK 19:48 sebhalilora elya bhombe afwanaje abhantu bhonti bhahwandamano nawo bhahutejezya.
LUK 20:1 Yabha isiku limo, ali asambelezya abhantu Mwibhanza na alombelele enongwa enyinza, agosi abhe makuhani na Simbi pandwemo na zehe bhabhaliye nanali.
LUK 20:2 Bhabhora, bhayanga, 'Tibhore obhomba amambo ego humaha ganu nantele yonu yapiye amaha ege?”
LUK 20:3 Wagalula wabhabhora, 'Nane ambabhobhozye amwe enongwa zimo mbori
LUK 20:4 owoziwa owa Yohana. Je, wapumile amwanya au wabhantu? '
LUK 20:5 Bhagamzanya bhebho hwa bhebho, wayanga, 'Nkashere, `Tije ufumile amwanya, ayanje, ` Basi, mbona semwamwetesha?'
LUK 20:6 Nkatije tiyanje aje ufumire hwa bhantu; abhantu bhonti bhanzatikhome na mawe afwanaje bhamweteshe oYohana aje kuhwe. '
LUK 20:7 Bhagalula aje sagatimenye hwa ufumere.
LUK 20:8 O Yesu wabhabhola, “'Wala ane sembhabhola amwe humaha gananu gebhomba amambo ega.”
LUK 20:9 Wanda abhabhore abhantu hufwa no ogu, “Omntu omo atotira ogonda ogwe mazabibu, wapanjizya bhabhalima, wabhara wakhala hunsi eyamwabho humuda ogwinji.
LUK 20:10 Na wakati owakonje asontezyezye owe mbombo owamwabho bhakhoma ono wape bhakenyesya bhatunga mmakhono aliwene.
LUK 20:11 Wasontezya newembombo owa mwabho bhakhama wape bhakenyesya bhatanga namakhono- wene.
LUK 20:12 Wasonteleya no watatu ono wape bha vwalazya bhataga hwonze.
LUK 20:13 Basi ogosi owe gonda ogwe mizabibu ayanjile, embombewele? Embahusontezye omwana wane wegene ane. Olwenje bhagamwogopa omwene. '
LUK 20:14 Lelo bhala abhalima nabhalorile bhashauliyene bhene hwe bhene bhayanga ono wagare eshi tigoje ili agalo ubhe wetu. '
LUK 20:15 Bhataga hwonze hugonda ogwe mizabibu bhagoga. Basi ogosi owe gonda elye mzabibu abhabhabhombe wele?
LUK 20:16 Awahenze nabhatezye bhabhalima bhala nogonda gula ogwe mizabibu, anzabhapele abha mwabho nabhovwa ego bhayanga, 'Basi gasafumire ega'
LUK 20:17 Wabhalangulila amaso wayanga emana yakwe yenu eshi izu eli lyalisibwilwe, iwe lyabhalikhene wa ashi elyo liwe igosi lyalishenje'?
LUK 20:18 Nkashele kila muntu yayigwela piwe elyo abhabudushe walyayihugwela lyayihusya tee. '
LUK 20:19 Bhape asimbi na gosi makuhani bhahanzile hukhate esula yeyo, bhabhogopa abhantu afwanaje bhamenye aje ofwano ogu abhayanjire bhebho.
LUK 20:20 Bhazijira zijira bhasontezya owa pelelezye bhahwibhesheye aje bhantu bhelyoli ili bhatonele afumire nenjango zyakwe bhapute hubheshe katika enzi eye utawala owa liwali.
LUK 20:21 Bhabhozya bhayanga sambilezi timenye eyaje oyanga na sambelezye gagali gelyoli wala sojali echeo eshamntu bali osambelezya idara elyo Ngolobhe elyelyoli.
LUK 20:22 Eshi je harari tipile o Kaisari esonga au seshashesho?”
LUK 20:23 Lelo omwene amenye azyongora hwabho wabhabhora,
LUK 20:24 “Mbonesi edinari. Eno waje namandi gananu?” Bhagalula, “Ya Kaisari.”
LUK 20:25 Wabhabhora, 'Basi, evya Kaisari mpele oKaisari, nevya Ngolobhe mpeleje Ongolobhe.'
LUK 20:26 Wala sagabhawezizye ahutake hunongwa zyakwe hwitagalila elya bhantu. Bhaswiga amajibu gakwe bhapoma.
LUK 20:27 Yabha bhamo bhamo Masaduayo bhabhalila, bhala bhabhayanga yaje na humo azyoshe bhabhozya,
LUK 20:28 bhayanga, “Sambelezi, oMusa atisimbiye eyaje omntu nkafwelwe noholo wakwe ali noshe lelo salinomwa na amweje ono oshe apapile oholo wakwe abhana.
LUK 20:29 Basi bhali ahola saba owahwande ahejele oshe wafwa sali na mwana,
LUK 20:30 na owabhele(wamwega ola oshe wafwa sali no mwana).
LUK 20:31 Hata owatatu wamwega na bhamwabho wonti saba, bhafwa sebhaleshile abhana.
LUK 20:32 Humalisholo wafwa ola oshe wape.
LUK 20:33 Basi katika azyoshe ayibha she wananu? Afanaje ahegwilwa nabho wonti saba. '
LUK 20:34 O Yesu wabhora, “Abhana abhe ulimwengu ogu bhahwega nahwegwe.
LUK 20:35 Lelo bhala bhabhabhaziwa emwanya ela na hula azyoshe hwabhabhafwiye sebhahwega wala sebhahwegwe.
LUK 20:36 Wala sebhawezizye afwa nantele afwanaje mlengana wene na malaika bhape bhana bha Ngolobhe, shila shabhali bhazyoshe.
LUK 20:37 Lelo eyaje abhafwa bhayizyoha hata yo Musa alangwilwe owaje owe sazo epo payanjile Ogosi aje yo Ngolobhe owa Ibrahimu na Ongolobhe owa Isaka na Ongolobhe owa Yakobo.
LUK 20:38 Wape se Ngolobhe owabhafwe bali bhabhali bhomi, afwanaje wonti bhakhara hwamwahale.”
LUK 20:39 Asimbi bhamo bhagalula bhabhola, 'Sambezi, oyanjile shinza. '
LUK 20:40 Wala sebhawezizye hubhuzye enongwa baada eye go.
LUK 20:41 Wabhabhora abhantu bhayanga wele aje oKristi mwana wa Daudi?
LUK 20:42 Afwanaje oDaudi yoyo ayanga mchuo esha Zaburi: Ogosi abholele Gosi wane: Okhale okhono gwane ogwendelo,
LUK 20:43 hata embabheshe adui bhaho abha litengo elya bheshe amagaga. '
LUK 20:44 Basi Daudi ahukwizya 'Gosi', shili wele mwana wa Daudi?”
LUK 20:45 Na bhantu bhonti nabhali bhahutejezya abhabhorele asambeleziwe bhakwe,
LUK 20:46 'Hwilindaji na simbi bhasongwa ajende bhakwete amenda amatari na lamhana msokoni na khale hwitagalila elye mabhunza na khara amatego agahwitagalila pashikurukuru.
LUK 20:47 Mlya enyumba ezyafwele na hunafiki bhaputa eputo entali. Ebho bhayipata alongwa eshi gosi. '
LUK 21:1 Wabhosya amaso gakwe wabhalola atakili bhaponya esadaka zyabho mwibogosi elye mbuto.
LUK 21:2 Walola ofwele omo pena aponya mla esenti zibhele.
LUK 21:3 Wayanga embabhora ono ofwele opena aponyizye zaidi ashile mwenti.
LUK 21:4 Afwanaje ebho bhonti bhaponyizye esadaka eshoma shashonjelezye zaidi bali ono hupena wakwe aponyizye vyonti vyali navyo.”
LUK 21:5 Na bhantu bhamo bhamo nabhali bhayanga enongwa ezya shimanza ejinsi shari pambwilwe humawe aminza ne salama ezya bhantu ayanjire,
LUK 21:6 “Ega gamgalola, insiku zyayenza ambapo selyaisagala iwe juu eiwe ambalyo salyaibozolwa.”
LUK 21:7 Bhabhozya bhayanga, “Sambelezi, amambo ega gayibha ndii? Gape yenu ishara yakwe eyaje amabo ego gali papepe afumire?”
LUK 21:8 Wayanga, “Enyaji msije mgakhopelwa. Afwanaje bhinji bhayenza hwitawa lyane, bhayanga, 'Ane nene, 'antele 'Owakati uparamiye basi msabhabhenjezye ebho.
LUK 21:9 Namwe namwayovwa enongwa ezye ibho nefitina, mgajetishiwe, afwanaje ego segali n ebudi afumire nasoti lelo ula oumalishoro seuhwenza nanali.”
LUK 21:10 Esho abhabhorere, “Itaifa lyaisogola akhomane ni taifa, na umwene na khomane no mwene.
LUK 21:11 Hwayibha na matesya amagosi agensi ne nzala ne tauni hwonti na mambo agatisye ne ishara engosi afume amwanya.
LUK 21:12 Lelo sagasele ego gonti afumire bhayibhakhata na bhavisye, bhayibhatwala hwitagalila eye mabhanza na bhaponye mwijela, natwalwe hwitagalila elya mwene na maliwali kwajili eyitawa lyane.
LUK 21:13 Na ego gayibha ushuda hwilimwe.
LUK 21:14 Basi kusudiri humoyo genyu asinte asebhe sebhe asoti shambhajibu,
LUK 21:15 afwanaje ane embabhapele ilomu ne hekima ambaya atisi bhenyu bhonti sebhayiwezya abhashinde yape wala ayipinje.
LUK 21:16 Namwe bhayibhalavya ayise bhenyu na horo bhenyu, na mwenyu ma rafiki bhenyu, wape bhayifisya bhamo bhamo.
LUK 21:17 Namwe bhayibhavitu abhantu bhonti kwajili eyitawa lyane.
LUK 21:18 Lelo selyayite hata lisisi limo elye mmatwe genyu.
LUK 21:19 Namwe gagole hwenyu mwayiziponia enafisi genyu.
LUK 21:20 Lelo epo namwayilola iboma elye Yerusalemu lizyongolelwe na bhanajeshi esho mmanyaje eyaje anachishe hwakwe huparamiye.
LUK 21:21 Esho bhabhali huyahuda na bhabhali pahati yakwe bhashembelelaje hwonze, na bhabhali humaganda bhaganjehujinjile.
LUK 21:22 Afwanaje isiku ezyo zyazyo ezye shizanye ili gatinuziwe gonti gage.
LUK 21:23 Ole wabho abhe lwanda na bhabhahwosya katika ensiku ezyo afwanaje hwabha eshida nyinji mnsi nae ihasira juu ye taifa eli.
LUK 21:24 Bhayigwa hukhali owipanga wape bhayitekwa nyara na hwege katika amataifa gonti na eYerusalemu yayikhanywa na mataifa hata amajira age mataifa nagaitimiziwa.
LUK 21:25 Antale hwaibha ishara hwisanya no mwezi ne ntondwe na mnsi amalabha aga mataifa, bhaiswiga huvumi owe nongwa na maklabha labha gakwe.
LUK 21:26 Abhantu bhaivunjiha amoyo huwoga na ahwenyelezye amambo gehagaga ensi. Afwanaje amaha aga mwanya zyayinga.
LUK 21:27 Epo esho pabhayihulola Umwana owa Adamu nahwenza mwibhengo pandwemo na maha no utukufu ogwinji.
LUK 21:28 Basi amambo ego nagahwanda afumire changamhaji mbhosyaje amatwe genyu, afwanaje owaule wenyu uparamie.”
LUK 21:29 Wabhabhora ofwano, “Lyenyi ikwii na makwii agenje gonti.
LUK 21:30 Wakati nalimaliha apongore mlola na manye mwemwe yaje amajira oga konje gamalishe abha papepe.
LUK 21:31 Namwe shesho namlola amambo ega gahwanda afumire manyaji yaje umwene owa Ngolobhe uli papepe.
LUK 21:32 Amini, embabhora, eshikholo eshi seshashira hata ega gonti gatimile.
LUK 21:33 Emwanya nensi zyaishila lelo amazu gane segaishira na mwaha.
LUK 21:34 Eshi hwiyinyaji amogo genyu isibhe egalemewa no ulyavi, no ulevi, namasumbufu ege maisha ega. Isiku lila lyabhenzera nanari neshe atego shahwonza
LUK 21:35 afwanaje esho. Shashayibhenzara abhantu bhonti bhabhakhara pamaso gedunia yonti.
LUK 21:36 Eshi gonezyaji amwe shila wakati mlabhaje, ili mpate ahwaulwe katikaa ego gonti gagaifumira na hwemilele hwitagalila elya Mwana owa Adamu.”
LUK 21:37 Esho shira pasanya abhanga asambelezya maibhanza na nosiku abharaga agone mwigamba lyalihwetwa Mizeituni.
LUK 21:38 Na bhantu bhonti bhali hadamla khasha bhabhara mwibhanza ili hutejezye.
LUK 22:1 Bhapamila shikulukulu eye makati yeseponyezewe echachu yehwetwa shukulukulu eye pasaka.
LUK 22:2 Na gosi abhemakohani na simbi bhali bhahwanza idara elya hugoje, afwanaje bhali bhabhogopa abhantu.
LUK 22:3 Oshetani wamwinjila o Yuda yakwiziwa Iskariote, wape wamwo na bhala ethenashala.
LUK 22:4 Wasogola wabhata wayanga na gosi abha makuhani na jemedari ejinsi sha bhawezye hubheshe mmakhono gabho.
LUK 22:5 Bhasongwa, bhetehana nawo hupele ehela.
LUK 22:6 Weteha wanza enafasi eya husaliti hwabhahale pasepali obongono.
LUK 22:7 Yafishili isiku lye makati gasegaponyezeyea we echachu, ambayo yahanziwaga asinze epasaka.
LUK 22:8 Wabhasontezya o Petro no Yohana, wayanga bhalaji mtilenganyizye epasaka tipata alye.”
LUK 22:9 Bhabhola, “Uhwanza tibhale hwi?”
LUK 22:10 Wabhabhola, “Enya, nambhahwinjile mwibomba mbhatangane ulume akhete esonta owe menze. Mrundozyaje mbhahwinjile enyumba yabhahwinji omwahale.
LUK 22:11 Na mbhahubhula omwanesho nyumba, “Osambelezi ahubhola, ili hwii empanda eyajenyi, empate alye Epasaka omwo pandwemo na manyiziwa bhane?”
LUK 22:12 Wape abhabhalanje empanda engosi orufani, shimalishe asimbwe, lenganyi omwo.”
LUK 22:13 Wabhala, bhalola neshe shabhabholele bhayilenganya Epasaka.
LUK 22:14 Hata sala nayafiha akheye pashalye omwahale na bhala mitume pandwemo nawo.
LUK 22:15 Wabhabhola, “Entanianile tee ayilye epasaka ene pandwemo namwe sesele alabha hwane.
LUK 22:16 Afwanaje embabhola eyaje sendya nantele hata nehaitimizya oumwene owa Ngolobhe.”
LUK 22:17 Yabha o Yesu wega shikombe, nawamala asaligwe wayanga, eji eshi na mgabhane, je mwemwe hwamwe.
LUK 22:18 Afwanaje embabhola, sembamwele nantele papo eye mzabibu, mpaka umwene owa Ngolobhe nawayenza.”
LUK 22:19 Esho wega ibumunda nali amalile asalifye waumesula, nabhele, wayanga, ogu ni bele gwane ambao ufumiziwe kwajili eyahuumwe. Bhombaji eshi anizushe ane.”
LUK 22:20 Wega eshikombe shesho shesho nabhalya eshaye esha nosiku wayanga, eshikombe ndagano epya ezya danda lyane ambalyo litishe kwa ajili yahulimwe.
LUK 22:21 Lelo enyaji ola yansaliti alipandwemo, nane pameza.
LUK 22:22 Afwanaje mwana owa Adamu lyoli abhabhale neshe shekusudiwe lelo, Ole wakwe omntu ya husaliti!”
LUK 22:23 Bhandile abhozye bhebho hwa bhebho wenu miongoni mwabho ambaye agabhomba ijambo eli.
LUK 22:24 Esho wafumila adalihane bhebho bhene aje wenu wase bhelelwe abhe gosi ashile bhonti.
LUK 22:25 Wabhabhola, “Amwene abhabhantu abhemataifa bhana ugosi juu yabho na bhala bhabhali namamlaka juu yabho bhakwiziwa bhaheshimiwa bhalongozi.
LUK 22:26 Lelo sewanziwa abhesho hwilimwee amwe, ebadala yakwe leha ola ambaye gosi kati yahwilimwe abhe neshe ododu. Na ola yali wa mbimu tee abhe nenshe otumwa.
LUK 22:27 Afwanaje yayolihu ogosi ola yakhala pameza nola yabhomba embombo? Eshi seyayola yakheye pameza? Na ane esele kati yenyu ane netumiaha.
LUK 22:28 Lelo amwe mwemwe mwendeleye abhanane kati amalabha gane au (alengwe).
LUK 22:29 Embapela amwe umwene neshe shla Ubaba shampiye ane umwene,
LUK 22:30 je mpate alye na mwele pameza yane huumwene wane. Na mwikhala mmatengo age enzi mwaizilonga evikholo kumi na zibhele ezya Israeli.
LUK 22:31 Simoni, Simoni, manya aje, Shetani alabhile abhaje ili abhapete nenshe engano.
LUK 22:32 Lelo embalabhiye, yaje olyeteho lyaho lugaje munwe, nawe nohaya ulya obhazenje oholo bhaho.”
LUK 22:33 Wabhola, “Gosi, nendi pandwemo nawe, ana endi tayali abhale mwijela au hata hufwe.”
LUK 22:34 Wayanga, “Ehubhola Petro, ehanda sebhakuje sanyono, sosele awe ahane mala hatatu eyaje somenye.”
LUK 22:35 Wabhabhozya eshi epo, nehabhasontezyezye semwali nifuko walu omkoba wala evilato, mwapongoshewe na hantu?” Bhayanga “Haa.”
LUK 22:36 Wabhabhola, lelo eshi yali nifuko ayeje wape yali nomkoba ayeje, wape yasagali ni panga, na akazye ijoo lyakwe akale.
LUK 22:37 Afwanaje embabhola, ega gagasimbiwiwe segali ne budi atimiziwe hwiline, eyaje abhaziwe pandwemo nebho bhanankanya, afwanaje ewasiwa gali nomalishilo wakwe.”
LUK 22:38 Bhayanga, “Gosi, enya! Epa gahwili amapanga gabhele.” Wene.
LUK 22:39 Wafuma wabhala mpaka mwigamba elya Mzietuni enshe ekawaida yakwe, asambeleziwa bhakwe bhape bhalongozanya nawo.
LUK 22:40 Nawafiha pala abhabholele, labhaji aje mganji ahwinji mndengo.
LUK 22:41 Omwahale wahwibagula nabho nenshe kias esha ponye iwe, wafugamila amafugamo watabha,
LUK 22:42 ayanga, “Ee Baba, nkashele mapenzi gaho, onefwezye eshikombe eshi lelo senapenzi gane, eshi gahuliwe gabhombeshe.”
LUK 22:43 Omalaika afume amwanya wafumila wapela amaha.
LUK 22:44 Wape shila shali mmalabha, wonjezya alabhe tee, ehali yakwe yabha nenshe amalavula age danda galagala pansi.
LUK 22:45 Nawasogola hula alabhe hwakwe wabhalila asambelezewa bhakwe, wabhaga bhagonile otulo ogwa kogobhale,
LUK 22:46 wabhabhora, yenu mgonile otulo? Ogoli, mlabhe msahabha ahwinjile mndengo.'
