LUK 22:47 Basi nahali katika ayanje, enya obongano wa bhantu, nola yakwiziwa Yuda, ambaye ni moja yabhala mitume abhatagali hwitagalila wapalamila hwa Yesu ili ayayile.
LUK 22:48 o Yesu wabhola, “Yuda, wamsaliti omwana owa Adamu esha huyayile?”
LUK 22:49 Na bhala bhabhali papepe nawo nbhalola gagafumila, bhayanga, “Gosi, tibhakhoma na mapanga”?
LUK 22:50 Omo wabho wakhoma obhomba mbombo wa kuhani gosi, wadumla ikutu elya hulero.
LUK 22:51 U Yesu wagalula woyanga, “Bhanji hulu hweli. Wapalamasya ikutu waponia.
LUK 22:52 U Yesu wabhabhola agosi bhemakuhani, na maakida abhibhanza, nazee bhebhenzele juu yakwe, “Eshi mwenzele mweli na mapanga nu ndugu nensheje mkhata ya fyola?
LUK 22:53 Shila lisiku nali pandwomo namwe mwibhanza semwasontezyezye amakhono lelo ene ndiyo sala yenyu. Lakini hii ni saa yako, na mamlaka age nkisi.
LUK 22:54 Bhakhata, bhamwega, bhabhala nawo munyumba eya kuhani ogosi. Nu Petro alondolelaga sahutali.
LUK 22:55 Nabhamalile ahwasya omwoto pahati eye shibhanja bhakheye pandwemo, wape u Petro akheye nabho.
LUK 22:56 Ndipo obhomba mbombo omo walola akheye papalabha, walangulila amaso wayanga nono ali pandwemo nawo.
LUK 22:57 Wakhana, wayanga, ee, she, semenye.
LUK 22:58 Pamanda hashe, omuntu owamwabho alolile wayanga, Petro wanyanga, “Ee mntu, se nene.”
LUK 22:59 Antele lyashita isala limo, omntu owamwabho wakasa ayanje, “Lyoli ono ali pandwemo nawo afwanaje omwahale nantele Mgalilaya.”
LUK 22:60 Petro wayanga, “Ee mntu, sendimenye lyo yanga.” Na pepo, pepo nali katika ayanje, ehanda ahakujile.
LUK 22:61 Gosi wagaluha wamwenya u Petro. U Petro walizuha lila izu elya Gosi, ejinsi shabholele, “Sanyono sesele akuje ehanda obhahane mala hatatu.”
LUK 22:62 Wafuma hwonze waula humansai.
LUK 22:63 Na bhala bhantu bhali bhahukhata u Yesu, bhabhombile edhihaka bhakhoma.
LUK 22:64 Bhavwenesya amaso, bhanda hubhozye, bhozye bhayanga, kuwa wenu yakhonule?”
LUK 22:65 Bhafumizya nengwa mwabho nyinji gahuliji.
LUK 22:66 Hata nahwashiye, bhatangene amwabho abheshi gosi, na gosi abhe makuhani nusimbi bhateta mwikoloti lyabho bhayanga,
LUK 22:67 nkashile, “Awe wa Klisiti, tibhole.” Wabhabhola ewapo embabhola, semuwezizya ahweteshele tee,
LUK 22:68 na nkashele mbabhozye sembhagalule.”
LUK 22:69 Lelo ahwanda eshi na hwendele, Omwana owa Adamu abhabhe akheye okhono ondelo ogwe maha aga Ngolobhe.”
LUK 22:70 Bhonti bhayanga, “Eshi awe oli Mwana wa Ngolobhe?” Na Yesu wabhabhola, “Amwe myanjile ane nene.”
LUK 22:71 Bhayanga, “Yesnu tihwanza nantele oushahidi afwanaje ate tete tovwezya afume mwilomu lyakwe yoyo.”
LUK 23:1 Bhemelela obungano gwonti, bhatwala hwa Pilato.
LUK 23:2 Bhandile hutake, bhayanga, “Tilolile ono natezya itaifa lyetu na bhazubhile abhantu bhagaje hupele Okaisari, esonga ayanjile eyaje omwhale yoyo ni Klisiti, Mwene.”
LUK 23:3 Pilato wabhozya, wayanga, “Awe wewe omwene Owayahudi?” Wagalula wabhabhola, “Awe wayanga.”
LUK 23:4 Pilato wabhola agosi abhemakohani na mabungono, “Sendilola izu lyalili libhibhi hwa mntu ono”.
LUK 23:5 Wape bhahwikazile sana, bhayanga, “Abhasonje sonje abhantu, amanyizyaga evyahudi yonti, afume Galilaya mpaka ohu.”
LUK 23:6 U Pilato nawovwa ego abhozyezye nkashele ono mntu wa Hugalilaya?
LUK 23:7 Na apete enongwa eyaje alichini wa Herode, atwalile wa Herode, afwanaje omwahale wape ahali hu Yerusalemu ensiku ezyo.
LUK 23:8 Na Herode nalolile u Yesu ashimile tee afwanaje ali ahwanza tee hulole afume ensiku nyinji. Afwane nesho ayovwezye enongwe zyakwe, wasobhela alole ishala yebhambilwe nomwahale.
LUK 23:9 Wabhozya enongwa nyinji omwahale sewagalulo lyalyonti.
LUK 23:10 Agosi abhemakuhani na simbi bhimelela bhataka humaha gonti.
LUK 23:11 Basi Herode wabhombo lema, pandwemo na sikali bhakwe, wasolanya na wakwalizye amenda amenza, esho wawezye hwa Pilato.
LUK 23:12 Basi isiku lila Herode na Pilato bhakonde ne abhe lafiki afwanaje epo ahwanda bhali bhavisenye bhebho hwe bhebho.
LUK 23:13 Na Pilato wabhatanya agosi wa makuhani na gosi na bhantu,
LUK 23:14 Wabhola, “Mntu ono mletile hwiline nensheje atezyo abhantu nane enyaa, enamuye amambo gakwe hwitagalila lyenyu, ka sendilolile hwamwahale ikosa lyalyonti katika enongwa zya mtakile.
LUK 23:15 Wala, hata o Herode, nkashile awezizye hwilite basi enyua, sagalilole enongwa yayonti lyabhombile lyali hwanziwa aje afwanje.
LUK 23:16 Esho basi embahuwelele nahumwalule.
LUK 23:17 (Esho, Pilato yukazimisizye humwaulile ofungwa omo isiku elye esikulukulu).
LUK 23:18 Bhahwaga ibwago wonti pandwemo bhayanga, “Mwefwe ono, otuulile o Baraba!”
LUK 23:19 Wape mntu watagwelwe mwijele kwaji fitina efumile hwiboma, kwajili yengoga.
LUK 23:20 Basi Pilato wayanga nabho mala habhele hushila shanzaga humwaulile u Yesu.
LUK 23:21 Lelo bhabwaga ibwago, bhayanga, “Msulubishe, msulubishe.”
LUK 23:22 Wabhola emala eyatatu, afwane wele, ono abhombile mabhibhi wele, sendolile hwamwahale enongwa zyazihwanziwa aje afwe, basi nkashele na welela embahumwaile.”
LUK 23:23 Lelo bhafumia amazu hunguvu zyonti, bhabhabha asulubiwe. Amazu gabho gamena.
LUK 23:24 Pilato walonga aje gabhahwunza gubhombeshe.
LUK 23:25 Wamwaula ola yabhatajile mwisela kwajili eyefilina nu negoga, ola yabhamwanzaga wafumia o Yesu bhabhombele shabhahwanza.
LUK 23:26 Nabhalai bhahusogotya, bhakhatu omntu omo, o Simoni Omkirene, ali afumile hugonda bhalweha ikhobhanyo aweje hwikhosi lyakwe u Yesu.
LUK 23:27 Obungano ogosi owabhantu bhalondolela na bhashe bhabhali bhahikhoma evifubha na huzundelele.
LUK 23:28 U Yesu wabhagulushila wayanga amwe mwalendu abhahu Yerusalemu, msuhandilele ane, shwililasi enafsi zyenu na bhana bhenyu.
LUK 23:29 Eshi, enyi ensiku zihwenze nabhayinga hafu bhabhuli bhagumba nufyanda vyao vyase vipapa na mabhelo ga segahwosya.
LUK 23:30 Esho nabhayanda agabhozye amagamba tigweleli notugamba tigubekayi.
LUK 23:31 Afwanaje nkashile bhabhomba amambo ega hwikwi ilyoro, ebhabhe wele hwilyo?”
LUK 23:32 Bhatwala bhabhele abhamwabho abhe makasa bhabudwe pandwemo nuwo.
LUK 23:33 Nabhafishile pamopame papa kwiziwa Fuvu litwe, epo pasulubisizye omwahale panda wemo ba bhemakosa omo oupande owendelo omo opande omongo.
LUK 23:34 U Yesu waga, “Baba, ubhasajile afwanaje sebhemenge lyabhabhomba bhagabhanya amenda gakwe, bhakhoma ekora.
LUK 23:35 Abhantu bhemelela bhenye bhala agosi bhape bhabhombela ezalau, bhayanga, “Ahauye abhanje. Ahwiyu ule yoyo nkashile yu Klisiti owa Ngolobhe oteule wakwe.”
LUK 23:36 Bhala asikali bhape bhazalale bhabhalila nu huletele esiki,
LUK 23:37 ohu bhayanga nkashile awe oli mwene owa yahudi, hwiyaule umwene”
LUK 23:38 Pamwanya yakwe pali amandishi, “ONO NDIYO MWENE WA MWENE WAYAHUDI.”
LUK 23:39 Nomo owabhala owikosa yabhakhomeleye aujile, wayanga, “Eshi awe sagawe Klisiti? Hwiyaule enafsi yuho nute.”
LUK 23:40 Lelo ula owabhele wagalula waidamila wayanga, “Awe sohwumwogopa hata Ongolobhe, nawe olimundongo zyezyo?
LUK 23:41 Gape gelyoli hwaliti atee, afwanaje tipewa oshahara gwetu, gwaguhwanziwa humamba getu. Eshi ono sabhombile lyalyonti lyasaga ufaa.”
LUK 23:42 Basi wayanga, “Yesu, onizushe nawayinjila humwene waho.”
LUK 23:43 U Yesu wabhola, “Eteha, ehubhola, sanyono eshi onzubha pandwemo nane Paradiso.”
LUK 23:44 Epo yuli efishile esala eya saa sita, yabha nkisi juu ya pasi ponti hadi saa tisa,
LUK 23:45 esanya lipongoshe okhozyo lwakwe, elyenda elye shibhanza lyazembuha paha.
LUK 23:46 U Yesu walila hwizu igosi, wayanga, “Baba makhono gaho, enjibheha eroho yane,” Na wamala ayanje ego wadumula eroho.
LUK 23:47 Ula Oakida nuwalula gagafumie atukuzizye Ongolobhe, wayanga, “Lyoli omntu ono aliwelyoli.”
LUK 23:48 Na mubungano gonti ega bhantu bhabhali bhabhungene ahwenye amambo ego nabhalolile gagabhombeshe bhabhala amwabho bhahwi khoma khoma evifubha.
LUK 23:49 Nabhonti bhamanye nawo na bhala abhashe bhalongozenye nawo afume Hugalilaya, bhemelela sahutuli, bhahwenga amambo ego.
LUK 23:50 Na enya wafumila omntu omo itawa lyakwe yo Yusufu, ambaye mntu wa hwikolo ti, omntu, omwinza owe lyoli,
LUK 23:51 (Wala saga alyeteshe ishauli lyabho), wape mntu wa Armathaya, iboma elya yahudi, antele awenyelezya umwene owa Ngolobhe.
LUK 23:52 Omntu oyo abhalile huwa Pilato, ahanzaga apewa obele gwa Yesu.
LUK 23:53 Wagwisya wagubwenesya esanda yakitani waubhaha mwakaburi lyalibenwe paka pansi, lyelyali sabhe hwelwe omntu mhati yakwe.
LUK 23:54 Na isiku lila lyali lisiku elye mandalizi, elyatoye lyanda ahwinjile.
LUK 23:55 Nabhala abhashe, bhahenzele nawo afume Hugalilaya bhalondoleye, bhayilola inkongwa na bele gwakwe sagwabhehwelwe.
LUK 23:56 Bhawela bhabhomba tayali anukato na marashi. Ni siku elyatoye bhamile neshi shabhamuye.
LUK 24:1 Hata isiku elyahwanda elye longo, nalyahandaga asha, bhabhalile hunkongwa bhatwali amanukato gabhabheshele tayali.
LUK 24:2 Bhalyaga ula iwe liungulusiwe patali ne nkongwe.
LUK 24:3 Bhinjila sebhagulola obele gwa Gosi o Yesu.
LUK 24:4 Yabha napali bhakongobhala kwajili eizu elyo, enya, abhantu bhahemeleye papepe nabho, bhakwete amenda galangasala ngasa.
LUK 24:5 Bhape nabhinjila nowoga bhinama kifudifudi hata pamankondi, ebho bhabhabholele, yenu mhumwanza yali mwomi hwabhafwe?
LUK 24:6 Nomo epa, azyoshele! izuhaji shayanjile namwe nali ahweli Hugalilaya,
LUK 24:7 ayanjile aynziwe omwana owa Adamu akhatwa namakhono ga bhala abhe dhambe na asulubiwe, na zyoshe isiku elya tatu.”
LUK 24:8 Bhagizuha amazu gakwe,
LUK 24:9 bhasogola hunkongwa bhawela bhabhabhola bhala kumi na bhumwabho bhonti enongwa ezye mambo ego gonti.
LUK 24:10 Bhape yo Maria Magdalena, no Joana, no Maria onyina Yakobo, na bhala abhashe bhamwabho bhabhali pandwemo nabho.
LUK 24:11 Ebho bhabhabholele asontezewa enongwa eye mambo ego, enongwa zyabho zyabhoneshe ajezye walangani hwabhahee wala sebhabhetesheye.
LUK 24:12 Lelo o Petro asogoye abhalile sashembela paka hunkongwa, waundama wagodezya mhati, wavilola vila evitambala evya sanda vyene. Wahwibhali saswiga gagafumie.
LUK 24:13 Na enya, isiku lilila abhantu bhabhele miongoni mwabho bhali bhabhala hu shijiji shimo itawa lyakwe Emmau, sha shali hutali ne Yerusalemu neshe ajende amasala gabhele.
LUK 24:14 Wape bhali bhayanga bhebho hwa bhebho enongwa ezye amambo ego gonti gagafumie.
LUK 24:15 Yabha katika ayanje na bhozanye hwabho, u Yesu yoyo wapalamila walongozanya nabho.
LUK 24:16 Amaso gabho gafumbwa sebhamanya.
LUK 24:17 Wabhabhola, “Nongwa wele ezi zyamuyanga eshi namjenda?” Bhemelela bhapinta humaso gabho.
LUK 24:18 wagalula omo wabho, itawa lyakwe yo Kleopa, wabhola, “Je awe umwene olijenyi pa Yerusalemu hata sogamenye gagafumiye omwo ensiku ezi?
LUK 24:19 U Yesu wabhozya, “Mambo genu?” bhabhola, “Mambo aga Yesu owa Hunazareti, yali mntu kuwa, yalinowezo abhombe na yanje hwitagalila elya Ngolobhe nahwabhantu bhonti.
LUK 24:20 Nantele ejinsi agosi abhe makuhani na gosi abhabhantu shabhakhete na hulonje aje afwe bhasulubisya.
LUK 24:21 Nate halititegemele lyaje omwahale yabhabhe wabhaule Israeli. Zaidi eyego gonti sanyono elya tatu afume nagabhombesha amambo ago.
LUK 24:22 Antele abhashe bhamo bhamo abhamwetu bhatisitusizye, bhabhalile hunkonge wa sapwiti khasha.
LUK 24:23 Sabhagulolile obele gwakwe, bhenza bhayanga yaje abhatokeye omalaika bhabhayanjile aje mwomi.
LUK 24:24 Na bhamwabho bhabhali pandwemo natee bhabhala hunkongwa bhalola shesho nenshe bhala abhashe shabhayanjile. Aje omwahale sebhalolile.
LUK 24:25 Wabhabhola, “Amwe mwesemmanya mwemli na moyo amamwamu aga hweteshe gonti gabhayanjile akuwa.
LUK 24:26 Eshi seyanziwaga Klisiti apate amalabha ego na hwinjile katika oufukufu wakwe?”
LUK 24:27 Wanda afume wa Musa na kuwa bhoonti, wabhabhola mnsimbo gonti amambo gagahuhusu omwahale yoyo.
LUK 24:28 Bhapalamila shila eshijiji shabhabhalaga, wape abhombile nenshe aje ahwanza ahwendele hwitagalila.
LUK 24:29 Bhayanga nawo, “Khala pandwemo nate, afwanaje isanya liswiye na usanya umalishe winjilo mhati akhale nabho.
LUK 24:30 Yabha nawakhula nabho pashalye, wega ikati, wasaya, waumesula, wabhapela.
LUK 24:31 Gadamla amaso gabho bhamanya, esho watega hwitagalila lyabho.
LUK 24:32 Bhabholana, “Je amoyo getu seguhashile mhati yetu, ipo nali ayanga nate mwidala, natigulile ensimbo?”
LUK 24:33 Bhasogola esaa yeyo, bhawela Huyerusalemu. bhabhaga bhale kumi na moja bhatangene abhahale bhala bhali pandwemo nabhahale,
LUK 24:34 bhayanga, “Ogosi azyoshele lyoli lyoli, wape abhoneshe hwa Simoni.”
LUK 24:35 Bhape bhabhapela enongwa ezye mambo aga mwidala ne jinsi shamanyishe abho katika amesule ikati.
LUK 24:36 Na bhali katika ayanje enongwa zyo yoyo mwenyewe ahemeleye pahati yabho, wabhabhola, “Amani ebhe namwe.”
LUK 24:37 Bhasituha bhogopa tee, bhaseha aje bhalola roho.
LUK 24:38 Wabhabhola, mbona mkogobhala? Na yenu mlola ewasiwasi humoyo genyu?
LUK 24:39 Enyi amakhono gane na manama gone, yaje nene mwenyewe, hatikati, mlole afwanaje eroho seli nobele wa amafupa nenshe namundova ane aje endi nagwo.”
LUK 24:40 Na wayanga ego wabhalanga amakhono gakwe na magaga gakwe.
LUK 24:41 Basi nabhali sebhetesheye ashe, ohubhaswiga, abhabholele, mli neshalye shashonti epe?
LUK 24:42 wapela eshipande eshe samaki wa kuokwa.
LUK 24:43 Wege, walya hwitagalila lyabho.
LUK 24:44 Esho wabhabhola, “Ego gagego amazugane gahabhabholele nanali endipandwemo namwe, eyaje ni lazima gatimile gonti gehasibwilwe katika torati eya Musa na ga kuwa ne Zaburi.”
LUK 24:45 Esho wabhalanga enjele zyabho bhapate ahwelewe ensimbo.
LUK 24:46 Wabhabhola, “Shasho shahasimbwilwe, eyaje Klisiti lazima ateseke, na fufushe isiku elya tatu.
LUK 24:47 Naje amataifa gonti gailombelelwa hwitawa lyakwe enongwa ezye tebona hwefwezyewe edhambi ahwanda afume Myerusalemu.
LUK 24:48 Namwe mwemli bhashahiji abhe mambo ega.
LUK 24:49 Na enya, embaletela juu yenyu ehadi eya Baba wane, lelo khalaji omu mwiboma, hata mvwenehwe oweza afume amwanya.
LUK 24:50 Walongozya mpaka Bethania. Wabhosya amakhono gakwe wabhasayila.
LUK 24:51 Yabha katika abhasayile, wahwibagula nabho, wegwa amwanya ambinguni.
LUK 24:52 Bhaputa, esho bhawela Huyerusalemu bhabhali nashime ohu gosi.
LUK 24:53 Bhape bhali bhakheye mhati mwibhanza, na husifu Ongolobhe.
JOH 1:1 Hula ahwande hwa hali izu lyali pamo no Ngolobhe, izu ali yo Ngolobhe.
JOH 1:2 Eli, Ezu, Nalya handaga lyali pamo no Ngolobhe.
JOH 1:3 Evintu vyonti vyabhombeshe ashilile omwene, asibhe omweje na hamo ata hantu hamo hahabhombeshe.
JOH 1:4 Muhati yakwe mwali no womi, na wope owomi wali lukhozyo lwa bhantu bhonti.
JOH 1:5 Olukhozyo lwakholaga munkisi, enkisi yapotilwe aluzimye.
JOH 1:6 Pahali omuntu watumwilwe afume hwa Ngolobhe, ola itawa lyakwe ali yo Yohana.
JOH 1:7 Ahanzele nanshi keeti ahakikisye ahusu olukhozyo, aje bhonti nkabhapate ahweteshele ashilile hwamwene.
JOH 1:8 O Yohana sagali lukhozyo, ila ahenzele nkahakikisye ahusu lula olukozyo.
JOH 1:9 Esho alilukhozyo lwelyoli lula lwalwahenzaga munsi lyope lwapanga shila muntu.
JOH 1:10 munsi, na ensi yabhombwelwe ashilile omwahale, na ensi seyamenye.
JOH 1:11 Ahaenzele hwabhantu bhakwe, na awantu wakwe na abhantu wakwe sebhaposheye.
JOH 1:12 Ila hwabhala abhinji bhabhaposheye, bhabhahetesheye itawa lyakwe, nebho abhapiye elyoli eyaje bhana bha Ngolobhe,
JOH 1:13 Bhabhapepwe, se hwidanda, wala hulusongwo lwe bele, sio olusongwo lwa muntu, ila lwa Ngolobhe yoyo.
JOH 1:14 Lyope izu lyabhoshe lwebele na lyakhala muhati yeetu, tiulolile oumwamu wakwe, oumwamu nashi wa muntu mwene wahenzele afume hwa Daada, amemile uwene ne lyoli.
JOH 1:15 O Yohana ahakikizye ahusu omwene, na afumizye izu ayanje, “Ono yayola wanayanjile enongwa zyakwe najile, “Ola wayenza pamande yane yo gosi ashile ane, afuatanaje ahali kabla yaline.”
JOH 1:16 Afuatanaje ashilile oluu golosu lwake, ate tenti tiposheye wene eshipawa baadaye shipawa.
JOH 1:17 Afuatanaje endajizo zyaliletilwe ashilile oMusa. Ewene ne lyoli vyahenzele ashilile oYesu Kilisti.
JOH 1:18 Nomo omuntu walolile Ongolobhe omuda gwagwonti. Omuntu mwene ambayo yo Ngolobhe, walipashifubha sha Daada, abhombile aje omwene amanyishe.
JOH 1:19 Na olu luhakikisyo lwa Yohana lula adimi na lawi bhabhatumwilwe hwa mwene na Yahudi ahubhozye, “Aje awe wenanu?”
JOH 1:20 Bila asyoshe syoshe saga akhene, aje “Anesene Kilisiti.”
JOH 1:21 Esho bhabhaozyezye, “eshi awe we nanu esalezi?” We Eliya? Ajile, “Ane see yayoyo.” Wajile we kuwaa? Ajile,” Hagha.”
JOH 1:22 Antele bhabhozya, “Wee nanu, aje nkati bhapele ijibu bhabhatitumile”? Uhwihakikisya bhole wewe humwene?”
JOH 1:23 Waga, “Ane ne lizu lyakwe walila mwipoli: 'Golosyaji idala lya Ngolobhe,' na okuwa oIsaya shayanjile.”
JOH 1:24 Eshi bhahali abhantu bhatumwile na Mafalisayo. Bhabhozyezya aje,
JOH 1:25 “Yenu ohwozya eshi nkashewe Kilisiti wala see we Eliya okuwaa?”
JOH 1:26 O Yohana abhabhozyezye ajile, “Embozya hu menze. Ata sheshi mhati yenyu ahwemelela omuntu wa semumenye amwe.
JOH 1:27 Onu ndiyo wanzahwenze pamande yaline. Ane sihwanziwa alegezye ekamba zye vilato.”
JOH 1:28 Enongwa ezi zyabhombeshe ohwo hu Bethania, hwisyela lye Yordani, esehemu ambayo oYohana alihwozya.
JOH 1:29 Isiku lyalyafwatile oYohana alolile uYesu ahwenza hwa mwene ajile, “Enya mwanangole wa Ngolobhe wahwega embibhi zya munsi!
JOH 1:30 ono yayola wana yanjile enongwa zyakwe najile, “Omwene wayenza hwi akhosi yane yo gosi ashile ane, afwatanaje ali hwitazi lyaline.'
JOH 1:31 Senamenye omwene, ila shabhombeshe esho aje nkobheneshe mu Israeli, aje nahenzele nabhozyaga na menze.”
JOH 1:32 O Yohana ahakikisizye, “Aje nalolile Ompepo ahwiha afume amwanya ofwana ngwe njebha, yasageye pamwanya yakwe.
JOH 1:33 Ane senamenye ila omwene wantumile aje enozyaje na menze ambozyezye, 'ola wobhalole empempo ehwiha na khale pamwanya yakwe, Oyo waibhozya hwo Mpepo Ofinjile.'
JOH 1:34 Endolile na ehakikisizye aje ono Mwana wa Ngolobhe.”
JOH 1:35 Nantele isiku lyalyafuatile oYohana ali ayemeleye pandwemo na bhanafunzi bhakwe bhabhele,
JOH 1:36 bhalolile oYesu ajenda no Yohana ajile, “Enyaji, Omwana ngole wa Ngolobhe!”
JOH 1:37 bhabhele bhamwonvwezye oYohana nayanga ega bhafuatile oYesu.
JOH 1:38 Nantele oYesu agalushe na bhalole abhanafunzi bhala bhahulondolela, nabhabhozye, “Mhwanza yenu?” Bhajile, “Labi, (emaana yakwe 'mwalimu,' ukhala hwii?”
JOH 1:39 Wabhabhozya, “Enzaji mulole.”Nantele bhabhalile alole pale pakhalaga; bhakheye pamo nawo isiku elyo, afwatanaje yali efishile saa kumi eshi.
JOH 1:40 Omomo wa bhala bhabhele bhabhamwonvwezye oYohana nayanga nantele bhafwatile oYesu ali yo Andeleya, oholo wakwe oSimoni Petulo.
JOH 1:41 Alolile oholo wakwe oSimoni omwana nahubhozye, “Tipete Omasihi” (maana yakwe Kilisiti).
JOH 1:42 Bhaleta hwa Yesu. O Yesu amwezi na ajile, “Awe we Simoni omwana wa Yohana” obhakwiziwe Kefa,” (maana yakwe 'Petulo').
JOH 1:43 Isiku lyalyafuatile oYesu lwahanzaga asogole abhale huGalilaya, amwajile oFilipo na hubhozye, “Nfwate ane.”
JOH 1:44 O Filipo ali khaya wa hu Bethsaida, ekhaya ya Andrea no Petulo.
JOH 1:45 O Filipo amwajile o Nathanaeli na hubhozye aje timwajile ola oMusa wa handishe enongwa zyakwe mu ndajizyo na Kuwaa. O Yesu omwana wa Yusufu, afume hu Nazareti.
JOH 1:46 O Nathanaeli abhozyezye, “Aje ahantu ahinza hawezizye afumile hu Nazareti?” O Filipo abhozezye, Aje enzaga olole.”
JOH 1:47 U Yesu walola oNathanaeli ahwenza hwa mwene wayanga, “Waga oyenye Omwisraeli welyoli lyoli wasaga ali nilenka muhati yakwe!”
JOH 1:48 O Nathanaeli wabhozya, “Amenyebhole ane?” O Yesu wabhozya, “Salisele oFilipo ahukwizye nawahali pansi yikwi.”
JOH 1:49 O Nathanaeli wayanga, “Waga Mwalimu awe oli Mwana wa Ngolobhe! Awe oli mwene we Wisraeli”!
JOH 1:50 O Yesu wayanag wabhozya, “Aje afuatanaje nabhozezye 'nalilolile pansi yikwi aje ohweteshele obhalole embombo engosi ashile ezi.”
JOH 1:51 O Yesu wabhabhozya aje eteshile etesheli embabho lya mubhazilole emwonya zihwiguha, mubhabhalole ahalozelu wazubha na hwishe amwanya hwa Mwana wa Adamu.”
JOH 2:1 Baada ye nsiku zitatu, hwa ne harusi ohwo hukana ye Galilaya no nyina wakwe oYesu ali ohwo.
JOH 2:2 O Yesu na bhanafunzi bhakwe bhali bhalihwe hu harusi.
JOH 2:3 Lwabhamali shelwe ne divai, onyina wakwe oYesu abhozezye, “Sebhali ne divai.”
JOH 2:4 O Yesu ajile, “Oshe oyo ego ane gahusu yenu ane? Ensiku zyane anezilisele afishile.”
JOH 2:5 Onyina wakwe abhabhozezye atumwa, “Hahonti hanzabhabhozye bhombaji.”
JOH 2:6 Eshi hwali ne nsonta sita zye mawe pala pabhele pa nawe munsikulukulu zya Yahudi, shila muntu ali noumemuwe nzio zibhele zitatu.
JOH 2:7 O Yesu wabhawozya, “Zimemyi amenze ensonta mawe.” Bhamemeya bhamememya paka pamwanya.
JOH 2:8 Nantele wabhabhozya bhala aboyieji, “Hashe esalezi mtulwe hwa bhabhahudumu agosi bhe meza.” Bhabhomba nanshi shalibhalajiziwe.
JOH 2:9 Ohudumu ogosi abhonjile gala amenze gagali gabadilishe abhe divai, ila sagamenye hwagafumaga (ila atumwa watapaga amenze bhagamenye hwa gafumaga). Pamande bhakwizya omwene harusi na
JOH 2:10 hubhozye, “Kila muntu ahwanda abhahudumile abhantu edivai ila sebhagamenye. Abhapele bhabhapiye edivai yasaga nyinza”
JOH 2:11 Oujiza ogugwa hu Kana ya Galilaya, gwali gwa hwande gweshimanyilo uujiza gwa bhombile oYesu, akwinkule oumwamu wakwe, esho abhanafunzi bhakwe bhamwetesheye.
JOH 2:12 Baada yene, oYesu, onyina wakwe, aholo wakwe na wanafunzi bhakwe bhabhalile hunsi ye Kaperanaumu na bhakheye ohwo ensiku ndodo.
JOH 2:13 Epasaka ya Bhayahudi yali epalamiye afishe, oYesu abhalile hu Yelusalemu.
JOH 2:14 Abhajile bhabhakazya eng'ombe, engole ne njebha Mshibhanza. Nantele na wabadilisha fedha walikuwa wameketi ndani ya Hekalu.
JOH 2:15 akatengeza mjeledi wenye vifundo, akawatoa wote walikuwemo katika hekalu, ikijumuisha ng'ombe na kondoo. Nabhavunzilanaga ehela na zigaluzanye emeza zyabho.
JOH 2:16 Bhabhakazya enjebha abhabhozezye, “Efwi evintu vyenye bheshi hutali nepa, leshi abheshe ibhanza lya Ngolobhe pakazizye.”
JOH 2:17 Abhanafunzi bhakwe bhakomboha aje ehandihwe, “Owivu we nyumba yaho waindya.”
JOH 2:18 Agosi bheshi Yahudi bhajile, shimanyilo bhole shawaiilanga alengane nambo ega gebhomba?”
JOH 2:19 O Yesu wayanga, libomoli ibhanza eli nane embalizenje hunsiku zitatu.”
JOH 2:20 Agosi bha Yahudi bhayanga, “Wagatabhombile amah alobaini na sita awe oiga ubhazenje hunsiku zitatu?”
JOH 2:21 Japo, omwa ayanjile iwanza ayanjilaga obele gwakwe.
JOH 2:22 Esho pamande nkawafufuha afume hwa bhafwe, abhanafunzi wakwe bhakomboha aje ayanjile esho, weteshela izu ne njango ene o Yesu yatanguliye ayanje.
JOH 2:23 Lwa hali hu Yelusalemu owakati wa Pasaka, owakati we shikulukulu abhantu abhinji bhalyetesheye itawa lyakwe, na bhaloliwe embembo zya bhombaga.
JOH 2:24 Ila oYesu saga abheteshe afuatanaje abhamanye awantu bhonti.
JOH 2:25 Sagahanzaga omuntu wawonti ahubhozye alengane ne shabhali awantu afuatanaje amenye hahali muhati yabho.
JOH 3:1 Hwa hali omuntu oFalisayo itawa aliyo Nikodemo, wali jumbe mwibaraza lya Yahudi.
JOH 3:2 Omuntu abhaliye Ogosi oYesu na hubhozye nabi timenye aje awe oli mwalimwa afume hwa Ngolobhe, afuataje nomo umuntu wagabhombe ezi zyo bhomba awe paka abhanje nawe.”
JOH 3:3 O Yesu ajile, “Atesheli, atesheli, umuntu sawezizye ahwinjile amwanya paka apapwe emara yabhele.”
JOH 3:4 O Nikodemo ajile, “Agapapwa bhole wakati endi gogolo? Sawezizye ahwinjile muvianda mwa nyina wakwe emara ya bhele, na papwe shigabha?”
JOH 3:5 O Yesu ajile etesheli etesheli umuntu nkasaga papwe humenze na hu Mpepo, sawazizye ahwinjile hwa Ngolobhe.
JOH 3:6 Hahapepwe hubele hubele, hahapepwe husi Loho heshiroho.
JOH 3:7 Ungaje aswije shanabhozezye, 'lazima apape emara ya bhele.'
JOH 3:8 Ehala evugula hwahonti hwehwanza abhale izu lyakwe mliovwa, ila semuhwelewa hwefuma wala ata hwebhala sashili ehali ya wantu bhabhapepwe hushiroho.
JOH 3:9 O Nikodemo ajile, nayanje, Enongwa iziu ziwezehena?”
JOH 3:10 O Yesu ajile, “Awe oli mwalimwa we Israeli, sogamenye amambo ega?
JOH 3:11 Eteshela, eteshela, ehubhozya hala hati hamenye tihayanga hwa hala hatihalolile. Ila semwaposhenje olweteshelo wetu.
JOH 3:12 Nkashe embabho zezye enongwa zyepa pansi na semuhweteshele nkanaibhabhozya ezya mwanya?
JOH 3:13 Afuatanaje nomo wazubhile humwanya mbinguni ila omwahale ahishile, Omwana wa Adamu.
JOH 3:14 Nansi shila oMusa shabhosezye enzoha mwipoli, shesho shesho Omwana wa Adamu abhosewe,
JOH 3:15 aje bhonti bhabha yetesha wapataje owomi wewila wila.
JOH 3:16 Hunamna ene Ongolobhe aigene insi, paka afumizye omwana wakwe waje umuntu wowonti wai humweteha aganje teje mowomi we wila wila.
JOH 3:17 Ongolobhe sagatumile mwana wakwe munsi aje alonje ensi, ahenzele aje ensi efyolwe no mwahale.
JOH 3:18 Wahumweteshela omwahale sagailongwa. Umwene wasagahumweteshela alongwile tayali sababu salyeteshela itawa lya Mwana wa Ngolobhe.
JOH 3:19 Ene yenongwa eyalongwe, aje olukhozyo lwenzele munsi, awantu wasongwelwe enkisi ashile olughozyo alengane embombo zyabho zya mbibhi.
JOH 3:20 omntu wowonti wabhomba embibhi aluvitwa olukhozyo wala sahwenza mulokhozyo aje embombo zyakwe zigabhoneha wene.
JOH 3:21 Omwene, wabhomba zyelyoli ahwenza hulukhozyo aje embombo zyakwe zibhoneshe aje ziwoombwa hulunyenyekelo lwa Ngolobhe.
JOH 3:22 Badala yego, oYesu pamo na bhanafunzi bhakwe bhabhalile hunsi ye Yudea. Ohwo akheye muda pamo nabho ali abhozya.
JOH 3:23 O Yohana aliahwozyaohwo hu Ainea pepe na Salim afutanaje hwaliamenze minii hula. Abhantu bhahenzaga hwa mwahale ahwozewe,
JOH 3:24 afuatanaje oYohana alisaponyiziwe mwijela.
JOH 3:25 Hwafumiye amadali abhanafunzi bha Yohana na Myahudi ahusu evikulukulu vya hwiyozye.
JOH 3:26 Bhabhalile hwa Yohana bhabhabhozezye aje, “Rabi, omwene wohali nawo hwisyela Lisoho Yordani, omwene wahahakikisizye enongwa zyakwe, enya, obhozya awantu bhonti bhabhala bhahulondolela.”
JOH 3:27 O Yohana ajile omuntu sagaposhela hantu haonti ila nkashe apewilwe afume amwanya.
JOH 3:28 Amwe mwemwe muhakikisizye aje nayanjile aje, 'ane sene Kilisiti', pamande yakwe nayanjile, 'aje entumwilwe hwitazi lyakwe.'
JOH 3:29 Omwene wali no bibi harusi yo mweji we harusi. Eshi manyani wa mweji we harusi, wahwemelela na tejizye asongwa tee afutanaje izulya bwana harusi. Ene esalezi lusongwo lwane lwalukamilishe.
JOH 3:30 Ahwanziwa ahwonjelele na ehwanziwa apongoshe.
JOH 3:31 Omwene wafuma humwanya, ali hugonti omwene wali wa munsi afuma munsi na ayanga enongwa zyeshi ngolobhe. Omwene wafuma humwana ali pamwanya pagonti.
JOH 3:32 Omwene wayanga gala gagalolile nagomvwe, nomo waposhela enongwa zyakwe.
JOH 3:33 Omwene waposheye enongwa zyakwe ahakikisizye aje Ongolobhe welyoli.
JOH 3:34 Afuatane naje omwane watumwilwe no Ngolobhe ayanga enongwa zya Ngolobhe. Afatanaje sahupela Ompepo eshipimo.
JOH 3:35 Odaada ahugana Omwana na apiye evintu vyonti mumakhono gakwe.
JOH 3:36 Omwane ne humweteha oYesu ali no womi we wilawila, ila hwola wasa humwogopa oYesu sagaiulola owomi, ila khatana pamwanya yakwe.
JOH 4:1 O Yesu na wamanya aje aMafalisayo bhomwezye aje amemile na bhozye ashile oYohana,
JOH 4:2 (japokuwa oYesu yoyo ali sahwonzya ila awanafunzi bhakwe),
JOH 4:3 afumile hu Yudea na bhale hu Galilaya.
JOH 4:4 Esho hwali muhimu ashilile hu Samaria.
JOH 4:5 Na afishile hunsi ye Samalia, yehwetwagasi Sikari, karibu no sehemu ela o Yakobo yapiye mwanawakwe oYusufu.
JOH 4:6 Eshi sima sha Yakobo shali epo. O Yesu ali alitile alengane ne safari na akhala karibu ne shi sima. Gwali muda wa gwa pasanya.
JOH 4:7 Oshe oSamalia ahenzele atape menze, no Yesu abhozye, “Mpele amenze emwele.”
JOH 4:8 Afuatanaje abhanafunzi bhakwe abhafunzi bhali bhabhalile hujini akale esholye.
JOH 4:9 Ola oshe abhozya, “Shibha bhole awe wo Myahudi, kuniomba mimi mwanamke Msamaria, andabhe amenze ga mwele?” Afuatanaje Ayahudi sebhasangana na Samaria.
JOH 4:10 O Yesu wayanga, “Ogamenye ashipawa sha Ngolobhe, nola wahubhozya aje, 'Mpele menze, 'handawalabhile, handapiye amenze ge womi.”
JOH 4:11 Oshe ayanga, “'Gosi sagoli nidebe lya tapile, na eshisima shitali. Obhawapate hwi Amenze ge womi?
JOH 4:12 Aje awe oli gosi, ashile odaada wetu oYakobo, ola watipiye eshi sima eshi, na yeye mwenyewe na watoto wake pamoja na mifugo yake wakanywa maji ya kisima hiki?”
JOH 4:13 O Yesu wayanga, “Wawonti amwelile amenze obhapate eshomelwa nantele,
JOH 4:14 ila omwene wenzahupele amenze ega sagaibha neshomelwa nantele. Baadaye menze gembahupele ganzabhe chemichemi yebubujiha wila wila.”
JOH 4:15 Ola oshe wabhozya, “Ogosi, engalabha amenze ego nkengaje olole eshomelwa, na enganje alabhe ahenze epa atape menze.”
JOH 4:16 O Yesu wabhozya, “bhala kwizye olume waho, nantele uyenzaje.”
JOH 4:17 Oshe wabhozya wage, “Sendi nolume.” O Yesu wayanga, “Aje oyajile sawa, 'Aje sendi nolume;'
JOH 4:18 afuatanaje oli nalumo wa sanu, mo wope wolinawo esalaze se lume waho. Hweli oyanjile lyoli!”
JOH 4:19 Oshe wabhozya, “Ogosi aje elole ajewe oli kuwa.
JOH 4:20 Yise bhetu bhaputile pigamba amwe mwiga aje Yerusalemu ndiyo sehemu ambayo awantu bhahwanzia waapute.”
JOH 4:21 O Yesu ajile, “Weshe, niteshele, ensiku zihwenza nasemwaihuputa Daada huigamba eli au hu Yelusalemu.
JOH 4:22 Amwe mubhantu muputa hasemuhamanye, afuatanaje ofyilwe ufuma hwa Yaudi.”
JOH 4:23 Hata sheshi, ensiku zihwenza, neshi zihweli epa, nabhaihuputa Daada hu shiroho ne lyoli, afuatanaje oDaada abhanza abhantu bhabhali esho aje abhantu bhakwe bhabhahuputa.
JOH 4:24 Ongolobhe weshi Roho, bhabhahuta bhahwanziwa bhaputaje hushiroho ne lyoli, afuatanaje odaada abhanza abhantu ebho bhabhahupata.”
JOH 4:25 Oshe ola abhozya, “Emenye aje Yesu ohwenza, (wohwetwa Kilisiti). Ono nayenza aitibhozya gonti.”
JOH 4:26 O Yesu abhozya, “Ane woyanga nane nene.”
JOH 4:27 Insiku ezyo abhanafunzi bhakwe bhawela. Bhope bhaswigaga yenu ali ayanga noshe, ila nomo walenjele ahubhozye, “Ohwanza yenu?” au “Yenu ayanga nawo?”
JOH 4:28 Esho oshe ola ayileha ensonta yakwe abhalile husokoni abhabhozye abhantu,
JOH 4:29 “Enzaji mwenye omuntu wambozezye enongwa zyane zyonti zyebhomba, aje egawezehana aje agabhayo Kilisiti?”
JOH 4:30 Bhafumile hu sokoni bhenza hwamwene.
JOH 4:31 Pasanya abhanafunzi bhakwe bhalambile wajile, “Mwalimu alya eshalye.”
JOH 4:32 ila omwene abhabhozezye, “Ane endi nashalye shasemushimenye amwe.”
JOH 4:33 Abhanafunzi bhabhozanya, nomo waleteye ahantu hahonti alye,” Aje bhaletile?”
JOH 4:34 O Yesu abhabhozya, “Eshalye shane hubhombe ensongwo zyakwe omwene wantumile nakamilisye embombo yakwe.
JOH 4:35 Aje, semuyanga, 'Bado mezi gasanu emvuna ebhabhe tayari?” Embabho enyaji amagonda shagali tayari hu mvuna!
JOH 4:36 Omwene wavuna aposhela na wonganye amatunda gewomi we wila wila, ili aje omwane watota na wope wavuna bhasongwe pandwemo.
JOH 4:37 Afuatanaje enjango ene ye lyoli, 'Omomo atotile awamwabho ayawila.'
JOH 4:38 Nabhatumile avune hasemwambeleye, Wamo bhabhombile embombo namwe mwinjiehulishimo lwe mbombo yabho.”
JOH 4:39 Asamaria abhinji munsi ela bhamwetesheye afwatane ne taarifa ele yashe wayangaga enongwa zyonti zyanabhombile.”
JOH 4:40 Shesho Asamaria bhahenzele bhahenzebhalambile aje akhale pamo na bhahale ahakhala hwa bhene ensiku kuni na mbili.
JOH 4:41 Abhinji bhonti bhamweteshela alengane ni izu lyakwe.
JOH 4:42 Bhabhozya ola oshe, “Tihweteshela sio aje hunongwa zyaho, afuatanaje ate tete tomvwezye, na esauti tihwelewa aje lyoli ono fyozi we nsi.”
JOH 4:43 Baada ye nsiku ezyo zibhele, asogoye na bhale hu Galilaya.
JOH 4:44 Afuatanaje omwane yoyo atangazezye aje okuwaa saline heshima munsi yakwe yoyo.
JOH 4:45 Nahenzele afume hu Galilaya, Bhahu Galilaya bhakaribisizye bhali bhalolile embombo zyonti zyabhombile hu Yelusalemu hwahwali eshikulukulu, afwataneje abhene bhahuruliye hushi kulu kulu.
JOH 4:46 Ahenzele nante hu Kana ye Galilaya ohwo hwaguzenye amenze abhe divai. Pali no afisa ambaye omwana wakwe ali winu ohwo hu Kaperanaumu.
JOH 4:47 Na homvezye aje oYesu afumile hu Yudea na abhalile hu Galilaya, abhalile hwa Yesu na hulambe aishe aponye omwana wakwe, wakati ali karibu afwe.
JOH 4:48 O Yesu nkabhozya, “Amwe nkasemloli ehalama na mahajabu semuwezizye ahweteshele.
JOH 4:49 Olongozi ahayanga, “Gosi iha pansi omwana wane sali seele nafwe.”
JOH 4:50 O Yesu ahabhozya, “Bhalaga omwana waho mwomi.” Ola omuntu aheteshela izu lyayanjile oYesu wabhala wahwisogolela.
JOH 4:51 Lwali ahwiha, abhomba mbombo bhakwe bhaposheye na hubhozye omwana waho ali mwomi.
JOH 4:52 Esho wabhabhozya muda nshi ou nafuu. Bhajibu, “Igamo umuda gwesa saba ehoma ehamalishe.”
JOH 4:53 Eshi ogosi bhakwe ahamanya aje umuda gwagula oYesu gwayanjile, “Mwana waho mwomi.” Esho omwene ne familia yakwe bhaheteshela.
JOH 4:54 Ene yali halama yabhele yabhombile oYesu afumile hu Yudea abhale hu Galilaya.
JOH 5:1 Baada yepo hwali neshikulukulusha Yahudi no Yesu alizubhile abhale hu Yelusalemu.
JOH 5:2 Hula hu Yelusalemu hwali ni birika pandyango gwe ngole, lyalyalihwetwa hu lugha yeShiabrania hu Bethzatha, lyape lili na matao gasanu.
JOH 5:3 Abhantu bhinji abhinu bhahali, ampofu, avewete, bhabhahomele bhali bhagonile mumatao ego. {Khatililaga: Amazu ge sitali 3 segabhoneha mu nakala enyinza zi mwaha. “Bhagolezezye amenze avwalanganye.”') Hwa hali owakati umo ohalozelu muhati ya Gosi na vwalanganye menze.
JOH 5:4 Ola wa hali wa kwanza ahwinjile muhati amenze nagavwalanganywa oyo abhanga mwomi afumilane na hahonti hahali ha khetwe omuda ogwo.
JOH 5:5 No muntu wali abhinile humaha thelathini na nane wli mhati ye matao.
JOH 5:6 O Yesu nalolile agonile mhati ye matao nawamanya aje agonile pala omuda gwinji oYesu abhozya, “Ajile ohwanza abhe mwomi?”
JOH 5:7 Ola abhinu ajile, “Gosi sendi no muntu wambeshe mwi birika omuda amenze nagavwalanganywa. Lwelenga ahwinjile omuntu owenje antangulila.”
JOH 5:8 O Yesu wabhozya, “Bhoha ayeje igodolo lya ho obhalaje.”
JOH 5:9 Omuntu ola wapona, wega eshitala shakwe na wabhala. Isiku elyo lyali lisiku lye Sabato.
JOH 5:10 Ayahudi bhabhozya omuntu ola waponyiziwe, “Sanyono lisiku lya Sabato, solohusiwa abebe igodoro lyaho.”
JOH 5:11 Omwene ajile waponiziwe yayoyo wambozezye, “Ege igodoro lyaho bhalaga.”
JOH 5:12 Bhabhozezye, “Wenu wabhozyezye 'Ege igodoro lyaho bhalaga?'”
JOH 5:13 Haha nkashe ola waponile sagamenye, afwatanaje oYesu ali asogoye shi siri. Afuatanaje hwali awantu winji esehemu eyo.
JOH 5:14 Pamande yakwe oYesu amweje ola umuntu mshibhanza na hubhozye, “Enya, aponole! “Uganje abhombe mbibhi nantele ogakhomana ni jambo ibhibhi sana.”
JOH 5:15 Omuntu ola abhalile abhabhozye Ayahudi aje oYesu wamponezye.
JOH 5:16 Eshi, afuatanaje amambo ego Ayahudi bhayemvezye oYesu, afuatanaje abhombile amambo ega isiku lye Sabato.
JOH 5:17 O Yesu wabhabhozya, “Odaada wane abhomba embombo paka esalezi nane ebhomba embombo.”
JOH 5:18 Hunamuna eye Ayahudi bhahendeleye azidi bhahanzaga aje sababu yanankanye eSabato, ila hukwizye Ongolobhe oDaada wakwe, alihweshele sawa no Ngolobhe.
JOH 5:19 O Yesu ajile, “Etesheli, etesheli, Omwana sagabhomba ahantu hahonti ila hala halolile Oise wakwe abhomba, afuatanaje hahonti habhomba Oise haheho hanzabhombe Omwana.
JOH 5:20 Afuatanaje oDaada agene Omwana, na ahulanga kila hantu habhomba na ahaulanga amambo amagosi ashile ega ili nkamuswigage.”
JOH 5:21 Afuatanaje nanshi shila oDaada nafufula awafwe na abhapele owomi, sheshesho Omwana wope ahupele wowonti wagene.
JOH 5:22 Afuatane naje oDaada sahulonga wowonti, ila apiye Omwana alonje hwonti
JOH 5:23 ili bhonti bhamwogope Omwana sebhahu mwogopa oDaada. Umwene wasihumwogopa Omwana sahamwogope no Daada wantumile.
JOH 5:24 Eteshela, eteshela, omwene wahonvwa izu lyane na humweteshele wantumile ali no womi we wilawila na sagailongwa. Yaani ashilile afume hunfwa ahwinjile huwomi.
JOH 5:25 Eteshela, eteshela, embabhozya ensiku zihwenza na zihweli lula abhafwe nabhayovnwa izu lyakwe Omwana wa Ngolobhe, na bhonti bhabhayonvwa waikhala.
JOH 5:26 Nanshi shila oDaada shali nowomi mhati yakwe yoyo,
JOH 5:27 shesho apiye Omwana abhe no womi wope oDaada apiye Omwana amamlaka ili aje alongaje afuatanaje Mwana wa Adamu.
JOH 5:28 Munganje shangale hweli afuatanaje zihwenza ensiku abhafwe hbonti bhabhali mumakaburi bhayonvwa izu lyakwe
JOH 5:29 na bhope bhaifuma hunze: hwabhabhombaga enyinza ulyovyosyolwe womi, bhabhabhombaga embibhi oluvyosnsyo lwa longwe.
JOH 5:30 Sengabhomba ahantu hahonti afume huline nene. Nanshi shehovwa, shesho shelola alonje na alonje hwane hwe lyoli afuatanaje sehwanza she songwa ane, ila shasongwa omwane wantumile.
JOH 5:31 Nkashe ehwihakikisya nene, luhakikisyo lwane selwabhanga lwe lyoli.
JOH 5:32 Ahweli wamwabho wahakikisya ahusuane emanya aje lyoli uluhakikisho lwa hakikisizya ane we lyoli.
JOH 5:33 Mutumile hwa Yohana wope ahakikisizye lyoli.
JOH 5:34 Hata sheshi ulihakikisyo lwenduposhela selufuma hwa bhantu. Ninayasema haya ili kwamba mweze kuokolewa.
JOH 5:35 O Yohana ali lukhozyo lwalwa hahaga, na khozye mwahali tayari aisongwe huu muda ododo olukhozyo lwakwe.
JOH 5:36 Ulwetesho lwendi nalwo gosi ashile lula lwa Yohana, humbombo zila Odaada yza mpiye azikamilisye, anzyo embombo zyezibhomba zibhonesya aje Odaada antumile.
JOH 5:37 Odaada wantumile yoyo ahakikisizye ahusu ane. Semuwaile ahomvwe izu lyakwe au alole obele gwakwe omuda gwagwonti.
JOH 5:38 Semulinalyo izu lyakwe nkalikhale muhati afuatanaje semwamwetesheye omwene wantumile.
JOH 5:39 Mugenyelezya amazu msewa aje muhati yakwe muli owomi wewila wila, gego amazu gahakikisya ehabari zyane
JOH 5:40 semuhwanza ahwenez huline nkampate owomi wewilawila.
JOH 5:41 Siposhela huhwhiyonvwe afume hwa wantu,
JOH 5:42 ehwelewa aje nalumo olugano lwa Ngolobhe muhati yenyu.
JOH 5:43 Enenzele hwitawa lya Daada wane, semwamposheye. Nkashe owenje ayenze hwitawa lyakwe handamwaposheye.
JOH 5:44 Aje mwahenzaga ahweteshele amwe mwamposhela esifa afume hwa kila muntu wenyu ila semuhwanza esifa yefuma hwa Ngolobhe mwene?
JOH 5:45 Msagaje ane embabhatake hwitazi lya Daada. Wabhataka amwe yo Musa, ambayo mubheshele ategemele hwa mwa hale.
JOH 5:46 Mugali aje mhumweteshele oMusa, handamunetesheye nane afuatanaje ahaandishe ahusu ane.
JOH 5:47 Nkase muhwetehsele bhole amazu gane?
JOH 6:1 Baada ye enongwa ezi, oYesu abahlile hu Bahari ye Galilaya nantele huhweta isombe lye Tiberia.
JOH 6:2 Obhongano ogosi gwali guhufuata afuatanaje bhalolile ealama zyabhombile hwa bhala bhabhali bhawinu.
JOH 6:3 O Yesu azubhile pamwanya hadi sehemu ya pamwanya hwigamba na akhaye ohwo na bhanafunzi bhakwe
JOH 6:4 (Epasaka, ye shikulukulu sha Yahudi yali efishile).
JOH 6:5 O Yesu abhosezye amaso amwanya nalole owinji wa bhantu bhahwenza hwamwene, wabhozya oFilipo, “Tibhala hwii akale amabumunda aje ebhankabhapate alye”?
JOH 6:6 (Ila oYesu agayanjile ega hwa Filipo apimaga pima afuatanaje omwene yoyo amenye haibhomba).
JOH 6:7 O Filipo ajile, “Ata mabumunda hela hata dinari mia mbili seganzatosye shila muntu apate hashe hashe.”
JOH 6:8 O Andrea, omo webhanafunzi bhakwe ohoho wakwe oSimoni Petro abhozyezye
JOH 6:9 O Yesu, “Ahweli osahala epa ali na mabumunda gasanu ne samaki zi bhele, eshi ene ekhondeye yenu hwa bhantu abhinji enamuna ene?”
JOH 6:10 O Yesu abhozya, “Aje bhakhazyi abhantu pansi” (kulikuwa na nyasi nyingi mahali pale). Hivyo wanaume wapata elfu tano wakakaa chini.
JOH 6:11 Pamande oYesu wega amabumunda gasanu wasombwezye wabhagabhila bhala bhabhakheye. Shesho wabhagabhila esamaki alengane shabha hanzaga.
JOH 6:12 Abhantu nabhahakuta, abhabhozya abhanafunzi bhakwe, “Bhonganyi evigalizi vyavisageye aje nkaviganje ateje vyovyonti.”
JOH 6:13 Bhabhonganya na memwe evitondo kumi ne vibhele, evipande vye mabumunda visanu vyavyasageye na bhala bhabhalyanga.
JOH 6:14 Pamande abhantu na bhalola embombo zya bhombile bhajile, “Lyoli ono yayola okuwaa wahwenza munsi.”
JOH 6:15 O Yesu nagunduye aje bhahwanza ahukhate ili aje bhabheshe aje mwene wabho, ahwitenjile, nantele abhalile hwigamba omwene mwene.
JOH 6:16 Nahwali lyabhela, abhanafunzi bhakwe bhalushile abhale hwidimi idodo.
JOH 6:17 Bhapandile mwitoli bhali bhalobhoha abhale hu Kaperanaumu. (Enkisi yali eyenyiye no Yesu ali sele sayenzele hwabhene).
JOH 6:18 Eshipindi esho ehala engosi yali evugula, ne nsombe yali ehwendelela achafushe.
JOH 6:19 Nantele abhanafunzi bhakwe na bhali wakhomile emakasia kama shilini natano au thelathini wahalola oYesu ajenda pamwanya ye somba azuwilile itoli, wahogopa.
JOH 6:20 Ila wabhabhozya, “Nene mganjehwogope.”
JOH 6:21 Antele bhalitayali ahunyemle mwitoli, itoli nalyafihoa insi ya bhalaga.
JOH 6:22 Isiku lyalyafuatile, obhongano gwa hemeleye oupande wensombe bhalolaga aje nalimo itoli lya mwabho ila lila ambalyo oYesu na bhanafunzi bhakwe bhali sebhalipandile ila abhanafunzi bhakwe bhali bhahwibhaliyee bhebho.
JOH 6:23 (Japokuwa hwa hali amitoli gamo gafumaga hu Tiberia peepe ne sehemu hwabha lyanga amabumunda baada ya Gosi afumwe ulusalifyo).
JOH 6:24 Omuda embongano na bhamanya aje se yo Yesu wala sebhanafunzi bhakwe bhali hula, abhene bhebho wapende mwitoli bhabhala hu Kaperanaumu bhalondola oYesu.
JOH 6:25 Na bhahapata esehemu ya mwabho ye oimi dodo bhabhozya, “Mwalimwa ohenzele ndii ohu?”
JOH 6:26 O Yesu ayanga, abhabhozya, Etisheli, etisheli, munaanza ane, sio aje mwazilolile embombo ila afuatanaje mwaliye amabumunda nakute.
JOH 6:27 Leshi ashibhombela embombo eshalye shashi na nchiha, ila mshibhombele embombo eshalye shashikhala wilawila shila omwana wa Adamu shaibhapela, afuatanaje Ongolobhe Odaada abheshele omuhuri pamwanya yakwe.”
JOH 6:28 Pamande bhabhozya, “Hantu hahwanziwa abhombe aje abhombe embombo ya Ngolobhe?”
JOH 6:29 O Yesu ajibu, “Ene ye mbombo ya Ngolobhe: aje mwenteshe omwene wa ntumile.”
JOH 6:30 Bhabhozya, “Aje alama anshi zyobhabhombe, aje tibhazilole na humweteshele? Obhabhombe bhole?
JOH 6:31 Adaada bhetu bhaliye emanna mwipoli, nanshi sheyaandihwe, “Abhapiye amabumunda afume amwanya nkabhalye.”
JOH 6:32 O Yesu abhabhozya, “Etisheli, etisheli, sio yo Musa abhapiye amabumunda afume amwanya, bali Baba yangu ndiye awapaye mkate wa kweli kutoka mbinguni.
JOH 6:33 Afuatanaje ibumunda lya Ngolobhe lyalila lyalihwiha afume amwanya naipele ensi owomi.
JOH 6:34 Eshi bhabhozya, “Bhaga Gosi tipelaje amabumunda wilawila.”
JOH 6:35 O Yesu ahaga, “Ane endi libumunda lye womi, omwene wa hwenza huline sagailola enzala omwene wane teshela sagaichisila enzara omwene waneteshela sagaichisila na mwaha eshomelwa.”
JOH 6:36 Ijapokuwa embabhozezye aje, mundolile, lakini semuhweteshela.
JOH 6:37 Bhonti oDaada wampiye bhanzahwenze huline, na wawonti wahwenza huline senaihutaga honze kabisa.
JOH 6:38 Afwatanaje enishile afume amwanya, sehwahubhombe olusongwo lwane, ila ulusongwo lwa wantumile.
JOH 6:39 No olu lwo lusongwo lwakwe wantumile, aje nsatezye hata muntu omo bhala bhombiye, ila ehaibhazyosya isiku lya mwisho.
JOH 6:40 Afuatanaje ega gasongwa Odaada wane, aje wawonti wa humwenya Omwana na humweteshele apate owomi wewila wila; wenu wanaihuzyonsya isiku elya mwisho.
JOH 6:41 Pamande ayahudi walalamishila ahusu omwene afuatanaje ayanjile, “Ane endi libumunda lyalihwiha afume amwanya.”
JOH 6:42 Bhayanga, “Ono seyo Yesu omwana wa Yusufu, odaada wakwe no nyina wakwe timenye? Shili bhole esalezi aiga, 'Enishile afume humwanya`?”
JOH 6:43 O Yesu ahayanga, ajile, “Muganje alalamishalane mhati yenyu mwemwe.
JOH 6:44 Nomo omuntu wahwenza huline nkashe savutilwe no Daada wane wantumile, nane naihuvyonsya isiku elya mwisho.
JOH 6:45 Afuatanaje eyandihwe hwa kuwaa, 'Bhanzasambelezewe no Ngolobhe.' Shila wayomvwezya asambeleye afume hwa Daada, ahwenza huline.
JOH 6:46 Sio aje ahweli omuntu walolile Odaada, ila omwene wafuma hwa Ngolobhe- alolile Odaada.
JOH 6:47 Eteha, eteha omwene wanetesheye ali no womi wewilawila.
JOH 6:48 Ane endi libumunda lye womi.
JOH 6:49 adaada bhetu bhaliye emanna mwipoli, bhahafwa.
JOH 6:50 Eli ndiyo libumunda lyalihwiha afume amwanya, ili omuntu alye nkaganje afwe.
JOH 6:51 Ane endi libumunda lyalikhala lyalilishile afume amwanya. Nanshi omuntu wawonti nkalye ibumunda eli, aihwizya wilawila. Ibumunda lye mbefumye bele gwane alengane no womi ensi.”
JOH 6:52 Ayahudi bhavitwa bhebho hu bhebho bhanda abisanye bhaiga, “Omuntu ono awezizye bhole atipele obele gwakwe tiilye?”
JOH 6:53 Nantele oYesu wabhbhozya, “Etesheli, etesheli, nkashe semwailya obele gwa Mwana wa Adamu na mwele idanda lyakwe, semwaibha nowomi muhati yenyu.
JOH 6:54 Wawonti wailya obele gwane na mwele idanda lyane ali no womi wewilawila, nane naihuvyonsya isiku lya mwisho.
JOH 6:55 Afwatanaje obele gwane shalye she lyoli, ni danda lyane shimwelo she lyoli.
JOH 6:56 Omwe wagulya obele gwane na mwele idanda lyane akhala muhati yane, nane mhati yakwe.
JOH 6:57 Nanshi Odaada we womi shantumile, nanshi shakheye alengane no Daada, wakwe no mwene aikhala alengangane.
JOH 6:58 Eli libumunda lyali hwihaafume amwanya, sio nanshi shila Adaada wenyu bhaliye bhafwa. Omwene wanzalye ibumunda eli ayikhala wilawila.
JOH 6:59 O Yesu ayanjile enongwa ezi mshibhanza nahali afundizya hu Kaperanaumu.
JOH 6:60 Abhinji abhanafunzi bhakwe bhahomvweze ega, bhayanjile, “Eli lifundizyo likhone wenu wawezizye aliposhele?”
JOH 6:61 O Yesu afuatanaje amenye aje abhanafunzi bhakwe bhalalamiha iswali eli libhavisya, akawambia je jambo hili linawakwaza?
JOH 6:62 Eshi shaibha na waihulola omwana wa Adamu naihwiha afume hwahweli kabisa?
JOH 6:63 Yo Mpempo yayoyo wafumya owomi. Obele saguhwavwa nkahamo. Amazu ge njanjile hulimwe ga mpempo no womi.
JOH 6:64 Bhahweli abhantu hulimwe bhasebhahweteshela.” afuatanaje oYesu amenye fume hale ola wasaga hweteshela na ola omwene wanzahusyonshele.
JOH 6:65 Wabhabhozya, aje shasheshi nabhabhozezye aje nomo omuntu wayenza huline ila apewilwe no Daada.”
JOH 6:66 Baada yega abhanafunzi bhakwe wonti wawela akhosi na khatane nawo nantele.
JOH 6:67 O Yesu wabhabhozya bhala kumi na bhabhele, “Aje namwe muhwanza asogole?”
JOH 6:68 O Simoni oPetulo wayanga, “Gosi tibhale hwa nanu afatanaje awe oli ni izu lya womi wewilawila,
JOH 6:69 natetesheye na manye aje awe oligolosu wa Ngolobhe.”
JOH 6:70 O Yesu wayanga, “Aje ane senabhachaguye amwe, na omo wenyu yo setano?
JOH 6:71 Eshi aliayanga ahusu oYuda, omwana wa Simoni Iskariote, afwatanaje ali yoyoyo ali pamo na bhala kumi na bhabhele, ambaye wasyonsheye oYesu.
JOH 7:1 Pamande ye mambo ega oYesu asafiliye eshi hu Galilaya, afuatanaje sagaasongwelwe abhala huu Yahudi afwatanaje huuyahudi wapangaga ahubude.
JOH 7:2 Eshi eshikulukulu sha Yahudi, eshi kulukulu ye Vibanda, ya pepee.
JOH 7:3 Aholo wakwe nkabhozya, “Sogala apantu epa obhale hu Yahudi, abhanafunzi bhaho bhagalole amambo gobhomba.
JOH 7:4 Nomo wabhomba lyolyonti hu shi siri nkashe omwene yoyo ahwanza ajulihane pazelu. Nkashe obhomba ega, hwilanje wewe hwabha munsi.”
JOH 7:5 Hata bhaholo bhakwe sebhamwetesheye.
JOH 7:6 O Yesu nkabhabhozya, “Insiku zyane sezifishile bado, ila ensiku zyenyu kila muda zihweli.
JOH 7:7 Abhamunsi sebhawezizye abhavitwe amwe, ila bhamvitwa ane afuatane embahakikisya aje ambombo zyao mbibhi.
JOH 7:8 Zubhaji abhale hu shikulukulu; ane sembala hu shikulukulu afuatanaje omuda gwane guli seele afishe.”
JOH 7:9 Nayanga enongwa izyo hwa bhahala, asageye hu Galilaya.
JOH 7:10 Hata sheshi, aholo bhakwe na bhabhalile hushikulukulu wope nkahabhala, sio apazelu bali pasirisiri.
JOH 7:11 Ayahudi bhali bhahufuata hushikulukulu naje, “Ali hwii?”
JOH 7:12 Hwali no luyangano lwinji muhati mlubhongano ahusu omwene. Wamo bhajile, “Muntu mwinza.” Bhamwabho wajile, “Ndadi abhatezya olubhongano.”
JOH 7:13 Hata sheshi nomo wayanjile pazelu ahusu omwahale afuatanaje bhabhogope Ayahudi.
JOH 7:14 Ensiku zye shikulukulu nazyahali katikati, oYesu azubhile abhale mshibhanza na hwande asambelezye.
JOH 7:15 Ayahudi bhaswigaga na nayanje, “Huu namna wele omuntu amanye enongwa enyinji? Sasambeleye nkahashe.”
JOH 7:16 O Yesu ayanga naje, “Emanyizyo zyane se zyaline, ila zyoola wantumile.
JOH 7:17 Nkashe wawonti anzasongwe abhombe olusongwo lwakwe omwene, anzamanye emanyizyo ezi, aje zifuma hwa Ngolobhe, au aje eyanga afume huline nene.
JOH 7:18 Shila wayanga gagafuma hwa mwene yoyo ahwenza umwamu wakwe, na shila wahwanza oumwamu wakwe omwene wantumile, omuntu omuntu oyo we lyoli, na muhati yakwe nahumo abhombeshe zye malenka.
JOH 7:19 O Musa sagabhapiye amwe endajizyo? Ila nomo hata weka hulimwe wabhomba endajizyo. Yenyu muhwanza ambude?
JOH 7:20 Amabhongano gayanga, “Aje oli na mapepo. Wenu wahanza ahubude?”
JOH 7:21 O Yesu wayanga wagaa, “Ombombile embombo yeeka, namwe mwenti muswijile afuatanajenesho.
JOH 7:22 O Musa abhapiye etohara (sio aje efuma hwa Musa, ila efuma hwa daada), na hu Sabato mhutahiri omuntu.
JOH 7:23 Nkashe omuntu anzaposhele etohara hwi siku lye Sabato aje endajizyo zya Musa zinganje nankanywe, yeenu munvitwa ane afwatanaje ebheshele omuntu abhe mwinza kabisa hu Sabato?
JOH 7:24 Mganje alonje alengane sha mlola, ila alonje hulyoli.
JOH 7:25 Bhamo bhamo uYelusalemu bhaga, “Seyayono wabhahu mwanza ahude?
JOH 7:26 Enya, oyanga pazelu, na sebhayanga hahonti alengane no mwene. Sawezizye aje egabha aje alongozi bhamenye elyoli aje ono yo Kilisiti, ewezizye abhe?
JOH 7:27 Timenye aje omuntu ono afumila hwii. O Kilisti lwayenza, atasheshii, nomo wailola aje afuma hwii.”
JOH 7:28 O Yesu afumiaga izu lyakwe mwibhanza, asambele zyaga naje, “Amwe mwenti mumenye ane na mumeenye hwe fuma. Senamenye hubele gwane, ila omwene wantumile welyoli, semumenye omwene.
JOH 7:29 Emenye omwene afuatanaje enfumile hwa mwene na antumile.”
JOH 7:30 Bhalenga ahaate, ila nomo ata omo wabhosezye okhono gwakwe ahusu omwene afuatanaje esaa yakwe yaali seele afishe.
JOH 7:31 Hata sheshi bhinji mubhongano bhamwetesheye. Bhajile, “Kilisiti lwa yeenza, aibhomba embombo nyinji ashile zyabhombile omuntu ono?”
JOH 7:32 Amafarisayo bhabhonvwezye amawongano wakwepelena enongwa ezi eshi oYesu, na agosi bha dimi na Mafarisayo bhatumile amaafisa aje ahukhate.
JOH 7:33 O Yesu nkayanga, “Ali seele insiku ndodo embabhe pandwemo namwe, napamande naibhala hwa mwene wantumile.
JOH 7:34 Munanza ila semubhandole; hula hwembala, semubhawezye ahwenze.”
JOH 7:35 Abhayaudi bhayangama bhene hu bhene, “Omuntu ono anzabhale hwii aje tipotwe ahulole? Anzabhale hwa bhabhanyampene mhati ya yunanu bhamanyinzye Ayunani?
JOH 7:36 Nongwa bhole ene yayanjile, 'Mwainanza nantele semwainaga; hula hwembala semwaiwezya ahwenze'?”
JOH 7:37 Esalezi hunsiku zya mwisho, isiku igosi lye shikulukulu, pYesu ahemeleye azurizwe izu ajile, “Nkashe wa wonti ali ne sshomelwa, ayenze huline amwele.
JOH 7:38 Omwene waneteshe ane, nanshi amazu shagayanjile, afume mhati yakwe ganza hwiteshe amasoho gemenze gewomi.”
JOH 7:39 Ila ayanji ega alengane hushi Roho, afuatanaje bhala bhabhamwetesheye bhayihuposhela; Ompempo ali seele safumiziwe alengane naje oYesu ali samwamihwe.
JOH 7:40 Bhamo bhelubhongano, nabhahomvwezye enongwa eezi, bhajile, “Yoli ono kuwaa.”
JOH 7:41 Bhamo bhayanjile, “Ono Kilisiti.” Ila bhamo bhamo bhajile, “yenu, oKilisiti awezya afume hu Galilaya?
JOH 7:42 Amaazu segayanga aje oKilisiti aifuma hushikholo sha Daudi na afume hubenselehemu, hushi jiji shahali oDaudi?
JOH 7:43 Shesho, pala pabhoha olugabhano mhati yelubhongamo alengane no mwahale.
JOH 7:44 Bhamo mhati yabho handabhakhete, ila nomo wagolosezye okhono gwakwe hwa mwene.
JOH 7:45 Bhala ofisa bhawela hwa gosi adimi na Mafarisayo, bhope bhabhabhozya, “Yenu semletile?”
JOH 7:46 Amaofisa bhajile, “Nomo omunti wawayile ayanje nanshi ono haani.”
JOH 7:47 Amafarisayo nkabhahaga, “Namwe nantele mtejile?
JOH 7:48 Ahweli omuntu wawonti hwa gosi wahumweteha, au wawonti hwa Mafarisayo?
JOH 7:49 Ila ebha amabhongano bhasebhemenye endwajizyo - wapete amakhosi.”
JOH 7:50 O Nikodemo abhabhozya (omwene wabhaliye oYesu imwaha, ali pamo na Mafarisayo),
JOH 7:51 “Aje endajizyo zyetu ziholonga omuntu ila atejezewe na soti na amanye habhomba?”
JOH 7:52 Bhayanjile na hubhozye, “Ivi nawe ofumila hu Galilaya? Anza na oyenye aje nomo okuwaa wafumila hu Galilaya.”
JOH 7:53 Pamande shila munti ahabhala akhaya yakwe.
JOH 8:1 O Yesu abhalile hwigamba lye Mzeituni.
JOH 8:2 Khasha shampwiti ahenza nantele hushibhanza, na abhantu bhonti bhabhalila; ahakhala bhasambeleyezye.
JOH 8:3 Abhandishi na Mafarisayo bhaletela oshe wa khetwe humbombo yehuni. Bhabheha pahati.
JOH 8:4 Epo nkabhabhalila oYesu, “Mwalimu, oshe ono akhetwe mu huni, mumbombo lyoli.
JOH 8:5 Esalezi, endajizyo, zya Musa atilajizizye awapole na mawe abhantu nanshi ebho, oyigabhole hwego?
JOH 8:6 Bhanyanjile ega ahutejesezye aje nkabhabhe ne nongwa ya hutake, ila oYesu au ndeme mpansi ahaandiiha mwinkondi hwa dole hakwe.
JOH 8:7 Na bhahendeleye ahubhozye, ahemeleye na bhabhozye, “Omwene wasali nembibhi mhati yenyu, abhe wahwande ahupole amawe.”
JOH 8:8 Waundama nantele pansi, wadola mwinkondi hushidole shakwe.
JOH 8:9 Nabhahonvwa ego, bhasogoye omo baada ya wamwabho ahwande waliigogolo hata. Owamalishile wabho mwene, paamo no she waali pahati yabho.
JOH 8:10 O Yesu ahemeleye na nahubhozye wee shee wewe, bhabhatakile bhali hwii? Nomo ata weka walonjile?”
JOH 8:11 Wagaa, “Nomo ata weka Gosi.” O Yesu waaga, “Hata nene sihulonga. Bhalaga hwi dala lyaho; ahwande esalezi na hwendelele oganje abhombe embibhi nantele.”
JOH 8:12 Nantele oYesu ayanga na bhantu waga, “Ane endi lukhozyo lyensi; omwene wanzandondolele saganzajende munkisi ila anzabhe nolukhozyo lwe womi.”
JOH 8:13 Amafarisayo bhabhozye, “Ohwihakikisya wewe; oluhakikisyo lwaho see lwe yooli.”
JOH 8:14 O Yesu ayanga ahaga, “Hata nkashe ehwihakikisya neen oluhakikisyo lwane, lwe yooli. Emenye hwe nfumile na hwe mbala, ila amwe semumenye hwe nfumile wala hwembala.
JOH 8:15 Amwe mulonga shibele; ane sehulonga wawonti.
JOH 8:16 Ane hata nkashe elonje, endonga yane ye lyoli afuatanaje sendi nemwene, endi paamo no daada wantumile.
JOH 8:17 Ena, hundajizyo zyenyu iyandihwe aje oluhakikisyo lwa bhantu bhabhelilwe lyoli.
JOH 8:18 Ane ne hwihakikisye, no Daada wantumile ahakikisya.”
JOH 8:19 Bhabhozya, “Odaada waho ali hwii?” O Yesu ahaaga, “ane semumenye hata Odaada wane semumenye, mgali aje mumenye ane handa mmenye Odaada wane wope.”
JOH 8:20 Ayanjile enongwa ezi alipepe no lubhutilo nali asambelezya mshibhanza, na ali nomo ata weka wakhete afuatanaje esaa yakwe yaali seele afishe.
JOH 8:21 Eshi abhabhozya nantele, “Nahwisogolela mwainanza na mwaifwela mumbibhi zyenyu. Hula hwe mbala semuwezizye ahwenze.”
JOH 8:22 Abhayahudi bhajile, “Obhahwibude humwene, omwene wayanjile, 'hula hwe mbala semuwezezye ahwenze'?”
JOH 8:23 O Yesu abhabhozye, “Mufuma pansi; ane efuma amwanya. Amwe muli bha munsi omu; ane sendi wa munsi omu.
JOH 8:24 Eshi eshi, nabhabhozezye aje mwaifwa mumbibhi zyenyu. Labuda mweteshele aje ANE NENE, mwaifwa mu mbibhi zyenyu”.
JOH 8:25 Eshi bhabhozya, “Awe we nanu?” O Yesu wabhabhozya, Gala ganabhabhozezye ahwande huwandilo.
JOH 8:26 Endi ne nongwa nyinji ezya yanje nalonje ahusu amwe. Hata sheshi, omwene wantumile we lyoli ne nongwa zyamwonvwezye afume hwa mwene, enongwa ezi nayanga hwa bha Munsi.”
JOH 8:27 Sebhamwelewe aje ali ayanga nabho ahusu Odaada.
JOH 8:28 O Yesu ajile, Namu bhahubhosye amwanya Omwana wa Muntu, nkamwailola aje NENE, naje sebhomba lyalyonti nemwene. Nanshi Odaada shansambelezezye, ayanga enongwa ezi.
JOH 8:29 Omwane wantumile ali pamo nane, na omwene sandeshile nemwene, alenganaje shila muda ebhomba gala gasongwa.”
JOH 8:30 O Yesu lwayangaga enongwa ezyo bhinji bhamweteshe.
JOH 8:31 O Yesu ayange hwa Yahudi bhala bhabhamweteshe, “Nkashe mubhakhale mwizu lyane, epo mubhabhe bhanafunzi bhane lyoli,
JOH 8:32 namwe mubhaimanya elyoli, na elyoli ebhabhabheshe bhaushe.”
JOH 8:33 Bhajile, Ate tili shi kholo sha Ibulahimu na mwaha setiwayile abhebhaboyi bha muntu wawonti; obhayanje bhole aje, “Tibhabhe bhauusu?”
JOH 8:34 O Yesu wabhabhozya, “Etesheli, etesheli, embebhozya, wawonti wabhomba embibhi boyi we mbibhi.
JOH 8:35 Boyi sakhala pakhayo omuda gwonti; omwana akhala nsiku zyonti.
JOH 8:36 Eshi eshi, nkashele Omwana aibhabheha bhausu, mwaibha bhausu lyoli.”
JOH 8:37 Embamenye aje amwe mlishikholo sha Ibulahimu; muhwanza angoje alengane ni izu lyane selili no khalo mhati yenyu.
JOH 8:38 Eyanga enongwa zyenzilolile pamo na Daada wane, namwe pia mubhomba enongwa zya mwahonvwezye hwa daada wenyu.”
JOH 8:39 Bhayanjile na hubhozye, “Odaada wetu yo Abulahamu.” O Yesu abhabhozya nkashe mungali bhana bha Ibulahimu, handamubhomba embombo zyakwe o Ibulahimu.
JOH 8:40 Hata sheshi munanza hungoje, omuntu walenjele elyoli aje ehomvwezye afume hwa Ngolobhe. O Ibulahimu sagabhombile esho.
JOH 8:41 Mubhomba mbombo ya daada wenyu.” Bhabhozya, “Setapepwe muuhuni, tili Odaada omo, yo Ngolobhe.”
JOH 8:42 O Yesu abhabhozya, “Nkashe Ongolobhe yo Daada wenyu, handa mungene ane, afuatanaje handa mungene ane, afuatanaje enfumile hwa Ngolobhe; wala sehenzele hubeele gwane ila hwa mwene wantumile.
JOH 8:43 Yenu semgelewa amazu gane? Afuatanaje semuwezizye avumilile agatejezye amazu gane.
JOH 8:44 Amwe mli bha Daada wenyu, osetano na mhwanza abhombe oluziliho lya Daada wenyu. Aligoji ahwande huwando na sawezizye ahwemelele mlyoli afuatanaje elyoli nemo mhati yakwe. Nkayanga ilenka, ayanga afume mmwoyo gwakwe afuatanaje wilenka na Odaada wilenka.
JOH 8:45 Hata sheshi, afuatanaje eyanga zye lyoli, semueteshela.
JOH 8:46 Wenu hulimwe wahakikisye aje endine mbibhi? Nkashe eyanga zye lyoli, yenu semuneteshela?
JOH 8:47 Omwene wali wa Ngolobhe ateje zya amazu ga Ngolobhe; afwatanaje semulibha Ngolobhe.”
JOH 8:48 Ayahudi wayanjile na hubhozye, setiyanjile yoli aje awe oli Samaria na oli ni pepo?”
JOH 8:49 O Yesu ajile, sendi ni pepo; ila ehumwogopa Odaada wane, amwe semunogopa.
JOH 8:50 Sehwanza oumwamihwe; waline ali weka wahwanza na lonje.
JOH 8:51 Etesheli, etesheli, embabhozya, nkashe wawonti ayilikhata izu lyane, sagailola enfwa na mwaha.”
JOH 8:52 Ayahudi bhabhozya, “Esalaze tamanya aje oli ni pepo. O Abulahamu na kuwaa bhafwiye; oiga, “Nkashe omuntu akhate izu lyaho, saganzabhonje enfwa'.
JOH 8:53 Awe soli gosi ashile odaada wetu oAbulahamu bhafwiye shenje? Akuwaa bhope bhafwiye. Awe ohwibheha we nanu?”
JOH 8:54 O Yesu ajile, “Nkashe ehwizuvya nemwene, oumwihwe wane bure; yo Daada waline wanzuvya - ola wa muhuyanga aje Ngolobhe wenyu.
JOH 8:55 Amwe semumenye omwahale, ila ane emenye omwene. Nkashe embaje, 'semenye,' embabhe nanshi amwe, wilenka. Hata sheshi, engaemenyeamazu gakwe engakhete.
JOH 8:56 Odaada wenyu oAbulahamu asongwelwe na walilola isiku lyane na aalilolile na asongwelwe.”
JOH 8:57 Ayahudi bhabhozya,”Sofisizye omuri we maha amusini bado, nawe ololile o Ibulahimu?”
JOH 8:58 O Yesu abhabhozya, “Etesheli, etesheli, embabhozya, o Ibulahimu salibado apapwe, ANE EHWENDI.”
JOH 8:59 Nkabhatola amawe aje bhakhome, O Yesu ahobhele ahafuma honzehu shibhanza.
JOH 9:1 O Yesu nali ashile alolile omuntu okipofu ahwande apapwe hwamwehale.
JOH 9:2 Abhanafunzi bhakwe bhabhozezye, “Mwalimu, “Wenu wabhombile embibhi, omuntu ono au yo yise no nyina paka apapwa mpofu?”
JOH 9:3 O Yesu ayanga, “Se yayono omuntu wala aise wakwe no nyina wakwe aje bhabhabhombila embibhi, yaani embombo zya Ngolobhe zikwinkushe ashilile hwa mwene.
JOH 9:4 Tihwanziwa abhombe embombo zyakwe shahuli pasanya. Osiku uhwenza pasetaiwezya abhombe embombo.
JOH 9:5 Omuda gwendi munsi, ane endi lukhozyo.”
JOH 9:6 O Yesu nayaanga amazu ega, aswiye mwinkondi, abhombele itotoo huu mate, na wapaha ola omuntu amaso na lila itope.
JOH 9:7 Wabhozya, bhalaga oyoje mwidimi lye Siloamu (Yebhoneha aje 'watumilwe').” Eshi omuntu abhalile anawe na wawela alola.
JOH 9:8 Ajilani bhakwe ola omuntu bhabhalolile hula ahwande aje labizi bhajile, Aje! ono wenje ola omuntu wakhalaga na labhizye?” bhamo bhajile, Na yoyo.”
JOH 9:9 Na bhamo bhamo bhajile, ndadi ono alengane nabho.” Ila ali ayaanga, NENE.”
JOH 9:10 Bhabhozya, “Esalezi amaso gaho gafunkushe bhole?”
JOH 9:11 Ajibuye, omuntu wahwetwa Yesuu abhombele itoto na pashe mmaso gane na mbozye, 'Bhalaga Siloamu unawe.' Esheshi nabhalile na nanawile nanapete alole.”
JOH 9:12 Bhabhozezye, “Ali hwii?” Ajile, “Maanyi.”
JOH 9:13 Bhatwalile ola omuntu wawaile abhe mpofula hwa Mafarisayo.
JOH 9:14 Lyope lyali lisiku lye Sabato oYesu lwa lengeye amatoto na hwigule amaso gakwe.
JOH 9:15 Amafarisayo bhabhozya ahandile bhole alole. Abhabhozya, “Abheshele itole mumaso gane, nanawile, neshi elola.”
JOH 9:16 Bhamo Amafarisayo bhajile, “Omuntu ono safumile hwa Ngolobhe afwatanaje saikhete eSabato.” Bhamo bhamo bhajile egawezehana wole omuntu we mbibhi abhombe embombo nanshi ezyo hwa wantuna gabhanyisha mhati yabho.
JOH 9:17 Nkabhabhozya ola ompofila nantele oyiga bhole ahusu omwahale afuatane naje ahiguye amaso gaho?” Ompofu wagaa, “Kuwaa.”
JOH 9:18 Hata isinku ezi Ayahudi sebhamweteshe aje ali mpofula wope apete alole paka pabhabhakwizizye oise no nyina wapete alole.
JOH 9:19 Bhabhobhozezye aise no nyina, Aje, ono mwana wenyu wamuyiga apepwe mpofu? awezizye bhole alole esalezi?”
JOH 9:20 Aise no nyina bhajile, “Timenye aje ono mwana wetu na aje apepwe mpofula.
JOH 9:21 Shili bhole esalezi alola, setimenye no ola wamwiguye amaso setimenye. Bhozezi yoyo. Muntu gosi. Anzahwiyelezye yoyo.”
JOH 9:22 Aise no nyina bhayanjile enongwa ezi afuatanaje bhahogope Ayahudi. Shila Ayahudi bhahetehene aje nkashe wawonti ayeteha aje oYesu oKilisti, aitengwa Wibhanza.
JOH 9:23 Hunamuna ene, oise no nyina wakwe bhajile, “Omuntu gosi, bhozyaji yoyo.”
JOH 9:24 Hu mara ya bhele, bhakwizizye ola omuntu wawaile abhe mpofula na hubhozye, “Pele Ongolobhe oumwamihwe. Timenye aje omuntu ono muntu we mbibhi.”
JOH 9:25 Ola omuntu ahayanga, “Abhe we mbibhi, ane sehwelewa. Ahantu hamo hemenye nali mpofula: esalezi ehwenya.”
JOH 9:26 Eshi nkabhabhozya, “Abhombeye yenu? Ahiguye amaso gaho?”
JOH 9:27 Ajile, “Embabhozezye ila amwe semuhwonvwa! Yenu mhwanza ahonvwe nantele? Amwe semuhwanza abhe bhanafunzi bhakwe nantele?
JOH 9:28 Bhalijile naje, “Awe oli mwanafunzi wakwe, ikla ate tili bhanafunzi bha Musa.
JOH 9:29 Timenye aje Ongolobhe ayanjile no Musa, ila hwomo omuntu, seti menye hwafuma.”
JOH 9:30 Ola omuntu ayanga na bhahozye, “Yenu, enongwa ezi zyaswije, aje semumenye hwafuma, na ayiguye amaso gane.
JOH 9:31 Timenye aje Ongolobhe sabhonvwa abhembibhi, nkashe omuntu wawonti ahuputa Ongolobhe na abhombe olusongwo lwakwe, Ongolobhe mwonvwa.
JOH 9:32 Ahwande peyandile Insi ene sewaile abhoneshe omuntu aiguye amaso gamuntu wapepwe mpofula.
JOH 9:33 Egalije omuntu ono safumile hwa Ngolobhe, handasabhombile hahonti.”
JOH 9:34 Bhayanjile na hubhozye, “Uhapepwe mumbibhi mhaani, awe atisambelezya ate?” Nkabhabhenga mshibhanza shabho.
JOH 9:35 O Yesu ahonvwezye aje bhamwefizye mshibhanza. Amweje na hubhozye, “Aje ohumweteha Omwana wa Muntu?”
JOH 9:36 Ayanjile naje, “Wenu, Gosi, aje nkemweteshe?”
JOH 9:37 O Yesu abhozya, “Uloolile, woyanga nawo yayoyo.”
JOH 9:38 Ola omuntu ayanga, “Gosi ehweteshela epo nkafugamiye.
JOH 9:39 O Yesu ayanga, “Alonje enenzele Munsi omu aje bhala bhasebhahwenya bhapete ahwenye nabhala bhabhahwenya bhabhe mpofula.”
JOH 9:40 Bhamo Amafarisayo bhalipamo nawo bhahonvwa amazu ege nahubhozye, “Nate eshi tili mpofula?”
JOH 9:41 O Yesu abhabhozya, “Nkashe mgali bha mpofu, handasemli ne mbibhi. Hata sheshi muyiga, 'Tilola,' embibhi zyenyu zikheye.”
JOH 10:1 Etesheli, Etesheli embabhozya, ola wasahwinjila ashilile mundyango gwi goma lye ngole, ila azubha hwidala lya mwabho, omuntu oyo mwibha na fyozi.
JOH 10:2 Omwane wa hwinjila mundyango yodimi we ngole.
JOH 10:3 Hwa mweme olinzi we dyango ahwigulilwa. Engolezolyonvwa izu lyakwe na azikwi zya engole zyakwe hu matawa gabho na zifumye honze.
JOH 10:4 Naizifumya honze ezye zyazili zyakwe azitangulila ne Ngolobhe zihulondolela, afuatanaje bhalimenye izu lyakwe.
JOH 10:5 Sezinzahumwanze ojenyu ila zinza hupemushile, afuatane sezigamenye amazu ga jenyu.”
JOH 10:6 O Yesu ayanga ofwana ogu hwabhene, ila sebhazyelewe enongo ezi zyali ayanag hwa bhene.
JOH 10:7 O Yesu ayanga nabho nantele, “Etesheli, etesheli, embabhozya, Ane endi ndiango gwe ngole.
JOH 10:8 Bhonti bhabhatanguliye bhibha na bhafyozi, ila engole zibhonvwa.
JOH 10:9 Ane endi ndiango. Wawonti wahwinjila ashilile huline, aifyoliwa ainjila muhati na fume, wope aipata edyo.
JOH 10:10 Omwibha sahwenza ila ahwibhe, agoje, natezye, enenzele nkawepate owomi bhabhe nawo winji.
JOH 10:11 Ane endi dimi mwinza. Odimi omwinza afumya owomi wakwe huu ngole.
JOH 10:12 Oboyi wabhehwelwe, nasio aje dimi, ola engole se vyoma vyakwe, azilola embwa zihwenza na azileha na zishembele.
JOH 10:13 Ne mbwa zikhata na nyampanye. Zishembela afuatanaji oboyi wabhe hwelwe sazisajila engole.
JOH 10:14 Ane endi dimi mwinza embamenye bhabhali bhahuline, wope wamenye ane.
JOH 10:15 Odaada amenye, nane emenye Odaada, nane eufumwa owomi wane hungole.
JOH 10:16 Endi nazyo engole zimo zyasaga zya mwigoma eli ezyo zyope ehwanziwa azilete, zyope zinzahonvwe izu lyane zibheligoma limo no dimi omo.
JOH 10:17 Ene ndiyo maana Odaada angene: Eeufumye owomi wane alafu nantele aweje.
JOH 10:18 Nomo wawega afume huline, ila eufumya nene. Endi waamuzi gwa ufumye na endi waamuzi ogwagwefwe nantele. Endiposheye elajizyo eli afume hwa Daada.”
JOH 10:19 Olwaganyishe lwafuma afume hwa yahudi afuatana na maazu ega.
JOH 10:20 Abhinji bhabho wahaga, “Ali ni pepo ndii na pelusu yenu muhumwonvwa?”
JOH 10:21 Bhamo bhayanga, “Ege semazu gamuntu wali ni pepo. Ipepo ligamwigula amaso ompofu?”
JOH 10:22 Nkashahenza Eshikulukulu Shabhehwe Wakifu hu Yelusalemu.
JOH 10:23 Hwali shipindi shi sasa, oYesu ali ajenda mushibhanza muukumbi wa Sulemani.
JOH 10:24 Ayahudi nkabhazyongola na hubhozye, “Paka ndii waibheha nsebho? nkashe awe we Kilisiti, tibhozye peupe.
JOH 10:25 O Yesu ajile, “Embabhozezye ila semuhweteshela. Embombo zyenzibhomba witawa lya Daada wane, ezyo zihakikisha pamwanya yane.
JOH 10:26 Ata sheshi ahweteshela alenganaje amwe semuli ngole zyane.
JOH 10:27 Engole zyane zihonvwa izu lyane; Enzimenye, zyope zinanza ane.
JOH 10:28 Embapiye owomi wewilawila sebhatega na mwaha, nomo hata weka waibhafyola afume mukhono gwane.
JOH 10:29 Odaada wane, wampiye ebho, yo Gosi ashile bhamwabho bhonti, na nomo hata weka wali no uwezo wa fyole mukhono gwa Daada.
JOH 10:30 Ane no Daada tili hantu hamo.”
JOH 10:31 Bhanyemla amawe aje nkabhapole nantele.
JOH 10:32 O Yesu abhabhozya, “Embalanjile embombo enyinji enyinza afume hwa Daada. Hu mbombo zyalihu kati yezyo zyamuhwanza ampole na mawe?”
JOH 10:33 Ayahudi bhahaga, “Setihupola na mawe hu mbombo yayonti yeli nyinza, ila okufuru awe wo muntu ohwibheha aje oli Ngolobhe.”
JOH 10:34 O Yesu abhabhozya, “Seya handihwe mundajizyo zyenyu, 'Nayanjile, “'Amwe muli mangolobhe'”?”
JOH 10:35 Nkashe abhakwizizye mangolobhe, hwa bhala Izu lya Ngolobhe lya bhenzeye (na Maazu segawezi abudwe),
JOH 10:36 muyanga ahusu ola Odaada afumizye na husontezye munsi, 'Osalanya,' alengane naje nayanjile, 'ane endi Mwana wa Ngolobhe'?
JOH 10:37 “Nkashe sebhomba embombo zya Daada wane, mungaje aneteshele.
JOH 10:38 Ata sheshi, nkashe ezibhomba, ata nkasemuneteshela, zyetesheli embombo aje muwezye amanye na hwelewe aje Odaada ali muhati yane nane muhati ya Daada.”
JOH 10:39 Bhalenga na hu khate oYesu, ahwisogoleye afume mumakhono gabho.
JOH 10:40 O Yesu ahwibhalila hwi syelelye Yordani esehemu hula oYohana hwahozyaga ahwande, ahakhala ohwo.
JOH 10:41 Abhantu abhinji bhahenza hwa Yesu. Bhahendeleye ayanje, “O Yohana lyoli sagabhombile eishara yoyonti, ila enongwa zyonti zyayanjile Yohana ahusu omuntu ono zye yoli.”
JOH 10:42 Abhantu abhinji bhamweteshela oYesu epo.
JOH 11:1 Omuntu omo itawa lyakwe ali yo Lazalo ali bhinu. Afumiye hu Bethania, eshijiji sha Mariamu na odaada wakwe oMasa.
JOH 11:2 Ali yo Mariamu yayola wapeshe Ogosi Amarhamu na hufute amagaga gakwe hwii sisi lyakwe, ola oholo wakwe oLazalo wali bhinu.
JOH 11:3 Ailombo ebha bhatumile oujumbe hwa Yesu na yanje, “Gosi, enya ola wogene abhawa.”
JOH 11:4 O Yesu na honvwa ajile, “Empongo ene se yafwe, ila, baada yeshoye umwamihwe wa Ngolobhe aje Omwana wa Ngolobhe apate amwamihwe ashilile hwenyo empongo.”
JOH 11:5 O Yesu agene oMasa no dada wakwe no Lazalo.
JOH 11:6 Lwa honvwezye aje oLozalo bhinu, oYesu akheye insiku izbhele ashizanye pala pahali.
JOH 11:7 Eshi baada yelyo abhabhozya abhanafunzi bhakwe, “Saali huu Yahudi nantele.”
JOH 11:8 Abhanafunzi bhabhozya, “Mwalimu, Ayahudi bhali bhalenga ahupole na mawe, na aweohonza awele hwohwo nantele?”
JOH 11:9 O Yesu ayanga, “Esala zya pasanya sezili kumi ne zibhele? Omuntu ajenda pasanya sawezizye abomele, afuatanaje alola hulukhozyo lwa pasanya.
JOH 11:10 Ata sheshi nkashe anzajende no siku, anzabomele afuatanaje olukhozyo nalumo muhati yakwe.”
JOH 11:11 O Yesu ayanga enongwa ezi, baada ye nongwa ezi, abhabhozya, “Owamwetu oLazalo agonile, ila embala aje empate ahubhosye afume mutulo.”
JOH 11:12 Abhanafunzi bhabhozya, “Gosi, nkashe agonile, anzabhoshe.
JOH 11:13 Ensiku izyo oYesu ali ayanga ahusu enfwa ya Lazalo, ila abhene bhamenye aje ayanga ahusu agone otulo.
JOH 11:14 O Yesu nkayanga na bhene pazelu pazelu, “O Lazalo afwiye.
JOH 11:15 Lusongwo lwendiinalwo hulimwe aje senahali hula aje mubhe no lweteshelo. Saali hwa mwene.”
JOH 11:16 O Tomaso wa hetwaga Pacha, abhozya abhanafunzi amwabho, “Nate saalitifwe pamo no Yesu.”
JOH 11:17 O Yesu lwa henzaga amweje oLazalo akheye mwilende insiku zine.
JOH 11:18 Yope e Bethania yaali pepe ne Yelusalemu nanshi ekilometa arubaini ne zisanu eshi.
JOH 11:19 Abhinji kati ya Yahudi bhahenzele hwa Masa no Mariamu abhazinde alengane no holo wabho.
JOH 11:20 O Masa ahonvwa aje oYesu ahwenza, abhalile akhomane nawo, ila oMariamu ahendeleye akhale pakhaya.
JOH 11:21 O Masa abhozya oYesu, “Gosi, nkashe ogabhiye epa, okolo wane handa safwiye.
JOH 11:22 Ata sheshehwelewa aje lyalyonti lyobhalabhe afume hwa Ngolobhe, anzahupele.”
JOH 11:23 O Yesu abhozya, okolo waho anzavyoshe nantele.”
JOH 11:24 O Masa abhozya, emenye aje anzavyonshe huu vyoho wi siku lya mwisho.”
JOH 11:25 O Yesu abhozya, “Ane endi luvionsyono womi; omwane waneteshela, ata nkashe aifwa, hata sheshi aibha ahwizya;
JOH 11:26 no mwene wahwizya na netehsele ane saga ifwa. Uhweteshela eli?”
JOH 11:27 Wabhozya aje, “'Sawa, Gosi ehweteshela aje awe oli Kilisiti, Mwana wa Ngolobhe, omwene wa hwenza munsi.”
JOH 11:28 Nahamala ayanje eli, abhalile ahukwizye odada wakwe oMariamu hufaraga. Ajile, “Omwalimu ali epa nantele ahukwizya.”
JOH 11:29 O Mariamu na hovwezye ega, abhoshele nanali na bhale hwa Yesu.
JOH 11:30 Wope oYesu ali sayenzele aliseele muhati ye shijiji, aliseele lwa khomanaga no Masa.
JOH 11:31 Ayahudi bhabhali no Maliamu munyumba na bhala bhabhli wahuzinda, bhabhoshele nanali na afume honze, bhalondoleye; bhamenye aje abhala hwi kaburi aje alile ohwo.
JOH 11:32 O Mariamu, ahafiha pala oYesu palolaga na agwiye pansi pamagaga gakwe na hobhozye, “Gosi, nkashe ogahali epa, oholo wane hande sagaafwiye.”
JOH 11:33 O Yesu nalola alila, na Ayahudi bhahenzele pamo nawo bhali bhalila huu moyo gabho na sebhelele;
JOH 11:34 ajile, “Mugonizye hwii? Bhabhozye, Gosi, enza oyenye.”
JOH 11:35 O Yesu alilile.
JOH 11:36 Ayahudi nkabhayanga, “Oyenye sha gene oLazalo!”
JOH 11:37 Bhamo muhati yabho bhajile, “Sio yayono, omuntu wabhombile amaso gola wali mpofu, sagabhombile ono muntu aje agaje afwe?”
JOH 11:38 O Yesu alilaga humwoyo gwakwe nantele, abhalile hwi lende. Hwali ligwenya, niiwe libhehwele pamwanya lyakwe.
JOH 11:39 O Yesu ajile, “Lyefwi iwe.” O Masa, oilombo wakwe oLazalo, omwene wafwiye, abhozya oYesu, “Gosi, hu muda ogu, obele gubhabhe gu bholile, alenganaje ali fwee ensiku zine.”
JOH 11:40 O Yesu abhozya, “Ane senabhozezye aje, nkashe ohweteshela, obhaulole oumwamu wa Ngolobhe?”
JOH 11:41 Nnkabhalyefwa iwe. O Yesu abhosya amaso gakwe amwanya naje, “Daada, ehusombezya afuatanaje onomvwa.
JOH 11:42 Namenye aje ononvwa omuda gwonti, ila alengane no lubhongano lwalwe meleye anzongole aje enjanjile ega, aje bhapate ahweteshele aje awe ontumile.”
JOH 11:43 Naayanga ega, alilile hwizu igosi, “Lazalo, fuma honze!”
JOH 11:44 Ofwe afumile honze apinyilwe amakhono na magaga husanda zyakhatile, na amaso gakwe apinyilwe ne shitambala.” O Yesu abhabhozya, “Mwigulili muleshele abhalaje.”
JOH 11:45 Oyahudi abhinji bhabhahenzele hwa Mariamu nalole oYesu habhombaga, bhamweteshela;
JOH 11:46 bhamo bhabhalile hwa Mafarisayo na bhabhozye enongwa zyazibhombile oYesu.
JOH 11:47 Agosi bha dimi na Mafarisayo bhabhongene pandwemo mwi baraza na yaanje, “Tibhabhombe yenu? Omuntu ono abhoembombo enyinji.
JOH 11:48 Nkashe tibhahuleshe eshi mwene, bhonti bhanza humweteshe; Alumi bhayenza na hweje vyonti evyetu ni taifa lyetu.”
JOH 11:49 Hata omuntu omuntu muhati yabho, oKayafa, waali dimi Ogosi omwaha ogwo, abhabhozya, “Semumenye hahonti.
JOH 11:50 Sahusebhelela aje ehwanziwa aje omuntu omo afwe esababu ya bhanje ashile itaifa lyonti na litega.”
JOH 11:51 Eege sohagayanjile afuatanaje no mwene, mhati yakwe, ali dimi ogosi omwaha gula, ayanjile aje oYesu aifwa sababu ya bha munsi;
JOH 11:52 na se huje hwabha munsi bhene ila oYesu apate abhabhonganye abhana bha Ngolobhe bhabha nyanpene hutali hutali.
JOH 11:53 Eshi ahwandile isiku elyo na hwendelela bhapanjile ahugoje oYesu.
JOH 11:54 O Yesu sagajendile apazelu pazelu hwa Yahudi, ila asogeye epa na bhale ensi yelipeepe ni poli hunsi yehwetwa Efraimu. Epo akheye nabhanafunzi.
JOH 11:55 Epasaka ya Yahudi yali pepe, na bhinji bhazubhile abhale hu Yelusalemu honze yensi sheli sele ePasaka nkabhahwiyozye bhebho.
JOH 11:56 Bhali bha humwanza oYesu, na ayanje kila muntu na bhali bhemeleye mshibhanza, “Musebha yenu? Aje saga ayenza mushi kulukulu?”
JOH 11:57 Owakati ou ogosi wa dimi na Mafarisayo bhali bhafumizye endajizyo aje nkashe omo aimanya oYesu hwali, ahwanziwa afumye etaarifa aje nkabhapate ahukhate.
JOH 12:1 Isiku ilya sita selisele ePasaka, oYesu abhalile hu Bethania, hwa hali oLazalo, omwene wali avyonshele afume hwa bhafwe.
JOH 12:2 Bhalenganyizya eshalye shana ndabhela owho, no Martha abhombelaga owakati owo oLazaro ahali pamo na bhale bhabhakheye pashalye pandwemo no Yesu.
JOH 12:3 Pamande oMariamu ahege eratli ye manukato gagalenganyiziwe hu nardo enyinza, gagali ne maana engosi, wapaha oYesu mumagaga, na husyomole hwi sisi lyakwe; enyumba yonti yamemile nunsi gwe manukato.
JOH 12:4 O Yuda Iskariote, omo we bhanafunzi bhakwe, ambaye wanzahugalushe oYesu, ajile,
JOH 12:5 “Yenu amanukato ega segagalu ziwanyaga huu mpeya mia zitatu na bhapele apena?”
JOH 12:6 Wope ayanjile ego, sio aje hubhasajile apena, afuatanaje ali mwibha: omwene ali wa bheshe ehela na ali ahwega zimo zyazibhelwe omwo zya mwene yoyo.
JOH 12:7 O Yesu ajile, “Leshi abheshe hali naho alengane ni siku lya syelwe hwane.
JOH 12:8 Apena mwaibha nabho ensiku zyonti ila ane semwaibha nane ensiku zyontii.”
JOH 12:9 Owinji ogosi wa Yahudi bhapete amanye aje oYesu ali ohwo bhopebhenza, sio aje yo Yesu tu ila bhalole no Lazaro ola oYesu wavyonsezye afume hwa bhafwe.
JOH 12:10 Bhope agosi bhayangene aje wagoje oLazaro;
JOH 12:11 alengane no mwale abhinji katika Wayahudi walienda zao bha bhalile ahumweteshela oYesu.
JOH 12:12 Na isiku ila bhele uwinji gosi wali hushikulukulu bhahonvwezye aje oYesu ahwenza hu Yelusalemu,
JOH 12:13 bhahejile amasamba ge mikwige mitende na afume hoze na abhale ahumwejelele na bhakhomile ekelele, “Hosana! Asailwe wahwenza hwitawa lya Gosi, Omwene we Israeli.”
JOH 12:14 O Yesu ayeje enyana-ye punda ayipandale; nanshi shila shehandihwe,
JOH 12:15 “Oganje ahwogope, lendu Sayuni; enya, Omwene waho ahwenza, apende enyana-ye punda.”
JOH 12:16 Abhanafunzi bhakwe sebhagelee amambo ega epo ahwande; ila oYesu na mwamihwe, nkabhakomboha aje amambo ega gahandihwe na huje abhombile amambo ega hwa mwene.
JOH 12:17 Lila ikundi lyalya pandwemo no Yesu lula lwa kwizyaga oLazaro afume mwilende, bhahakikisya hwabhanje.
JOH 12:18 Yali alengane neshi aje uwinji wa bhantu bhabhalile ahuposhele alenganaje bhahomvwezye aje abhombole embo eyo.
JOH 12:19 Amafarisayo bhakwepelana bhene hwa bhene, “Enya, esalezi semuwezizey abhombe lya lyonti; enya, ensi ebhalile hwa mwene.”
JOH 12:20 Bhamo Ayunani bhali pandwemo na bhala bhabhalile apute hushikulukulu.
JOH 12:21 Ebhabhaliye oFilipo, wafumile Betsaida ye Galilaya, bhalabha bhaga, “Gosi, ate tiziliha ahulole oYesu.”
JOH 12:22 O Filipo ahabhala abhozya o Andrea; Andrea no Filipo bhabha ahubhozye oYesu.
JOH 12:23 O Yesu ayanga ahaga, “Esala efishile hwa Mwana wa Adamu amwamihwe.
JOH 12:24 Etesheli, etesheli, embabhozya, abhenyu he ngano nkase hagwiye pansi hafwa, hakhala shesho hene; ila nkahafwa, hana pape endondo zinyinji.
JOH 12:25 Omwane wasongwa owomi wakwe anzautezye; ila ola wauvitwa owomi wakwe munsi omu anzaugolosye hata womi wewila wila.
JOH 12:26 Omuntu wawonti wanza ambombele ane, andondolelaje; nane pehwendi omuntu wane paibha. Omuntu wawonti wabhombela ane anzanogope.
JOH 12:27 Esalezi omwoyo gwane guhwalangana: nane enje bhole? 'Odaada, anfyozye esala ene'? Ndio maana enjifishiye esala ene.
JOH 12:28 Odaada, alimwamishe itawa lyaho.” Izu ilinza afume humwanya na huje, “Endimwamisha nantele embali mwamishe nantele.”
JOH 12:29 Olubhongano lwalwahemeleye peepe nawo bhahonvwa, bhayanga aje huli omungurumo. Bhamo bhajile, “Ohalo ozelu ayanjile nawo.”
JOH 12:30 O Yesu abhabhoyza naje, “Izu ili selya henzele huline, ila hwalimwe.
JOH 12:31 Esalezi oulonje wensi ene ehweli: Esalezi ogosi wensi aitagwa honze.
JOH 12:32 Nane nkemwamihwe munsi, embarute bhonti huline.”
JOH 12:33 Wayanjile ego abhonesyaga aje enfwa bhole ya mwaifwa.
JOH 12:34 Olubhongano lwaga, “Ate tonvwezye hundajizyo aje oKillisiti aibha wilawila. Awe oiga bhole, 'Omwana wa Adamu amwamihwe pamwanya'? Ono Omwana wa Muntu wenu?”
JOH 12:35 O Yesu abhabhozya, “Olukhozyo luhweli pandwemo namwe omuda ododo. Bhalaji afuatane naje mlinalyo olukhozyo, aje enkisi nkepotwe aitole. Omwene wabhala munkisi samenye hwabhala.
JOH 12:36 Muli nalwo olukhozyo, lweteshelaji olukhozyo olwo nkamubhe bhana bhelukhozyo.” O Yesu ayanjile ega ahwisogolela ahobha bha salole.
JOH 12:37 Japo oYesu abhombile eishara nyinji witazi lyabho, ila sebha mwetesheye
JOH 12:38 lifishe izu lya kuwaa oIsaya, lyayanjile: “Gosi, wenu waizyeteshela enongwa zyetu? Okhono gwa Gosi gwiguliwe wenu?”
JOH 12:39 Ndio maana abhene sebhahetesheye, alengane naje oIsaya ayanjile nantele,
JOH 12:40 “Abhadiye amaso, na agabheshele makhome amoyo gabho, bhageteha engabhaponia.”
JOH 12:41 O Isaya ayanjile enongwa ezi afuatanaje alolile oumwamu wa Yesu na ayanjile enongwa zyakwe.
JOH 12:42 Ila, hata bhagosi abhinji bhamweteshe oYesu; ila alengane na Mafarisayo, sebhaheteha bhahogope atengwe msibhanza.
JOH 12:43 Bhasongwelwe ahwilole hwa bhantu ahwilole ahwilole hwa Ngolobhe.
JOH 12:44 O Yesu afumizye izu lyakwe naje, “Omwene waneteshela ane, saneteshela nene wene ila nola wantumile ane,
JOH 12:45 omwane wambonela ane ahubho ane ahubhonela yayola wantumile.
JOH 12:46 Ane nahenzele nanshi olukhozyo munsi aje shila muntu waneteshela aganje akhale munkisi.
JOH 12:47 Nkashe omuntu wawonti anzahonvwe amazu gane sagakhata, ane sehulonga; afuatanaje sagahenzele ailonje insi ila injifyole insi.
JOH 12:48 Omwene wananza ane nkasage teha amazu gane, ali nawo wahulonga: izu ilyo lyenjenjile lyalyaihulonga isiku lya mwisho.
JOH 12:49 Afwanaje ane senayanjile hunafsi yane. Ila yo Daada wantumile, omwene yoyo andajizizye lye mbalombelele na yanje.
JOH 12:50 Ane emenye aje endajizyo zyakwe zye womi wewilawila; ila ego gelombelela ane - nanshi Odaada shambozezye, shashesho shelombelela hwa bhene.”
JOH 13:1 Isalezi seliseele eshikulukulu ye pasaka, afuatanaje oYesu amenye aje esala ya efishile eyaje aifuma munsi omo abhale hwa daada, endwemo abhagene abhantu bhakwe bhabhali munsi, abhagene oupeo.
JOH 13:2 Osetano abhehwelwe haani humwoyo gwa Yuda Iskariote, omwana wa simoni, ahushitushile oYesu.
JOH 13:3 O Yesu amenye aje odaada abheshele evintu humakhono gakwe naje afumile hwa Ngolobhe nantele ali abhala hwa Ngolobhe.
JOH 13:4 Abhoshele pashalye na ahalile pansi omwenda gwa honze. Ahejile itaulo ahwifunjile yoyo.
JOH 13:5 Nkahaponya amenze mumbakuri na wanda abhozye amagaga abhanafunzi bhakwe na bhapugute ni taulo lya hwifunjile yoyo.
JOH 13:6 Ahenza hwa Petro, na oPetro ahabhozya, “Gosi, uhwanza anazye amagaga gane?”
JOH 13:7 O Yesu ayanga na hubhozye, “Lyebhomba solimenye esalezi ila eshi obhahwelewe pamande.”
JOH 13:8 O Petro abhozya, “Sobhanozye amagaga gane na mwaha.” O Yesu ajile, “Nkashe sembahumwezye sobhabhe ne sehemu pandwemo nane.”
JOH 13:9 O Simoni Petro abhozya, “Gosi, onganjenozye amagaga gane wene, ila namakhono ni twe lyane.”
JOH 13:10 O Yesu abhozya, “Wawonti wayojile sahwanziwa ahwoje ila amagaga gakwe, nahuje mwinza obele gwakwe gwonti; amwe muli bhinza, ila se mwenti.”
JOH 13:11 O Yesu amenye ola wanzahugalushile; ndio maana ajile, semwenti mli bhinza.”
JOH 13:12 O Yesu lwali abhozizye amagaga gabho na wega omwenda gwakwe na khale nantele, abhabhozya, “Aje Muhwelewa hale hembabhombela?
JOH 13:13 Mukwizya ane “Mwalimu” nantele myiga Gosi ene yoli, afuatanaje endi shesho.
