JOH 13:14 Nkashe ane ne Gosi ne mwalimu, embozizye amagaga genyu, amwe namwe ehwanziwa abhozye amwenyu amagaga.
JOH 13:15 Embapiye ofwana aje amwe mubhombe nanshi ane zyanabhombile hulimwe.
JOH 13:16 Etesheli, Etesheli, embabhozya, oboyio segosi ashile ogosi wakwe; wala yule ambaye ametumwa ni mkuu kuliko yule aliye mtuma.
JOH 13:17 Nkashe ozimenye enongwa ezi osaiwaje nkobhazibhombe.
JOH 13:18 Seyanga aje amwe mwenti, afuatanaje embamenye bhala bhembachaguye - eyanga ezi ili aje amazu gawezye akamilishe: 'Omwene walya ibumunda lyane ambasesezye ikhaata lyakwe.'
JOH 13:19 Embabhozya izii esalezi shalilisele afume aje nkalyaifumila, mwawezye ahweteshele aje ane NENE.
JOH 13:20 “Etesheli, etesheli, embabhozya, wamposhela ane ahuposhela yayola wantumile mimi.”
JOH 13:21 O Yesu lwa yangaga ega, ayanzihwe hu mwoyo, ahakikisizye na yanje, “Etesheli, etesheli, embabhozya aje omo wenyu aingaluha.”
JOH 13:22 Abhanafunzi bhakwe bha henyanya, bhahuswiga aje wenu wahuyanga.
JOH 13:23 Hwali ne meza, omo we bhanafunzi bhakwe ahagamiye musifubha mwa Yesu ola oYesu wagene.
JOH 13:24 O Simoni oPetro abhozezye omwanafunzi ono na huje, “Tibho wenu wahuyanga.”
JOH 13:25 Omwanafunzi ola wahagamiye mshifubha mwa Yesu na hubhozye, “Gosi, yonanu?”
JOH 13:26 O Yesu ajile, “Wemba tobhezye ishipande shi bumunda na hhupele.” Shesho nali atobhezezye ibumunda, apiye oYuda omwana wa Simoni Iskariote.
JOH 13:27 Baada yi bumunda, Osetano amwinyiye. O Yesu ahabhozya, “Haala howanza abhombe habhombe nanali.”
JOH 13:28 Nomo omuntu pameza wamenye emaana ya Yesu ayanje enongwa ezi hwa mwahale.
JOH 13:29 Bhamo bhasebhele aje afuatanaje oYuda ekhete ifuko lye mpeya, oYesu abhozya, “Kala evintu vyatihwanza vye shikulukulu,” au aje ahwanziwa afumye evintu hwa peena.
JOH 13:30 O Yuda na hejelela ibumunda, ahafuma honze nanali; hwali sikuu.
JOH 13:31 O Yuda lwali asogoye, oYesu ayanjile, “Eshi omwana wa Adamu amwamihwe, no Ngolobhe amwamihwe hwa mwehale.
JOH 13:32 Ongolobhe anzahumwamishe hwa mwene yoyo, na anza humwamishe nanali.
JOH 13:33 Bhana mwadodo, ehwendi pamo namwe omuda dodo. Mubhananze, nkashe shanabhabhozizye Ayahudi, 'Hwembala, semuwezizye ahwenze.' esalaze embabhozya amwe, nantele.
JOH 13:34 Embapiye endizyo empya, aje mganane nanshi ane shehabhagene amwe, shesho shesho namwe ehwanziwa aganane mwemwe hu mwemwe.
JOH 13:35 Afuatanaje neli awantu bhanzamanye aje amwe muli bhanafunzi bhane, nkashe muli no lugano shila omo no wamwabho.”
JOH 13:36 O Simoni Petro abhozezye, “Gosi, ubhala hwii?” O Yesu ayanga, “Apantu pe haibhala esalezi sobhawezye anfuate, ila obhananze pamande.
JOH 13:37 O Petro abhozya, “Gosi, yenu ensafuate hata salezi? Ane embafumwe olwizyo lyane huliwe.”
JOH 13:38 O Yesu ajile, “Aje obhafumwe olwizyo shauli ya huline? Etesheli etesheli ehubhozya, ehanda sebhakuje bila haana mara hatatu.”
JOH 14:1 Oganje aguleshe omwoyo gwaho abhe ahwalangane. Ohumweteshela Ongolobhe neteshele nane.
JOH 14:2 Mu nyumba ya Daada wane muli mabhombo minji agakhale; nkashe semugali esho hande ebhozezye, afuatanaje embala abhalenganyizye apakhale awe.
JOH 14:3 Nkashe embale nabhalenganyizye nayenza nantele abhakaribizye hwa line, aje pendi ane namwe mubhanje.
JOH 14:4 Mumenye idala hwembala.”
JOH 14:5 O Tomaso abhozezye oYesu, “Gosi, setimenye hwobhala; Aje! Tibhalimanye bhole idala?
JOH 14:6 O Yesu abhozezye, “Ane endili dala, lyoli, no womi; nomo wagenza hwa Daada ila ashilile huline.
JOH 14:7 Nkashe mugamenye ane, handamumenye no Daada wane nantele; ahwande esalezi na hwendelele muhamanya na mulolile omwane.”
JOH 14:8 O Philipo abhozya oYesu, “Gosi, tilanje Odaada, esho shibhabhe shitiyiye.”
JOH 14:9 O Yesu abhozya, “Sendi pandwemo namwe hu muda otali, no oliseele somenye ane, Philipo? Wawonti wandolile ane alolile Odaada; shili bhole oyanga, 'Tilanje Odaada'?
JOH 14:10 Semuhweteshela aje ane endi muhati ya Daada, oDaada ali muhati yane? Amazu geyanga hulimwe seyanga kulengana nane nene; baadala yakwe, Odaada wa hwizya mhati yane abhomba embombo yakwe.
JOH 14:11 Neteshele ane, aje ehwendi muhati ya Daada, no Daada ahweli mhati yane; shesho neteshe ane afutane nembombo zyane eshi.
JOH 14:12 Etesheli, etesheli, embabhozya, omwane waneteshela, ane embombo zila zyebhomba, aibhomba embombo ezyo wope nantele na aibhomba hata embombo engosi afuatanaje embala hwa Daada.
JOH 14:13 Hahonti hamulabha hwitawa lyane, embabhombe aje Odaada nkamwamihwe hwa Mwana.
JOH 14:14 Nkashe mulabhe ahantu hahonti hwi tawa lyane, eho embabhombe.
JOH 14:15 Nkashe mubhangane, mubhazighate endajizyo zyane.
JOH 14:16 Nane embahulabhe Odaada, Wope anzabhapele omwavwi wamwabho aje abhe pandwemo namwe wilawila,
JOH 14:17 Ompempo we lyoli. Ensi sewezizye ahuposhele omwane afuatana naje seuhulola, au humemwe omwene, ata sheshi amwe mumenyo omene, afuatane na aibha muhati yenyu.
JOH 14:18 Senaibhaleha mubhene; Naiwela hulimwe.
JOH 14:19 Hu nsiku endodo, ensi seyayindola nantele, ila amwe mundola. Afuatane naje ahwizya namwe mwaizya nantele.
JOH 14:20 Hwi siku elyo mwaimanya aje ane ehwendi muhati ya Daada, naje amwe muli muhati yane, naje ane endi muhati yenyu.
JOH 14:21 Wawonti wakhata endajizyo na zibhombe, yayola omo wangene ene na wangene ane; na wangene ane aiganwa no Daada wane, naihugana na naihwibhonesya ane nene hwa mwene.”
JOH 14:22 O Yuda (siyo Iskariote) abhozya oYesu, “Gosi, Aje! Yenu yebha fumile aje obhahwibhonesye wewe?
JOH 14:23 O Yesu ayanjile ajile, “Nkashe wawonti wangene, abhakhate izu lyane. Odaada wane anza hugane, na tibhahwenze hwa mwene na tibhabheshe okhalo gwetu pandwemo no mwahale.
JOH 14:24 Wawonti wasangene ane, sakhata amuzu gane. Izu lya mhonvwa se lya line ila Daada wantumile.
JOH 14:25 Enjanjile enongwa ezi hwalimwe, omuda gwe hwizya pandwemo namwe.
JOH 14:26 Ata sheshi, Mfariji, Ompepo Ofinjile, lyane Odaada aihutuma hwitawa lyane, aibhasambelezya enongwa zyonti na aibhabheha aje mkoboshe gonti gehayanjile hulimwe.
JOH 14:27 Olusongwo embapele olusongwo lwane amwe. Sembapele na ensi sepela. Muganje abheshe amoyo genyu abhe no walangano, no bhonga.
JOH 14:28 Mwahonvwezye shila shehabhabhozezye, esogola nantele naiwela hulimwe.' Nkashe mugangene ane, mwenzabhe no losongwo afuatanaje embala hwa Daada, afuatanaje Odaada gosi ashile ane.
JOH 14:29 Esalezi yanje namwe amazu gaminji, afuatanaje ogosi wensi ene ahwenza omwene saali ne nguvu pamwanya yane.
JOH 14:30 Sembayanje namwe amazu gaminji, afuatanaje ogosi wensi ene ahwenza omwene saali ne nguvu pamwanya yane,
JOH 14:31 aje ensi epate amanye aje egene Odaada, ehomba hala Odaada handajizya ane, nanshi shila shampiye endajizyo. Bhoshi, tifume apantu epa.
JOH 15:1 Ane endi mzabibu ogu gwe lyoli, odaada wane omwene mkulima we mzabibu.
JOH 15:2 Isamba lya salipapa endondo, elyefwa ila isamba lya lipapa endondo alyefwa ili aje nkali papaje tee.
JOH 15:3 Amwe muli bhinza alengane ne nongwa yembabhozezye.
JOH 15:4 Mukhale muhati yane na muhati yenyu. Nanshi isamba seligapapa lyene nkaselili mumuzabibu, shesho namwe, nkase mukhala muhati yane.
JOH 15:5 Ane endi mzabibu; amwe muli nsamba. Wakhala muhati yane nane muhati yakwe, omuntu ono apapa endondo zinyinji, afuatanaje bila ane amwe simuwezizye abhombe embombo yayonti.
JOH 15:6 Nkashe omuntu wawonti wasaga abhakhale muhati yane, abhatagwe nanshi osamba na hwome; abhantu bhabhonganya amasamba na agataje humwoto, na galongolela.
JOH 15:7 Nkashe mubhakhale muhati yane, na nkashe amazu gane ganzakhale muhati yenyu, labhaji lyalyonti lya mubhahwanze, namwe mubhabhombelwe.
JOH 15:8 Hweli odaada amwamihwe, naje mupapa endondo zinyinji naje bhanafunzi bhane.
JOH 15:9 Nkashe odaada wane shangene ane, ane nane embagene amwe, khalaji mulugano lwane.
JOH 15:10 Nkashe mubhakhate endajizyo zyane, mubhakhale mulugano lwane nashi shehete endajizyo yza daada wane na khale mulugano lwakwe.
JOH 15:11 Enjanjile enongwa ezi hulimwe aje olusongwo lwane lubhe muhati yenyu na aje olusongwo lwenyu lubhombeshe abhe golusu.
JOH 15:12 Olu lulajizyo lwane aje mganane amwe hu mwemwe nanshi sembagene amwe.
JOH 15:13 Nomo omuntu waali nolugano ogosi ashile ou aje afumwe olwizo lwakwe eshauli ya bhanje.
JOH 15:14 Amwe muli bha mwetu nkamubhabhombe gala gembalajizya.
JOH 15:15 Sembakwizyabhaboyi, afuatanaje oboyi samanya kila habhomba ogosi wakwe. Embakwizya amwe bhamwetu, alenganaje embabhozezye enongwa zyonti zyenonvwezye afume hwa Daada.
JOH 15:16 Semwansaluye ane ila ane nabhasaluye amwe na bhabheshe aje mubhalaje apape endondo, na endondo zyenyu zipate akhale. Eli lili eshi aje hahonti hamulabha hwa Daada hwi tawa lyane, anzabhapele.
JOH 15:17 Enongwa ezi embalajizya aje mganane shila muntu nowamwabho.
JOH 15:18 Nkashe ensi enzabhavitwe, mumanye aje ebhanvitwe nene sheli seele abhavitwe amwe.
JOH 15:19 Nkashe mugali bha munsi, ensi handa ebhagene nanshi bha mwabho; Afuatanaje amwe semuli bha munsi na afwatanaje senabhachaguye afume munsi, afuatane neshi insi ebhavitwa.
JOH 15:20 Komboshi izu lyana bhabhozezye, 'Oboyi se gosi ashile ogosi wakwe.' Nkashe bhanjenvezye ane, bhaibhaye nvya lyane, handabhakhete iklyalimwe lyape.
JOH 15:21 Bhaibhabhombela amambo ega gonti alengane ni tawa lyane alengane sebhamenye ola wantumile.
JOH 15:22 Nkashe engalisenenzele na bhabhozye handasabhabhombile embibhi, ila esalezi sebhali noudhuru hu mbibhi zyabho.
JOH 15:23 Wanvwitwa ane ahuvitwa yo Daada nantele.
JOH 15:24 Nkashe sembombile embombo muhati yabho enganomo omo wabho waibhombile, handasebhali ne mbibhi; ila esalezi wabhombile gonti gabhele bhalolile na bhvitilwe ane no Daada wane.
JOH 15:25 Ene efumila aje izu likamilishe lyalyandihwe mundajizyo: 'Zyabhowanvitwa ane bila li kosa.'
JOH 15:26 Wazinda ayenzele, wembahufume hulimwe afume hwa Daada, ono yayono, Ompepo we lyoli, wafuma hwa Daada, aihakikisizya.
JOH 15:27 Amwe mhakikisizya afuatanaje muuli pandwemo nane afume ahwande.
JOH 16:1 Embabhozya enongwa ezi aje mganje avisye.
JOH 16:2 Bhaibhafumya mwonze mumabhanza; lyoli esala ehwenza shila waibhabuda aisebha aje abhomba mbombo enyinza hwa Ngolobhe.
JOH 16:3 Bhaibhabhomba enongwa ezi alengane sebhamanye Odaada wala sebhamenye ane.
JOH 16:4 Embabhozezye enongwa ezi aje ensiku nkazyafiha zyafumile mwaiwezya agakomboshe na shila shanabhabhozezye muwezye bhene. Sembhabhozezye alengane ne nongwa ezi ahwande huwandilo alenganaje nali pandwemo namwe.
JOH 16:5 Japo esalezi, embala hwola wantumile; ia nomo omo wenyu wambozezya, “Obhala hwii?”
JOH 16:6 Alengane enjanjile enongwa ezi hulimwe, ozungumizu umemile muoyo genyu.
JOH 16:7 Ata shesho, embabhozya elyoli: shinza hulemwe nkanasogola; afuatanaje wabhazinzya sagayenza hulimwe; ila nkanabhala naihutuma hulimwe.
JOH 16:8 Nkawenza oyo wabhazinzya aiyomezya ensi ahusiane ne mbibhi, ahusiane ne lyoli na ahusiane nolonzi.
JOH 16:9 Ahusiane ne mbibhi, alenganaje sebhaneteshe ane,
JOH 16:10 ahusiane ne lyoli, afuatanaje embala hwa Daada na semwaindola nantele;
JOH 16:11 ahusiane no lonzi alenganaje ogosi we nsi ene alongwilwe.
JOH 16:12 Endinago minji gabhabhozye, ila semubhagelewe esalezi.
JOH 16:13 Ila, omwene, Ompepo welyoli, nkawenza aibhalongozya mulyoli yonti; afuatanaje sagaiyanga hu sababu yakwe yoyo; ila wawonti ganzagonvwe anzagayanje amambo ego; na aigabhonesya hulimwe amambo gagayenza.
JOH 16:14 Omwene aimwamiha ane, alenganaje aigayanga mambo gane na agatangazye hulimwe.
JOH 16:15 Evintu vyonti vyalinavyo oDaada vyaline; eshi eshi, enjanjile aje Ompepo ayaga amambo gane na gabhonesye hulimwe.
JOH 16:16 Bado ensiku ndodo, semwaindola nantele; baada ye muda ododo nantele, mwaindola.”
JOH 16:17 Bhamo awanafunzi bhakwe bhabhozanya, “Ye yenu yatibhozya, “omuda ododo, na semwaindola nantele,' no omuda ododo nantele,' mwaindola,' alengane embale hwa Daada?”
JOH 16:18 Eshi eshi bhayanga, “Hantu nshi hayanga, 'Bado omuda odod'? Setimenye zyayanga.”
JOH 16:19 O Yesu alolile aje wazilishe ahubhozezye, wope ayanga, “Muhubhozezya mubhene ahusu eli, shenjanjile, 'Bado omuda ododo, semwaindola nantele; baada ye muda ododo mwaindola'?
JOH 16:20 Etesheli, etesheli, embabhozya, mwalila na hwilombozye, ila ensi yayisongwa, mwazugumile, ila ensi enzugumila yenyu yaigaluha lusongwo.
JOH 16:21 Oshe abhazugumizu lula lwa bhano uchungu alengane naje omuda gwa pape gufishile; ila nkawa papa omwana, sakomboha nantele ambabha, afuatanaje no lusongwo lwakwe aje omwana apepwe munsi.
JOH 16:22 Amwe nantele muzugumiye esalezi, ila naibhalola nantele; na moyo genyu gaisongwa na nomo waiwezye abhefwezye olusongwo lwenyu.
JOH 16:23 Isiku elyo semwaimbozya enongwa. Etesheli, etesheli, Embabhozya nkamulabhe lyalyonti hwa Daada, aibhapela hwi tawa lyane.
JOH 16:24 Paka semulabhile lyalyonti witawa lyane; labhaji mubhaposhele aje olusongwo lwenyu lukamilishe.
JOH 16:25 Enyanjile namwe hunjango yasemanyiha, ila esala ehwenza senaiyanga hujango yasemanyiha baada yesho naibhabhoyza papa zelu ahusu Odaada.
JOH 16:26 Isiku elyo mwailabha hwitawa lyane, sembabhozya aje nailabha hwa Daada husababu yenyu;
JOH 16:27 Afuatanaje Odaada yoyo abhagene alenga mungene ane na afuatanaje muneteshe aje enfumile hwa Daada.
JOH 16:28 Nafumile hwa Daada na enenzele munsii; nantele, esogola munsi na embala hwa Daada”.
JOH 16:29 Abhanafunzi bhakwe bhabhozya, “Oloola, esalezi oyanga papazelu na sotumila amalibho.
JOH 16:30 Esalezi, timenye aje amenye amambo gonti, na sohwanza omuntu wawonti abhozezye enongwa. Afutanaje tihweteshela aje ofuma hwa Ngolobhe.
JOH 16:31 O Yesu ajile, “Esalezi eneteshe?”
JOH 16:32 Enya, esala ehwenza, yoli nalyoli ifishile, mwainuha kila muntu amwabho mwaindeha nene. Ila sendi nemwene afuatanaje oDaada ahweli nane.
JOH 16:33 Embabhozya amambo ega aje muhati yane mubhe na songwe. Munsi muli amashida, ila hwipeli omwoyo, enjitolile ensi.
JOH 17:1 O Yesu ayanjile amambo ega; nantele abhozya amaso gakwe ahwenyelezye amwanya na yanje, “Daada, esala efishile; mwamishe omwana waho ili omwana wope nkamwamishe awe -
JOH 17:2 nashi shila shopiye enguvu huu vyonti vyavili nobele aje abhapele owomi wewilawila bhonti wopiye.
JOH 17:3 Ou wowomi wewilawila: aje bhamanye awe, Ongolobhe we lyoli na woli humwene, nolo wotumile, oYesu Kilisti.
JOH 17:4 Namwamishe epa pansi, naimalezye embombo yohampiye aje enjibhombe.
JOH 17:5 Esalaezi, Daada, omwamishe ane pamoja nawe wewe huumihwe uula wendi nowo pandwemo nawe sheti seele abhombwe ensi.
JOH 17:6 Nalikwinkuye itawa lyaho hwa bhantu bhompiye epa pansi. Bhali bhantu bhaho; ila wampiye ane. na bhope bhalikhete izu lyaho.
JOH 17:7 Esalezi ohwelewa aje shila hantu hompiye ane hafumile huliwe,
JOH 17:8 hu mazu gala gompiye ane— Embapelile abhahale amazu ego. Wagejeleye nantele na wamanya aje ane enfumile huliwe, na bheteshela aje awe wontumile.
JOH 17:9 Embaputila abhahale. Senjiputila ensi ila bhala bhompiye afuatanaje abhahale wahuliwe.
JOH 17:10 Evintu vyonti evyahuline vyahuliwe na vila vyolinavyo vyahuline nane emwamihwa hwevyo.
JOH 17:11 Ane sehwendi nantele munsi, ila bhahale bhahweli munsi, nane esalezi ehwenza huliwe. Daada Wozelu, omwoyo obhasonje hwi tawa lyaho lila bhabhe nolwonvano nanshi shila ane nawe shatili no lwonvwano.
JOH 17:12 Nanali nabho, nabhasonjele hwitawa lyompiye; Nawasonjele, na nomo mhati yabho watejile ila omwana otezu, amazu nkagatimile.
JOH 17:13 Esalezi ehwenza huliwe; ila eyanga ega munsi aje olusongwo lwane lugoloshe muhati yabho bhebho.
JOH 17:14 Embapiye izu lyaho; embavitilwe aje abhene sebha munsi, nanshishi ane shasendi wa munsi.
JOH 17:15 Sembaputila aje obhefwe munsi ila obhasonje nola obhibhi.
JOH 17:16 Abhene sebhamunsi nanshi shila ane shasenali wa munsi.
JOH 17:17 Ubhabheshe bhagolosu huliwe wewe mu lyoli; izu lyahaho ye lyoli.
JOH 17:18 Wantunile munsi, naane embafumile munsi.
JOH 17:19 Alengane nabhene ane neene ehwifumya huliwe aje wope nkabhahwifumyaje huliwe hwela elyoli.
JOH 17:20 Sio aje ebha bhene bhembaputila na bhala bhabha yeteshela ishilile izu lyaho
JOH 17:21 aje bhope ebho bhabhe no lwonvwano nanshi shila awe Daada, sholi muhati yane nane muhati yaho. Embaputila aje abhene bhawezye abhe muhati yetu ili ensi nkeyeteshele aje awe wontumile.
JOH 17:22 Omwamihwe ula wompiye ane - nane embapiye abhehali, aje bhawezye abhe no lwonvwano nanshile ate shatili no lwonvwano -
JOH 17:23 Ane muhati yabho wope muhati yane, aje nkabhawezye akamilisiwe huu, aje ensi nkemanye aje yooli awe wontumile, na abhagane, nanshi shila awe shongene, ane.
JOH 17:24 Daada hala hompiye ane - Eziliha aje abhene wope bhawezye abhe pandwemo nane apantu pehwendi wawezye alole oummwamihwe wane, ula wompiye: afuatanaje awe ohangane ane shagelisele misingi gensi.
JOH 17:25 Daada welyoli, ensi seyamenye awe, ila ane namenye awe; na bhamenye aje ohantumile.
JOH 17:26 Nabhashele aje itawa lyaho limanyishe hwa bhene, embalibheshe limanyishe aje olwonvwano olwo lwo hangene ane luwezye abhe muhati yabho, nane embezye abhe muhati yabho.”
JOH 18:1 O Yesu nayanga enongwa ezi, asogoye na bhanafunzi bhakwe ahwenyezye entebha ye Kidron, hwa hwali ne bustani, huula omwene na bhanafunzi bhakwe bhahinjila muhati yakwe.
JOH 18:2 Esheshi ola oYuda, wahanzaga ahugalushe, wope aimenye eshemu eyo, afuatanaje oYesu abhalaga husehemu ela mara hahinji abhalaga na bhanafunzi bhakwe.
JOH 18:3 Wope oYuda, nawapata ikundi lya sikari na maofisa afume hwa gosi adimi bhahenza ne tala, ikurunzi ne silaha.
JOH 18:4 Wope oYesu, ohu amenye shila hantu hahali habhombeha zaidi yakwe ahwifumizye hwitazi na abhabhozya, “Wenu wamuhumwanza?”
JOH 18:5 Wope wajile, oYesu Mnazareti.” O Yesu abhabhozya, “Ane nene” Wope oYuda wagalushe oYesu ahali ayemeleye na asikari bhala.
JOH 18:6 Eshi eshi embabhozya, “Ane nene” bhawela shingunga bhagwa pansi.
JOH 18:7 Wabhabhozya nantele, “Wenu wa muhumwanza? Bhope waga nantele “oYesu Munazareti.”
JOH 18:8 O Yesu wabhobhozya, “Embabhozezye aje ana nene; eshi nkashe munaanza ane, bhaleshi ebha abhnje bhabhalaje.”
JOH 18:9 Ega gali esho aje lila izu likamilishe; pala nayangaga; hwa bhala bhohampiye, senatezizye hata weka.”
JOH 18:10 O Simoni Petro, waali ni panga, wega nahudumule ikutu lya hundeelo oboyi wa Dimi ogosi. Ni tawa lyakwe oboyi ola ali yo Malko.
JOH 18:11 O Yesu abhozya oPetro, “Wezya ipanga lyaho hu ala yakwe. Yenu ensamwelee eshikombe shila shampiye oDaada?”
JOH 18:12 Eshi lila ikundi lya skari na jemedari, na boyi bha Yahudi, bhakhata oYesu na hupinye.
JOH 18:13 Wope walongola nasoti pa hwa Anasi, amwane ali khoi wa Kayaafa, ola wali wa Dimi ogosi omwaha ogwo.
JOH 18:14 O Kayafa wabhapiye oushauri Ayahudi yahanziwaga aje omuntu omo afwe husababu ya bhantu.
JOH 18:15 O Simoni oPetro alondoleye oYesu, na shesho omwanafunzi wamwabho. Nola omwanafunzi ali afamahamiha hwa dimi ogosi, wope ahinjila pandwemo no Yesu mwibehewa ilya Chungaji ogosi;
JOH 18:16 o Petro ali ayemeleye honze hu ndiango. Ola omwanafunzi wa manyishe hwa dimi ogosi, afumile honze abhala ayanje nola oshe oboyi waalindaga ondiango na humwinjizye oPetro.
JOH 18:17 Ola oboyi walindaga ondiango, abhozezye oPetro, “Aje awe solo pandwemo na bhantu bha muntu ono?” Wope ajile, “Ane wenje.”
JOH 18:18 Na bhala aboyi bha gosi bhahemeleye apantu pala; bhapembile omwoto afuatanaje hwali isasa, na shesho bhali bhahwota omwoto aje apate ilyoto. Wope oPetro ali nabho, ahwote omwoto ali ayemeleye.
JOH 18:19 Odimi ogosi abhozezye oYesu ahusu abhanafunzi bhakwe ne nsambelezyo zyakwe.
JOH 18:20 O Yesu ajile, “Enjebho zyezye pazelu ensi; Ane na sambelezezye wilawila mshibhanza na pantu pala Ayahudi pabhabhonganaga. Nane senayanjile lyalyonti.
JOH 18:21 Yenu mwabhozezyaga? Bhabhozyaji ahusu hala hanayanjile. Ebha abhantu bhamenye amambo gananjile.
JOH 18:22 O Yesu nahayanga ezyo, omo wa gosi ali ayemeleye wa khoma oYesu hu khono ogwakwe na pamande waga, “Esho, shashi hwanziwa ahugamule odimi ogosi?”
JOH 18:23 Wope oYesu ajile, “Nkashe enjanjile enongwa zyazyonti embibhi obhe keti hwego amabhibhi, na nkashe egomoye shinza yenu ekhomwa?
JOH 18:24 O Anasi atwala oYesu hwa Kayafa hwa chungaji ogosi ali afungulwe.
JOH 18:25 O Simoni oPetro ali ayemeleye wahwikosya ilyoto yoyo. Bhala abhantu bhabhozya. “Aje, awe nawe soli pandwemo na bhanafunzi bhakwe?” Wakhana waga, “Ane weenje.”
JOH 18:26 Omo omo waboyi bhachungaji ogosi, waali holo wa lume waadulwe ikutu, ajile, “Se wewe elolile hula hu bustani?”
JOH 18:27 O Petro akhana nantele, na Ehanda ahekuga.
JOH 18:28 Bhahamwega oYesu afume hwa Kayafa paka hu Praitorio. Hwali shapwiti na mazansha. Abhene bhebho sebhahinjiye ePraitorio bhasiye ahwiyonvwe ailye epasaka.
JOH 18:29 O Pilato abhabhalilia ahayanga. “Ahaga listako bhole lyalihuhusu omuntu ono?”
JOH 18:30 Bhayanga na hubhozye, “Nkashe ono muntu agalisebhomba mbibhi, handa setiletile huliwe.”
JOH 18:31 O Pilato abhabhozya, “Mweji amwe mwemwe, mulonje alengane nendijizyo zyenyu bhope.” Ayahudi bhabhozya, “Endajizyo sezitibhozya abude omuntu wawonti.”
JOH 18:32 Bhayanjile ezi aje izu lya Yesu likamilishe izu lya ayanjile ahusu enfwa yakwe.
JOH 18:33 O Pilato ahinjila nantele hu Praitorio akwizya oYesu; ahabhozya, “Aje, awe oli mwene wa Ayahudi?”
JOH 18:34 O Yesu ajile, “Aje, awe ombozya ni swali eli ohwanza amanye au afuatanaje bhatumile aje ombozye ane?”
JOH 18:35 Wope oPilato ajile, “Ane sendi Yahudi, aje seshashesho?” Ikabela lyenyu no chungaji ogosi ebho bhabhaletile huline; awe obhombile yenu?
JOH 18:36 O Yesu ajile; oumwene wane sewamu omu, nkashe oumwene wane ugaali wa munsi omu aboyi bhane handa bhahomaniye waganje anfume hwa Yahudi. Lyoli oumwene wane seufuma epa” Pansi
JOH 18:37 O Pilato abhozya, “Aje awe eshi oli mwene?” O Yesu ajile, “awe shili shoyanga aje ane endi mwene, afuatana neshi napepwe alenganeshi ane enenzele munsi aje embe keti weela elyoli. Wawonti waali neyo elyoli elitejezya izu lyane.
JOH 18:38 O Pilato abhozya, “Elyoli yenu?” Wope nayanga ego ahabhala hwa Yahudi na bhabhozye “Selola nkahamo hwa muntu ono.
JOH 18:39 Amwe mulinoutamaduni wamubhomba emwegulile ofungwa omo owakati we Pasaka. Aje muhwanza aje embigulile omwene wa Yahudi.”
JOH 18:40 Bhahomile ekelele bhaile, sio ono, tigulile oBaraba.” Wope oBaraba alifyozi.
JOH 19:1 O Pilato amwejile oYesu na hushete.
JOH 19:2 Bhala asikari bhapotile aminvwa nalenganye taji. Bhaibheha pitwe lya Yesu na hukwatizye amenda ge rangi ye nshamwamu nshamwamu.
JOH 19:3 Bhamwenzela na aje, “Awe mwene wa Yahudi! na hukhome hu makhono gabho.
JOH 19:4 O Pilato afumile honze na bhabhozye abhantu, “Enyaji embaletela ono omuntu hulimwe aje mumanye ane senalilolile ibhibhi lyalyonti muhati yabho.”
JOH 19:5 Eshi oYesu afumile honze; ali akwete etaji ye minvwa na menda amashamwamu. O Pilato ayanga, “Enyaji abhozya mwenyi omuntu ono epa!”
JOH 19:6 Omuda ochungaji ogosi wa gosi nabhahalola oYesu, bhakhoma ekelele bhaga, “Yenvyaji, yenvyaji.” O Pilato abhabhozya, “Mwenji amwe mwemwe muyenvyaje, afuatanaje ane sendilola akosa muhati yakwe.”
JOH 19:7 Ayahudi bhabhozya oPilato, “Ate tili ne ndajizyo, na hundajizyo yeeyo ehwanziwa afwe afuatanaje omwene ahwilola aje mwana wa Ngolobhe.”
JOH 19:8 O Pilato nahonvwa enongwa ezyo azidile ahwogope,
JOH 19:9 ahinjila Mpraitorio nantele na hubhozye oYesu, “Awe ofuma hwii? Ata sheshi, oYesu sagayanjile.
JOH 19:10 Nantele iPilato abhozya, “Aje, awe soyanga nane? Aje, awe somenye aje ane endi nouwezo wa humwigugulile no uwezo wa huyemvye?”
JOH 19:11 O Yesu ajile, “Ogali ne nguvu ashile ane ogalisopewilwe afume amwanya. Eshi, omuntu wanefwizye huliwe ali ne mbibhi engosi.”
JOH 19:12 Afumilane ni jibu eli, oPilato ahanzaga ahuleshe weene, ila Aayahudi wahakhoma ekelele bhaga, “Nkashe obhahuleshe wene awe soli wamwabho oKaisari: Shila wahwibheha aje mwene ayanga shingunga sha Kaisari.”
JOH 19:13 O Pilato na honvwa enongwa aleta oYesu honze nantele ahakhala pitengo lye lonzi pala papamanyi she aje sakafu, ila hushiEbrania, Gabhatha.
JOH 19:14 Isiku lye maandalizi ge pasaka nalyafishile, omuda gwe saa tanda. O Pilato abhozya Ayahudi, “Enyaaji omwene wenyu ono epa!”
JOH 19:15 Bhakhoma ekelele, “Sogozi, sogozi, muyenvye!” O Pilato abhabhozya, “Aje eyenvye omwene wenyu?” Wope Ochungaji ogosi ajile, “Ate setili no mwene ila o Kaisari.”
JOH 19:16 O Pilato nkafumya oYesu hwabhene aje ayenvewe.
JOH 19:17 Wope bhamwega oYesu, wope wafuma, ohu anyemuye eshikhobhe hanyo shakwe yoyo paka hula hufuvu litwe, hu Shiebrania bhaiga hu Golgota.
JOH 19:18 Nkabhayenvya oYesu na bhala alume bhabhele, omo oupande ou owamwabho oupande ou, no Yesu pahati yabho.
JOH 19:19 O Pilato ahandiha eshimanyilo na bheshe pamwanya pashi khobhehanyo. Epo pahandihwe: YESU WENAZALETI, OMWENE WA YAHUDI.
JOH 19:20 Abhinji bha Yahudi bhabhazya eshimanyilo esho pantu pala pabhayenvezye oYesu pali pepe ne khaaya. Eshi manyilo esho shahandihwe hushi Ebrania, hushi Rumi na hushi Yunani.
JOH 19:21 Ogosi bha dimi bha Yahudi bhabhozya oPilato, “Sio hwandishe, 'Omwene wa Yahudi; ila omwene ajile ane endi mwene Wayahudi.”
JOH 19:22 Wope oPilato ajile, “Genandishe enandishe.”
JOH 19:23 Askari nabhayenvya oYesu, bhahega amenda gakwe na gagabhanye vilondo viine, shila sikari ilondo limo, Shesho inkanzu, lila selyalilisonilwe ila lyali litabhilwe lyonti afumile pamwanya.
JOH 19:24 Bhakwepelana bhebho hu bhebho, “Tinganje alipasule ila tikhome yekola aje libhe lyananu.” Eli lyafumiye aje lila izu likamilishe, lila lyalyajile bhagabhenye amenda gane, no ninkanza lyane bhakhomeye ekola.”
JOH 19:25 Asikari bhabhombile embombo ezi. Onyina wakwe oYesu, no dada wa nyina wakwe, oMariamu oshe wa Kleopa no Mariamu Magedelena - abhashe ebha bhali bhemeleye pepe neshi khobhehanyo sha Yesu.
JOH 19:26 O Yesu nalolile onyina wakwe pamonola omwanafunzi wagene bhemeleye peepe, abhozye onyina wakwe, “Wee shee, enya, lola omwana waho ono epa!”
JOH 19:27 Abhozya omwanafunzi, “Enya, ono epa onyina waho. “Afume esala eyo ola omwanafunzi amwega abhale akhaya yakwe.
JOH 19:28 Baada yelyo, o Yesu amenye aje gonti gamalishe gamalishiye aje akamilisye amaazu, ajile, “Elola eshomelwa.”
JOH 19:29 Eshelelo shashilimemile shali shibhehwelwe pala, bhabheha esifongo yememile Isiki pamwanya ye ufito we hisopo, bhabheshela mwilomu lyakwe.
JOH 19:30 Wope oYesu naibhonga ezyo, ajile, “Emalishe.” Pamande aundamiha itwe lyakwe, aibheha eroho yakwe.
JOH 19:31 Afwatanaje waali wakati wahwiyandaale, afuatanaje amabele segahanziwaga asagale pashikhobhehanyo owakati we Sabato (afuatanaje eSabato yaali ye muhimu), ayahudi bhalabhile oPilato aje amagaga gabho bhala bhabhali bhayenvezewa gabudulwe, naje na mabeele gabho bhagisye.
JOH 19:32 Osikari ahenza abudule amagaga gamuntu owa kwanza no wa bhele ali ayonvewa pandwemo no Yesu.
JOH 19:33 Nabhafishila oYesu, bhamweje afwiye eshieshi sebhabudula amagaga gakwe.
JOH 19:34 Ata sheshi omo wa sikari alese oYesu hu mbazu ne mpalala, gahafuma amenze gidanda.
JOH 19:35 Wope walolile eli afumwizye olweteho no lweteho lwakwe lwe lyoli. Omwene amenye hayanjile he lyoli aje namwe mweteshele.
JOH 19:36 Enongwa ezi zyahali aje lila izu lyalya ya ngwilwe nkalifishile, “Nomo hata omo wamwene waibudulwa.”
JOH 19:37 Nantele izu lyamwabho liyiga, “Bhahumwenya omwene wabhalese”
JOH 19:38 Baadaye nongo ezi oYusufu we Arimathaya, afuatanaje ali mwanafunzi wa Yesu, ila shi siri abhogope Ayahudi, alabhile oPilato aje agweje obele gwa Yesu. Wope oPilato apiye oluhusa. O Yusufu ahenza agwefwe obele gwa Yesu.
JOH 19:39 Wope o Nikodemo ola olwahwande wafwatile oYesu no siku wope ahenzele. Omwene aletile osangano manemane no udi, oumwamuwe latili mia e yeeka.
JOH 19:40 Bhahega obele gwa Yesu bhagupinya mumpongoso ye shitani pandwemo na gala amafuta, nanshi shahali ekawaida ya Yahudi omuda gwa syele.
JOH 19:41 Apantu oYesu pabhayenvezye pali nee bustani; muhati yela ebustani mwali ni kaburi ipya sayahali omuntu wawaile asyelwe omwo.
JOH 19:42 Afuatanaje lyali lisiku lye maandalizi hwa Yahudi, na afuatanaje lila ikaburi lyali peepe, bhahagoni oYesu muhati yakwe.
JOH 20:1 Khasha isiku lya hwande lya mulwa sanu, shahuli nkisi, oMariamu Magederena ahenzele hwi kaburi; ahalola lila lila iwe lyepile pikaburi.
JOH 20:2 Ahashembela abhale hwa Simoni oPetro na hwola omwanafunzi wamwabho ola oYesu wagene, nkabhabhozya, “bhamwejile Ogosi mwikaburi, na setihwelewa hula hwabhagonizye.”
JOH 20:3 O Petro no mwanafunzi ola wamwabho bhahafuma abhale hwi kaburi.
JOH 20:4 Bhonti bhanyilile pandwemo; ola omwanafunzi wamwabho anyililiye tee ashile oPetro nagishe hwi kaburi abhe wa hwande.
JOH 20:5 Ahemelela na hwenye ikaburi; alola ela empogoso egonile, ila sagaahinjiye muhati.
JOH 20:6 Wope oSimoni oPetro wope ahafiha ahinjila muhati yi kaburi. Wailola ela empogoso egonile pala
JOH 20:7 nela eleso yayali hwitwe lyakwe seyali ogonile pandwemo ne mpogoso yayagonile panshenje yakwe.
JOH 20:8 Ola omwanafunzi wamwabho wope ahunjiye muhati yi kaburi; walola na hweteshele.
JOH 20:9 Afuatanaje paka owakati owo bhaali seele sebhagamenye amaazu aje yalazimishe oYesu afufushe nantele hwa bhafwe.
JOH 20:10 Abhanafunzi wahala nantele mukhaya zyabho.
JOH 20:11 O Mariamu ali ayemeleye pi kaburi alila, aali ahwendelela alile ahemeleye ahenya mwikaburi.
JOH 20:12 Ahabhalola ahalo ozelu bhabhele bhabhali no waje ozelu bhakheye omo hwitwe owa mwabho hu magaga apantu oYesu paali agonile.
JOH 20:13 Bhope bhabhozya, “Oshe, yeenu olila?” Wope afuatanaje bhamwejile Ogosi wane, naane seehwelewa hwa bhabheshele.”
JOH 20:14 Nahayanga ego, agalushe na hulole oYesu ali ayemeleye. Ila sagamenye aje ali yo Yesu.
JOH 20:15 Wope oYesu abhozya, “Maye yenu olila? Ohumwanza wenu?” Wope ohumwenyu yayola walenganya ebustani abhozya, “Gosi, nkashe wewe womwejile, mboozye, hwoobheshele nane embahumweje.”
JOH 20:16 O Yesu abhozya, “O Mariamu.” Wope agaluha yoyo na hubhozye hu Shiaramu, “Raboni,” esho hwahuje, “Mwalimu.”
JOH 20:17 O Yesu abhozya, “Oganje nguse, afuatane naje senzubhile abhale hwa Daada; ila obhale hwa holo bhane obhabhozye aje embazubhe abhale hwa Daada wane ola waali Daadi wenyu, Ongolobhe wane no Ngolobhe wenyu.”
JOH 20:18 O Mariamu oMagedelena ahenza abhabhozya abhanafunzi, “Elolile Ogosi,” naje abhozezye amambo ega.
JOH 20:19 Na hwahali ndyabheela, isiku elyo, isiku lya hwande lya mulwasanu, na mandiango gaali gafungwilwe pala abhanafunzi pabhahali hubhogope Ayahudi, oYesu ahenzele na hwemelele pahati yabho n abhabhozye, “Olusongwo lubhe hulimwe.”
JOH 20:20 Na hayanga ego abhalanga amakhono gakwe no bhazu lwakwe. Wope abhanafunzi nabhalolile Ogosi bhasongwelwe.
JOH 20:21 O Yesu abhabhozya nantele, “Olusongwo lubhe namwe. Nanshi Odaada shantumile ane, shesho shesho nane nabhafumile amwe.”
JOH 20:22 O Yesu nayanga ego, abhavuvia abhabhozya, Posheli Ompempo Ofinjile.
JOH 20:23 Wawonti wamuhusajila embibhi, bhasajilwe; na bhala bhamwaibhafunjila bhaifunjilwa.”
JOH 20:24 O Tomaso, omo wa bhala kumi na bhabhele, wahetwaga Didimasi, sagali na bhanafunzi amwabho oYesu lwa henzaga.
JOH 20:25 Bhala abhanafunzi amwabho bhabhozya pamande, “Tilolile Ogosi.” Wope abhozya, “Nkashe sembalole eshimanyilo she nsumari mumakhono gakwe, nabheshe evidole vyane hwesho eshimanyilo, nantele abheshe amakhono gane hubhazu lwakwe sembahweteshele.”
JOH 20:26 Na zyashila ensiku nane abhanafunzi bhali ampande nantele, wope oTomaso ali pandwemo nabho. A andiango nagafungwa oYesu ahemeleye pahati yabho. Na ayanjile, “Olusongwa lubhe namwe.”
JOH 20:27 Ahabhozya oTomaso, leeta eshidole shaho na alole amakhono gane; leeta eepa amakhono gaho obheshe pabhazu lwane; oganjebhe wasaahweteshela obhee wa hweteshela.”
JOH 20:28 Wope oTomaso ayanga ahaaga, “Gosi wane nantele Ngolobhe wane.”
JOH 20:29 O Yesu abhozya, Afuatanaje waandola, oyetesheye. Bhasailwe bhala bhabhahweteshela, bilaalole.”
JOH 20:30 O Yesu abhombile ezyaswije nyinji hwitazi lya bhanafunzi, zyasagaziwaile ahwandihwe mushitabu eshi;
JOH 20:31 ezi zyandihwe aje nkamweteshe laje aje oYesu yo Kilisiti, mwana wa Ngolobhe, aje namu hweteshela mubhe no womi hwitawa lyakwe.
JOH 21:1 Baada ye nongwa ezyo oYesu ahwibhonesya nantele hwa bhanafunzi hunsombe ye Tiberia; eshi sha sheshi shahwibhonesezye yooyo:
JOH 21:2 O Simoni o Petro alipandwemo no Tomaso wa kwiziwa Didimas, o Nathanaeli wa hu kana ye Galilaya, abhana bha Zebedayo na bhanafunzi bhamwabho bhabhele bha Yesu.
JOH 21:3 O Simoni Patro abhozya, “Ane embala ahwonze ensamaki.” Bhope bhabhozya, “Ate nate tibhala nawe.” Wahabhala bhahinjila mwi toli, ila nusiku owo bhonti sebhapete hahonti.
JOH 21:4 Shapwinti na hwahasha, oYesu ahemeleye hufukweni, wope abhanafunzi sebhamanyaga aje aali yo Yesu.
JOH 21:5 O Yesu abhabhozya, “Bhavijana, muli hahonti ahalyee?” Bhope bhayanga bhaga, “Hamuna.”
JOH 21:6 Wabhabhozya, “Isyii owavu oupande wendeelo witoli, namwe munzapate hashee, “Bhahisya owavu bhope sebhawezizye aakuunye nantele afuatanaje esamaki zyali nyinji.
JOH 21:7 Ola omwanafunzi oYesu wagene wabhozya Petro, “Yo Gosi.” Wope oSimoni Petro lwa honvwa aje yo Gosi, wahwipinya omwenda gwakwe (afuatanaje sagaakwete shinza), pamande wahwiponya mwinsombe.
JOH 21:8 Bhala abhanafunzi bhamwabho wahenza mwotori (sebhali hutali ne pwani, yali mita mia yeva afume ufukweni), bhope bhali bhakunya zila enyavu zyali zimemile ensamaki.
JOH 21:9 Na bhafiha hufwekweni, wagulola omwoto gwe kaala pala pamwanya yakwe pali ne nsamaki pandwemo na mabumunda.
JOH 21:10 O Yesu abhabhozya, “Leeti zimo ensamaki zyamwonzile esalezi eshi.”
JOH 21:11 O Simoni Petro waazubha aguvute gula owavu gwagwali gumemile ensamaki engosi, esamaki zyali 153; hata nkashe zyali nyinji, ula owavu sewazembushe.
JOH 21:12 O Yesu abhabhozya, “Enzaji mupate vigulilo ilomu.” Nomo ata weka hwa bhanafunzi walenjele ahubhozye, “Awe we weenu?” Bhamenye aje ali yo Gosi.
JOH 21:13 O Yesu ahenza, ahega lila ibumunda, pamande abhapela, abhomba shesho huunsamaki zila.
JOH 21:14 Ene yaali mara tatu oYesu hwa bhanafunzi bhakwe baada ya ovyionshe afume hwabhafwe.
JOH 21:15 Baada ya hwigule ilomu, oYesu abhozya oSimoni Petro, “Simoni mwana wa Yohana aje, ongene ane ashile ebha?” O Petro ahaga, “Ena, Gosi; “Awe omenye aje ane agene.” O Yesu abhozya, “Lisya awanangole bhane.”
JOH 21:16 Abhabhozya emara ya bheele, “Simoni mwana wa Yona, aje, ongeene?” O Petro ahaga, “Ena, Gosi; awe omenye aje ane egene. “O Yesu ahaga, “Dima engole zyane.”
JOH 21:17 Abhozya nantele emara ya tatu, “Simoni, mwana wa Yohana, Aje ongene?” Wope oPetro azugumila huu shila shabhozezye mara hatatu, “Aje awe ongene?” Wope ahaga, “Gosi, omenye gonti; omenye aje egene.” O Yesu ahaga, Lisya engole zyane.
JOH 21:18 Eteshela, eteshela, ehubhozya, nawahali kijana wamanyene akwate amenda weewe na abhale hwa hwonti hwo hwanza; ila nawaibhagoogolo waigolosya amakhono gaho, no weenje aihukwatizya amenda na hutwale hwa sohwanza abhale.”
JOH 21:19 O Yesu ayanjile ega aje abhonesye aje nfwa bhole o Petro yagamwamishe Ongolobhe. Nayanga ega, abhozya oPetro, “Onfwate.”
JOH 21:20 O Yesu agalushe na hulole ola omwanafunzi ola oYesu wagene wabhalondola- Ono yayola wahagamiye pashifubha sha Yesu omuda gwe shalyee sha na ndabhela na hubhozye, “Gosi, wenu wanzahugalushe?”
JOH 21:21 O Petro alolile nantele wabhozya oYesu, “Gosi, Ono omuntu anzabhombe eyenu?”
JOH 21:22 O Yesu ahaga, “Nkashe ehwanza aje asagale paka lwanayenza, elyo lihusu yenu?” Nfwaate.”
JOH 21:23 Enongwa ene yaahendelela mhati mwa bhala aholo, aje omwanafunzi ono sagaifwa. Ila oYesu sagabhozezye oPetro aje omwanafunzi oyo faafwa, “Nkashe ehwanza aje omwene asagale paka lwanayenza gahuhusu yenu?”
JOH 21:24 Ono yo mwanafunzi wafumya oluhakikisyo lwe enongwa ezi na timenye aje oluhakikisyo lwakwe lwe lyoli.
JOH 21:25 Gahweli amambo gamwabho gaminji oYesu gabhombile. Zigadolilwe zyonti elola aje ensi ene seyahenzaga aye avibheshe evitabu vyavigadolilwe.
ACT 1:1 Eshitabu shila eshikulu nasimbile, Theofilo, nahayanjile zyonti zyahandile uYesu abhombe na manyizye,
ACT 1:2 mpaka isiku uYesu lyahejelewe humwanya. Eli lyabhombeshe uYesu nawafumya eamri ashilile hwa Umpepo Ufinjile hwa atumwe bhakwe bhabhasaluye.
ACT 1:3 Baada ye mayemba agateswe, abhoneshe ali mwomi ne mbonesyo nyingi zyazyabhoneshe. Hunsiku amalongo gane ahwibhonesezye hwa bhantu bhakwe nayanje ezyeumwe zya Ngulubhi.
ACT 1:4 Na patangene nabho abhalajizizye aje bhasahasogole mu Yelusalemu, lelo bhagule edagano zyayanjile, “Zyamwahumvwaga neyanga afume huline
ACT 1:5 aje uYohana abhozya naminzi lelo ane embabhozye nu Mpepo Ufinjile nkazyashila ensiku zishe.”
ACT 1:6 Nabhakhomene pandwimo bhahabhuzya, “Aje eshi jibha lwubhabhagomoshezye oumwene a Izraeli?”
ACT 1:7 Umwene ahaga se shinza hulimwe amanye ezyahwibhesheye umwene Ungulubhi.”
ACT 1:8 Lelo mubhaposhe ikhone nawinza hulimwe Umpepo Ufinjile, namwe mwaibha bhaketi bhane, mu Yelusalemu, mu Uyahudi mu Samaria, na humalishilo uwensi.”
ACT 1:9 Nawayanga ezyo uYesu wabhuha wanyamulwa humwanya nabhamwenya, ibhengo lyakwinshila watega sebhalola na maso gabho.
ACT 1:10 Nulwabhahwenya humwanya kwa makini akienda, ghafula, abhantu bhabhili bhemelela pahati yabho bhakwite amenda amazelu.
ACT 1:11 Bhaga, “Mwe bhantu bha hu Galilaya, yenu mwimeleye epa?” Muhwenya abhala humwanya? Unu uYesu yamuhulola abhala humwanya ahwenza shesho sha muhulola abhala.
ACT 1:12 Nabhanvwa isho bhaela afume hwigamba lye mizeituni, abhale hu Yerusalemu humwendo wa Sabato.
ACT 1:13 Nabhafiha bhahabhala hwigulu amatawa gabho bhabhebha. Petro, Yohana, Yakobo, Andrea, Filipo, Thomaso, Batholomayo, Mathayo, Yakobo Omwana wa Alfayo, Simoni Zelote nu Yuda Umwana wa Yakobo.
ACT 1:14 Bonti ebho bhabhungene neshi umuntu umo, bhahendelela ne mputo. Bhali na abhashe, uMariamu unyina wa Yesu, nailumbu bhakwe.
ACT 1:15 Ensiku zila uPetro ahimilie pahati pa holo bhala bhahali abhantu 120, ahaga,
ACT 1:16 Mwe bhantu ehali huje enongwa zya Ngulubhi zitimile, zyayanjile Umpepo Ufinjile hwilomu lya Daudi zyazyayanjile uYuda, yabhalongole bhaala bhabhakete uYesu.
ACT 1:17 Umwene ali pamo nate aposhile ifungu lyakwe elye faida humbombo ene.”
ACT 1:18 (Neshi umuntu unu akalile ugunda huhela ila eye mbibhi zyakwe nepo ahagwiye abazuhu ivyanda na maula gahafuma na hwitishe.
ACT 1:19 Bhonti bhabhakhalaga hu Yerusalemu bhuhumvwizye na ieneo elyo hahalyeta itawa hunjango yabho “Akeldama” ugwo “gunda gwi danda.”)
ACT 1:20 “Mushitabu eshe Zaburi shijile, 'Ambe ugunda gwakwe gubhe lisami asahakhale umuntu nkumo;' tikunde, 'Umuntu uwinje ayeje enafasi yakwe eyelongozi.'
ACT 1:21 Elyo lye muhimu aje ulume umoyajendaga pandwimo nate lula uYesu nalihulite nahinjilaga nafume,
ACT 1:22 ahwande lila uYohana na hozyaga abhantu mpaka isiku lila uYesu nahabhushile abhale humwanya, lazima abhe keti we luzyuho pandwimo nate.
ACT 1:23 “Bhabhala hwitagalila alume bhabhili, uYusufu yahetelwe Barnaba, itawa elya mwabho ali yu Yusto, nu Mathiya.
ACT 1:24 Abene bhalabha bhaga, “Awe, Ngolobhe umenye amoyo gabhantu bhonti tilaaba abhantu yusaluye
ACT 1:25 ahweje enafasi ya Yuda yabhombile embibhi nasogole hulite.”
ACT 1:26 Bhakhoma ekula ekula yagwila uMathiya yabhehwelwe pandwemo na bhaala atumwe ilongo nu weka.
ACT 2:1 Nalyahafiha isiku elye Pentekoste, bhonti bhabhongene pandwemo.
ACT 2:2 Gwahabhafumila ungulumo afume humwanya neshi ugwihala ehali. Gwamema munyumba yonti mwabhakheye.
ACT 2:3 Zyahabhafumila emele neshi, zigabhanyishe nabhe pamwanya ya shila muntu (pitwe).
ACT 2:4 Bhonti bhapata Umpepo Ufinjile bhahanda ayanje enjango ezyenje neshi Umpepo shasungwilwe umwene.
ACT 2:5 Bhahali ayahudi bhabhakhalaga mu Yelusalemu bhabhaputaga bhabhafuma shila nsi pansi.
ACT 2:6 Ungulumo gula nabhahunvwa abhantu bhahabhungana ahwenze atejelezye bhahabha ne wasiwasi shila muntu ahumnwizye bhayanga hunjango yakwe yuyo.
ACT 2:7 bhonti bhahaswiga bhahaga ebha bhonti se bha hu Galilaya bhabha yanga epa?
ACT 2:8 Yeenu ate tibhumvwa hunjango yetu yatapipwe nayo?
ACT 2:9 Waparthia na Waamedi na Waelamu, nebho bhabhakhala hu Mesopotamia, no Uyahudi, na Kapadokia, no hu Ponto nu hu Asia,
ACT 2:10 hu Frigia, Pamfilia, no hu Misri, na hula hu Libya paka hu Kirene, na bhajenu bhonti bhabhafumile hu Rumi,
ACT 2:11 Ayahudi na bhaongofu, Abhakrete bhonti tubhomvwa nazyo bhatambula embombo engosi Ungulubhi zyabhomba.”
ACT 2:12 Bhonti bhaswiga sebhahazyaganya mwitwe; hahanda abhuzanye bhene, “Eshi hwa huje yeenu?”
ACT 2:13 Lelo bhamo bhahatanila bhahaga, “Ebha bhakholilwe.”
ACT 2:14 Lelo uPetro ahimilila pandwemo na bhala ilongo na woka nabhabhule huje mwe mubhantu mwenti mwa mukhala hu Yudea namwe mwenti mwamukhala epa pa Yerusalemu, muntejelezye enongwa zyane muzizingatizye humoyo genyu.
ACT 2:15 Abhantu ebha sebhakholilwe neshi shamuibha, esala ezi saa tatu zyashampwiti.
ACT 2:16 Lelo mumanye huje ezi zyazila zyazyayangwilwe no ukuwe uYoeli;
ACT 2:17 Zyaibha ensiku ezya humalishilo; ayanga Ungulubhi, naibhitila Umpepo Ufinjile abhantu bhonti. Abhana bhenyu asahala na lendu bhaikuwa, abhana bhenyu bhailola embonesyo, na gogolo bhailota enjozi.
ACT 2:18 Nantele abhomba mbombo bhane abhashe ehaibhitila Umpepo wane bhope bhaikuwa.
ACT 2:19 Naibhalanga enswijizyo humwanya ne mbonesyo pansi pa dunia, idanda, umwoto, na tukusye elyosi.
ACT 2:20 Ni sanya lyaigaluha hisi no mwezi abhe lidanda, salisele ahwinze isiku Igosi lya Ngulubhi.
ACT 2:21 ehaibha shila muntu yailikwizya itawa la Ngulubhi ayokoha.'
ACT 2:22 Mubhantu mubhi Israeli, umvwi enongwa ezi: U Yesu wa hu Nazareti, Ungulubhi yabhasaluliye na hulete hulimwe ne mbombo engosi Ungulubhi zyabhombile ashilile hwa mwene, namwe mwazilolile namwe muzimenye zyonti zyabhombile-
ACT 2:23 Lelo hunongwa ya mapango gakwe gapanjile afume hale nenjele zyakwe Ungulubhi, aje aihufumya humakhono ga bhantu aabhibhi ananzi, namwe mwahabuda,
ACT 2:24 Ungulubhi umwene ahazyusya ahayefwa enfwa muhati yakwe kwa sababu seyaweze hene aje enfwa etabhaale.
ACT 2:25 U Daudi ayanjile ajile, 'Nahalolile Ugosi wane hwitagalila lyane, umwene ali hukhono gwane ulilo sembahwogope.
ACT 2:26 Umwoyo gwane gwahasungwa nu mele gwane gwasungwilwe. Gwope ubili gwane gwaikhala ni khone.
ACT 2:27 Subhaguleshe umwoyo gwane gubhale hwazimu, nantele subhahuleshe ubhomba mbombo waho alole uvunzu.
ACT 2:28 Awe umbunisizye idala elye womi; ubhandeshe ememe uluseshelo humaso gaho.'
ACT 2:29 Bhaholo, bhane enjanje ezya ise wetu u Daudi: umwene afwiye asyelelwe nenkungwa yakwe ehweli hulite mpaka asanyunu eshi.
ACT 2:30 Umwene ali kuwe na amenye huje Ungulubhi alapile hundapo zyakwe huje ahaihubhiha umo umwana wakwe hwitengo lyakwe elye umwene.
ACT 2:31 Eli alilolile shansele, nantele ayanjile huje aizyuha uYesu Kilisiti, 'sigalehwilwe hwazimu nu bili gwakwe sigagwavundile.'
ACT 2:32 Unu uYesu - Ungulubhi azyusizye, nate tili bhaketi bhakwe.
ACT 2:33 Eshi uYesu ali hukhono ulilo ugwa Ngulubhi, nantele ayejeleye ulaganyo ulwa Umpepo Ufinjile afume hwa Yise wakwe, asuhinye ululagano olu hulite neshi shamulola na hwumvwe.
ACT 2:34 Umwene uDaudi sigalushile abhale humwanya, lelo ajile, 'OGOSI (Ungulubhi) wane ayanjile hwa Gosi wane,
ACT 2:35 “khala hukhono gwane ulilo, mpaka nehaibhabheha elyakhalile na khanyena manama gaho.
ACT 2:36 Aisraeli bhonti bhamanye huje uYesu unu yabhabudile Ungulubhi abhishile aje abhe Gosi ashile Agosi bhonti abhamunsi.”
ACT 2:37 Nabhumvwa isho enongwa zyabhalasa humwoyo gabho, bhabhabhuzya aPetro na bhamwabho tikhonzye wili eshi?”
ACT 2:38 U Petro waga, “Mulambe mwoziwe, shila muntu hwitawa lya Yesu Kristi muposhele ulusajilo ulwe mbibhi zyenyu, namwe mubhaposhe Umpepo Ufinjile.
ACT 2:39 Olu olulagano lwenyu na bhana bhenyu na bhantu bhabhali uhutali na bhaala bhonti bhabhaikwiziwa nu Ngulubhi aje bhinze.”
ACT 2:40 Hunongwa ezya mwabho ajile hwi ponii na bhantu bhensiku ezi abhe mbibhi.”
ACT 2:41 Abhantu bhazyeteha enongwa zila bhoziwa abhantu elfu zitatu(3000) ikanisa lyahonjelela.
ACT 2:42 Bhahendelela adiile mumanyizyo zya atumwe bha Yesu bhali nu umoja, bhalyanga pandwimo na puute pandwimo.
ACT 2:43 Uwoga wahabhinjila abhantu ne mbombo ezyaswijizye zyahabhoneha Ungulubhi zyabhombile ashilile hwa tumwe bhakwe.
ACT 2:44 Bhonti bhabhahitishie izu lya Ngulubhi bhahakhalaga pandwimo ne vintu vyabhali navyo vyali vya bhonti,
ACT 2:45 evintu vyabhali navyo bhakazyaga bhagabhilaga shila muntu shahanzaga.
ACT 2:46 Ensiku zyonti bhali nu mwoyo gumo mushibhanza, bhamensulaga amabumunda mukhaya nalye eshalye shobho nuluseshelo nu mwoyo ugolosu;
ACT 2:47 bhalumbaga Ungulubhi bhakonde lwe na bhanti bhonti. Shila lisiku abhantu bhahonjelelelaga mushibhanza bhaala bhabhahokahaga.
ACT 3:1 U Petro nu Yohana bhabhalaga hushibhanza apuute, yahali saa tisa.
ACT 3:2 Umuntu umo alinanchisi manama afume shapipwe, bhahanyemulaga shila lisiku bhabhehaga mundyango ugweshibhanza, gwagwahitwaga gwinza, aje abhalabhaje abhantu bhabhahwinjila mushibhanza.
ACT 3:3 Nawabhalola aPetro nu Yohana bhazubhula aje bhinjile mushibhanza, wabhalaabha esadaka.
ACT 3:4 U Petro nu Yohana bhamwenya hu maso bhaga,”tenye ate.”
ACT 3:5 Ula unanjisu manama wabhenya, wasubhila apelwe ahantu hahonti afume hwabhene.
ACT 3:6 Umwene uPetro waga ane sendi ne, “hela wala edhahabu, lelo hendi naho hehupela. Hwitawa elya Yesu Kilisiti wa Nazareti, emelela.”
ACT 3:7 U Petro wakhata ukhono ulilo wabhusya, amafugamo gakwe gapata ikhone.
ACT 3:8 Umuntu ula wimilila najende na rusherushe winjila mushibhanza nu Petro nu Yohana ohu ajenda yuyo ohu ahulumba Ungulubhi.
ACT 3:9 Abhantu bhonti nabhalola ajenda bhalumba Ungulubhi.
ACT 3:10 Bhamanya huje yayula yalinanjisu manama yalabhaga esadaka pandyango gweshibhanza; abhantu bhahaswiga embombo Ungulubhi zyabhombile hwa muntu ula.
ACT 3:11 Abhantu nabhalola umuntu ula abhomiliye aPetro nu Yohana, bhashimbila muukumbi wawahetelwe wa Sulemani, bhahaswijile tee.
ACT 3:12 U Petro nawalola isho, wabhabhu ula abhantu bha Israeli, yeenu muswiga? Nantele mutenya ate aje ate tetimwemelesizye umuntu unu hwi khone lyetu?”
ACT 3:13 Ungulubhi wa Ibulahimu, Ungulubhi wa Isaka, nuwa Yakobo, Ungulubhi wa Yise bhetu, amwemeshe utumishi wakwe uYesu. Unu amwe mwahakhanile hwa Pilato, nantele uPilato, ahanzaga huleshele wene.
ACT 3:14 Mwahakhene Umfinjile wa Ngulubhi umuntu Umwinza, mwahamwanza abhigulile unyambuda aleshelwe wene.
ACT 3:15 Amwe mwabudile umwene uwi womi, lelo Ungulubhi azyusya afume hwabhafwe - Ate tili bhaketi bhakwe.
ACT 3:16 Eshi, ulweteho hwitawa lya Yesu, unu lwalupiye ikhone elyajendele umuntu unu yamuhulola na kujua, alifanywa kuwa na nguvu. Imani ambayo inapitia kwa Yesu imempa yeye afya hii kamilifu, mbele yenu ninyi nyote.
ACT 3:17 Eshi, Bhaholo, bhane elola mwabhombile esho hunongwa yelema, atubhalongozi bhenyu shabhabhombile.
ACT 3:18 Lelo enongwa zya yanjile Ungulubhi ashilile akuwe bhakwe aje uYesu ailabha zibhombishe eshi.
ACT 3:19 Eshi mulabhe na galushe, nke mbibhi zyenyu zyepe nkazyenze ensiku ezya sungwe naseshelele nayenza umwene uYesu;
ACT 3:20 Aitumwa uYesu yasalulwe nu Ngulubhi hulimwe.
ACT 3:21 Umwene yayuyo emwanya lazima zimwejelele mpaka evintu vyonti navyaigaluha, vyayanjile Ungulubhi ashilile akuwe bhakwe afinjile.
ACT 3:22 Lyoli uMusa ayanjile, 'Huje Ugosi Ungulubhi aja aihubhiha ukuwe neshi ane afume hwa holo bhenyu. Mwaihumwonvwelezya shila hantu haibhabhuula amwe.
ACT 3:23 Ihaibha aje shila muntu yasagaa ihutejelezya okuwe uyo aibhengwa ayepe pabhamwabho.'
ACT 3:24 Lyoli, akuwe bhonti ahwandile hwa Samueli na bhaala bhabhapyanie pamwene bhatangazizye naziyanje ensiku ezi.
ACT 3:25 Amwe mulibhana bhakuwe neilagano Ungulubhi lyalagine na gogolo bhetu abhemande neshi shayayanjile nu Ibrahimu, 'Aje abhana bhe mpapo yaho abhantu bhonti bha munsi bhaisaiwa.'
ACT 3:26 Ungulubhi pa wamwimiha uYesu waleta hulimwe nasoti huje abhasaye amwe nkamwagaluha nahuzileshe embibhi zyenyu.”
ACT 4:1 U Petro nu Yohana nabhayangaga na bhantu agosi abheshibhanza na linzi beshibhanza na masadukayo bhahabala.
ACT 4:2 Bhavitilwe tee sababu uPetro nu Yohana bhabhamanyizyaga abhantu huje uYesu azyushile afume hwabhafwe.
ACT 4:3 Bhabhakhete nabhafunje mwijela bhahadila mumwo paka shandao lwakwe maana hwali lyabhela.
ACT 4:4 Abhantu bhinji bhabhahunvwizye izu lya Ngulubhi bhalyeteshe; humbazyo bhaali abhantu elfu zisanu 5000.
ACT 4:5 Isiku ilyashandano lwakwe azehe na simbi, bhahabhungana pandwimo hu Yelusalemu.
ACT 4:6 U Anasi ugosi uwishibhanza, nu Kayafa, nu Yohana, nu Iskanda, bhonti bhabhali bhaholo bha anasi ugosi wishibhanza.
ACT 4:7 Bhabhabhunganila aPetro nu Yohana bhabhabhiha pahati, bhabhabhuzya, “Hwikhone wili nahwitawa lya nanu mubhomba ezi?”
ACT 4:8 U Petro, pamememile Umpepo Ufinjile wabhabhuula, “Waga amwe mubhazee na mubhantu, mwenti,
ACT 4:9 eshite sanyunu tibhuziwa hwijambo elinza lyalibhombishe hwa muntu ula ubhinu huje aponile?
ACT 4:10 Eshi mulimanye elyo na hwabhantu bhonti abha Israeli, huje hwitawa elya Yesu uwa Nazareti amwe yamwabudile Ungulubhi umwene azyusize afume hwabhafwe, hwitawa lyakwe umuntu unu ayemeleye namwe muhulola.
ACT 4:11 U Yesu Kilisti liwe elyapanjenje amwe mwajenzi mwalikhanile. Namo uwokovu hwa muntu uwenje yayonti ula.
ACT 4:12 Na umo uwokovu hwa muntu uwenje yayonti. Nalimo itawa elyamwabho lyatipewilwe tibhantu pansi epa lyatibhajiye ahwokolewe.”
ACT 4:13 Bhaala agosi nabhalola uPetro nu Yohana, sebhasaga nahamo nantele bhaali bhantu bhekawaida wene ata eelimu sebhali nayo, bhahaswiga, bhahamanya huje abhantu ebha bhali nu Yesu.
ACT 4:14 Bhalolile umuntu ula yaali nanjisu manama ayemeleye nabho sebhali nezyayanje nazimo.
ACT 4:15 Lelo nabhahabhuula atumwe bha Yyesu huje sogoli pa bhungano, bhahanda abhuzanya bheene.
ACT 4:16 Tibhombe wile na bhantu ebha? Lyalibhombishe na bhene setibhajiye alikhane abhantu bhonti bhalilolile bhoonti bhabhakhala mu Yerusalemu; hatuwezi kulikataa hilo.
ACT 4:17 Eshi, amba tibhakhane bhasayanje nantele hwitawa eli elilya libhombishe lisahanyampane esahumvwe ensi yonti.
ACT 4:18 Bhabhakwizya uPetro nu Yohana bhaga musayanje nantele hwitawa eli musabhuyile amanyizye hwitawa eli.
ACT 4:19 Lelo uPetro nu Yohana bhahagamula bhahaga nkasheshinza abhumvwe amwe tileshe ahumwumvwe Ungulubhi yanji mwemwe lelote setibhajiye aleshe.
ACT 4:20 Ate setibhanje aleshe ayanje zyatizilolile na zyumvwe.”
ACT 4:21 Nabhabhakhana uPetro nu Yohana, bhabhaleha bhasogole. Maana sebhazilolie ezyamwabho ezyabhatake nantele abhantu bhonti bhazilolile zyazyabhombishe umuntu yalifwemanama ajenda.
ACT 4:22 Umuntu ula yalifwemanama amaha gakwe agapapwe gali amaha amalongo gane.
ACT 4:23 U Petro nu Yohana nabhawela hwa bhamwabho bhabhabhulazyonti zyabhabhulilwe na gosi bhala.
ACT 4:24 Nabhahumvwisho bhahapuuta hwa Ngulubhi palishimo bhali Ngulubhi awe wuhabhumbile ensi nemwanya ne vyonti vyavili umwo,
ACT 4:25 Ngulubhi witu hu Mpepo waho Ufinjile, uhayanjile nu ise witu uDaudi, mtumishi wako, huje, “Yeenu apagani bhaleta efujo, nantele bhasibha embibhi?
ACT 4:26 Abhamwene na bhabhatawala bhahwipanjile shibhibhi hwa Gosi na hwa Yesu.”
ACT 4:27 Lyoli, uHerode nu Pontio Pilato, na pagani na bhaIsraeli, bhahitihine abhombe embibhi hwa gosu uwitu uYesu yupashile amafuta.
ACT 4:28 Bhabhungine bhonti pandwimo bhahaibhomba zyonti zyuhayanjile afume hale aje zyaibhombe ha ata shazisele abhombeshe.
ACT 4:29 Eshi awe Gosi, witu taanwe tabhomba mbombo bhaho utipeele ikhone tiyangaje enongwa zyaho nkahwogope nazimo
ACT 4:30 ugolosye ukhono gwaho Ngulubhi ubhombe ezyaswijizye abhantu ashilile hwitawa lya Yesu Ugosi witu.”
ACT 4:31 Nabhamala apute pala pabhakheye payinga bhaliyanga izu lya Ngulubhi nahwogope Umpepo Ufinjile abhapiye ikhone.
ACT 4:32 Bhaala bhontu bhabhalyeteshe izu bhakhiye pandwimo evintu vyonti vyabhali navyo basanginye vyahabha vyabho bhonti numo yajile eha hanimwene; badala yake walikuwa na vitu vyote shirika.
ACT 4:33 Hwikhone igosi atumwe bha Yesu bhayangaga natangazye embombo engosi zyabhombile uYesu nahuje uYesu azyushile na eneema engosi ehali pamo nabho.
ACT 4:34 Numo umuntu yahishilwaga maana bhabhali neviwaja na magunda bhakazyaga ihela zyonti bhaziletaga hwatumwe bha Yesu atumwe bhazigabhanyaga
ACT 4:35 na kuviweka chini ya miguu ya mitume. Na mgawanyo ulifanywa kwa kila muumini, kulingana na shila muntu apelwaga afuatane ne shida yakwe sheli.
ACT 4:36 U Yusufu, umulawi, afumile hu Kipro, apewilwe itawa bhahakwizya yu Barnabasi na mitume (emaana yakwe mwana we lusubhilo).
ACT 4:37 Akazizya ugunda ehela zyonti azileta hwatumwe bha Yesu.
ACT 5:1 Umuntu, umo itawa ali yu Anania, nushi wakwe uSafira bhakazizye eshuma,
ACT 5:2 ehela zimo bhafisa wope ushe azimenye zyabhabhombile, waleta zyazyasagiye hwatumwe.
ACT 5:3 U Petro wabhuzya, “U Anania, yeenu ushetani agumemizye umwoyo gwaho uyanga ilenga hwu Mpepo Ufinjile na fise ihelu zyasisagiye muziletile epa?
ACT 5:4 Navyahali hulimwe sevyali vyenyu? nuhalisile akazya suhali namaamuzi navyo yeenu uhasibhile abhombe ezi? Nukhopiya muntu ukhopiyo Ungulubhi.”
ACT 5:5 Ahumvwaje esho, u Anania wagwa pansi wafwai abhantu bhonti bhayeta bhabhomvwizye ezi.
ACT 5:6 Na avijana(Asahala) bhanyatula bhabhala asyeele.
ACT 5:7 Amasala nagafiha gatatu ushiwakwe wope afiha samanyile zyazimwajile ulume wakwe.
ACT 5:8 U Petro wabhuzya ugunda gwamukazizye ehela zyazyezi nyene u Safira waga ee zyazyezyo.”
ACT 5:9 U Petro waga yeenu mupatene hukhopele ilenga Umpepo Ufinjile? Angalia, miguu ya wale waliomzika mme wako iko mlangoni, na watakubeba na kukupeleka nje.”
ACT 5:10 Wope wagwa wope wafwa avijana bhabhala bhasyela pabhasyilile ulume wakwe.
ACT 5:11 Ikanisa lyonti lyogopa na bhantu bhonti bhabhahumvwizye.
ACT 5:12 Embonesyo nyinji ezyashangazye zyabhombishe hwa bhantu ashilile humakhono gatumwe bhahali bhonti muukumbi wa Sulemani.
ACT 5:13 Numo umuntu uwinji yasangine nabho abhantu bhabhashinshime nabhapele eheshima engosi tee.
ACT 5:14 Ikanisa lyahonjelela alume na bhashe bhabhaposhelaga uYesu,
ACT 5:15 abhantu bhanyemulaga abhinu nabhabheshe mwidala, aje u Petro nashila inzyogozi lyakwe libhashilile.
ACT 5:16 Nantele abhantu, afume munshenje ye Yerusalemu bhabhaletile abhinu na bhabhali na mashetani, bhonti bhaponile
ACT 5:17 Lelo ugosi wishibhanza na bhala bhabhamwavwaga embombo (abhemadhehebu ga masadukayo); bhaali nu kero
ACT 5:18 bhahabhakhata atumwe bhabhafunjila mwiijela lya bhonti.
ACT 5:19 Nu siku umalaika wenza wigula amandyango gijela wabhalongola hwonze,
ACT 5:20 “Waga bhalaji mwemelele mwikanisa mubhabhuule abhantu enongwa ezye Womi owu.”
ACT 5:21 Nabhumvwa isho bhabhala mwikanisa nahuhenga bhabhamanyizya abhantu okuhani(ugosi weshibhanza) na bhaalabhali nabho bhakwizanya ibalaza lyonti bhabhatuma hubhakwizye atumwe mwijela.
ACT 5:22 Nabhafiha hwijela bhahega atumwe nabhamo mwijela bha bhala bhabhapeela etharifa,
ACT 5:23 “Bhaga tejile abhantu nabhamo mwijela, na mandyango gonti gafungwilwe sheshinza nalinzi bhahweli mundyango nitigula tejile afungwe enabhamo muhati.”
ACT 5:24 Usikari ugosi we hekalu na bhagosi bhahayetile sana pabhu mvwa huje afungwe nabhamo bhasiibha bhaga tibhabhombe wile ni jambo eli.
ACT 5:25 Umuntu umo wenza wabhabhula huje abhantu bhaala bhamwabhapinyile bhali hwa mwabho bhemeleye bhamanyizya.”
ACT 5:26 Usikari nabhantu abhanje bhabhala bhabhega shashinza bila fujo, bhahogope abhantu huje bhagabhakhoma na mawe.
ACT 5:27 Nabhabhaleta bhabhabheha pi baraza. Ugosi weshibhanza wa bhabhuuzya
ACT 5:28 tabhakhine amanyizye hwitawa lya muntu ula muyimemizye eYerusalemu emanyizyo zyenya musungwa alete idanda lya muntu ula hulite.”
ACT 5:29 Lelo uPetro natumwe bhaga, “Lazima timwumvwe Ungulubhi ashile abhumvwe abhantu.
ACT 5:30 Ungulubhi waise bhetu azyusizye uYesu yamwabudile na hulembezye mwikwi.
ACT 5:31 Ungulubhi amwimishe hukhono gwakwe ulilo, abheshele abhe Gosi abhe mwokozi, hwa Israeli, nkabhalambe embibhi abhasajila.
ACT 5:32 Ate tilibhaketi bhega gonti, nu Mpepo Ufinjile, Ungulubhi yabhapelile bhaala bhabhahumwitiha.”
ACT 5:33 Ajumbe bhi baraza nabhumvwa isho elyoyo lyabhakhata bhaga bhabhabude atuwe.
ACT 5:34 Ufarisayo umo itawa lyakwe yu Gamalileli, ali mwalimu we sheria, yahemehwaga sana na bhantu waga abhantu ebo bhafume panze nasoti.
ACT 5:35 Halafu wabhabhuula waga amwe, “Mubhalume mubha Israeli, mwenye sana zyamulwabhombe na bhantu ebha.
ACT 5:36 Ahali umuntu itawa yu Theuda ahwibheshele huje muntu gosi, sana abhantu mia nne bhafutile. Umuntu uyo bhahabuda bhonti bhabhafuataga bhanyampine nategane.
ACT 5:37 Ahali uwamwabho ali yo Yuda wa hugalilaya, lwabhahabhazyaga abhantu(esensa) wope atejile na bhantu bhakwe bhonti bhanyampene.
ACT 5:38 Eshi embabhuula abhantu ebha bhaleshi embombo ene nkayabhantu ebhateje yene.
ACT 5:39 Lelo nkashele ya Ngulubhi, semubhajiye aiwezye; musahabhoneshe huje mulwa nu Ngulubhi.” Bhamweteshela zyayanjile.
ACT 5:40 Bhabhakwizya bhinjila munyumba bhabhakhoma, nabhabhuule huje musahayanje nante hwitawa eli elya Yesu, bhabhaleha bhasogola.
ACT 5:41 Bhasogola shabhashiye aje tikhomwa hunongwa yitawa elya Yesu nazalauliwe.
ACT 5:42 Ensiku nzyonti mwikanisa bhalumbililaga na manyizye abhantu aje uYesu yu Kilisti nu mwokozi.
ACT 6:1 Ikanisa palyahonjelelaga akule abhantu bhahabha bhinji, gahanda abhe amalulumwo hwa shirika Ayahudi abheshi Yunani bhabhalulumwaga aba Ebrania, huje afwele bhabho sebhabhagabhilaga shinza eshalye bhabhewaga.
ACT 6:2 Atumwe bhabhakwizya ashirika bhonti, bhahaga seshinza ate alileshe izu lya Ngulubhi na bhatenganye amwe humambogeshalye.
ACT 6:3 Eshi salulii abhantu saba abhinza bhabhali nu Mpepo Ufinjile tibhabhishe humbombo ene.
ACT 6:4 Nate tibhakhale na deele mwizu lya Ngulubhi na puute.”
ACT 6:5 Ezyo enongwa zyabha nyinza bhasalula u Stefano, umuntu uwelweteshelo nu Mpepo Ufinjile, nu Filipo, Prokoro, Nikanori, Timoni, Parmena, na Nikolao, wa hu Antiokia.
ACT 6:6 Bhabhaleta hwa tumwe, abhantu ebha, bhabhapuutila na bhabhabheleshela amakhono gabho.
ACT 6:7 Izu lya Ngulubhi lyavwambana na ashirika bhonjelela mu Yelusalemu bhope agosi bheshibhanza bhabhinji bhalyeteshe izu lya Ngulubhi.
ACT 6:8 Nu Stefano, muntu yali ne neema nikhone abhombaga amambo minji aga Ngulubhi agaswijizye hwa bhantu.
ACT 6:9 Lelo bhahinza abhantu abhe Sinagogi lyalihwefwa Mahuru, nelya Bhakirene nelya Waeskanderia, na bhahukilikia na hu Asia. Abhantu ebha bhabisaniaga nu Stefano.
ACT 6:10 Lelo, sigabhawezizye ashindane nu Stefano umwene ali ne hekima nu Mpepo Ufinjile yayangaga mwa Stefano.
ACT 6:11 Abhantu ebho bhayanga na bhantu bhabhasuliha bhaga, “Mugaje uStefano aligaga uMusa nu Ngulubhi tumviwizye tete.”
ACT 6:12 Bhabhabuula azee, nasimbi, bhabhala bhakhata uStefano, bhaleta hwi baraza.
ACT 6:13 bhabhaleta aketi abhilenga, bhaga, “umuntu unu sigaleha ayanje embibhi epa apa tuntumu ahuliga wu Ngulubhi nesheria ya Musa.
ACT 6:14 Tumvwizye nayanga huje bhashi uYesu abhapananganye esheria zyetu ezyeshikhaya zyatapelilwe nu Musa.”
ACT 6:15 Shila muntu yaali pibaraza amaso gakwe gamwenya hulineshi umalaika.
ACT 7:1 Ugosi we shibhanza waga,”ezi enongwa zye lyoli”?
ACT 7:2 U Stefano wagamula waga, “Bhaholo bhane na bhaise bhane ntejelezi zyeyanga: Ungulubhi yabhunishie uise wetu u Ibulahimu nahali hu Mesopotamia, sasele asamile ensi ene eye hu Harani,'
ACT 7:3 Ungulubhi ahabhuula ahagu epa awe munsi ene usame ubhale hunsi yembahulanje'.
ACT 7:4 Wasogola wasama hunsi ya Hukardayo wakhala hu Harani, afume epo, uise wakwe nawafwiwa, Ungulubhi waleta munsi ene yabhakhala eshi.
ACT 7:5 Sigapiya nahamo ahagale, siga alinapo ata pibhishe eshinama. Lelo Ungulubhi alaginye u Ibulahimu sasele apate umwana huje aipelwa ensi ene aje aiigala nabhana bhakwe.
ACT 7:6 Ungulubhi ayanjile nawo eshi abhana bhaho hunsi eyeshijinyi na akhaya bhaibhabhiha bhaboyi bhabho(bhafubhilwa) nantele bhaibhabhomba embibhi humahaemia zine 400.
ACT 7:7 Ungulubhi ahaga naibhalonga abhantu bhabhaibhabhombela embibhi abhe ensi eyo, abhantu bhane naibhagalusya bhayenza ampuute ane munsi ene.'
ACT 7:8 Wapela uIbulahimu ilagano lye tohara, u Ibulahimu wabha ise wa Isaka watahiri isiku elya nane; u Isaka wabha ise wa Yakobo, uYakobo wabha yise wa yise bhetu ilongo na bhabhili.
ACT 7:9 Aise bhetu bhalolela ukero(umwone) uYusufu bhakazya hu Misri, Ungulubhi ali pandwimo nawo,
ACT 7:10 ungulubhi aponizye na malabha gonti, Ungulubhi wapela ineema, ne hekima hwa Farao, uFarao wabhiha aje abhe gosi munsi yonti na munyumba yakwe.
ACT 7:11 Enzala ihagwiye hunsi yonti eya hu Misri ba hu Kanani, abhantu bhapiite amalabha sana abhaise bhetu sebhali neshalye.
ACT 7:12 U Yakobo nawumvwa huje hu Misri, hulineshalye, abhatumile aise bhetu ulwahwande.
ACT 7:13 Nabhabhalile ulwabhili uYusufu ahwibhonisizya hwa holo bhake aholo bha Yusufu bhamanyiha hwa Farao.
ACT 7:14 O Yusufu wabhatuma aholo bhakwe bhabhale humweje uise wabho na bhanji bhakhalaga nabho bhonti bhaali amalongo saba na bhasanu 75.
ACT 7:15 U Yakobo wiha hunsi ya hu Misri, umwene wafwa naise bhetu bonti.
ACT 7:16 Bhabhega mpaka hushekemu bhasyelwa munkungwa yakalile uIburahimu ne hela hwa bhana bha Hamori hula hu Shekemu.
ACT 7:17 Ululagano lula Ungulubhi lwalaginne nu Ibulahimu na lwapalamila, abhantu nabhonjelela uwinji hula hu Misri,
ACT 7:18 aheenza umfumu uwamwabho hu Misri, abhasuliha abhantu aje bhabhavitwe abha Israeli, nabude abhaana adodo aje bhasahonjelele apapane.
ACT 7:19 Umfumu uyo abhakhopela abhantu nabhasulishe, bhabhabhombile embibhi aise bhetu nataje abhana bhabho aje bhasahabhe bhoomi.
ACT 7:20 Ulwo uMusa aapepwe; ali mwinza hwa Ngulubhi, walelwa amezi gatatu muntumba ya ise.
ACT 7:21 Unyina watabhila ahatundu wazyema ne lami wabhala wataga umwale wa Farao wabhala watola walela neshi unyina.
ACT 7:22 U Musa wafundiziwa enfunizyo zyonti ezyeshi Misri; ali nikhone munongwa na bhombe.
ACT 7:23 Nawafisya amaha amalongo gane (40), wasiibha humwoyo aje ashuule hwa holo bhakwe abhana bha Israeli.
ACT 7:24 Walola uholo wakwe abhone lwa nu Mmisri watanjila wakhoma ula Umsri wabuda:
ACT 7:25 umwene asibhile huje aholo bhakwe bhabhaje ayinzele atokole Ungulubhi atumile fwanii aholo bhakwe sebhasibhile isho.
ACT 7:26 Isiku ilya mwabho wabhaga abha Israeli bhalwa bheene; walenga abhamulanye waga amwe mulibhaholo yeenu mulwa mubhene?
ACT 7:27 Ulayalwanga nuwamwabho wabunshila hula wabhuula waga wenu yabhishile awe aje ubhe tanzanyi wetu?
ACT 7:28 Uhwanzaje ungoje neshi uhagojile Ummisri ula igamo?”
ACT 7:29 U Musa washimbila ahwumvwe isho; wabhala hu Midiani, uhwo wabha yise wa bhana bhabhili.
ACT 7:30 Amaha amalongo gane nagashila, umalaika ahajendela hwijangwa mwatatango hahahaga umwoto.
ACT 7:31 U Musa ahaswiga ajawalola atatango hahwaha umwoto, lelo sehalungulila, nawalinga ahazubhilile, wumvwa izu liyanga,
ACT 7:32 'Ane ne Ngulubhi wa yise bhaho, uIbulahimu, nu Isaka, nu Yakobo'. U Musa wogopa nayinje se hwenye.
ACT 7:33 Ungulubhi wabhuula waga satula evilato vyaho, puyimiliye epa nsintuntumu.
ACT 7:34 Engalolile amalabha gabhantu bhane na mayemba gabhali nago hu Misri; Ane enishile abhavwe; eshi enza etume, ubhale hu Misri.'
ACT 7:35 Unu uMusa yabhakhine yabhajile wenu yabhishile awe ubhe gamulanyi wetu?'- Ungulubhi yatumile abhookole afumiye mumwoto atatango nahahahaga.
ACT 7:36 U Musa abhalongozizye afume hu Misri ashilile hwijangwa Ungulubhi abhombile amambo minji agaswijizye hu Misri ashilile hwa Musa bhalobhoshe ebahari abhalongozizye humaha amalongo nane'.
ACT 7:37 Yu Musa yunu yabhabhuulile abhantu huje Ungulubhi aibhaletela ukuwe yali neshane afume hulimwe'.
ACT 7:38 Unu muntu yaali hubhungano, hula hwijangwa nu malaika yayanjile nawo hwigamba lya Sinai. Unu yayula yaali na ise bhetu, unu yayula ahe eleye izu elyomi natipele ate.
ACT 7:39 Unu yayula aise bhetu bhahakhanile, bhabunshiye uhutali na humoyo gabho bhagalushe hu Misri.
ACT 7:40 Eshipindi esho bhahabhuula u Haruni.'bhahaga tilenganyizye ungulubhi(mangulubhi) atilongozye uMusa manyi zyazimwajile uhwo.
ACT 7:41 Bhagomba(bhalinganya) endama hunsiku izyo bhafumyia ne sadaka hundama bhaisungwa embombo ye makhono gabho.
ACT 7:42 Ungulubhi ahavitwa ahabhaleha bhapuute entondwe sazyasimbilwe eshakuwe aje mwamfumizizye ane esadaka ezyevyuma hwijangwa humaha amalongo gane amwe bha Israeli?
ACT 7:43 Muyetesha ihema elyatanganile elya Moleki ne ntondwa ya Ungulubhi refani, ne shifwani shamulingenye na puute hwa bhene: eshi embabhabhenje embabhatwale ohutali ashile hu Babeli.'
ACT 7:44 Aise bhetu bhaali ni hema elyatanganile, Ungulubhi shayanjile nu Musa huje alenganye neshi lila shalilolile.
ACT 7:45 Eli lihema aise bhetu, ojoshwa pabhaletaga ensi ene Ungulubhi pabhabhenjele akhaya aise bhetu sabhasile ahwinze ensi ene ezi zya esho mpaka ensiku ezya Daudi,
ACT 7:46 umwene ahetehwe nu Ngulubhi,' na alabhile ahwanze ukkhalo hwa Ngulubhi wa Yakobo.
ACT 7:47 Lelo u Sulemani azenjeye Ungulubhi enyumba.
ACT 7:48 Eshi umwene Ungulubhi sigaakha munyumba zyazizengwilwe namakhono neshi ukuwezya yanjile,
ACT 7:49 Emwanya litengo lyane elye ufumu na ensi pabhishe amanama gane. Mubhanzenjele nyumba wili?, ayanga Ungulubhi: na apatuye ane paposhi?'
ACT 7:50 Ukhono gwane segwagwogu gwabhombile ezi zyonti?'
ACT 7:51 Amwe mubhensingo ehome mwasigamtahiliwe amoyo na makutu, mwamuhupinga Umpepo Ufinjile,' mubhomba neshi shabhabhombaga aise benyu.
ACT 7:52 Kuwe wili hwa kuwe bhonti aise bhenyu bhasiga bhabhatesile? Bhabhabudile akuwe bhonti bhabhakuwaga ahwenze hwa ula Umuntu Umwinza,'neshi mulumenye na hubude,
ACT 7:53 amwe mwamwaposhiye esheria ela yamwalajiziwe nantele semwahanzaga aikhate.”
ACT 7:54 Ajumbe nabhonvwa enongwa ezyo zyabhavwalazya humwoyo bhamwenya eshibhibhi e Stefano.
ACT 7:55 Lelo umwene, uStefano abhe amemile Umpepo Ufinjile wenya amaso gakwe humwanya waulola utuntumu wa Ngulubhi,' nu Yesu akhiye hukhono ulilo gwa Ngulubhi.
ACT 7:56 U Stefano waga, “Enzilola emwanya zigushe nu Yesu ayimiliye hukhono ulilo gwa Ngulubhi.”
ACT 7:57 Lelo abhantu abhi baraza bhabwaga ibwago, igosi bhadinda amakutu gabho bhashimbilila bhakhata,
ACT 7:58 bhapanya hwunzi ye khaya bhakhoma na mawe” naketi bhasatula amenda gabho bhabhiha pamanama gasahala umo itawa yu Sauli.
ACT 7:59 Nabhahwendelela ahupuule na mawe umwene wenya amaso gakwe humwanya waga Yesu, ejelela eroho yane,'.
ACT 7:60 Wafugamila wakwizya hwizu igosi waga gosi wane Yesu usabhabhazizye embibhi ezi zyabhabhomba. “Nawayanga isho wapuma wafwa.
ACT 8:1 U Sauli ahali nabhohitihanaga ahubude u Stefano. Wope u Sauli na ahandile abhatese bhonti akristi habhahali mu Yerusalemu na bhonti bhabhanyampine bhaali humajimbo ga Yudea na hu Samaria, bhasagiye bha mitume bhene.
ACT 8:2 Abhantu bha Ngulubhi bhasyela uStefano bhazondiye enzondo engosi tee.
ACT 8:3 Lelo uSauli alitesile sana ikanisa. Ashilaga shila nyumba abhakhate na bhakwesanjile hwunze nabhaponyezya mulumande(mwijela) abhashe na bhalume, na kuwatupia gerezani.
ACT 8:4 Bhaala bhabhanyampine abheene bhalumbililaga izu lya Ngulubhi.
ACT 8:5 U Filipo ahishiye hu Samaria alumbililaga izu elya Ngulubhi.
ACT 8:6 Ubhungano nabhalola zyazibhombeha nu Filipo; bhazibheha humoyo gabho nahwitishile.
ACT 8:7 Abhantu bhabhali bhabhinu bhaponile amipepo mabhibhi gabhafumile abhantu uhu bhakholaawa na bhaala afwemanama bhaponile.
ACT 8:8 Ensi ela bhasungwile sana.
ACT 8:9 Ahali umuntu umo itawa lyakwe ali yu Simoni umuntu uyo alini tunga ashangazyaga tee ensi ya bha Samaria, umuntu uyo agaga umwene gosi saana bonti bhatimihaje.
ACT 8:10 Abhasamaria bhonti bhahatejelezya ahwande umwa paka agosi abhantu bhaga umuntu unu ezi zyabhomba zifuma hwa Ngulubhi.”
ACT 8:11 Bhatejelezya maana abhaswijizizye tee nsiku nyinji ni tuunga lyakwe.
ACT 8:12 Nabhahatejelezya uFilipo nalumbililaga uumwene uwa humwanya ni tawa lya Ngulubhi lyalyaponyaga abhantu ashilile hwitawa lya Yesu bhahoziwe alume na bhashe.
ACT 8:13 Wope uSimoni aheteshe ahoziwe nalileshe itunga lyakwe, ahendelela alongozanye nu Filipo; aswijile sana nahazilola Ungulubhi ashilile hwa Filipo zyazibhombeha ngosi tee.
ACT 8:14 Atume nabhahumvwa aje abhahu Samaria bhalyeteshe izi lya Ngulubhi, bhahabhatuma uPetro nu Yohana.
ACT 8:15 Nabhafiha hula bhabhapuutila aje bhaposheele Umpepo Ufinjile.
ACT 8:16 Ensiku zyonti izyo baalisile ahuposhele Umpepo Ufinjile bhonti lelo bhahoziwe hwitawa lya Yesu.
ACT 8:17 U Petro nu Yohana bhabhabhishila amakhono bhabhapuutila, bhope baposhela Umpepo Ufinjile.
ACT 8:18 U Simoni nawalola abhantu bhahuposhela Umpepo Ufinjile nabhabheshilwa amakhono na atume wanza aje abhapele ihela,
ACT 8:19 Waga, “Mpeli nane ouwezo, owo aje shila muntu yehubhishila amakhono aposhelaje Umpepo Ufinjile.”
ACT 8:20 U Petro wabhuula waga ihela zyaho nawe wayo mtejele uhwo ubhishile aje ekarama ya Ngulubhi tipelwa ni hela.
ACT 8:21 Suli ni hama hwu mbombo ene umwoyo gwaho segugoloshe hwa Ngulubhi.
ACT 8:22 Eshi laamba hwa Ngulubhi ulwinje abhahusajile ensebho zyaho embibhi ezyo.
ACT 8:23 Elola umwoyo gwaho segulishinza hunanchishe gupinyilwe ne mbibhi.”
ACT 8:24 U Simoni waga ilabha mumpuutile hwa Ngulubhi ezi zyamuyanjile zisahanaje.
ACT 8:25 U Petro nu Yohana pabhawelaga afume uhwo bhalumbiliye muvijiji vivinja evya Samaria pamande bhawela hu Yerusalemu.
ACT 8:26 Umalaika wa Ngulubhi wayanga nu Filipo waga sogola ushilile idala elya ntende(hu kusini) lwalihwishila hu Yerusalemu abhalile hu Gaza.” (Idala eli lili mwijangwa).
ACT 8:27 U Filipo wabhala. Walola umuntu uwa hwi Ethiopia, afumle apuute hu Yerusalemu umuntu unu ali hasule ali gosi hu nyumba ya malkia wa hwi Ethiopia.
ACT 8:28 Akhiiye mwi gari lyakwa abhazyaga ibhangili lya Isaya igari palijenda abhale amwabho.
ACT 8:29 Umpepo wabhuula uFilipo zubhilila hwi gari elyo upalamane nalyo.
ACT 8:30 “U Filipo walishimbilila igari lila wamwunvwa ula umuntu abhazya mwibhangili elya Isaya wabhuzya uzyiliwe zyubhazya umwo?”
ACT 8:31 Umuntu ula uMwiethiopia waga embahwelewe wili umuntu nkasiga andongozye? Wakhope lezya uFilipo aje ainjile mwigari lyakwe bhakhale bhonti.
ACT 8:32 Ibhangili lyabhazyaga pasimbilwe eshi alongoziwe neshi engole nabhabhalanayo asinze; apumile myee neshi engole, sigahiguye ilomu lyakwe:
ACT 8:33 Azugumile hwakwe alongwe hwakwe hwa hepile: Weenu yaiyanga eshizazi shakwe(empapo yakwe)? amaisha gakwe gepile munsi.”
ACT 8:34 Ula uhasule mwithiopia wabhuuzya uFilipo unu umuntu yebhazya umu enongwa ezi zyakwe yuyo awe zya muntu winji”?
ACT 8:35 U Filipo wamwandila mwumwo munongwa zyabhazyaga mwibhangili lya Isaya hulumbilile izu lya Yesu.
ACT 8:36 Nabhandelela abhale bhafiha papali na menze ula uhasule wabhuzya uFilipo enya amenze ega epa henu hahansinti zya ahwoziwe?
ACT 8:37 u Filipo waga nkuyitishe ebhajiye ula Umwithiopia waga eneteshe huje uYesu mwana wa Ngulubhe, ula Umwithiopia wimiliha igari lyakwe.
ACT 8:38 Bhiha bhonti mwigari bhatumbushila mumenze, uFilipo nu mwithiopia uFilipo wamwozya(wabhatizya).
ACT 8:39 Nabhazubha afume muminzi bhonti Umpepo wanyatula uFilipo wasagala yu Mwithiopia mwene Umwithiopia wasogola nigari lyakwe abhalile shashiye humwoyo.
ACT 8:40 Lelo uFilipo abhuinishe hu azoto alumbililaga muvijiji na mujini mpaka afishile hu Kaisaria.
ACT 9:1 Lelo uSauli, ahindiliye atiisye abhantu bha Ngulubhi bhabhamwitishe uYesu, abhalile hwa Gosi uwishibhanza
ACT 9:2 alabhiile ekarata yesimbilwe alabhe abhakhate bhaala bhoonti abhidala eli bhabhali mumasinagogi abhalume nabhashe, abhapinye na bhale hub Yerusalemu.
ACT 9:3 Na hendelelaga ashuule apalanila afishe hu Dameski ulukhozyo lwahakhozya afume humwanya lwazyungula ponti',
ACT 9:4 uSauli wagwa pandi wumvwa izu lihukwizya liyiga Sauli, Sauli, yeenu ohumnvisya?”
ACT 9:5 U Sauli wagamu waga awe wenanu Gosi? Ugosi waga, “Ane ne Yesu wumnvisya nantese;
ACT 9:6 Lelo bhuuha ubhale hujini hwa wabhalaga ubhalabhuulwe ezyabhombe
ACT 9:7 Abhantu bhabhashuulile nu Sauli bhahapuma kati bhahumnvwa izu lelo umuntu yayanga sebhalolile.
ACT 9:8 U Sauli wabhuuha pansi ahalinga ahwenye ahega amaso segalola, bhakhata ukhono bhaleta paka hu Dameski.
ACT 9:9 Ensiku zitatu saa lya sigaamwela, siga ahwenya.
ACT 9:10 Ahali umanyile(umwanafunzi) hu Dameski itawa yu Anania, u Yesu wayanga nawo Anania. U Anania waga ane epa, Gosi.
ACT 9:11 “Ugosi waga bhuuha ubhale ushilile hwidala lyalihwitwa Nyofu, uyinjile munyumba ya Yuda ubhuzye aje umuntu yafumile hu Tarso umuntu uyo ali salaabha(alisapuuta);
ACT 9:12 alolilo humbonesyo umuntu itawa lyakwe yu Anania ahubhishila lyakwe yu Anania ahubhishila amakhono pitwe aje alole amaso.
ACT 9:13 U Anania wagamula uYesu waga inumnvwizye hwa bhantu bhinji embibhi zya bhabhombiye abhantu bhaho uhwo hu Yerusalemu;
ACT 9:14 Epa pope ali ne kalata yefumile hwa Gosi weshibha, abhakhate bhonti bhabhalikwizya itawa lyaho.
ACT 9:15 Lelo Ugosi uYesu waga bhalaga awe, umuntu uyo esaluye alyeje itawa lyane hwapagana hwamfumu bensi na hwa aIsraeli.
ACT 9:16 Embahulolesye amambo minji gaiteswa hunongwa yi tawa lyane”.
ACT 9:17 U Anania wabhala winjila munyumba mula wamwaga uSauli wabheshela amakhono waga wee Sauli, Ungulubhi ula yutangene nawo na winzaga ohu antumile upone ulole amaso na umposhele Umpepo Ufinjile.
ACT 9:18 Nawabheshela amakho, vyalagala evintu neshi amakhonda afume humaso amaso giguhawanda alole, wimilila, bhwoziwa; walya eshalye wapata ikhone.
ACT 9:19 Wakhala natumwe ohwo hu Dameska ensiku nyinji.
ACT 9:20 Ulwo wabha ahulumbillia uYesu huje Mwana wa Ngulubhi.
ACT 9:21 Abhantu bhonti bhaswiga bhaga seeyayunu yalavyaga abhantu bhahalikwizyaga itawa eli hula hu Yerusalemu? Ata hwohu ahenzeye mbombo yeyo aje abhakhate nabhatwale hwa gosi hu Yerusalemu.”
ACT 9:22 U Sauli apeete anguvu ezyalumbilile Ayahudi bhabhakhala hu Dameski bhachanganyikiwe nahulole huje uYesu aje lyoli yu Kilisiti.
ACT 9:23 Ensiku nazyashila zinyinji, Ayahudi bhetehana huje bhabude usauli.
ACT 9:24 Lelo uSauli wamanya bhamwubhilaga mundyango pasanya nu siku aje bhabude.
ACT 9:25 Bhaala bhabhamanyizyaga usauli bhahafumizya mwidirisha bhahapinyila eshitundu nulugalabho bhahamwisya ansoso.
ACT 9:26 U Sauli nawafiha hu Yerusalemu, ahalinga asangane nabha Kilisiti amwabho, lelo abhene bhase guhaga, sigabhahitishiye aje uSauli apendushe amweteshe uYesu.
ACT 9:27 U Barnaba wamwega na hutwale hwa mitume nabhabhuule shapendushe nesha tangine nu Yesu mwidala na bhala hu Dameski, neshalumbilye hu Dameski nkahwogope.
ACT 9:28 Atangine nabho nabhahinjilaga nafume mu Yerusalemu. Wayanga nkahwogope itawa lya Yesu,
ACT 9:29 abhuzanyaga na Ayahudi abheshi Yunani bhalingaga shila lisiku ahubude.
ACT 9:30 Aholo bhakwe nabhamanya ezyo bhatolosya bhatwala hu Kaisaria, aje abhale hu Tarso.
ACT 9:31 Eshi ikanisa elya Uyahudi na hu Samaria na hu Galilaya lya hatengaana lyahagwizya umwoyo nu Mpepo Ufinjile ahabhatenganya ikanisa lyahonjelela uwinji.
ACT 9:32 U Petro pazyungulaga ohu wuihwo alumbilile ibhangili ahafiha hu Lida abhajendea Kilisiti bhabhali uhwo.
ACT 9:33 Ohwo walola umuntu umo itawa lyakwe yu Ainea, ubili gwakwe alizilisu humaha nane; maana alikuwa amepooza.
ACT 9:34 U Petro wabhuula waga, “Ainea, uYesu Kilisti ahuponya bhuhapugonile, U Ainea wapona wa bhuha.
ACT 9:35 Abhantu bhonti bhabhakalaga hu Lida nahu Sharoni nabhahalola umuntu uyo bhahapenduha bhahamweteha uYesu.
ACT 9:36 Ahali umwanafunzi umo hu Yafa itawa yu Tabitha, emaana yakwe hwa huje “Dorkasi” Ushi unu abhabhombelaga enyinza abhantu apiina.
ACT 9:37 Lumo ahabhina empuungo ahafwa bhahamwozya bhahagonia hwigulu.
ACT 9:38 E Lida sigayali hutali ne Yafa, bhatuma abhanafunzi hwa Petro abhantu bhabhili bhabhuula uPetro bhaga usahakhabhie saali hu mwitu”.
ACT 9:39 U Petro wabhuuha walongozanya nabho. Nabhafiha bhatwala hwigulu, abhashe abhafwile bhalanga amakoti na menda gabhasonelaga u Dorkasi nahali sha mwomi.
ACT 9:40 U Petro wabhafumia panzi bhonti nabhafuma uPetro wafugamila wapuuta, wapuutila uDorkasi wadamula amaso walola uPetro, wakhala pansi.
ACT 9:41 U Petro wakhata ukhono wabhusya wabhakwizya bhaala abantu bhabhafumizye hwunzi na bhinjila wabapela umuntu wabho ali mwomi
ACT 9:42 Ezi zyazibhombishe zyamanyiha hu Yafa hwonti abhantu bhabhinji bhapenduha bhagalushila uYesu.
ACT 9:43 U Petro ahakhiye ensiku zye nyinji hu Yafa nu muntu umo itawa yu Simoni, yalinganyaga insungwa.
ACT 10:1 Ahali umuntu umo hunsi ya hu Kaisaria, itawa ali yu Kornelio, ali gosi weshipuga eshe Kiitalia.
ACT 10:2 Ali muntu wa Ngulubhi na afumiaga esadaka zinyinji abhapelaga abhantu, aputaga hwa Ngulubhi ensiku zyonti.
ACT 10:3 Yahali saa tisa ezya pasanya ahalola embonesyo ahalola umalaika ahwenza hwa mwene ula umalaika wabhuula u “Kornelio!
ACT 10:4 U Kornelio wamwenya tee ula umalaika, wayeta tee waga huliyenu gosi? Umalaika waga esadaka zyaho ne mpuuto zyaho zifishile hwa Ngulubhi na zilizyahwizushe.”
ACT 10:5 Bhatume abhantu hu Yafa bhakwizye uPetro.
ACT 10:6 Akhala hwa Simoni yalinganya ensunga enyumba yakwe eli munsenje ye bahari.”
ACT 10:7 Ula umalaika nawasogola, u Kornelio wabhakwizya aboyi bhakwe bhabhili nu sikari umo yaputaga nawo nahubhombele embombo.
ACT 10:8 U Kornelio wabhabhuula zyonti zyazilolile wabhatuma hu Yafa.
ACT 10:9 Nabhaapulamila afishe hujini, u Petro wazubha hwigulu apuute.
ACT 10:10 Nantele enzala yalumile tee nabhali ateleshe walola embonesyo,
ACT 10:11 walola emwanya eyigushe walola ahantu hali neshumwenda hahwiha pansi ne nshenje zine.
ACT 10:12 Muhati yakwe vyahali evintu vyonti evyomi vyaviliwa manama gane, ne vyavihwavula nevyaviluha humwanya.
ACT 10:13 Wumnvwa izu liyanga lyaga Petro sinza ulye”.
ACT 10:14 U Petro waga sigaembwahile alya evintu evichafu.
ACT 10:15 U Petro wumvwa nantele ulwabhili izu liyiga vyazijozizye Ungulubhi uganje ayanje huje vibhibhi.
ACT 10:16 Eli lyabhombisha hatatu hala ahombo hazubha humwanya nantele.
ACT 10:17 U Petro nasibha embonesyo izyo, abhantu bhabhatumwilwe nu Kornelio bhabhabhafishile bhemeleye mundyango bhabhuzilizya enyumba yali uPetro.
ACT 10:18 Bhabhuuzilizya aje uSimoni yahwetwa Petro nkakhala omu.
ACT 10:19 U Petro pali seebhe embonesyo zila Umpepo Ufinjile wabhuula huja abhantu bhatatu bhahuhwanza hwonze.
ACT 10:20 Bhuha iha panji ulongozanye nabho embatumile weene leha ahwogope.”
ACT 10:21 U Petro wabhaga bhimiliye wabhabhuzya mwenzeye yeenu? Nene nemunanza?”
ACT 10:22 Atitumile umuntu umo gosi weshipuga muntu puuti, abhuulelwe nu malaika aje ubhale akhaya yakwe ayumvwe zyuli nazyo.”
ACT 10:23 U Petro wabhakaribisya munyumba, shampwiti yakwe bhasogola bhonti, u Petro wabega abhantu abhahu Yafa bhashe bhalongozanya nawo.
ACT 10:24 Shandabho yakwe bhafiha hu Kaisaria. Bhamwaga uKornelio abhaguulila abhunginye ajirani bhakwe na bhaala bhonti bha munyumba yakwe.
ACT 10:25 U Petro nawafiha u Kornelio wabhala huposhe waundamila mmanama gakwe abhonesye huje atinishe.
ACT 10:26 U Petro wabhusya waga ane nanee endi muntu neshiawe.”
ACT 10:27 U Petro naliyanje nawe ayinjila anyumba wega abhantu bhabhungine bhabhinji.
ACT 10:28 Wabhabhuula huje amwe mwemwe mulolile huje ate namwe setisangana. Lelo Ungulubhi andamiye aje usahabhakwizye abhantu bhembozizye ane aje bhachafu.
ACT 10:29 Ndiyo maana ewenzele eshi muyanje zyamunkwizizizye.”
ACT 10:30 U Kornelio wagamula waga ensiku zine zyashilile esala neshi ezi nalipuute munyumba yane, umuntu winza akwite amenda amazelu,
ACT 10:31 Wambula waga “Kornelio empuuto zyaho ne sadaka zyaho zifishile humwanya hwa Ngulubhi nazili zyahwizushe hwa mwene.
ACT 10:32 Eshi tuma umuntu hu Yafa ukwizya uSimoni yahwitwa Petro akhala hwa muntu yahwitwa Simoni yalinganya ensunga enyumba yakwe eli munshenje ye bahari.
ACT 10:33 Nabhahwinze umwene abhayanje namwe.
ACT 10:34 U Petro wayanga waga lyoli neteha huje Ungulubhi siga ali no upendeleo.
ACT 10:35 Umuntu yayonto yahumwitiha umwene wope Ungulubhi ahumweteha umuntu uyo.
ACT 10:36 Enongwa zyayangaga na bha Israeli zyali zya bhantu abhe mataifa gonti ashilile hwa Yesu Kilisti-
ACT 10:37 namwe bhayo mumenye lyalya fumiye hu Yudea hwonti na lyahandiye hu Galilaya u Yohana nawatangazya ahwoziwe.
ACT 10:38 Lila lyalyabhombehaga nu Yesu Ungulubhi apishe amafuta aga Umpepo Ufinjile ni khone abhalaga aponile abhantu bhabhayembaga nu shetani Ungulubhi ali pandwemo nawo.
ACT 10:39 Ate tilibhaketi bha mambo gonti gagabhombishe hunsi zya Uyahudi na hu Yerusalemu-unu uYesu yabhabudile na hulembezye mwikwi.
ACT 10:40 Unu umuntu Ungulubhi azyusizye isiku elyatatu na manyihane,
ACT 10:41 siga hwa bhantu bhonti umwene abhonishe hwa abhantu bhakwe bhabhasaluye, ate tetalyanga nawo na mwele nawo nawazyuha afume hwa bhafwe.
ACT 10:42 Atilajizizye alumbilile hwa bhantu bhonti aje unu yabhehwelwe nu Ngulubhi aja abhe gamulanyi wa bhafwe na bhomi.
ACT 10:43 Na akuwe bhakuwilwe, huje shila muntu yaihumwitiha aisajilwa embibhi zyakwe ashilile hwitawa lyakwe.”
ACT 10:44 U Petro nahendelelaga ayanje Umpepo Ufinjile wabhinjila abhonti bhabhali munyumba mula bhabhatejelezyaga.
ACT 10:45 Bhaala bhahenzele nu Petro bhabhatahiriwe- bhaswijile tee huje bhope amataifa(apagani) Ungulubhi abhapeela Umpepo Ufinjile.
ACT 10:46 Bhabhahumvwizye bhayanga injango ezyenje na hulumbilile Ungulubhi. U Petro waga,
