1CO 11:6 Nke unshi agubishe itwe lyakwe asyenkule insinsi zyakwe ziwe mfupi. Maana zyinso umuntu unshi asyenkule insisi zyakwe au akatwe basi azigubishe itwe lyakwe.
1CO 11:7 Si hwanziwa unume agubishe itwe lyakwe, pipo umwene shifani ishi tuntumu uwa Ngulubhi. Lakhini tuntumu uwanume.
1CO 11:8 Unume sagahafumile hwa nshi ila unshi ahafumiline nu nume.
1CO 11:9 Unume saga abhumbilwe kwajili ya nnshi. Ila unshi ahabhumbilwe kwajili ya nume.
1CO 11:10 Ndyo maana unshi ahwanziwa abhe ishala na mamlaka hwitwe lyakwe kwa sababub ya malaika.
1CO 11:11 Hata shimisho hwa Gosi, unshi nuno bila nume au unume nila nshi, unume numo.
1CO 11:12 Maana ndeshe unshi nkahafumile hwa nume, shishila unume ahafumiline nu nshi. Ni vintu vyonti vifuma hwa Ngulubhi.
1CO 11:13 Muyilonje mwimimwi: Lyoli! unshi apute Ungulubhi bila agubishe itwe lyakwe?
1CO 11:14 Afume imandi sebhamanyizya iya huje unume nkabha ni nsisi intali tuntumhukwakwe? maana apewilwe zila insisi intali ndeshe umwanda wakwe?
1CO 11:15 Je afume imandi sebhamanyizya huje unshi nkabha ni nsisi intali tuntumu wakwe?
1CO 11:16 Maana apewilwe zila insisi intali ndeshe umwenda wakwe. Nku umuntu wowonti ahwanza adalisye wala ishibhanza sha Ngulubhi.
1CO 11:17 Hundajizyo zyezihwinza, ani sihubhatima. Maana amwi lwe mubhungana se hwi faida ila huhasala.
1CO 11:18 Maana ihumvwa, huje lwe mubhungana mshibhanza, huli nu lugabhanyo kati yinyu nani hadodo ihwitiha.
1CO 11:19 Kwa ihwanziwa zibhe intaamyo kati yinyu aje bhabhaala, bhebhitihwilwe bhamanyishe hulimwe.
1CO 11:20 Maana lemubhungana shemulya seshalye sha Gosi.
1CO 11:21 Lwe mulya kila muntu alya ishalye shakwe yuya kabla ya bhanji sebhaliye. hata unu ali ni nzala, unu akholilwe.
1CO 11:22 Je semuli ni nyumba iyalile na mwelele? Je mzarabhunye ishibhanza sha Ngulubhi na hubhapele insoni bhesebhali na Hantu? Njanje henu hulimwe? Imbatime? Simbatuma hwi ili!
1CO 11:23 Maana nahaposhile afume hwa Gosi shila shimbapiye amwi aje Ugosi uYeesu, usiku alongwa ahejile ikati.
1CO 11:24 Baada ya salifye, abhuvunzile naje ubhu wembili wani, “Ubhu we mbili wani, wewili kwaajili yinyu. Mubhombe ishi hunkumbushe ani.”
1CO 11:25 Nashinishi ahejile inshikombe baada yalye, naje “Ishikombe ishi ndajizyo midanda lyani.” Mbhombe ishi hahinji kila le mumwela hwa hunkumbushe ani.”
1CO 11:26 Uwakati wowonti lemulya ishalye ishi na hushimwelele ishikombe, mlumbilila ufwewa Yesu mpaka lwa hayiyinza.
1CO 11:27 Kwa hiyo wowonti ya lya ishalye au hushimwelele ishikombe isho isha Yesu sheyihwanziwa, abhabhe ayipiye ubhibhi wimbili ni danda lya Yesu.
1CO 11:28 Umuntu ayibhuzilizye yuyo asuti, nkalyanje ishalye na mwelele ishikombe.
1CO 11:29 Maana yalya na mwele bila asubhilile ubili alya na mwele alongwe hwakwe yuyo.
1CO 11:30 Nduyo maana abhantu abhinji bhabhinu bhamo bhafwiye.
1CO 11:31 Lakhini nke twayenya timti setahayilongwa ishibhakaka.
1CO 11:32 Ila lyetilongwa nu Yesu, tiwelwa ili huje tisahalongwe peka ni nnsi.
1CO 11:33 Ishi, bhakaka na dada bhani, lwe mubhungama mpate alye, mugulilane.
1CO 11:34 Umuntu nkani nzala alye hukhaya yakwe hujelwe mubhungana peka nsahabhe hulongwi humambo aganjige msimbile naibhabhuzya lyenayiyinza.
1CO 12:1 Ahusu ikalama izyamumwoyo, aka na dada bhani sihwanza musahamanye.
1CO 12:2 Muminye lwe mwahai bhapanzi mwahalongozewilwe afwate humadala gogo gesagamwalongoze wizyo nago.
1CO 12:3 Ishi ihwanza huje mumanye aje numo wowonti yayanga hu Mpepo wa Ngulubhi ayanga aje “U Yesu alaniwilwe.” Numo wowo yayiyanga, “UYesu yu Bwana,” ila hwa Mpepo Umfinjile.
1CO 12:4 Ishi naziliho ikalama tofauti, ila Umpepo yeyula.
1CO 12:5 Na kuna huduma tofauti tofauti, bali Bwana ni yeye yule.
1CO 12:6 Huli iaina mbali mbali, izyi mbombo, lakini Ungulubhi yeyula yazibhomba imbombo hubhonti.
1CO 12:7 Ishi kila muntu apewa uufunuo uwampe hufaida ya bhonti.
1CO 12:8 Maana umuntu weka apewa inzwi nu Umpepo uwihekima, nu winji izwi lyi maarifa uMpepo yuyula.
1CO 12:9 Hwa winji ahumpela ulwitiho hu Mpepo yeyula, na hwa winji ikalama iya uponyaji hwa Mpepo weka.
1CO 12:10 Hwa winji amatendo aginguvu, nu winji ukuwa. Na hwa winji uuwezo uwa pambanule umpepo, nu uwi aina mbalimbali izyi lugha na hwawinji itafasili zyi lugha.
1CO 12:11 Lakhini uMpepo yuyula yabhomba imbombo izi zyonti ahumpela, kila muntu ikalama ndeshe shachagula umweene.
1CO 12:12 Ndeshe shila umbili weka, wope umbili huli ni vilungo ivyinji, vyonti vyimbili bhubhulashi shanisho nu Kilisiti.
1CO 12:13 Kwa maana hu Mpepo weka hamna Abhayahudi au Bhayunani, huje twebhatumwa au huru na tentitahamwelile uMpepo weka.
1CO 12:14 Kwa maana umbili sashiungo sheka ila vyinji.
1CO 12:15 Nkushe inama libhayanje, “aje ani siganyobhe, nani wayo indi sehemu ya mbili,” iyo seyibhubhomba aje husahabhe mu yi mbili.
1CO 12:16 Na nkeshele ibhutwi libhanje anisindi linso ani sehemu yi mbili, “iyo lyo seyihuyibhomba aje saga sehemu yimbili.
1CO 12:17 Nkushele numbili wonti bhubhabhe maso, handi hulihwoshi ubhahwumvwe? Nkushele ubili wonti bhubhe likutwi, Wenu uwanunsye?
1CO 12:18 Lakini Ungulubhi ahabhishile kila shilungo isha mbili amahali pakwe ndeshe shapanjile yuyo.
1CO 12:19 Nankushele vyonti vyahali ishilungo sheka, umbili hunibhuli hwi?
1CO 12:20 Ishi ivulungo vyinji, lakini umbili gweka.
1CO 12:21 Ilyinso selingubhuzya unkhono, “sindinuhaja nawe.” Wa itwe selinga vibhuzya ivinama sindi ni haja nawe.”
1CO 12:22 Lakini ivilungo ivyi mbihi vyevilo leha aje vili ni heshima hadodo vihwanziwa hani.
1CO 12:23 Ni vilungo ivyi mbili vyulola aje vili ni heshima hadodo tuvipela iheshima hani ni virungo vyitu vyesevili nu mvuto vilinuwinza hani.
1CO 12:24 Ni shi ivirungo vyitu vyesavili nu mvuto sevili ni haja iyapewe iheshima, kwa kuwa tayari vina heshima. Lakini Mungu ameviunganisha viungo vyote pamoja, hani ya vila vyeseviheshimiwa.
1CO 12:25 Abhabhombile isho ili pasahabhe nu lugabhanyo ulwi mbili ila ivilungo vyonti vitunzane hulugano lwa peka.
1CO 12:26 Lwe ishilungo sheka nkesha vwalala, ivilungo vyonti vivyalata au sheka nkeshitimwa iviungo vyonti visha peka.
1CO 12:27 Ishi amwi mbili wa Kilisti, na ivirungo kila sheka shene.
1CO 12:28 Na Umurungu ambhile mwikanisa abhande atumwa abhombili akuwa, abatu abhalimu, na bhala bhebhabhomba amatendo amagosi, alafu ikalama izyauponwe bhala bhebhahwavwa bhala bhebhabhomba imbombo izyalongozye, na bhonti bhebhali ni aina mbalimbali izyi lugha.
1CO 12:29 Ati tenti bhatumwa? Ati tenti bhakuwa? Tenti bhalimu? Tenti tibhomba amatendo agimaujiza?
1CO 12:30 Je ati tili ni kalama iya uponyaji? Tenti tiyanga ilugha? Tenti titafsili ilugha?
1CO 12:31 Mwanze sana ikalama ingosi. Hani imbabhalolesye idala ilyinza hani.
1CO 13:1 Tije huje iyanga ikabila zya bhantu ni zya malaika. Nkushele sindi ni nulugano indi shaba yililila nuupatu wewavuma.
1CO 13:2 Na huje indi ni kalama iyi unabii nu ummanye uwilyoli zyeziyifishile na maarifa aje indi nu lwitiho ulwasamye amagamba. Lelo huje nkesindi nu lugano na hamo ahantu.
1CO 13:3 Na tije huje imunya ivintu vya ni na hubhalisye apina na huje injifumya umbili gwani aje impye numwoto. Nkushe sindi nu lugano nahamo ahantu.
1CO 13:4 Ulugano bhujimba bhufadhili. Ulugano sebhuyitufya au huyilole. Sebhuli ni ngosi
1CO 13:5 au uwandilizi. Sebhuhwanza amambo gakwe, sebhulola ukhali haraka, wala sebhubhazya amabhibhi.
1CO 13:6 Sebhusha huwalangani. Badala yakwe, bhusha ni lyoli.
1CO 13:7 Ulugano lujimbila amambo gonti luhwitiha amambo gonti, bhuli nu dandamazu humambo gonti.
1CO 13:8 Ulugano selumaliha. Nkushe huli na akuwa, bhanzashile. Nkushele huli iluga zinzashile. Nkushele huli na maarifa ganzashile.
1CO 13:9 Pipo timinye aje husehemu tibhomba ukuwa.
1CO 13:10 Lakini aje ila yiliho sikamilishe ila yesili kamili yayishila.
1CO 13:11 Le nahali mwana, nahayanjile ndeshe umwana, nahasibhililaga ndeshe umwana, nahamulaga ndeshe umwana. Nahamulaga ndeshe umwana, Leunahabha gosi, nahabhishile apatali amambo gishana.
1CO 13:12 Pipo isalizi tilola ndeshe hwigarasi ndeshe amaso huhisi, lakhini isiku lila tahayilolana humaso maso. Ishi imanya huje kwa sehemu, lakhini uwakati bhula nahayimanya hani aje shimanyihana haani.
1CO 13:13 Ishi amambo iga gatatu gadumu ulwitiho usubhizyo lyelihwinza nuu olugano. Lakini igosi hani ulugano.
1CO 14:1 Uwanze ulugano na tamani tee ekarama zwa rohoni, zaidi tee mpata afumye ulukuwo.
1CO 14:2 Maana umwahale yayanga kuvahulugha sayanga na bhantu ayanga no Ngolobhe. Afwanaje nomo yahwelewa afwanaje ayanga amambo gagafisishe katika Roho.
1CO 14:3 Lelo umwahale yafumya ukuwa, ayanga na bhantu na abhazenje abhapele umwoyo na abhafaliji.
1CO 14:4 Umwahale yayanga lugha ahwizenga yoyo, nantele umwahale yafumya ukuwa ashizenga eshibhanza.
1CO 14:5 Eshi etamani aje amwe mwenti myanje lulugha lelo zaidi yego etamani aje mfumyaie ukuwa. Umwahale yafumya ukuwe gosi ashile umwahale yayanga hu lugha (au abhaje uwafafanule), ili aje eshibhanza shipate azengwe.
1CO 14:6 Lelo eshi, kolu ni yilombo bhane nkenenze hwilimwe na ayanje hu lugha, embabhavzwe yenu amwe? Sebwezizwe, esipokuwa eyanga namwe hwidala elye ufunuo, au hwidala elye enjele au ukuwa au hwidala elye isambelezwo.
1CO 14:7 Nkashile evintu vyasevino womo nkashele efilimbi au eshinubi nkashele sezifumya izu zwazili payo, ibhamanyishewele aje huntushi hahahwanga?
1CO 14:8 Eshi nkashile ebhe endundwe ibhafumya izu lyaselimanyiha ni shanamna wele umntu abhamanye aje muda wele ungwa hwilenganye ungwa hwibho?
1CO 14:9 Shesho na mwe. Nkamfumye humele izu lyasaliliwazi ni kwa namna wele aelewe yamyanga? Mwabha myanga, na nomo yabhabhelewe.
1CO 14:10 Nemo ewasiwasi aje elugha nyinji aziminji munsi, na nemo hata emo yaselinemana.
1CO 14:11 Antele nkebhe semenye imana eyelugha, ambabhe jenyi hwamwahale mwene yayanga wape yayanga abhabhe jenyi hwiline.
1CO 14:12 Shesho na mwe. Afwatanaje mtamani tee alole ahavisye kikisye wa Roho, anzi aje mzidi tee alizenje ibhanza.
1CO 14:13 Eshe, umwahale yayanga hu lugha na alabhe apewe afanule.
1CO 14:14 Nkashele nkendabha hu lugha eroho yane elabha lelo enjele zwane sezinamadondo.
1CO 14:15 Embombe yenu? Embalabhe huroho yane, antele embalabhe hunjele zwane. Imbatele huroho yane na mbatele hunjele zwane antele.
1CO 14:16 Antele nkalombe Ongolobhe huroho mwene yalijenyi abhahweteshewele “Amina” nofumya emwasalipa, wakoti sazimenye zwoyanda?
1CO 14:17 Antele lyoli awe usalifwa shinza, antele ula uwenje sazengwa.
1CO 14:18 Ehusalifwa Ungolobhe afwatanaje eyanga hu lugha zaidi yamwene mwenti.
1CO 14:19 Lelo mwibhanza ni heri enjanje amanzu ngasanu hunjele zwane ili embamanyezwe abhaje, zaidi eyayanje enongwa kumi elfu hu lugha.
1CO 14:20 Nkolo no yilombo bhane, mgajebhe bhana katika asebhe hwenyu. Badala yakwe, mhwa vwanu nembibhi, bhanji neshi abhana abhela. Lelo katika asebhe hwenyu mubhe bhantu bhagosi.
1CO 14:21 Isibwilwe katika sheria hwabhantu abhe lugha ezwamwao na humalomu agajenyi embayanje na bhantu ebha. Wala antele sebhanza novwe ayanga uGosi.
1CO 14:22 Esho enjango mbonesyo sio hwabhalinalyeteho hwa bhala bha sebhamolyeteho lelo afumye ukuwe mboneseyo hwabhelyeteho elelo hwabhala bhabhali no lyeteho.
1CO 14:23 Eshi, nkebhe eshibhanza shonti shitangene pandwemo na bhonti bhayanga enjango na unjenyi na bhasebhali nolyeteho bhinjie, je sebhanzayanje aje namna azimu?
1CO 14:24 Lelo nkebhe mwenti mfumya ukuwe yasali nolyeteho au unjenyi winjila abhavutwe nagonti gabhahovwe abhalongwe na gonti gagayangwa.
1CO 14:25 Esiri ezwe mwoyo wakwe nkazifunuliwa. Amantikeo yakwe, wenzagagwa ahwina mehwinama na hupute Ongolobhe. Wenzaga humweteshe aje Ungolobhe alipamoja namwe.
1CO 14:26 Henu hahafwata eshi nkolo no yilombo bhane? Namtangana pandwemo shila muntu ane Zaburi, ana sembelezwo ane mbonezwo ane njango au afasiri. Bhombi kila hantu ili mlizenje ibhanza.
1CO 14:27 Nkashile kila muntu ayanga hunjango, bhabhaje bhabhele au bhatatu na shila mntu shatanilane na umuntu lazima atafasiri haha ya ngwilye.
1CO 14:28 Lelo nkashile nomo umntu wa tafsiri, basi kila muntu akhale kati mhati mshibhanza. Basi kila muntu ayaje mwene hwa Ngolobhe.
1CO 14:29 Na akuwabhabhele au bhatatu bhayanje bhamwa bhatejelezwaje ili bhafasiri shashiyangwilwe.
1CO 14:30 Lelo yakheye nkawafunuliwa ijambo katika huduma ulayayangaga apomaje kati.
1CO 14:31 Afwatanaje shila muntu awezizwe afumye ukuwa amo baada ya wamwao ili aje shila muntu awezwe asambelele na bhonti bhawezwe apati omwoyo.
1CO 14:32 Afatanaje roho eya kuwazili pansi ya bhenyelezi bhabha kuwa.
1CO 14:33 Afwanaje Ungolobhe se Ngolobhe uwemabhibhi, bali we amani. Neshe sheli katika amabhanza gonti age bhelyeteho,
1CO 14:34 Mhwanziwa abhashe bhakhala je kati mwibhanza afwanaje sebhahwanziwa ayanje. Baada yakwe bhawaziwa abhe bhanyekevu neshe esheria seyanga.
1CO 14:35 Nkashile hahweli hahonti bhatamani asambele, basi bhabhabhoziwaje alume bhabho amwabho afwanaje soni hwa she ayaje mshibhanza.
1CO 14:36 Je izu elya Ngolobhe lyafumile hwilimwe? Je libhafishe amwe tu?
1CO 14:37 Nkashele omuntu ahwilola aje wakuwe au wa rohoni iwanziwa agamanya amambo gembasimbila agaje ndajizwo ezwa Gosi.
1CO 14:38 Lelo nkasagamenye ega hayaleshi agajetambuliwe.
1CO 14:39 Esho basi kolo na yilombo bhane, anzi tee afumye ukuwa wala mgaje huzubhile umuntu yoyonti ayanje unjango.
1CO 14:40 Lelo amambo gonti gabhombehaje huwinza na hutaratibu.
1CO 15:1 Eshi embizusya bha kolo na mwailombo juu yizu lyana bhalombeleye amba mwaliposheye na hwemelele nalyo.
1CO 15:2 Katika izu eli mwaushe nkashele mubhalikhate imara izu lyanabhalombeleye amwe afanaje mwaheteshe wene.
1CO 15:3 Nkashele pawandilo shanaposheye humuhimu naletile hwilimwe: neshe shehweli aje arengane ne nsimbo, Kristi afwiye kwajili yembibhi zwetu,
1CO 15:4 alengane nensimbo asyelelwe naje azwoshele isiku elyatatu.
1CO 15:5 Naje abhonesha bhwa Kefa, antele hwabhala kumi na bhabhele.
1CO 15:6 Antele abhoneshe hwa wakati umo abhoneshe hwa kolo na hwayiombo zaidi ya bhantu mia zisanu. Abhinji bado bhali womi, lelo bhamo bhagonile utulo.
1CO 15:7 Antele abhoneshe hwa Yakobo, antele abhonesha hwa tumwa bhonti.
1CO 15:8 Mwisho wa gonti, abhoneshe hwiline neshe shila hwa mwana yapepwe husiku zwasezilisawa.
1CO 15:9 Afwanaje ane endi dodo hwa mitume. Sehwanziwa akwiziwe mtume, eshabhanza esha Ngolobhe
1CO 15:10 Lelo hu neema eya Ngolobhe endi neshe shehali na neema yakwe hwaline seyali yewene. Badala yakwe nabhombile ebidii ashile wonti. Lelo senaline ne bali neema eya Ngolobhe yeli mhati yane.
1CO 15:11 Eshi nkashile nene au bhebho ulombelela esho taminile esho.
1CO 15:12 Eshe nkashele Kristi alombele we aje asyoshele hwa bhafwe, ebhe hwele mubhabhobho muyigo nahumo azwoshe bhabhafwiye?
1CO 15:13 Lelo nkashele nahumo azwoshe abhafwe basi hata Kristi sagazweshele.
1CO 15:14 Na nkashile Kristi sagazwoshele esho alombelele hwetu hubhe hwewene imani yetu abhe yewene.
1CO 15:15 Na tipatihene aje bhashahidi bhwilenka ahusu Ungolobhe kwa sababu tishuhudie Ungolobhe sha hwisalo aje azwozwe Kristi wakati sagazwozwezwe.
1CO 15:16 Nkashile abhafwe sebhazwoha, U Yesu wape sagazwoshele.
1CO 15:17 Nkashile Kristi sagazwoshele ahwamini hwetu ni bure na msele mlimbibhi zwenyu.
1CO 15:18 Esho hata bhala bhabhafwiye katika Kristi bhape bhatejele.
1CO 15:19 Nkashele humaisha ega gene yaje tilinoujasili hwa wakati wa wayenza mhati mwa Kristi abhantu wonti, atee tibhalongwe zaidi ya bhantu wonti.
1CO 15:20 Lelo eshi Kristi azwoshele afume hwabhafwiye, madodo agahwande gabhala bhabhafwiye.
1CO 15:21 Afwanaje efwa ehenzele ashilile umuntu, antele ashilile muntu azwosyewe hwa bhabhafwiye.
1CO 15:22 Afwatanaje nkashele katika u Adamu bhantu bhonti bhafwa, esho nantele katika Kristi bhayibhombwa womi wakati ubhenze hwakwe.
1CO 15:23 Lelo kila muntu katika shapajile hwakwe kristi madondo aga hwande antele bhala bhabhli Kristi bhayibhomba bhomi wakati uwahwenza hwakwe.
1CO 15:24 Ndipo waibha umalilo, pala uKristi nayibha akabidhi umwene uwa Ngolobhe uBaba. Ene pala nayibha akomesya oungozi wonti nemamlaka gonti ne nguvu zwonti.
1CO 15:25 Afwatanaje lazima atawale mpaka nayibhabheha abhibhibha kwe pansi eye magagakwe.
1CO 15:26 Ubhibhi uamalishile uwnankayiziwe efwa.
1CO 15:27 Afwanaje “abheshele kila hantu pansi pamanamagakwe.” Lelo neyanga abheshele kila hantu ni wazi aje ene sehusizwa bhala bhabhabhehwelwe kila muntu pansi yakwe yoyo.
1CO 15:28 Wakati evintu vyonti vibhehwelwe pansi yakwe, antele Umwana wakwe yoyo ayibhelwa pansi ya mwahele ambaye abheshele evintu vyonti pansi yakwe. Ene ebhoneshe ili kwamba Ungolobhe uBaba abhe gonti katika vyonti.
1CO 15:29 Au nantele bhabhombe yenu bhala bhabhahozwe kwajili bhabhafweye? Nkashile abhafwa sebhazwoha tee, yenu antele bhahozi wa kwajili yabho?
1CO 15:30 Naye nu tilimhatari kila sala?
1CO 15:31 Kolo na Yilombo bhane ashilile ahwisifu hwane katika amwe ambayo endinayo o katika Kristi Yesu Gosi wetu etangazwa eshe efwa kila lisiku.
1CO 15:32 Esaidila yenu katika enyelezwo ezwe bhanadamu nkashele nakhomene wanyama akhali ohwo hwa Efeso, nkashile bhabhafwiye? “Sebhazwoha leha basi tilyaje na mwele, afwanaje sandabho taifwa.”
1CO 15:33 Mganje akhopelwe sololile amabhibhi gunankanya etabia enyinza.
1CO 15:34 “Mubhanje nekiasi! mkhalaje katika lyoli mgaje ahwendele abhombo embibhi. Afwanaje bhamobhamo kati yenyu sebhanowelewa uwa Ngolobhe eyanga eshi kwa esoni zwenyu.
1CO 15:35 Lelo umuntu uhwenje abhayanje, Hwele abhafwe bhazwoha? Wape bhayenza neshe hwelebhwele nobele?”
1CO 15:36 Awe ulilema tee! shila shahatotile seshiwezizwe ahwande amele isipokua shifwiye.
1CO 15:37 Na shila shotota se bele ambao gwaibha bali mbeyu yechi puye ahwezizwe abhengano au hantu ahamwao.
1CO 15:38 Lelo Ungolobhe ayipela ubele shasongwelwe umwahale na katika kila mbeyu bele ngwakwe mwenyewe.
1CO 15:39 Amabele gonti segelengene isipokuwa gahweli amabele gwa bhantu ubele gumo gwe makoko na ubele gumo wenyonyi gumo kwe samaki.
1CO 15:40 Antele gahweli amabele amwanya na mabele agapansi. Lelo uhwinza wakwe ubele ugwamwanya ni halimo nowa pansi hwenje.
1CO 15:41 Huli uwinza umo wisaya na uwinza umo wemwezi, na uwinza umo wentondwe afwatanaje entondwe emo elegene nento ndwe uwinza.
1CO 15:42 Esho shashihweli nante azwozwewe bhabhafwiye shitotwa shinanjiha shashimela seshinanjiha.
1CO 15:43 Shitolilwe katika amatumizi agekawada shimezewa katika uwinza shitotilwa katika uswogusu shimezewa katika enguvu.
1CO 15:44 Shitotilwe katika ubele wa silishimezwa katika ubele ushiroho nkashile kuguhweli ubele ugwe asili gwape ugweshiro guhweli.
1CO 15:45 Esho antele esimbwilwe muntu uwa hwanda yuadamu abhombwelwe roho yekhala.” u Adamu uwamalisholo abhombeshe roho yefumya owomi.
1CO 15:46 Lelo uwe shiroho sagahenzele kwanza bali uwe asili napande uweshiroho.
1CO 15:47 Umuntu uwa hwande wa pansi alengenyezewe humankondi. Umuntu uwabhele afumile umwanya.
1CO 15:48 Neshe ula yalenganyiziwe humana ondi shesho antele bhala bhabhale ngenywe humankondi. Nkashile ula umuntu umbinguni shahweli nantele bhala abhamwanya.
1CO 15:49 Kama ambavyo tumebeba mfano wa mtu wa mavumbi, tutabeba pia mfano wa mtu wa mbinguni.
1CO 15:50 Eshe embabhola kolo na yilombo bhane aje ubele nedanda seviwezizwa aghale umwene uwa Ngolobhe, hata uwanankaye uwaghale wasiunajiha.
1CO 15:51 Enye! Embabhola amwe esiri eyelyoli: Hetaifwa ntenti bali tenti bhonti bhaigalunyiwa.
1CO 15:52 Taigalunyizwa katika uwa sizue na damlehwiliso katika endundwe eyahumalisho, afwatanale endundwe zwailila na bhabhafwiye bhaizwoha nehali eyesitenachishe.
1CO 15:53 Maana uu wananjishe lazima ukwate waseunanjiha nogu wa fwa lazima ukwate wasegwa fwe.
1CO 15:54 Lelo uwakati owo wa nachishe wakwatiziwa sintenachishe huu uwafwe nkaukwate usintefwe, ndipo gwayenza enjango ambao usibwilwe, “Efwa emililwe katika ashindwe.”
1CO 15:55 “Efwa umenezwe waho ulihwi? Fwa ulihwi ulwoyo ulihwi?”
1CO 15:56 Ulyoyo uwefwa ni ubhibhi na enguvu ye ubhibhi ni sheria.
1CO 15:57 Lelo ehusalifwa Ungolobhe, atipela ate amene ashilile uGosi wetu uYesu Kristi!
1CO 15:58 Eshi bhasungwena bhakolo na mwailombo bhanji imara na mgaje ayinje. Antele yibhombi embombo eya Gosi, kwa sababu mumenye aje embombo yenyu katika Gosi sio wene.
1CO 16:1 Eshi amasango hwa mwitu akristu, neshi shanalajizyaga humakanisa ga Hugalatia, muhwanziwa asanje.
1CO 16:2 Isiku limo hulungi shila muntu asanja ahantu hahonti abheshe habhe sango, aje nahaihwenza muhagaje sanguzanye.
1CO 16:3 Nihayinza, umuntu yayonti yamwaihusalula, ehaihutuma pandwemo nekalata eya sadaka zyamufumizye abhale nazyo hu Yerusalemu.
1CO 16:4 Nkasheshashisho, tabhalaje tenti nabho.
1CO 16:5 Lelo nahayenza hulimwe, ni haishilila hu Makedonia. Maana naishilila hu Makedonia.
1CO 16:6 Ulwenje nahaikhala namwe mpaka ensiku ezisasa zimalishe aje muhanavwe hunshulo yane hwahwonti hwebhala.
1CO 16:7 Eshi sigaehwenza abhalole maana esubhila ahwenze akhale namwe ensiku zyenyinji hashe nkashele Ungulubhi wanavwa.
1CO 16:8 Lelo naikhala hu Efeso mpaka ensiku ezye Pentekoste,
1CO 16:9 undyango ubaba gwigushe huliwe, na bhabha mvitwa binji bhabhampenga.
1CO 16:10 Eshi u Timotheo nawenza, mulole huje ali namwe bila ahwogope, abhomba embombo ya Ngulubhi, neshi shebhomba ane.
1CO 16:11 Umuntu yayonti asahazalaue. Mumwavwaje mwidala lyakwe. Hulutengano, ili ayenze huline. Ane ehusubhila aje ayenze na holo.
1CO 16:12 Holo wetu u Apolo. Napiye umwoyo tee huje ayenze abhajendelele amwe pandwemo na holo. Lakinin aliamua kutokuja kwa sasa. Hata hivyo, atakuja wakati ana nafasi.
1CO 16:13 Mubhe maso, mwemelele shinza, bhombaji shilume, mubhe ni khone.
1CO 16:14 Eshi zyonti zya mubhomba mbhombaji nulugano.
1CO 16:15 Muyimenye ekhaya ya Stefana. Mumenye hujabhali bhakristi bha hwande hula hu Akaya, na huje bhahwibheshele bhibho yabhakristi. Eshi embabhula amwe, bhakulu na bhailumbu bhane,
1CO 16:16 mubhanje bhahogowe hwa bhantu neshi ebho, na hwa bhantu bhonti bhabhahwavwa embombo na bhala bhabha bhomba embombo nate.
1CO 16:17 Ensungwilwe pabhenzele a Stefana, u Fotunato, nu Akiko. Bhemeleye pa mwahanziwaga aje mwe melele amwe.
1CO 16:18 Kwa kuwa wameifurahisha roho yangu na yenu. Kwa hiyo sasa, watambueni watu kama hawa.
1CO 16:19 Amakanisa ga hu Asia bhatumile endamuhu hulimwe. U Akila nu Priska bhabhalamushe hwitawa lya Yesu, pandwemo ni kanisa lyalili munyumba yabho.
1CO 16:20 Akulu bhane na bhailumbu bhane bhonti bhabhalamuha mulamuhanaje. Hulunonelo ulwe mwoyo uzelu.
1CO 16:21 Ane, ne paulo, esimba eshi hukhono gwane.
1CO 16:22 Aje umuntu yayonti yasagene Ungulubhi amayeego gabhe nu mwene. Wugosi witu uYesu, enza!
1CO 16:23 Eneema ya Gosi witu uYesu ibhe namwe.
1CO 16:24 Ulugano lwane lubhe pandwemo namwe mwitawa lya Yesu Kristi.
2CO 1:1 U Paulo, utumwe wa Yesu hlugano lwa Ngulubhi, nu Timotheo uholo witu, hwubhibhanza isha hu Korintho, na hwa Kristu bhonti bhabhali humukoa gwanti gwa hu Akaya.
2CO 1:2 Ulusajilo no lusehelo lwalufuma hwa Ngulubhi Yesu Kristu lubhe namwe.
2CO 1:3 Alumbwe Ungulubhe wa Gosi witu uYesu Kristu, umwene Ngulubhi welusajilo nantele Ngulubhi we luzinzyo lwoti.
2CO 1:4 Ungulubhi atizinzya ate humalabha getu, aje nate tibhazinyaje bhabhali mumalabhatibhazinzyaje nabhanja huluzinzyo lwatizinzizye ate Ungulubhi.
2CO 1:5 Neshi amalabhi ga Kristu shagahwonjelela husababu yetu nu luzinzyo luhwonjelela hulite ashilile hwa Yesu Kristu.
2CO 1:6 Lelo nkatitamansiwa, titamansiwa hunongwa ye luzinzyo lwenyu nu wokovu wenyu, nkashele tuzinziwa, tizinziwa, tizinziwa hunongwa yeluzinzyo lwenyu uluzinzyo lwenyu lubhomba embombo pamuhweteshela amalabha galabaga uYesu namuvulila neshi patuvumilila ate.
2CO 1:7 Nu ujasili wetu hulimwe ulishinza, tumenye aje namwahitishie amalabhi, muhweteshela nuluzinzyo.
2CO 1:8 Sagatuhwanza aje mubhe bhalema, bhaholo, gatalinago hu Asia. Tabhonelwe pakasetamenye huje taibhabhomi nantele.
2CO 1:9 Twali nulongwe ulwafwe eli lyatibheshele huje tusahwisubhile tetee, aje tisubhilaje Ungulubhi yazyusya nabhafwe.
2CO 1:10 Atokoye nenfwa, abhatokole nantele, tibheshele uujasiri wetu aje abhatokole nantele.
2CO 1:11 Abhabhombe eshi neshi amwe namutaavwa humputo zyenyu abhinji bhaayenza asalifye huniaba yetu hunongwa ye upendelelo lwe lusajilo humputo zyenyu.
2CO 1:12 Tihwisunvya eli, oushuha wiza amili yetu uwinza we mwoyo hwa Ngulubhi aje tajendeleye pansi, namwe siyo ne hekima ya munsi. Tumefanya hivi hasa na ninyi, na sio katika hekima ya ulimwengu, lelo hu neema ya Ngulubhi.
2CO 1:13 Setibhasimbila zyasigamuzibajiye abhazye awe ahwelewe. Endinoujasiri
2CO 1:14 kwamba kwa sehemu mutelewe nantele endinuujasiri aji isiku elya Yesu Ugosi wetu, taibha sababu yenyu hunongwa ye mabado genyu, neshi shamwaibha hulite.
2CO 1:15 Nali noujasiri aje nahanzaga ahwenze hulimwe nasoti aje nkamwejelele efaida eyahwenze awe hulimwe ulwabhili.
2CO 1:16 Napanjile ahwenze nanabhalaga hu Makedonia, ata nanawelaga napanjile ahwinze, nante amwe antume ane nabhalaga hu Uyahudi.
2CO 1:17 Nanasibhaga eshi, je, nalunzanyaga humwoyo? Je napangashibi nadamu huje eje “Ena, ena” ndadi, ndadi huwakati umo?
2CO 1:18 Lelo Ungulubhi shamwinza, setiyanga aja, “Ndadi” Awe “Ewa.”
2CO 1:19 Abhe umwana wa Ngulubhi uYesu Kristu, u Silwano, nu Timotheo nanee tabhatangazizizye huje hwamwene tiyiga “Ena” au “Ndadi” hwa mwene tiyiga “Ena.”
2CO 1:20 Maana ululagano lwa Ngulubhi huje “Ena” humambo gonti, hwa mwene zyonti huje “Ena” mwamwenye esho ashilile hwa mwene tiiga “Amina” hutuntumu wa Ngulubhi.
2CO 1:21 Yu Ngulubhi yatihakikisyi ati namwe mwa Yesu aje atitumile.
2CO 1:22 Abeshele eshimanyilo (omuhuru) hulite nantele atipiye no Mpepo wakwe mumoyo getu aje shibhe shilongolo shaitipela pamande.
2CO 1:23 Ehubhuzya Ungulubhi ambule zyasigana henzeye hu Koritho, aje ensabhabidushile amwe.
2CO 1:24 Eli siyo huje tibhonesya sa aluhwanziwa ulweteshelo lwetu aje shalubhe, tibhombha pandwemo namwe hunongwa.
2CO 2:1 Nahamuye nene huje ensahenze hulimwe nemvitilwe.
2CO 2:2 Nkanene nabhavisizye, eshi wenu yagansungwizya ane, eshi yayula yawavisizye ane?
2CO 2:3 Nasimbile neshi shanalolile huje isahavwalale na bhala bhabhasababisizye aje ensongwe. Endinoujasiri huje amwe mwenti aja uluseshelo lwawi lwalula lwamwalinalwo namwe.
2CO 2:4 Shesho nabhasimbiye amwe afuatane na mayemba magosi na malabha gahumwoyo na mansoza gaminji. Sewahanzaga huje embavisye. Nahanzaga aje mumanye ulugano lwane ulahumwoyo hulimwe mulumanye.
2CO 2:5 Nkahweli umuntu yayonti yamvisizye, sigamviye ane, lakini kwa kiwango fulani bila kuweka ukali zaidi nemwene - abhavisizye nawe bhayo.
2CO 2:6 Eli isombo lya muntu hwabhinjiliyiye.
2CO 2:7 Eshi badadala ya husomvye musaajile nahuzinzye. Bombi isho ili asahateeje nensebho enyiwji.
2CO 2:8 Nane embabhasumbe pawinji namwaihubhombela uyo.
2CO 2:9 Nabhasimbiye huje embalenje aje muli nulwitishilo hushila hantu.
2CO 2:10 Nkamusaajile umuntu yayonti nane ehusaajila umuntu uyo shila yenyu mwemwe hunonongwa ya Yesu.
2CO 2:11 Tibhomba eshi huje ushetani asahatikhonele, ate setibhalema na mambo gakwe.
2CO 2:12 Ungulubhi ni guliye undyango nanahenzele alumbilile izu ya Yesu husi ya Troa.
2CO 2:13 Lelo sihali nuluseshelo humwoyo hunongwa yahajesenamwajile uholo wane u Tito, nabhaleshile nahawela hu Makedonia.
2CO 2:14 Asalipwaje Ungulubhi, ambaye katika Kristu mara zote hutuongoza sisi katika ushindi. Yatibhomba aje timenaje na huje tinunshilaje ensi yonti.
2CO 2:15 Ate hwa Ngulubhi tilinunshili uwinza uwa Yesu bhonti bhabhahwaulwa na bhasigabhahwaulwa(bhabhateega).
2CO 2:16 Hwa bhantu bhabhatega nunshili wenfwa paka hwenfwa na bhala bhahwaulwa nushiliwe womi paka nuwomi. Wenu yavibhajiye evi?
2CO 2:17 Ate setetetikazya izu lya Ngulubhi hufaida yetu. Lelo aye humwoyo uzelu ugwinza tiyanga mwa Yesu neshishatitumwa nu Ngulubhi.
2CO 3:1 Mwie, twandile tandile awiawidhuvhe tubhene? Hatuwaza kalata yachagulanye hulimwi amalwafume huli limwi khashele awadhuu, ishitu tuwanza?
2CO 3:2 Amwe mwi mwe mlikalata yitu gachagulanye, gosi mbiha na manyilwe nawadhuawadhu waudhi.
2CO 3:3 Namubhoneha aje amwemlikalata afume wa Kristi. Iyafumiziwe nadhi, sangasihwa nakhono amanuwino ama uhala wa Ngulubhi umwumi hagaisibwa wiwimbao zi mawe. Ama moyo gabhanadamu.
2CO 3:4 Ubhu udadamazu watulinao mwa Ngulubhi ubhu ajende ashizanye wa mwana usu Kristi.
2CO 3:5 Angahatuyani twithe awisye hahuthi au hahafuma hulithi amanagakwe awi yamiwitu hufuma wa Ngulubhi.
2CO 3:6 Yu Ngulubhi watubhomba hunje tuwezye huuja awe tuatumwa vhindajizyo ipha izi ndajizyo saga kalata ilazya hala umwenye kalata ibhunda lelo uhala aleta uumii.
2CO 3:7 Ishi imbombo yifwe iyihali ipuzwa mmasimbo mwanya mmawe ihenza manyishiheza manyi manyi shisisya bha mu Israeli sahenya lwuthi lwuthihata maso wa Mose. Phipo yisisya wimaso gakwe, usishwa bhulafi filanga.
2CO 3:8 Ishi imbombo yahala saga ihabha nu mwamu sana katika usisya?
2CO 3:9 Lwali lelo hala hahafanyilwe usisya lwawandilo haga nuubhusisya hataishimaine ahadodo!
2CO 3:10 Khamba hala hahafanyilwe usisya lwawandilo haga nuubhusisya hataishimaine, ahadodo!
2CO 3:11 Khamba hala haha winza hagosi hashila hali nubhusishwa uwaubhuza wabhushe la wawa hali uwahweza khashele wilawila sha nushishwai.
2CO 3:12 Khatu hwitiha esho, tunighuvhu sana.
2CO 3:13 Sagatuli ni Mose, ubha uje tubhanje waze wila na wila pamaso gakwe, huje abhadhu muIsraeli bhasiwe lwudti uwa humalishila hu thithya bhulawahepanga.
2CO 3:14 Lelo thibho zyabho zhapi nyibwe. pakaisiku lwawaze bhubhula bhusagalashila isha manyile ulufingano lwihali. Shabhi bhiwilwe shilwe wazi, pipho uKristi mwene iwefewa hutali.
2CO 3:15 Lakini hata thanyunu lwa lwunthi uMose sha manyilwa, lwawawazhe lukhala amwanya moyo gao.
2CO 3:16 Lelo umnthu pagoluhana wa Bwana, ulwa wanze lufewa.
2CO 3:17 Eeshi Bwana uhala. Apa pa linu hala wa Bwana, hubha nuwaushe.
2CO 3:18 Eshi anthi nthi tubhepa palishimo na maso gasawanza ulwauweze tuula unthithwa uBwana. Tuwadhuhana mhathi shila shitukufu afume ubhutukufu afume engiga emo utukufu wa Bwana ya mwao, nashi shashishi afume Bwana, amashi pa Roho.
2CO 4:1 Pipo tuli ni mbombo ene, khashele shishili tuiposhile, huluma satubhakhate etamaa.
2CO 4:2 Pamandi yakwe, tukhanile amadala ngantughensoni vya vyubheele hatukhala na malibho, satibhombela shibhibhi izyo lwa Ngulubhi, awasilisye lwa lililyoli, tuwibhonesyatete zamila ya kila mutu witaziilya Ngulubhi.
2CO 4:3 Nkashele alumbilele hwetu hwobheele, iyabhele hwabhala bhene bhabhatega.
2CO 4:4 Asalule hwabho Ungulubhi winsi ene abhapofo la enjele zyabho zyasazihweteha hahafumila habhawezya alole ulukhozyo ululambilelo umwamu wa Kristi, wali fwano gwa Nngulubhi.
2CO 4:5 Afwatanaje satu hwitangazya tete, ila Ukristi uGosi, natitete nashi patubhalongozya hunongwa ya Yesu.
2CO 4:6 Afwatane yayoyo ayanjile, “Ulukhozyo lwa ikhola afume nkisi. “Aitangazyezye moyo getu, afumye ulukhozyolwenjele yiutukufu wa Ngulubhi ubhoneshelo wa Yesu Kristi.
2CO 4:7 Lelo tubhuto muvyombo vilongo ili nkebhoneshe nguvu ingositee ya Ngulubhi sagayetu.
2CO 4:8 Tutamyashila halisagati khophelwa tulola u wasi wasi ila satukata tamaa.
2CO 4:9 Tuyimba hatu bhombilwe tutagwapansi satuhwangamila.
2CO 4:10 Insikuzyonti tinyemula mubele gwetu enfwa ya Yesu, aje uwomi wa Yesu uubhonehanaje mmabele getu.
2CO 4:11 Ati tatuli bhomi insiku zyonti tefeziwe afwe hunongwa ya Yesu, aje uwomi wa Yesu ubho neshe mumabele getu gishibinadamu.
2CO 4:12 Afatanaje, ifwa ibhomba ibhomba imbombo muhati yetu.
2CO 4:13 Ila tulinabho Umpepo alengane na lweteshilo alagane na shila shashahandiwe, “Iheteshele, esho ehayanjile.” Ate nantele tuhwiteshela antele tiyanga.
2CO 4:14 Tuminye aje ola wazyonsezye Ugosi uYesu nantele ayituzyo syaate pamo numwihale, tumenya aje ayituleta ati pamo namwe nubhoneshelo wakwe.
2CO 4:15 Shila hantu hali kwa ajili yenyu aje, neema shiwenela hwa bhantu abhinji, ensumbezyo zizi daje ahwonjelele umwamu uwa Ngulubhi.
2CO 4:16 Esho satu hwanza ahwolowe. Ijapo hunzi tukulupa muhati tubhombwa shipya kila lisiku.
2CO 4:17 Hushipindi ishi ishi ufupi amayemba yalisya ati huwomi umwamu wauzida ivipimilo vyunti.
2CO 4:18 Afwatanaje satizama hu vintu vyavibhoneha bali vyasagavibhoveha. Ivintu vyatigawezya avilole vyesavibhonehana vya wiwila;
2CO 5:1 Timenyeje ekhaya eyensi yatikhala omu ena chiha yatizenga afume hwa Ngolobhe. Nyumba yashele selenganywa, namakhono agabhantu. Eyo nyumba eyewila eya mwanya.
2CO 5:2 Omwaputile omu, tibhawa tinyonywa akwatiziwe, ekhaya yetu eyamwauya.
2CO 5:3 Tinyonywa hweliakwate setilola ajetiliwelele.
2CO 5:4 Hakika natili mhati mwihema eli tibhawa natamenwa setihwanza ahwabhulwe badae yamwene. tihwanza akwatiziwe aje hala haliafwiye hamilwe no whomi.
2CO 5:5 Ula yatibheshelete huhantu eha yo Ngolobhe yatipie Ompepo nashi endagano nashihala hahayenza.
2CO 5:6 Mbhanje bhadandamazu ensiku zyonti. Mbhanje maso na mlikhaya hubele tilihutali no Gosi.
2CO 5:7 Afateje tijenda hulweteho saga uhwalole wheshotili bhadandamazu.
2CO 5:8 Shinza tibhahutali afume hubele nekhaya pandwemo no Gosi.
2CO 5:9 Hwesho tibhomba aje hwilengo lyetu nkasheletili akhaya olwenje hutali tikhondezye omwene.
2CO 5:10 Eshi lazima teuti tibhonehaje whitagali whitango lyalo njele elya Kristi. Aje shila mntu abheaposheye hala hahawhanziwa humambo gaga bhombeshe hubele shalishe nkashele minza olwenje mabhibhi.
2CO 5:11 Eshi eshamanye owoga owa Gosi, tibhasoha abhantu shila satiweli gabhoneha waziwa Ngolobhe. Esobhela ajegahovweha humoyo genyu.
2CO 5:12 Setilenga bhakhopelele amwenantele. Natilole atenashi abhelyoli. Ebadala yakwe tibhapela amwe hwilole wetu, ajembanje namajibu hwabhala, bhabhawilola aje bhebho lelosehahala hali mhati mwemwoyo.
2CO 5:13 Nkashele titomoshwe ne njele, kwa sababu ya Ngolobhe. Nkashele tilinehakiri zyetu zyazinyinza, kwajili yetu.
2CO 5:14 Fataneje olugano olwa Kristi abidizye, fatanejetilinelyoli aje: omntuomo afwiye hubhautu bhonti, wheshobhonti bhafwiye.
2CO 5:15 No Kristi afwiye whabhantu bhonti aje bhala bhabhakhala bhakhalaje bhewe wha mwene. Lazima bhakhale hwa mwene yafwiye nantele azyoshele.
2CO 5:16 Wheshi ahwande eshiahwendelele setihulonga omntu alengane neshawheli eshabhantu, afwatanaje epo hwande tamwenyezyaga oKristi sashilieshi. Lelo eshi setihulonga omntu yoyonti whesho nantele.
2CO 5:17 Eshi nkashele omntu alimhati mwa Kristi, oyohabhombe ahapya. Amambo egehale gashilile. Enya gali mapya.
2CO 5:18 Evintu vyonti vifumilawa na Ngolobhe. Atikhamenye ate hwa mwene yoyoashilile wha Kristi, atipiye embomba iya bhabhonganye.
2CO 5:19 Esho huyanje hwa Kristi, Ongolobhe alinolulenganyo mnsi yakwe yoyo, sagaabhazye amakosa agabho. Abheshela hulite izu elye olenganyo.
2CO 5:20 Hwesho tisalulwa awakilisye whaKristi, aje Ongolobhe abhombaga olufaa lwakwe ashilile huliti tibhasunda amwe wa Kristi mlenganywe no Nngolobhe!”
2CO 5:21 Afanyile oKristi abhe sadaka himbibhi zyetu. Omwene yayoyo sagabhombile embibhi abhombile esho aje atetibhe nelyoli eya Ngolobhe hwa mwene.
2CO 6:1 Whesho abhombe embombo emo tibhalabha amwe msaheje eneema eya Ngolobhe bila yagafumila.
2CO 6:2 Eshi ayanga, “Ensiku zyazyahetewe ezyensi ehali makini hulimwe, “Enya” ishi lisiku lyalyetewhe. Enya eshilisiku elyafyolwe.
2CO 6:3 Setibheha iwe elya zijewitagalila mntu yayonti, afataneje sagatianzila embombo yetu, aje eletwe husifa embibhi.
2CO 6:4 Ebadala yakwe, tibhilola tete humbombo yetu yonti, ajetili bhaputi bhaNgolobhe. Tilibhaputi bhakwe najimbilile, mateso, taabu, okhome wekhalo,
2CO 6:5 akhomwe, apinywe, owandizi, abhombe embombo hubidii, otulo no siku nenzala,
2CO 6:6 huzelu enjele, ejimbilile, owinza, hu Mpepo ufunjile, oluganano lyoli.
2CO 6:7 Tilibhaputibhakwe wizuelyalioli hunguvu ezia Ngolobhe. Tiline nendoso eyahaki eyekhono olelo no mongo.
2CO 6:8 Tibhomba embombo nenshishi na zalauliwe, neukhali no winza. Tikhatwa aje tilibhilenka wakati tilibhe kweli.
2CO 6:9 Tibhomba embombo nashiaje setimanyishe tisele timanyishe shinza. Tibhomba embombo nashibhabha fwilye enyatiseletikhana, tibhomba embombo nashibhanha somba humatendo getu sionashi bhabhalongwilwe nafwe.
2CO 6:10 Tibhomba embombo nashibhabhaswiga, lelo insiku zyonti. Tisongwa tibhomba embombo nashi apena, lelo titajilisya abhinji. Tibhomba embombo nashiaje setipata ahantu nantele tetitabhala kila hantu.
2CO 6:11 Tiyanje elyoli hulimwe Owakorintho, namuyogetu giguliwe hubaba.
2CO 6:12 Amoyo genyu segazigwa nate, mzigwa nensebhazyenyu mwemwe.
2CO 6:13 Eshi akalanye huhaki eyanga nashiabhana iguli - amoyo genyu mwoubaba.
2CO 6:14 Osabhewowauti nabhala bhasebhaputa. Tilinensepanonshi nabene katinelyoli nebhombibhi? Natele hulinsepamonshi umwanga ne nkisi?
2CO 6:15 Meteshelanonsi Okristi awezizye abhenayo usetano? Olwenje yahweteha alinosanguzanyonshi nola yashele saheteshe?
2CO 6:16 Huliolwetehanonshi lwalueli enyumba eya Ngolobhe neshifwani? Atetili nyumba ya Ngolobhe. Yali mwomi, najendenabo embabhe Ngolobhe ayanyinjile. Embakhale nabhene najende nabo embabhe Ngolobhe wabhobhape bhabhabhe bhantu bhane.”
2CO 6:17 Esho, “Epihwabhene mubagushe hwabhene, ayanga Ogosi. “Osapala mansye ahantu ahachafu, embabhakalibize amwe.
2CO 6:18 Embabhe babahulimwe namwe mbabhe bhanabhane alume na abhashe,” ayanga Ogosi o Mwenyezi.
2CO 7:1 Bhakholo bhane, kwa kuwa tihandiwe eshi, tihwiyozye tete huu nongwa zyazitibheba aje tibhanje bhagwenyu humoyo. Tiwanzaje ouzelu huhofu ya Ngolobhe.
2CO 7:2 Bhombaji eli sehuje embauna afuatenaje aje muli mumoyo getu! Setivisizye omuntu nkoma. Setifaidishe hufaida ya muntu wowonti.
2CO 7:3 Eyanga eli sehuje embauna afuatanaje aje muli mumoyo getu, ate hulite afwe pandwemo akhale pandwemo.
2CO 7:4 Endi no ujasili winji mhati yenyu, ememile luzinzanyo. Ememile lusongwo hata mumayemba getu gonti.
2CO 7:5 Tahenzele hu Makedonia, amabele getu segali notoyo. Baada yesho, tapele etabu hunamuna zyonti na khomwe evita upande wa honze ne hofu upande wa muhati.
2CO 7:6 Ila Ongolobhe, wabhawafaliji bhawo lowe, atifalijile lwa henzaga o Tito.
2CO 7:7 Sehwali huhwenzelo hwake tu aje Ongolobhe atizizya. Yali pia efaraja zila Otito zyaposheye afume hulimwe. Omwene atibhozyezye ulugano Ogosi lwa mlinanalyo, ozugumizu wenyu, mwamwali no wogawoga kwa ajili ya huline, shesho mzidile awe no lusho tee.
2CO 7:8 Hata nkashe eshitabu bhabhombile no lu sikitiho, ane seusebhebhelela. lakini esebhelela nanahenya owalaka owu wabhabhombile aje mzugumile. ila mwalino zugumizu humuda ododo.
2CO 7:9 Eshi sendi ne laha, sehuje mwali ne shida, afuatanaje azugumile hwenyu hwa bhaletile mtoba. Mwapete ozugumizu weshi Ngolobhe, shesho mwayembele se hu hasara kwa sababu ya hulite.
2CO 7:10 Afuatanaje oluzugumilo lwe shingolobhe luleta etoba ambago gukamilisha uwaushe bila abhe na malabhawa. Uzumizu wa munsi, ata sheshi galeta enfwa.
2CO 7:11 Enyaji ehuzuni yeshi ngolobhe ehapapa azma anshi engosi mhati yenyu. Namna wele isebhewe lelo lyaliligosi mhati yenyu lya goloshe aje semwali ne hatia. Kwa jinsi gani uchungu wenu ulivyokuwa mkubwa, hofu yenu, matamanio yenu, bidii yenu, na shauku yenu kuona kwamba haki inapaswa kutendeka! katika kila jambo mmethibitisha wenyewe kutokuwa na hatia.
2CO 7:12 Pamoja naje nawaandishiye amwe, sehuje mwali na makosa, wala sehwa muntu wayembele ne mbibhi embatishiye aje ogosu we moyo genyu gajulihane hwa limwe hu maso ga Ngolobhe.
2CO 7:13 Aje esababu yeshi aje tifarijiha. Enyonje zya ye luzinzyo lwetu, tete, tisongwelwe hata ashizanye kwa sababu ye lusho lwa Tito, afutanaje ishiroho shakwe shi burudisiwa namwe mwenti.
2CO 7:14 Afuatana nanshi sana hwiyovwezye alengane namwe, senali nensoni. Shingunga shakwe, nkashele izu lyata yangile hulimwe lyali lye lyoli, ahwiyonve hwenyu ahusu mwe hwa Tito gatigolosya aje lyoli.
2CO 7:15 Olugano lwakwe hulite gosi sana lakini nakomboha olweno lwenyi mweti, shila shamwakalibizizye omwene huwoga na hwogope.
2CO 7:16 Ensongwele afuatanaje endi nenguvu kamili muhati yenu.
2CO 8:1 Tibhanza aje mumanye, kolo no ilombo, ahusu eneema yo Ngolobhe ila yefumile humakanisa ge Makedonia.
2CO 8:2 Owakati amayemba amagosi, owinji ulosongwo lwabho olwonjelelo lwa apena bhabho upepe outajili ogosi we mpiana.
2CO 8:3 Afuatanaje endolile aje bhafumizye alengane shabhafishiye hata ashizanye shabhafishiye.
2CO 8:4 Humoyo gwabho wewo na tilambe ohwimji bhatilabhi ashiriki embombo hwa puti.
2CO 8:5 Ene seyafumile nanshi shatategemeye. Badala ya kwanza bhahwifumizye bhembho hwa Ngolobhe. Alafu bhahwifumizye bhibho hulite no hunsongo zya Ngolobhe.
2CO 8:6 Esho tabhozezye o Tito, wali ayanzisizye embombo ene, alete muogolosu enongwa ene yempiana ahusu amwe.
2CO 8:7 Amwe mlinavyovinji kila hantu hulweteshelo, hujango, hunjele hu njimbizyo na hwomvano hulete. Esho mhakikisyaje aje mubhanje no winji we mpiana.
2CO 8:8 Seyanga eli aje lazima. Baadala yakwe, eyanga eli ili apime oupendo wenyu alenganisye na bhantu abhanje.
2CO 8:9 Afwatanaje ehwelewa eneema yoya Gosi wetu oYesu Kristi. Hata nkashe alitajili, husababu yenyu ali pena. Ili ashilile oupena wakwe mwezye abhe bhatajili.
2CO 8:10 Hwijambo eli embabhapele oushauli wawaibhavwa. Omwaha gumo gwa shilile semwahandile wene, abhombe ijambo. Esho mwazilishe abhombe.
2CO 8:11 Esalazi likamilisya nansi samwahali nehamu eyabhombe, je, mwahenzakaga aliwezye alilete hugolosu, alangane nashamgawezya.
2CO 8:12 Alengane naje muli nehamu eyabho ijambo eli ni jambo linza lyalihwetehwa. Lazima lyemelele huhantu ha kila muntu hali naho, sio aje nashi hasagali naho omuntu.
2CO 8:13 Afwatanaje embo ene sio aje wamo wapataje ounafuu aje amwe mtingwile baadala yakwe abhesawa.
2CO 8:14 Owinji weselazi ubhatwikwe hwa hala habhahwanza. Ene yayeyo aje owinji uwezye ahwavwe ama hitaji genyu, na aje hubha wasa.
2CO 8:15 Ene eli nanshi sayahandihwe, omwene wali nevinji sagali na hantu nkahamo haha sagali wope wahahali nevidodo sagali notolwe.”
2CO 8:16 Lakini ashimihwaje Ongolobhe, wabheshele mmwoyo ogwa Tito omwoyo gula gwahwitume na sajile amboyo endinayo sababu yenyu.
2CO 8:17 Afwatanaje sio tu aje aposheye amaombi getu hwope omwene alinabidii ahusuane amaombi ego ahanzele hulimwe humwoyo gwakwe yoyo.
2CO 8:18 Titumile pamoja no holo wetu waho vwewa muhati mumakanisa vhwa ajili yembombo yakwe aliyanje izu.
2CO 8:19 Se sheshi tu, hwope bhasaluye wema kanisa ashole nate alengane nalinyemle ibhombo eli lyempena ene sababu yeumwamu wa Ngolobhe yoyo na ehamu yetu ya hwavwe.
2CO 8:20 Tihwiyefwa uwezekano waje wawonti ahwanziwa alengane nate alengane no upyana ou watiubebebile.
2CO 8:21 Tihwenye abhombe kila lyalili linza, sio tu witazi lya Ngolobhe, hata witazi lya awantu.
2CO 8:22 Nantele tihutuma oholo wamwabho pandwemo nabho. Tipimile hinji, tilole aje alinehamu humbombo inyinji. Hata sheshi alinebidii ashizanye afwatane naje ujasili ogosi wali nawo muhati yenyu.
2CO 8:23 Hunongwa zya Tito, ali mshirika wa mwetu huline ali ahomba mbombo husababu yenyu nanshi hwa holo bhetu atumwa na makanisa. Bheheshima hwa Kristi.
2CO 8:24 Shesho bhalangaji olwomvwano lwenyu mubhonesyaje humakanisa sababu ya hwiyomvwe hwetu esababu yenyu.
2CO 9:1 Ategelane ne huduma afwatane na bhoziwa shinza sana hwilini abhasimbile.
2CO 9:2 Emenye husu eshauku yenyu ambaya nahwivuniye hwa bhantu abha hu Makedonia. Nabhabholele Akaya elitayali afume hu mwaha gwagushilile. Ehamu yenyu ebhapiye umwoyo abhiji abahale abhombe.
2CO 9:3 Eshi embasontezwezwe aholo ili eshi ahwilole hwetu ahusu amwa gagaje wene, na eli antele handa mwabhanga tayari, neshe shenayajile handu mwanga.
2CO 9:4 Antele nkashile umuntu yayonti uwa hu Makedonia nkayenze pandwemo nane nabhaje semlitayari tenzaga alole esoni seyanga lyalyonti ahusu amwe afwanaje endi malidadi tee atoka ne mwane.
2CO 9:5 Esho nalolile yali mhimu abhalabha aholo ahwenze hwilimwe na alenganye amipango hani kwa jili yezawadi zwa mwalagenye urusayo. Nate tilineshe ahantu hahabholelwe.
2CO 9:6 Esebho zwazwezi omntu yatota hasha wape aivuna hashe na yoyonti yatota hwilengo elya lusayo wape aivuna ulusayo.
2CO 9:7 Basi kila muntu afumye shasebhele humwoyo gwakwe. Basi agajefumye eshakongobhale kongobhala wala agaje fumye alazimizwe afwataneje Ongolobhe ahusongwa ola yafumya no lusayo.
2CO 9:8 Ongolobhe awezizwe humwonjezwe kila baraka kwajili eyahwilimwe, antale shila lisiku amambo gonti, muwezwe agaje gonti gamuhwanza antele yayibha aje muwezwe ahwonjezwe kila tendo ilinza.
2CO 9:9 Neshe shesimbwilwe: “Anankenye utakili wakwe na aufumye hwapena elyoli yakwe ekheye wilawila.”
2CO 9:10 Wape afumizwe embeyu hwamuntu ni mbumunda kwajili yeshalwe nantele aifumya na hwonjezwe embeyu yenyu kwajili eyatote. Umwahale ayonjezwa amavuno agelyoli yenyu.
2CO 9:11 Mwaitajilishiwa hwashashonti shila ili nantele muwezwe abhe bha nepyana enebhebhete abhe nesalifwo hwa Ngolobhe ashilile hwiliti.
2CO 9:12 Esha bhombe ehuduma ene sio aje ebhapalamazwa amahilaji gabhoziwa bhene. Antele ehwonjezwa amatendo aminji agahusalifwe Ongolobhe.
2CO 9:13 Antele apime hwenyu na aha kikiziwe kwa huduma ene antele mubha hutelele Ongolobhe humwogope na humueteshe hwenyu izu elya Kristi. Antele mubhahutelele Ongolobhe hupwana uhwe karama zwenyu hwava hale hwashila muntu.
2CO 9:14 Bhabhatamani, na bhabhalabha kwajili yenyu bhabhombo eshi kwa sababu eye neema engosi eya Ngolobhe yelipandwemo namwe.
2CO 9:15 Esalifwo zubhe hwa Ngolobhe hu karama yakwe yaseyajiha!
2CO 10:1 Une ne Paulo, nene ebalabha huu nyenyekevu na uhugowe uwa Kristi. Nane endihogowe wakati nkendi hwitagalila lwenyu, Nina umalidada hwilimwe wakati nendi uhutali namwe.
2CO 10:2 Embalabha amwe aje wakati nehwendi pandwemo namwe, sewanza abhe malidadi na hwiyamini hwilini nene. Lelo esebha ehwanza abhe malidadi wakati embakhoma bhala bhabhasebha aje tikhala jinsi eshebele.
2CO 10:3 Antele nkashile tijenda katika belesetikhomana ibho kwa jinsi eyebele.
2CO 10:4 Antele endoso zwatilumila akhomani se zwebele. Antele zilina maha ageshi Ngolobhe anankanya engome zwa zihwefwa tee mijadara yetezwa.
2CO 10:5 Antele tinankanya kila chenye mamlaka gagahwinula ashile amataifa aga Ngolobhe. Tibhomba atekaye shila sebho eyogope hwa Kristi.
2CO 10:6 Tipewewe utayari uwa kuadhibu kilo matendo lyasa lihopa mara tu utii abha kamili.
2CO 10:7 Enya shila shashiliwazi hwitagalila lwenyu. Nkashile yoyonti yasohwa aje umwahale wa Kristi, na hebu ahwikumbuzwe yoyo mwenyewe aje tu shahweli wa Kristi, esho shatili ate antele tili shesho.
2CO 10:8 Afwanaje hata nkembahwilole hashe tee ahusu mamlaka Ugosi agafumizwe kwajili eyahwiliti abhazenje amwe na sio abhana nkanye sembalole esoni.
2CO 10:9 Sehwanza eli libhone aje embogofwe amwe hwu nkalata zwane.
2CO 10:10 Shila bhamo abhantu bhayanga, “Enkalata zwane hali na zilinamaha, lelo eshebele umwahale zaifu. Enjengo zwakwe sezihwaziwa atejelezewe.”
2CO 10:11 Umba abhantu bhenamna enyo bhelewe aje shila shatiyanga unkalata wakati natili hutali, ni lyolilyoli tilishalipandwemo namwe pala.
2CO 10:12 Setibhale uhutali tee ahwibhonganye tete au ahwilangisye tete na bhala ambao bhuhwisifu bhebho. Lelo nabhahwipama bhebho nab shila muntu wao salinejele.
2CO 10:13 Ate hata shesho setibhalwivune, ashele empaho. Badala yakwe tibhabhombe shesho tu mhati eye mpaho ambayo Ungolobhe atipimie ate empaho yefiha utali uwenyu shauhweli.
2CO 10:14 Afwanaje setahwiyonjizwezwe. Tete natabhafishiye amwe tali bhahwande afishe uhutali neshe uwenyu ewilombelelo lya Kristi.
2CO 10:15 Selihwivunile ashile ampaho ahusu embombo ezwa bhanje. Badala yakwe titegemela neshe ulyeteho lyenu shalukula aje ieneo lyenyu elye mbombo libhapanushe tee, antele bado ibhabhe muhati eye mpaho eye lyoli.
2CO 10:16 Titegemela huveli aje tiwezwe alombele endombelelo hata hwenye mikoa zaidi yenyu. Setibhahwikune ahusu embombo yebhombeha katika sehemu ezwamwao.
2CO 10:17 “Antele yoyonti yahwilola katika Gosi.”
2CO 10:18 Hwa maana siyo yola yahwisibitisya yoyo asibitiziwa. Isipokuwa, yoyo ambaye Ugosi ahusibitizwa.
2CO 11:1 Esebha huje mwenjeshelanaje nane humambo egeshilema hwahuje lyoli muhwenjeshelana nane. Hwa huje endinokelo namwe.
2CO 11:2 Endinokelo ogwa Ongolobhe humbombo yenyu, awande isiku palwafishile hulimwi ulwegano ogwa lume omo. Naidie abhatwale amwe hwa Kristi nashi walendu amwiza.
2CO 11:3 Lakini ehwogopa huje engabhomba nashi ezoha ehahopeye o Eva hwihenga lyakwe esebho zyenyu zigabhatezya hutali afume mubada shesho nyiza hwa Kristi.
2CO 11:4 Hwa huje ufwani gwa muntu uwenje ageza huhombelele uYesu owamwabho owenjenola watalumbeleye. Hushifwani huje mwaposhela opepo owenje nula wamwaposheye nashi ufwani huje mwaposhela izu elyenje nalila lyamwahovyezye. Mwanjimba goti ego huje huyiyee!
2CO 11:5 Hwa huje anesendingene nabhala awantu bhabhali bila hantu bhala bhabha kwiziwe antumi ahwiza.
2CO 11:6 Ane nemwene nomowandogozezye afumwe amazyu, sagaendiesho hunjele hwalyolyoti lila tilibhombile humanyishe hwenyu.
2CO 11:7 Je nabhombile mbibhi ahwishe nene ilimwe mubhe amwanya? Hwa huje nalumbelele wenee izuu elya Ngolobhe awahulimwi.
2CO 11:8 Nafyulile amabhaza gamwabho naposhele wanavwize afume amwabho huje embweye abhalishe amwe.
2CO 11:9 Panali namwe nalihali eyeupena lakini saganalabhile hohonti, eshida zyane zyanjiye aholo bhahenzele afume hu Makedonia. Kwa kila hantu nahwizijile nene esibhelizigo hulimwi, embawendele abhombe shesho.
2CO 11:10 Nashi elyoli sehweli mhati yane, ohu ahwintofye hwane senaipomezewa katika ensi iya Akaya.
2CO 11:11 Yenu? hahuje sembagene? Ongolobhe amenye huje embagene.
2CO 11:12 Lakini lilalyebhomba, embalibhombe na engalibhomba huje ehwiziye omwoyo hwabhala bhabhaziliha umwoyo nashi satihweli galagala gabha sobhela.
2CO 11:13 Hwa huje bhala bhatumwa bhilenka bhabhomba mbombo abhilenga bhahwigaluzya huuje bhatumwa bha Kristi.
2CO 11:14 Neeli sagaliswijisha hwa huje uSetano ahwigaluzanya yuyo nashi ohala uzelu nu bhozyo.
2CO 11:15 Eli sagalitisha hwaa bhabhomba mbombo bhakwe aigaluzanye bhabhe nashi abhomba mbombo bhelyoli omwisho gwabho gwaibha nashi amatendo gabho gawaziwa.
2CO 11:16 Eyanga nantele agaje abhe omtu wowoti wasebha huje ane sagaendini njele. Lakini kambhombe, nejeleli ane nashi olema nane ahwintuntumule hashee.
2CO 11:17 Lila lyeyayanga ahwintuntumile naajivune hagale gwa nu gosi, lakini eyanga nashi ulemaa.
2CO 11:18 Hwa huje abhantu abhinji bhahwilola hubele, embahwintutumle nane.
2CO 11:19 Hwa huje mwakhatene huhwinza nuubhibhi, amwee namwee muhwisizye!
2CO 11:20 Yenu mkhatana numuntu kabheshe mmateso nashi samnyapana kati yenyu, nashi abhabheshe bhabhomba mbombo amwe hufaida yakwe, nashi ahwibheshe humwanya mhala, au kashile abhabhome humaso.
2CO 11:21 Embayanje nesoni huje talibhahwinu sana abhombe eshoo. Nabadonkashile aweli wahwilola— eyanga nashi olema— nane embahwilole.
2CO 11:22 Je, abhene Bhayahudi? Nane endishesho. Je abhene Bhaisraeli? Nane shesho. Je, abhene bhahwa Iblahimu? Nane shesho.
2CO 11:23 Je, abhene bhatumwa bha Kristi? (Eyanga nashi umuntu wezyepile enjele zyane.) Ane sananyene. Endinashi pambombo ehome sana uhutali sana ugaga endimchabho, ashilile ahomwe naashilile ahomwe, apalamile ehatali enyinji hata afwe.
2CO 11:24 Afume hwa Bhayahudi eposheye malahasanu, abhomwe mala alobaini afume limo.”
2CO 11:25 Mala hatatu nabhomwilwe nendesa. Mala limo nabhomwilwa amawe. Mala hantatu nanusulishe mumeli enjendile nusiku na pasanya mbahali wazi.
2CO 11:26 Naliinee safali izye wilawila, nehatali ezya mmeze, nehatali ezya ambuda, nehali ezyafume hwabhantu bhanenene, nehatali zya bhantu hwimataifa, nehatali iyammeze, nehatali iyamwipoli, nehatali iya mwiwaa, nehatali iyafume waholo bhane adodo.
2CO 11:27 Endi mbombo ehome namaisha amakhome lumo lumo etoloha nu siku sagagona nashi ezala nahomelwe, mala nyinji afunje, lumo embe welele nisasa.
2CO 11:28 Hutali na hantu hohoti, naliwahitume kila lisiku naline wasiwasi namabhaza. Yonanu obhinu nanene saga endibhinu?
2CO 11:29 Yonanu wasababisizye omo agwe mbiwi, nane sembile mhati?
2CO 11:30 Hwahuje nane ehwivuna, na embahwivune ahusu nahabhonesha ubhinu wane.
2CO 11:31 Ongolobhe nu Daada owa Gosi uYesu, oyo umene atufiwa wenee, amenye huje ane sekhopela.
2CO 11:32 Hula hu Dameski, ugosi uwe mkoa pasi ya mwene aleta aliagudima omji gwa Dameski huje ahante.
2CO 11:33 Lakini abhehwele mshikapo, ashilile mwidirisha na mlubhomba, nanusulishe akhatwe mmabhona gakwe.
2CO 12:1 Ilazimisya awivhune, lelo nahamo haha wonjelela nilwo. Ishi iwendelela insivhozyani na gafunuliwe afume humwanya wa Bwana.
2CO 12:2 Uhumanya muntu omo katika Kristu unu amaha kumi na naganji ganni gagashi shilile kashele shimbele au huzi yebele, anisi minye, Ungulubhi amenye iyanyakulima humwanya wingo imwanya iyatatu.
2CO 12:3 Namanya huje umuntu onu khamaimba shimbeli— au hunzi anisaiminye—
2CO 12:4 afhulilwe abhale humwanya hadi mupaladiso na nahuve amabhwo amiza sana bha bhantu yayandi agayanje.
2CO 12:5 Wali kwa ajiyayo ivuna. Lelo khanine nimwe nesivuna. Lelo alingane nusafuwani.
2CO 12:6 Khashele iwaza wivune, aghashele iwaza wivune, sanabha lema eshomana ninzanga ayanje uwanaluooli. Lelo imbaleshe evune, asiwepo uwansivhila shinje wigo gabhoneha muhati au gala gabhabhuvwa afume hulini.
2CO 12:7 Sigaiza wivune alengane nengoo gaga vfumile ighafwananana na manjele. Wisho sagaimbavhe mbili gwani ihabhomba nusentano ashambulila ani, aje engande galuhane insawivune.
2CO 12:8 Mala hatatu ihapepeha wa Bwana wili, angadahavhe wao, wavhe nashani.
2CO 12:9 Wope ahambula, “Uwihaziwa niwani uyile kwajiliyaliwe, wahuje inguvhu iwobwa huwinu. Isho, ihazasana awivhune elingane uwinu wanii ili ishi uwezo wa Kristi uwezye akhale pamwanya palini.
2CO 12:10 Phepoiwezya kwaajili ya Kristi, afwatane nuvhinu namaligo, naimba nishilavhe, nishishisiliha winu, antele imba nguvu.
2CO 12:11 Anindilemai amwe mwa mwa mukandinizye shijanja, wagawe isumwangwa namwe. Pipipo nsali mwanasana wio awawitwa vhatumwa— wiza, hata kama anisaga initwe hantu.
2CO 12:12 Ishi manyilo shalwoli shatumwa nzyambishe pahati napati hati pinyu na hutabhu, imanyilo namanjele ni mbombo ingosi.
2CO 12:13 Nishibhu nri mwali bha muhimu bhansi hani kulinko umwafutile umwasagile, pipo lelo sihali lizigo hulimwi? Mu hobhoshe hwilwo!
2CO 12:14 Enyi! ane inditayali awhinze hulimwi mala yatatu. Sihabhazigo hulimwi, pipo siwanza ahantu hahonti hulimwi. Iwaza aje amwi. Pipo awana hawaziwa abhavhishe bhunto kwa ajili ya pafhi. Bhabha mbawanzawa abhishe imbuto.
2CO 12:15 Ihaimoga hani etumile natumilwe kwaajili yimoyo nginyu. Khamba imbaganile hani iwaziwa angane hashe?
2CO 12:16 Lelo nishi shashirire, sigaiha wilishile. Lelo pipo indijanja sana, ani nihakhente amweindhi nishi yabha gahusovhusana, ani nibha khite awe ishi indhi nishi yabhajile hujanja.
2CO 12:17 Ishi ehejile wibhombele faida wayahyuthi witumile hulimwi?
2CO 12:18 Imwinishe u Tito ahweze hulimwi, ihi hatuma uholo uwinhi palishimo nao. Lelo Tito awa bhabha mbela faida amwi? Lelo, satajenda lalila? Lelo satajenda na magaga getu gagala?
2CO 12:19 Mumanya isho huje awalilo hanti iha tawiyumilaga ntinti hulimwi? Witalila lwa Ngulubhi, na katika Kristi, talitu yanga shila siku shila wa muntu twabhulanga abhamanyizyezye amwi.
2CO 12:20 Lelo ibhogopa huje piha iinza ama izha ibhaga amwe nishi pinsu ngwa. Lelo ibhogopa uje mugawezya asinte nanaje aani ni nishi pamusungwa. Isho gaishiwogopa huje hugawa nayangane, ukelo ulipuhanilyoyo anyonwe zya munyipuya ubima afasi amaseho ivigosi namao.
2CO 12:21 Iwogopa huje piibhuya na tena Ngulubhi wani agawezya eniswe witazi lwinyu. Iwogopa ingawezya avitililwe nahwinji ihi mho abhombabhivhi shahusili ishi. Nio bhasambile i vantu, nu malaya agabhomba.
2CO 13:1 Ine mala yatatu abheze hulimwi. “Shila lyalitakwilye lazima lizegwe nu hakika uwashaidi bhabhili au bhatatu.”
2CO 13:2 Imalile ayanje ibho abhomba imbibhi shalisi abhana wanji bhutyi lyulyo pihali bhubho imala ya bhili iyanga natena pihayinza na iyele: Sagaibha vumilila.
2CO 13:3 Imbabhula amwe ili kwa sababu muwanza uketi huje uKilisti ayanga ajendele ane. Umwe itaga yuganu hulimwi, badaya mwene umwene wikhone muhati mulimwi.
2CO 13:4 Pepo bhasubisya payuganu, lelo alimwomi wikhone ulwa Ngulubhi pipo natiwaya tulibha yuganu muhatyi mwakwe, lelo tuikhala nabho wikhonelwa Ngulubhi. Pepo natyi tu ndani yake twaikala muhati wikhone ilwa Ngulubhi.
2CO 13:5 Wiyenyaji mwemwe muwiyenye khashele muliniamani. Muwi pimaje mwemwe. Hamungundula huje UYesu U Kilisti? Ali mhati mulimwi, umwene mwawili khasashashisho itamwakisiwaga.
2CO 13:6 Ini ujasili huje mwaigundula ahuje ate satakhanilye.
2CO 13:7 Ishi tulavha wa Ngulubhi huje munganda abhombe tyi abhibhi. Silabha huje tunje abhoneshe huje sagatupitile injelo, badayakwe ilabha musabhombe hahotyi shishiza, ingawa tugawezwa abhoneshe tumenilye ni njelo.
2CO 13:8 Pipo ati zaga tubhajile abhombe hahotyi shingunga nilyolyi, lelo kwajili yilyo lyitu.
2CO 13:9 Lelo tumojela patubha bhayaganu amwe mubhanikhone. Tulabha pia muweze abhombwe mlikamili.
2CO 13:10 Ingasimba amambo iga pala pindi hutali namwe, ilipimbonishe iganje abhonesye ukhali hulimwi. Saga iwanza atumile amamulaka uBwana aphile ane abhazenje wala si abhananganye panzi.
2CO 13:11 Lelo mwalume na mubhashimonjelaji mumbaje imbombo kwa ajili yalejesye, mupewe umwoyo mutihane mwe kwa mwe, mukhale huwaushe. Nu Ngulubhi uwilugano nuwaushe abhe palushimo namwe.
2CO 13:12 Lamuhanaji kila muntu hu mbusu inyinza.
2CO 13:13 Abhamini bhalamuha.
2CO 13:14 Umwene wa Bwana Yesu UKilisti ulungano ulya Ngulubhi na ubhushilika uwi Roho umwinza bhuvhe palishimo namwe.
GAL 1:1 Ane ne Paulo ne mtume. Anesendi mtumwa afume whabhantu wala ashilile wabhantu, lelo ashilile wa Yesu Kristu no Ngolobhe oBaba yavyose seyafume wabhafwe.
GAL 1:2 Pandwemonaholo bhontinani engandishi amakanisa aga Galatia.
GAL 1:3 Owene obhenamwe nolutengano waufumile whaNgolobhe oBaba wetu no Gosi oYesu Kilisti,
GAL 1:4 yawifumizye yayo afwatane nolugano lwangolobhe wetu no Baba.
GAL 1:5 Whamwene hubhe otuntumu owawilawila.
GAL 1:6 Eswiga aje mgaluhana nanaliwizielyenje eswiga aje mgaluhana hutaliwanomwene. Yabhakwiziizye huwewe wa Yesu.
GAL 1:7 Nalimoizuilyenje lelobhaliabhantu bhabhanankanya amwe mayemba agalulanyeizulya Kristu.
GAL 1:8 Hata nkashele tete olweuje ohalao zelu, afumemwanya abhalombelele hulimweizu shenje nashilya tibhalombeleye hulimwe.
GAL 1:9 Nashisatianjile awandile neshifyanga nautele nkasheleumntu abhalombelele, hulimweizu lyalilishenje, “nashila mwaliovweze oyo na ayejewe.”
GAL 1:10 Eshi ehwawa osimishizyo owabhantu olwenje wa Ngolobhe? Ehwanzaje embasongwezye abhantu? Nkashele iwendelela abhasungwezye abhantu? Anesendi mtumwa wa Kristu.
GAL 1:11 Bhaholo ewanzaje mmanye aje izulyehabhalombeleye selyafumile nabhantu.
GAL 1:12 Sihapetefume whamntu wala sehafundizizye badala yakwe. Ehali langouwa Yesu Kristu wane.
GAL 1:13 Mwovwe ajeolwizyolwane olwahunyuma Olwahunyuma olwedinieya Kiyahudi, shehali panga amayemba hukhali ikanisa lya Ngolobhe sana ashileeshipimo na nyangamizye.
GAL 1:14 Ehendeleye hudini Eyekiyahudi sana aholobhane abhinji abhayahudi ehalinebidii sana notupango otwababa bhane.
GAL 1:15 Lelo Ongolobhe asungwelwe ansalule ane. Afumemvwanda mwamaye. Ankwizizye ane ashilile huwene hwakwe
GAL 1:16 ahubhonesezye omwana mhati mwaline, aje ehulombelela omwene mwabhantu bhashele sebhahuputa. Nantelesehanzile owajenshe owebele ni danda
GAL 1:17 sehazubhile abhale huYerusalemu wabhala bhabhali watumwa kabuyaline. Saseleomwene ehabhalile Uarabuni pamande ehawhuyile hudemesiki.
GAL 1:18 Pesho humahagatatu ehazubhile abhale hu Yerusalemu ahujendele oKefa, nakhalanawo nakhalananawo. Ensiku kumi natano.
GAL 1:19 Lelosehalolile otumwa abhamwabho ila O Yakobo oholo wakwe no Gosi.
GAL 1:20 Enya hwitagalila elya Ngolobhe sekhopelahwalilalye hwandiha hulimwe.
GAL 1:21 Nantele ehabhalile humikowa aga Shamu nahu Kilikia.
GAL 1:22 Sehabhonehaga humaso aga hwikanisa ilya Uyahudi gala galaga Kristu,
GAL 1:23 lelohalibhahovwa wewe aje yatiyenvaga eshi alombelea olweteho yanankanyaga.”
GAL 1:24 Bhahusombezya Ongolobhe awande huline
GAL 2:1 Afume amaha kuminanne na bhabile habhili muYerusalemu peka nu Barnaba. Pia nahamwejihe u Tito nabhalile pipo Ungulubhi ayimanyisishye huline aje ihwanziwa imbale.
GAL 2:2 Nahabhishile mwilongolela lyabhoizwi lye mlumbileye hubhantu abhinsi. (Lelo na yinje hwa hwifise yalolosya jobhalongozi kamili). Nabho mbile iishi aje imanye aje sinshimbila pamo senashimbiye lwene.
GAL 2:3 Lelo hata yu Tito, ahali peka nani, yahali mu yahali Muyunani, alazimisizwe atahiliwe.
GAL 2:4 Ijambo ili lyahafumiye pipo ya holo abhilenga bhebhahinzile hufiso apelelezye uwabhushe wetulinawo mwa Kiristi Yesu. Bhanyonyilwe aje tibhe bhatumwa bhindajizyo.
GAL 2:5 Setwa yifumizye hubhitishe hata hwi saa lyeka, huje izwi ilyilyoli lisyale bila agahuhake humwuyu.
GAL 2:6 Lelo bhala bhebhayangwilwe aje bhahali bhalongozi sebhasanjiye hohonti huline honti hebhobho mbaga seshali shi maana huline. Ungulubhi sahwitiha uupendeleo wa bhanadamu.
GAL 2:7 Pamandi bhahandola initihwilwe alumbilile izwi hubhala bhesaga bhatahililwe. Ihali ndeshe u Petro alumbilile izwi hwa bhalasaga bhatahililwe.
GAL 2:8 Ungulubhi yayibhombile imbombo muhati uwa Petro hwa tumwa bhebhatahililwe ahabhombile imbombo hati yani na mubhantu abha munsi.
GAL 2:9 Lula u Yakobo, nu Yohani, nu Kefa, bhaloleshe aje bhahazenjile ishibhanza, bhahaminye uwene wenapewilwe ani bhatiposhile hushibanza ani nu Barnaba. Bhahabhombilishi aje tibhale hubhantu abha munsi nkebhabhale hubhala bhebhatahiliwilwe.
GAL 2:10 Tena bhatwanzile ati hubhakumbushe apina nani wayonahasungwizye abhombe imbombo iyo.
GAL 2:11 U Kefa na ahinza huAntiokia, nahankhanile waziwazi pipo ahakosiye.
GAL 2:12 Kabla yi bhantu bhano afume hwa Yakobo na bhantu bhinsi. Lakini abhantu bhala ne bhahinza ahaleshile na sogole afume hwa bhantu abhinsi. Ahogopaga abhantu bhebha hwanza itohala.
GAL 2:13 Tena Abhayahudi bhamo bhaha bhwagana nubhunafiki peka nu Kefa. Amatoke gahaliishi hata yu Barnaba ahinjiye mubhunafiki uwo.
GAL 2:14 Lakini lwenalolaje sebhalifwata ibhangili ilyi lyoli nahamuzizye u Kefa pamaso gabho bhonti amwe nke mwe Bhayahudi, mlinitabia zya bhantu bhi mataifa badala yi tabia zyi shiyahudi?”
GAL 2:15 Ati twebhayahudi apapwe se bhantu bhi insi abhi mbibhi”
GAL 2:16 mmanye aje numo yabhaziwa ilyoli humatendo gisheria. Badala yakwe bhabhaziwa ilyoli muhati mwa Yesu Kilisti, twahonzile nulwitiho muhati mwa Yesu Kristu. Ili huje tibhaziwe ilyoli hulwitiho muhati mwa Yesu na siyo amatendo gi shelia. Humatendo gishelia nagumo umbili gwewayabhaziwa ilyoli.
GAL 2:17 Lakini nike tihumwanza Ungulubhi atibhazizye ilyoli, muhati mwa Kilisti tiyilola tiniti aje tilini mbibhi, je uKilisti abhombilwe ntumwa wimbibhi? Seshi nisho!
GAL 2:18 Nkenazenga usubhilo gwani adime ishelia isubhuli lyenaluyu injilolesya nini aje imvunza ishelia.
GAL 2:19 Asilile musheha mfwiye mushelia kwahiyo uhwanziwa akhale munyobhe zya Ngulubhi.
GAL 2:20 Injimbihe peka nu Yesu. Senini habhili yikhala ila yu Yesu akhala muhati muline. Amaisha giakala aga mumbili inkhala hulwitiho. Muhati mwa Ngulubhi ya ngiine ani ahayifumya kwajili yaline.
GAL 2:21 Tejelezya uweene wa Ngulubhi nkushele ilyoli yaliho ashilile nasi uYesu handi afwiye bure.
GAL 3:1 Bhagalatia mulibhalema lisowele ibhibhi lyalibhanankenye? Antele uYesu Kilisti sagahwibhonezwezwe aje agogwilye hwitagalila humapo genyu?
GAL 3:2 Ane ewanza aje emanye eli afume hwilumwe. Je mwahambiye Roho humatendo age bele au alyeteho wla lyumwahovzwe?
GAL 3:3 Antele amwe mlibhalema paka esho? antele mwahandile hweshi Roho ili mmale eshe bele?
GAL 3:4 Antele mwalabhile humbo aminji wene, nkashile lyoli galigewene?
GAL 3:5 Antele umwahale afumizwe Roho maha kati ya bihwilimwe na bhombe amatendo agamaha kati ya hwilimwe abhombo humatendo ageshelia au ahovwe pandwemo no lyeteko?
GAL 3:6 U Abrahamu amweteshe Ongolobhe abhaziwe aje welyoli”.
GAL 3:7 Sheshile manyaji aje bhalo bha bhahumweteha bhana bha u Abrahamu.
GAL 3:8 Ensimbo ya kuhwilwe aje Ungolobhe abhabhazizwe elyoli abhantu bhasebhaputa hwidala elyelyuteho pawandilo bha Ebrahimu: “ashilile awe bhasebhaputa bhonti bhayisayilwa.”
GAL 3:9 Hwitagalila bhala ambao bhana lyeteho bhabarikiwaje pandwemo no Abrahamu ambaye alinolyeteho.
GAL 3:10 Bhala ambao bhategemela amate ndo age sheria bhalipansi pamakhosi antele isimbwilwe alinamakhosi shele muntu yasalipandwemo na mambo gonti gagasimbilwe mshitabu eshe sheria, agabhombe gonti.”
GAL 3:11 Eshi huliwazi hwa Ngolobhe semubhaziwa elyoli hata amohwidalo elyesheria afwanaje yalinelyoli bhakhala hulyeteho.”
GAL 3:12 Eshelia sefumilana nolyeteho badala yakwe “Antele abhomba hwahusheria aikhala kisheria.”
GAL 3:13 U Kilisti atauye ate afume mumakhosi eyesheliya antele abhombeshe makhosi kwajili eyahwiliti antele isibwilwe aje shele muntu alinamakhosi ya khomelewe pamwanya eyikwi, lyalilaje.”
GAL 3:14 Ilengo lyalilyaje usayo lwalwali wa Ibrahimu zigezele hwabhantu abhema taifa hwidala elya Yesu Kilisti, ili liwezwe aposhele ehadi eya Roho ashilile hulyeteho.
GAL 3:15 Bhaholo eyanga hushibinadamu. Hata wakati ilagano elyeshibinadamu limalishe abhehwe imara nomo yagawezwa alipuzwa wala ahwunjezwe.
GAL 3:16 Eshe ahadi zyayanjele hwa Ibrahimu huvikholo vyakwe. Sayanga, “aje evikholo” amarusye awingi. antele ambaye yo Kilisti.
GAL 3:17 Eshi eyanga eshi, esheria yehenzeleamaha 430 sehwefwa ilagano elyahwisalo lyalyabhehwelye no Ngolobhe.
GAL 3:18 Antele kashile ulugano ugenzele hwidala elyehadi. Eshe Ungolobhe afumizwe wene hwa Ibrahimu hwidala elye ahadi.
GAL 3:19 Yenu eshi esheria bhayefwinzwe? yalongozyezye husababu eyemakosa paka eshikholo esha Ibrahimu ayenze hwabhala ambao hwabhale bhalagene. Esheria ehabhehwelye neshinikizo ashilile u malaika hukhono gwa upatanishi.
GAL 3:20 Eshi upanyi amanisya tee muntu umo, Ungulubhi ahomo mwene.
GAL 3:21 Eshi je esheria ehwelishinyume neahadi zwa Ngolobhe? atahashe antele nkashile esheria yehali ifuiziwe yalinamaha agalete owomi, lyoli agapatihene husheria.
GAL 3:22 Antene badala ye nsimbo lifunjele amambo goti pasi yembibhi. Ungolobhe abhombile esheili ndagano zwakwe zitaule ate ashilile hulyeho lyu Yesu Kilisti iwezehane apatihane hwabhala bhabhetishe.
GAL 3:23 Antele sabhasele aweteshe hwa Kilisti sahenzele talitifungwilye anabhe pasi yesheria hadi hwenze ufunuo wa lyeteho.
GAL 3:24 Eshe eyo esheria yabhombile olongozi wetu hadi Kilisti ahenzele ili atele tubhaziwe elyoli nolyeteho.
GAL 3:25 Eshe abhe ulyeteho lyenzele setihweli pansi ya mwenyelezi.
GAL 3:26 Eshe amwe mwene mbhana bha Ngolobhe ashilile hulyeteho lya Kristu Yesu.
GAL 3:27 Bwonti bhabhozwe hwa Kristu mkwete U Kristu.
GAL 3:28 Momo UMyahudi wala UMyunani, mtumwa wala umwaule, ulume afwanaje amwe mwenti mliomohwa Kristu Yesu.
GAL 3:29 Nkashile amwe mlibhe Kristu, basi mlishikholo sha Ibrahimu, wagali alenganisye nendagano.
GAL 4:1 Iyanga aje abhanadamu upyani yu mwana, sagaali nuutofauti numtumwa, Gata nkesho tabhale wishoma shonti.
GAL 4:2 Ibadala yakwe, ali pansi yisimamizi na bhabhaghatiliye hadi umda gugubheshewelwe nobaba wakwe.
GAL 4:3 Shesho natee, lwatali bhana, talemwilwe nu utumwa wikanuni zya humwanzoni zya monsi.
GAL 4:4 Baada yimuda gugulisahihi afishe, Ungolobhe atwalile umwanawakwe, wapapwilwe noshe, upapwa pansi yindajizyo.
GAL 4:5 Awombile eshi ili ahubhagombole bhala bhabhali pansi yindajizyo ilitipewe ihali yabhe hansi bhanabhakwe.
GAL 4:6 Eshi aje amwe mulibhana, Ongolobhe atwalile upepo wamwanawakwe mhati yimoyo getu, upepo, alila, “Abba, Baba.”
GAL 4:7 Hunamuneyo awe siguli mtumwa natena eshi ulimwana. Nkeshi uli mwana, eshi awe ulipyani abhilile hwa Ngolobhe.
GAL 4:8 Hata shamumbele, humanye Ungolobhe, mwali bhatumwa hwa bhala bhi asili saga bhalongobhe nzela.
GAL 4:9 Eshi isalezi huje mmenye Ungolobhe, au huje mmanyishe no Ngolobhe yenu muwelela tena mkanuni ziubhinu zya humwanzoni zyasagazili ni shoma? Eshi muhwanza tena abhe bhatumwa?
GAL 4:10 Mulema huwenyelezi insiku lilisalu lilwe, utukulo lwimwezi, amajira, na maha. Ihogopa kwa jili yenyu.
GAL 4:11 Ihogopa hunamuna emo injiyanzizye shaha.
GAL 4:12 Imbabhalabha, bhaholo mubhe hansi shindeho, indi hansi shamuleho. Sagamwankoseye.
GAL 4:13 Eshi mmenye aje yaali kwajili yimpongo yembele yaje natangazwaga iizu humwenyu humala ya hwande.
GAL 4:14 Ingabha ihali yane yembele yabhabheshele hwalenjewe, saganza yanye au huhane. Ni badala yakwe mwamposheleye hansi uhala uzelu wa Ngolobhe, hansi aje nali Kristi Yesu yoyo.
GAL 4:15 Eshi luhwi alosongo lwenyu? afwatanaje imbasimisizye humwenyu aje, nkiwezehana andi mwasenya amaso genyu nahumpele ane.
GAL 4:16 Nebho saba, Eshi indi aduwi wenyu afwatanaje ihubhawola ilyoli?
GAL 4:17 Bhahanza shushomela ila saga huminza. Bhahwanza hubhatenganisye amwe nane ili mubhafwate.
GAL 4:18 Shinza sana wila abhe ni shomela husababu zilishinza nasagagumuda tougwanalinamwa.
GAL 4:19 Bhanabhane mubhadodo, imbinile inkuni kwa ajili yenyu hadi uKilisti aumbishe mhati yenyu.
GAL 4:20 Andinasongwa abhe pamoja namwe isalezi na badilisye isauti yane, kwa sababu indinamashaka juuu yenyu.
GAL 4:21 Mbozi, amwe mmunyonywa awe pansi yindajizo, sagamwevwazye indajizyo yiyanga?
GAL 4:22 Iyandihwilwe aje u Abrahamu alina bhana bhishilume bhabhele, weka hola onshe umutumwa na uwamwao hashe umwaushe.
GAL 4:23 Hata shesho, ola umutumwa apapwilwe hubele tou, ila ola oshe umwaushe apapwilwe huusobhizi.
GAL 4:24 Amambo ega gawezehana ahelezwe hwatumile atenganisye, afwataje abhashe ebha bhalengana na mapatano gabhele. Limo afume hwigamba Sinai. Lipapa abhana bhabhali bhatumwa, ono yu Hajiri.
GAL 4:25 Eshi u Hajiri ligamba Sinai leleleho hu u Arabuni. Lilenganisiwa ni Yerusalemu yisalezi afwatanaje mutumwa palishimo na bhana bhakwe.
GAL 4:26 Ila i Yerusalemu oleho pamwanya yiwaule, nene ndiyo yumaye wetu.
GAL 4:27 Afwatanaje isimbiwilwe, “Songwaji, “awe nshe uligomba awe wasaga upapa. Gholaga iholo na ghomaga ihalanga hwasongwe, awe wasagaulinuuzowefu wa pape. Eshi abhinji bhanabhakwe wali gomba, hani ya bhala wola wali nunume.”
GAL 4:28 Eshi bhaholo, amwe mulibhana hansi u Isaka, amwe mulibhana wilosobhizi.
GAL 4:29 Whinsiku zila ambawe mumuntu apapwilwe humjibu wembele anyanzizye ola wapapwilwe humjibu wimpepo hata husalezi huli shesho.
GAL 4:30 Iizi liyigawele? “Mwefwe oshe umtumwa pamoja nu mwana wakwe wishilume. Afwatanaje umwana washe umutumwa sagaipyana pamoja nu mwana washe umwaule.”
GAL 4:31 Eshi, bhalolo, ate sagatibhana bhanshe mutumwa, ila tilibhana bhanshe umwauzi.
GAL 5:1 Afuataneji Kilisti atipiye owaule nkatibhebhaule, eshiemeleli shinza nantele mgaje khatwe na mabhibhi agamsi.
GAL 5:2 Enya anene Paulo emba bhola aje nkashele mubhatahilwe uKilisti sabhabho mbele nalimo lila.
GAL 5:3 Nantele ehubhonzye olumeyatahilwe aje ahwaziwa awitume hudajizyo zyoti.
GAL 5:4 Bhabha bheshele hutali no Kilisiti, bhala bhoti mwamubhaziwa elwoli hundajizyo mugwiye patali no wene.
GAL 5:5 Nantele hidala elwapepo huwiza tigolela odandamu awe lyoli.
GAL 5:6 Nashi Okilisti o Yesu atahilwe nasintetahilwe nemo amana gagati yimani nyeno ye bhomba embombo ashelelee olugano humanye ahatu.”
GAL 5:7 Mwali mtumba shinza yo nanu gobhahwanileasinte yagope elyoli?
GAL 5:8 Asohwe na bhombe ezyo sahu fumu hwamwene omweneyabha kwizye amwe.
GAL 5:9 Okhali nashe unankanya unankenye ahatu noti.
GAL 5:10 Edinenso bhezyo namwe ashilile o Gosi aje semubhasebhe hwidala elyamwabho lyalyonti yayuti ola yandabhatezye adanyemle edongo yakwe yuyo mwene yayotiola.
GAL 5:11 Mwaholo nkashe ehwendelela alombelelee etohala, yenu nantele eyemba? Hwiswali elyo halahahali hiza pi khobhe hanye handawe zye anankanye.
GAL 5:12 Ejango zyane aje bhala bhabhalongozyo shibhibhi bhandahwiyefwe bhene.
GAL 5:13 Ongolobhi abhakwizizye amwe mwaholo huwaule muganje autumile owaule wenyu nashi olweteho humbele. Nanantele hwakwe hulugono mwavwanuje mwemwe hwahwe.
GAL 5:14 Hwehube edajizyo zyoti zikamili she hunyomezyo emo yope ene. “Lazima agane yapalemene nawe ashiwewe humwene.”
GAL 5:15 Nantele nkashe mlumana na lezane mhwiyenye nkashele mhwinankonye mbhehwe mbhena.
GAL 5:16 Eyanga jedaji na mpepo nantele sambha malezye enyonyo enzyembile.
GAL 5:17 Nkashile ambele guli enyonyo engosi ahwe njelele hapepo no mpepo ali neyoyo ngosi ahwenjele le mbele ezi zikhomana kila muno wamwene. Gaga pamiye aje semu bhomba evitu vya muhwa za abhombe.
GAL 5:18 Nantele nkashile ompepo abhalongola amwe, sagamhwe semheli pasi ye dajizyo.
GAL 5:19 Eshi embombo eye belee ebhoneha. Yope yayene ohuni, ogwenyusu, mwibha,
GAL 5:20 emputo eyeshifwani itonga, mtuyasaga, mhovwana, ibho, malibho, enkuni, ashidane, malongono, abaguhane humabhaza,
GAL 5:21 evubhi, omwezi, olyavi na gamwabho gamiji gagalinashego. Embasuda amwe nashi sana shasudile olwahwande, aje bhala bhabha bhombombo nashi ezyo sagabhai gala oumwene wa Ngolobhi.
GAL 5:22 Nantele idondolo elya Mpepo olugano, ashime, owiza, avumilile, owatu owiza, ahwamini,
GAL 5:23 ohogowe hashe, nazimo edajizyo zyezikhana enongwa nashiezyo.
GAL 5:24 Hatabhali bhakilisti uoyesabhaguyevyezye obeleepamono sudozyobho enyonyo zwobho embibhi.
GAL 5:25 Nkashele tidela huMpepo nantele tibhajende nu Mpepo.
GAL 5:26 Mugaje ahwivume, tigaje ahwandizanye kilamtu nowamwabho nantele tiganje alolane evumbi
GAL 6:1 Holo, nkashe umuntu akhetwe nembibhi, amwe mwamli bhe shiroho, mhwanziwa ahugwezye oyo oholo humwoyo gwehogowe. Ohu mhwiyenyaje mwemwe aje msahajelwe.
GAL 6:2 Mwejelanaje amazigo, mwaimemezewa nendajizyo zya Kilisti.
GAL 6:3 Omuntu wawonti nkahwilola aje mwinza oyo nomo ahwikhopela yoyo.
GAL 6:4 Kila muntu ayenye embombo yakwe ndipo nkanzabhe na hantu hahwisombezye, bila ahwilenganisye no muntu owenje.
GAL 6:5 Afuatanaje kila muntu ayenyemula izigo lyakwe yoyo.
GAL 6:6 Omuntu wafundiziwe izu lye womi ashirikisysaje ogosi wakwe aminza.
GAL 6:7 Mganjeakhopelwe. Ongolobhe sazalauliwa. Omuntu hala hatota hahala haiyuna.
GAL 6:8 Kila muntu watota embeyu hubele aivuna amabhibhi, omwene watota embeyu huShiroho, avuna owomi wewiilawila afume huShiroho.
GAL 6:9 Tigajealite abhombe aminza, afutanaje taivuna huwakati wakwe tashe nkashe setaizilamwa.
GAL 6:10 Esho basi nkashe tiwa no muda, tiwombe aminza kila muntu. Tiwombe aminzo sana hasa bhabhali wapufi bhabhali mlwetesholo.
GAL 6:11 Enyaji nugosi we barua yensimbile no khono gwane nene.
GAL 6:12 Bhala bhabhahwanza abhombe eminza huwenyowe bele bhabhebho wahomezya atahiriwe. Bhabhomba esho nkabhaganje hunjile mmanyemba ge shi khobhehanyo sha Kilisti.
GAL 6:13 Afuatanaje ebho bhabhatahiriwe abhene sebhashirika endajizyo. Wahwanza amwe mtahiriwe mkabha hwisombezyaje amabele genyu.
GAL 6:14 Chaganjebhoneshe ehwiyomvwa ila hushi khobhehanyo sha Gosi wetu oYesu o Kilisti.
GAL 6:15 Afuatanaje seshihwelehwehwa atahiriwe au asintenatahiriwe aje hantu baada yepo empampo empye mhimu.
GAL 6:16 Afuataneje wonti bhabhaghala namna ene, bhabhe ne lusho na sajilane ibhe humwanya yabho wonti, na pamwanya ye Isiraeli ya Ngolobhe.
GAL 6:17 Esalezi eshi omuntu wawontiasantamansye, afuatamaje nyemuyeechapa zya Yesu mbele gwane.
GAL 6:18 Eneema ya Gosi wetu oYesu Kilisti ebhe ne viroho vyenyu, bhaholo. Amina.
EPH 1:1 U Paulo, utumwe wa Kristi Yesu whagane no Ngolobhe, whabhabhehwelwe kwajili ya Ngolobhe bhabhaleho hu Efeso na bhali golosi mwa Yesu Kristi.
EPH 1:2 Ibule naibhe humwenyu jwinza yifuma hwa Ngolobhe u Baba wetu na ugosi Yesu Kristi.
EPH 1:3 Ngolobhe na Baba wa Gosi wetu Yesu Kristi alumbelelwe. Yeyo watisaile katika insayo zyamumoyo, katika apantu pahumwanya mhati mwaKristi.
EPH 1:4 Shahusele umbwe ense, Ungolobhe atisaluye ate tete wheteha katika Kristi. Atisaluye ate ili tiwezye abhe tagolosu tasagatilalamishiwa whilongelela lyakwe.
EPH 1:5 Katika ulugano Ungolobhe atisaluye hwandilo whahuteje hansi abhanabhakwe whidala lya Yesu Kristi. Awombile ishi whisababu aganilwe awombe shila shanyonyilwe.
EPH 1:6 Zizifumila mkwakwe huje Ungolobhe awhinuliwa whiweneyi tuntumu ebhi shosho atishiliye wene whidala lya lugano wakwe.
EPH 1:7 Alengane nu ganwe wakwe, tilinuwaushe ashilile mwidanda lyake, ukhowoshe wimbibhi. Tilinayo eli husababu utabhazivibule yakwe.
EPH 1:8 Awombe wene ene abhe nyinji kwasababu yetu huhekima ni njele.
EPH 1:9 Ungolobhe awombile ieleweshe humwetu ela ilyoli yiyobhele humipango, alingane ni hamu yayaloleshe mhati ya Kristi.
EPH 1:10 Umda gwimida gwasagakuli na mapongosoga kamilisheha mipango gakwe, Ungolobhe ayivibheha peka kila shintu shahumwanya na shaihumwanya yense muhati ya Kilisti.
EPH 1:11 Mwa Kristi tali tisalulilwe na hutikusudile hata kabla yimunda. Ene yali yatokeene nu mpango wawomba ivintu vyonti whikweli lwimagano gakwe.
EPH 1:12 Ungolobhe awombile osho ili tiwezye abhe na huyilole nutuntumusi wakwe. Talibhawhande abhe nuda ndamazu muhati ya Yesu.
EPH 1:13 Yali whida lya Yesu aje mwahe vwezye iizu lilyoli iizu lilokole wenyu whidala lya Yesu. Yali whamwene aje mweteshe na bheshe we umhuji gwa pepo ufinjilwe watawe umhusi gwa pepo ufinjilwe watasobhezelwe.
EPH 1:14 Upepo ndo dhamana yiupyano lwetu hadi atabhale lwalwaipatihana. Ene yahuilole nutuntumusu wakwe.
EPH 1:15 Alengane neli, afume umuda gwa nahevwesye aje ulweteho lwenyu muhati mwagosi u Yesu na ahusu iagano lwenyu whabhala wonti bhategwilwe kwajili yakwe.
EPH 1:16 Sigindeshile ahunsalifwe Ungolobhe kwaajili iyenyu na hubhatashe mu mputo
EPH 1:17 Ilabha aje Ungolobhe wa Gosi uwetu U Yesu Kristi, ubabu wituntumusu, wituntumubu, aibhapela umoyo gwinjele, amakwinkule givfahamu wakwe.
EPH 1:18 Ilabha aje amaso genyu gahumoyo gabhewhe ulukhozyo. Ohame amanye uwhi udanda mazu wakwiziwe whenyu, ilabha aje mumanye utabhazo wituntumu wapyane whakwe bhalipeka na bhala bhabhabhesheshewelwe kwaajili yakwe.
EPH 1:19 Ilabha aje umanye ugosi uuzidile engovu yakwe mhati yetu yatiheleha. Ou ugosi ufuma na nawombe imbombo mongoro zyakwe.
EPH 1:20 Ene ngovo yayawombile imbombo muhati ya Kristi wakati Ongolobhe lwazyosezye afume whazimu na hukhazye munyobhe yakwe yahundelo paapli pamwanya.
EPH 1:21 Akhazizye UKristi pamwanya uhutali mugosi, imamulaka, ongovo, pakhale, na kila litawa lyaitawha. Akhazizye U Yesu sagatu hwakati ou hata humuda gogowewhenzu.
EPH 1:22 Ungolobhe avitabhye ivintu vyonti pansi yimanama ga Kristi. Amombile umwene abhe litwe pamwanya yivintu katika ishibhanza.
EPH 1:23 Shibhanza lilibele gwakwe, ugolosu lwakwe lolo lumenyu ivintu vyonti mumadala gonti.
EPH 2:1 Shila shamshili shilasha mwafwile hutula nongwa nzyenyu ni bhivyi zyenyu.
EPH 2:2 Ishashahali huje iga awande mwajendaga afhatane nabhalilo kinsiine. Mwali mjenda adaje uwatabhile wimaha gimwanya ine ya pepo yakwe yibhomba imbombo wala atulano nongwa.
EPH 2:3 Natiwayo pahosi ipo twaliibho asawa mwintiha. Twabhombanga enamunayinyonyo zibhivhi izyemabile getuu, twali tubhombazyai ganile manbiligitu shata nmenye twinte. Lelo Ungulubhi mwinjii wipwa na phipo yilunganoolakwe ulugosi lwahatugana athii.
EPH 2:4 Lelo Ungulubhi mwinjii wipwa na phipo yilunganoolakwe ulugosi lwahatugana athii.
EPH 2:5 Ahabhalilo atalibhaafwe mumbivhizyetu.
EPH 2:6 Unguluvhi atuzyuswa palisimo natubhombe akhalepalishimo mahali pamwanya muhati yakwe iya Kristi U Yesu.
EPH 2:7 Abhomba ishi habhalilo habhalilozyanzi awezye ni bhoneswe ukabhi ugosi uwihazi wakwe atulanje anti idala atulanje ili idala liwemavu awakwe muhanti mwa Kristi U Yesu.
EPH 2:8 Humwoyi abhagombulewi dalayilyinteho naishisashamile hulinti yu Ngulubhi atusuntile.
EPH 2:9 Hagaifumila nimbo ahahafumila agandabhe umo uwasumbe.
EPH 2:10 Huje anti tulimbombo ya Ngulubhi tuumbelwe nu Kristi uYesu abhombe amizha imbombizya Ngulubhi aliapanga awande ulwinje lwehali huno gwayetu ilitujendaje muhapango.
EPH 2:11 Mkumbushe epo ulwenje mwalibhantu bhapanzii ishifwa tanebhabili. Muwitwa “salmlivhizha shila shashihwita shizha ishibhelye shashibho bhwa nakhono gamuntu.
EPH 2:12 Muhanti mhwo mhwo amwe mwabangulwee nu Kristi mwalibhajenyi wa bhathu Israeli. Mwali bhajenyi hulu fingoo lwakhoshelene munziumuuu.
EPH 2:13 Leloo eshi alanganaje uKristi uYesu namwe rula nhihali mwalihutali nu Ngulubhi widanda lwaKristi.
EPH 2:14 Nphipo umwene abhahabhawilye abhiha omoo. Eshibhelengwa hwe amanganya ulumba lwa pahenyee. Uoolugu.
EPH 2:15 Phepo akomesya mambo gamulile nupango iliaumbe mutu uomoo upya muhati yakwe. Afanye uwaushe.
EPH 2:16 Aomba ishi apatanisya eviphugavhili vyabhadyu abhi ligalu vhadhu bhigamo wa Ngulubhi alangane shivikonhehayo widalalyishikhoehanyo aguzolo thezya uluvisanyo.
EPH 2:17 Usu ahadha nawaule mubhe ahaushe amwiumwa lihutali nuwaushe wahwa ahali nuwalishe wavhene vhala vhali phephe.
EPH 2:18 Ishi widala lwa Yesu atii tuvhawile tunifwasi wagula umwoyo gumo awinjile wadada.
EPH 2:19 Ishilelo amwii muwantu mwaliwapazi samulibhajezhi nabhajenyi antele ishi mrikhaya pamopene nabhala bhabagulwa hunongwa Ngulubhi nabhombi munyumba mwa Ngulubhi.
EPH 2:20 Muzenjilwe mulwata lwatumwa na kuwa UKristi UYesu yuyo alilingaga igosi lwapanshinje.
