EPH 2:21 Umwene inyumba yundhi iyunganiziwe palishimo nabhve nyumba mwaputile muhati mwapapa.
EPH 2:22 Muhati yakwe amwe na mwezengwa palishimo ni maha pakhale Ngulubhi mwahala uzuli.
EPH 3:1 Afuatane naje nini, Paulo, nempinywa wa Yesu Kilisti kwaajili yinyu mubhinsi.
EPH 3:2 Imanya aje muvwizye hunongwayi mbombo yi wene ila Ngulubhi yahampiye kwaajili yinyu.
EPH 3:3 Ihubhasimbila afumilane shezili ugubulwo sheubhugubulilwe lyenahandishe hufupi wikalata ilyingi.
EPH 3:4 Na bhazya iga ungamanya uwinza wani mulyoli ubhu wewuyifisile hunongwa ya Kilisti.
EPH 3:5 Hu mpapwo inzyinji ilyoli ili sewabhombilwe bhulooleshe hu bhana bhabhantu. Ila kwa sasa umewekwa wazi kwa Roho kwa Mitume waliotengwa na Manabii.
EPH 3:6 Ilyoli lyelayifisile huhuje abhantu abhi insi bhape bhaahli amwetu na ajumbe bhamwetu bhabhili tilipeka ni ahadi ya Yesu Kilisti ashilile izwi.
EPH 3:7 Hwihi imbombishe mbobhambombo humpeysa ya weene ya Ngulubhi yampiye ani ashilile imbombo yi nguvu zyakwe.
EPH 3:8 Ungulubhi ahafumizye impesa ini huline hata nkushe ani indi dodo hubhonti hubhala bhabhabaguliliwe hunongwa ya Ngulubhi. Impesya ni huhije ihwanziwa hubhalumbilile abhimbi izwi lyelili nu tabhazi wesebhuleleha kwa Yesu.
EPH 3:9 ihanziwa hubhalumbilile abhantu bhoti aje umpyango gwa Ngulubhi uwisili. Umpango ugu gwahafisilwe amaha minsi gegashilile nu Ngulubhi ya vibhumbile ivintu vyonti.
EPH 3:10 Ili lyali aje ashilile ishibhanza agosi bhoontu abhapamwanya, bhamanye isehemu inyinji izyi maandi izyi hekima ya Ngulubhi.
EPH 3:11 Iga handigafumiye ashilile umpango wa wila wewukamilishe muhati mwa Yesu Kilisti gosi wetu.
EPH 3:12 Pipo hwa Yesu tilinudandamazu nu uwezo uwabhe nu dandamazu hwi dala lyi lwitu hukwakwe.
EPH 3:13 Iishi ihumbalabha ingaje azila mwe humayimba gaa kwaajili yinyu, iga tuntumu winyu.
EPH 3:14 Afuatane ni shi insugamila hwa ngosi.
EPH 3:15 Hwa mwene kila bhantu abah humwanya na bhantu abhapamwanya pansi, likwiziwilwe itawa.
EPH 3:16 Ilabha mubhapele uweene afumilane mutabhazi wituntumu wakwe abhabhishe (abhagomye) hu nguvu ashilile hwa Mpepo wakwe, yali muhati mulimwe.
EPH 3:17 Ilabha huje UKiristu muhati mmoyo ginyu ashilile ulwitiho.
EPH 3:18 Ilabha huje mubhe ni shinanu umusingi gwi lugano lwakwe mubhe mwigano lyake nke mumanye ahwelewe, peka na bhantu bhebhamwitishe mupana na mutali ni kimo ni kina shi lugano lwa Kitisti.
EPH 3:19 Ilabha huje mumanye ugosi wi lugano lwa Kiristi lwe lushilile ifahamu. Mubhombe izi nke mumemwe ugolosi wonti uwa Ngulubhi.
EPH 3:20 Ishi hwa mwene yangabhomba ijambo lyolyonti zaidi ya gonti getilabha na getigasibha ashilile hu nguvu zyakwe yibhomba imbombo muhati yitu,
EPH 3:21 hwa mwene hubhe nu funtumu mushibhanza hwa Yesu Kilisti hu mpapo zyonti wila na wila. Amina
EPH 4:1 Antele nkashile yagaliliwe hwa jili ya Gosi, embalabhe mjende shinzashinza na uwite ambao Ungolobhe abhakwizizwe.
EPH 4:2 Mukhale esha wishindishe eshi Gosi no hogowe no ujimbi. Mwejelanaje esha ganane.
EPH 4:3 Umbaji ajimbizwe na bheshe umoja uwe Roho katieshefungo eshe lyeteho.
EPH 4:4 Huli ubele gume ne Roho emo neshe shamli antele mwali mkwiziwe eshi uhakika upambamle umo uwewite wenyu.
EPH 4:5 Ugosi aliumo ulyeteho lumo, ulwuzwo lumo. Ungolobhe omo
EPH 4:6 na uBaba wabhonti. Umwahale we mambo gonti na gonti gali mhati yakwe.
EPH 4:7 Shilo muntu apewewe eshipawa afwatane neshipimo esha pawa esha Kristi.
EPH 4:8 Neshe nsimbo shaziyanga: “Alushile amwanya eshi alogozwezwe abhe pinywe uwe utumwa. Afumizi evipawa wa bhantu.”
EPH 4:9 Yenu emana ya, “Alushe,” isipokuwa ahishile epande zwonti ezwa pasi pa dunia?
EPH 4:10 Umwahule ahishile yoyola umuntu ambaye nantele alushile patali juu ye mwanya zwonti. Abhombile esho ili abhehwakwe uwe kati evintu vyonti.
EPH 4:11 Kristi afumizwe evipawa kama neshe asontizi akuwa abhanjilisti, adimi, amwalimwa.
EPH 4:12 Abhombile eshe abhawezeshe abhalyeteho ili embombo eyuzeje ubele ugwa Kristi.
EPH 4:13 Abhomba eshi hadi ate tenti tifishile undwemo uwe lyeteho na amaalifa aga mwana wakwe Ungolobhe. Abhombile esho hadi tiwezwe akhome neshe bhala bhabhafishie ekimo kamili esha Kristi.
EPH 4:14 Ene antele tigaje bhebhana tigaje ruswe ruswe ohu no hwo ili tigaje ahwegwe na kila aina eye hala elyefundisho, age hila ezwa bhantu hu njelenje uwa khopehanye wautejile.
EPH 4:15 Eshi tiyanje elyoli eye lugano nakule zayidi hwidala lyonti mhati yakwe itwe yo Kristi.
EPH 4:16 Kristi abhonganisizwe pandwemo ubele ugwa bhoziwa guunganisiwe ubele gwonti gukwe nazenjeshe gwogwo hulugano.
EPH 4:17 Antale eyanga eli, embalabha hwa Gosi: Mgaje ajende antele neshe abhantu abhamataifa wabhajenda muubatiuli uwenjele zwao.
EPH 4:18 Bhaponyizwe enkisi museo zwao bhatagwilwe afume huwomi uwa Ngolobhe hulema wauli mhati yao kwa sabu ya ukhome uwe moyo gao.
EPH 4:19 Sebha hwiyovwa esoni bhahwikabizizwe bhebho huntavu humatendo gao age ntavu, kila aina ya uwimi.
EPH 4:20 Nantele eshi seshasho shamwanyiye ahusu Kristi.
EPH 4:21 Elola antele mwovzwe ahusu umwahale elola aje mwali mmanyiziwa hwamwahale neshe elyoli yilimuhati ya Yesu.
EPH 4:22 Lazima mwaule amambo gonti gagajendelela ne njendelelo zweyu ezwe mwaha, uuntu uwemwaha uuntu uwemwaha waubhola afwate ne tamaa ezwe hopelo.
EPH 4:23 Auli untu wenyu uwemwaha ili nkaombwe shipya huroho eye njele zwenyu.
EPH 4:24 Bhombi eshe muwezwalane no Ngolobhe. Ubhombwelwe hehaki eye uzelu uwe lyoli.
EPH 4:25 Eshi bheshi patali ukhopelaji. “Yangaji elyoli, shila muntu no jirani wakwe,” afwanaje tili bhaputi aje shila munti hwa wamwao.
EPH 4:26 Mbhaje ne nguru, lelo mgayejeswe sumlinazwe nguru zwenyu.
EPH 4:27 Mganje hupele usetano moyo.
EPH 4:28 Yeyonti yahwibha lazima gajewibhe antele. Badala yakwe lazima abhombe embombo. Abhombe ambombo efaida humakhono gakwe ili awezwe humwavwe umuntu yalineshida.
EPH 4:29 Ekauli embibhi egaje afume mumalomo genyu. Badala yakwe enongwa lazima gafume mumalomu genyu abhapele efaida bhala bhabhahavwa.
EPH 4:30 Nantele mgaje hunkungubhazwe Roho ufije uwa Ngolobhe hwa mwahale mubhehwelye muwaule hunsiku eye waule.
EPH 4:31 Lazima mubheshe hutali ukhali wonti, nelyoyo ne nkuni ibho na endigo pandwemo na shila namna eye mbibhi bhaji bhinza mwemwe hwa mwemwe.
EPH 4:32 Mubhanje ne huruma msajilana je mwemwe hwa mwemwe, neshe shila Ungolobhe ashilile Kristi shabha sajiye amwe.
EPH 5:1 Amwe mubhe bhantu bhahulowdozye Ungulubhi, muli bhana bhakwe bhabhagewe.
EPH 5:2 Mujendaje mulugano lwakwe, neshi uYesu natiganile ate, ahwifumizye yuyo husababu yetu umwene ali sadaka nedhabihu, abhe nushili nyinza yahusungwezye Ungulubhi.
EPH 5:3 Oumalayano uchafu ne mbimbi ezyamwo ziganjetambulwe hulimwe, neshi shashihwanziwa hwa bhabhamwaminile,
EPH 5:4 emvisyo zisahatambulwe, enjango ezyeshilemalema, au entanilo ezyakenyensanye, ego segali sawa nafuu asalifye.
EPH 5:5 Mubhajiye abhe no uhakika aje umuntu yalimalaya, yalichafu, nuyaziliha, uyo apuuta shifwani siga alinougale wowonti hwa Ngulubhi. Umuntu hwa Ngulubhi.
EPH 5:6 Umuntu yayonti asabhakhopele nenongwa zyakwe, hushali ye mambo ega elyoyolya Ngulubhi lihwenza hwa bhana bhasebhahweteha.
EPH 5:7 Eshi usakundane nabho.
EPH 5:8 Maana amwe emande mwalinkisi, eshi muli mulukhozyo hwa Yesu, mujendaje neshi abhana bhabhali mulukhozyo.
EPH 5:9 Amatunda gamulukhozyo gabho ngenye uwinza wonti, ehaki nuukweli.
EPH 5:10 Anzaga haalo hahahusungwi zya Ungulubhi.
EPH 5:11 Huganjebhe ahwavwanwe nezya hunkisi zyasenyinza, epoawe bhehaga embombo enyinza.
EPH 5:12 Maana embombo zyabhabhombela hunkisi zyensoni ata huziyanje.
EPH 5:13 Amambo gonti gagavundulwa nulukhozyo gabha pazelu,
EPH 5:14 shila hantu hahavundulwe nu lukhozyo habha mulukhozyo, nayanje huje, bhuha awe wugowa utulo, bhuha afume hwabhafwe UYesu abhahukhozezye ulukhozyo.”
EPH 5:15 Mubhanje bhazingatizi pamjenda, siyo aje mubhanje neshi abhantu bhasigabha nenjele mubhanje neshi abhinjele.
EPH 5:16 Musahalembele mukhalaganaje ensiku ezi zyembibhi.
EPH 5:17 Musahabhe bhalema mumanyaje aje zyasungwa Ungulubhi zizyalihu.
EPH 5:18 Musahakholwe, ehombwa ehulongola umuntu humbibhi nu nanzi.
EPH 5:19 Afazali mumenye Umpepo Ufinjile mumoyo genyu. Yangajishila muntu nuwamwabho muzinzanyaja, ne ng'oma, zyazigwizya hwa Gosi.
EPH 5:20 Ensiku zyonti musalifyaje Ungulubhi mwitawa lya Yesu Kristi nu Ngulubhi uise witu.
EPH 5:21 Hwifumyi mwemwe shila muntu nuwamwao hunshinshi ya Yesu Kristi.
EPH 5:22 Mubhashe muhwifumiaje hwa lume bhenyu neshi hwa Yesu Kristi Ugosi.
EPH 5:23 Ulume litwe lya she wakwe neshi uYesu shali litwelyi kanisa ulume fyulwe wa beele gwashe wakwe.
EPH 5:24 Lelo neshi ikanisa shalili pansi pa yasu, namwe mubhashe shamubhanje hwalume bhenyu kwa shila hantu.
EPH 5:25 Mubhalume, mubhaganaje abhashe bhenyu neshi U Yesu shahaliganile ikanisa ahafwiye hunongwa yakwe.
EPH 5:26 Abhombile esho ahanzaga aje libhe lifinjile. Alyozizye nalizelusye na menze mwizu lyakwe.
EPH 5:27 Abhombile esho aje ahwitwalile yuyo ikanisa ituntumu lyaselili na makosa nkagamo wala embibhi zyazyonti na hahahonti hahlewigenelego lyali lituntumu nuzeluwonti.
EPH 5:28 Shishila, alume bhope bhabhaganaje ashe bhabho neshi amabili gabho bhebho, yahugana ushe wakwe ahwigawa yuyo.
EPH 5:29 Nkumo umuntu yaguvitwa ubili gwakwe pavonti agutunza nagulisye nagugane, neshi uYesu shaligene ikanisa lyakwe.
EPH 5:30 Ate tiibhashirika bhakwe nu bili gwakwe.
EPH 5:31 “Hushauli ene olume aihuleha uise nu nyina wakwe aibhala nushe wakwe nakhale nawo na ebho bhabhili bhaibha muntu umo”.
EPH 5:32 eli lihwifisile leloane eyanga ezya Kristi ni kanisa.
EPH 5:33 Lelo, shila muntu agawe ushe wakwe neshi shahwigawa umwene, wope ushe ashinshimaje ulume wakwe.
EPH 6:1 Mubhana bhogopaji apafi bhenyu hu shi Ngolobhe afuatanaje ene ye lyoli.
EPH 6:2 “Obhonje ne neshinshi hwa isewaho na hwa nyina waho” (Afutanaje ene ndajinzyo eya hwande yeli ne ndagano),
EPH 6:3 “nkasibhe nafu hulimwe nkamukhalaje olwizyo otali munsi.”
EPH 6:4 Amwe mwa baba, mganje bhavisye abahna bhenyu na bhasababisye ilyoyo, baada yesho, walelaji na bhasunde hundajizyo zya Gosi.
EPH 6:5 Amwe mwabhomba mbombo bhogopaji agosi bhenyu wepa pansi neheshima engosi na yinje no owoga wawafuma. mumoyo genyu mubhewoga hwa bhene nanshi satihu mwogopa omwene Kilisti.
EPH 6:6 Uwoga wenyu usahabhe pala tu agosi bhenyu na bhabhenya na wasovye. Baada yakwe, mubhanje woga nanshi atumwa bha Kilisti. Bhombaji zya songwa Ongolobhe afume mmoyo genyu,
EPH 6:7 bhabhombeleji hu moyo genyu gonti, afuatanaje mhubhombela Gosi wala se bhantu,
EPH 6:8 mhwanziwa amanye aje kilo libhombo omuntu lya bhomba, aipata e zawadi afume hwa Gosi, atabhe tumwa au mwigule.
EPH 6:9 Namwe mwagosi bhombaji shesho hwa tumwa bhenyu. Mganje abhogofye nkamumenye aje Ogosi wabhonti yayola waliwanya. Nkamumanye aje na humo apendelele mhati yakwe.
EPH 6:10 Esho mubhanje ni lyomi hwa gosi mvuwezo wilyomi lyakwe.
EPH 6:11 Kwati esilaha zyonti zya Ngolobhe, ili nkamuwezye ahwemelele shingunga sha setano.
EPH 6:12 Afuatanaje ibhoo lyetu seli danda ne nyama, huli zaidi ye umwene noutawala we roho na tabhala bha munsi bhe mabhibhi ne nkisi, shizanye empopo hu sehemu ya humwanya.
EPH 6:13 Eshi kwati esilaha zyonti zya Ngolobhe, ili nkamuwezye akhala sawa ashi zanye amabhibhi hunsiki ezi embibhi. Baada ya male kila hantu, myemelela sawa.
EPH 6:14 Hwahuje eemlelaji sawa. Bhombaji eshi afutanaje mfungwile nkanda ne lyoli pashifubha.
EPH 6:15 Bhombaji eshi mubhanje mkwete ouhaani mmagaga genyu walombe lele izu lye waushe.
EPH 6:16 Hu kila namna mweje engao ye lweteshelo yayaihumwavwa azimwe olutisyo lwa bhibhi.
EPH 6:17 Kwataji enkofilwa ye woziwa ni panga lye shoroho, ambalyo lizu lya Ngolobhe.
EPH 6:18 epo ne mputo zyayo ne dua. Putaji huu shirolo umuda gwonti. Enyenyo ene mubhanje bha hwenye muda gwonti hu uvumilivu wonti ne mpute zyabhaputile aputi bhonti.
EPH 6:19 Putaji sababu ya huline, ili nkepwe izu nihwigula ilomu lyane. Putaji aje nkenele zyaje huu huu dandamazu elyoli ehobhela yeyanjila olulombelelo.
EPH 6:20 Ashilile ululombelelo ane endibalozi nenfungwilwe amanyoro aje muhati enjanje no ujasiri kama nanshi sehwiyomvezye ayanje.
EPH 6:21 Amwe mumanye amambo gane shehwendelela, o Tikiko oholo wane owamwetu otumwa ohogowe hwa gosi, aibhabhonzya kila hantu.
EPH 6:22 Entumwilye hulimwe hwi lengo kabisa, aje mumanye azizye amoyo getu.
EPH 6:23 Olutengano lubhe hwa holo, no lwomvwano no lweteshelo afame hwa Ngolobhe Ogosi oYesu Kristi.
EPH 6:24 Uwene nate na bhonti wagene ogosi oYesu Kilisti hulwo mvwano lula wa saga ufwa.
PHI 1:1 U Paulo nu Timotheo abeshibha sha Yesu Kristi, hwa Bhaala bhabhabagulwe hushauli ya Yesu bhabhakhala hu Filipi, pandwemo na bheenyi na bheenyi adodo.
PHI 1:2 Eneema ebhe hulimwe nu tengane waufuma hwa Ngulubhe uise witu nu hwa Yesu Kristi.
PHI 1:3 Ehusalifya Ungulubhi wane shila pembizuha amwe mwenti.
PHI 1:4 Ensiku zyonti shila neputa embaputila, nu mwoyo gwane gusongwa nembaputila.
PHI 1:5 Endinensalifyo nyinji hushauli yelweteho mwibhangili ahwande isiku elyahwande paka sanyunu eshi.
PHI 1:6 Endi nouhakika aje umwene yahandile embobho enyinza hulimwe abhahwendelele aimalezye mpaka isiku lya Yesu Kristi Ugosi wetu.
PHI 1:7 Sawa huliwe ahwiyomvweshinza maana embabheshele humwoyo gwane. Amwe mulibhashirika bhamwitu mu neema mufungwe wawe nana litanjilaga ibhangili.
PHI 1:8 Ungulubhi keti wane, shembasukwilwe amwe mwenti mulugano lwa muhati mwa Yesu Kristi.
PHI 1:9 Awe elabha huje: ulugano lwenyu lwonjelele hahinji na munjeele zyonti.
PHI 1:10 Elaabha kwa ajili yeli aje mubhe ne njeele eyzapime na salule amambo aminza tee. Nantele embalabhila huje mubhe bhinz bila ahwilonje embibhi humwoyo hwisikulya Yesu.
PHI 1:11 Nantele Ungulubhi abhamemye enyinza mu moyo genyu gagafuma hwa Yesu Kristu, no tuntumune nsumbo zya Ngulubhi.
PHI 1:12 Eshi bhaholo bhawe, ehwanza aje, mumanye huje, amambo gala gagfumiye hulimwe galikhonzizye ibangili aji libhalaje hwitagalila.
PHI 1:13 Hashisho empinyo yaneya bhampinyile hushauli wa Yesu vimanyishe hwalinzi bha Gosi na hwa bhantu bhonti.
PHI 1:14 Na aholo bhinji hwa Ugosi U Yesu, hunongwa zye mpinyo zyane, abhantu bhalumbililaizi nkasaje nahamo nantele bila ahwogope.
PHI 1:15 Lelo bhamo bhahulumbilila u Yesu na moyo amabhibhi nibho nantele bhamo bha alumbilila na moyo aminza.
PHI 1:16 Bhaala bhabhahulumbilila uYesu hulugano bhamenye huje ane embehwelwe epa aje endyumile izu.
PHI 1:17 Nantele bhamo bhahulumbilila Ukristi hufaida yabho nu mwoyo ubhibhi. Bhaiga jee ane embapate amalabha nempengozya bhampinyile.
PHI 1:18 Eshi? Sesaga, nkahushibhibhi au shinza, Kristi alumbililwa humadala gonti nanewayo esungwa. Pipo endimenye
PHI 1:19 eli huje lyaindetela ane huje eni gushu mufungwe wane. Elilyaifumila hunongwa yemputo zyenyu nu musaada gwa Umpepo wa Yesu Kristi.
PHI 1:20 Afuatane nensubhilo ezyelyoli huje ane sehailola ensoni. Naibha nelyoo lyonti. Neshi ensikuzyonti neshi, esubhilahuje, U Yesu aihwizuvya hubili uwawe, nkashele huwomi au hunfwa.
PHI 1:21 Huline ane afwe shinza nakhale huline yu Kristu.
PHI 1:22 Lelo akhale nkahwinza hubeele ehuletela Ungulubhi embombo enyinza, mawyi sendimenye elyasalule.
PHI 1:23 Maana ebhuhwa tee nensebho zibhili. Esungwa aguleshe ubili ogu embale akhale hwa Yesu eho hesamani tee tee.
PHI 1:24 Hwope asagale mubili ogu shinza hushauli yenyu.
PHI 1:25 Afwatane aje endinouhakika nelii, emenye huje nahaisagala huje embanjese hwendelela akhale pandwimo namwe mwenti, hunongwaye itishilo lwinyu.
PHI 1:26 Neli libhelete uluseshelo ugusi hulimwe mwa Yesu Kristi, oluseshelo lwinyu lubhahwonjelele, ane abhe pandwemo namwe.
PHI 1:27 Muhwanziwa ulwizyo lwenyu munjendo enyiza shalihwanza izulya Ngulubhi aje mubhalaje, bhombaji esho ili nkanayenza au nkasanayenza, ehonvwaje aje mwe meleye, muli numwoyo gumo na lwenyu izu nulweteshelo lwenyu pandwemo.
PHI 1:28 Musahagundushe ahawtu hohonti hahabhombwa na bhantu abhibhi bhenyu. Ezi mbonesya huje abhantu ebha bhananzi.
PHI 1:29 Lelo hulimwe mbowesyozye wokovu waufuma hwa Ngulubhi. Maana amwe mupewilwe kwa ajili ya Yesu se humwitishe wewe
PHI 1:30 lelo na malabhi hwa mwene. Maana mulinibho lilalila neshi lya mwalilolile huline nantele mwonvwezye hujebado endinalyo weshi.
PHI 2:1 Nkashile huheli apewe umwoyo nu Kristu. Nkashile luweli olusobhezyo lufuma mlugano lwakwe. Nkashile uhweli ulubhongano lwa Opepo.
PHI 2:2 Malelezi ulusovyo lwane mbhaje pandwemo mbhanje nulugano lumo, nkambha pandwemo opepo, nabhenembombo emo.
PHI 2:3 Ugaje owombe umwene nahwilole. Mubhanje bhahwiyisye nkawabhalola abhanje huje bhinza ashile awe.
PHI 2:4 Omtu aagje wenye amambo gakwe yuyo ayenyaje na aga bhanje.
PHI 2:5 Mubhaje numwoyo nashi Kristi u Yesu.
PHI 2:6 Umwene alisawa nu Ngolobhe sagahwibheshele huje sawa nu Ngolobhe hatu ahakhatane naho.
PHI 2:7 Lakini umwene abhiyisizye yuyo. Ahejile ubeleogwa hwitume ahwibhonesezye pamaso gabhantu. Abhoneshe mwanadamu.
PHI 2:8 Umwene abhiyisizye nashi ikwii abhale afye afye pashihobhehanyo.
PHI 2:9 Pepo Ungolobhe asukyezye haanu. Apiye itawa igosi ashile amatawa goti.
PHI 2:10 Abhombile goti hwitawa ilya Yesu kila lifugamo lifungamile. Amafugamo gabhantu abha humwanya na bhabhali pamwanya pansi na bhabhali bhilongo pasi.
PHI 2:11 Abhombile engo huje umele guyaje U Yesu Kilisti yugonsi nusisya owa Ngolobhe nu daada.
PHI 2:12 Hwahuje bhamwetu bhane nashisamhwina esinku zyosagahuje pewendi hata pendinomo bhombaji owaule wenyu mwemwe uwoga nayinganishe.
PHI 2:13 Hwahuje Ongolobhe abhomba embombo mhati yenyu abhapela amaha agabhombele imbombo gala gasongwa umwene.
PHI 2:14 Hwombaji embombo zyonti wala mgaje munjunishe wala abwazanye.
PHI 2:15 Hwombaji shesho huje mgajeligwe na mlibhana bha Ngolobhe. Usengerusu wasagali ni mbibhi bhombaji ego mubhanje lukhozwo pansi epapo eyamabhibhi na mabhibhi.
PHI 2:16 Khataji sana amazyi ega agewomi hujeembe wazo bhezewe isiku elya Kilisti embamanye huje sagananyilile wene saga na bhombile embombo wenu.
PHI 2:17 Mmenye huje bhantufya nashi esadaka pamwanya ye dhabihu nembombo eye lweteho esogwa naesogwele pandwemo namwe mwenti.
PHI 2:18 Pepapepa namwe msogwelwe natele msogwele pandwemo nane.
PHI 2:19 Ane itegemela hwa Gosi uYesu ehulanyizya hwa Timotheo hulimwi sheshi apepepe ewazahuje mpelee nane umwoyo nanaiaamanya amambo genyu.
PHI 2:20 Hwa huje sendinuwamwabho uwawenye nashi umwene walinilyoli sababu yenyu.
PHI 2:21 Abhanje bhonti bhanagaga embatume abhene bhahwanza embombo zyabho ezyavene wene, nasagazyahuje zya abhombe embombo eye Yesu Kilisti.
PHI 2:22 Hwa huje mmenye egharama zyakwe, nashu umwana walelwa nuishe wakwe papepo pahwombile embombo pandwemo nane alumbelele.
PHI 2:23 Hwahuje esobheye hutume halaka hulimwi ilikemanye henu habhafumile hulini.
PHI 2:24 Hwahuje endinuhakika hwitawa lya Gosi huje embahweze nene naihweza papapepe.
PHI 2:25 Endihwendala ewaziwa hugalusije hulimwi Epafradito. Umwene holo wane nantele bhomba mbombo tenti nane, naskari wamwetu umwene tumwa nantele puti wenyu kwajili ya vintu evyalini.
PHI 2:26 Alinowoga agene huje abhepandwemo namwe mweti hwahuje ahovyezye wamwabho huje bhinu.
PHI 2:27 Maana lyoli alibhinu shesho apululie afye. Lakini Ongolobhe asanjile ni pwana lyakwe hagali pamwanya yakwe. Umwene alipamwanya yane hwahuje ansibhe nahwisanje na hwisanje.
PHI 2:28 Hwa huje hehugalusya ninali amwenye lyaliwezeha na huje pamvahulele mwasogwe nana embave enefizye esebho.
PHI 2:29 Zobhelaji u Epafradito hwidal lya Gosi sogwanji huwiza woti muhwiyishaje hwa mtu nashioyo.
PHI 2:30 Hwa huje alimbombo ezya Kristi apalamiye aafye apululilye amaisha gakwe sababu yawamwabha avombele amambo asaga waile ahwombe mmbombo nashieyo numo wowoti wahwombile nashioyo hutali nane.
PHI 3:1 Sungwaji hwa Gosi. Sinzilola intamyo hubhasimbile habhili amazwi gegala amazwi iga gabhabhapele.
PHI 3:2 Muyogopaje ni mbwa. Muyogopaje na bhabhomba imbombo abhabhibhi. Muyogopaje na bhebhahuyitema amabhihi gabho.
PHI 3:3 Atwa tili tohara. atu tihumputa Ungulubhi hulwabhushilo lwa Yesu Kilisti. Yesetuli nu dandamazu mumbili.
PHI 3:4 Nkushele hwali nu muntu uwahunsubhile umbili uguani handi imbombile isho haani.
PHI 3:5 Lelo natahililwe isihu ilya nane napapilwe mshirokho. ishabhaizilaeli newishirokholo ishaBenjamini ne mweBulania uwa Bhaebrania. katika huzimalizye indajazyo izyaMusa nali Falisayo.
PHI 3:6 Hu nguvu zyani nalyimvizye Ikanisa. Ishibhanza aje tulitishe ilyoliyi sheria senahali ni lawama husheria.
PHI 3:7 Lelo katika amambo ganti gingalolile aje minza huline ni nahagabhazya aje takataka pipo nahamminye U Kristi.
PHI 3:8 Hu lyoli ihungabhazya amambo gonti aje hasara afumilane nu winza uwalumanye u Yesu Kristi Ugosi wani. Kwaajili yakwe indeshile amambo gonti ingabhazya ndeshe itakataka ili imwaje U Kristi
PHI 3:9 iloleshe muhati yakwe sindini lyoli iyani ninini. Afume musheria ila indinayo ilyoli yifumilana nulwitiho lwa Kristi lwelufuma hwa Ngulubhi, umwene msingi ugwa mlwitaho.
PHI 3:10 Ishi ihwanza humanye umwimi ni nguvu iyizyusye wakwe nu ushirika wi mayimba gakwe. Ihanza agalulanywe nu Kilisti hu shifwani shimfwa yakwe,
PHI 3:11 hwashi imbe nusubhilizyo muzyusyo wa bhafwe.
PHI 3:12 Selyoli aje ingapiite amambo iga au huje indi nugolosu hwigo, ila injitahidi apate shila sheshipatihana hwa Yesu Kristi.
PHI 3:13 Bhaholo bhani simanya aje impite tiyali amabo iga. Ila ibhomba ijambo lyeka ihwiwa mwisinda ihwenyezya mwilongolela.
PHI 3:14 Injitahidi afishile amalengo na makusudi ili impate ingiga ulukwizyo lwa Ngulubhi mwa Yesu Kristi.
PHI 3:15 Twenti twetikuliye ulokole tihwanziwa ahwanze ishi nkeshele umo abhasibhe hunamna tofauti ahusu ijambo lyolyonti ilya Ngulubhi nantele abhalyigule hulimwe.
PHI 3:16 Hata huyo umuda nkewafiha tibhale shinisho.
PHI 3:17 Bhaholo bhwa mumfwate ani mubhenye sana bhala bhebhajenda hudadavu webhuli ndeshe ati.
PHI 3:18 Bhinji bhebhakhala bhebhala mala nyinji imbabhuzya na ishi imbabhuzya humansozi - bhinji bhakhala ndeshe abhalugu abhikhobhehanyo isha Yesu Kilisti.
PHI 3:19 Humpelela hwabho nanjisu. Pipo Ungulubhi wabho vyanda, ni shiburi shabho nsoni zyabho. Bhasibhilila amambo agamusi.
PHI 3:20 Pe ukhalo witu bhuli humwanya hwe tuhunsubhila ummulokozi witu uYesu Kilisti.
PHI 3:21 Abhagalulanye amabili gitu amabhinu ndeshe amabili gakwe utuntumu; hwunguvu zizila huvizibiti ivintu vyonti.
PHI 4:1 Bhaya bhatikondenebhane, amwe nembagene, mshiyenetaji yane. Emeleli sawasawa Hwagosi, enyi bhamanyanibhembagena.
PHI 4:2 Ehubhozya Eudia, nantele ehubhozya awe Sintike, muwezye olwovwana olwinza kati yenyu. Afataneje amwe mwentibhabhele mwagenenogosi.
PHI 4:3 Nantele embabhozye nantele amwemwabhomba mbombo bhamwetu mbhavwe ebha abhashe afataneje bhatumishe pandwemo nane. Ayanje izu lya Gosi natili no Kelementi, pandwemo na atumwa abhamwabho abhagosi abhene, amatawagao gandiwhemshitabu eshewhomi.
PHI 4:4 Whangosi ensiku zyonti. nantele embayanje, olusongwo.
PHI 4:5 Ohogowenyu bhubhonehaja hwa bhantu bhonti Ogosi alipepe.
PHI 4:6 Ogande whianzye whijambo lyolyonti. Gamwhanza agenyu gabhonehanaje bha Ngolobhe.
PHI 4:7 Olweteho lwa Gosi, lwalulilugosi ashile enjele zyonti ebhazije amoyo nensebho zyenyu olwa lwa Kristi o Yesu.
PHI 4:8 Bhayu bhaholo bhane gasebhelelaji amambo gonti egelyoli, olwiho, ehaki, nowinza, uligano, nagala, aminza, gonti, galiminza, nagala, gagawanziwa, asalifye.
PHI 4:9 Gabhombelelaji embombo gala gamwamanjilaga gamwaposheyega mwahovwaganagalagamwa wetu oweminza abhabhenamwe.
PHI 4:10 Endinoluseshelo ogosi sana hulimwe na wagosi afwataneje amwe mbhonesezye eniya yahwihusizye hulimwe eyemahitaji gane. Lioli epoimande mwagene ansajile humaitajigane engawa semwayajile enafasi eyansaidile.
PHI 4:11 Seyanga eshoaje ehwipe ahantu wavilavye hwanzaane ehwimazizye ayeehaliyonti.
PHI 4:12 Emenye eshakhale nehali eyapongeshelwe naehali ya bhene vintu, humazingila gonti ega ane emanyie wakati owakute no wakatiowahweshe, yani vinji vyehwanziwa.
PHI 4:13 Embwezizye abhombe ega ahwaviliwe nomwene yampela enguvu.
PHI 4:14 Hata esho, mwabhombile shinza ashilikiane nane amalabhagane.
PHI 4:15 Amwe mwa Filipi mmenye aje ahwandilekwizu nehasogoye hu Makedonia, nalimo ikanisa lyalya navwizye humambo gagahusu apeli inaposhele, amwe mbhene.
PHI 4:16 Hata nehali hu thesolanike amwe mwantumie awavwohahinji humahitaji gane.
PHI 4:17 Seyangaje ehwanza evyewene eyanga aji enyinza zyazileta efaida hulimwe.
PHI 4:18 Eposheye evintu vyonti, neshi ememezewe ne vintu evyenje eviji. Emposheye evintu vyenyu afume wa Epafradito. Vintu vinza vyavinurishila shinza vyonti vihweteshelwa vyonti vye sadaka yehukhondela Ongolobhe.
PHI 4:19 Kwesho Ongolobhe wane abhabha memie gamuwanza agenyu utajiri wautuntumi wakwe O Yesu Kristi.
PHI 4:20 Eshi hwa Ngolobhe nahwa Baba wetu obhenotuntumowawilana wila. Amina.
PHI 4:21 Endamhozyau zifishile kila yaputa wa Kristi o Yesu aganwe bhendi nabho epa bhabhalamha.
PHI 4:22 Nantele bhabhaputa bhontiepa bhabhalamha. Hasabhala ebheshikholo sha Kaisari.
PHI 4:23 Neshi eneema eyagosi wetu O Yesu Kristi ebhene na moyo genyu.
COL 1:1 U Paulo umtume wa Kristi u Yesu, shahuanza Ungolowe nu Timoti uholowetu,
COL 1:2 hulweteho na huwaholo awagolosu hwa Kristi wawaleho Hukolosai. Uweene uwe humwenyu nu pumu, afume hwa Ngolowe Udaada weti.
COL 1:3 Tihusalipwa Ungolowe, Udaada weti wa Yesu UKristi, tihuwalawila hani hani.
COL 1:4 Tumvyenze ulweteho wamlinao hwa Yesu Ukristi nu lugano wamlinao hwa wantu wonti bhabhaguliwe awe hua Ngolowe.
COL 1:5 Mli nulugano walioli uweshelwe humwanya awe wenyu. Mwahomvyezye aje agole lioli, shalisele izwi ni injili,
COL 1:6 eyo inyezelehu mwenyu. Inzwi lipapa amadondo liwala musimonti liwomba mhanti yentu ahuande isiku liamuhahovyenzye na manyile lioli uwene wa Ngolobhe.
COL 1:7 Eli izwi lyammanyie afume hwa Epafra, uganwwe wetu, umuwomba mbombo uwamwentu, muomba mbombo ugolosu wa Kristi ubadra uwetu.
COL 1:8 U Epafra auwombile uonehane humwenti uugano wenyu Hwampepo.
COL 1:9 Huje ulugano ouu ahwandi isiku hatahahovyenzye sagatileshile huwaputile. Tilishatillawa aje mmeme injelee, ihekima yonti, injele yahupepo.
COL 1:10 Tilishatilawa aje mjendaje na jimbe hwa Bwana hwidala lilipendezye. Tilishatilawa aje mpape amadondo shila mbombo inyinza munzawe ni njele iya Ngolowe.
COL 1:11 Tilawa mposhele ingovu ni ngovu izyi tuntumu wakwe naje tijimbanje na jimbizanye tonti.
COL 1:12 Tilawa aje mshanje tisalipua huadaada yawawombile amwe muwe wakwe hulweteho uselu.
COL 1:13 Atikomboe afume huutawala wa nkhisi na hutusamizizye huumwene wa Mwana wakwe uganwe.
COL 1:14 Hwa Mwana wakwe tikombolilwe, tisanjililwe hu mbiwi.
COL 1:15 Umwana aliye yu Ngolowe yasagaawoneha, upapwe wahuande ya wumbe vyonti.
COL 1:16 Umwene ivitu vyonti vyahawombwilwe izyahumisanya, izyamunsi viviloleha, visagaviloleha. nkavya enzi, nkavya tawale vyangovu vyonti vyahawubwelwe nu mwene kwaajili yakwe.
COL 1:17 Umwene aleho wahuande kabla ya vyonti, umwene ivinti vyonti vihatene peka.
COL 1:18 Umwene litwe li pele yaani ishiwanza, umwene wahuande, papwe wahuande afume mwawafyeye. Huje alini nafasi ya huande mvintu vyonti.
COL 1:19 Huje Ungolobhe ahasongwelwe aje ufinyile wakwe wonti ukhala mhati yakwe,
COL 1:20 apatanishe ivintu vyonti hwidala lya Mwana wakwe. Ungolowe aahawombile upumu ashirile idanda lya mshikhomanyo wakwe. Ungolobhe ahapatanisizye wintu vyonti ivyakwe mwene. Nkha vintu vya munsi au ivintu vyahumwanya.
COL 1:21 Amwe nantele mwahali wajenu hwa Ngolobhe mwahali wawiwi wakwe hujele na humbombo imbiwi.
COL 1:22 Eshi awawonganyenye amwe hu bele wakwe ashilile afye. Ahawombile esho ili awalete amwe muwagolosu wasaga walinimbiwi wala intavu hwitangalila lyakwe,
COL 1:23 nkamuza jende mlweteshelo mkamilishe mlishinza msahasogole mdandamaje hunzwi. Hi ndiyo injili iliyotangazwa kwa kila mtu aliyeumbwa chini ya mbingu. Elino ane ni Paulo indi muwomba mbombo.
COL 1:24 Eshi ishiye lwipata amalawa kwa ajili yamwe. Nanee iwomba hubele gwane shishipungoha humatawa gane hwa Kristi hubele gwakwe, ishipanga.
COL 1:25 Ane nimuomba mbombo wishipanga husawasawa ni mbombo nyimpewilwe afume Hwangolowe hwaajili yamwe, amyemye izwi lya Ngolobhe.
COL 1:26 Ene ilioli siri ifisilwe amaha minchi huvizazi. Eshi saga siri hwa wonti wawali nu lweteshelo hwa mwene.
COL 1:27 Ungolowe awazile wala wahwanza huwawonesha utaajiri wa utuntumu wa siri ya ulioli mhanti yawantu munsi zyonti. Huje UKristi aleho mhati yenyu, udandamazu nu tuntumu uuhwenza.
COL 1:28 Uno yuyulatihutengemela Tihusunda kila muntu, tihumanyizya kila muntu injele yonti, ili tulete kila muntu huungolosu hwa Kristi.
COL 1:29 Ane ihujilavya na ikazana afuatane ni ngovu zyakwe zyaziwomba imbombo mhati yane nu ngovu.
COL 2:1 Dewaza huje mmanye sendi namayemba humbombo yenyu, wabhoti mwemli hu Laodikia na hwabhonti bhasaga bhandolile amaso gane hubele.
COL 2:2 Ebhomba embombo amoyo gabho huje bhatetelwe abhahwishe pandwemo mlugano nabhe mtabhala zoti nuwinji ugwa lyoli uwenjele, aimanye esili eya Ngolobhe oyo uKristi.
COL 2:3 Afumilane noyo enjele vifisilwe.
COL 2:4 Eyanga huje umtu wowonti agabhabhombela imbibhi hunogwa enzwabhopele.
COL 2:5 Hata sendinamwe pandwemo hubele, lakini endinamwe nupepo. Esogwelwe abhalole upanyihiho gwenyu gwizanidandi neulweteho lwenyu mwa Kristi.
COL 2:6 Nashi samposheye uKristi Ogosi, jendaji mwidala lyakwe.
COL 2:7 Mzengwe ashibile umwene, mzegwe numwene, mlwetebo nashi samwasundilwe, nakogwe husalifwo enyingi.
COL 2:8 Mwenyaje umutu wowoti asibhateje hunjele enogwa zyezili wene mganje hopelwe na lengane namaposhelo gabhantu, alengane na mambo gapansi nasagagalengana nu Kristi.
COL 2:9 Hwahuje ashilile umwene uwinza uwa Ngolobhe ghwope ahali mhati yebele.
COL 2:10 Namwe mmemile ashilile umwene. Umwene litwe wihone ashile agosi bhontii.
COL 2:11 Ashilile umwene mwatuliwe hutobala, sagaiwobwa na bhantu awepe mbele gwenyama ashilile tohala ya Kristi.
COL 2:12 Mwaselelwe pandwemo hudala lya hozewe hwidala lyeteho ashilile Ongolobhe wazwoshele afume hwabhafwe.
COL 2:13 Napafwiye ashilile embibhi zyenyu nasitetailiwe humabele genyu abhabheshele bhomi pandwemo natisajile embibhi zyetu zyoti.
COL 2:14 Atefwizye msebho ezya madeni zyahandihwe shenje nate ahefwizye goti nabhomele pa lukhobhehanyo.
COL 2:15 Ahefwizye idandi lyoti ilya gosi abheshele apazelu mgabheshe sikulukulu yeushindi hwidala likhobhehanyo lyakwe.
COL 2:16 Hwahuje umtu wowonti asibhalonje amwe kwaajili yeshalye au amwele, ebhe shelehe au umwezi upya au isiku lya tuye.
COL 2:17 Ega gati mazwogoni gembombo yeweza hwahuje goti ego Kilisti.
COL 2:18 Umuntu wowonti asifyulwe enjega yakwe agajezilishe ayishe au hala uzelu umutu nashioyo awenya embombo yailolile abhopelwe ne sebho zyakwe ezya mbele.
COL 2:19 Umwene sagakhatizya itwee. Hufume mwitwe nubele gwakwe namafupa akhatane nakhatanizye pandwemo akule na kulilo mwa Ngolobhe.
COL 2:20 Nkashile mwafwiye pandwemo nu Kilisti humadala gensi, mmbona mkhala nashi abhe nsii:
COL 2:21 “Mganje khaate wala antome wala msahapalamazye”?
COL 2:22 Goti ega galapiziwe huje uhwihwi uhweza na matumizi na maelekezo ne manyizyo izya bhantu.
COL 2:23 Indajizyo ezi nenjele nedini zyezilenganyiziwe ahwiyishe na mayemba agebele. Lakini goti usuugwo ezibele.
COL 3:1 Nkashele Ongolobhe abhavyosezye pandwemo no Kristi, ganzajiamambo gamwauya gashele o Kristi akhala hukhono gwakwe ogwahushilome wa Ngolobhe.
COL 3:2 Sebhaji amambo gagali amwanya gashelesegaoegenzi.
COL 3:3 Afwatanaje mfwinye naolukhalo lwenyu gafisilwe pandwemo no Kristi hwa Ngolobhe.
COL 3:4 O wakati o Kristi naibhoneha, afwateje lukhalo lwenyu, shashesho namwe nantele mwaibhonehana no mwene hutuntumu.
COL 3:5 Esho gafisi amambo gagalipansiyai omalaya, ochafu, azilishe shibhibhi, eniyaimbibhi, nanyonywe, eyo mputo oilenka.
COL 3:6 Afwataneje amambo ega ilyoyo elya Ngolobhe libhenza, whabhana bhashelesesebha whogopa.
COL 3:7 Afwataneje amambo ega amwe nantele mwajendilehwego nna mwakhalaga hwabhene.
COL 3:8 Eshi lazima mgefye amambo ega gonti yau. Ilyoyo, enkuni enia embibhi, indigo, nenongwa embibhi, gagafuma mwilomulyenyu.
COL 3:9 Msakhopelane mwewhamwe afatane mwabhue ubhuntu wenyu owehale ne mbombo yakwe.
COL 3:10 Mkwate ubhuntu opya, wahwubhombashipya nenjele afume no lengano whayola yabhomba.
COL 3:11 Hunjele ezi nomo Myunani, no Mmyuhadi atahiliwe nasinte tailiwe, obhazo nosagabhaza otumwa yasagali tumwa lelopesho oKristi yomambo gonti wagonti.
COL 3:12 Nkashele asalulwe bhangolobhe, abhoziwa naabhelwo vwano, hwikwattizi owhuntu owinza, epyana awhishe opole na ajimbe.
COL 3:13 Ejelanaji mwemwehwamwe. Sajilanaji shilamuntu nowamwabho, nkashele umntu alamiha whawamwabho asajileshashila, nashi ogosi sabhhasajie amwe.
COL 3:14 Ega amambo gonti, mganane eshoshenyezyo shegolosi.
COL 3:15 E amani eya Kristi ebhalongozye amoyo genyu. Ehalishe enashe olweteho eli huje mwakwiziwe hubelegumo mbhenolusalifo.
COL 3:16 Izu elya Kristi likhale mhatiyenyu hubhutajiri. Neshinshi yontii fundizanyaji na ajehane mwemwe namwe nahwembe, enyembo, ne nyembo zya humwoyo e, mbaji salifiaji amogogenyu wha Ngolobhe.
COL 3:17 Hahonti hambhomba whizu olwe whitawailya Gosi O Yesu, peliensalifyo Ongolobhe oBaba ashilile whamwene.
COL 3:18 Mbhashe ihaji hwalumebhenyu, nashisasungwa Ogosi.
COL 3:19 Amwebhalume bhagani abhashe bhenyu msabhebhakhali whabhene.
COL 3:20 Wana bhogopaji apaji bhenyu humambogoti, eshosasungwa Ogosi.
COL 3:21 Mwababa mgaje whandizye abahna bhenyu. bhasahilamwe.
COL 3:22 Fasontelezi bhogopi agosi bhenyu hubele na mambo gonti, saga huhuduma eyimasonashiabhantu. Nashi abhantu bhasombezye wene nahumoyo uwelwoli mwogopaji Ongolobhe.
COL 3:23 Hahonti hambhomba bhombaji afume mioyo genyu nashi Ogosi nate hwabhantu.
COL 3:24 Mmenyeaje mbhapate etunzo eyatabhale afumeusha Gosi yo Kristi Ogosi yamhuputa.
COL 3:25 Eshiwawhonti yabhomba gasheleseminza abhapate longwe hunjendo zya shelesenyinza gabhombele amnawhemele.
COL 4:1 Mwagosi, fumiwa sontezi enongwazyalizyali nenyiza. Mmenye aje mnawo ogosi humwanya.
COL 4:2 Mwendelele abhe lyoli huputo. Khali masa hwelyo nasombezye.
COL 4:3 Putuje pamo huaji yetu nantele, ena nantele Ongolobhi aigule alyango ogwizulyakwa, ayanji esili zwalyoli eya Kilisti. Hunongwa ene empinyilwe amanyolo.
COL 4:4 Ejiga mputaje endibheshe pawalele, nashi sehwaziwa ayaje.
COL 4:5 Bhalaga hunshinshi hwa bhala bhabhali ohohoze, abhalenalinali nesiku.
COL 4:6 Enangwa zyenyu zibhene wene esiku zyoti, nantele gakhole omwoni esiku zyoti, emmanye she hwanzwa ahugalule omtu.
COL 4:7 Hunongwazye zinazaane, O Tikiko adagabhombe gaga manyeshi hulimwi. Omwene holo mwe obhambombo umwinza no tumwi owa mwetu tenti hwa Gosi.
COL 4:8 Ehutu mahalli mwe hweli nkamumanye enongwa huliti ate nantele aje mmanye abhapele omwoyo.
COL 4:9 Ebatumabhoti na Onesimo, oholo wetu oganwe omwiza omo owenyu, bhazabhabhule kila mtu hahafule epa.
COL 4:10 Aristarko, opinye owamwetu, abhalamha, mweti no Maliko ovyala wakwa Barnaba yamwahambilile alongozi afume hwa mwene, “Nkashele aiyenza hulimwi mwambilili,”
COL 4:11 Nantele o Yesu yabhaiga Yusto bhabhene bha tahilwe bhabho mbambombo bhamwetu hwa mwene wa Ngolobhi. Bhali luzizyo hulini.
COL 4:12 Epafra abhalamuha. Omwene alipaka nate nantele tumwiwa Kilisti Yesu. Omwene abhomba nali nali huputo nantele nkawezye ahwemelele shishiza ahakikizye owiza ashelele amiza gote aga Ngolobhi.
COL 4:13 Hwahuje ejelezyezye, aeje abhomba embombo nalinli hwajili yenyu hwabhala bhabhali hula Laodekia, na hwebho bhabhali Hierapoli.
COL 4:14 Luku ola oganga ya genwe nu Dema bhabhalamuha.
COL 4:15 Bhabhalamuha aholo bhane bhabhaahwo Laodekia, na Nimfa, neshi bhiza shila sha shili ohwo munyumba yakwe.
COL 4:16 Ikalata eli palyaibha limanyelye mwebho namwe emanyilwe hwi bhaza elya Laodekia.
COL 4:17 Yaga hawa Arkipo, “enya ala mbambo ela yamwa hambile ashelelee Wagosi aje onwaziwa amalezye.”
COL 4:18 Idamuhoene eu hu makhono gane nene - Paulo. Gakomboshi amanyolo gane. Owene ubhenamwe.
1TH 1:1 Paulo, Silwano nu Timotheo wishivanza lya Tethesalonike pipo ungulubhe uDada nu Gosi u Yesu U Kilisti. Wene nu waushe bhumwe.
1TH 1:2 Tufumwa ulumbizyo wangulubhe habhili aje yinyu mwinti palatuntabula hunyibutozyituu.
1TH 1:3 Tubhabuha witagalila lya Ngulubhi nu Dada witagalila lya yinyuuu yitwiha, ubhovi lyi lungano, unkumbelezyo wuli nuda damazu uwami wapamandii uliwadada uYesu Kilisti.
1TH 1:4 Mwamituu mwaganilye nu Ngulubhi, timanyile akugwe winyuu.
1TH 1:5 Ni ishi izyo lyituu shalyaheza hulitii sigawino ngwatuu, wikhone nupepo usangalusu. Lelo wiisho ishawahenza mmenye atii twali bholii muhatiye yinyuu lihabha lyalimwi.
1TH 1:6 Mwalibhantu wejeshele atii nungosi, nishi pamwoshile izyo namaimba nubhosu uufuma upepo usangalusu.
1TH 1:7 Agabhoneha mwabhashimanyilo wautii Makedonia Akaiya ibhawitishe.
1TH 1:8 Pipo izyo lya Ngulubhi lyenilemwutii sana wa Mekadonia na Akaiya bhene. Nantele yititiolyi nyulwa Ngulubhi humanyishe woti. Efumeiepo hatuwanza Eyanjehahonti.
1TH 1:9 Phepovhio awene bhatazwa uvhoneshelo witu wali bhulili namwe, bhayangasha mwagalushila Ungulubhi afume humazimu na bhombele Ungulubhi umwumwanalyoli.
1TH 1:10 Bhafumizye inongwa aje mugula umwana wakwe humanya, yazyuzyusiwe afumehuzimuu. Yunanu yu Yesu yatubhiha bhaushe afumee wilyoyo lyalayinza.
1TH 2:1 Amwe bhayaa, mmenye mwemwe huje ate natahenzele hulimwe setahenzele wene.
1TH 2:2 Mmenye huje ulwahwande talabhile tee nantele bhatibhombeye embibhi enzyensoni hula hufilipi, amwe mumenye. Lelo tahwikazile hwa Ngulubhi ayanje ibangili lyakwe pamoja na mayemba aminji.
1TH 2:3 Ate ensundozye tu sezyafumene nembibhi, wala muntavu wala mumwoyo ubhibhi.
1TH 2:4 Ate neshi ateteshe Ungulubhi na hweteshelwe mwibhangii enzyo zyatiyanga. Tiyanga siyo huje tibhasungwezyaje abantu, tihusongwezya Ungulubhi. Ungulubhi mwene yasepa amoyo getu.
1TH 2:5 Ate setayanjile enongwa enzyahwillesye hulimwene, Neshi shamumenye, wala ate setatumiye ewongwa ezyensinjizizyo zye nziliho, Ungulubhi keti wetu ate setahanzalaga utuntumu hwa bhantu,
1TH 2:6 Wala afume hulimwe au hwabhantu abhanje. Handatibhajiedai apendelelwe huje ate tilibhatumwe bha Yesu.
1TH 2:7 Lelo talibhahogowe hulimwe nensi umaye shazinzya abhana bhakwe yuyo.
1TH 2:8 Hu namna ewe tali niganwe hulimwe, ati tali tayari abhashikisye siyohuje ibangili lya Ngulubhe lyene lelo na maisha getu tete kwasababu mulibha mwetu.
1TH 2:9 Amwe bhaholo muhwizuha embombo na mayemba getu. Na tabombaga embombo nu siku na pasanya aje tusahagwe melele umuntu yayonti. Uwakati uwo, tabhalumbelye ibhangililya Ngulubhe.
1TH 2:10 Amwe mulibhaketi bha Ngulubhi, Nufinjile nantele bila ya fujinjile nantele bilaa ya muntu atilulumwe, takakhile shinza namwe mwamumweteshe uYesu.
1TH 2:11 Shesho huje mumenye aje shiliwele shila muntu umoumo, neshi ubaba shalihina bhana bhakwe tabhapelie umwoyo na bhasubhizye na hwilolele.
1TH 2:12 Aje mwahanziwaga ajendelele weshi ulukwizyo lwenyu hwa Ngulubhi yabhakwizizye huumwene nu tuntumu wakwe.
1TH 2:13 Kwa sababu tihusalifya Ungulubhi shila wakati neshi shamwahejeleye afume hulite enongwa zya Ngulubhi mwazyejeleye siyohuje nongwa zya bantu. Mwazyejeleye huje nongwa zya bhomba embombo hulimwe mwamulyeteshe.
1TH 2:14 Eshiamwe bhaholo, mubhebhantu bhafuatizye amakanisa ga Ngulubhe gagali hwa Bhayahudi mwa Yesu Kilisti. Maana namwe mwayembele humambo kagaala afumehwa bhantu bhenyu, neshi gagali fume hwa Bhayahudi.
1TH 2:15 Bhaali Bhayahudi bhabhaagojile uYesu pandwemo na aakuwe, Bhayahudi bhabhaatibhenjele tifume hwonzesebhahusungwezya Ungulubhe nantele bhabhibhi hwa bhantu bonti.
1TH 2:16 Bhatizijiye huje tisahaya nje na bhantu bhasiga Bhayahudi, aje bhope bhaposhele uwokovu. Afume epo abhantu bhahwendelela ne mbibhi zyao, mpaka amakhome gabhenzela.
1TH 2:17 Ate bhaholo, talehene namwe hashe shebele, siga talehene shiputi. Taabhombile hunguvu zyetu nahunziliho engosi, abhalole amaso genyu.
1TH 2:18 Pepo tahanzaga ahwenze hulimwe, aneene Paulo, nahanzaga ahwenze lumo nu lwa mwao, lelo usetano anzigiiye.
1TH 2:19 Ahwilole hwetu pamande hwaibha yeenu au nuluse shelo, au fwalo gwataivunila hwa gosi uwetu uYesu naayenza? Eshi semwemwe neshi shabhali abhaje?
1TH 2:20 Hwa huje amwemulituntuntu wetu nuluseshelo lwetu.
1TH 3:1 Natalije, setiweza ajimbe haui tasebheleje whalishinza asagale hula waasene tibhene.
1TH 3:2 Tatumile oTimotheo, oholowetu obhomba mbombo wangolobhe widalailyeizu lya Kiristi, abhapelu. Enguvu na bhapomezye, afwatawe nolweteholwetu.
1TH 3:3 Twabhombile ega afataneje asahabhe yayonti, owayete afatawaje, amayemba ega aje mwemwe mmenye aje tisaluliwe whelii.
1TH 3:4 Lyoli natalinatali pandemo namwe tatalile bhabhozye, ajetalipepe apate, amayemba Ego yafumiele nashisammanya.
1TH 3:5 Nautele nehalije sembwezizye ajimbe, ehatumile nkemanyeaje olweteho lwenyuiaje abhajelile nahwashi. Abhajelile nembombo yetu yabhawene.
1TH 3:6 Lelo o Timotheo ahenzele hule afume hulimwe, atiletela enongwa enyinga. Enzyewomi noluganano lwenyu, atibholeleje, mlinekombosyo. Enyiza enzyetu, naje mgeneandole nashi ate, nate tizilishe abhalole amwe.
1TH 3:7 Afatane esho bhaholo tawisobhezye tee, namwe afwatawaje olweteho lwenyu, netabu namayemba getugonti.
1TH 3:8 Wheshi tihwizya nkashelemwemelee shinzawagosi,
1TH 3:9 Eshi tisombezye nsombeshi tipele, Ongolobhe hulimwe huluseshello lwonti hatilinaho: witagalila lyangolobhe pamwanya yenyu?
1TH 3:10 Tibhalabha sana osiku napasanya aje tiwezye agolole amasogenyu nabhonjezye hahatapuohe hulweteho lwenyo.
1TH 3:11 Ongolobhe wetu no Baba oMwanesho, nogosi wetu oYesu atilongozye idala lyetu lyonti. tifishehulimwe.
1TH 3:12 Ongolobhe abhabheshe mwonjelele nameme hulugano nkamganana nabhagane abantu bhonti nashisatibhabhombela amwe.
1TH 3:13 Naabhombe eshi agapele eguvu amoyogetu gashanombuno uwinza witagalila lya Ngolobhe wetu nashi nayensaogosi wetu oYesu pandwemo na nagolosu bhakwe bhonti.
1TH 4:1 Waholo tihuwapela umoyo tihuwalawa hwa Yesu uKilisti. Shila shatiyenje mposheye afume hulite shihwanziwa ajende, husaye Ungolobhe, idala elioliamuwalaje hani.
1TH 4:2 Mumenye ziatiwawozezie ashilile hwa Yesu aje zyenu.
1TH 4:3 Ego miza hwa Ngolobhe: Huyozye ahane izinaa,
1TH 4:4 Wekaweka amenye akhale nushi wakwe mwene huumoyo uzelu ni shishi.
1TH 4:5 Usahawe nushii wanyonywe nubele (nazi awatu wamusi wasaga wamwenye Ungolobhe).
1TH 4:6 Asahawe umuntu wowonti yanzafyemele impaho ziahukosele uholo wakwe, nunongwa ene. U Bwana yuyo asomba isiasa shonti na huwawozye.
1TH 4:7 Ungolobhe sagaahatukwizizie aje tiwe ni ntavu. Ahatikwizizye tiwe numoyo uzelu.
1TH 4:8 Eshi yakhanasangakhana watu ahukhana yu Ngolobhe, yahupela Umpepo Ufinjile wakwe.
1TH 4:9 Hunongwa zya ulugomo waholo waho sagaihusimbila awaamanyizizye Ungolobhe agan'ane tete kwa tete.
1TH 4:10 Imenye mwahawombile egagonti hwawaholo wawaleho hu Makedonia wonti, Eshi tihuwalawa muwaholo muombe shinza hani.
1TH 4:11 Tihuwalawa mnyonywaje akhale musi nupumu humbombozyenyu, na wombeji imbombo hunyowe zyenyu, nazishatiwalajizizye.
1TH 4:12 Wombaga ega nkujendaje sheinza ni shishi hwawantu wawalihonze wi lweteho, usahagaye liolionti lila.
1TH 4:13 Sagatihuanza amwe aje msahamanye muwaholo aje ewowagonilegona msahazugumile lihwenza.
1TH 4:14 Nkatihweteha aje u Yesu ahafyiye nantele ahazyoshele, Ungolobhe aiwatwala peka nu Yesu wawagonile hwitawa liakwe.
1TH 4:15 Tihuwawozya amwe hwizwi ilya Bwana aje tiwatutiliwomi lwahaiyenza u Bwana sagatahaiwatangalila wala wagonile ufwe. U Bwana yoyo ahaihwiha afume humwanya. Ahaiyeza peka ni palapanda ya Ngolobhe, wawafwinye hwitawa lya Yesu wahaizyoha.
1TH 4:16 U Bwana yoyo ahaihwiha afume humwanya. Ahaiyeza peka nuhala uzelu ugosi peka ni palapanda ya Ngolobhe, wawafwinye hwitawa lya Yesu wahaizyoha.
1TH 4:17 Awomi wawasageye wahaisangana humawengo peka wahainyanyela u Bwana humwana tahaiwa nu Bwana isiku zyonti.
1TH 4:18 Myanganaje amazwi ega Mwe, mwe, mwe.
1TH 5:1 Sheshi entumi esalezi nezi hale, bholo hagamne haja eyabhandishile abhantu hohoti amwenyu.
1TH 5:2 Hwahuje mwemwe mmenye ahwenza ongonsi nashi omwibha nusiku.
1TH 5:3 Pala pavayinga apinza na pinza pagahwenza amabhibhi gabhenzela nanali, nashi guhumwenzela omaye wali ni vyanda abhantu sagabhaipona hwidala lyolyoti.
1TH 5:4 Lelo bhaholobhane sagamlimnginsi hatalyenze insiku nashi ahweenza umwibha.
1TH 5:5 Hwa huje amwe mwenti mli bhana bhasihozwo nantele mlibhana bhapasanya nantele sagatili bhana bha musiku wala mnginsi.
1TH 5:6 Eesho tinganje gonele nashi wamo sabha gonera tibhanje masho nantele bhasovu.
1TH 5:7 Hwahuje bhabha gona bhagona nusiku bhabah kholwa bhakholwa nusiku.
1TH 5:8 Hwahuje ate tili bhana bha pasanya nateletibhe maaso, tikwate nkwela nulweteho nu lugano, nenkofilwa iyenjela agatibhiha pinza ahwaushe hunsiku zyezihweza.
1TH 5:9 Hwahuje Ungolobhe sagatisaluye huwandilo hujeali nenkuniii, hwahuje tipete ahwaushe hwidalaelwa goosi uYesu U Kilisti.
1TH 5:10 Yuyo atifweleye huje nkatibhe masoo au tigonele talhala padwemo enawoo.
1TH 5:11 Hwahuje yanganaji nazenganaji mwemwe hwa mwemwe nashi sambhomba.
1TH 5:12 Holowane tibhalabha mubhamanye bhala bhabha twumwa mhati yenyu bhabhali pamwanya yenyu huijo ogosi, nabhala abha pansi bhabha sunda.
1TH 5:13 Tibhalabha nantele mubhamanye nabhapele usalifyo mulubhongano lwenyu mwemwe.
1TH 5:14 Tabhalajizya bhaholo mubhasunde bhala bhasaga bhabhala wolowolo bhapeli umwoyo bhabha hwizirile bhavwanji apena mntukumile hwawontie.
1TH 5:15 Enyaji asahabhe omuntu wawonti yasovya amabhibhi hwamabhibhi hwamntu yoyonti hwahuje bhombaji gagali minza hwamntu omo omo na bhonti.
1TH 5:16 Sogwanyi ensiiku zyonti.
1TH 5:17 Puntaji ensiku zyonti.
1TH 5:18 Salifyaji Ongolobhe hwahantu hohonte hwahuje gonti lugano lwa Ngolobhe huliwi nu Yesu U Kilisti.
1TH 5:19 Msahazimwe opepo.
1TH 5:20 Mganje hunshente onkohwa.
1TH 5:21 Lenganji amambo gonti mkhataje elinza.
1TH 5:22 Mwepeshe hubhoneshelo owaubhibhi.
1TH 5:23 Ongolobhe owalutengano abhashimizye huwogolosu opepo omwoyo vibhahwe bila sebho ahwiize hwakwe ogosi wetu uYesu Kilisti.
1TH 5:24 Ola wabhakwizizye mwaminifu wope abhomba.
1TH 5:25 Bhaholo tipuntilaji tenti.
1TH 5:26 Bhalamhanji aholo bhonti nayailane ouzelu.
1TH 5:27 Embabhola hwitawa lya gonsi huje ikalata eeli limanyilwe hwa holo bhoti.
1TH 5:28 Ewenee iya gonsi wetu U Yesu Kilisti abhe nate ntenti.
2TH 1:1 U Paulo nu Silwano, nu Timotheo, shibhanza mwa Ngolobhe nudada wetu nu gosi uYesu Kilisti.
2TH 1:2 Uwene ubhe hulimwi nurutengano afume hwa Ngolobhe udada uwetu nugosi uYesu UKristi.
2TH 1:3 Ihwanziwa husalifye Ongolobhe ensikuzyoti hulimwi bhaholo. Eshisashi hwaziwa hwahuje mkula mlugano lwenyu hwa wowoti mwonjelelaje owinji.
2TH 1:4 Ntente tiyanga ahwilole mmabhanza ga Ngolobhe. tiyanga entumi eyewene yamlinayo eyemayemba gonti tiyanga enongwa enzya mayemba gamvumilila.
2TH 1:5 Evi vifyani efya logwe nalyoli nu Ngolobhe ashilile ega mbhaziwa ahwinjile bhuumwene waNgolobhe husababu yamwene mpate amayemba
2TH 1:6 Hwahuje halali alipwe nu Ngolobhe abhapele amayemba bhala bhabhaye vya amwe,
2TH 1:7 nabhapele asogwe amwe mwemyemba pandwemo namwe aibhomba ega paibhoneha Ogosi uYesu paifuma amwanya pandweemo nuhala uzelu neguvu zyake.
2TH 1:8 Mhanti yaluhozwo abhabha sombe ashisasi bhala bhabhasaga bha mwenye Ongolobhe nabhala bhabha sagahozya iizuu ilya Gosi wetu U Yesu.
2TH 1:9 Bhaipata amayemba nabudwe wilawila bhezabhe hutalii nugosu otuntumu ni ndandi lyakwe.
2TH 1:10 Aivomba ensiku lyaihwinza ayemeshelwa navantuvakwe vwaisagogwawoti bhabhaposheye. Nulusimisizyo lwake lwamanyishe hulimwi.
2TH 1:11 Hwahuje tibhaputila ensiku zwoti tilabha huje Ngolohe wetu bhabhaziwe huje bhamanyene akwiziwe. Tilabha huje ubhombe ahantu ahinza nambombo iyewene nenguvu.
2TH 1:12 Tibhalabha huje lyemehwaje itawa lya Gosi u Yesu tilabha huje ayemewaye umwene mwenee Ongolobhe nu Gosi U Yesu Kilisti.
2TH 2:1 Eshi ahunze hwa Yesu uBwana wetu U Yesu UKiristi awunganya, tikhale peka numwene: tihuwalavya amwe muwaholo wetu,
2TH 2:2 aje msahatamiwe nantele msahayaziwe nalinali hu Mpepo au hunongwa, hukalata, yilolehana aje isiku ilia Bwana tayari lyezeli.
2TH 2:3 Umntu asahahopela hwidala lyolyonti sagalihueza lila lyagwe umuntu wimbiwilifumile shoti awoneshe, uola umwana wi mbiwi.
2TH 2:4 Uno yuyola azinjila nantele ahuilola hahonti hahaputwa. Hahafumila epo, akhala mshiwamnza isha Ngolobhe ahuilolesya umwene awanji yu Ngolobhe.
2TH 2:5 Mwe, saga mkumbuha aje lwanahali namwe nahawawozyezye humambo eegaa?
2TH 2:6 Eshi mmenye shishi huzuwila aje aoneshe isiku ziakwe lwaliafia.
2TH 2:7 Isiri yula umuntu wimbiwi awomba imbombo eshu, aleho yazijila eshi mpakalwa haiepa mwidala.
2TH 2:8 Oula umiwi lwahaiwa pazelu ubwana Yesu ahaibuda nu moyela wilomu lyakwe. UBwana ahaimwomba awe saga hantu hohoti nufunuo wahuenza hwakwe.
2TH 2:9 Ahunzeala umiwi ihaiwa mbombo ya shetani hungovu zyonti, ishiwonesho, na amawonesho gilenkha,
2TH 2:10 ilenka lyonti liwalangani amambo eego gahaiwa hwa wala wawate ujile, huje sangawaposheye ulugano wa liolioli sangawakombolelwe ewo.
2TH 2:11 Shesho Ungolobhe ahuwapela imbombo yili ni mbiwi aje weteshe ilenka.
2TH 2:12 Haha fumila epo huje wahailongwa, wala wasagateshe lioli awene wahasongwezye uwalangani.
2TH 2:13 Eshi ihuaziwa husalipye Ungolobhe hani amwe muwaholo mganilwe nu Bwana. Huje uBwaan ahawasaluye amwe muwe wahuande akombolewe kwa uwoziwa wa Umpepo nulweteho wa lioli.
2TH 2:14 Eli lyanahawa hakwizizye amwe ashirile izwi muwajie akawe utundumu wa Bwana Yesu UKristi.
2TH 2:15 Mwe wahalo, emelelaji shinza umanyaji ulautamaduni mmanyiziwe hwizwi ni karata zyetu.
2TH 2:16 Eshi, U Bwana witu U Yesu UKristu yeyo mwene nu Nngolobhe, udaada wetu yatuganile na hutipele uwila nudandamazu uwinza uwakhale uuhuenza ashilile wene,
2TH 2:17 awasowelezye na gombe amoyo genyu, ashilile inzuri ni mbombo inyinza.
2TH 3:1 Iishi bhiholo tulabhilaji huje ezyo lya dada liwezye abhale wonti nabhwimishilye shalishili payoo hulimwi.
2TH 3:2 Labhaji aje tukomboshe afume humbivyi nabhantu ambambivyi wahuje sagabhunti abha ulyeteho.
2TH 3:3 Lelo uGosi ahwitishilya, wayisisimizya amwa nagulila afume mwola ubhivyi.
2TH 3:4 Tulinguvhu nuGosi ulemwe aje abhomba mwayendela abhombe antele mwayendelela abhombe egatubhalajizya.
2TH 3:5 Ugosi awezye alongozye amoyo ginyuu mlugano wijivyi ubhuu waKilisti.
2TH 3:6 Eshitubhalajizya, bhiholo mmuli tawalyakwe uBwana Yesu Kilisti, huje mmwepushe ula uholo ula akhala maisha igiwolo sagiisho gagafumina nahapango hasa mwa poshile hulintee.
2TH 3:7 Phipo amwi mminye huje mwigajegatubho mbaanti. Hagatakhalaga pokanamwe nishibhala bhasabhanishoga.
2TH 3:8 Hagatalyanga ahatolu hammuntu yayunti hagatasombelega afumeepo twabhombaga embombo usiku na pasanya humbo hummwile lishile umuntu amwe.
2TH 3:9 Twabhomba esho hagahuje satani lyawamle twabhomba esho ili tubheshineshe luhulimwi mutudaje ati.
2TH 3:10 Lwatwali pamopenena mwitwabhalajizye, “Khashele umuntu ayasabhomba embombo angandeelye.”
2TH 3:11 Muhati umuo tuhuvhwa ajee bhamoo wawilibha bhalinuwolo pomlisho amwe habhabhomba embombo wantu mbatiho.
2TH 3:12 Ishi bho tuvhalajizya nasamizye Bwana Yesu Kristu, ilazimihahuje ulamtu abhombaje imbombo na pummemyee na lye shalye shao vhivhoo.
2TH 3:13 Lelo amwi, bhiholo, mungande azilishe amoyo abhombe ganalyoli.
2TH 3:14 Khashele mutu yayunti hagawanza ehuvye izyo lwitu umu mkalata ene. Muvhe maso nawo mugande sangane nabhi ili akenye.
2TH 3:15 Muganda humwejele ajelugu lelo msundaje nishi hwiholo.
2TH 3:16 Ugosi uluvyano nyunyo apele lubhano pahati amadala gunti Ugosi avhe na mwe mwenthi.
2TH 3:17 Ululamuho lwani ni Paulo hukhono gwani nene, ambashoshimanyilo hukalata ishi simba.
2TH 3:18 Mwoyi ngwadada wetu U Yesu Ukristi iwezye abhenamwe mwindei.
1TI 1:1 U Paulo, Utumwa wa Yesu Kristi, alengane ne ndajizyo zya Ngolobhe watokoye ate O Yesu Kristi wali jasili wetu,
1TI 1:2 hwa Timotheo omwana wane welyoli hulweteshelo lwa lufuma hwa Ngolobhe o Baba no Kristi oYesu obhwa wetu.
1TI 1:3 Nashi sanabhozyezye nanasogolaga abhale hu Makedonia, osagala hu Efeso ili aje owezye abhabhozye abhantu aje waganjefundizye enongwa ezyenje.
1TI 1:4 Nantele bhaganje tejezye enongwa zye vilale ne ozoza zye shikholo zya sezili no mwisho. Ezyo zileta amabisanyo ashile awavwe ahwengwa Ngolobhe gwe lweteshelo.
1TI 1:5 Ilengo lye ndajizyo ezyo luganano lwalufuma humoyo aminza humwoyo ogwinza na hulweteshelo lwe lyoli.
1TI 1:6 Abhantu wamo wakosile shashahanziwaga bhazileshile endijizyo ezi bhagulishiye enongwa zyabho endema ndema.
1TI 1:7 Bhawanza aje bhabhanje waalimu bhe ndajizyo, lelo sebhawelewa habhayanga au habhasimisizya.
1TI 1:8 ila tihwelewa aje endajizyo nyinza hwa muntu waizufumila sawasawa.
1TI 1:9 Tehwelewa aje, endajizyo sezya bhehwelwe kwa ajili ya muntu we lyoli ila hwa bhala bhabhana na nkanye endajizyo na bhe mbibhi, abhantu bhasebhaputi abhe mbibhi, nabhasebhali no Ngolobhe nabhe mbibhi. Etungwilwe hwebho bhabhahudu ababa na maye bhabho, hwebho agoji,
1TI 1:10 kwa ajili yamalaya nebho awantu azinzi, nebho bhabhateka awantu nabhabhombe watumwa, sebabu yilenka, na shahidi bhilenka, na bhonti na bhonti bhabhali shingunga ne nongwa yenpiana.
1TI 1:11 Enongwa ezi zifumilana izu lye umwamu wa Ngolobhe welusayo na ambayo hweyo bhaniminile.
1TI 1:12 Ehusalifya o Yesu Kristi Ogosi wetu. Ampiye enguvu abazizye ane aje endi mwaminifu, na wambeha pambombo yanewe.
1TI 1:13 Nali muntu wemasola, watese na we wibho. Lakini ansajiye afuatanaje na bhombile bila amanye siyo senaputaga.
1TI 1:14 Eneema ya Ngolobhe wetu imemile lwetweshelo no lwomvwano wawuli hwa Kristi oYesu.
1TI 1:15 Enongwa ezi zya hwetehwe na ahwanziwa aposhelewe nabhantu whonti, aje Okristi oYesu ahenzele munsi ahwokole bhe mbibhi. Ane endi bhibhi ashile wonti.
1TI 1:16 Lakini ane napewilwe ehuluma aje mhati yane ane, awande gonti, oKristi oYesu awonesezye ou vumilivu wonti. Abhombile esho nanshi omfano gwa wonti bhabhai humweteshela omwene ashilile owomi wewilawila.
1TI 1:17 Na esalezi omwene wasagali no umwisho, wasaga afwa, wasabhoneha, Ongolobhe mwene, ebhe heshima no umwamu wewilawila. Amina.
1TI 1:18 Eweha endajizyo eli witazi lyaho Timotheo, mwana wane. Ewomba eshi alengane no kuwaa wawahepere epa kwanza elengane nawe aje obhe nawe muvitu evinza.
1TI 1:19 Obhombe esho ili nkobhe no lweteshelo no mwoyo ogwinza bhamo bhamo wakhene ega walutezya ulweteshero.
1TI 1:20 Nashi shila ohemenayo no o Alekizanda ambao upiye o setano aje awafundizye bhaswilije.
1TI 2:1 Hubhe emade gonti, ehwanza eputo ne shiputo na putilwe na salifwe hwa bhantu bhoti,
1TI 2:2 huje amwene bhoti bhabhali muu gosi aje timanye adele husiku enyinza abhatauwa bhoti abhe shishi.
1TI 2:3 Eli linza nantele lihwete wa hwi tagalila hwa Ngolobhe ofwozi wetu.
1TI 2:4 Omwe ansongwa aje abhantu bhonti bhafwolwe nantele bhaimanye elyoli.
1TI 2:5 Hwa huje ahweli Ongolobhe omo, nantele ali okhomanyi omo owa Ngolobhe na bhantu yali Kilisti oYesu.
1TI 2:6 Ahwifumize mwene afidiye hwa bhonti, gagalolile hunsiku zyezibhalile.
1TI 2:7 Nantele ane nemwene eha bhombile abhe jube eyangalyoli sagaeyanga ilenga. Ane edi manyizi hwa bhantu bhasebha puta hunyinza zyalwoli.
1TI 2:8 Nantele uhwanza alume papoti bhapute na bhosye amakhono amiza bila avitwe nasanje.
1TI 2:9 Shesho nantele abhashe bhahwikwatizye amendega gahwetewa hushishi nahizije. Bhaganje bhene nsisi zyazitawilwa ne zahabu, ne Lulu, na menda agehele engosi.
1TI 2:10 Nantele ejigabhakwale amenda gaga hwanziwa abhashe bhabhahwete oputi ashelele embobo enyiza.
1TI 2:11 Oshi ahwimanzye abhe shibhatama nantele neshishi yoti.
1TI 2:12 Ogaje huluhusu oshe amanzye nantele abhe gosi pamwanya palume nante akhalemye.
1TI 2:13 Nantele oHadamu abhombwelwe ahwade nantele oEva.
1TI 2:14 O Hadamu sagakhopelelwe lelo she akhopelelwe tee nashi abagulwe.
1TI 2:15 Hata eshi afwolwashilole apape abhana nkashelebhai yedelela ashilele owinza no lugano na lwozwo nenjele enyinza.
1TI 3:1 Enjango ewe ehwaminiha: nkashele umuntu asongwa abhe Mwemelezi, ahwanza embombo enyinza.
1TI 3:2 Omwemelezi lazima asabhe ne mbuno. Lazima abhe lume owasheomo nautele abhene kiasi, epyana, yali no utalatibu, opezi. Lazima abhe no uwezo owafundizye.
1TI 3:3 Agajebhe wamwele evikali, asibhe wibho, abhe hogowe, abhe no lungano. Lazima asabhe wagane ehela.
1TI 3:4 Ebhanziwaje abhemelelaje shinza abhantu abhakhaya yakwe, na bhana bhakwe, ehwanziwaaje bhogopaje no lwiho lwunti.
1TI 3:5 Nkashele omntu samenye abhemelele abhantu bhakhaya yakwe yoyo, abhasonjewole ikaisa elya ikanisa elya Ngolobhe?
1TI 3:6 Asabhe puti opya, asahenzeaga hwiyaula nagwe naibongwe nashi obhibhi.
1TI 3:7 Lazima ne njendo enyinza wabhala bhonti bhabhali hwonze, asahenze agagwa akenye no tego ogwa bhibhi.
1TI 3:8 Ashemansi shesho, ehwanziwa aje bhabhe ajimbe nehema, bhasabhene nijango embibhi. Bhasamwele evikhali ashile ekawaida olwenje abhenetama.
1TI 3:9 Abhewawute humwoyo uginza gula ogwe lyali ne imani yehifhinguliwe.
1TI 3:10 Bhabhe bhenyezewe nasoti, alafu bhafunzizye afwatane sebhali ne mbumo.
1TI 3:11 Abhashe shesho bhabhe no lwiho. Bhasahabhe bhasinjizi. Bhabhe hashe no waminifu hu mambo gonti.
1TI 3:12 Ashemansi bhabhe bhalume ebhebhashe omo omo. Lazima bhabhemelelaje abhana bhabhowekhaya ziabho.
1TI 3:13 Bhala bhabha bhombashinza bhapata olwemelelo olwinza nodandamu ogosi, hiyimani yeli hwa Kristi oYesu.
1TI 3:14 Ehandishe amambo ega hulimwe enzahwenze hulimwe sheshi karibu.
1TI 3:15 Nkashe nolobhela, esimba omanye eshabhale hunyumba ya Ngolobhe, yashelelili likanisa lya Ngolobhe, yali mwomi owemelelo nwelioli.
1TI 3:16 Nasagahakhanwa aje lyoli eyebhuNgolobhe wawiguliwe ognsi: “Abhoneshe hubele, wazibitizya neRoho, wabhoneha wantumi, watangaziwa mwamwabho abhensi, bhasongwa ensiyonti, bhamwega amwanya hutukufu.”
1TI 4:1 Eshi Opepo ayanga pazeluzelu huje ehale zihweza bhamo bhaileha apinza nabhe maso atejeze opepo ezilenka na manyizye nuhala omwilu gagaifudiziwa agilenga malibho
1TI 4:2 esebho zyabho zyaigaluzanyiwa.
1TI 4:3 Waiwazijila aweje naposhele evyale huje Ongolobhe abhombele vitumishe asalifye wamo bhabho bhaposhela nabhe bhamenye lyoli.
1TI 4:4 Kila hatu hahahweli Ongolobhe abhombelehiza. Nahamo hasatiposhela asalifye hahahwazihwa akhanwe.
1TI 4:5 Hwa huje shibhozewa ashilile izu lya Ngolobhe na hudala elya eputo.
1TI 4:6 Kashile ubhagabheshe amanongwa ega hwitagalila lya aholo, obhabhe tumwa omwiza wa Yesu Kristi. Kashile bhalevizye hunongwa ye winza nahuje amanyizye aminza goga fwata.
1TI 4:7 Lakini zihane evilale vya msii vila vyeviganwa na bhashe agogolo afumepo manyila wewe owiza.
1TI 4:8 Hwa huje amazoezi agebele gawaziwa hashee huje uwinza gawaziwa eshihumambo goti. Abheshe ahadi husiku izya sheshinagala gagahwiza.
1TI 4:9 Amazu ega gaposhelelwe uwaziwa ahwiteshelwe hanii.
1TI 4:10 Hwa huje diomana titeseha natibhomba embombo ahwitume sana hwahuje tilinao odandamazu ashilile Ongolobhe alimwomi omwene ofyozi wabhantu bhoti, lakini huje bhabha huposhela.
1TI 4:11 Ogayanje na abhamanyizye amambo ego.
1TI 4:12 Omuntu wowonti sahwaziwa ahwisye osahala waho. Afumepo obheshilole zyo hwabhonti bhabha huposhela, katika ayanje, ajende, aganane, owinza na ahwiyozye.
1TI 4:13 Mpaka penaihweza khalaga amanyile naasundane, naamanyizye.
1TI 4:14 Ugajehwewe eshibhonesyezyo sheshili mhati yaho huje wapewilwe ashilile okho wa huje abheshelwe amakhono nazee.
1TI 4:15 Ogenye amambo ega. Ukhale katika ego akule hwaho hubhe wazi hwabhantu bhonti. Oyenyaje sana idala lyabho na manyizye.
1TI 4:16 Khalaga mamambo ego. Maana pobhombesho obhahwifyole umwene na bhala bhabha hutejezya.
1TI 5:1 Ugajehudamira ulume umzee. Bali upele umwoyo neshe uyise waho. Ubhapele umwoyo asahala abheshilume neshe aje bhaholo bhaho.
1TI 5:2 Upele umwoyo abhashe ashikolo kama neshe anyine bhaho na abhashe alenduneshe ayilombo bhaho huhuwinza wonti.
1TI 5:3 Uubhaheshimu afwele bhala bhabhali bhafwele lyoli lyoli.
1TI 5:4 Lelo nkeshele ufwele anabhana au namama ubhaleshe bhahwifunza abhonesye eheshima hwabhantu bha mnyumba yao bhebho uleshe bhabhasaidile aise bhabho. Aminza afwanaje ene nyinza hwitagalila elya Ngolobhe.
1TI 5:5 Lelo ufwele uwelyoli lyoli yayola yalehwilwe mwene wope abheshele na pambo male hwa Ngolobhe. Esiku zwonti aputa nalabhe esala usiku na pasanya.
1TI 5:6 Hata esho ufwele ula yakhala netuma afwiye lwapo mwomi.
1TI 5:7 Na ulombelele ege amambo ili kwamba bhagajebhe bhahwiune.
1TI 5:8 Eshi nkashile umuntu sabhalela ahoro bhakwe, tee bhala bhabhalimwao alaniwe na akhene ulyeteho na bhibhi ashile yasalinolyeteo.
1TI 5:9 Basi ushe gasimbisiweje abhe fwele abhaje namaha gasegaposhe sitini, abhanje fwele yali nolume umo.
1TI 5:10 Lazima abhanje amanyisye humatendo aminza abhanje abhalelile abhana bhakwe abhanje anepya hwanjenyi au abhanje abhasaidi aputi bhamwao, au ahwifumizwe humbombo yeyonti enyeza.
1TI 5:11 Lelo hwabhala afwele alendu ukhane abhabheshe hudadi yefwele kwasababu nkabhakhatwe ne taama agebele bhahwanza ahwengwe, hwidala eli bhahwinjila matama agebele zidi ya Kristi bhahwanza ahwengwe.
1TI 5:12 Hwidala eli bhahwinjila mhatia bhabudulanya hwifumye hwabho uhwelyoli.
1TI 5:13 Nantele bhahwiyinjizwa humazowea. Eye wolo abhahale bhazwogola khaya kwa khaya siyo aje bholo tu, bala antele bhabha bhasenkenyaji bhabhuhwinjilile abhale abhahale bhayanga amambo gasehwanziwa agayanje.
1TI 5:14 Eshi ane ehwanza abhashe alendu bhengwaje bhupapaje abhana, bhasimamilaje enyumba zwao ili bhagaje hupele ubhibhi enafasi ya tilonje kwa abhombe embibhi.
1TI 5:15 Kwa sababu bhamo bhao bhagulusi usetano.
1TI 5:16 Nkashile ushe yayonti uwelyeteho ana fwele, basi awavwe ili eshibhanza shigaje alemelye ili libhasailadiaje bhala bhabahli bhafwele lyolilyoli.
1TI 5:17 Basi bhala agosi bhalongozwa shinza mubhaheshimu aje bhahwaziwa abaheshimu marahahinji hasa bhala bhabha hwishuguliswa amwanzywe izu elya Ngolobhe.
1TI 5:18 Afwatanaje amasimbilo gayanga ugaje hufunje eng'ombe elo mu nalya eshalye ubhomba mbombo ahwanziwo ushala wakwe.”
1TI 5:19 Ugaje aposhe mashitaka hwagosi sipokua bhahweli ashahidi bhabhele au bhadatu.
1TI 5:20 Ehulajizwa ubha nkhane hwitagalilo elyebhantu wonti ili abhanje bhasageye labda bhagayeta.
1TI 5:21 Ehulujizwa kwa thati hwetagalila lya Ngolobhe, na hwitagalila ya Kristi uYesu, na bha malaika aleule aje uzitunze endajizwo ega bila asalulanye yoyonti na aije uganje abhombe ejambo lyolyonti apendele.
1TI 5:22 Ugaje hubheshele umuntu yoyonti okhono nanali ugaje ashiliki ibibhi zwa muntu uwe je uhwanziwa ahwilinde wewe mwenyewe ubhaje mwinza.
1TI 5:23 Sehwanziwa amwile amenzegene. Badala yakwe, unywelaje mvinyo hashe kwajili yevyanda nempongo yaho ye mara kwa mara.
1TI 5:24 Ibibhi baadhi ezwa bhantu zibhoneha wene zibhatagalile hundongo lelo baadhi ya bibhi zwa bhantu bhamo zibhafwata.
1TI 5:25 Hwisalo shesho baadhi ya yembombo enyinza zihwelewe hwa pawelele lelo hata zimo sezwaifisiha.
1TI 6:1 Bhala wonti bhabhali pansi yijoko hansi abhatumwa bhabhajele agosi bhao hansi bhi iheshima zyonti, bhahanziwa awombe esho ili itawa lya Ngolobhe na amanyizyo gagajialigwe.
1TI 6:2 Abhatumwa bhabhali nu gosi bhabheteshe bhangajehubhasyoshele kwa sababu abhene holo. Badala yakwe bhabhatumishile hani. Kwasababu agosi bhabhahavwa imbombo zyawo bhabheteshe nabhaganilwe. Fundizyaga na lumbelele amambo ego.
1TI 6:3 Nkesho umuntu omo amanyizya whateje na sagahugeteha amaelekezo agetu gawhaminishe, gagali mazu ga Gosi wetu uYesu Kristi, nkasagabhahulyeteha imanyizyo lililongozya hugolosu.
1TI 6:4 Umuntu oyo ahujidai sagamenye hohonti. Badala yakwe nu pezu namadalihanyo pamwanya yinjago, injango ezi zipapa uwivu, iwo, indigo, ishauku imbibhi,
1TI 6:5 nu pezu wimara kwa mara kati yi bhantu bhe njele zizinanjishe bhasebha aje uwutanwa lidala lyabhe bhatabhazi”
1TI 6:6 Eshi uwugolosu nalizishe faida ingosi.
1TI 6:7 Kwa sababu sagatahenzele na shoshonti panse. Wala sagatiwezya aheje shoshonti afume panse.
1TI 6:8 Ibadala yakwe titosewe ni shalye na menda.
1TI 6:9 Eshi ewo bhabha whanza abhe ni ntabhazi bhagwa hunjelo, katika umtego. Bhagwa huukwelengusu umwinji ni nyanyu imbibhi, na hushintu shoshonti, shishihubhawomba abhantu bhadwine na maangamizi unanganyi.
1TI 6:10 Afwatanaje asongwe ihela ni wandilo wiaina zyonti zimbibhi. Abhantu ambao bhanyonywa eyo, bhateywiwhilwe uhutali nulweteho na bhajoshizye bhene nsewo inyingi.
1TI 6:11 Eshi awe wamuntu wa Ngolobhe, gashembele amambo ego. Fwata ilyoli, ugolosu, uwinza, ulugano, ujivwi, nuu pomakati.
1TI 6:12 Khoma iwo ilinza lilweteho. Lemelela uwomi wiwila wakwiziwilwe. Yali husababu ene aje ufumye usimishizi whilongolela lya simishizi abhinji whalila lililinza.
1TI 6:13 Ihapela indajizyo ene whilongelela lya Ngolobhe, wasababisya ivintu vyonti akhae, na whilongolela lya Yesu Ukristi, wayanjile yili lyoli wha Pontio uPilato:
1TI 6:14 Yibheshe indajizyo whilyoli bila amashaka, hadi Ugosi wetu lyayihenza uYesu uKristi.
1TI 6:15 Ongolobhe ayidhihilisya ulwenzo lyakwe umuda gog- Ungolobhe, Unsayiwe, engovo yene, umwene watabhala, ugosi walongozya.
1TI 6:16 Mwene akhala wila wakhala mu mwuzelu wosojelelwa. Nomo umuntu wawezya hunolo wala tete humwenye. Hukwakwe ibheheshimu nuuweno wiwila. Amina.
1TI 6:17 Bhawozye atabhazi monse omu bhangajihyituntumule, na bhangajitegemele uwutabhazi, wuwuli sagawiuhakika. Ibadayakwe, bhahanziwa ategemele Ongolobhe. Waliutipela utabhazi wonti wilyoli ili tisongwe.
1TI 6:18 Bhawozye bhawombaje aminza, bhatajilishe humbombo inyinza, bhabhe bhabhe bhakalibizi numutayali wafumye.
1TI 6:19 Whidala elyo bhanzahujibheshe umusingi umwinza humambo gagawhenza ili bhawezye akhate ukholo wowo.
1TI 6:20 I Timothewo, ulinda shila shupewilwe. Jefwe namapanjizanyo gishikwelengusu amadalihanyo gahujikhane gagali gilenga gahwetwa njele.
1TI 6:21 Baazi ya bhantu bhahugatangazya amambo ego nesho bhakosile ulweteho. Ineema ibhe pamoja nawe.
2TI 1:1 U Paulo umutume wa Yesu kristi sha hwanza Ungolobhe, sawasawa nu Ngolobhe shahaidile uwomi uuli mhati ya Kristi Yesu,
2TI 1:2 hwa Timotheo umwana yaganilwe: Uwene nu pumu afume hwa Ngolobhe udaada wa Kristi Yesu U Bwana wentu.
2TI 1:3 Ihusalipya Ungolobhe, yihumwombele shilola shinza nanzi shahawa wombile awadaada wentu, lwihwizuha ane iputa daima pamunsi
2TI 1:4 ishasenya inyonywa alole aje imemeje asongwe. Ihwinzuha amasonzi gaho.
2TI 1:5 Indi sihuzusya ahusu lweteho waho lioli, owo ulwahwande wahakheye hwa bibi waho u Loisi nu manye wano Uyunisi. Imenye aje ulweteho uwo ukhalamhanti yaho.
2TI 1:6 Eshi ane uhuhuzusya azinjizye ishipaji sha Ngolobhe shishileho mhati lyaho hwi idala lyaweshelwe inyowe zyane.
2TI 1:7 Uno Ungolobhe sanga ahatupiye impepo lya wonga, ila ngingovu na yilugano ni shinshi.
2TI 1:8 Awe usahailolele insoni yahunyanje uBwana wentu, nu wahuline ane ni Paulo impinyilwe nao. Huje indeho humalawa yii inzwi sawasawa ni ingovu zya Ngolobhe.
2TI 1:9 Yu Ngolobhe yatukomboye na hulukwizye huu winto ugolosu. Saga ahawombile esho afuatane ni mbombo izyentu ila alengane nuweene na umupango ugwanke yonyo. Ahatupiye amambo ego hwa Kristi Yesu ghangasele omasala ahuenze.
2TI 1:10 Lakini eshi ukombolwe wa Ngolobhe ulipa zelu uwahwenze umlokozi wenti uKristi Yesu. U Kristi yakomesha ufye na alente uwomi wasanga uduga huu zelu winzwi.
2TI 1:11 Aje ane nahasaluliwe awe nombelelo, mtume na umwalimu.
2TI 1:12 Ane ilawa nantele, ila sagailola insoni maana imenye umwene yamkombonye. Isimisizye aje umwene alini ngovu huhatunzye hala hahaweshele kwa ajili ya isiku lila.
2TI 1:13 Uyuzushe ifwano yi nongwa ya ugolosu uuhovyezye afume huline. Peka nu lweteho na ulugano ulelo mhanti ya Kristi Yesu.
2TI 1:14 Gaweshe amambo aminza gapelile Ungolobhe ashilile upepo ufinjile uhale mhanti yetu.
2TI 1:15 Umenye aje wonti wawakhala huu Asia wahaleshile. Hwikundi eli waleho Figelo nu Hemogene.
2TI 1:16 U Bwana aisajile inyumba ya Onesiforo amasala minchi ahanghelezezye sanga ahandoleye insoni umnyololo gwane.
2TI 1:17 Badala yakwe lwahali hu Roma ahanazile hani na ahanajile.
2TI 1:18 Ungolobhe amwavyaje apele irehema afume humwakwe isiku lila. Umwene ananavyinze lwanahali hwa Efeso, awe umenye shinza.
2TI 2:1 Ishi mwana wane, upelwe ikhone huwaushe uwauli muhati muliwe mwa Kristi u Yesu.
2TI 2:2 Ni mbombo uzuyuvhizye kwangu muhati mwa keti awinji, ubhatwalile wabhantu abhawaminiha ibho bha wezizye amanyizye abhanji.
2TI 2:3 Nimana amayimba palishimo naani, nishi sikali umwema wa Kristi Yesu.
2TI 2:4 Numo usikali uwa tumiha lwulwo uwabhombaimbombo zikawadi zyamuzhiihinhe izikhaloubhu, iliaje aphendezye ubosi wakwe ugosi.
2TI 2:5 Nantele muntu uwashindananishi abhanji zanya, hagabha ngiga khasaanyilile adanje uataratibu.
2TI 2:6 Ni lazima huje uwalima bhanje wawi bibidisye abhale poshele inguru yima vuno gakwe.
2TI 2:7 Nalamba huje iyanga huje uBwana aligane ni mbombo zhyunti.
2TI 2:8 Mwizuhaje uYesu Kristi, afume ishikholo sha Daudi, ola azyuha afume wa bhafwe. Hi alingane zinazyoizya nu mbelele,
2TI 2:9 huje isho shashintesa hata nangalile mwinjela napinye na manyololo nishi uwanajile lelo inongwa zya Ngulubhi lelo inongwa zya Ngulubhi hazi pinywa na manyololo.
2TI 2:10 Ishi ivumilila imbombo zyunti wa bhala wala Ungulubhi ahabha salula, aje bhope, bhapete awauliwe ubho mwa Kristi Yesu pandwemo nu usisyea uwila na wila.
2TI 2:11 Ijago ihinie iwaminishe: “ili tufwile pamo penenao taikhala taikhala nao,
2TI 2:12 ngatujimba taita bhala nao wope kama tukhana umwene bhope aitukhana wope atu khana.
2TI 2:13 khasatabha tuwaminiha, umwene aisagala wawaminishe hawezya awikhane yuyo.”
2TI 2:14 Wakumbusye inongwa zya Ngulubhi huje waleshe alongone huje inongwa nongwa waleshe saga galimana nimoishi afumiliane nili uwibhovu wala awa nthejelezya.
2TI 2:15 Bhomba awiyumele humaha hujintiwe nu Ngulubhi nishije uli bhomba mbombo inipato mbombo yasagalala lalamishilwe litumie izi lwalwoli shishinza.
2TI 2:16 Uwiyepusye ninongwa zya munzhi ngalongola zaidi ateje.
2TI 2:17 Bhayangana yangana ego gayendelela ni ilomola ilihola muhati omwo abhele uhaminoyanufileto.
2TI 2:18 Bhebho wantu bhananjile sanuwana lwoli wayinga azyuusiwe tayali hufishile ufumile waga lulanya ulwintishelo pahanti ipo wamo wamo.
2TI 2:19 Hata isho, usingi gwa Ngulubhi gwa bukamilishe, gakasimbilwe ugu, “Ungulubhi abhaminye awali bhamwene shila ya litambula itawa lwakwe oyo wa mwene, nashila ya tambula aje Bwana alazisiwa aiyefwe ni dhavu.”
2TI 2:20 Hunyumba ishi kabhi, saga huje viliivhombo igorodi shabantu nantena ivilelo vya mapishi nilogo. Vimo vhwabho awongopwe vimo satumile bila awongopwe.
2TI 2:21 Khamba umutu aiyozye yuyo afume ame ambeshe saziwo gopwa umweneshombo shashihwogopwa shivhihilwe hali imala Bwana, atayalishiwe washila mbombo inyiza.
2TI 2:22 Uzinyilaje izyaziletaa nyonye izya husahala, udhaje uda wanalwoli uwaushe ulugano na hosheshe na bhala bhahukugabhe Bwana humwoyo uzelu.
2TI 2:23 Lelo ukhane ula ulema maswali gishopuluzi ego galeta.
2TI 2:24 Alwe hagahuwa ziwa umuntu wagulumbhi hauwazi ibho hahawazi wa unogowa wantu mbunthi anje awezye amazye jivhi.
2TI 2:25 Ihwaziwa abhalejesye bhala abha hu khana epo hubhazi walo woloehwaziwa awehobhowa wantu bhunti unu abhafaidisye abhapele ahwiyisye huimanye lyoli.
2TI 2:26 Bhamanye apate injele na nantele na hwiyefwe mu tego gwaseno, pumande bhatekwile nu mwehale yilugano ulwakwe.
2TI 3:1 Lakini umanye huje insiku izyahumpelela hwahayibha ni nyakati ihome.
2TI 3:2 Pipo abhantu bhahayiyigana bhene bhahayizigana ihela bhayiyitima, abhayilole abhizihaka bhesebha hubhitua apafi bhabho wasiokua na shukulani na waovu.
2TI 3:3 Bhesebhali nu lugano ulwimandi bhesabhahwanza akhale ahinza na wowonti bhebhachonganisya bhebhali ni vurugu bhesebhaganile aminza.
2TI 3:4 Bhahayibha bhasaliti bhakaidi abhahuyigane bhubho na agane ianasa kuliko hugane Ungulubhi.
2TI 3:5 Hunzi bhahumputa Ungulubhi, lakini bhahuzikhana nguvu zyakwe muyepusye na bhantu ibho.
2TI 3:6 Pipo baadhi yabho bhalume bhebhahwinjila mufamilia zya bhantu na hubhasonshelezye abhashi ajinga ibhantu ibha bhamemile imbibhi. Bhebhalongozewa humbibhi ni nyonywoizwa kila aina.
2TI 3:7 Abhantu ibha bhamanyila insiku zyonti, lakini sebhabhwezizye hufishile uufahamu ulwilyoli.
2TI 3:8 Ndeshe shila u Yane nu Yambre bhahimiliye shinyume na Musa. Hwi dala ili abhalimu ibha abhilenga bhahwimilila shinyume ni lyoli. Bhantu bhebhananjishiwilwe insibho zyabhobhesabhahwitihwa ahusiane na lwitiho.
2TI 3:9 Lakini sebhayifiha apatali. Maana upumbavu wabho wayibhabhiha apazeru hubhantu bhonti ndeshe sheyahali hubha abhantu.
2TI 3:10 Lakini awe ufwatile amafundisho gani umwenendo wani, amakusudi gani, ulwitiho lwani ubhuvumilivu wani ulugano lwani usitahilivu wani,
2TI 3:11 amateso amaumivu na gegahanije hula hu Antiokia, Ikonio na Listra. Nagavumiliye amayimba. Ugosi ahanokuye hugonti.
2TI 3:12 Bhonti bhebhahwanza akhale amaisha agahumpute Ungulubhi mwa Kristi Yesu bhabhateswe.
2TI 3:13 Abhantu abhabhibhi na bhalenga bhabhazidi abhe bhabhomba mbibhi hani. Bhayabhapotosya abhanji abhene bhibho bhapotosizwe.
2TI 3:14 Lakini awe nyimilile humambo iga gewagamanye na hugitishe hudandamazu. Pipo uminye aje umanyiye hwananu.
2TI 3:15 Uminye afume huwana waho wagaminye amazwi aminza iga gangaletela iheshima lyilwitiho hwa Yesu Kristi.
2TI 3:16 Kila lyelyandihwilwe lipewilwe umwoyi nu Ngulubhi. Lifaa humafundisyo agifaida hwa shaushi na lekezisye amakosa na fundisye ihaki.
2TI 3:17 Ili huhinje umuntu wa Ngulubhi abhe kamili abhe apewilwe inyenzo zyonti kwaajili ya bhombe imbombo inyinza.
2TI 4:1 Ihupela ilajizyo imwanu hwa Ngulubhi nu Yesu Kristi, yayibhalouga abhimi nabhafwe, pipo ahwigulilwe hwakwe nabhu mwini wakwe.
2TI 4:2 Lumbilila izwi ubhe tayari hu muda wewuhwanza nawesebhu bhanziwa. Ubhabhuzye abhantu imbibhi zyabho ukhajilizye huuvumilivu wonti mimanyizyo.
2TI 4:3 Zyahaiyinza insiku zye abhantu sebhaiyejelana na mafundisho agilyoli. Badaka yakwe bhaiyanzila abhalimu amanyizye ni nyonywo zyabho. Hwidala ili amakutwi gabho gahayibha matekenyu.
2TI 4:4 Bhahayileha atejelezye amafundisyo agilyoli na geushile ihadithi.
2TI 4:5 Lakini awe ubhe ngolosu humambo gonti, jimbilila amakhome bhomba imbo iya numbilizi utimizye ihuduma yaho.
2TI 4:6 Pipo ani tiyari imiminilwe umuda uwasogole hwani bhulipipi.
2TI 4:7 Ishindine ni lyoli umwendo imbumalizizye ulwotoho indudimile.
2TI 4:8 Ingiga yilyoli ibhihwile kwaajili yani yu Gosi, ahayilonga hulyoli ahayimpela isiku lila. Na siyo huline tu hata hubhonti bhebhahugulila hwi shauku aloleshe hwakwe.
2TI 4:9 Mjitahidi ahwinze huline haraka.
2TI 4:10 Kwa kuwa uDema andeshile. Ayiganile insi iyilelo abhalile Sesalonike, Kreseni ahabhalie huGalatia, na Tito ahabhalile Dalmatia.
2TI 4:11 U Luka mwini ndiyo alinati. Umwenje unyinze nawo uwene wimuhimu huline katika ihuduma.
2TI 4:12 Intumile Tikiko Efeso.
2TI 4:13 Lila ijoho lyenahalileshile Troa hwa Karpo, lwe wahayiyinza hulilete peka na vila ivitabu ha ivya ngozi.
2TI 4:14 U Alekizanda yapunza ivyumahambambiye imbibhi iyinji ugo ahayilipa afatane na matendo gakwe.
2TI 4:15 Nawe ubhanje nawo maana yahapinjile sana amazwi gitu.
2TI 4:16 Katika atetele hwani hwahande numo umuntu wowonti yayimiliye peka nani, badala yakwe kila mtu ahandeshile Ungulubhi asahabhazizye ihatia.
2TI 4:17 Lakini Ungulubhi ahimiliye peka nani ahampela inguvu, huje ashilile huline izwi liyangwe hwukamilifu na mataifa bhapute ahwuvwe nahokolilwe mwilomu lyi Simba.
2TI 4:18 Ugosi ayinepusha na matendo gonti amabhibhi na hunokole kwaajili yi bhumwene uwahumwanya. Utuntu bhubhe hukwakwe wilawila. Ameni
2TI 4:19 Mundamshile u Pulusika, nu Akila ni nyumba iya Onesiforo.
2TI 4:20 U Erasto ahasyalile whwo hu Korintho, lakini utilifimo ahaneshile hu Mileto shali mminu.
2TI 4:21 Ufanye haraka uyinze kabula yi shipindi shimpepu. Eubulo alamshe wope, Pude, Lino, Claudia na aholo bhonti.
2TI 4:22 Ungulubhi abhe namwi peka nu mwoyo waho, Uweene bhenawee.
TIT 1:1 U Paulo utumwa nu Ngulubhi nutumwa nu Yesu UKristi hulwitio lwateuliwa wa Ngulubhi mahala ga lwoli galeta mahala gisangahusu.
TIT 1:2 Wawile musubhiluo lyiumi wawila wula Ngulubhi siga awajilea wandeilenga watusubhivhizye awa nde wila na wila.
TIT 1:3 Igamasala gakwe akwinkula izyoo lwakwe munongwa uwapvile anee aulumbelele. Ihaziwa abhombe ismihulazimisye yaguvu ya Ngulubhi ufhulo wetu.
TIT 1:4 Wa Tito, umwana uwanalwoli aligane nishawamini wakwe ulusulo lwituu, huyi ugwiphana nu waushea fume wa Ngulubhi uDada nu Yesu Ukristi ufhulu wetu.
TIT 1:5 Hunongwa ene ihale ha Krete, huje ugali nganye imongwa zyutii izya zyasagalile hagamalishe na vhavhishe Azehee wishiwaza kila khaya nishipalaji zyaga.
TIT 1:6 Azehe wishivhaza wasahalalamishe, ulume abhanje nushi omwo walina wana awaminiwa wasayangwa ama wasani ishisvii.
TIT 1:7 Ni muhimu wavhenyii, yawimila uwi nyumba iya Ngulubvi aga ndavhe uli silaumu, amganda lalamishe angamutu wibwango uwasawikhana. Alazimiha angahve mwalahombwa ga ndafumilane numwene agandevhe wivho asaheze avhe wanyonyoywe amanyonye.
TIT 1:8 Usimamizi awanje wakalibisye, yawaza uwiza awanje mudhu wijele. Zyunhi awe wana lyoli, uyahuputa Ungulubhi uwakha nayuya.
TIT 1:9 Unu awezya asimamile inyipoto izyana lwolisha manyizye. Ili awezyaaje awa pinye moyo gibhawamazye apele gamanyizye amiza lyawezya awapendulanya awandulanye awahukhana, afanaje winji wazileshe indajizyo hasa wala tohala inongwa yao yamapuli yapuluzya bhakhopela.
TIT 1:10 Pipo awawitejele wiji hasa watohala utunongwa twao twapuruzye. Wakhopela nawalongozye awadhu araposhe.
TIT 1:11 Iwaziwa abhazije abhadhuniivho bhawamanyizya gala gasatafundizye agasagawazi wa kwa fainda idhi dhinho ni wananganye nganya uwizyo wudhi.
TIT 1:12 Mutiyao, mutu upole ayanga, “Wakrete wali ni lenga lwasalimaliha bhavhivhi makhanu hatali bholo natena bhapafuu.”
TIT 1:13 Enya gawelezewa gana lwoli ishiubhakhane wikhone liwazye ayanje ilwoli mulwizyo.
TIT 1:14 Awe ungandawisanganye nivilalo au ndalozya sazi papa izya Kiyahudi ama hamutii zwabhabhu abha bhawuzya khosi wanalwoli.
TIT 1:15 Wabhobhi walishiza ivhibhu na shimo shalishiza afatane inzi ozyao dhilika zyaozi chafuliwe.
TIT 1:16 Wahwitiha humanye Ungulubhi, lelo imbombo zyao zikhana abhene wani nthavu habhawiyisyeswa sabhahakisiwe humbombe inyiza.
TIT 2:1 Pamo awe gayanje gala gagabhalilana nalanganyizye gelweteho.
TIT 2:2 Azehe bhabhe hashe, ishishi, uhogowe, ulweteho ulwinza, nulugano na nujivwi.
TIT 2:3 Shesho abhashe abhazehe lazima isalazyonti bhajilolense bhewo bhene hansi bhegolosu, na bhabagabhasenkenyaji. Bhangajabhe bhatumwa bhihombwa.
TIT 2:4 Wapaswa amanyizye gagali muhogowe lubhalenganye abhalendo nuhogowe hubhagane alume bhao na abhana bhawo.
TIT 2:5 Bhanziwa hubhafundizye abhe nuluhogowe, bhinza, bhabheha shinza inyumba zyawo, bhihaje whalume bhawo bhewo. Bhalazimiha awombela Ngolobhe lingajealigwe.
TIT 2:6 Whinamuna yeyo yeyo, wapanji umoyo avijana bhishilume bhabhe nuhogowe.
TIT 2:7 Na mumadala gonti jibhehaji bhewo abhe shifwani katika imbombo inyinza; na lwamumanyizya, lolesyaji winzahani ni shishi.
TIT 2:8 Yangaji iizu lyengovo lyasagalili ni kasolo kwa sababu sagaali ni libhibhi lyolyonti humwanya yetu.
TIT 2:9 Bhatumwa bhihaje wha gosi bhawo hushi hantu. Bhahanziwa hubhasongwezye nasagadasanye nawo.
TIT 2:10 Sagabhahanziwa awhibhe. Hahawhanziwa, bhahanziwa alolesye ulweteho lonti ulwinza ili aje katika amadala gonti Bhagapambe amamanyizyo gonti gagahusu Ongolobhe unkombozi wetu.
TIT 2:11 Afwatanaje ineema ya Ngolobhe iloleshe hubhantu wonti.
TIT 2:12 Ihutifundizya akhane ambo gasaga kishi Ngolobhe nanyonywe wishense. Ihutifundizya akhale whihogowe, whilyoli, na hwida lishi Ngolobhe whisala ogu.
TIT 2:13 Isala zyatitalaji aposhele itegemeo lyetu lilusayo mwaloleshe muutuntumu wa Ngolobhe wetu ugosi na ummokozi wetu Kristi.
TIT 2:14 U Yesu ajifumizye yoyo kwaajili yetu ili hutokole afume mumbibhi na hutebheshe bhinza, kwajili yakwe abhantu bhasalulilwe bhali nihamu ya wombe imbombo inyinza.
TIT 2:15 Gayanje na hugasimishizye amambo ego. Khalipila kwa amamlaka gonti. Usaheteshe umuntu wowonti asholanyenye.
TIT 3:1 Ubhakumbusye ahwishehwa longozi na gosi hubhitishe nabhe tiyali humbombo zyonti nyinza.
TIT 3:2 Ubhakumbusye bhagandi hu mmombele imbibhi umuntu wowonti bhagandi adalisanye, bhabhapele umnda ahwamule alolesye ahwishe hubhantu bhonti.
TIT 3:3 Pipo twi twali ni nsibho imbibhi nukhali, twalimutegwe. Tuhali bhatumwa hunyenywe inyinji ni sitarehe. Tahakhiye nulukelo namubhibhi. Tahavisizye na visanye.
TIT 3:4 Lelo asajilwe hwa Ngolobhi umulokozi wetu nu lugano lwakeve hwa bhanadamu lwa haloleshe,
TIT 3:5 seyahali humatendo gitu agilyoli getu ahabhombile ila twahokoshe huwene wakwe. Atwokoye hwa kwile uhwapapwe shipya na bhumbwe shipya hwa Mpepo Umfinjile.
TIT 3:6 Ungulubhi ahitile Umpepo umfinjile hani hulite ashilile hwa Yesu Kilisti umlokozi wetu.
